          ||1 mahābhārate ādiparwam ||

 

              anukramaṇīparwa
                  1


nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiwa narottamam |
dewīṃ saraswatīṃ caiwa tato jayamudīrayet ||0||

lomaharṣaṇaputra ugraśrawāḥ sūtaḥ paurāṇiko naimiṣāraṇye śaunakasya kulapaterdwādaśawārṣike satre | 001 |

samāsīnānabhyagacchadbrahmarṣīnsaṃśitawratān |
winayāwanato bhūtwā kadācitsūtanandanaḥ ||2||

tamāśramamanuprāptaṃ naimiṣāraṇyawāsinaḥ |
citrāḥ śrotuṃ kathāstatra pariwawrustapaswinaḥ ||3||

abhiwādya munīṃstāṃstu sarwānewa kṛtāñjaliḥ |
apṛcchatsa tapowṛddhiṃ sadbhiścaiwābhinanditaḥ ||4||

atha teṣūpawiṣṭeṣu sarweṣwewa tapaswiṣu |
nirdiṣṭamāsanaṃ bheje winayāllomaharṣaṇiḥ ||5||

sukhāsīnaṃ tatastaṃ tu wiśrāntamupalakṣya ca |
athāpṛcchadṛṣistatra kaścitprastāwayankathāḥ ||6||

kuta āgamyate saute kwa cāyaṃ wihṛtastwayā |
kālaḥ kamalapatrākṣa śaṃsaitatpṛcchato mama ||7||

sūta uwāca||

janamejayasya rājarṣeḥ sarpasatre mahātmanaḥ |
samīpe pārthiwendrasya samyakpārikṣitasya ca ||8||

kṛṣṇadwaipāyanaproktāḥ supuṇyā wiwidhāḥ kathāḥ |
kathitāścāpi widhiwadyā waiśampāyanena wai ||9||

śrutwāhaṃ tā wicitrārthā mahābhāratasaṃśritāḥ |
bahūni samparikramya tīrthānyāyatanāni ca ||10||

samantapañcakaṃ nāma puṇyaṃ dwijaniṣewitam |
gatawānasmi taṃ deśaṃ yuddhaṃ yatrābhawatpurā ||11||

pāṇḍawānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca sarweṣāṃ ca mahīkṣitām ||11||

didṛkṣurāgatastasmātsamīpaṃ bhawatāmiha |
āyuṣmantaḥ sarwa ewa brahmabhūtā hi me matāḥ ||12||

asminyajñe mahābhāgāḥ sūryapāwakawarcasaḥ |
kṛtābhiṣekāḥ śucayaḥ kṛtajapyā hutāgnayaḥ ||13||

bhawanta āsate swasthā brawīmi kimahaṃ dwijāḥ ||13||

purāṇasaṃśritāḥ puṇyāḥ kathā wā dharmasaṃśritāḥ |
itiwṛttaṃ narendrāṇāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām ||14||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ||

dwaipāyanena yatproktaṃ purāṇaṃ paramarṣiṇā |
surairbrahmarṣibhiścaiwa śrutwā yadabhipūjitam ||15||

tasyākhyānawariṣṭhasya wicitrapadaparwaṇaḥ |
sūkṣmārthanyāyayuktasya wedārthairbhūṣitasya ca ||16||

bhāratasyetihāsasya puṇyāṃ granthārthasaṃyutām |
saṃskāropagatāṃ brāhmīṃ nānāśāstropabṛṃhitām ||17||

janamejayasya yāṃ rājño waiśampāyana uktawān |
yathāwatsa ṛṣistuṣṭyā satre dwaipāyanājñayā ||18||

wedaiścaturbhiḥ samitāṃ wyāsasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ |
saṃhitāṃ śrotumicchāmo dharmyāṃ pāpabhayāpahām ||19||

sūta uwāca||

ādyaṃ puruṣamīśānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam |
ṛtamekākṣaraṃ brahma wyaktāwyaktaṃ sanātanam ||20||

asacca saccaiwa ca yadwiśwaṃ sadasataḥ param |
parāwarāṇāṃ sraṣṭāraṃ purāṇaṃ paramawyayam ||21||

maṅgalyaṃ maṅgalaṃ wiṣṇuṃ wareṇyamanaghaṃ śucim |
namaskṛtya hṛṣīkeśaṃ carācaraguruṃ harim ||22||

maharṣeḥ pūjitasyeha sarwaloke mahātmanaḥ |
prawakṣyāmi mataṃ kṛtsnaṃ wyāsasyāmitatejasaḥ ||23||

ācakhyuḥ kawayaḥ kecitsampratyācakṣate pare |
ākhyāsyanti tathaiwānye itihāsamimaṃ bhuwi ||24||

idaṃ tu triṣu lokeṣu mahajjñānaṃ pratiṣṭhitam |
wistaraiśca samāsaiśca dhāryate yaddwijātibhiḥ ||25||

alaṅkṛtaṃ śubhaiḥ śabdaiḥ samayairdiwyamānuṣaiḥ |
chandowṛttaiśca wiwidhairanwitaṃ widuṣāṃ priyam ||26||

niṣprabhe'sminnirāloke sarwatastamasāwṛte |
bṛhadaṇḍamabhūdekaṃ prajānāṃ bījamakṣayam ||27||

yugasyādau nimittaṃ tanmahaddiwyaṃ pracakṣate |
yasmiṃstacchrūyate satyaṃ jyotirbrahma sanātanam ||28||

adbhutaṃ cāpyacintyaṃ ca sarwatra samatāṃ gatam |
awyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ yattatsadasadātmakam ||29||

yasmātpitāmaho jajñe prabhurekaḥ prajāpatiḥ |
brahmā suraguruḥ sthāṇurmanuḥ kaḥ parameṣṭhyatha ||30||

prācetasastathā dakṣo dakṣaputrāśca sapta ye |
tataḥ prajānāṃ patayaḥ prābhawannekawiṃśatiḥ ||31||

puruṣaścāprameyātmā yaṃ sarwamṛṣayo widuḥ |
wiśwedewāstathādityā wasawo'thāśwināwapi ||32||

yakṣāḥ sādhyāḥ piśācāśca guhyakāḥ pitarastathā |
tataḥ prasūtā widwāṃsaḥ śiṣṭā brahmarṣayo'malāḥ ||33||

rājarṣayaśca bahawaḥ sarwaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥ |
āpo dyauḥ pṛthiwī wāyurantarikṣaṃ diśastathā ||34||

saṃwatsarartawo māsāḥ pakṣāhorātrayaḥ kramāt |
yaccānyadapi tatsarwaṃ sambhūtaṃ lokasākṣikam ||35||

yadidaṃ dṛśyate kiñcidbhūtaṃ sthāwarajaṅgamam |
punaḥ saṅkṣipyate sarwaṃ jagatprāpte yugakṣaye ||36||

yathartāwṛtuliṅgāni nānārūpāṇi paryaye |
dṛśyante tāni tānyewa tathā bhāwā yugādiṣu ||37||

ewametadanādyantaṃ bhūtasaṃhārakārakam |
anādinidhanaṃ loke cakraṃ sampariwartate ||38||

trayastriṃśatsahasrāṇi trayastriṃśacchatāni ca |
trayastriṃśacca dewānāṃ sṛṣṭiḥ saṅkṣepalakṣaṇā ||39||

diwasputro bṛhadbhānuścakṣurātmā wibhāwasuḥ |
sawitā ca ṛcīko'rko bhānurāśāwaho rawiḥ ||40||

putrā wiwaswataḥ sarwe mahyasteṣāṃ tathāwaraḥ |
dewabhrāṭtanayastasya tasmātsubhrāḍiti smṛtaḥ ||41||

subhrājastu trayaḥ putrāḥ prajāwanto bahuśrutāḥ |
daśajyotiḥ śatajyotiḥ sahasrajyotirātmawān ||42||

daśa putrasahasrāṇi daśajyotermahātmanaḥ |
tato daśaguṇāścānye śatajyoterihātmajāḥ ||43||

bhūyastato daśaguṇāḥ sahasrajyotiṣaḥ sutāḥ |
tebhyo'yaṃ kuruwaṃśaśca yadūnāṃ bharatasya ca ||44||

yayātīkṣwākuwaṃśaśca rājarṣīṇāṃ ca sarwaśaḥ |
sambhūtā bahawo waṃśā bhūtasargāḥ sawistarāḥ ||45||

bhūtasthānāni sarwāṇi rahasyaṃ triwidhaṃ ca yat |
wedayogaṃ sawijñānaṃ dharmo'rthaḥ kāma ewa ca ||46||

dharmakāmārthaśāstrāṇi śāstrāṇi wiwidhāni ca |
lokayātrāwidhānaṃ ca sambhūtaṃ dṛṣṭawānṛṣiḥ ||47||

itihāsāḥ sawaiyākhyā wiwidhāḥ śrutayo'pi ca |
iha sarwamanukrāntamuktaṃ granthasya lakṣaṇam ||48||

wistīryaitanmahajjñānamṛṣiḥ saṅkṣepamabrawīt |
iṣṭaṃ hi widuṣāṃ loke samāsawyāsadhāraṇam ||49||

manwādi bhārataṃ kecidāstīkādi tathāpare |
tathoparicarādyanye wiprāḥ samyagadhīyate ||50||

wiwidhaṃ saṃhitājñānaṃ dīpayanti manīṣiṇaḥ |
wyākhyātuṃ kuśalāḥ kecidgranthaṃ dhārayituṃ pare ||51||

tapasā brahmacaryeṇa wyasya wedaṃ sanātanam |
itihāsamimaṃ cakre puṇyaṃ satyawatīsutaḥ ||52||

parāśarātmajo widwānbrahmarṣiḥ saṃśitawrataḥ |
māturniyogāddharmātmā gāṅgeyasya ca dhīmataḥ ||53||

kṣetre wicitrawīryasya kṛṣṇadwaipāyanaḥ purā |
trīnagnīniwa kaurawyāñjanayāmāsa wīryawān ||54||

utpādya dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pāṇḍuṃ widuramewa ca |
jagāma tapase dhīmānpunarewāśramaṃ prati ||55||

teṣu jāteṣu wṛddheṣu gateṣu paramāṃ gatim |
abrawīdbhārataṃ loke mānuṣe'sminmahānṛṣiḥ ||56||

janamejayena pṛṣṭaḥ sanbrāhmaṇaiśca sahasraśaḥ |
śaśāsa śiṣyamāsīnaṃ waiśampāyanamantike ||57||

sa sadasyaiḥ sahāsīnaḥ śrāwayāmāsa bhāratam |
karmāntareṣu yajñasya codyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||58||

wistaraṃ kuruwaṃśasya gāndhāryā dharmaśīlatām |
kṣattuḥ prajñāṃ dhṛtiṃ kuntyāḥ samyagdwaipāyano'brawīt ||59||

wāsudewasya māhātmyaṃ pāṇḍawānāṃ ca satyatām |
durwṛttaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāmuktawānbhagawānṛṣiḥ ||60||

caturwiṃśatisāhasrīṃ cakre bhāratasaṃhitām |
upākhyānairwinā tāwadbhārataṃ procyate budhaiḥ ||61||

tato'dhyardhaśataṃ bhūyaḥ saṅkṣepaṃ kṛtawānṛṣiḥ |
anukramaṇimadhyāyaṃ wṛttāntānāṃ saparwaṇām ||62||

idaṃ dwaipāyanaḥ pūrwaṃ putramadhyāpayacchukam |
tato'nyebhyo'nurūpebhyaḥ śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau prabhuḥ ||63||

nārado'śrāwayaddewānasito dewalaḥ pitṛn |
gandharwayakṣarakṣāṃsi śrāwayāmāsa wai śukaḥ ||64||

duryodhano manyumayo mahādrumaḥ; skandhaḥ karṇaḥ śakunistasya śākhāḥ |
duḥśāsanaḥ puṣpaphale samṛddhe; mūlaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro'manīṣī ||65||

yudhiṣṭhiro dharmamayo mahādrumaḥ; skandho'rjuno bhīmaseno'sya śākhāḥ |
mādrīsutau puṣpaphale samṛddhe; mūlaṃ kṛṣṇo brahma ca brāhmaṇāśca ||66||

pāṇḍurjitwā bahūndeśānyudhā wikramaṇena ca |
araṇye mṛgayāśīlo nyawasatsajanastadā ||67||

mṛgawyawāyanidhane kṛcchrāṃ prāpa sa āpadam |
janmaprabhṛti pārthānāṃ tatrācārawidhikramaḥ ||68||

mātrorabhyupapattiśca dharmopaniṣadaṃ prati |
dharmasya wāyoḥ śakrasya dewayośca tathāświnoḥ ||69||

tāpasaiḥ saha saṃwṛddhā mātṛbhyāṃ parirakṣitāḥ |
medhyāraṇyeṣu puṇyeṣu mahatāmāśrameṣu ca ||70||

ṛṣibhiśca tadānītā dhārtarāṣṭrānprati swayam |
śiśawaścābhirūpāśca jaṭilā brahmacāriṇaḥ ||71||

putrāśca bhrātaraśceme śiṣyāśca suhṛdaśca waḥ |
pāṇḍawā eta ityuktwā munayo'ntarhitāstataḥ ||72||

tāṃstairniweditāndṛṣṭwā pāṇḍawānkaurawāstadā |
śiṣṭāśca warṇāḥ paurā ye te harṣāccukruśurbhṛśam ||73||

āhuḥ kecinna tasyaite tasyaita iti cāpare |
yadā ciramṛtaḥ pāṇḍuḥ kathaṃ tasyeti cāpare ||74||

swāgataṃ sarwathā diṣṭyā pāṇḍoḥ paśyāma santatim |
ucyatāṃ swāgatamiti wāco'śrūyanta sarwaśaḥ ||75||

tasminnuparate śabde diśaḥ sarwā winādayan |
antarhitānāṃ bhūtānāṃ niswanastumulo'bhawat ||76||

puṣpawṛṣṭiḥ śubhā gandhāḥ śaṅkhadundubhiniswanāḥ |
āsanpraweśe pārthānāṃ tadadbhutamiwābhawat ||77||

tatprītyā caiwa sarweṣāṃ paurāṇāṃ harṣasambhawaḥ |
śabda āsīnmahāṃstatra diwaspṛkkīrtiwardhanaḥ ||78||

te'pyadhītyākhilānwedāñśāstrāṇi wiwidhāni ca |
nyawasanpāṇḍawāstatra pūjitā akutobhayāḥ ||79||

yudhiṣṭhirasya śaucena prītāḥ prakṛtayo'bhawan |
dhṛtyā ca bhīmasenasya wikrameṇārjunasya ca ||80||

guruśuśrūṣayā kuntyā yamayorwinayena ca |
tutoṣa lokaḥ sakalasteṣāṃ śauryaguṇena ca ||81||

samawāye tato rājñāṃ kanyāṃ bhartṛswayaṃwarām |
prāptawānarjunaḥ kṛṣṇāṃ kṛtwā karma suduṣkaram ||82||

tataḥ prabhṛti loke'sminpūjyaḥ sarwadhanuṣmatām |
āditya iwa duṣprekṣyaḥ samareṣwapi cābhawat ||83||

sa sarwānpārthiwāñjitwā sarwāṃśca mahato gaṇān |
ājahārārjuno rājñe rājasūyaṃ mahākratum ||84||

annawāndakṣiṇāwāṃśca sarwaiḥ samudito guṇaiḥ |
yudhiṣṭhireṇa samprāpto rājasūyo mahākratuḥ ||85||

sunayādwāsudewasya bhīmārjunabalena ca |
ghātayitwā jarāsandhaṃ caidyaṃ ca balagarwitam ||86||

duryodhanamupāgacchannarhaṇāni tatastataḥ |
maṇikāñcanaratnāni gohastyaśwadhanāni ca ||87||

samṛddhāṃ tāṃ tathā dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍawānāṃ tadā śriyam |
īrṣyāsamutthaḥ sumahāṃstasya manyurajāyata ||88||

wimānapratimāṃ cāpi mayena sukṛtāṃ sabhām |
pāṇḍawānāmupahṛtāṃ sa dṛṣṭwā paryatapyata ||89||

yatrāwahasitaścāsītpraskandanniwa sambhramāt |
pratyakṣaṃ wāsudewasya bhīmenānabhijātawat ||90||

sa bhogānwiwidhānbhuñjanratnāni wiwidhāni ca |
kathito dhṛtarāṣṭrasya wiwarṇo hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ ||91||

anwajānāttato dyūtaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sutapriyaḥ |
tacchrutwā wāsudewasya kopaḥ samabhawanmahān ||92||

nātiprītamanāścāsīdwiwādāṃścānwamodata |
dyūtādīnanayānghorānprawṛddhāṃścāpyupaikṣata ||93||

nirasya widuraṃ droṇaṃ bhīṣmaṃ śāradwataṃ kṛpam |
wigrahe tumule tasminnahankṣatraṃ parasparam ||94||

jayatsu pāṇḍuputreṣu śrutwā sumahadapriyam |
duryodhanamataṃ jñātwā karṇasya śakunestathā ||95||

dhṛtarāṣṭraściraṃ dhyātwā sañjayaṃ wākyamabrawīt ||95||

śṛṇu sañjaya me sarwaṃ na me'sūyitumarhasi |
śrutawānasi medhāwī buddhimānprājñasaṃmataḥ ||96||

na wigrahe mama matirna ca prīye kurukṣaye |
na me wiśeṣaḥ putreṣu sweṣu pāṇḍusuteṣu ca ||97||

wṛddhaṃ māmabhyasūyanti putrā manyuparāyaṇāḥ |
ahaṃ twacakṣuḥ kārpaṇyātputraprītyā sahāmi tat ||98||

muhyantaṃ cānumuhyāmi duryodhanamacetanam ||98||

rājasūye śriyaṃ dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍawasya mahaujasaḥ |
taccāwahasanaṃ prāpya sabhārohaṇadarśane ||99||

amarṣitaḥ swayaṃ jetumaśaktaḥ pāṇḍawānraṇe |
nirutsāhaśca samprāptuṃ śriyamakṣatriyo yathā ||100||

gāndhārarājasahitaśchadmadyūtamamantrayat ||100||

tatra yadyadyathā jñātaṃ mayā sañjaya tacchṛṇu |
śrutwā hi mama wākyāni buddhyā yuktāni tattwataḥ ||101||

tato jñāsyasi māṃ saute prajñācakṣuṣamityuta ||101||

yadāśrauṣaṃ dhanurāyamya citraṃ; widdhaṃ lakṣyaṃ pātitaṃ wai pṛthiwyām |
kṛṣṇāṃ hṛtāṃ paśyatāṃ sarwarājñāṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||102||

yadāśrauṣaṃ dwārakāyāṃ subhadrāṃ; prasahyoḍhāṃ mādhawīmarjunena |
indraprasthaṃ wṛṣṇiwīrau ca yātau; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||103||

yadāśrauṣaṃ dewarājaṃ prawṛṣṭaṃ; śarairdiwyairwāritaṃ cārjunena |
agniṃ tathā tarpitaṃ khāṇḍawe ca; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||104||

yadāśrauṣaṃ hṛtarājyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraṃ; parājitaṃ saubalenākṣawatyām |
anwāgataṃ bhrātṛbhiraprameyai; stadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||105||

yadāśrauṣaṃ draupadīmaśrukaṇṭhīṃ; sabhāṃ nītāṃ duḥkhitāmekawastrām |
rajaswalāṃ nāthawatīmanāthawa; ttadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||106||

yadāśrauṣaṃ wiwidhāstāta ceṣṭā; dharmātmanāṃ prasthitānāṃ wanāya |
jyeṣṭhaprītyā kliśyatāṃ pāṇḍawānāṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||107||

yadāśrauṣaṃ snātakānāṃ sahasrai; ranwāgataṃ dharmarājaṃ wanastham |
bhikṣābhujāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ mahātmanāṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||108||

yadāśrauṣamarjuno dewadewaṃ; kirātarūpaṃ tryambakaṃ toṣya yuddhe |
awāpa tatpāśupataṃ mahāstraṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||109||

yadāśrauṣaṃ tridiwasthaṃ dhanañjayaṃ; śakrātsākṣāddiwyamastraṃ yathāwat |
adhīyānaṃ śaṃsitaṃ satyasandhaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||110||

yadāśrauṣaṃ waiśrawaṇena sārdhaṃ; samāgataṃ bhīmamanyāṃśca pārthān |
tasmindeśe mānuṣāṇāmagamye; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||111||

yadāśrauṣaṃ ghoṣayātrāgatānāṃ; bandhaṃ gandharwairmokṣaṇaṃ cārjunena |
sweṣāṃ sutānāṃ karṇabuddhau ratānāṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||112||

yadāśrauṣaṃ yakṣarūpeṇa dharmaṃ; samāgataṃ dharmarājena sūta |
praśnānuktānwibruwantaṃ ca samya; ktadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||113||

yadāśrauṣaṃ māmakānāṃ wariṣṭhā; ndhanañjayenaikarathena bhagnān |
wirāṭarāṣṭre wasatā mahātmanā; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||114||

yadāśrauṣaṃ satkṛtāṃ matsyarājñā; sutāṃ dattāmuttarāmarjunāya |
tāṃ cārjunaḥ pratyagṛhṇātsutārthe; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||115||

yadāśrauṣaṃ nirjitasyādhanasya; prawrājitasya swajanātpracyutasya |
akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta yudhiṣṭhirasya; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||116||

yadāśrauṣaṃ naranārāyaṇau tau; kṛṣṇārjunau wadato nāradasya |
ahaṃ draṣṭā brahmaloke sadeti; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||117||

yadāśrauṣaṃ mādhawaṃ wāsudewaṃ; sarwātmanā pāṇḍawārthe niwiṣṭam |
yasyemāṃ gāṃ wikramamekamāhu; stadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||118||

yadāśrauṣaṃ karṇaduryodhanābhyāṃ; buddhiṃ kṛtāṃ nigrahe keśawasya |
taṃ cātmānaṃ bahudhā darśayānaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||119||

yadāśrauṣaṃ wāsudewe prayāte; rathasyaikāmagratastiṣṭhamānām |
ārtāṃ pṛthāṃ sāntwitāṃ keśawena; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||120||

yadāśrauṣaṃ mantriṇaṃ wāsudewaṃ; tathā bhīṣmaṃ śāntanawaṃ ca teṣām |
bhāradwājaṃ cāśiṣo'nubruwāṇaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||121||

yadāśrauṣaṃ karṇa uwāca bhīṣmaṃ; nāhaṃ yotsye yudhyamāne twayīti |
hitwā senāmapacakrāma caiwa; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||122||

yadāśrauṣaṃ wāsudewārjunau tau; tathā dhanurgāṇḍiwamaprameyam |
trīṇyugrawīryāṇi samāgatāni; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||123||

yadāśrauṣaṃ kaśmalenābhipanne; rathopasthe sīdamāne'rjune wai |
kṛṣṇaṃ lokāndarśayānaṃ śarīre; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||124||

yadāśrauṣaṃ bhīṣmamamitrakarśanaṃ; nighnantamājāwayutaṃ rathānām |
naiṣāṃ kaścidwadhyate dṛśyarūpa; stadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||125||

yadāśrauṣaṃ bhīṣmamatyantaśūraṃ; hataṃ pārthenāhaweṣwapradhṛṣyam |
śikhaṇḍinaṃ purataḥ sthāpayitwā; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||126||

yadāśrauṣaṃ śaratalpe śayānaṃ; wṛddhaṃ wīraṃ sāditaṃ citrapuṅkhaiḥ |
bhīṣmaṃ kṛtwā somakānalpaśeṣāṃ; stadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||127||

yadāśrauṣaṃ śāntanawe śayāne; pānīyārthe coditenārjunena |
bhūmiṃ bhittwā tarpitaṃ tatra bhīṣmaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||128||

yadāśrauṣaṃ śukrasūryau ca yuktau; kaunteyānāmanulomau jayāya |
nityaṃ cāsmāñśwāpadā wyābhaṣanta; stadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||129||

yadā droṇo wiwidhānastramārgā; nwidarśayansamare citrayodhī |
na pāṇḍawāñśreṣṭhatamānnihanti; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||130||

yadāśrauṣaṃ cāsmadīyānmahārathā; nwyawasthitānarjunasyāntakāya |
saṃśaptakānnihatānarjunena; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||131||

yadāśrauṣaṃ wyūhamabhedyamanyai; rbhāradwājenāttaśastreṇa guptam |
bhittwā saubhadraṃ wīramekaṃ prawiṣṭaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||132||

yadābhimanyuṃ pariwārya bālaṃ; sarwe hatwā hṛṣṭarūpā babhūwuḥ |
mahārathāḥ pārthamaśaknuwanta; stadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||133||

yadāśrauṣamabhimanyuṃ nihatya; harṣānmūḍhānkrośato dhārtarāṣṭrān |
krodhaṃ muktaṃ saindhawe cārjunena; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||134||

yadāśrauṣaṃ saindhawārthe pratijñāṃ; pratijñātāṃ tadwadhāyārjunena |
satyāṃ nistīrṇāṃ śatrumadhye ca tena; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||135||

yadāśrauṣaṃ śrāntahaye dhanañjaye; muktwā hayānpāyayitwopawṛttān |
punaryuktwā wāsudewaṃ prayātaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||136||

yadāśrauṣaṃ wāhaneṣwāśwasatsu; rathopasthe tiṣṭhatā gāṇḍiwena |
sarwānyodhānwāritānarjunena; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||137||

yadāśrauṣaṃ nāgabalairdurutsahaṃ; droṇānīkaṃ yuyudhānaṃ pramathya |
yātaṃ wārṣṇeyaṃ yatra tau kṛṣṇapārthau; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||138||

yadāśrauṣaṃ karṇamāsādya muktaṃ; wadhādbhīmaṃ kutsayitwā wacobhiḥ |
dhanuṣkoṭyā tudya karṇena wīraṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||139||

yadā droṇaḥ kṛtawarmā kṛpaśca; karṇo drauṇirmadrarājaśca śūraḥ |
amarṣayansaindhawaṃ wadhyamānaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||140||

yadāśrauṣaṃ dewarājena dattāṃ; diwyāṃ śaktiṃ wyaṃsitāṃ mādhawena |
ghaṭotkace rākṣase ghorarūpe; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||141||

yadāśrauṣaṃ karṇaghaṭotkacābhyāṃ; yuddhe muktāṃ sūtaputreṇa śaktim |
yayā wadhyaḥ samare sawyasācī; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||142||

yadāśrauṣaṃ droṇamācāryamekaṃ; dhṛṣṭadyumnenābhyatikramya dharmam |
rathopasthe prāyagataṃ wiśastaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||143||

yadāśrauṣaṃ drauṇinā dwairathasthaṃ; mādrīputraṃ nakulaṃ lokamadhye |
samaṃ yuddhe pāṇḍawaṃ yudhyamānaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||144||

yadā droṇe nihate droṇaputro; nārāyaṇaṃ diwyamastraṃ wikurwan |
naiṣāmantaṃ gatawānpāṇḍawānāṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||145||

yadāśrauṣaṃ karṇamatyantaśūraṃ; hataṃ pārthenāhaweṣwapradhṛṣyam |
tasminbhrātṛṇāṃ wigrahe dewaguhye; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||146||

yadāśrauṣaṃ droṇaputraṃ kṛpaṃ ca; duḥśāsanaṃ kṛtawarmāṇamugram |
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ śūnyamadharṣayantaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||147||

yadāśrauṣaṃ nihataṃ madrarājaṃ; raṇe śūraṃ dharmarājena sūta |
sadā saṅgrāme spardhate yaḥ sa kṛṣṇaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||148||

yadāśrauṣaṃ kalahadyūtamūlaṃ; māyābalaṃ saubalaṃ pāṇḍawena |
hataṃ saṅgrāme sahadewena pāpaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||149||

yadāśrauṣaṃ śrāntamekaṃ śayānaṃ; hradaṃ gatwā stambhayitwā tadambhaḥ |
duryodhanaṃ wirathaṃ bhagnadarpaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||150||

yadāśrauṣaṃ pāṇḍawāṃstiṣṭhamānā; ngaṅgāhrade wāsudewena sārdham |
amarṣaṇaṃ dharṣayataḥ sutaṃ me; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||151||

yadāśrauṣaṃ wiwidhāṃstāta mārgā; ngadāyuddhe maṇḍalaṃ sañcarantam |
mithyā hataṃ wāsudewasya buddhyā; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||152||

yadāśrauṣaṃ droṇaputrādibhistai; rhatānpāñcālāndraupadeyāṃśca suptān |
kṛtaṃ bībhatsamayaśasyaṃ ca karma; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||153||

yadāśrauṣaṃ bhīmasenānuyātena; aśwatthāmnā paramāstraṃ prayuktam |
kruddhenaiṣīkamawadhīdyena garbhaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||154||

yadāśrauṣaṃ brahmaśiro'rjunena; muktaṃ swastītyastramastreṇa śāntam |
aśwatthāmnā maṇiratnaṃ ca dattaṃ; tadā nāśaṃse wijayāya sañjaya ||155||

yadāśrauṣaṃ droṇaputreṇa garbhe; wairāṭyā wai pātyamāne mahāstre |
dwaipāyanaḥ keśawo droṇaputraṃ; paraspareṇābhiśāpaiḥ śaśāpa ||156||

śocyā gāndhārī putrapautrairwihīnā; tathā wadhwaḥ pitṛbhirbhrātṛbhiśca |
kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ duṣkaraṃ pāṇḍaweyaiḥ; prāptaṃ rājyamasapatnaṃ punastaiḥ ||157||

kaṣṭaṃ yuddhe daśa śeṣāḥ śrutā me; trayo'smākaṃ pāṇḍawānāṃ ca sapta |
dwyūnā wiṃśatirāhatākṣauhiṇīnāṃ; tasminsaṅgrāme wigrahe kṣatriyāṇām ||158||

tamasā twabhyawastīrṇo moha āwiśatīwa mām |
sañjñāṃ nopalabhe sūta mano wihwalatīwa me ||159||

ityuktwā dhṛtarāṣṭro'tha wilapya bahuduḥkhitaḥ |
mūrcchitaḥ punarāśwastaḥ sañjayaṃ wākyamabrawīt ||160||

sañjayaiwaṅgate prāṇāṃstyaktumicchāmi māciram |
stokaṃ hyapi na paśyāmi phalaṃ jīwitadhāraṇe ||161||

taṃ tathāwādinaṃ dīnaṃ wilapantaṃ mahīpatim |
gāwalgaṇiridaṃ dhīmānmahārthaṃ wākyamabrawīt ||162||

śrutawānasi wai rājño mahotsāhānmahābalān |
dwaipāyanasya wadato nāradasya ca dhīmataḥ ||163||

mahatsu rājawaṃśeṣu guṇaiḥ samuditeṣu ca |
jātāndiwyāstrawiduṣaḥ śakrapratimatejasaḥ ||164||

dharmeṇa pṛthiwīṃ jitwā yajñairiṣṭwāptadakṣiṇaiḥ |
asmiṃlloke yaśaḥ prāpya tataḥ kālawaśaṃ gatāḥ ||165||

wainyaṃ mahārathaṃ wīraṃ sṛñjayaṃ jayatāṃ waram |
suhotraṃ rantidewaṃ ca kakṣīwantaṃ tathauśijam ||166||

bāhlīkaṃ damanaṃ śaibyaṃ śaryātimajitaṃ jitam |
wiśwāmitramamitraghnamambarīṣaṃ mahābalam ||167||

maruttaṃ manumikṣwākuṃ gayaṃ bharatamewa ca |
rāmaṃ dāśarathiṃ caiwa śaśabinduṃ bhagīratham ||168||

yayātiṃ śubhakarmāṇaṃ dewairyo yājitaḥ swayam |
caityayūpāṅkitā bhūmiryasyeyaṃ sawanākarā ||169||

iti rājñāṃ caturwiṃśannāradena surarṣiṇā |
putraśokābhitaptāya purā śaibyāya kīrtitāḥ ||170||

tebhyaścānye gatāḥ pūrwaṃ rājāno balawattarāḥ |
mahārathā mahātmānaḥ sarwaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥ ||171||

pūruḥ kururyaduḥ śūro wiṣwagaśwo mahādhṛtiḥ |
anenā yuwanāśwaśca kakutstho wikramī raghuḥ ||172||

wijitī wītihotraśca bhawaḥ śweto bṛhadguruḥ |
uśīnaraḥ śatarathaḥ kaṅko duliduho drumaḥ ||173||

dambhodbhawaḥ paro wenaḥ sagaraḥ saṅkṛtirnimiḥ |
ajeyaḥ paraśuḥ puṇḍraḥ śambhurdewāwṛdho'naghaḥ ||174||

dewāhwayaḥ supratimaḥ supratīko bṛhadrathaḥ |
mahotsāho winītātmā sukraturnaiṣadho nalaḥ ||175||

satyawrataḥ śāntabhayaḥ sumitraḥ subalaḥ prabhuḥ |
jānujaṅgho'naraṇyo'rkaḥ priyabhṛtyaḥ śubhawrataḥ ||176||

balabandhurnirāmardaḥ ketuśṛṅgo bṛhadbalaḥ |
dhṛṣṭaketurbṛhatketurdīptaketurnirāmayaḥ ||177||

awikṣitprabalo dhūrtaḥ kṛtabandhurdṛḍheṣudhiḥ |
mahāpurāṇaḥ sambhāwyaḥ pratyaṅgaḥ parahā śrutiḥ ||178||

ete cānye ca bahawaḥ śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ |
śrūyante'yutaśaścānye saṅkhyātāścāpi padmaśaḥ ||179||

hitwā suwipulānbhogānbuddhimanto mahābalāḥ |
rājāno nidhanaṃ prāptāstawa putrairmahattamāḥ ||180||

yeṣāṃ diwyāni karmāṇi wikramastyāga ewa ca |
māhātmyamapi cāstikyaṃ satyatā śaucamārjawam ||181||

widwadbhiḥ kathyate loke purāṇaiḥ kawisattamaiḥ |
sarwarddhiguṇasampannāste cāpi nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ||182||

tawa putrā durātmānaḥ prataptāścaiwa manyunā |
lubdhā durwṛttabhūyiṣṭhā na tāñśocitumarhasi ||183||

śrutawānasi medhāwī buddhimānprājñasaṃmataḥ |
yeṣāṃ śāstrānugā buddhirna te muhyanti bhārata ||184||

nigrahānugrahau cāpi widitau te narādhipa |
nātyantamewānuwṛttiḥ śrūyate putrarakṣaṇe ||185||

bhawitawyaṃ tathā tacca nātaḥ śocitumarhasi |
daiwaṃ prajñāwiśeṣeṇa ko niwartitumarhati ||186||

widhātṛwihitaṃ mārgaṃ na kaścidatiwartate |
kālamūlamidaṃ sarwaṃ bhāwābhāwau sukhāsukhe ||187||

kālaḥ pacati bhūtāni kālaḥ saṃharati prajāḥ |
nirdahantaṃ prajāḥ kālaṃ kālaḥ śamayate punaḥ ||188||

kālo wikurute bhāwānsarwāṃlloke śubhāśubhān |
kālaḥ saṅkṣipate sarwāḥ prajā wisṛjate punaḥ ||189||

kālaḥ sarweṣu bhūteṣu caratyawidhṛtaḥ samaḥ ||189||

atītānāgatā bhāwā ye ca wartanti sāmpratam |
tānkālanirmitānbuddhwā na sañjñāṃ hātumarhasi ||190||

sūta uwāca||

atropaniṣadaṃ puṇyāṃ kṛṣṇadwaipāyano'brawīt |
bhāratādhyayanātpuṇyādapi pādamadhīyataḥ ||191||

śraddadhānasya pūyante sarwapāpānyaśeṣataḥ ||191||

dewarṣayo hyatra puṇyā brahmarājarṣayastathā |
kīrtyante śubhakarmāṇastathā yakṣamahoragāḥ ||192||

bhagawānwāsudewaśca kīrtyate'tra sanātanaḥ |
sa hi satyamṛtaṃ caiwa pawitraṃ puṇyamewa ca ||193||

śāśwataṃ brahma paramaṃ dhruwaṃ jyotiḥ sanātanam |
yasya diwyāni karmāṇi kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ||194||

asatsatsadasaccaiwa yasmāddewātprawartate |
santatiśca prawṛttiśca janma mṛtyuḥ punarbhawaḥ ||195||

adhyātmaṃ śrūyate yacca pañcabhūtaguṇātmakam |
awyaktādi paraṃ yacca sa ewa parigīyate ||196||

yattadyatiwarā yuktā dhyānayogabalānwitāḥ |
pratibimbamiwādarśe paśyantyātmanyawasthitam ||197||

śraddadhānaḥ sadodyuktaḥ satyadharmaparāyaṇaḥ |
āsewannimamadhyāyaṃ naraḥ pāpātpramucyate ||198||

anukramaṇimadhyāyaṃ bhāratasyemamāditaḥ |
āstikaḥ satataṃ śṛṇwanna kṛcchreṣwawasīdati ||199||

ubhe sandhye japankiñcitsadyo mucyeta kilbiṣāt |
anukramaṇyā yāwatsyādahnā rātryā ca sañcitam ||200||

bhāratasya wapurhyetatsatyaṃ cāmṛtamewa ca |
nawanītaṃ yathā dadhno dwipadāṃ brāhmaṇo yathā ||201||

hradānāmudadhiḥ śreṣṭho gaurwariṣṭhā catuṣpadām |
yathaitāni wariṣṭhāni tathā bhāratamucyate ||202||

yaścainaṃ śrāwayecchrāddhe brāhmaṇānpādamantataḥ |
akṣayyamannapānaṃ tatpitṛṃstasyopatiṣṭhati ||203||

itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ wedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet |
bibhetyalpaśrutādwedo māmayaṃ pratariṣyati ||204||

kārṣṇaṃ wedamimaṃ widwāñśrāwayitwārthamaśnute |
bhrūṇahatyākṛtaṃ cāpi pāpaṃ jahyānna saṃśayaḥ ||205||

ya imaṃ śuciradhyāyaṃ paṭhetparwaṇi parwaṇi |
adhītaṃ bhārataṃ tena kṛtsnaṃ syāditi me matiḥ ||206||

yaścemaṃ śṛṇuyānnityamārṣaṃ śraddhāsamanwitaḥ |
sa dīrghamāyuḥ kīrtiṃ ca swargatiṃ cāpnuyānnaraḥ ||207||

catwāra ekato wedā bhārataṃ caikamekataḥ |
samāgataiḥ surarṣibhistulāmāropitaṃ purā ||208||

mahattwe ca gurutwe ca dhriyamāṇaṃ tato'dhikam ||208||

mahattwādbhārawattwācca mahābhāratamucyate |
niruktamasya yo weda sarwapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||209||

tapo na kalko'dhyayanaṃ na kalkaḥ; swābhāwiko wedawidhirna kalkaḥ |
prasahya wittāharaṇaṃ na kalka; stānyewa bhāwopahatāni kalkaḥ ||210||






              parwasaṃgrahaparwa
                  2


ṛṣaya ūcuḥ||

samantapañcakamiti yaduktaṃ sūtanandana |
etatsarwaṃ yathānyāyaṃ śrotumicchāmahe wayam ||1||

sūta uwāca||

śuśrūṣā yadi wo wiprā bruwataśca kathāḥ śubhāḥ |
samantapañcakākhyaṃ ca śrotumarhatha sattamāḥ ||2||

tretādwāparayoḥ sandhau rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ waraḥ |
asakṛtpārthiwaṃ kṣatraṃ jaghānāmarṣacoditaḥ ||3||

sa sarwaṃ kṣatramutsādya swawīryeṇānaladyutiḥ |
samantapañcake pañca cakāra rudhirahradān ||4||

sa teṣu rudhirāmbhassu hradeṣu krodhamūrcchitaḥ |
pitṛnsantarpayāmāsa rudhireṇeti naḥ śrutam ||5||

atharcīkādayo'bhyetya pitaro brāhmaṇarṣabham |
taṃ kṣamasweti siṣidhustataḥ sa wirarāma ha ||6||

teṣāṃ samīpe yo deśo hradānāṃ rudhirāmbhasām |
samantapañcakamiti puṇyaṃ tatparikīrtitam ||7||

yena liṅgena yo deśo yuktaḥ samupalakṣyate |
tenaiwa nāmnā taṃ deśaṃ wācyamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ||8||

antare caiwa samprāpte kalidwāparayorabhūt |
samantapañcake yuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍawasenayoḥ ||9||

tasminparamadharmiṣṭhe deśe bhūdoṣawarjite |
aṣṭādaśa samājagmurakṣauhiṇyo yuyutsayā ||10||

ewaṃ nāmābhinirwṛttaṃ tasya deśasya wai dwijāḥ |
puṇyaśca ramaṇīyaśca sa deśo waḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||11||

tadetatkathitaṃ sarwaṃ mayā wo munisattamāḥ |
yathā deśaḥ sa wikhyātastriṣu lokeṣu wiśrutaḥ ||12||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ||

akṣauhiṇya iti proktaṃ yattwayā sūtanandana |
etadicchāmahe śrotuṃ sarwamewa yathātatham ||13||

akṣauhiṇyāḥ parīmāṇaṃ rathāśwanaradantinām |
yathāwaccaiwa no brūhi sarwaṃ hi widitaṃ tawa ||14||

sūta uwāca||

eko ratho gajaścaiko narāḥ pañca padātayaḥ |
trayaśca turagāstajjñaiḥ pattirityabhidhīyate ||15||

pattiṃ tu triguṇāmetāmāhuḥ senāmukhaṃ budhāḥ |
trīṇi senāmukhānyeko gulma ityabhidhīyate ||16||

trayo gulmā gaṇo nāma wāhinī tu gaṇāstrayaḥ |
smṛtāstisrastu wāhinyaḥ pṛtaneti wicakṣaṇaiḥ ||17||

camūstu pṛtanāstisrastisraścamwastwanīkinī |
anīkinīṃ daśaguṇāṃ prāhurakṣauhiṇīṃ budhāḥ ||18||

akṣauhiṇyāḥ prasaṅkhyānaṃ rathānāṃ dwijasattamāḥ |
saṅkhyāgaṇitatattwajñaiḥ sahasrāṇyekawiṃśatiḥ ||19||

śatānyupari caiwāṣṭau tathā bhūyaśca saptatiḥ |
gajānāṃ tu parīmāṇametadewātra nirdiśet ||20||

jñeyaṃ śatasahasraṃ tu sahasrāṇi tathā nawa |
narāṇāmapi pañcāśacchatāni trīṇi cānaghāḥ ||21||

pañcaṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi tathāśwānāṃ śatāni ca |
daśottarāṇi ṣaṭprāhuryathāwadiha saṅkhyayā ||22||

etāmakṣauhiṇīṃ prāhuḥ saṅkhyātattwawido janāḥ |
yāṃ waḥ kathitawānasmi wistareṇa dwijottamāḥ ||23||

etayā saṅkhyayā hyāsankurupāṇḍawasenayoḥ |
akṣauhiṇyo dwijaśreṣṭhāḥ piṇḍenāṣṭādaśaiwa tāḥ ||24||

sametāstatra wai deśe tatraiwa nidhanaṃ gatāḥ |
kaurawānkāraṇaṃ kṛtwā kālenādbhutakarmaṇā ||25||

ahāni yuyudhe bhīṣmo daśaiwa paramāstrawit |
ahāni pañca droṇastu rarakṣa kuruwāhinīm ||26||

ahanī yuyudhe dwe tu karṇaḥ parabalārdanaḥ |
śalyo'rdhadiwasaṃ twāsīdgadāyuddhamataḥ param ||27||

tasyaiwa tu dinasyānte hārdikyadrauṇigautamāḥ |
prasuptaṃ niśi wiśwastaṃ jaghnuryaudhiṣṭhiraṃ balam ||28||

yattu śaunakasatre te bhāratākhyānawistaram |
ākhyāsye tatra paulomamākhyānaṃ cāditaḥ param ||29||

wicitrārthapadākhyānamanekasamayānwitam |
abhipannaṃ naraiḥ prājñairwairāgyamiwa mokṣibhiḥ ||30||

ātmewa weditawyeṣu priyeṣwiwa ca jīwitam |
itihāsaḥ pradhānārthaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarwāgameṣwayam ||31||

itihāsottame hyasminnarpitā buddhiruttamā |
swarawyañjanayoḥ kṛtsnā lokawedāśrayewa wāk ||32||

asya prajñābhipannasya wicitrapadaparwaṇaḥ |
bhāratasyetihāsasya śrūyatāṃ parwasaṅgrahaḥ ||33||

parwānukramaṇī pūrwaṃ dwitīyaṃ parwasaṅgrahaḥ |
pauṣyaṃ paulomamāstīkamādiwaṃśāwatāraṇam ||34||

tataḥ sambhawaparwoktamadbhutaṃ dewanirmitam |
dāho jatugṛhasyātra haiḍimbaṃ parwa cocyate ||35||

tato bakawadhaḥ parwa parwa caitrarathaṃ tataḥ |
tataḥ swayaṃwaraṃ dewyāḥ pāñcālyāḥ parwa cocyate ||36||

kṣatradharmeṇa nirjitya tato waiwāhikaṃ smṛtam |
widurāgamanaṃ parwa rājyalambhastathaiwa ca ||37||

arjunasya wane wāsaḥ subhadrāharaṇaṃ tataḥ |
subhadrāharaṇādūrdhwaṃ jñeyaṃ haraṇahārikam ||38||

tataḥ khāṇḍawadāhākhyaṃ tatraiwa mayadarśanam |
sabhāparwa tataḥ proktaṃ mantraparwa tataḥ param ||39||

jarāsandhawadhaḥ parwa parwa digwijayastathā |
parwa digwijayādūrdhwaṃ rājasūyikamucyate ||40||

tataścārghābhiharaṇaṃ śiśupālawadhastataḥ |
dyūtaparwa tataḥ proktamanudyūtamataḥ param ||41||

tata āraṇyakaṃ parwa kirmīrawadha ewa ca |
īśwarārjunayoryuddhaṃ parwa kairātasañjñitam ||42||

indralokābhigamanaṃ parwa jñeyamataḥ param |
tīrthayātrā tataḥ parwa kururājasya dhīmataḥ ||43||

jaṭāsurawadhaḥ parwa yakṣayuddhamataḥ param |
tathaiwājagaraṃ parwa wijñeyaṃ tadanantaram ||44||

mārkaṇḍeyasamasyā ca parwoktaṃ tadanantaram |
saṃwādaśca tataḥ parwa draupadīsatyabhāmayoḥ ||45||

ghoṣayātrā tataḥ parwa mṛgaswapnabhayaṃ tataḥ |
wrīhidrauṇikamākhyānaṃ tato'nantaramucyate ||46||

draupadīharaṇaṃ parwa saindhawena wanāttataḥ |
kuṇḍalāharaṇaṃ parwa tataḥ paramihocyate ||47||

āraṇeyaṃ tataḥ parwa wairāṭaṃ tadanantaram |
kīcakānāṃ wadhaḥ parwa parwa gograhaṇaṃ tataḥ ||48||

abhimanyunā ca wairāṭyāḥ parwa waiwāhikaṃ smṛtam |
udyogaparwa wijñeyamata ūrdhwaṃ mahādbhutam ||49||

tataḥ sañjayayānākhyaṃ parwa jñeyamataḥ param |
prajāgaraṃ tataḥ parwa dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cintayā ||50||

parwa sānatsujātaṃ ca guhyamadhyātmadarśanam |
yānasandhistataḥ parwa bhagawadyānamewa ca ||51||

jñeyaṃ wiwādaparwātra karṇasyāpi mahātmanaḥ |
niryāṇaṃ parwa ca tataḥ kurupāṇḍawasenayoḥ ||52||

rathātirathasaṅkhyā ca parwoktaṃ tadanantaram |
ulūkadūtāgamanaṃ parwāmarṣawiwardhanam ||53||

ambopākhyānamapi ca parwa jñeyamataḥ param |
bhīṣmābhiṣecanaṃ parwa jñeyamadbhutakāraṇam ||54||

jambūkhaṇḍawinirmāṇaṃ parwoktaṃ tadanantaram |
bhūmiparwa tato jñeyaṃ dwīpawistarakīrtanam ||55||

parwoktaṃ bhagawadgītā parwa bhīṣmawadhastataḥ |
droṇābhiṣekaḥ parwoktaṃ saṃśaptakawadhastataḥ ||56||

abhimanyuwadhaḥ parwa pratijñāparwa cocyate |
jayadrathawadhaḥ parwa ghaṭotkacawadhastataḥ ||57||

tato droṇawadhaḥ parwa wijñeyaṃ lomaharṣaṇam |
mokṣo nārāyaṇāstrasya parwānantaramucyate ||58||

karṇaparwa tato jñeyaṃ śalyaparwa tataḥ param |
hradapraweśanaṃ parwa gadāyuddhamataḥ param ||59||

sāraswataṃ tataḥ parwa tīrthawaṃśaguṇānwitam |
ata ūrdhwaṃ tu bībhatsaṃ parwa sauptikamucyate ||60||

aiṣīkaṃ parwa nirdiṣṭamata ūrdhwaṃ sudāruṇam |
jalapradānikaṃ parwa strīparwa ca tataḥ param ||61||

śrāddhaparwa tato jñeyaṃ kurūṇāmaurdhwadehikam |
ābhiṣecanikaṃ parwa dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ ||62||

cārwākanigrahaḥ parwa rakṣaso brahmarūpiṇaḥ |
prawibhāgo gṛhāṇāṃ ca parwoktaṃ tadanantaram ||63||

śāntiparwa tato yatra rājadharmānukīrtanam |
āpaddharmaśca parwoktaṃ mokṣadharmastataḥ param ||64||

tataḥ parwa parijñeyamānuśāsanikaṃ param |
swargārohaṇikaṃ parwa tato bhīṣmasya dhīmataḥ ||65||

tato'śwamedhikaṃ parwa sarwapāpapraṇāśanam |
anugītā tataḥ parwa jñeyamadhyātmawācakam ||66||

parwa cāśramawāsākhyaṃ putradarśanamewa ca |
nāradāgamanaṃ parwa tataḥ paramihocyate ||67||

mausalaṃ parwa ca tato ghoraṃ samanuwarṇyate |
mahāprasthānikaṃ parwa swargārohaṇikaṃ tataḥ ||68||

hariwaṃśastataḥ parwa purāṇaṃ khilasañjñitam |
bhawiṣyatparwa cāpyuktaṃ khileṣwewādbhutaṃ mahat ||69||

etatparwaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ wyāsenoktaṃ mahātmanā |
yathāwatsūtaputreṇa lomaharṣaṇinā punaḥ ||70||

kathitaṃ naimiṣāraṇye parwāṇyaṣṭādaśaiwa tu |
samāso bhāratasyāyaṃ tatroktaḥ parwasaṅgrahaḥ ||71||

pauṣye parwaṇi māhātmyamuttaṅkasyopawarṇitam |
paulome bhṛguwaṃśasya wistāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||72||

āstīke sarwanāgānāṃ garuḍasya ca sambhawaḥ |
kṣīrodamathanaṃ caiwa janmocchaiḥśrawasastathā ||73||

yajataḥ sarpasatreṇa rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya ca |
katheyamabhinirwṛttā bhāratānāṃ mahātmanām ||74||

wiwidhāḥ sambhawā rājñāmuktāḥ sambhawaparwaṇi |
anyeṣāṃ caiwa wiprāṇāmṛṣerdwaipāyanasya ca ||75||

aṃśāwataraṇaṃ cātra dewānāṃ parikīrtitam |
daityānāṃ dānawānāṃ ca yakṣāṇāṃ ca mahaujasām ||76||

nāgānāmatha sarpāṇāṃ gandharwāṇāṃ patatriṇām |
anyeṣāṃ caiwa bhūtānāṃ wiwidhānāṃ samudbhawaḥ ||77||

wasūnāṃ punarutpattirbhāgīrathyāṃ mahātmanām |
śantanorweśmani punasteṣāṃ cārohaṇaṃ diwi ||78||

tejoṃśānāṃ ca saṅghātādbhīṣmasyāpyatra sambhawaḥ |
rājyānniwartanaṃ caiwa brahmacaryawrate sthitiḥ ||79||

pratijñāpālanaṃ caiwa rakṣā citrāṅgadasya ca |
hate citrāṅgade caiwa rakṣā bhrāturyawīyasaḥ ||80||

wicitrawīryasya tathā rājye sampratipādanam |
dharmasya nṛṣu sambhūtiraṇīmāṇḍawyaśāpajā ||81||

kṛṣṇadwaipāyanāccaiwa prasūtirwaradānajā |
dhṛtarāṣṭrasya pāṇḍośca pāṇḍawānāṃ ca sambhawaḥ ||82||

wāraṇāwatayātrā ca mantro duryodhanasya ca |
widurasya ca wākyena suruṅgopakramakriyā ||83||

pāṇḍawānāṃ wane ghore hiḍimbāyāśca darśanam |
ghaṭotkacasya cotpattiratraiwa parikīrtitā ||84||

ajñātacaryā pāṇḍūnāṃ wāso brāhmaṇaweśmani |
bakasya nidhanaṃ caiwa nāgarāṇāṃ ca wismayaḥ ||85||

aṅgāraparṇaṃ nirjitya gaṅgākūle'rjunastadā |
bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarwaiḥ pāñcālānabhito yayau ||86||

tāpatyamatha wāsiṣṭhamaurwaṃ cākhyānamuttamam |
pañcendrāṇāmupākhyānamatraiwādbhutamucyate ||87||

pañcānāmekapatnītwe wimarśo drupadasya ca |
draupadyā dewawihito wiwāhaścāpyamānuṣaḥ ||88||

widurasya ca samprāptirdarśanaṃ keśawasya ca |
khāṇḍawaprasthawāsaśca tathā rājyārdhaśāsanam ||89||

nāradasyājñayā caiwa draupadyāḥ samayakriyā |
sundopasundayostatra upākhyānaṃ prakīrtitam ||90||

pārthasya wanawāsaśca ulūpyā pathi saṅgamaḥ |
puṇyatīrthānusaṃyānaṃ babhruwāhanajanma ca ||91||

dwārakāyāṃ subhadrā ca kāmayānena kāminī |
wāsudewasyānumate prāptā caiwa kirīṭinā ||92||

haraṇaṃ gṛhya samprāpte kṛṣṇe dewakinandane |
samprāptiścakradhanuṣoḥ khāṇḍawasya ca dāhanam ||93||

abhimanyoḥ subhadrāyāṃ janma cottamatejasaḥ |
mayasya mokṣo jwalanādbhujaṅgasya ca mokṣaṇam ||94||

maharṣermandapālasya śārṅgyaṃ tanayasambhawaḥ ||94||

ityetadādhiparwoktaṃ prathamaṃ bahuwistaram |
adhyāyānāṃ śate dwe tu saṅkhyāte paramarṣiṇā ||95||

aṣṭādaśaiwa cādhyāyā wyāsenottamatejasā ||95||

sapta ślokasahasrāṇi tathā nawa śatāni ca |
ślokāśca caturāśītirdṛṣṭo grantho mahātmanā ||96||

dwitīyaṃ tu sabhāparwa bahuwṛttāntamucyate |
sabhākriyā pāṇḍawānāṃ kiṅkarāṇāṃ ca darśanam ||97||

lokapālasabhākhyānaṃ nāradāddewadarśanāt |
rājasūyasya cārambho jarāsandhawadhastathā ||98||

giriwraje niruddhānāṃ rājñāṃ kṛṣṇena mokṣaṇam |
rājasūye'rghasaṃwāde śiśupālawadhastathā ||99||

yajñe wibhūtiṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭwā duḥkhāmarṣānwitasya ca |
duryodhanasyāwahāso bhīmena ca sabhātale ||100||

yatrāsya manyurudbhūto yena dyūtamakārayat |
yatra dharmasutaṃ dyūte śakuniḥ kitawo'jayat ||101||

yatra dyūtārṇawe magnāndraupadī nauriwārṇawāt |
tārayāmāsa tāṃstīrṇāñjñātwā duryodhano nṛpaḥ ||102||

punarewa tato dyūte samāhwayata pāṇḍawān ||102||

etatsarwaṃ sabhāparwa samākhyātaṃ mahātmanā |
adhyāyāḥ saptatirjñeyāstathā dwau cātra saṅkhyayā ||103||

ślokānāṃ dwe sahasre tu pañca ślokaśatāni ca |
ślokāścaikādaśa jñeyāḥ parwaṇyasminprakīrtitāḥ ||104||

ataḥ paraṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu jñeyamāraṇyakaṃ mahat |
paurānugamanaṃ caiwa dharmaputrasya dhīmataḥ ||105||

wṛṣṇīnāmāgamo yatra pāñcālānāṃ ca sarwaśaḥ |
yatra saubhawadhākhyānaṃ kirmīrawadha ewa ca ||106||

astrahetorwiwāsaśca pārthasyāmitatejasaḥ ||106||

mahādewena yuddhaṃ ca kirātawapuṣā saha |
darśanaṃ lokapālānāṃ swargārohaṇamewa ca ||107||

darśanaṃ bṛhadaśwasya maharṣerbhāwitātmanaḥ |
yudhiṣṭhirasya cārtasya wyasane paridewanam ||108||

nalopākhyānamatraiwa dharmiṣṭhaṃ karuṇodayam |
damayantyāḥ sthitiryatra nalasya wyasanāgame ||109||

wanawāsagatānāṃ ca pāṇḍawānāṃ mahātmanām |
swarge prawṛttirākhyātā lomaśenārjunasya wai ||110||

tīrthayātrā tathaiwātra pāṇḍawānāṃ mahātmanām |
jaṭāsurasya tatraiwa wadhaḥ samupawarṇyate ||111||

niyukto bhīmasenaśca draupadyā gandhamādane |
yatra mandārapuṣpārthaṃ nalinīṃ tāmadharṣayat ||112||

yatrāsya sumahadyuddhamabhawatsaha rākṣasaiḥ |
yakṣaiścāpi mahāwīryairmaṇimatpramukhaistathā ||113||

āgastyamapi cākhyānaṃ yatra wātāpibhakṣaṇam |
lopāmudrābhigamanamapatyārthamṛṣerapi ||114||

tataḥ śyenakapotīyamupākhyānamanantaram |
indro'gniryatra dharmaśca ajijñāsañśibiṃ nṛpam ||115||

ṛśyaśṛṅgasya caritaṃ kaumārabrahmacāriṇaḥ |
jāmadagnyasya rāmasya caritaṃ bhūritejasaḥ ||116||

kārtawīryawadho yatra haihayānāṃ ca warṇyate |
saukanyamapi cākhyānaṃ cyawano yatra bhārgawaḥ ||117||

śaryātiyajñe nāsatyau kṛtawānsomapīthinau |
tābhyāṃ ca yatra sa muniryauwanaṃ pratipāditaḥ ||118||

jantūpākhyānamatraiwa yatra putreṇa somakaḥ |
putrārthamayajadrājā lebhe putraśataṃ ca saḥ ||119||

aṣṭāwakrīyamatraiwa wiwāde yatra bandinam |
wijitya sāgaraṃ prāptaṃ pitaraṃ labdhawānṛṣiḥ ||120||

awāpya diwyānyastrāṇi gurwarthe sawyasācinā |
niwātakawacairyuddhaṃ hiraṇyapurawāsibhiḥ ||121||

samāgamaśca pārthasya bhrātṛbhirgandhamādane |
ghoṣayātrā ca gandharwairyatra yuddhaṃ kirīṭinaḥ ||122||

punarāgamanaṃ caiwa teṣāṃ dwaitawanaṃ saraḥ |
jayadrathenāpahāro draupadyāścāśramāntarāt ||123||

yatrainamanwayādbhīmo wāyuwegasamo jawe |
mārkaṇḍeyasamasyāyāmupākhyānāni bhāgaśaḥ ||124||

saṃdarśanaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya saṃwādaścaiwa satyayā |
wrīhidrauṇikamākhyānamaindradyumnaṃ tathaiwa ca ||125||

sāwitryauddālakīyaṃ ca wainyopākhyānamewa ca |
rāmāyaṇamupākhyānamatraiwa bahuwistaram ||126||

karṇasya parimoṣo'tra kuṇḍalābhyāṃ puraṃdarāt |
āraṇeyamupākhyānaṃ yatra dharmo'nwaśātsutam ||127||

jagmurlabdhawarā yatra pāṇḍawāḥ paścimāṃ diśam ||127||

etadāraṇyakaṃ parwa tṛtīyaṃ parikīrtitam |
atrādhyāyaśate dwe tu saṅkhyāte paramarṣiṇā ||128||

ekonasaptatiścaiwa tathādhyāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||128||

ekādaśa sahasrāṇi ślokānāṃ ṣaṭśatāni ca |
catuḥṣaṣṭistathā ślokāḥ parwaitatparikīrtitam ||129||

ataḥ paraṃ nibodhedaṃ wairāṭaṃ parwawistaram |
wirāṭanagaraṃ gatwā śmaśāne wipulāṃ śamīm ||130||

dṛṣṭwā saṃnidadhustatra pāṇḍawā āyudhānyuta ||130||

yatra prawiśya nagaraṃ chadmabhirnyawasanta te |
durātmano wadho yatra kīcakasya wṛkodarāt ||131||

gograhe yatra pārthena nirjitāḥ kurawo yudhi |
godhanaṃ ca wirāṭasya mokṣitaṃ yatra pāṇḍawaiḥ ||132||

wirāṭenottarā dattā snuṣā yatra kirīṭinaḥ |
abhimanyuṃ samuddiśya saubhadramarighātinam ||133||

caturthametadwipulaṃ wairāṭaṃ parwa warṇitam |
atrāpi parisaṅkhyātamadhyāyānāṃ mahātmanā ||134||

saptaṣaṣṭiratho pūrṇā ślokāgramapi me śṛṇu |
ślokānāṃ dwe sahasre tu ślokāḥ pañcāśadewa tu ||135||

parwaṇyasminsamākhyātāḥ saṅkhyayā paramarṣiṇā ||135||

udyogaparwa wijñeyaṃ pañcamaṃ śṛṇwataḥ param |
upaplawye niwiṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaweṣu jigīṣayā ||136||

duryodhano'rjunaścaiwa wāsudewamupasthitau ||136||

sāhāyyamasminsamare bhawānnau kartumarhati |
ityukte wacane kṛṣṇo yatrowāca mahāmatiḥ ||137||

ayudhyamānamātmānaṃ mantriṇaṃ puruṣarṣabhau |
akṣauhiṇīṃ wā sainyasya kasya wā kiṃ dadāmyaham ||138||

wawre duryodhanaḥ sainyaṃ mandātmā yatra durmatiḥ |
ayudhyamānaṃ saciwaṃ wawre kṛṣṇaṃ dhanañjayaḥ ||139||

sañjayaṃ preṣayāmāsa śamārthaṃ pāṇḍawānprati |
yatra dūtaṃ mahārājo dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ pratāpawān ||140||

śrutwā ca pāṇḍawānyatra wāsudewapurogamān |
prajāgaraḥ samprajajñe dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cintayā ||141||

widuro yatra wākyāni wicitrāṇi hitāni ca |
śrāwayāmāsa rājānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ manīṣiṇam ||142||

tathā sanatsujātena yatrādhyātmamanuttamam |
manastāpānwito rājā śrāwitaḥ śokalālasaḥ ||143||

prabhāte rājasamitau sañjayo yatra cābhibhoḥ |
aikātmyaṃ wāsudewasya proktawānarjunasya ca ||144||

yatra kṛṣṇo dayāpannaḥ sandhimicchanmahāyaśāḥ |
swayamāgācchamaṃ kartuṃ nagaraṃ nāgasāhwayam ||145||

pratyākhyānaṃ ca kṛṣṇasya rājñā duryodhanena wai |
śamārthaṃ yācamānasya pakṣayorubhayorhitam ||146||

karṇaduryodhanādīnāṃ duṣṭaṃ wijñāya mantritam |
yogeśwaratwaṃ kṛṣṇena yatra rājasu darśitam ||147||

rathamāropya kṛṣṇena yatra karṇo'numantritaḥ |
upāyapūrwaṃ śauṇḍīryātpratyākhyātaśca tena saḥ ||148||

tataścāpyabhiniryātrā rathāśwanaradantinām |
nagarāddhāstinapurādbalasaṅkhyānamewa ca ||149||

yatra rājñā ulūkasya preṣaṇaṃ pāṇḍawānprati |
śwobhāwini mahāyuddhe dūtyena krūrawādinā ||150||

rathātirathasaṅkhyānamambopākhyānamewa ca ||150||

etatsubahuwṛttāntaṃ pañcamaṃ parwa bhārate |
udyogaparwa nirdiṣṭaṃ sandhiwigrahasaṃśritam ||151||

adhyāyāḥ saṅkhyayā twatra ṣaḍaśītiśataṃ smṛtam |
ślokānāṃ ṣaṭsahasrāṇi tāwantyewa śatāni ca ||152||

ślokāśca nawatiḥ proktāstathaiwāṣṭau mahātmanā |
wyāsenodāramatinā parwaṇyasmiṃstapodhanāḥ ||153||

ata ūrdhwaṃ wicitrārthaṃ bhīṣmaparwa pracakṣate |
jambūkhaṇḍawinirmāṇaṃ yatroktaṃ sañjayena ha ||154||

yatra yuddhamabhūdghoraṃ daśāhānyatidāruṇam |
yatra yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ sainyaṃ wiṣādamagamatparam ||155||

kaśmalaṃ yatra pārthasya wāsudewo mahāmatiḥ |
mohajaṃ nāśayāmāsa hetubhirmokṣadarśanaiḥ ||156||

śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya yatra pārtho mahādhanuḥ |
winighnanniśitairbāṇai rathādbhīṣmamapātayat ||157||

ṣaṣṭhametanmahāparwa bhārate parikīrtitam |
adhyāyānāṃ śataṃ proktaṃ saptadaśa tathāpare ||158||

pañca ślokasahasrāṇi saṅkhyayāṣṭau śatāni ca |
ślokāśca caturāśītiḥ parwaṇyasminprakīrtitāḥ ||159||

wyāsena wedawiduṣā saṅkhyātā bhīṣmaparwaṇi ||159||

droṇaparwa tataścitraṃ bahuwṛttāntamucyate |
yatra saṃśaptakāḥ pārthamapaninyū raṇājirāt ||160||

bhagadatto mahārājo yatra śakrasamo yudhi |
supratīkena nāgena saha śastaḥ kirīṭinā ||161||

yatrābhimanyuṃ bahawo jaghnurlokamahārathāḥ |
jayadrathamukhā bālaṃ śūramaprāptayauwanam ||162||

hate'bhimanyau kruddhena yatra pārthena saṃyuge |
akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta hatwā hato rājā jayadrathaḥ ||163||

saṃśaptakāwaśeṣaṃ ca kṛtaṃ niḥśeṣamāhawe ||163||

alambusaḥ śrutāyuśca jalasandhaśca wīryawān |
saumadattirwirāṭaśca drupadaśca mahārathaḥ ||164||

ghaṭotkacādayaścānye nihatā droṇaparwaṇi ||164||

aśwatthāmāpi cātraiwa droṇe yudhi nipātite |
astraṃ prāduścakārograṃ nārāyaṇamamarṣitaḥ ||165||

saptamaṃ bhārate parwa mahadetadudāhṛtam |
atra te pṛthiwīpālāḥ prāyaśo nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ||166||

droṇaparwaṇi ye śūrā nirdiṣṭāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ ||166||

adhyāyānāṃ śataṃ proktamadhyāyāḥ saptatistathā |
aṣṭau ślokasahasrāṇi tathā nawa śatāni ca ||167||

ślokā nawa tathaiwātra saṅkhyātāstattwadarśinā |
pārāśaryeṇa muninā sañcintya droṇaparwaṇi ||168||

ataḥ paraṃ karṇaparwa procyate paramādbhutam |
sārathye winiyogaśca madrarājasya dhīmataḥ ||169||

ākhyātaṃ yatra paurāṇaṃ tripurasya nipātanam ||169||

prayāṇe paruṣaścātra saṃwādaḥ karṇaśalyayoḥ |
haṃsakākīyamākhyānamatraiwākṣepasaṃhitam ||170||

anyonyaṃ prati ca krodho yudhiṣṭhirakirīṭinoḥ |
dwairathe yatra pārthena hataḥ karṇo mahārathaḥ ||171||

aṣṭamaṃ parwa nirdiṣṭametadbhāratacintakaiḥ |
ekonasaptatiḥ proktā adhyāyāḥ karṇaparwaṇi ||172||

catwāryewa sahasrāṇi nawa ślokaśatāni ca ||172||

ataḥ paraṃ wicitrārthaṃ śalyaparwa prakīrtitam |
hataprawīre sainye tu netā madreśwaro'bhawat ||173||

wṛttāni rathayuddhāni kīrtyante yatra bhāgaśaḥ |
wināśaḥ kurumukhyānāṃ śalyaparwaṇi kīrtyate ||174||

śalyasya nidhanaṃ cātra dharmarājānmahārathāt |
gadāyuddhaṃ tu tumulamatraiwa parikīrtitam ||175||

saraswatyāśca tīrthānāṃ puṇyatā parikīrtitā ||175||

nawamaṃ parwa nirdiṣṭametadadbhutamarthawat |
ekonaṣaṣṭiradhyāyāstatra saṅkhyāwiśāradaiḥ ||176||

saṅkhyātā bahuwṛttāntāḥ ślokāgraṃ cātra śasyate |
trīṇi ślokasahasrāṇi dwe śate wiṃśatistathā ||177||

muninā sampraṇītāni kaurawāṇāṃ yaśobhṛtām ||177||

ataḥ paraṃ prawakṣyāmi sauptikaṃ parwa dāruṇam |
bhagnoruṃ yatra rājānaṃ duryodhanamamarṣaṇam ||178||

wyapayāteṣu pārtheṣu trayaste'bhyāyayū rathāḥ |
kṛtawarmā kṛpo drauṇiḥ sāyāhne rudhirokṣitāḥ ||179||

pratijajñe dṛḍhakrodho drauṇiryatra mahārathaḥ |
ahatwā sarwapāñcālāndhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamān ||180||

pāṇḍawāṃśca sahāmātyānna wimokṣyāmi daṃśanam ||180||

prasuptānniśi wiśwastānyatra te puruṣarṣabhāḥ |
pāñcālānsaparīwārāñjaghnurdrauṇipurogamāḥ ||181||

yatrāmucyanta pārthāste pañca kṛṣṇabalāśrayāt |
sātyakiśca maheṣwāsaḥ śeṣāśca nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ||182||

draupadī putraśokārtā pitṛbhrātṛwadhārditā |
kṛtānaśanasaṅkalpā yatra bhartṛnupāwiśat ||183||

draupadīwacanādyatra bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ |
anwadhāwata saṅkruddho bhāradwājaṃ guroḥ sutam ||184||

bhīmasenabhayādyatra daiwenābhipracoditaḥ |
apāṇḍawāyeti ruṣā drauṇirastramawāsṛjat ||185||

maiwamityabrawītkṛṣṇaḥ śamayaṃstasya tadwacaḥ |
yatrāstramastreṇa ca tacchamayāmāsa phālgunaḥ ||186||

drauṇidwaipāyanādīnāṃ śāpāścānyonyakāritāḥ |
toyakarmaṇi sarweṣāṃ rājñāmudakadānike ||187||

gūḍhotpannasya cākhyānaṃ karṇasya pṛthayātmanaḥ |
sutasyaitadiha proktaṃ daśamaṃ parwa sauptikam ||188||

aṣṭādaśāsminnadhyāyāḥ parwaṇyuktā mahātmanā |
ślokāgramatra kathitaṃ śatānyaṣṭau tathaiwa ca ||189||

ślokāśca saptatiḥ proktā yathāwadabhisaṅkhyayā |
sauptikaiṣīkasambandhe parwaṇyamitabuddhinā ||190||

ata ūrdhwamidaṃ prāhuḥ strīparwa karuṇodayam |
wilāpo wīrapatnīnāṃ yatrātikaruṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||191||

krodhāweśaḥ prasādaśca gāndhārīdhṛtarāṣṭrayoḥ ||191||

yatra tānkṣatriyāñśūrāndiṣṭāntānaniwartinaḥ |
putrānbhrātṛnpitṛṃścaiwa dadṛśurnihatānraṇe ||192||

yatra rājā mahāprājñaḥ sarwadharmabhṛtāṃ waraḥ |
rājñāṃ tāni śarīrāṇi dāhayāmāsa śāstrataḥ ||193||

etadekādaśaṃ proktaṃ parwātikaruṇaṃ mahat |
saptawiṃśatiradhyāyāḥ parwaṇyasminnudāhṛtāḥ ||194||

ślokāḥ saptaśataṃ cātra pañcasaptatirucyate |
saṅkhyayā bhāratākhyānaṃ kartrā hyatra mahātmanā ||195||

praṇītaṃ sajjanamanowaiklawyāśruprawartakam ||195||

ataḥ paraṃ śāntiparwa dwādaśaṃ buddhiwardhanam |
yatra nirwedamāpanno dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||196||

ghātayitwā pitṛnbhrātṛnputrānsambandhibāndhawān ||196||

śāntiparwaṇi dharmāśca wyākhyātāḥ śaratalpikāḥ |
rājabhirweditawyā ye samyaṅnayabubhutsubhiḥ ||197||

āpaddharmāśca tatraiwa kālahetupradarśakāḥ |
yānbuddhwā puruṣaḥ samyaksarwajñatwamawāpnuyāt ||198||

mokṣadharmāśca kathitā wicitrā bahuwistarāḥ ||198||

dwādaśaṃ parwa nirdiṣṭametatprājñajanapriyam |
parwaṇyatra parijñeyamadhyāyānāṃ śatatrayam ||199||

triṃśaccaiwa tathādhyāyā nawa caiwa tapodhanāḥ ||199||

ślokānāṃ tu sahasrāṇi kīrtitāni caturdaśa |
pañca caiwa śatānyāhuḥ pañcawiṃśatisaṅkhyayā ||200||

ata ūrdhwaṃ tu wijñeyamānuśāsanamuttamam |
yatra prakṛtimāpannaḥ śrutwā dharmawiniścayam ||201||

bhīṣmādbhāgīrathīputrātkururājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||201||

wyawahāro'tra kārtsnyena dharmārthīyo nidarśitaḥ |
wiwidhānāṃ ca dānānāṃ phalayogāḥ pṛthagwidhāḥ ||202||

tathā pātrawiśeṣāśca dānānāṃ ca paro widhiḥ |
ācārawidhiyogaśca satyasya ca parā gatiḥ ||203||

etatsubahuwṛttāntamuttamaṃ cānuśāsanam |
bhīṣmasyātraiwa samprāptiḥ swargasya parikīrtitā ||204||

etattrayodaśaṃ parwa dharmaniścayakārakam |
adhyāyānāṃ śataṃ cātra ṣaṭcatwāriṃśadewa ca ||205||

ślokānāṃ tu sahasrāṇi ṣaṭsaptaiwa śatāni ca ||205||

tato'śwamedhikaṃ nāma parwa proktaṃ caturdaśam |
tatsaṃwartamaruttīyaṃ yatrākhyānamanuttamam ||206||

suwarṇakośasamprāptirjanma coktaṃ parikṣitaḥ |
dagdhasyāstrāgninā pūrwaṃ kṛṣṇātsañjīwanaṃ punaḥ ||207||

caryāyāṃ hayamutsṛṣṭaṃ pāṇḍawasyānugacchataḥ |
tatra tatra ca yuddhāni rājaputrairamarṣaṇaiḥ ||208||

citrāṅgadāyāḥ putreṇa putrikāyā dhanañjayaḥ |
saṅgrāme babhruwāhena saṃśayaṃ cātra darśitaḥ ||209||

aśwamedhe mahāyajñe nakulākhyānamewa ca ||209||

ityāśwamedhikaṃ parwa proktametanmahādbhutam |
atrādhyāyaśataṃ triṃśattrayo'dhyāyāśca śabditāḥ ||210||

trīṇi ślokasahasrāṇi tāwantyewa śatāni ca |
wiṃśatiśca tathā ślokāḥ saṅkhyātāstattwadarśinā ||211||

tata āśramawāsākyaṃ parwa pañcadaśaṃ smṛtam |
yatra rājyaṃ parityajya gāndhārīsahito nṛpaḥ ||212||

dhṛtarāṣṭrāśramapadaṃ widuraśca jagāma ha ||212||

yaṃ dṛṣṭwā prasthitaṃ sādhwī pṛthāpyanuyayau tadā |
putrarājyaṃ parityajya guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratā ||213||

yatra rājā hatānputrānpautrānanyāṃśca pārthiwān |
lokāntaragatānwīrānapaśyatpunarāgatān ||214||

ṛṣeḥ prasādātkṛṣṇasya dṛṣṭwāścaryamanuttamam |
tyaktwā śokaṃ sadāraśca siddhiṃ paramikāṃ gataḥ ||215||

yatra dharmaṃ samāśritya widuraḥ sugatiṃ gataḥ |
sañjayaśca mahāmātro widwāngāwalgaṇirwaśī ||216||

dadarśa nāradaṃ yatra dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
nāradāccaiwa śuśrāwa wṛṣṇīnāṃ kadanaṃ mahat ||217||

etadāśramawāsākhyaṃ pūrwoktaṃ sumahādbhutam |
dwicatwāriṃśadadhyāyāḥ parwaitadabhisaṅkhyayā ||218||

sahasramekaṃ ślokānāṃ pañca ślokaśatāni ca |
ṣaḍewa ca tathā ślokāḥ saṅkhyātāstattwadarśinā ||219||

ataḥ paraṃ nibodhedaṃ mausalaṃ parwa dāruṇam |
yatra te puruṣawyāghrāḥ śastrasparśasahā yudhi ||220||

brahmadaṇḍawiniṣpiṣṭāḥ samīpe lawaṇāmbhasaḥ ||220||

āpāne pānagalitā daiwenābhipracoditāḥ |
erakārūpibhirwajrairnijaghnuritaretaram ||221||

yatra sarwakṣayaṃ kṛtwā tāwubhau rāmakeśawau |
nāticakramatuḥ kālaṃ prāptaṃ sarwaharaṃ samam ||222||

yatrārjuno dwārawatīmetya wṛṣṇiwinākṛtām |
dṛṣṭwā wiṣādamagamatparāṃ cārtiṃ nararṣabhaḥ ||223||

sa satkṛtya yaduśreṣṭhaṃ mātulaṃ śaurimātmanaḥ |
dadarśa yaduwīrāṇāmāpāne waiśasaṃ mahat ||224||

śarīraṃ wāsudewasya rāmasya ca mahātmanaḥ |
saṃskāraṃ lambhayāmāsa wṛṣṇīnāṃ ca pradhānataḥ ||225||

sa wṛddhabālamādāya dwārawatyāstato janam |
dadarśāpadi kaṣṭāyāṃ gāṇḍīwasya parābhawam ||226||

sarweṣāṃ caiwa diwyānāmastrāṇāmaprasannatām |
nāśaṃ wṛṣṇikalatrāṇāṃ prabhāwānāmanityatām ||227||

dṛṣṭwā nirwedamāpanno wyāsawākyapracoditaḥ |
dharmarājaṃ samāsādya saṃnyāsaṃ samarocayet ||228||

ityetanmausalaṃ parwa ṣoḍaśaṃ parikīrtitam |
adhyāyāṣṭau samākhyātāḥ ślokānāṃ ca śatatrayam ||229||

mahāprasthānikaṃ tasmādūrdhwaṃ saptadaśaṃ smṛtam |
yatra rājyaṃ parityajya pāṇḍawāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ ||230||

draupadyā sahitā dewyā siddhiṃ paramikāṃ gatāḥ ||230||

atrādhyāyāstrayaḥ proktāḥ ślokānāṃ ca śataṃ tathā |
wiṃśatiśca tathā ślokāḥ saṅkhyātāstattwadarśinā ||231||

swargaparwa tato jñeyaṃ diwyaṃ yattadamānuṣam |
adhyāyāḥ pañca saṅkhyātāḥ parwaitadabhisaṅkhyayā ||232||

ślokānāṃ dwe śate caiwa prasaṅkhyāte tapodhanāḥ ||232||

aṣṭādaśaiwametāni parwāṇyuktānyaśeṣataḥ |
khileṣu hariwaṃśaśca bhawiṣyacca prakīrtitam ||233||

etadakhilamākhyātaṃ bhārataṃ parwasaṅgrahāt |
aṣṭādaśa samājagmurakṣauhiṇyo yuyutsayā ||234||

tanmahaddāruṇaṃ yuddhamahānyaṣṭādaśābhawat ||234||

yo widyāccaturo wedānsāṅgopaniṣadāndwijaḥ |
na cākhyānamidaṃ widyānnaiwa sa syādwicakṣaṇaḥ ||235||

śrutwā twidamupākhyānaṃ śrāwyamanyanna rocate |
puṃskokilarutaṃ śrutwā rūkṣā dhwāṅkṣasya wāgiwa ||236||

itihāsottamādasmājjāyante kawibuddhayaḥ |
pañcabhya iwa bhūtebhyo lokasaṃwidhayastrayaḥ ||237||

asyākhyānasya wiṣaye purāṇaṃ wartate dwijāḥ |
antarikṣasya wiṣaye prajā iwa caturwidhāḥ ||238||

kriyāguṇānāṃ sarweṣāmidamākhyānamāśrayaḥ |
indriyāṇāṃ samastānāṃ citrā iwa manaḥkriyāḥ ||239||

anāśrityaitadākhyānaṃ kathā bhuwi na widyate |
āhāramanapāśritya śarīrasyewa dhāraṇam ||240||

idaṃ sarwaiḥ kawiwarairākhyānamupajīwyate |
udayaprepsubhirbhṛtyairabhijāta iweśwaraḥ ||241||

dwaipāyanauṣṭhapuṭaniḥsṛtamaprameyaṃ; puṇyaṃ pawitramatha pāpaharaṃ śiwaṃ ca |
yo bhārataṃ samadhigacchati wācyamānaṃ; kiṃ tasya puṣkarajalairabhiṣecanena ||242||

ākhyānaṃ tadidamanuttamaṃ mahārthaṃ; winyastaṃ mahadiha parwasaṅgraheṇa |
śrutwādau bhawati nṛṇāṃ sukhāwagāhaṃ; wistīrṇaṃ lawaṇajalaṃ yathā plawena ||243||






              pauṣyaparwa
                  3


sūta uwāca||

\bg

janamejayaḥ pārikṣitaḥ saha bhrātṛbhiḥ kurukṣetre dīrghasatramupāste |
tasya bhrātarastrayaḥ śrutasena ugraseno bhīmasena iti | 001 |
teṣu tatsatramupāsīneṣu tatra śwābhyāgacchatsārameyaḥ |
sa janamejayasya bhrātṛbhirabhihato rorūyamāṇo mātuḥ samīpamupāgacchat | 002 |
taṃ mātā rorūyamāṇamuwāca |
kiṃ rodiṣi |
kenāsyabhihata iti | 003 |
sa ewamukto mātaraṃ pratyuwāca |
janamejayasya bhrātṛbhirabhihato'smīti | 004 |
taṃ mātā pratyuwāca |
wyaktaṃ twayā tatrāparāddhaṃ yenāsyabhihata iti | 005 |
sa tāṃ punaruwāca |
nāparādhyāmi kiñcit |
nāwekṣe hawīṃṣi nāwaliha iti | 006 |
tacchrutwā tasya mātā saramā putraśokārtā tatsatramupāgacchadyatra sa janamejayaḥ saha bhrātṛbhirdīrghasatramupāste | 007 |
sa tayā kruddhayā tatroktaḥ |
ayaṃ me putro na kiñcidaparādhyati |
kimarthamabhihata iti |
yasmāccāyamabhihato'napakārī tasmādadṛṣṭaṃ twāṃ bhayamāgamiṣyatīti | 008 |
sa janamejaya ewamukto dewaśunyā saramayā dṛḍhaṃ sambhrānto wiṣaṇṇaścāsīt | 009 |
sa tasminsatre samāpte hāstinapuraṃ pratyetya purohitamanurūpamanwicchamānaḥ paraṃ yatnamakarodyo me pāpakṛtyāṃ śamayediti | 010 |
sa kadācinmṛgayāṃ yātaḥ pārikṣito janamejayaḥ kasmiṃścitswawiṣayoddeśe āśramamapaśyat | 011 |
tatra kaścidṛṣirāsāṃ cakre śrutaśrawā nāma |
tasyābhimataḥ putra āste somaśrawā nāma | 012 |
tasya taṃ putramabhigamya janamejayaḥ pārikṣitaḥ paurohityāya wawre | 013 |
sa namaskṛtya tamṛṣimuwāca |
bhagawannayaṃ tawa putro mama purohito'stwiti | 014 |
sa ewamuktaḥ pratyuwāca |
bho janamejaya putro'yaṃ mama sarpyāṃ jātaḥ |
mahātapaswī swādhyāyasampanno mattapowīryasambhṛto macchukraṃ pītawatyāstasyāḥ kukṣau saṃwṛddhaḥ |
samartho'yaṃ bhawataḥ sarwāḥ pāpakṛtyāḥ śamayitumantareṇa mahādewakṛtyām |
asya twekamupāṃśuwratam |
yadenaṃ kaścidbrāhmaṇaḥ kañcidarthamabhiyācettaṃ tasmai dadyādayam |
yadyetadutsahase tato nayaswainamiti | 015 |
tenaiwamutko janamejayastaṃ pratyuwāca |
bhagawaṃstathā bhawiṣyatīti | 016 |
sa taṃ purohitamupādāyopāwṛtto bhrātṛnuwāca |
mayāyaṃ wṛta upādhyāyaḥ |
yadayaṃ brūyāttatkāryamawicārayadbhiriti | 017 |
tenaiwamuktā bhrātarastasya tathā cakruḥ |
sa tathā bhrātṛnsaṃdiśya takṣaśilāṃ pratyabhipratasthe |
taṃ ca deśaṃ waśe sthāpayāmāsa | 018 |
etasminnantare kaścidṛṣirdhaumyo nāmāyodaḥ |
tasya śiṣyāstrayo babhūwurupamanyurāruṇirwedaśceti | 019 |
sa ekaṃ śiṣyamāruṇiṃ pāñcālyaṃ preṣayāmāsa |
gaccha kedārakhaṇḍaṃ badhāneti | 020 |
sa upādhyāyena saṃdiṣṭa āruṇiḥ pāñcālyastatra gatwā tatkedārakhaṇḍaṃ baddhuṃ nāśaknot | 021 |
sa kliśyamāno'paśyadupāyam |
bhawatwewaṃ kariṣyāmīti | 022 |
sa tatra saṃwiweśa kedārakhaṇḍe |
śayāne tasmiṃstadudakaṃ tasthau | 023 |
tataḥ kadācidupādhyāya āyodo dhaumyaḥ śiṣyānapṛcchat |
kwa āruṇiḥ pāñcālyo gata iti | 024 |
te pratyūcuḥ |
bhagawataiwa preṣito gaccha kedārakhaṇḍaṃ badhāneti | 025 |
sa ewamuktastāñśiṣyānpratyuwāca |
tasmātsarwe tatra gacchāmo yatra sa iti | 026 |
sa tatra gatwā tasyāhwānāya śabdaṃ cakāra |
bho āruṇe pāñcālya kwāsi |
watsaihīti | 027 |
sa tacchrutwā āruṇirupādhyāyawākyaṃ tasmātkedārakhaṇḍātsahasotthāya tamupādhyāyamupatasthe |
prowāca cainam |
ayamasmyatra kedārakhaṇḍe niḥsaramāṇamudakamawāraṇīyaṃ saṃroddhuṃ saṃwiṣṭo bhagawacchabdaṃ śrutwaiwa sahasā widārya kedārakhaṇḍaṃ bhawantamupasthitaḥ |
tadabhiwādaye bhagawantam |
ājñāpayatu bhawān |
kiṃ karawāṇīti | 028 |
tamupādhyāyo'brawīt |
yasmādbhawānkedārakhaṇḍamawadāryotthitastasmādbhawānuddālaka ewa nāmnā bhawiṣyatīti | 029 |
sa upādhyāyenānugṛhītaḥ |
yasmāttwayā madwaco'nuṣṭhitaṃ tasmācchreyo'wāpsyasīti |
sarwe ca te wedāḥ pratibhāsyanti sarwāṇi ca dharmaśāstrāṇīti | 030 |
sa ewamukta upādhyāyeneṣṭaṃ deśaṃ jagāma | 031 |
athāparaḥ śiṣyastasyaiwāyodasya dhaumyasyopamanyurnāma | 032 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ preṣayāmāsa |
watsopamanyo gā rakṣasweti | 033 |
sa upādhyāyawacanādarakṣadgāḥ |
sa cāhani gā rakṣitwā diwasakṣaye'bhyāgamyopādhyāyasyāgrataḥ sthitwā namaścakre | 034 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pīwānamapaśyat |
uwāca cainam |
watsopamanyo kena wṛttiṃ kalpayasi |
pīwānasi dṛḍhamiti | 035 |
sa upādhyāyaṃ pratyuwāca |
bhaikṣeṇa wṛttiṃ kalpayāmīti | 036 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
mamāniwedya bhaikṣaṃ nopayoktawyamiti | 037 |
sa tathetyuktwā punararakṣadgāḥ |
rakṣitwā cāgamya tathaiwopādhyāyasyāgrataḥ sthitwā namaścakre | 038 |
tamupādhyāyastathāpi pīwānamewa dṛṣṭwowāca |
watsopamanyo sarwamaśeṣataste bhaikṣaṃ gṛhṇāmi |
kenedānīṃ wṛttiṃ kalpayasīti | 039 |
sa ewamukta upādhyāyena pratyuwāca |
bhagawate niwedya pūrwamaparaṃ carāmi |
tena wṛttiṃ kalpayāmīti | 040 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
naiṣā nyāyyā guruwṛttiḥ |
anyeṣāmapi wṛttyuparodhaṃ karoṣyewaṃ wartamānaḥ |
lubdho'sīti | 041 |
sa tathetyuktwā gā arakṣat |
rakṣitwā ca punarupādhyāyagṛhamāgamyopādhyāyasyāgrataḥ sthitwā namaścakre | 042 |
tamupādhyāyastathāpi pīwānamewa dṛṣṭwā punaruwāca |
ahaṃ te sarwaṃ bhaikṣaṃ gṛhṇāmi na cānyaccarasi |
pīwānasi |
kena wṛttiṃ kalpayasīti | 043 |
sa upādhyāyaṃ pratyuwāca |
bho etāsāṃ gawāṃ payasā wṛttiṃ kalpayāmīti | 044 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
naitannyāyyaṃ paya upayoktuṃ bhawato mayānanujñātamiti | 045 |
sa tatheti pratijñāya gā rakṣitwā punarupādhyāyagṛhānetya guroragrataḥ sthitwā namaścakre | 046 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pīwānamewāpaśyat |
uwāca cainam |
bhaikṣaṃ nāśnāsi na cānyaccarasi |
payo na pibasi |
pīwānasi |
kena wṛttiṃ kalpayasīti | 047 |
sa ewamukta upādhyāyaṃ pratyuwāca |
bhoḥ phenaṃ pibāmi yamime watsā mātṛṇāṃ stanaṃ pibanta udgirantīti | 048 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
ete twadanukampayā guṇawanto watsāḥ prabhūtataraṃ phenamudgiranti |
tadewamapi watsānāṃ wṛttyuparodhaṃ karoṣyewaṃ wartamānaḥ |
phenamapi bhawānna pātumarhatīti | 049 |
sa tatheti pratijñāya nirāhārastā gā arakṣat |
tathā pratiṣiddho bhaikṣaṃ nāśnāti na cānyaccarati |
payo na pibati |
phenaṃ nopayuṅkte | 050 |
sa kadācidaraṇye kṣudhārto'rkapatrāṇyabhakṣayat | 051 |
sa tairarkapatrairbhakṣitaiḥ kṣārakaṭūṣṇawipākibhiścakṣuṣyupahato'ndho'bhawat |
so'ndho'pi caṅkramyamāṇaḥ kūpe'patat | 052 |
atha tasminnanāgacchatyupādhyāyaḥ śiṣyānawocat |
mayopamanyuḥ sarwataḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ |
sa niyataṃ kupitaḥ |
tato nāgacchati ciragataśceti | 053 |
sa ewamuktwā gatwāraṇyamupamanyorāhwānaṃ cakre |
bho upamanyo kwāsi |
watsaihīti | 054 |
sa tadāhwānamupādhyāyācchrutwā pratyuwācoccaiḥ |
ayamasmi bho upādhyāya kūpe patita iti | 055 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
kathamasi kūpe patita iti | 056 |
sa taṃ pratyuwāca |
arkapatrāṇi bhakṣayitwāndhībhūto'smi |
ataḥ kūpe patita iti | 057 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
aświnau stuhi |
tau twāṃ cakṣuṣmantaṃ kariṣyato dewabhiṣajāwiti | 058 |
sa ewamukta upādhyāyena stotuṃ pracakrame dewāwaświnau wāgbhirṛgbhiḥ | 059 |
\eg


pra pūrwagau pūrwajau citrabhānū; girā wā śaṃsāmi tapanāwanantau |
diwyau suparṇau wirajau wimānā; wadhikṣiyantau bhuwanāni wiśwā ||60||

hiraṇmayau śakunī sāmparāyau; nāsatyadasrau sunasau waijayantau |
śukraṃ wayantau tarasā suwemā; wabhi wyayantāwasitaṃ wiwaswat ||61||

grastāṃ suparṇasya balena wartikā; mamuñcatāmaświnau saubhagāya |
tāwatsuwṛttāwanamanta māyayā; sattamā gā aruṇā udāwahan ||62||

ṣaṣṭiśca gāwastriśatāśca dhenawa; ekaṃ watsaṃ suwate taṃ duhanti |
nānāgoṣṭhā wihitā ekadohanā; stāwaświnau duhato gharmamukthyam ||63||

ekāṃ nābhiṃ saptaśatā arāḥ śritāḥ; pradhiṣwanyā wiṃśatirarpitā arāḥ |
anemi cakraṃ pariwartate'jaraṃ; māyāświnau samanakti carṣaṇī ||64||

ekaṃ cakraṃ wartate dwādaśāraṃ pradhi; ṣaṇṇābhimekākṣamamṛtasya dhāraṇam |
yasmindewā adhi wiśwe wiṣaktā; stāwaświnau muñcato mā wiṣīdatam ||65||

aśwināwindramamṛtaṃ wṛttabhūyau; tirodhattāmaświnau dāsapatnī |
bhittwā girimaświnau gāmudācarantau; tadwṛṣṭamahnā prathitā walasya ||66||

yuwāṃ diśo janayatho daśāgre; samānaṃ mūrdhni rathayā wiyanti |
tāsāṃ yātamṛṣayo'nuprayānti; dewā manuṣyāḥ kṣitimācaranti ||67||

yuwāṃ warṇānwikurutho wiśwarūpāṃ; ste'dhikṣiyanti bhuwanāni wiśwā |
te bhānawo'pyanusṛtāścaranti; dewā manuṣyāḥ kṣitimācaranti ||68||

tau nāsatyāwaśwināwāmahe wāṃ; srajaṃ ca yāṃ bibhṛthaḥ puṣkarasya |
tau nāsatyāwamṛtāwṛtāwṛdhā; wṛte dewāstatprapadena sūte ||69||

mukhena garbhaṃ labhatāṃ yuwānau; gatāsuretatprapadena sūte |
sadyo jāto mātaramatti garbha; stāwaświnau muñcatho jīwase gāḥ ||70||

ewaṃ tenābhiṣṭutāwaśwināwājagmatuḥ |
āhatuścainam |
prītau swaḥ |
eṣa te'pūpaḥ |
aśānainamiti | 071 |
sa ewamuktaḥ pratyuwāca |
nānṛtamūcaturbhawantau |
na twahametamapūpamupayoktumutsahe aniwedya gurawa iti | 072 |
tatastamaśwināwūcatuḥ |
āwābhyāṃ purastādbhawata upādhyāyenaiwamewābhiṣṭutābhyāmapūpaḥ prītābhyāṃ dattaḥ |
upayuktaśca sa tenāniwedya gurawe |
twamapi tathaiwa kuruṣwa yathā kṛtamupādhyāyeneti | 073 |
sa ewamuktaḥ punarewa pratyuwācaitau |
pratyanunaye bhawantāwaświnau |
notsahe'hamaniwedyopādhyāyāyopayoktumiti | 074 |
tamaśwināwāhatuḥ |
prītau swastawānayā guruwṛttyā |
upādhyāyasya te kārṣṇāyasā dantāḥ |
bhawato hiraṇmayā bhawiṣyanti |
cakṣuṣmāṃśca bhawiṣyasi |
śreyaścāwāpsyasīti | 075 |
sa ewamukto'świbhyāṃ labdhacakṣurupādhyāyasakāśamāgamyopādhyāyamabhiwādyācacakṣe |
sa cāsya prītimānabhūt | 076 |
āha cainam |
yathāśwināwāhatustathā twaṃ śreyo'wāpsyasīti |
sarwe ca te wedāḥ pratibhāsyantīti | 077 |
eṣā tasyāpi parīkṣopamanyoḥ | 078 |
athāparaḥ śiṣyastasyaiwāyodasya dhaumyasya wedo nāma | 079 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ saṃdideśa |
watsa weda ihāsyatām |
bhawatā madgṛhe kañcitkālaṃ śuśrūṣamāṇena bhawitawyam |
śreyaste bhawiṣyatīti | 080 |
sa tathetyuktwā gurukule dīrghakālaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇaparo'wasat |
gauriwa nityaṃ guruṣu dhūrṣu niyujyamānaḥ śītoṣṇakṣuttṛṣṇāduḥkhasahaḥ sarwatrāpratikūlaḥ | 081 |
tasya mahatā kālena guruḥ paritoṣaṃ jagāma |
tatparitoṣācca śreyaḥ sarwajñatāṃ cāwāpa |
eṣā tasyāpi parīkṣā wedasya | 082 |
sa upādhyāyenānujñātaḥ samāwṛttastasmādgurukulawāsādgṛhāśramaṃ pratyapadyata |
tasyāpi swagṛhe wasatastrayaḥ śiṣyā babhūwuḥ | 083 |
sa śiṣyānna kiñciduwāca |
karma wā kriyatāṃ guruśuśrūṣā weti |
duḥkhābhijño hi gurukulawāsasya śiṣyānparikleśena yojayituṃ neyeṣa | 084 |
atha kasyacitkālasya wedaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ janamejayaḥ pauṣyaśca kṣatriyāwupetyopādhyāyaṃ warayāṃ cakratuḥ | 085 |
sa kadācidyājyakāryeṇābhiprasthita uttaṅkaṃ nāma śiṣyaṃ niyojayāmāsa |
bho uttaṅka yatkiñcidasmadgṛhe parihīyate tadicchāmyahamaparihīṇaṃ bhawatā kriyamāṇamiti | 086 |
sa ewaṃ pratisamādiśyottaṅkaṃ wedaḥ prawāsaṃ jagāma | 087 |
athottaṅko guruśuśrūṣurguruniyogamanutiṣṭhamānastatra gurukule wasati sma | 088 |
sa wasaṃstatropādhyāyastrībhiḥ sahitābhirāhūyoktaḥ |
upādhyāyinī te ṛtumatī |
upādhyāyaśca proṣitaḥ |
asyā yathāyamṛturwandhyo na bhawati tathā kriyatām |
etadwiṣīdatīti | 089 |
sa ewamuktastāḥ striyaḥ pratyuwāca |
na mayā strīṇāṃ wacanādidamakāryaṃ kāryam |
na hyahamupādhyāyena saṃdiṣṭaḥ |
akāryamapi twayā kāryamiti | 090 |
tasya punarupādhyāyaḥ kālāntareṇa gṛhānupajagāma tasmātprawāsāt |
sa tadwṛttaṃ tasyāśeṣamupalabhya prītimānabhūt | 091 |
uwāca cainam |
watsottaṅka kiṃ te priyaṃ karawāṇīti |
dharmato hi śuśrūṣito'smi bhawatā |
tena prītiḥ paraspareṇa nau saṃwṛddhā |
tadanujāne bhawantam |
sarwāmewa siddhiṃ prāpsyasi |
gamyatāmiti | 092 |
sa ewamuktaḥ pratyuwāca |
kiṃ te priyaṃ karawāṇīti |
ewaṃ hyāhuḥ | 093 |
yaścādharmeṇa wibrūyādyaścādharmeṇa pṛcchati | 094 |
tayoranyataraḥ praiti widweṣaṃ cādhigacchati |
so'hamanujñāto bhawatā icchāmīṣṭaṃ te gurwarthamupahartumiti | 095 |
tenaiwamukta upādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
watsottaṅka uṣyatāṃ tāwaditi | 096 |
sa kadācittamupādhyāyamāhottaṅkaḥ |
ājñāpayatu bhawān |
kiṃ te priyamupaharāmi gurwarthamiti | 097 |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
watsottaṅka bahuśo māṃ codayasi gurwarthamupahareyamiti |
tadgaccha |
enāṃ prawiśyopādhyāyinīṃ pṛccha kimupaharāmīti |
eṣā yadbrawīti tadupaharasweti | 098 |
sa ewamukta upādhyāyenopādhyāyinīmapṛcchat |
bhawatyupādhyāyenāsmyanujñāto gṛhaṃ gantum |
tadicchāmīṣṭaṃ te gurwarthamupahṛtyānṛṇo gantum |
tadājñāpayatu bhawatī |
kimupaharāmi gurwarthamiti | 099 |
saiwamuktopādhyāyinyuttaṅkaṃ pratyuwāca |
gaccha pauṣyaṃ rājānam |
bhikṣaswa tasya kṣatriyayā pinaddhe kuṇḍale |
te ānayaswa |
itaścaturthe'hani puṇyakaṃ bhawitā |
tābhyāmābaddhābhyāṃ brāhmaṇānpariweṣṭumicchāmi |
śobhamānā yathā tābhyāṃ kuṇḍalābhyāṃ tasminnahani sampādayaswa |
śreyo hi te syātkṣaṇaṃ kurwata iti | 100 |
sa ewamukta upādhyāyinyā prātiṣṭhatottaṅkaḥ |
sa pathi gacchannapaśyadṛṣabhamatipramāṇaṃ tamadhirūḍhaṃ ca puruṣamatipramāṇamewa | 101 |
sa puruṣa uttaṅkamabhyabhāṣata |
uttaṅkaitatpurīṣamasya ṛṣabhasya bhakṣayasweti | 102 |
sa ewamukto naicchat | 103 |
tamāha puruṣo bhūyaḥ |
bhakṣayaswottaṅka |
mā wicāraya |
upādhyāyenāpi te bhakṣitaṃ pūrwamiti | 104 |
sa ewamukto bāḍhamityuktwā tadā tadṛṣabhasya purīṣaṃ mūtraṃ ca bhakṣayitwottaṅkaḥ pratasthe yatra sa kṣatriyaḥ pauṣyaḥ | 105 |
tamupetyāpaśyaduttaṅka āsīnam |
sa tamupetyāśīrbhirabhinandyowāca |
arthī bhawantamupagato'smīti | 106 |
sa enamabhiwādyowāca |
bhagawanpauṣyaḥ khalwaham |
kiṃ karawāṇīti | 107 |
tamuwācottaṅkaḥ |
gurwarthe kuṇḍalābhyāmarthyāgato'smīti ye te kṣatriyayā pinaddhe kuṇḍale te bhawāndātumarhatīti | 108 |
taṃ pauṣyaḥ pratyuwāca |
prawiśyāntaḥpuraṃ kṣatriyā yācyatāmiti | 109 |
sa tenaiwamuktaḥ prawiśyāntaḥpuraṃ kṣatriyāṃ nāpaśyat | 110 |
sa pauṣyaṃ punaruwāca |
na yuktaṃ bhawatā wayamanṛtenopacaritum |
na hi te kṣatriyāntaḥpure saṃnihitā |
naināṃ paśyāmīti | 111 |
sa ewamuktaḥ pauṣyastaṃ pratyuwāca |
samprati bhawānucchiṣṭaḥ |
smara tāwat |
na hi sā kṣatriyā ucchiṣṭenāśucinā wā śakyā draṣṭum |
patiwratātwādeṣā nāśucerdarśanamupaitīti | 112 |
athaiwamukta uttaṅkaḥ smṛtwowāca |
asti khalu mayocchiṣṭenopaspṛṣṭaṃ śīghraṃ gacchatā ceti | 113 |
taṃ pauṣyaḥ pratyuwāca |
etattadewaṃ hi |
na gacchatopaspṛṣṭaṃ bhawati na sthiteneti | 114 |
athottaṅkastathetyuktwā prāṅmukha upawiśya suprakṣālitapāṇipādawadano'śabdābhir hṛdayaṅgamābhiradbhirupaspṛśya triḥ pītwā dwiḥ parimṛjya khānyadbhirupaspṛśyāntaḥpuraṃ prawiśya tāṃ kṣatriyāmapaśyat | 115 |
sā ca dṛṣṭwaiwottaṅkamabhyutthāyābhiwādyowāca |
swāgataṃ te bhagawan |
ājñāpaya kiṃ karawāṇīti | 116 |
sa tāmuwāca |
ete kuṇḍale gurwarthaṃ me bhikṣite dātumarhasīti | 117 |
sā prītā tena tasya sadbhāwena pātramayamanatikramaṇīyaśceti matwā te kuṇḍale awamucyāsmai prāyacchat | 118 |
āha cainam |
ete kuṇḍale takṣako nāgarājaḥ prārthayati |
apramatto netumarhasīti | 119 |
sa ewamuktastāṃ kṣatriyāṃ pratyuwāca |
bhawati sunirwṛtā bhawa |
na māṃ śaktastakṣako nāgarājo dharṣayitumiti | 120 |
sa ewamuktwā tāṃ kṣatriyāmāmantrya pauṣyasakāśamāgacchat | 121 |
sa taṃ dṛṣṭwowāca |
bhoḥ pauṣya prīto'smīti | 122 |
taṃ pauṣyaḥ pratyuwāca |
bhagawaṃścirasya pātramāsādyate |
bhawāṃśca guṇawānatithiḥ |
tatkariṣye śrāddham |
kṣaṇaḥ kriyatāmiti | 123 |
tamuttaṅkaḥ pratyuwāca |
kṛtakṣaṇa ewāsmi |
śīghramicchāmi yathopapannamannamupahṛtaṃ bhawateti | 124 |
sa tathetyuktwā yathopapannenānnenainaṃ bhojayāmāsa | 125 |
athottaṅkaḥ śītamannaṃ sakeśaṃ dṛṣṭwā aśucyetaditi matwā pauṣyamuwāca |
yasmānme aśucyannaṃ dadāsi tasmadandho bhawiṣyasīti | 126 |
taṃ pauṣyaḥ pratyuwāca |
yasmāttwamapyaduṣṭamannaṃ dūṣayasi tasmādanapatyo bhawiṣyasīti | 127 |
so'tha pauṣyastasyāśucibhāwamannasyāgamayāmāsa | 128 |
atha tadannaṃ muktakeśyā striyopahṛtaṃ sakeśamaśuci matwottaṅkaṃ prasādayāmāsa |
bhagawannajñānādetadannaṃ sakeśamupahṛtaṃ śītaṃ ca |
tatkṣāmaye bhawantam |
na bhaweyamandha iti | 129 |
tamuttaṅkaḥ pratyuwāca |
na mṛṣā brawīmi |
bhūtwā twamandho nacirādanandho bhawiṣyasīti |
mamāpi śāpo na bhawedbhawatā datta iti | 130 |
taṃ pauṣyaḥ pratyuwāca |
nāhaṃ śaktaḥ śāpaṃ pratyādātum |
na hi me manyuradyāpyupaśamaṃ gacchati |
kiṃ caitadbhawatā na jñāyate yathā | 131 |

nāwanītaṃ hṛdayaṃ brāhmaṇasya; wāci kṣuro nihitastīkṣṇadhāraḥ |
wiparītametadubhayaṃ kṣatriyasya; wāṅnāwanītī hṛdayaṃ tīkṣṇadhāram ||132||

iti |
tadewaṃ gate na śakto'haṃ tīkṣṇahṛdayatwāttaṃ śāpamanyathā kartum |
gamyatāmiti | 133 |
tamuttaṅkaḥ pratyuwāca |
bhawatāhamannasyāśucibhāwamāgamayya pratyanunītaḥ |
prākca te'bhihitam |
yasmādaduṣṭamannaṃ dūṣayasi tasmādanapatyo bhawiṣyasīti |
duṣṭe cānne naiṣa mama śāpo bhawiṣyatīti | 134 |
sādhayāmastāwadityuktwā prātiṣṭhatottaṅkaste kuṇḍale gṛhītwā | 135 |
so'paśyatpathi nagnaṃ śramaṇamāgacchantaṃ muhurmuhurdṛśyamānamadṛśyamānaṃ ca |
athottaṅkaste kuṇḍale bhūmau nikṣipyodakārthaṃ pracakrame | 136 |
etasminnantare sa śramaṇastwaramāṇa upasṛtya te kuṇḍale gṛhītwā prādrawat |
tamuttaṅko'bhisṛtya jagrāha |
sa tadrūpaṃ wihāya takṣakarūpaṃ kṛtwā sahasā dharaṇyāṃ wiwṛtaṃ mahābilaṃ wiweśa | 137 |
prawiśya ca nāgalokaṃ swabhawanamagacchat |
tamuttaṅko'nwāwiweśa tenaiwa bilena |
prawiśya ca nāgānastuwadebhiḥ ślokaiḥ | 138 |

ya airāwatarājānaḥ sarpāḥ samitiśobhanāḥ |
warṣanta iwa jīmūtāḥ sawidyutpawaneritāḥ ||139||

surūpāśca wirūpāśca tathā kalmāṣakuṇḍalāḥ |
ādityawannākapṛṣṭhe rejurairāwatodbhawāḥ ||140||

bahūni nāgawartmāni gaṅgāyāstīra uttare |
icchetko'rkāṃśusenāyāṃ cartumairāwataṃ winā ||141||

śatānyaśītiraṣṭau ca sahasrāṇi ca wiṃśatiḥ |
sarpāṇāṃ pragrahā yānti dhṛtarāṣṭro yadejati ||142||

ye cainamupasarpanti ye ca dūraṃ paraṃ gatāḥ |
ahamairāwatajyeṣṭhabhrātṛbhyo'karawaṃ namaḥ ||143||

yasya wāsaḥ kurukṣetre khāṇḍawe cābhawatsadā |
taṃ kādraweyamastauṣaṃ kuṇḍalārthāya takṣakam ||144||

takṣakaścāśwasenaśca nityaṃ sahacarāwubhau |
kurukṣetre niwasatāṃ nadīmikṣumatīmanu ||145||

jaghanyajastakṣakasya śrutaseneti yaḥ śrutaḥ |
awasadyo mahaddyumni prārthayannāgamukhyatām ||146||

karawāṇi sadā cāhaṃ namastasmai mahātmane ||146||

ewaṃ stuwannapi nāgānyadā te kuṇḍale nālabhadathāpaśyatstriyau tantre adhiropya paṭaṃ wayantyau | 147 |
tasmiṃśca tantre kṛṣṇāḥ sitāśca tantawaḥ |
cakraṃ cāpaśyatṣaḍbhiḥ kumāraiḥ pariwartyamānam |
puruṣaṃ cāpaśyaddarśanīyam | 148 |
sa tānsarwāṃstuṣṭāwa ebhirmantrawādaślokaiḥ | 149 |

trīṇyarpitānyatra śatāni madhye; ṣaṣṭiśca nityaṃ carati dhruwe'smin |
cakre caturwiṃśatiparwayoge; ṣaḍyatkumārāḥ pariwartayanti ||150||

tantraṃ cedaṃ wiśwarūpaṃ yuwatyau; wayatastantūnsatataṃ wartayantyau |
kṛṣṇānsitāṃścaiwa wiwartayantyau; bhūtānyajasraṃ bhuwanāni caiwa ||151||

wajrasya bhartā bhuwanasya goptā; wṛtrasya hantā namucernihantā |
kṛṣṇe wasāno wasane mahātmā; satyānṛte yo wiwinakti loke ||152||

yo wājinaṃ garbhamapāṃ purāṇaṃ; waiśwānaraṃ wāhanamabhyupetaḥ |
namaḥ sadāsmai jagadīśwarāya; lokatrayeśāya puraṃdarāya ||153||

tataḥ sa enaṃ puruṣaḥ prāha |
prīto'smi te'hamanena stotreṇa |
kiṃ te priyaṃ karawāṇīti | 154 |
sa tamuwāca |
nāgā me waśamīyuriti | 155 |
sa enaṃ puruṣaḥ punaruwāca |
etamaśwamapāne dhamasweti | 156 |
sa tamaśwamapāne'dhamat |
athāśwāddhamyamānātsarwasrotobhyaḥ sadhūmā arciṣo'gnerniṣpetuḥ | 157 |
tābhirnāgaloko dhūpitaḥ | 158 |
atha sasambhramastakṣako'gnitejobhayawiṣaṇṇaste kuṇḍale gṛhītwā sahasā swabhawanānniṣkramyottaṅkamuwāca |
ete kuṇḍale pratigṛhṇātu bhawāniti | 159 |
sa te pratijagrāhottaṅkaḥ |
kuṇḍale pratigṛhyācintayat |
adya tatpuṇyakamupādhyāyinyāḥ |
dūraṃ cāhamabhyāgataḥ |
kathaṃ nu khalu sambhāwayeyamiti | 160 |
tata enaṃ cintayānamewa sa puruṣa uwāca |
uttaṅka enamaśwamadhiroha |
eṣa twāṃ kṣaṇādewopādhyāyakulaṃ prāpayiṣyatīti | 161 |
sa tathetyuktwā tamaśwamadhiruhya pratyājagāmopādhyāyakulam |
upādhyāyinī ca snātā keśānāwapayantyupawiṣṭottaṅko nāgacchatīti śāpāyāsya mano dadhe | 162 |
athottaṅkaḥ prawiśya upādhyāyinīmabhyawādayat |
te cāsyai kuṇḍale prāyacchat | 163 |
sā cainaṃ pratyuwāca |
uttaṅka deśe kāle'bhyāgataḥ |
swāgataṃ te watsa |
manāgasi mayā na śaptaḥ |
śreyastawopasthitam |
siddhimāpnuhīti | 164 |
athottaṅka upādhyāyamabhyawādayat |
tamupādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
watsottaṅka swāgataṃ te |
kiṃ ciraṃ kṛtamiti | 165 |
tamuttaṅka upādhyāyaṃ pratyuwāca |
bhostakṣakeṇa nāgarājena wighnaḥ kṛto'sminkarmaṇi |
tenāsmi nāgalokaṃ nītaḥ | 166 |
tatra ca mayā dṛṣṭe striyau tantre'dhiropya paṭaṃ wayantyau |
tasmiṃśca tantre kṛṣṇāḥ sitāśca tantawaḥ |
kiṃ tat | 167 |
tatra ca mayā cakraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ dwādaśāram |
ṣaṭcainaṃ kumārāḥ pariwartayanti |
tadapi kim | 168 |
puruṣaścāpi mayā dṛṣṭaḥ |
sa punaḥ kaḥ | 169 |
aśwaścātipramāṇayuktaḥ |
sa cāpi kaḥ | 170 |
pathi gacchatā mayā ṛṣabho dṛṣṭaḥ |
taṃ ca puruṣo'dhirūḍhaḥ |
tenāsmi sopacāramuktaḥ |
uttaṅkāsya ṛṣabhasya purīṣaṃ bhakṣaya |
upādhyāyenāpi te bhakṣitamiti |
tatastadwacanānmayā tadṛṣabhasya purīṣamupayuktam |
tadicchāmi bhawatopadiṣṭaṃ kiṃ taditi | 171 |
tenaiwamukta upādhyāyaḥ pratyuwāca |
ye te striyau dhātā widhātā ca |
ye ca te kṛṣṇāḥ sitāśca tantawaste rātryahanī | 172 |
yadapi taccakraṃ dwādaśāraṃ ṣaṭkumārāḥ pariwartayanti te ṛtawaḥ ṣaṭsaṃwatsaraścakram |
yaḥ puruṣaḥ sa parjanyaḥ |
yo'śwaḥ so'gniḥ | 173 |
ya ṛṣabhastwayā pathi gacchatā dṛṣṭaḥ sa airāwato nāgarājaḥ |
yaścainamadhirūḍhaḥ sa indraḥ |
yadapi te purīṣaṃ bhakṣitaṃ tasya ṛṣabhasya tadamṛtam | 174 |
tena khalwasi na wyāpannastasminnāgabhawane |
sa cāpi mama sakhā indraḥ | 175 |
tadanugrahātkuṇḍale gṛhītwā punarabhyāgato'si |
tatsaumya gamyatām |
anujāne bhawantam |
śreyo'wāpsyasīti | 176 |
sa upādhyāyenānujñāta uttaṅkaḥ kruddhastakṣakasya praticikīrṣamāṇo hāstinapuraṃ pratasthe | 177 |

sa hāstinapuraṃ prāpya nacirāddwijasattamaḥ |
samāgacchata rājānamuttaṅko janamejayam ||178||

purā takṣaśilātastaṃ niwṛttamaparājitam |
samyagwijayinaṃ dṛṣṭwā samantānmantribhirwṛtam ||179||

tasmai jayāśiṣaḥ pūrwaṃ yathānyāyaṃ prayujya saḥ |
uwācainaṃ wacaḥ kāle śabdasampannayā girā ||180||

anyasminkaraṇīye twaṃ kārye pārthiwasattama |
bālyādiwānyadewa twaṃ kuruṣe nṛpasattama ||181||

ewamuktastu wipreṇa sa rājā pratyuwāca ha |
janamejayaḥ prasannātmā samyaksampūjya taṃ munim ||182||

āsāṃ prajānāṃ paripālanena; swaṃ kṣatradharmaṃ paripālayāmi |
prabrūhi wā kiṃ kriyatāṃ dwijendra; śuśrūṣurasmyadya wacastwadīyam ||183||

sa ewamuktastu nṛpottamena; dwijottamaḥ puṇyakṛtāṃ wariṣṭhaḥ |
uwāca rājānamadīnasattwaṃ; swamewa kāryaṃ nṛpateśca yattat ||184||

takṣakeṇa narendrendra yena te hiṃsitaḥ pitā |
tasmai pratikuruṣwa twaṃ pannagāya durātmane ||185||

kāryakālaṃ ca manye'haṃ widhidṛṣṭasya karmaṇaḥ |
tadgacchāpacitiṃ rājanpitustasya mahātmanaḥ ||186||

tena hyanaparādhī sa daṣṭo duṣṭāntarātmanā |
pañcatwamagamadrājā wajrāhata iwa drumaḥ ||187||

baladarpasamutsiktastakṣakaḥ pannagādhamaḥ |
akāryaṃ kṛtawānpāpo yo'daśatpitaraṃ tawa ||188||

rājarṣiwaṃśagoptāramamarapratimaṃ nṛpam |
jaghāna kāśyapaṃ caiwa nyawartayata pāpakṛt ||189||

dagdhumarhasi taṃ pāpaṃ jwalite hawyawāhane |
sarpasatre mahārāja twayi taddhi widhīyate ||190||

ewaṃ pituścāpacitiṃ gatawāṃstwaṃ bhawiṣyasi |
mama priyaṃ ca sumahatkṛtaṃ rājanbhawiṣyati ||191||

karmaṇaḥ pṛthiwīpāla mama yena durātmanā |
wighnaḥ kṛto mahārāja gurwarthaṃ carato'nagha ||192||

etacchrutwā tu nṛpatistakṣakasya cukopa ha |
uttaṅkawākyahawiṣā dīpto'gnirhawiṣā yathā ||193||

apṛcchacca tadā rājā mantriṇaḥ swānsuduḥkhitaḥ |
uttaṅkasyaiwa sāṃnidhye pituḥ swargagatiṃ prati ||194||

tadaiwa hi sa rājendro duḥkhaśokāpluto'bhawat |
yadaiwa pitaraṃ wṛttamuttaṅkādaśṛṇottadā ||195||

              paulomaparwa
                  4

lomaharṣaṇaputra ugraśrawāḥ sūtaḥ paurāṇiko naimiṣāraṇye śaunakasya kulapaterdwādaśawārṣike satre ṛṣīnabhyāgatānupatasthe | 001 |
paurāṇikaḥ purāṇe kṛtaśramaḥ sa tānkṛtāñjaliruwāca |
kiṃ bhawantaḥ śrotumicchanti |
kimahaṃ bruwāṇīti | 002 |
tamṛṣaya ūcuḥ |
paramaṃ lomaharṣaṇe prakṣyāmastwāṃ wakṣyasi ca naḥ śuśrūṣatāṃ kathāyogam |
tadbhagawāṃstu tāwacchaunako'gniśaraṇamadhyāste | 003 |

yo'sau diwyāḥ kathā weda dewatāsurasaṅkathāḥ |
manuṣyoragagandharwakathā weda ca sarwaśaḥ ||4||

sa cāpyasminmakhe saute widwānkulapatirdwijaḥ |
dakṣo dhṛtawrato dhīmāñśāstre cāraṇyake guruḥ ||5||

satyawādī śamaparastapaswī niyatawrataḥ |
sarweṣāmewa no mānyaḥ sa tāwatpratipālyatām ||6||

tasminnadhyāsati gurāwāsanaṃ paramārcitam |
tato wakṣyasi yattwāṃ sa prakṣyati dwijasattamaḥ ||7||

sūta uwāca||

ewamastu gurau tasminnupawiṣṭe mahātmani |
tena pṛṣṭaḥ kathāḥ puṇyā wakṣyāmi wiwidhāśrayāḥ ||8||

so'tha wiprarṣabhaḥ kāryaṃ kṛtwā sarwaṃ yathākramam |
dewānwāgbhiḥ pitṛnadbhistarpayitwājagāma ha ||9||

yatra brahmarṣayaḥ siddhāsta āsīnā yatawratāḥ |
yajñāyatanamāśritya sūtaputrapuraḥsarāḥ ||10||

ṛtwikṣwatha sadasyeṣu sa wai gṛhapatistataḥ |
upawiṣṭeṣūpawiṣṭaḥ śaunako'thābrawīdidam ||11||






                  5


śaunaka uwāca||

purāṇamakhilaṃ tāta pitā te'dhītawānpurā |
kaccittwamapi tatsarwamadhīṣe lomaharṣaṇe ||1||

purāṇe hi kathā diwyā ādiwaṃśāśca dhīmatām |
kathyante tāḥ purāsmābhiḥ śrutāḥ pūrwaṃ pitustawa ||2||

tatra waṃśamahaṃ pūrwaṃ śrotumicchāmi bhārgawam |
kathayaswa kathāmetāṃ kalyāḥ sma śrawaṇe tawa ||3||

sūta uwāca||

yadadhītaṃ purā samyagdwijaśreṣṭha mahātmabhiḥ |
waiśampāyanawiprādyaistaiścāpi kathitaṃ purā ||4||

yadadhītaṃ ca pitrā me samyakcaiwa tato mayā |
tattāwacchṛṇu yo dewaiḥ sendraiḥ sāgnimarudgaṇaiḥ ||5||

pūjitaḥ prawaro waṃśo bhṛgūṇāṃ bhṛgunandana ||5||

imaṃ waṃśamahaṃ brahmanbhārgawaṃ te mahāmune |
nigadāmi kathāyuktaṃ purāṇāśrayasaṃyutam ||6||

bhṛgoḥ sudayitaḥ putraścyawano nāma bhārgawaḥ |
cyawanasyāpi dāyādaḥ pramatirnāma dhārmikaḥ ||7||

pramaterapyabhūtputro ghṛtācyāṃ rururityuta ||7||

rurorapi suto jajñe śunako wedapāragaḥ |
pramadwarāyāṃ dharmātmā tawa pūrwapitāmahāt ||8||

tapaswī ca yaśaswī ca śrutawānbrahmawittamaḥ |
dharmiṣṭhaḥ satyawādī ca niyato niyatendriyaḥ ||9||

śaunaka uwāca||

sūtaputra yathā tasya bhārgawasya mahātmanaḥ |
cyawanatwaṃ parikhyātaṃ tanmamācakṣwa pṛcchataḥ ||10||

sūta uwāca||

bhṛgoḥ sudayitā bhāryā pulometyabhiwiśrutā |
tasyāṃ garbhaḥ samabhawadbhṛgorwīryasamudbhawaḥ ||11||

tasmingarbhe sambhṛte'tha pulomāyāṃ bhṛgūdwaha |
samaye samaśīlinyāṃ dharmapatnyāṃ yaśaswinaḥ ||12||

abhiṣekāya niṣkrānte bhṛgau dharmabhṛtāṃ ware |
āśramaṃ tasya rakṣo'tha pulomābhyājagāma ha ||13||

taṃ prawiśyāśramaṃ dṛṣṭwā bhṛgorbhāryāmaninditām |
hṛcchayena samāwiṣṭo wicetāḥ samapadyata ||14||

abhyāgataṃ tu tadrakṣaḥ pulomā cārudarśanā |
nyamantrayata wanyena phalamūlādinā tadā ||15||

tāṃ tu rakṣastato brahmanhṛcchayenābhipīḍitam |
dṛṣṭwā hṛṣṭamabhūttatra jihīrṣustāmaninditām ||16||

athāgniśaraṇe'paśyajjwalitaṃ jātawedasam |
tamapṛcchattato rakṣaḥ pāwakaṃ jwalitaṃ tadā ||17||

śaṃsa me kasya bhāryeyamagne pṛṣṭa ṛtena wai |
satyastwamasi satyaṃ me wada pāwaka pṛcchate ||18||

mayā hīyaṃ pūrwawṛtā bhāryārthe warawarṇinī |
paścāttwimāṃ pitā prādādbhṛgawe'nṛtakāriṇe ||19||

seyaṃ yadi warārohā bhṛgorbhāryā rahogatā |
tathā satyaṃ samākhyāhi jihīrṣāmyāśramādimām ||20||

manyurhi hṛdayaṃ me'dya pradahanniwa tiṣṭhati |
matpurwabhāryāṃ yadimāṃ bhṛguḥ prāpa sumadhyamām ||21||

tadrakṣa ewamāmantrya jwalitaṃ jātawedasam |
śaṅkamāno bhṛgorbhāryāṃ punaḥ punarapṛcchata ||22||

twamagne sarwabhūtānāmantaścarasi nityadā |
sākṣiwatpuṇyapāpeṣu satyaṃ brūhi kawe wacaḥ ||23||

matpūrwabhāryāpahṛtā bhṛguṇānṛtakāriṇā |
seyaṃ yadi tathā me twaṃ satyamākhyātumarhasi ||24||

śrutwā twatto bhṛgorbhāryāṃ hariṣyāmyahamāśramāt |
jātawedaḥ paśyataste wada satyāṃ giraṃ mama ||25||

tasya tadwacanaṃ śrutwā saptārcirduḥkhito bhṛśam |
bhīto'nṛtācca śāpācca bhṛgorityabrawīcchanaiḥ ||26||






                  6


sūta uwāca||

agneratha wacaḥ śrutwā tadrakṣaḥ prajahāra tām |
brahmanwarāharūpeṇa manomārutaraṃhasā ||1||

tataḥ sa garbho niwasankukṣau bhṛgukulodwaha |
roṣānmātuścyutaḥ kukṣeścyawanastena so'bhawat ||2||

taṃ dṛṣṭwā māturudarāccyutamādityawarcasam |
tadrakṣo bhasmasādbhūtaṃ papāta parimucya tām ||3||

sā tamādāya suśroṇī sasāra bhṛgunandanam |
cyawanaṃ bhārgawaṃ brahmanpulomā duḥkhamūrcchitā ||4||

tāṃ dadarśa swayaṃ brahmā sarwalokapitāmahaḥ |
rudatīṃ bāṣpapūrṇākṣīṃ bhṛgorbhāryāmaninditām ||5||

sāntwayāmāsa bhagawānwadhūṃ brahmā pitāmahaḥ ||5||

aśrubindūdbhawā tasyāḥ prāwartata mahānadī |
anuwartatī sṛtiṃ tasyā bhṛgoḥ patnyā yaśaswinaḥ ||6||

tasyā mārgaṃ sṛtawatīṃ dṛṣṭwā tu saritaṃ tadā |
nāma tasyāstadā nadyāścakre lokapitāmahaḥ ||7||

wadhūsareti bhagawāṃścyawanasyāśramaṃ prati ||7||

sa ewaṃ cyawano jajñe bhṛgoḥ putraḥ pratāpawān |
taṃ dadarśa pitā tatra cyawanaṃ tāṃ ca bhāminīm ||8||

sa pulomāṃ tato bhāryāṃ papraccha kupito bhṛguḥ |
kenāsi rakṣase tasmai kathiteha jihīrṣawe ||9||

na hi twāṃ weda tadrakṣo madbhāryāṃ cāruhāsinīm ||9||

tattwamākhyāhi taṃ hyadya śaptumicchāmyahaṃ ruṣā |
bibheti ko na śāpānme kasya cāyaṃ wyatikramaḥ ||10||

pulomowāca||

agninā bhagawaṃstasmai rakṣase'haṃ niweditā |
tato māmanayadrakṣaḥ krośantīṃ kurarīmiwa ||11||

sāhaṃ tawa sutasyāsya tejasā parimokṣitā |
bhasmībhūtaṃ ca tadrakṣo māmutsṛjya papāta wai ||12||

sūta uwāca||

iti śrutwā pulomāyā bhṛguḥ paramamanyumān |
śaśāpāgnimabhikruddhaḥ sarwabhakṣo bhawiṣyasi ||13||






                  7


sūta uwāca||

śaptastu bhṛguṇā wahniḥ kruddho wākyamathābrawīt |
kimidaṃ sāhasaṃ brahmankṛtawānasi sāmpratam ||1||

dharme prayatamānasya satyaṃ ca wadataḥ samam |
pṛṣṭo yadabruwaṃ satyaṃ wyabhicāro'tra ko mama ||2||

pṛṣṭo hi sākṣī yaḥ sākṣyaṃ jānamāno'nyathā wadet |
sa pūrwānātmanaḥ sapta kule hanyāttathā parān ||3||

yaśca kāryārthatattwajño jānamāno na bhāṣate |
so'pi tenaiwa pāpena lipyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||4||

śakto'hamapi śaptuṃ twāṃ mānyāstu brāhmaṇā mama |
jānato'pi ca te wyaktaṃ kathayiṣye nibodha tat ||5||

yogena bahudhātmānaṃ kṛtwā tiṣṭhāmi mūrtiṣu |
agnihotreṣu satreṣu kriyāswatha makheṣu ca ||6||

wedoktena widhānena mayi yaddhūyate hawiḥ |
dewatāḥ pitaraścaiwa tena tṛptā bhawanti wai ||7||

āpo dewagaṇāḥ sarwe āpaḥ pitṛgaṇāstathā |
darśaśca paurṇamāsaśca dewānāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha ||8||

dewatāḥ pitarastasmātpitaraścāpi dewatāḥ |
ekībhūtāśca pūjyante pṛthaktwena ca parwasu ||9||

dewatāḥ pitaraścaiwa juhwate mayi yatsadā |
tridaśānāṃ pitṛṇāṃ ca mukhamewamahaṃ smṛtaḥ ||10||

amāwāsyāṃ ca pitaraḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ ca dewatāḥ |
manmukhenaiwa hūyante bhuñjate ca hutaṃ hawiḥ ||11||

sarwabhakṣaḥ kathaṃ teṣāṃ bhawiṣyāmi mukhaṃ twaham ||11||

cintayitwā tato wahniścakre saṃhāramātmanaḥ |
dwijānāmagnihotreṣu yajñasatrakriyāsu ca ||12||

niroṅkārawaṣaṭkārāḥ swadhāswāhāwiwarjitāḥ |
wināgninā prajāḥ sarwāstata āsansuduḥkhitāḥ ||13||

atharṣayaḥ samudwignā dewāngatwābruwanwacaḥ |
agnināśātkriyābhraṃśādbhrāntā lokāstrayo'naghāḥ ||14||

widhadhwamatra yatkāryaṃ na syātkālātyayo yathā ||14||

atharṣayaśca dewāśca brahmāṇamupagamya tu |
agnerāwedayañśāpaṃ kriyāsaṃhāramewa ca ||15||

bhṛguṇā wai mahābhāga śapto'gniḥ kāraṇāntare |
kathaṃ dewamukho bhūtwā yajñabhāgāgrabhuktathā ||16||

hutabhuksarwalokeṣu sarwabhakṣatwameṣyati ||16||

śrutwā tu tadwacasteṣāmagnimāhūya lokakṛt |
uwāca wacanaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ bhūtabhāwanamawyayam ||17||

lokānāmiha sarweṣāṃ twaṃ kartā cānta ewa ca |
twaṃ dhārayasi lokāṃstrīnkriyāṇāṃ ca prawartakaḥ ||18||

sa tathā kuru lokeśa nocchidyerankriyā yathā ||18||

kasmādewaṃ wimūḍhastwamīśwaraḥ sanhutāśanaḥ |
