twaṃ pawitraṃ yadā loke sarwabhūtagataśca ha ||19||

na twaṃ sarwaśarīreṇa sarwabhakṣatwameṣyasi |
upādāne'rciṣo yāste sarwaṃ dhakṣyanti tāḥ śikhin ||20||

yathā sūryāṃśubhiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ sarwaṃ śuci wibhāwyate |
tathā twadarcirnirdagdhaṃ sarwaṃ śuci bhawiṣyati ||21||

tadagne twaṃ mahattejaḥ swaprabhāwādwinirgatam |
swatejasaiwa taṃ śāpaṃ kuru satyamṛṣerwibho ||22||

dewānāṃ cātmano bhāgaṃ gṛhāṇa twaṃ mukhe hutam ||22||

ewamastwiti taṃ wahniḥ pratyuwāca pitāmaham |
jagāma śāsanaṃ kartuṃ dewasya parameṣṭhinaḥ ||23||

dewarṣayaśca muditāstato jagmuryathāgatam |
ṛṣayaśca yathāpūrwaṃ kriyāḥ sarwāḥ pracakrire ||24||

diwi dewā mumudire bhūtasaṅghāśca laukikāḥ |
agniśca paramāṃ prītimawāpa hatakalmaṣaḥ ||25||

ewameṣa purāwṛtta itihāso'gniśāpajaḥ |
pulomasya wināśaśca cyawanasya ca sambhawaḥ ||26||






                  8


sūta uwāca||

sa cāpi cyawano brahmanbhārgawo'janayatsutam |
sukanyāyāṃ mahātmānaṃ pramatiṃ dīptatejasam ||1||

pramatistu ruruṃ nāma ghṛtācyāṃ samajījanat |
ruruḥ pramadwarāyāṃ tu śunakaṃ samajījanat ||2||

tasya brahmanruroḥ sarwaṃ caritaṃ bhūritejasaḥ |
wistareṇa prawakṣyāmi tacchṛṇu twamaśeṣataḥ ||3||

ṛṣirāsīnmahānpūrwaṃ tapowidyāsamanwitaḥ |
sthūlakeśa iti khyātaḥ sarwabhūtahite rataḥ ||4||

etasminnewa kāle tu menakāyāṃ prajajñiwān |
gandharwarājo wiprarṣe wiśwāwasuriti śrutaḥ ||5||

athāpsarā menakā sā taṃ garbhaṃ bhṛgunandana |
utsasarja yathākālaṃ sthūlakeśāśramaṃ prati ||6||

utsṛjya caiwa taṃ garbhaṃ nadyāstīre jagāma ha |
kanyāmamaragarbhābhāṃ jwalantīmiwa ca śriyā ||7||

tāṃ dadarśa samutsṛṣṭāṃ nadītīre mahānṛṣiḥ |
sthūlakeśaḥ sa tejaswī wijane bandhuwarjitām ||8||

sa tāṃ dṛṣṭwā tadā kanyāṃ sthūlakeśo dwijottamaḥ |
jagrāhātha muniśreṣṭhaḥ kṛpāwiṣṭaḥ pupoṣa ca ||9||

wawṛdhe sā warārohā tasyāśramapade śubhā ||9||

pramadābhyo warā sā tu sarwarūpaguṇānwitā |
tataḥ pramadwaretyasyā nāma cakre mahānṛṣiḥ ||10||

tāmāśramapade tasya rururdṛṣṭwā pramadwarām |
babhūwa kila dharmātmā madanānugatātmawān ||11||

pitaraṃ sakhibhiḥ so'tha wācayāmāsa bhārgawaḥ |
pramatiścābhyayācchrutwā sthūlakeśaṃ yaśaswinam ||12||

tataḥ prādātpitā kanyāṃ rurawe tāṃ pramadwarām |
wiwāhaṃ sthāpayitwāgre nakṣatre bhagadaiwate ||13||

tataḥ katipayāhasya wiwāhe samupasthite |
sakhībhiḥ krīḍatī sārdhaṃ sā kanyā warawarṇinī ||14||

nāpaśyata prasuptaṃ wai bhujagaṃ tiryagāyatam |
padā cainaṃ samākrāmanmumūrṣuḥ kālacoditā ||15||

sa tasyāḥ sampramattāyāścoditaḥ kāladharmaṇā |
wiṣopaliptāndaśanānbhṛśamaṅge nyapātayat ||16||

sā daṣṭā sahasā bhūmau patitā gatacetanā |
wyasuraprekṣaṇīyāpi prekṣaṇīyatamākṛtiḥ ||17||

prasuptewābhawaccāpi bhuwi sarpawiṣārditā |
bhūyo manoharatarā babhūwa tanumadhyamā ||18||

dadarśa tāṃ pitā caiwa te caiwānye tapaswinaḥ |
wiceṣṭamānāṃ patitāṃ bhūtale padmawarcasam ||19||

tataḥ sarwe dwijawarāḥ samājagmuḥ kṛpānwitāḥ |
swastyātreyo mahājānuḥ kuśikaḥ śaṅkhamekhalaḥ ||20||

bhāradwājaḥ kauṇakutsa ārṣṭiṣeṇo'tha gautamaḥ |
pramatiḥ saha putreṇa tathānye wanawāsinaḥ ||21||

tāṃ te kanyāṃ wyasuṃ dṛṣṭwā bhujagasya wiṣārditām |
ruruduḥ kṛpayāwiṣṭā rurustwārto bahiryayau ||22||






                  9


sūta uwāca||

teṣu tatropawiṣṭeṣu brāhmaṇeṣu samantataḥ |
ruruścukrośa gahanaṃ wanaṃ gatwā suduḥkhitaḥ ||1||

śokenābhihataḥ so'tha wilapankaruṇaṃ bahu |
abrawīdwacanaṃ śocanpriyāṃ cintya pramadwarām ||2||

śete sā bhuwi tanwaṅgī mama śokawiwardhinī |
bāndhawānāṃ ca sarweṣāṃ kiṃ nu duḥkhamataḥ param ||3||

yadi dattaṃ tapastaptaṃ gurawo wā mayā yadi |
samyagārādhitāstena sañjīwatu mama priyā ||4||

yathā janmaprabhṛti wai yatātmāhaṃ dhṛtawrataḥ |
pramadwarā tathādyaiwa samuttiṣṭhatu bhāminī ||5||

dewadūta uwāca||

abhidhatse ha yadwācā ruro duḥkhena tanmṛṣā |
na tu martyasya dharmātmannāyurasti gatāyuṣaḥ ||6||

gatāyureṣā kṛpaṇā gandharwāpsarasoḥ sutā |
tasmācchoke manastāta mā kṛthāstwaṃ kathañcana ||7||

upāyaścātra wihitaḥ pūrwaṃ dewairmahātmabhiḥ |
taṃ yadīcchasi kartuṃ twaṃ prāpsyasīmāṃ pramadwarām ||8||

rururuwāca||

ka upāyaḥ kṛto dewairbrūhi tattwena khecara |
kariṣye taṃ tathā śrutwā trātumarhati māṃ bhawān ||9||

dewadūta uwāca||

āyuṣo'rdhaṃ prayacchaswa kanyāyai bhṛgunandana |
ewamutthāsyati ruro tawa bhāryā pramadwarā ||10||

rururuwāca||

āyuṣo'rdhaṃ prayacchāmi kanyāyai khecarottama |
śṛṅgārarūpābharaṇā uttiṣṭhatu mama priyā ||11||

sūta uwāca||

tato gandharwarājaśca dewadūtaśca sattamau |
dharmarājamupetyedaṃ wacanaṃ pratyabhāṣatām ||12||

dharmarājāyuṣo'rdhena rurorbhāryā pramadwarā |
samuttiṣṭhatu kalyāṇī mṛtaiwa yadi manyase ||13||

dharmarāja uwāca||

pramadwarā rurorbhāryā dewadūta yadīcchasi |
uttiṣṭhatwāyuṣo'rdhena rurorewa samanwitā ||14||

sūta uwāca||

ewamukte tataḥ kanyā sodatiṣṭhatpramadwarā |
rurostasyāyuṣo'rdhena suptewa warawarṇinī ||15||

etaddṛṣṭaṃ bhawiṣye hi ruroruttamatejasaḥ |
āyuṣo'tiprawṛddhasya bhāryārthe'rdhaṃ hrasatwiti ||16||

tata iṣṭe'hani tayoḥ pitarau cakraturmudā |
wiwāhaṃ tau ca remāte parasparahitaiṣiṇau ||17||

sa labdhwā durlabhāṃ bhāryāṃ padmakiñjalkasaprabhām |
wrataṃ cakre wināśāya jihmagānāṃ dhṛtawrataḥ ||18||

sa dṛṣṭwā jihmagānsarwāṃstīwrakopasamanwitaḥ |
abhihanti yathāsannaṃ gṛhya praharaṇaṃ sadā ||19||

sa kadācidwanaṃ wipro rururabhyāgamanmahat |
śayānaṃ tatra cāpaśyaḍḍuṇḍubhaṃ wayasānwitam ||20||

tata udyamya daṇḍaṃ sa kāladaṇḍopamaṃ tadā |
abhyaghnadruṣito wiprastamuwācātha ḍuṇḍubhaḥ ||21||

nāparādhyāmi te kiñcidahamadya tapodhana |
saṃrambhāttatkimarthaṃ māmabhihaṃsi ruṣānwitaḥ ||22||






                  10


rururuwāca||

mama prāṇasamā bhāryā daṣṭāsīdbhujagena ha |
tatra me samayo ghora ātmanoraga wai kṛtaḥ ||1||

hanyāṃ sadaiwa bhujagaṃ yaṃ yaṃ paśyeyamityuta |
tato'haṃ twāṃ jighāṃsāmi jīwitena wimokṣyase ||2||

ḍuṇḍubha uwāca||

anye te bhujagā wipra ye daśantīha mānawān |
ḍuṇḍubhānahigandhena na twaṃ hiṃsitumarhasi ||3||

ekānarthānpṛthagarthānekaduḥkhānpṛthaksukhān |
ḍuṇḍubhāndharmawidbhūtwā na twaṃ hiṃsitumarhasi ||4||

sūta uwāca||

iti śrutwā wacastasya bhujagasya rurustadā |
nāwadhīdbhayasaṃwigna ṛṣiṃ matwātha ḍuṇḍubham ||5||

uwāca cainaṃ bhagawānruruḥ saṃśamayanniwa |
kāmayā bhujaga brūhi ko'sīmāṃ wikriyāṃ gataḥ ||6||

ḍuṇḍubha uwāca||

ahaṃ purā ruro nāmnā ṛṣirāsaṃ sahasrapāt |
so'haṃ śāpena wiprasya bhujagatwamupāgataḥ ||7||

rururuwāca||

kimarthaṃ śaptawānkruddho dwijastwāṃ bhujagottama |
kiyantaṃ caiwa kālaṃ te wapuretadbhawiṣyati ||8||






                  11


ḍuṇḍubha uwāca||

sakhā babhūwa me pūrwaṃ khagamo nāma wai dwijaḥ |
bhṛśaṃ saṃśitawāktāta tapobalasamanwitaḥ ||1||

sa mayā krīḍatā bālye kṛtwā tārṇamathoragam |
agnihotre prasaktaḥ sanbhīṣitaḥ pramumoha wai ||2||

labdhwā ca sa punaḥ sañjñāṃ māmuwāca tapodhanaḥ |
nirdahanniwa kopena satyawāksaṃśitawrataḥ ||3||

yathāwīryastwayā sarpaḥ kṛto'yaṃ madbibhīṣayā |
tathāwīryo bhujaṅgastwaṃ mama kopādbhawiṣyasi ||4||

tasyāhaṃ tapaso wīryaṃ jānamānastapodhana |
bhṛśamudwignahṛdayastamawocaṃ wanaukasam ||5||

prayataḥ sambhramāccaiwa prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ sthitaḥ |
sakheti hasatedaṃ te narmārthaṃ wai kṛtaṃ mayā ||6||

kṣantumarhasi me brahmañśāpo'yaṃ winiwartyatām |
so'tha māmabrawīddṛṣṭwā bhṛśamudwignacetasam ||7||

muhuruṣṇaṃ winiḥśwasya susambhrāntastapodhanaḥ |
nānṛtaṃ wai mayā proktaṃ bhawitedaṃ kathañcana ||8||

yattu wakṣyāmi te wākyaṃ śṛṇu tanme dhṛtawrata |
śrutwā ca hṛdi te wākyamidamastu tapodhana ||9||

utpatsyati rururnāma pramaterātmajaḥ śuciḥ |
taṃ dṛṣṭwā śāpamokṣaste bhawitā nacirādiwa ||10||

sa twaṃ rururiti khyātaḥ pramaterātmajaḥ śuciḥ |
swarūpaṃ pratilabhyāhamadya wakṣyāmi te hitam ||11||

ahiṃsā paramo dharmaḥ sarwaprāṇabhṛtāṃ smṛtaḥ |
tasmātprāṇabhṛtaḥ sarwānna hiṃsyādbrāhmaṇaḥ kwacit ||12||

brāhmaṇaḥ saumya eweha jāyateti parā śrutiḥ |
wedawedāṅgawittāta sarwabhūtābhayapradaḥ ||13||

ahiṃsā satyawacanaṃ kṣamā ceti winiścitam |
brāhmaṇasya paro dharmo wedānāṃ dharaṇādapi ||14||

kṣatriyasya tu yo dharmaḥ sa neheṣyati wai tawa |
daṇḍadhāraṇamugratwaṃ prajānāṃ paripālanam ||15||

tadidaṃ kṣatriyasyāsītkarma wai śṛṇu me ruro |
janamejayasya dharmātmansarpāṇāṃ hiṃsanaṃ purā ||16||

paritrāṇaṃ ca bhītānāṃ sarpāṇāṃ brāhmaṇādapi |
tapowīryabalopetādwedawedāṅgapāragāt ||17||

āstīkāddwijamukhyādwai sarpasatre dwijottama ||17||






                  12


rururuwāca||

kathaṃ hiṃsitawānsarpānkṣatriyo janamejayaḥ |
sarpā wā hiṃsitāstāta kimarthaṃ dwijasattama ||1||

kimarthaṃ mokṣitāścaiwa pannagāstena śaṃsa me |
āstīkena tadācakṣwa śrotumicchāmyaśeṣataḥ ||2||

ṛṣiruwāca||

śroṣyasi twaṃ ruro sarwamāstīkacaritaṃ mahat |
brāhmaṇānāṃ kathayatāmityuktwāntaradhīyata ||3||

sūta uwāca||

ruruścāpi wanaṃ sarwaṃ paryadhāwatsamantataḥ |
tamṛṣiṃ draṣṭumanwicchansaṃśrānto nyapatadbhuwi ||4||

labdhasañjño ruruścāyāttaccācakhyau pitustadā |
pitā cāsya tadākhyānaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ sarwaṃ nyawedayat ||5||






              āstīkaparwa
                  13


śaunaka uwāca||

kimarthaṃ rājaśārdūlaḥ sa rājā janamejayaḥ |
sarpasatreṇa sarpāṇāṃ gato'ntaṃ tadwadaswa me ||1||

āstīkaśca dwijaśreṣṭhaḥ kimarthaṃ japatāṃ waraḥ |
mokṣayāmāsa bhujagāndīptāttasmāddhutāśanāt ||2||

kasya putraḥ sa rājāsītsarpasatraṃ ya āharat |
sa ca dwijātiprawaraḥ kasya putro wadaswa me ||3||

sūta uwāca||

mahadākhyānamāstīkaṃ yatraitatprocyate dwija |
sarwametadaśeṣeṇa śṛṇu me wadatāṃ wara ||4||

śaunaka uwāca||

śrotumicchāmyaśeṣeṇa kathāmetāṃ manoramām |
āstīkasya purāṇasya brāhmaṇasya yaśaswinaḥ ||5||

sūta uwāca||

itihāsamimaṃ wṛddhāḥ purāṇaṃ paricakṣate |
kṛṣṇadwaipāyanaproktaṃ naimiṣāraṇyawāsinaḥ ||6||

pūrwaṃ pracoditaḥ sūtaḥ pitā me lomaharṣaṇaḥ |
śiṣyo wyāsasya medhāwī brāhmaṇairidamuktawān ||7||

tasmādahamupaśrutya prawakṣyāmi yathātatham |
idamāstīkamākhyānaṃ tubhyaṃ śaunaka pṛcchate ||8||

āstīkasya pitā hyāsītprajāpatisamaḥ prabhuḥ |
brahmacārī yatāhārastapasyugre rataḥ sadā ||9||

jaratkāruriti khyāta ūrdhwaretā mahānṛṣiḥ |
yāyāwarāṇāṃ dharmajñaḥ prawaraḥ saṃśitawrataḥ ||10||

aṭamānaḥ kadācitsa swāndadarśa pitāmahān |
lambamānānmahāgarte pādairūrdhwairadhomukhān ||11||

tānabrawītsa dṛṣṭwaiwa jaratkāruḥ pitāmahān |
ke bhawanto'walambante garte'sminwā adhomukhāḥ ||12||

wīraṇastambake lagnāḥ sarwataḥ paribhakṣite |
mūṣakena nigūḍhena garte'sminnityawāsinā ||13||

pitara ūcuḥ||

yāyāwarā nāma wayamṛṣayaḥ saṃśitawratāḥ |
santānaprakṣayādbrahmannadho gacchāma medinīm ||14||

asmākaṃ santatistweko jaratkāruriti śrutaḥ |
mandabhāgyo'lpabhāgyānāṃ tapa ewa samāsthitaḥ ||15||

na sa putrāñjanayituṃ dārānmūḍhaścikīrṣati |
tena lambāmahe garte santānaprakṣayādiha ||16||

anāthāstena nāthena yathā duṣkṛtinastathā |
kastwaṃ bandhuriwāsmākamanuśocasi sattama ||17||

jñātumicchāmahe brahmanko bhawāniha dhiṣṭhitaḥ |
kimarthaṃ caiwa naḥ śocyānanukampitumarhasi ||18||

jaratkāruruwāca||

mama pūrwe bhawanto wai pitaraḥ sapitāmahāḥ |
brūta kiṃ karawāṇyadya jaratkārurahaṃ swayam ||19||

pitara ūcuḥ||

yataswa yatnawāṃstāta santānāya kulasya naḥ |
ātmano'rthe'smadarthe ca dharma ityewa cābhibho ||20||

na hi dharmaphalaistāta na tapobhiḥ susañcitaiḥ |
tāṃ gatiṃ prāpnuwantīha putriṇo yāṃ wrajanti ha ||21||

taddāragrahaṇe yatnaṃ santatyāṃ ca manaḥ kuru |
putrakāsmanniyogāttwametannaḥ paramaṃ hitam ||22||

jaratkāruruwāca||

na dārānwai kariṣyāmi sadā me bhāwitaṃ manaḥ |
bhawatāṃ tu hitārthāya kariṣye dārasaṅgraham ||23||

samayena ca kartāhamanena widhipūrwakam |
tathā yadyupalapsyāmi kariṣye nānyathā twaham ||24||

sanāmnī yā bhawitrī me ditsitā caiwa bandhubhiḥ |
bhaikṣawattāmahaṃ kanyāmupayaṃsye widhānataḥ ||25||

daridrāya hi me bhāryāṃ ko dāsyati wiśeṣataḥ |
pratigrahīṣye bhikṣāṃ tu yadi kaścitpradāsyati ||26||

ewaṃ dārakriyāhetoḥ prayatiṣye pitāmahāḥ |
anena widhinā śaśwanna kariṣye'hamanyathā ||27||

tatra cotpatsyate janturbhawatāṃ tāraṇāya wai |
śāśwataṃ sthānamāsādya modantāṃ pitaro mama ||28||

sūta uwāca||

tato niweśāya tadā sa wipraḥ saṃśitawrataḥ |
mahīṃ cacāra dārārthī na ca dārānawindata ||29||

sa kadācidwanaṃ gatwā wipraḥ pitṛwacaḥ smaran |
cukrośa kanyābhikṣārthī tisro wācaḥ śanairiwa ||30||

taṃ wāsukiḥ pratyagṛhṇādudyamya bhaginīṃ tadā |
na sa tāṃ pratijagrāha na sanāmnīti cintayan ||31||

sanāmnīmudyatāṃ bhāryāṃ gṛhṇīyāmiti tasya hi |
mano niwiṣṭamabhawajjaratkārormahātmanaḥ ||32||

tamuwāca mahāprājño jaratkārurmahātapāḥ |
kiṃnāmnī bhaginīyaṃ te brūhi satyaṃ bhujaṅgama ||33||

wāsukiruwāca||

jaratkāro jaratkāruḥ swaseyamanujā mama |
twadarthaṃ rakṣitā pūrwaṃ pratīcchemāṃ dwijottama ||34||

sūta uwāca||

mātrā hi bhujagāḥ śaptāḥ pūrwaṃ brahmawidāṃ wara |
janamejayasya wo yajñe dhakṣyatyanilasārathiḥ ||35||

tasya śāpasya śāntyarthaṃ pradadau pannagottamaḥ |
swasāramṛṣaye tasmai suwratāya tapaswine ||36||

sa ca tāṃ pratijagrāha widhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā |
āstīko nāma putraśca tasyāṃ jajñe mahātmanaḥ ||37||

tapaswī ca mahātmā ca wedawedāṅgapāragaḥ |
samaḥ sarwasya lokasya pitṛmātṛbhayāpahaḥ ||38||

atha kālasya mahataḥ pāṇḍaweyo narādhipaḥ |
ājahāra mahāyajñaṃ sarpasatramiti śrutiḥ ||39||

tasminprawṛtte satre tu sarpāṇāmantakāya wai |
mocayāmāsa taṃ śāpamāstīkaḥ sumahāyaśāḥ ||40||

nāgāṃśca mātulāṃścaiwa tathā cānyānsa bāndhawān |
pitṛṃśca tārayāmāsa santatyā tapasā tathā ||41||

wrataiśca wiwidhairbrahmanswādhyāyaiścānṛṇo'bhawat ||41||

dewāṃśca tarpayāmāsa yajñairwiwidhadakṣiṇaiḥ |
ṛṣīṃśca brahmacaryeṇa santatyā ca pitāmahān ||42||

apahṛtya guruṃ bhāraṃ pitṛṇāṃ saṃśitawrataḥ |
jaratkārurgataḥ swargaṃ sahitaḥ swaiḥ pitāmahaiḥ ||43||

āstīkaṃ ca sutaṃ prāpya dharmaṃ cānuttamaṃ muniḥ |
jaratkāruḥ sumahatā kālena swargamīyiwān ||44||

etadākhyānamāstīkaṃ yathāwatkīrtitaṃ mayā |
prabrūhi bhṛguśārdūla kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathyatāmiti ||45||






                  14


śaunaka uwāca||

saute kathaya tāmetāṃ wistareṇa kathāṃ punaḥ |
āstīkasya kaweḥ sādhoḥ śuśrūṣā paramā hi naḥ ||1||

madhuraṃ kathyate saumya ślakṣṇākṣarapadaṃ twayā |
prīyāmahe bhṛśaṃ tāta pitewedaṃ prabhāṣase ||2||

asmacchuśrūṣaṇe nityaṃ pitā hi niratastawa |
ācaṣṭaitadyathākhyānaṃ pitā te twaṃ tathā wada ||3||

sūta uwāca||

āyuṣyamidamākhyānamāstīkaṃ kathayāmi te |
yathā śrutaṃ kathayataḥ sakāśādwai piturmayā ||4||

purā dewayuge brahmanprajāpatisute śubhe |
āstāṃ bhaginyau rūpeṇa samupete'dbhute'naghe ||5||

te bhārye kaśyapasyāstāṃ kadrūśca winatā ca ha |
prādāttābhyāṃ waraṃ prītaḥ prajāpatisamaḥ patiḥ ||6||

kaśyapo dharmapatnībhyāṃ mudā paramayā yutaḥ ||6||

warātisargaṃ śrutwaiwa kaśyapāduttamaṃ ca te |
harṣādapratimāṃ prītiṃ prāpatuḥ sma warastriyau ||7||

wawre kadrūḥ sutānnāgānsahasraṃ tulyatejasaḥ |
dwau putrau winatā wawre kadrūputrādhikau bale ||8||

ojasā tejasā caiwa wikrameṇādhikau sutau ||8||

tasyai bhartā waraṃ prādādadhyardhaṃ putramīpsitam |
ewamastwiti taṃ cāha kaśyapaṃ winatā tadā ||9||

kṛtakṛtyā tu winatā labdhwā wīryādhikau sutau |
kadrūśca labdhwā putrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ tulyatejasām ||10||

dhāryau prayatnato garbhāwityuktwā sa mahātapāḥ |
te bhārye warasaṃhṛṣṭe kaśyapo wanamāwiśat ||11||

kālena mahatā kadrūraṇḍānāṃ daśatīrdaśa |
janayāmāsa wiprendra dwe aṇḍe winatā tadā ||12||

tayoraṇḍāni nidadhuḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ paricārikāḥ |
sopaswedeṣu bhāṇḍeṣu pañca warṣaśatāni ca ||13||

tataḥ pañcaśate kāle kadrūputrā winiḥsṛtāḥ |
aṇḍābhyāṃ winatāyāstu mithunaṃ na wyadṛśyata ||14||

tataḥ putrārthiṇī dewī wrīḍitā sā tapaswinī |
aṇḍaṃ bibheda winatā tatra putramadṛkṣata ||15||

pūrwārdhakāyasampannamitareṇāprakāśatā |
sa putro roṣasampannaḥ śaśāpaināmiti śrutiḥ ||16||

yo'hamewaṃ kṛto mātastwayā lobhaparītayā |
śarīreṇāsamagro'dya tasmāddāsī bhawiṣyasi ||17||

pañca warṣaśatānyasyā yayā wispardhase saha |
eṣa ca twāṃ suto mātardāsyatwānmokṣayiṣyati ||18||

yadyenamapi mātastwaṃ māmiwāṇḍawibhedanāt |
na kariṣyasyadehaṃ wā wyaṅgaṃ wāpi tapaswinam ||19||

pratipālayitawyaste janmakālo'sya dhīrayā |
wiśiṣṭabalamīpsantyā pañcawarṣaśatātparaḥ ||20||

ewaṃ śaptwā tataḥ putro winatāmantarikṣagaḥ |
aruṇo dṛśyate brahmanprabhātasamaye sadā ||21||

garuḍo'pi yathākālaṃ jajñe pannagasūdanaḥ |
sa jātamātro winatāṃ parityajya khamāwiśat ||22||

ādāsyannātmano bhojyamannaṃ wihitamasya yat |
widhātrā bhṛguśārdūla kṣudhitasya bubhukṣataḥ ||23||






                  15


sūta uwāca||

etasminnewa kāle tu bhaginyau te tapodhana |
apaśyatāṃ samāyāntamuccaiḥśrawasamantikāt ||1||

yaṃ taṃ dewagaṇāḥ sarwe hṛṣṭarūpā apūjayan |
mathyamāne'mṛte jātamaśwaratnamanuttamam ||2||

mahaughabalamaśwānāmuttamaṃ jawatāṃ waram |
śrīmantamajaraṃ diwyaṃ sarwalakṣaṇalakṣitam ||3||

śaunaka uwāca||

kathaṃ tadamṛtaṃ dewairmathitaṃ kwa ca śaṃsa me |
yatra jajñe mahāwīryaḥ so'śwarājo mahādyutiḥ ||4||

sūta uwāca||

jwalantamacalaṃ meruṃ tejorāśimanuttamam |
ākṣipantaṃ prabhāṃ bhānoḥ swaśṛṅgaiḥ kāñcanojjwalaiḥ ||5||

kāñcanābharaṇaṃ citraṃ dewagandharwasewitam |
aprameyamanādhṛṣyamadharmabahulairjanaiḥ ||6||

wyālairācaritaṃ ghorairdiwyauṣadhiwidīpitam |
nākamāwṛtya tiṣṭhantamucchrayeṇa mahāgirim ||7||

agamyaṃ manasāpyanyairnadīwṛkṣasamanwitam |
nānāpatagasaṅghaiśca nāditaṃ sumanoharaiḥ ||8||

tasya pṛṣṭhamupāruhya bahuratnācitaṃ śubham |
anantakalpamudwiddhaṃ surāḥ sarwe mahaujasaḥ ||9||

te mantrayitumārabdhāstatrāsīnā diwaukasaḥ |
amṛtārthe samāgamya taponiyamasaṃsthitāḥ ||10||

tatra nārāyaṇo dewo brahmāṇamidamabrawīt |
cintayatsu sureṣwewaṃ mantrayatsu ca sarwaśaḥ ||11||

dewairasurasaṅghaiśca mathyatāṃ kalaśodadhiḥ |
bhawiṣyatyamṛtaṃ tatra mathyamāne mahodadhau ||12||

sarwauṣadhīḥ samāwāpya sarwaratnāni caiwa hi |
manthadhwamudadhiṃ dewā wetsyadhwamamṛtaṃ tataḥ ||13||






                  16


sūta uwāca||

tato'bhraśikharākārairgiriśṛṅgairalaṅkṛtam |
mandaraṃ parwatawaraṃ latājālasamāwṛtam ||1||

nānāwihagasaṅghuṣṭaṃ nānādaṃṣṭrisamākulam |
kiṃnarairapsarobhiśca dewairapi ca sewitam ||2||

ekādaśa sahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ samucchritam |
adho bhūmeḥ sahasreṣu tāwatswewa pratiṣṭhitam ||3||

tamuddhartuṃ na śaktā wai sarwe dewagaṇāstadā |
wiṣṇumāsīnamabhyetya brahmāṇaṃ cedamabruwan ||4||

bhawantāwatra kurutāṃ buddhiṃ naiḥśreyasīṃ parām |
mandaroddharaṇe yatnaḥ kriyatāṃ ca hitāya naḥ ||5||

tatheti cābrawīdwiṣṇurbrahmaṇā saha bhārgawa |
tato'nantaḥ samutthāya brahmaṇā paricoditaḥ ||6||

nārāyaṇena cāpyuktastasminkarmaṇi wīryawān ||6||

atha parwatarājānaṃ tamananto mahābalaḥ |
ujjahāra balādbrahmansawanaṃ sawanaukasam ||7||

tatastena surāḥ sārdhaṃ samudramupatasthire |
tamūcuramṛtārthāya nirmathiṣyāmahe jalam ||8||

apāmpatirathowāca mamāpyaṃśo bhawettataḥ |
soḍhāsmi wipulaṃ mardaṃ mandarabhramaṇāditi ||9||

ūcuśca kūrmarājānamakūpāraṃ surāsurāḥ |
gireradhiṣṭhānamasya bhawānbhawitumarhati ||10||

kūrmeṇa tu tathetyuktwā pṛṣṭhamasya samarpitam |
tasya śailasya cāgraṃ wai yantreṇendro'bhyapīḍayat ||11||

manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtwā tathā netraṃ ca wāsukim |
dewā mathitumārabdhāḥ samudraṃ nidhimambhasām ||12||

amṛtārthinastato brahmansahitā daityadānawāḥ ||12||

ekamantamupāśliṣṭā nāgarājño mahāsurāḥ |
wibudhāḥ sahitāḥ sarwe yataḥ pucchaṃ tataḥ sthitāḥ ||13||

ananto bhagawāndewo yato nārāyaṇastataḥ |
śira udyamya nāgasya punaḥ punarawākṣipat ||14||

wāsukeratha nāgasya sahasākṣipyataḥ suraiḥ |
sadhūmāḥ sārciṣo wātā niṣpeturasakṛnmukhāt ||15||

te dhūmasaṅghāḥ sambhūtā meghasaṅghāḥ sawidyutaḥ |
abhyawarṣansuragaṇāñśramasantāpakarśitān ||16||

tasmācca girikūṭāgrātpracyutāḥ puṣpawṛṣṭayaḥ |
surāsuragaṇānmālyaiḥ sarwataḥ samawākiran ||17||

babhūwātra mahāghoṣo mahāmegharawopamaḥ |
udadhermathyamānasya mandareṇa surāsuraiḥ ||18||

tatra nānājalacarā winiṣpiṣṭā mahādriṇā |
wilayaṃ samupājagmuḥ śataśo lawaṇāmbhasi ||19||

wāruṇāni ca bhūtāni wiwidhāni mahīdharaḥ |
pātālatalawāsīni wilayaṃ samupānayat ||20||

tasmiṃśca bhrāmyamāṇe'drau saṅghṛṣyantaḥ parasparam |
nyapatanpatagopetāḥ parwatāgrānmahādrumāḥ ||21||

teṣāṃ saṅgharṣajaścāgnirarcirbhiḥ prajwalanmuhuḥ |
widyudbhiriwa nīlābhramāwṛṇonmandaraṃ girim ||22||

dadāha kuñjarāṃścaiwa siṃhāṃścaiwa winiḥsṛtān |
wigatāsūni sarwāṇi sattwāni wiwidhāni ca ||23||

tamagnimamaraśreṣṭhaḥ pradahantaṃ tatastataḥ |
wāriṇā meghajenendraḥ śamayāmāsa sarwataḥ ||24||

tato nānāwidhāstatra susruwuḥ sāgarāmbhasi |
mahādrumāṇāṃ niryāsā bahawaścauṣadhīrasāḥ ||25||

teṣāmamṛtawīryāṇāṃ rasānāṃ payasaiwa ca |
amaratwaṃ surā jagmuḥ kāñcanasya ca niḥsrawāt ||26||

atha tasya samudrasya tajjātamudakaṃ payaḥ |
rasottamairwimiśraṃ ca tataḥ kṣīrādabhūdghṛtam ||27||

tato brahmāṇamāsīnaṃ dewā waradamabruwan |
śrāntāḥ sma subhṛśaṃ brahmannodbhawatyamṛtaṃ ca tat ||28||

ṛte nārāyaṇaṃ dewaṃ daityā nāgottamāstathā |
cirārabdhamidaṃ cāpi sāgarasyāpi manthanam ||29||

tato nārāyaṇaṃ dewaṃ brahmā wacanamabrawīt |
widhatswaiṣāṃ balaṃ wiṣṇo bhawānatra parāyaṇam ||30||

wiṣṇuruwāca||

balaṃ dadāmi sarweṣāṃ karmaitadye samāsthitāḥ |
kṣobhyatāṃ kalaśaḥ sarwairmandaraḥ pariwartyatām ||31||

sūta uwāca||

nārāyaṇawacaḥ śrutwā balinaste mahodadheḥ |
tatpayaḥ sahitā bhūyaścakrire bhṛśamākulam ||32||

tataḥ śatasahasrāṃśuḥ samāna iwa sāgarāt |
prasannabhāḥ samutpannaḥ somaḥ śītāṃśurujjwalaḥ ||33||

śrīranantaramutpannā ghṛtātpāṇḍurawāsinī |
surā dewī samutpannā turagaḥ pāṇḍurastathā ||34||

kaustubhaśca maṇirdiwya utpanno'mṛtasambhawaḥ |
marīciwikacaḥ śrīmānnārāyaṇa urogataḥ ||35||

śrīḥ surā caiwa somaśca turagaśca manojawaḥ |
yato dewāstato jagmurādityapathamāśritāḥ ||36||

dhanwantaristato dewo wapuṣmānudatiṣṭhata |
śwetaṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ bibhradamṛtaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati ||37||

etadatyadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭwā dānawānāṃ samutthitaḥ |
amṛtārthe mahānnādo mamedamiti jalpatām ||38||

tato nārāyaṇo māyāmāsthito mohinīṃ prabhuḥ |
strīrūpamadbhutaṃ kṛtwā dānawānabhisaṃśritaḥ ||39||

tatastadamṛtaṃ tasyai daduste mūḍhacetasaḥ |
striyai dānawadaiteyāḥ sarwe tadgatamānasāḥ ||40||






                  17


sūta uwāca||

athāwaraṇamukhyāni nānāpraharaṇāni ca |
pragṛhyābhyadrawandewānsahitā daityadānawāḥ ||1||

tatastadamṛtaṃ dewo wiṣṇurādāya wīryawān |
jahāra dānawendrebhyo nareṇa sahitaḥ prabhuḥ ||2||

tato dewagaṇāḥ sarwe papustadamṛtaṃ tadā |
wiṣṇoḥ sakāśātsamprāpya sambhrame tumule sati ||3||

tataḥ pibatsu tatkālaṃ deweṣwamṛtamīpsitam |
rāhurwibudharūpeṇa dānawaḥ prāpibattadā ||4||

tasya kaṇṭhamanuprāpte dānawasyāmṛte tadā |
ākhyātaṃ candrasūryābhyāṃ surāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā ||5||

tato bhagawatā tasya śiraśchinnamalaṅkṛtam |
cakrāyudhena cakreṇa pibato'mṛtamojasā ||6||

tacchailaśṛṅgapratimaṃ dānawasya śiro mahat |
cakreṇotkṛttamapataccālayadwasudhātalam ||7||

tato wairawinirbandhaḥ kṛto rāhumukhena wai |
śāśwataścandrasūryābhyāṃ grasatyadyāpi caiwa tau ||8||

wihāya bhagawāṃścāpi strīrūpamatulaṃ hariḥ |
nānāpraharaṇairbhīmairdānawānsamakampayat ||9||

tataḥ prawṛttaḥ saṅgrāmaḥ samīpe lawaṇāmbhasaḥ |
surāṇāmasurāṇāṃ ca sarwaghorataro mahān ||10||

prāsāḥ suwipulāstīkṣṇā nyapatanta sahasraśaḥ |
tomarāśca sutīkṣṇāgrāḥ śastrāṇi wiwidhāni ca ||11||

tato'surāścakrabhinnā wamanto rudhiraṃ bahu |
asiśaktigadārugṇā nipeturdharaṇītale ||12||

chinnāni paṭṭiśaiścāpi śirāṃsi yudhi dāruṇe |
taptakāñcanajālāni nipeturaniśaṃ tadā ||13||

rudhireṇāwaliptāṅgā nihatāśca mahāsurāḥ |
adrīṇāmiwa kūṭāni dhāturaktāni śerate ||14||

hāhākāraḥ samabhawattatra tatra sahasraśaḥ |
anyonyaṃ chindatāṃ śastrairāditye lohitāyati ||15||

parighaiścāyasaiḥ pītaiḥ saṃnikarṣe ca muṣṭibhiḥ |
nighnatāṃ samare'nyonyaṃ śabdo diwamiwāspṛśat ||16||

chindhi bhindhi pradhāwadhwaṃ pātayābhisareti ca |
wyaśrūyanta mahāghorāḥ śabdāstatra samantataḥ ||17||

ewaṃ sutumule yuddhe wartamāne bhayāwahe |
naranārāyaṇau dewau samājagmaturāhawam ||18||

tatra diwyaṃ dhanurdṛṣṭwā narasya bhagawānapi |
cintayāmāsa wai cakraṃ wiṣṇurdānawasūdanam ||19||

tato'mbarāccintitamātramāgataṃ; mahāprabhaṃ cakramamitratāpanam |
wibhāwasostulyamakuṇṭhamaṇḍalaṃ; sudarśanaṃ bhīmamajayyamuttamam ||20||

tadāgataṃ jwalitahutāśanaprabhaṃ; bhayaṅkaraṃ karikarabāhuracyutaḥ |
mumoca wai capalamudagrawegawa; nmahāprabhaṃ paranagarāwadāraṇam ||21||

tadantakajwalanasamānawarcasaṃ; punaḥ punarnyapatata wegawattadā |
widārayadditidanujānsahasraśaḥ; kareritaṃ puruṣawareṇa saṃyuge ||22||

dahatkwacijjwalana iwāwaleliha; tprasahya tānasuragaṇānnyakṛntata |
praweritaṃ wiyati muhuḥ kṣitau tadā; papau raṇe rudhiramatho piśācawat ||23||

athāsurā giribhiradīnacetaso; muhurmuhuḥ suragaṇamardayaṃstadā |
mahābalā wigalitameghawarcasaḥ; sahasraśo gaganamabhiprapadya ha ||24||

athāmbarādbhayajananāḥ prapedire; sapādapā bahuwidhamegharūpiṇaḥ |
mahādrayaḥ prawigalitāgrasānawaḥ; parasparaṃ drutamabhihatya saswanāḥ ||25||

tato mahī prawicalitā sakānanā; mahādripātābhihatā samantataḥ |
parasparaṃ bhṛśamabhigarjatāṃ muhū; raṇājire bhṛśamabhisamprawartite ||26||

narastato warakanakāgrabhūṣaṇai; rmaheṣubhirgaganapathaṃ samāwṛṇot |
widārayangiriśikharāṇi patribhi; rmahābhaye'suragaṇawigrahe tadā ||27||

tato mahīṃ lawaṇajalaṃ ca sāgaraṃ; mahāsurāḥ prawiwiśurarditāḥ suraiḥ |
wiyadgataṃ jwalitahutāśanaprabhaṃ; sudarśanaṃ parikupitaṃ niśāmya ca ||28||

tataḥ surairwijayamawāpya mandaraḥ; swamewa deśaṃ gamitaḥ supūjitaḥ |
winādya khaṃ diwamapi caiwa sarwaśa; stato gatāḥ saliladharā yathāgatam ||29||

tato'mṛtaṃ sunihitamewa cakrire; surāḥ parāṃ mudamabhigamya puṣkalām |
dadau ca taṃ nidhimamṛtasya rakṣituṃ; kirīṭine balabhidathāmaraiḥ saha ||30||






                  18


sūta uwāca||

etatte sarwamākhyātamamṛtaṃ mathitaṃ yathā |
yatra so'śwaḥ samutpannaḥ śrīmānatulawikramaḥ ||1||

yaṃ niśāmya tadā kadrūrwinatāmidamabrawīt |
uccaiḥśrawā nu kiṃwarṇo bhadre jānīhi māciram ||2||

winatowāca||

śweta ewāśwarājo'yaṃ kiṃ wā twaṃ manyase śubhe |
brūhi warṇaṃ twamapyasya tato'tra wipaṇāwahe ||3||

kadrūruwāca||

kṛṣṇawālamahaṃ manye hayamenaṃ śucismite |
ehi sārdhaṃ mayā dīwya dāsībhāwāya bhāmini ||4||

sūta uwāca||

ewaṃ te samayaṃ kṛtwā dāsībhāwāya wai mithaḥ |
jagmatuḥ swagṛhānewa śwo drakṣyāwa iti sma ha ||5||

tataḥ putrasahasraṃ tu kadrūrjihmaṃ cikīrṣatī |
ājñāpayāmāsa tadā wālā bhūtwāñjanaprabhāḥ ||6||

āwiśadhwaṃ hayaṃ kṣipraṃ dāsī na syāmahaṃ yathā |
tadwākyaṃ nānwapadyanta tāñśaśāpa bhujaṅgamān ||7||

sarpasatre wartamāne pāwako waḥ pradhakṣyati |
janamejayasya rājarṣeḥ pāṇḍaweyasya dhīmataḥ ||8||

śāpamenaṃ tu śuśrāwa swayamewa pitāmahaḥ |
atikrūraṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ kadrwā daiwādatīwa hi ||9||

sārdhaṃ dewagaṇaiḥ sarwairwācaṃ tāmanwamodata |
bahutwaṃ prekṣya sarpāṇāṃ prajānāṃ hitakāmyayā ||10||

tigmawīryawiṣā hyete dandaśūkā mahābalāḥ |
teṣāṃ tīkṣṇawiṣatwāddhi prajānāṃ ca hitāya wai ||11||

prādādwiṣahaṇīṃ widyāṃ kāśyapāya mahātmane ||11||






                  19


sūta uwāca||

tato rajanyāṃ wyuṣṭāyāṃ prabhāta udite rawau |
kadrūśca winatā caiwa bhaginyau te tapodhana ||1||

amarṣite susaṃrabdhe dāsye kṛtapaṇe tadā |
jagmatusturagaṃ draṣṭumucchaiḥśrawasamantikāt ||2||

dadṛśāte tadā tatra samudraṃ nidhimambhasām |
timiṅgilajhaṣākīrṇaṃ makarairāwṛtaṃ tathā ||3||

sattwaiśca bahusāhasrairnānārūpaiḥ samāwṛtam |
ugrairnityamanādhṛṣyaṃ kūrmagrāhasamākulam ||4||

ākaraṃ sarwaratnānāmālayaṃ waruṇasya ca |
nāgānāmālayaṃ ramyamuttamaṃ saritāṃ patim ||5||

pātālajwalanāwāsamasurāṇāṃ ca bandhanam |
bhayaṅkaraṃ ca sattwānāṃ payasāṃ nidhimarṇawam ||6||

śubhaṃ diwyamamartyānāmamṛtasyākaraṃ param |
aprameyamacintyaṃ ca supuṇyajalamadbhutam ||7||

ghoraṃ jalacarārāwaraudraṃ bhairawaniswanam |
gambhīrāwartakalilaṃ sarwabhūtabhayaṅkaram ||8||

welādolānilacalaṃ kṣobhodwegasamutthitam |
wīcīhastaiḥ pracalitairnṛtyantamiwa sarwaśaḥ ||9||

candrawṛddhikṣayawaśādudwṛttormidurāsadam |
pāñcajanyasya jananaṃ ratnākaramanuttamam ||10||

gāṃ windatā bhagawatā gowindenāmitaujasā |
warāharūpiṇā cāntarwikṣobhitajalāwilam ||11||

brahmarṣiṇā ca tapatā warṣāṇāṃ śatamatriṇā |
anāsāditagādhaṃ ca pātālatalamawyayam ||12||

adhyātmayoganidrāṃ ca padmanābhasya sewataḥ |
yugādikālaśayanaṃ wiṣṇoramitatejasaḥ ||13||

waḍawāmukhadīptāgnestoyahawyapradaṃ śubham |
agādhapāraṃ wistīrṇamaprameyaṃ saritpatim ||14||

mahānadībhirbahwībhiḥ spardhayewa sahasraśaḥ |
abhisāryamāṇamaniśaṃ dadṛśāte mahārṇawam ||15||

gambhīraṃ timimakarograsaṅkulaṃ taṃ; garjantaṃ jalacararāwaraudranādaiḥ |
wistīrṇaṃ dadṛśaturambaraprakāśaṃ; te'gādhaṃ nidhimurumambhasāmanantam ||16||

ityewaṃ jhaṣamakarormisaṅkulaṃ taṃ; gambhīraṃ wikasitamambaraprakāśam |
pātālajwalanaśikhāwidīpitaṃ taṃ; paśyantyau drutamabhipetatustadānīm ||17||






                  20


sūta uwāca||

taṃ samudramatikramya kadrūrwinatayā saha |
nyapatatturagābhyāśe nacirādiwa śīghragā ||1||

niśāmya ca bahūnwālānkṛṣṇānpucchaṃ samāśritān |
winatāṃ wiṣaṇṇawadanāṃ kadrūrdāsye nyayojayat ||2||

tataḥ sā winatā tasminpaṇitena parājitā |
abhawadduḥkhasantaptā dāsībhāwaṃ samāsthitā ||3||

etasminnantare caiwa garuḍaḥ kāla āgate |
winā mātrā mahātejā widāryāṇḍamajāyata ||4||

agnirāśiriwodbhāsansamiddho'tibhayaṅkaraḥ |
prawṛddhaḥ sahasā pakṣī mahākāyo nabhogataḥ ||5||

taṃ dṛṣṭwā śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ prajāḥ sarwā wibhāwasum |
praṇipatyābruwaṃścainamāsīnaṃ wiśwarūpiṇam ||6||

agne mā twaṃ prawardhiṣṭhāḥ kaccinno na didhakṣasi |
asau hi rāśiḥ sumahānsamiddhastawa sarpati ||7||

agniruwāca||

naitadewaṃ yathā yūyaṃ manyadhwamasurārdanāḥ |
garuḍo balawāneṣa mama tulyaḥ swatejasā ||8||

sūta uwāca||

ewamuktāstato gatwā garuḍaṃ wāgbhirastuwan |
adūrādabhyupetyainaṃ dewāḥ sarṣigaṇāstadā ||9||

twamṛṣistwaṃ mahābhāgastwaṃ dewaḥ patageśwaraḥ |
twaṃ prabhustapanaprakhyastwaṃ nastrāṇamanuttamam ||10||

balormimānsādhuradīnasattwaḥ; samṛddhimānduṣprasahastwamewa |
tapaḥ śrutaṃ sarwamahīnakīrte; anāgataṃ copagataṃ ca sarwam ||11||

twamuttamaḥ sarwamidaṃ carācaraṃ; gabhastibhirbhānuriwāwabhāsase |
samākṣipanbhānumataḥ prabhāṃ muhu; stwamantakaḥ sarwamidaṃ dhruwādhruwam ||12||

diwākaraḥ parikupito yathā dahe; tprajāstathā dahasi hutāśanaprabha |
bhayaṅkaraḥ pralaya iwāgnirutthito; wināśayanyugapariwartanāntakṛt ||13||

khageśwaraṃ śaraṇamupasthitā wayaṃ; mahaujasaṃ witimiramabhragocaram |
mahābalaṃ garuḍamupetya khecaraṃ; parāwaraṃ waradamajayyawikramam ||14||

ewaṃ stutaḥ suparṇastu dewaiḥ sarṣigaṇaistadā |
tejasaḥ pratisaṃhāramātmanaḥ sa cakāra ha ||15||






                  21


sūta uwāca||

tataḥ kāmagamaḥ pakṣī mahāwīryo mahābalaḥ |
māturantikamāgacchatparaṃ tīraṃ mahodadheḥ ||1||

yatra sā winatā tasminpaṇitena parājitā |
atīwa duḥkhasantaptā dāsībhāwamupāgatā ||2||

tataḥ kadācidwinatāṃ prawaṇāṃ putrasaṃnidhau |
kāla āhūya wacanaṃ kadrūridamabhāṣata ||3||

nāgānāmālayaṃ bhadre suramyaṃ ramaṇīyakam |
samudrakukṣāwekānte tatra māṃ winate waha ||4||

tataḥ suparṇamātā tāmawahatsarpamātaram |
pannagāngaruḍaścāpi māturwacanacoditaḥ ||5||

sa sūryasyābhito yāti wainateyo wihaṅgamaḥ |
sūryaraśmiparītāśca mūrcchitāḥ pannagābhawan ||6||

tadawasthānsutāndṛṣṭwā kadrūḥ śakramathāstuwat ||6||

namaste dewadeweśa namaste balasūdana |
namucighna namaste'stu sahasrākṣa śacīpate ||7||

sarpāṇāṃ sūryataptānāṃ wāriṇā twaṃ plawo bhawa |
twamewa paramaṃ trāṇamasmākamamarottama ||8||

īśo hyasi payaḥ sraṣṭuṃ twamanalpaṃ puraṃdara |
twamewa meghastwaṃ wāyustwamagnirwaidyuto'mbare ||9||

twamabhraghanawikṣeptā twāmewāhuḥ punarghanam |
twaṃ wajramatulaṃ ghoraṃ ghoṣawāṃstwaṃ balāhakaḥ ||10||

sraṣṭā twamewa lokānāṃ saṃhartā cāparājitaḥ |
twaṃ jyotiḥ sarwabhūtānāṃ twamādityo wibhāwasuḥ ||11||

twaṃ mahadbhūtamāścaryaṃ twaṃ rājā twaṃ surottamaḥ |
twaṃ wiṣṇustwaṃ sahasrākṣastwaṃ dewastwaṃ parāyaṇam ||12||

twaṃ sarwamamṛtaṃ dewa twaṃ somaḥ paramārcitaḥ |
twaṃ muhūrtastithiśca twaṃ lawastwaṃ wai punaḥ kṣaṇaḥ ||13||

śuklastwaṃ bahulaścaiwa kalā kāṣṭhā truṭistathā |
saṃwatsarartawo māsā rajanyaśca dināni ca ||14||

twamuttamā sagiriwanā wasundharā; sabhāskaraṃ witimiramambaraṃ tathā |
mahodadhiḥ satimitimiṅgilastathā; mahormimānbahumakaro jhaṣālayaḥ ||15||

mahadyaśastwamiti sadābhipūjyase; manīṣibhirmuditamanā maharṣibhiḥ |
abhiṣṭutaḥ pibasi ca somamadhware; waṣaṭkṛtānyapi ca hawīṃṣi bhūtaye ||16||

twaṃ wipraiḥ satatamihejyase phalārthaṃ; wedāṅgeṣwatulabalaugha gīyase ca |
twaddhetoryajanaparāyaṇā dwijendrā; wedāṅgānyabhigamayanti sarwawedaiḥ ||17||






                  22


sūta uwāca||

ewaṃ stutastadā kadrwā bhagawānhariwāhanaḥ |
nīlajīmūtasaṅghātairwyoma sarwaṃ samāwṛṇot ||1||

te meghā mumucustoyaṃ prabhūtaṃ widyudujjwalāḥ |
parasparamiwātyarthaṃ garjantaḥ satataṃ diwi ||2||

saṅghātitamiwākāśaṃ jaladaiḥ sumahādbhutaiḥ |
sṛjadbhiratulaṃ toyamajasraṃ sumahārawaiḥ ||3||

sampranṛttamiwākāśaṃ dhārormibhiranekaśaḥ |
meghastanitanirghoṣamambaraṃ samapadyata ||4||

nāgānāmuttamo harśastadā warṣati wāsawe |
āpūryata mahī cāpi salilena samantataḥ ||5||






                  23


sūta uwāca||

suparṇenohyamānāste jagmustaṃ deśamāśu wai |
sāgarāmbuparikṣiptaṃ pakṣisaṅghanināditam ||1||

wicitraphalapuṣpābhirwanarājibhirāwṛtam |
bhawanairāwṛtaṃ ramyaistathā padmākarairapi ||2||

prasannasalilaiścāpi hradaiścitrairwibhūṣitam |
diwyagandhawahaiḥ puṇyairmārutairupawījitam ||3||

upajighradbhirākāśaṃ wṛkṣairmalayajairapi |
śobhitaṃ puṣpawarṣāṇi muñcadbhirmārutoddhutaiḥ ||4||

kiradbhiriwa tatrasthānnāgānpuṣpāmbuwṛṣṭibhiḥ |
manaḥsaṃharṣaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ gandharwāpsarasāṃ priyam ||5||

nānāpakṣirutaṃ ramyaṃ kadrūputrapraharṣaṇam ||5||

tatte wanaṃ samāsādya wijahruḥ pannagā mudā |
abruwaṃśca mahāwīryaṃ suparṇaṃ patagottamam ||6||

wahāsmānaparaṃ dwīpaṃ suramyaṃ wipulodakam |
twaṃ hi deśānbahūnramyānpatanpaśyasi khecara ||7||

sa wicintyābrawītpakṣī mātaraṃ winatāṃ tadā |
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ mayā mātaḥ kartawyaṃ sarpabhāṣitam ||8||

winatowāca||

dāsībhūtāsmyanāryāyā bhaginyāḥ patagottama |
paṇaṃ witathamāsthāya sarpairupadhinā kṛtam ||9||

sūta uwāca||

tasmiṃstu kathite mātrā kāraṇe gaganecaraḥ |
uwāca wacanaṃ sarpāṃstena duḥkhena duḥkhitaḥ ||10||

kimāhṛtya widitwā wā kiṃ wā kṛtweha pauruṣam |
dāsyādwo wipramucyeyaṃ satyaṃ śaṃsata lelihāḥ ||11||

śrutwā tamabruwansarpā āharāmṛtamojasā |
tato dāsyādwipramokṣo bhawitā tawa khecara ||12||






                  24


sūta uwāca||

ityukto garuḍaḥ sarpaistato mātaramabrawīt |
gacchāmyamṛtamāhartuṃ bhakṣyamicchāmi weditum ||1||

winatowāca||

samudrakukṣāwekānte niṣādālayamuttamam |
sahasrāṇāmanekānāṃ tānbhuktwāmṛtamānaya ||2||

na tu te brāhmaṇaṃ hantuṃ kāryā buddhiḥ kathañcana |
awadhyaḥ sarwabhūtānāṃ brāhmaṇo hyanalopamaḥ ||3||

agnirarko wiṣaṃ śastraṃ wipro bhawati kopitaḥ |
bhūtānāmagrabhugwipro warṇaśreṣṭhaḥ pitā guruḥ ||4||

garuḍa uwāca||

yathāhamabhijānīyāṃ brāhmaṇaṃ lakṣaṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ |
tanme kāraṇato mātaḥ pṛcchato waktumarhasi ||5||

winatowāca||

yaste kaṇṭhamanuprāpto nigīrṇaṃ baḍiśaṃ yathā |
dahedaṅgārawatputra taṃ widyādbāhmaṇarṣabham ||6||

sūta uwāca||

prowāca cainaṃ winatā putrahārdādidaṃ wacaḥ |
jānantyapyatulaṃ wīryamāśīrwādasamanwitam ||7||

pakṣau te mārutaḥ pātu candraḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ tu putraka |
śirastu pātu te wahnirbhāskaraḥ sarwamewa tu ||8||

ahaṃ ca te sadā putra śāntiswastiparāyaṇā |
ariṣṭaṃ wraja panthānaṃ watsa kāryārthasiddhaye ||9||

tataḥ sa māturwacanaṃ niśamya; witatya pakṣau nabha utpapāta |
tato niṣādānbalawānupāgama; dbubhukṣitaḥ kāla iwāntako mahān ||10||

sa tānniṣādānupasaṃharaṃstadā; rajaḥ samuddhūya nabhaḥspṛśaṃ mahat |
samudrakukṣau ca wiśoṣayanpayaḥ; samīpagānbhūmidharānwicālayan ||11||

tataḥ sa cakre mahadānanaṃ tadā; niṣādamārgaṃ pratirudhya pakṣirāṭ |
tato niṣādāstwaritāḥ prawawraju; ryato mukhaṃ tasya bhujaṅgabhojinaḥ ||12||

tadānanaṃ wiwṛtamatipramāṇawa; tsamabhyayurgaganamiwārditāḥ khagāḥ |
sahasraśaḥ pawanarajobhramohitā; mahānilapracalitapādape wane ||13||

tataḥ khago wadanamamitratāpanaḥ; samāharatparicapalo mahābalaḥ |
niṣūdayanbahuwidhamatsyabhakṣiṇo; bubhukṣito gaganacareśwarastadā ||14||






                  25


sūta uwāca||

tasya kaṇṭhamanuprāpto brāhmaṇaḥ saha bhāryayā |
dahandīpta iwāṅgārastamuwācāntarikṣagaḥ ||1||

dwijottama winirgaccha tūrṇamāsyādapāwṛtāt |
na hi me brāhmaṇo wadhyaḥ pāpeṣwapi rataḥ sadā ||2||

bruwāṇamewaṃ garuḍaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ samabhāṣata |
niṣādī mama bhāryeyaṃ nirgacchatu mayā saha ||3||

garuḍa uwāca||

etāmapi niṣādīṃ twaṃ parigṛhyāśu niṣpata |
tūrṇaṃ sambhāwayātmānamajīrṇaṃ mama tejasā ||4||

sūta uwāca||

tataḥ sa wipro niṣkrānto niṣādīsahitastadā |
wardhayitwā ca garuḍamiṣṭaṃ deśaṃ jagāma ha ||5||

sahabhārye winiṣkrānte tasminwipre sa pakṣirāṭ |
witatya pakṣāwākāśamutpapāta manojawaḥ ||6||

tato'paśyatsa pitaraṃ pṛṣṭaścākhyātawānpituḥ |
ahaṃ hi sarpaiḥ prahitaḥ somamāhartumudyataḥ ||7||

māturdāsyawimokṣārthamāhariṣye tamadya wai ||7||

mātrā cāsmi samādiṣṭo niṣādānbhakṣayeti wai |
na ca me tṛptirabhawadbhakṣayitwā sahasraśaḥ ||8||

tasmādbhoktawyamaparaṃ bhagawanpradiśaswa me |
yadbhuktwāmṛtamāhartuṃ samarthaḥ syāmahaṃ prabho ||9||

kaśyapa uwāca||

āsīdwibhāwasurnāma maharṣiḥ kopano bhṛśam |
bhrātā tasyānujaścāsītsupratīko mahātapāḥ ||10||

sa necchati dhanaṃ bhrātrā sahaikasthaṃ mahāmuniḥ |
wibhāgaṃ kīrtayatyewa supratīko'tha nityaśaḥ ||11||

athābrawīcca taṃ bhrātā supratīkaṃ wibhāwasuḥ |
wibhāgaṃ bahawo mohātkartumicchanti nityadā ||12||

tato wibhaktā anyonyaṃ nādriyante'rthamohitāḥ ||12||

tataḥ swārthaparānmūḍhānpṛthagbhūtānswakairdhanaiḥ |
widitwā bhedayantyetānamitrā mitrarūpiṇaḥ ||13||

widitwā cāpare bhinnānantareṣu patantyatha |
bhinnānāmatulo nāśaḥ kṣipramewa prawartate ||14||

tasmāccaiwa wibhāgārthaṃ na praśaṃsanti paṇḍitāḥ |
guruśāstre nibaddhānāmanyonyamabhiśaṅkinām ||15||

niyantuṃ na hi śakyastwaṃ bhedato dhanamicchasi |
yasmāttasmātsupratīka hastitwaṃ samawāpsyasi ||16||

śaptastwewaṃ supratīko wibhāwasumathābrawīt |
twamapyantarjalacaraḥ kacchapaḥ sambhawiṣyasi ||17||

ewamanyonyaśāpāttau supratīkawibhāwasū |
gajakacchapatāṃ prāptāwarthārthaṃ mūḍhacetasau ||18||

roṣadoṣānuṣaṅgeṇa tiryagyonigatāwapi |
parasparadweṣaratau pramāṇabaladarpitau ||19||

sarasyasminmahākāyau pūrwawairānusāriṇau |
tayorekataraḥ śrīmānsamupaiti mahāgajaḥ ||20||

tasya bṛṃhitaśabdena kūrmo'pyantarjaleśayaḥ |
utthito'sau mahākāyaḥ kṛtsnaṃ saṅkṣobhayansaraḥ ||21||

taṃ dṛṣṭwāweṣṭitakaraḥ patatyeṣa gajo jalam |
dantahastāgralāṅgūlapādawegena wīryawān ||22||

taṃ wikṣobhayamāṇaṃ tu saro bahujhaṣākulam |
kūrmo'pyabhyudyataśirā yuddhāyābhyeti wīryawān ||23||

ṣaḍucchrito yojanāni gajastaddwiguṇāyataḥ |
kūrmastriyojanotsedho daśayojanamaṇḍalaḥ ||24||

tāwetau yuddhasaṃmattau parasparajayaiṣiṇau |
upayujyāśu karmedaṃ sādhayepsitamātmanaḥ ||25||

sūta uwāca||

sa tacchrutwā piturwākyaṃ bhīmawego'ntarikṣagaḥ |
nakhena gajamekena kūrmamekena cākṣipat ||26||

samutpapāta cākāśaṃ tata uccairwihaṅgamaḥ |
so'lambatīrthamāsādya dewawṛkṣānupāgamat ||27||

te bhītāḥ samakampanta tasya pakṣānilāhatāḥ |
na no bhañjyāditi tadā diwyāḥ kanakaśākhinaḥ ||28||

pracalāṅgānsa tāndṛṣṭwā manorathaphalāṅkurān |
anyānatularūpāṅgānupacakrāma khecaraḥ ||29||

kāñcanai rājataiścaiwa phalairwaiḍūryaśākhinaḥ |
sāgarāmbuparikṣiptānbhrājamānānmahādrumān ||30||

tamuwāca khagaśreṣṭhaṃ tatra rohiṇapādapaḥ |
atiprawṛddhaḥ sumahānāpatantaṃ manojawam ||31||

yaiṣā mama mahāśākhā śatayojanamāyatā |
etāmāsthāya śākhāṃ twaṃ khādemau gajakacchapau ||32||

tato drumaṃ patagasahasrasewitaṃ; mahīdharapratimawapuḥ prakampayan |
khagottamo drutamabhipatya wegawā; nbabhañja tāmawiralapatrasaṃwṛtām ||33||






                  26


sūta uwāca||

spṛṣṭamātrā tu padbhyāṃ sā garuḍena balīyasā |
abhajyata taroḥ śākhā bhagnāṃ caināmadhārayat ||1||

tāṃ bhagnāṃ sa mahāśākhāṃ smayansamawalokayan |
athātra lambato'paśyadwālakhilyānadhomukhān ||2||

sa tadwināśasantrāsādanupatya khagādhipaḥ |
śākhāmāsyena jagrāha teṣāmewānwawekṣayā ||3||

śanaiḥ paryapatatpakṣī parwatānprawiśātayan ||3||

ewaṃ so'bhyapataddeśānbahūnsagajakacchapaḥ |
dayārthaṃ wālakhilyānāṃ na ca sthānamawindata ||4||

sa gatwā parwataśreṣṭhaṃ gandhamādanamawyayam |
dadarśa kaśyapaṃ tatra pitaraṃ tapasi sthitam ||5||

dadarśa taṃ pitā cāpi diwyarūpaṃ wihaṅgamam |
tejowīryabalopetaṃ manomārutaraṃhasam ||6||

śailaśṛṅgapratīkāśaṃ brahmadaṇḍamiwodyatam |
acintyamanabhijñeyaṃ sarwabhūtabhayaṅkaram ||7||

māyāwīryadharaṃ sākṣādagnimiddhamiwodyatam |
apradhṛṣyamajeyaṃ ca dewadānawarākṣasaiḥ ||8||

bhettāraṃ giriśṛṅgāṇāṃ nadījalawiśoṣaṇam |
lokasaṃloḍanaṃ ghoraṃ kṛtāntasamadarśanam ||9||

tamāgatamabhiprekṣya bhagawānkaśyapastadā |
widitwā cāsya saṅkalpamidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||10||

putra mā sāhasaṃ kārṣīrmā sadyo lapsyase wyathām |
mā twā daheyuḥ saṅkruddhā wālakhilyā marīcipāḥ ||11||

prasādayāmāsa sa tānkaśyapaḥ putrakāraṇāt |
wālakhilyāṃstapaḥsiddhānidamuddiśya kāraṇam ||12||

prajāhitārthamārambho garuḍasya tapodhanāḥ |
cikīrṣati mahatkarma tadanujñātumarhatha ||13||

ewamuktā bhagawatā munayaste samabhyayuḥ |
muktwā śākhāṃ giriṃ puṇyaṃ himawantaṃ taporthinaḥ ||14||

tatasteṣwapayāteṣu pitaraṃ winatātmajaḥ |
śākhāwyākṣiptawadanaḥ paryapṛcchata kaśyapam ||15||

bhagawankwa wimuñcāmi taruśākhāmimāmaham |
warjitaṃ brāhmaṇairdeśamākhyātu bhagawānmama ||16||

tato niṣpuruṣaṃ śailaṃ himasaṃruddhakandaram |
agamyaṃ manasāpyanyaistasyācakhyau sa kaśyapaḥ ||17||

taṃ parwatamahākukṣimāwiśya manasā khagaḥ |
jawenābhyapatattārkṣyaḥ saśākhāgajakacchapaḥ ||18||

na tāṃ wadhraḥ pariṇahecchatacarmā mahānaṇuḥ |
śākhino mahatīṃ śākhāṃ yāṃ pragṛhya yayau khagaḥ ||19||

tataḥ sa śatasāhasraṃ yojanāntaramāgataḥ |
kālena nātimahatā garuḍaḥ patatāṃ waraḥ ||20||

sa taṃ gatwā kṣaṇenaiwa parwataṃ wacanātpituḥ |
amuñcanmahatīṃ śākhāṃ saswanāṃ tatra khecaraḥ ||21||

pakṣānilahataścāsya prākampata sa śailarāṭ |
mumoca puṣpawarṣaṃ ca samāgalitapādapaḥ ||22||

śṛṅgāṇi ca wyaśīryanta girestasya samantataḥ |
maṇikāñcanacitrāṇi śobhayanti mahāgirim ||23||

śākhino bahawaścāpi śākhayābhihatāstayā |
kāñcanaiḥ kusumairbhānti widyutwanta iwāmbudāḥ ||24||

te hemawikacā bhūyo yuktāḥ parwatadhātubhiḥ |
wyarājañśākhinastatra sūryāṃśupratirañjitāḥ ||25||

tatastasya gireḥ śṛṅgamāsthāya sa khagottamaḥ |
bhakṣayāmāsa garuḍastāwubhau gajakacchapau ||26||

tataḥ parwatakūṭāgrādutpapāta manojawaḥ |
prāwartantātha dewānāmutpātā bhayawedinaḥ ||27||

indrasya wajraṃ dayitaṃ prajajwāla wyathānwitam |
sadhūmā cāpatatsārcirdiwolkā nabhasaścyutā ||28||

tathā wasūnāṃ rudrāṇāmādityānāṃ ca sarwaśaḥ |
sādhyānāṃ marutāṃ caiwa ye cānye dewatāgaṇāḥ ||29||

swaṃ swaṃ praharaṇaṃ teṣāṃ parasparamupādrawat ||29||

abhūtapūrwaṃ saṅgrāme tadā dewāsure'pi ca |
wawurwātāḥ sanirghātāḥ peturulkāḥ samantataḥ ||30||

nirabhramapi cākāśaṃ prajagarja mahāswanam |
dewānāmapi yo dewaḥ so'pyawarṣadasṛktadā ||31||

mamlurmālyāni dewānāṃ śemustejāṃsi caiwa hi |
utpātameghā raudrāśca wawarṣuḥ śoṇitaṃ bahu ||32||

rajāṃsi mukuṭānyeṣāmutthitāni wyadharṣayan ||32||

tatastrāsasamudwignaḥ saha dewaiḥ śatakratuḥ |
utpātāndāruṇānpaśyannityuwāca bṛhaspatim ||33||

kimarthaṃ bhagawanghorā mahotpātāḥ samutthitāḥ |
na ca śatruṃ prapaśyāmi yudhi yo naḥ pradharṣayet ||34||

bṛhaspatiruwāca||

tawāparādhāddewendra pramādācca śatakrato |
tapasā wālakhilyānāṃ bhūtamutpannamadbhutam ||35||

kaśyapasya muneḥ putro winatāyāśca khecaraḥ |
hartuṃ somamanuprāpto balawānkāmarūpawān ||36||

samartho balināṃ śreṣṭho hartuṃ somaṃ wihaṅgamaḥ |
sarwaṃ sambhāwayāmyasminnasādhyamapi sādhayet ||37||

sūta uwāca||

śrutwaitadwacanaṃ śakraḥ prowācāmṛtarakṣiṇaḥ |
mahāwīryabalaḥ pakṣī hartuṃ somamihodyataḥ ||38||

yuṣmānsambodhayāmyeṣa yathā sa na haredbalāt |
atulaṃ hi balaṃ tasya bṛhaspatiruwāca me ||39||

tacchrutwā wibudhā wākyaṃ wismitā yatnamāsthitāḥ |
pariwāryāmṛtaṃ tasthurwajrī cendraḥ śatakratuḥ ||40||

dhārayanto mahārhāṇi kawacāni manaswinaḥ |
kāñcanāni wicitrāṇi waiḍūryawikṛtāni ca ||41||

wiwidhāni ca śastrāṇi ghorarūpāṇyanekaśaḥ |
śitatīkṣṇāgradhārāṇi samudyamya sahasraśaḥ ||42||

sawisphuliṅgajwālāni sadhūmāni ca sarwaśaḥ |
cakrāṇi parighāṃścaiwa triśūlāni paraśwadhān ||43||

śaktīśca wiwidhāstīkṣṇāḥ karawālāṃśca nirmalān |
swadeharūpāṇyādāya gadāścograpradarśanāḥ ||44||

taiḥ śastrairbhānumadbhiste diwyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ |
bhānumantaḥ suragaṇāstasthurwigatakalmaṣāḥ ||45||

anupamabalawīryatejaso; dhṛtamanasaḥ parirakṣaṇe'mṛtasya |
asurapurawidāraṇāḥ surā; jwalanasamiddhawapuḥprakāśinaḥ ||46||

iti samarawaraṃ surāsthitaṃ; parighasahasraśataiḥ samākulam |
wigalitamiwa cāmbarāntare; tapanamarīciwibhāsitaṃ babhau ||47||






                  27


śaunaka uwāca||

ko'parādho mahendrasya kaḥ pramādaśca sūtaja |
tapasā wālakhilyānāṃ sambhūto garuḍaḥ katham ||1||

kaśyapasya dwijāteśca kathaṃ wai pakṣirāṭsutaḥ |
adhṛṣyaḥ sarwabhūtānāmawadhyaścābhawatkatham ||2||

kathaṃ ca kāmacārī sa kāmawīryaśca khecaraḥ |
etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ purāṇe yadi paṭhyate ||3||

sūta uwāca||

wiṣayo'yaṃ purāṇasya yanmāṃ twaṃ paripṛcchasi |
śṛṇu me wadataḥ sarwametatsaṅkṣepato dwija ||4||

yajataḥ putrakāmasya kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ |
sāhāyyamṛṣayo dewā gandharwāśca daduḥ kila ||5||

tatredhmānayane śakro niyuktaḥ kaśyapena ha |
munayo wālakhilyāśca ye cānye dewatāgaṇāḥ ||6||

śakrastu wīryasadṛśamidhmabhāraṃ giriprabham |
samudyamyānayāmāsa nātikṛcchrādiwa prabhuḥ ||7||

athāpaśyadṛṣīnhraswānaṅguṣṭhodaraparwaṇaḥ |
palāśawṛntikāmekāṃ sahitānwahataḥ pathi ||8||

pralīnānsweṣwiwāṅgeṣu nirāhārāṃstapodhanān |
kliśyamānānmandabalāngoṣpade samplutodake ||9||

tāṃśca sarwānsmayāwiṣṭo wīryonmattaḥ puraṃdaraḥ |
awahasyātyagācchīghraṃ laṅghayitwāwamanya ca ||10||

te'tha roṣasamāwiṣṭāḥ subhṛśaṃ jātamanyawaḥ |
ārebhire mahatkarma tadā śakrabhayaṅkaram ||11||

juhuwuste sutapaso widhiwajjātawedasam |
mantrairuccāwacairwiprā yena kāmena tacchṛṇu ||12||

kāmawīryaḥ kāmagamo dewarājabhayapradaḥ |
indro'nyaḥ sarwadewānāṃ bhawediti yatawratāḥ ||13||

indrācchataguṇaḥ śaurye wīrye caiwa manojawaḥ |
tapaso naḥ phalenādya dāruṇaḥ sambhawatwiti ||14||

tadbuddhwā bhṛśasantapto dewarājaḥ śatakratuḥ |
jagāma śaraṇaṃ tatra kaśyapaṃ saṃśitawratam ||15||

tacchrutwā dewarājasya kaśyapo'tha prajāpatiḥ |
wālakhilyānupāgamya karmasiddhimapṛcchata ||16||

ewamastwiti taṃ cāpi pratyūcuḥ satyawādinaḥ |
tānkaśyapa uwācedaṃ sāntwapūrwaṃ prajāpatiḥ ||17||

ayamindrastribhuwane niyogādbrahmaṇaḥ kṛtaḥ |
indrārthaṃ ca bhawanto'pi yatnawantastapodhanāḥ ||18||

na mithyā brahmaṇo wākyaṃ kartumarhatha sattamāḥ |
bhawatāṃ ca na mithyāyaṃ saṅkalpo me cikīrṣitaḥ ||19||

bhawatweṣa patatrīṇāmindro'tibalasattwawān |
prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ caiwa dewarājasya yācataḥ ||20||

ewamuktāḥ kaśyapena wālakhilyāstapodhanāḥ |
pratyūcurabhisampūjya muniśreṣṭhaṃ prajāpatim ||21||

indrārtho'yaṃ samārambhaḥ sarweṣāṃ naḥ prajāpate |
apatyārthaṃ samārambho bhawataścāyamīpsitaḥ ||22||

tadidaṃ saphalaṃ karma twayā wai pratigṛhyatām |
tathā caiwa widhatswātra yathā śreyo'nupaśyasi ||23||

etasminnewa kāle tu dewī dākṣāyaṇī śubhā |
winatā nāma kalyāṇī putrakāmā yaśaswinī ||24||

tapastaptwā wrataparā snātā puṃsawane śuciḥ |
upacakrāma bhartāraṃ tāmuwācātha kaśyapaḥ ||25||

ārambhaḥ saphalo dewi bhawitāyaṃ tawepsitaḥ |
janayiṣyasi putrau dwau wīrau tribhuwaneśwarau ||26||

tapasā wālakhilyānāṃ mama saṅkalpajau tathā |
bhawiṣyato mahābhāgau putrau te lokapūjitau ||27||

uwāca caināṃ bhagawānmārīcaḥ punarewa ha |
dhāryatāmapramādena garbho'yaṃ sumahodayaḥ ||28||

ekaḥ sarwapatatrīṇāmindratwaṃ kārayiṣyati |
lokasambhāwito wīraḥ kāmawīryo wihaṅgamaḥ ||29||

śatakratumathowāca prīyamāṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ |
twatsahāyau khagāwetau bhrātarau te bhawiṣyataḥ ||30||

naitābhyāṃ bhawitā doṣaḥ sakāśātte puraṃdara |
wyetu te śakra santāpastwamewendro bhawiṣyasi ||31||

na cāpyewaṃ twayā bhūyaḥ kṣeptawyā brahmawādinaḥ |
na cāwamānyā darpātte wāgwiṣā bhṛśakopanāḥ ||32||

ewamukto jagāmendro nirwiśaṅkastriwiṣṭapam |
winatā cāpi siddhārthā babhūwa muditā tadā ||33||

janayāmāsa putrau dwāwaruṇaṃ garuḍaṃ tathā |
aruṇastayostu wikala ādityasya puraḥsaraḥ ||34||

patatrīṇāṃ tu garuḍa indratwenābhyaṣicyata |
tasyaitatkarma sumahacchrūyatāṃ bhṛgunandana ||35||






                  28


sūta uwāca||

tatastasmindwijaśreṣṭha samudīrṇe tathāwidhe |
garutmānpakṣirāṭtūrṇaṃ samprāpto wibudhānprati ||1||

taṃ dṛṣṭwātibalaṃ caiwa prākampanta samantataḥ |
parasparaṃ ca pratyaghnansarwapraharaṇānyapi ||2||

tatra cāsīdameyātmā widyudagnisamaprabhaḥ |
bhauwanaḥ sumahāwīryaḥ somasya parirakṣitā ||3||

sa tena patagendreṇa pakṣatuṇḍanakhaiḥ kṣataḥ |
muhūrtamatulaṃ yuddhaṃ kṛtwā winihato yudhi ||4||

rajaścoddhūya sumahatpakṣawātena khecaraḥ |
kṛtwā lokānnirālokāṃstena dewānawākirat ||5||

tenāwakīrṇā rajasā dewā mohamupāgaman |
na cainaṃ dadṛśuśchannā rajasāmṛtarakṣiṇaḥ ||6||

ewaṃ saṃloḍayāmāsa garuḍastridiwālayam |
pakṣatuṇḍaprahāraiśca dewānsa widadāra ha ||7||

tato dewaḥ sahasrākṣastūrṇaṃ wāyumacodayat |
wikṣipemāṃ rajowṛṣṭiṃ tawaitatkarma māruta ||8||

atha wāyurapowāha tadrajastarasā balī |
tato witimire jāte dewāḥ śakunimārdayan ||9||

nanāda coccairbalawānmahāmegharawaḥ khagaḥ |
wadhyamānaḥ suragaṇaiḥ sarwabhūtāni bhīṣayan ||10||

utpapāta mahāwīryaḥ pakṣirāṭparawīrahā ||10||

tamutpatyāntarikṣasthaṃ dewānāmupari sthitam |
warmiṇo wibudhāḥ sarwe nānāśastrairawākiran ||11||

paṭṭiśaiḥ parighaiḥ śūlairgadābhiśca sawāsawāḥ |
kṣurāntairjwalitaiścāpi cakrairādityarūpibhiḥ ||12||

nānāśastrawisargaiśca wadhyamānaḥ samantataḥ |
kurwansutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ pakṣirāṇna wyakampata ||13||

winardanniwa cākāśe wainateyaḥ pratāpawān |
pakṣābhyāmurasā caiwa samantādwyākṣipatsurān ||14||

te wikṣiptāstato dewāḥ prajagmurgaruḍārditāḥ |
nakhatuṇḍakṣatāścaiwa susruwuḥ śoṇitaṃ bahu ||15||

sādhyāḥ prācīṃ sagandharwā wasawo dakṣiṇāṃ diśam |
prajagmuḥ sahitā rudraiḥ patagendrapradharṣitāḥ ||16||

diśaṃ pratīcīmādityā nāsatyā uttarāṃ diśam |
muhurmuhuḥ prekṣamāṇā yudhyamānā mahaujasam ||17||

aśwakrandena wīreṇa reṇukena ca pakṣiṇā |
krathanena ca śūreṇa tapanena ca khecaraḥ ||18||

ulūkaśwasanābhyāṃ ca nimeṣeṇa ca pakṣiṇā |
prarujena ca saṃyuddhaṃ cakāra pralihena ca ||19||

tānpakṣanakhatuṇḍāgrairabhinadwinatāsutaḥ |
yugāntakāle saṅkruddhaḥ pinākīwa mahābalaḥ ||20||

mahāwīryā mahotsāhāstena te bahudhā kṣatāḥ |
rejurabhraghanaprakhyā rudhiraughaprawarṣiṇaḥ ||21||

tānkṛtwā patagaśreṣṭhaḥ sarwānutkrāntajīwitān |
atikrānto'mṛtasyārthe sarwato'gnimapaśyata ||22||

āwṛṇwānaṃ mahājwālamarcirbhiḥ sarwato'mbaram |
dahantamiwa tīkṣṇāṃśuṃ ghoraṃ wāyusamīritam ||23||

tato nawatyā nawatīrmukhānāṃ; kṛtwā taraswī garuḍo mahātmā |
nadīḥ samāpīya mukhaistatastaiḥ; suśīghramāgamya punarjawena ||24||

jwalantamagniṃ tamamitratāpanaḥ; samāstaratpatraratho nadībhiḥ |
tataḥ pracakre wapuranyadalpaṃ; praweṣṭukāmo'gnimabhipraśāmya ||25||






                  29


sūta uwāca||

jāmbūnadamayo bhūtwā marīciwikacojjwalaḥ |
prawiweśa balātpakṣī wāriwega iwārṇawam ||1||

sa cakraṃ kṣuraparyantamapaśyadamṛtāntike |
paribhramantamaniśaṃ tīkṣṇadhāramayasmayam ||2||

jwalanārkaprabhaṃ ghoraṃ chedanaṃ somahāriṇām |
ghorarūpaṃ tadatyarthaṃ yantraṃ dewaiḥ sunirmitam ||3||

tasyāntaraṃ sa dṛṣṭwaiwa paryawartata khecaraḥ |
arāntareṇābhyapatatsaṅkṣipyāṅgaṃ kṣaṇena ha ||4||

adhaścakrasya caiwātra dīptānalasamadyutī |
widyujjihwau mahāghorau dīptāsyau dīptalocanau ||5||

cakṣurwiṣau mahāwīryau nityakruddhau taraswinau |
rakṣārthamewāmṛtasya dadarśa bhujagottamau ||6||

sadā saṃrabdhanayanau sadā cānimiṣekṣaṇau |
tayoreko'pi yaṃ paśyetsa tūrṇaṃ bhasmasādbhawet ||7||

tayoścakṣūṃṣi rajasā suparṇastūrṇamāwṛṇot |
adṛṣṭarūpastau cāpi sarwataḥ paryakālayat ||8||

tayoraṅge samākramya wainateyo'ntarikṣagaḥ |
ācchinattarasā madhye somamabhyadrawattataḥ ||9||

samutpāṭyāmṛtaṃ tattu wainateyastato balī |
utpapāta jawenaiwa yantramunmathya wīryawān ||10||

apītwaiwāmṛtaṃ pakṣī parigṛhyāśu wīryawān |
agacchadapariśrānta āwāryārkaprabhāṃ khagaḥ ||11||

wiṣṇunā tu tadākāśe wainateyaḥ sameyiwān |
tasya nārāyaṇastuṣṭastenālaulyena karmaṇā ||12||

tamuwācāwyayo dewo warado'smīti khecaram |
sa wawre tawa tiṣṭheyamuparītyantarikṣagaḥ ||13||

uwāca cainaṃ bhūyo'pi nārāyaṇamidaṃ wacaḥ |
ajaraścāmaraśca syāmamṛtena wināpyaham ||14||

pratigṛhya warau tau ca garuḍo wiṣṇumabrawīt |
bhawate'pi waraṃ dadmi wṛṇītāṃ bhagawānapi ||15||

taṃ wawre wāhanaṃ kṛṣṇo garutmantaṃ mahābalam |
dhwajaṃ ca cakre bhagawānupari sthāsyasīti tam ||16||

anupatya khagaṃ twindro wajreṇāṅge'bhyatāḍayat |
wihaṅgamaṃ surāmitraṃ harantamamṛtaṃ balāt ||17||

tamuwācendramākrande garuḍaḥ patatāṃ waraḥ |
prahasañślakṣṇayā wācā tathā wajrasamāhataḥ ||18||

ṛṣermānaṃ kariṣyāmi wajraṃ yasyāsthisambhawam |
wajrasya ca kariṣyāmi tawa caiwa śatakrato ||19||

eṣa patraṃ tyajāmyekaṃ yasyāntaṃ nopalapsyase |
na hi wajranipātena rujā me'sti kadācana ||20||

tatra taṃ sarwabhūtāni wismitānyabruwaṃstadā |
surūpaṃ patramālakṣya suparṇo'yaṃ bhawatwiti ||21||

dṛṣṭwā tadadbhutaṃ cāpi sahasrākṣaḥ puraṃdaraḥ |
khago mahadidaṃ bhūtamiti matwābhyabhāṣata ||22||

balaṃ wijñātumicchāmi yatte paramanuttamam |
sakhyaṃ cānantamicchāmi twayā saha khagottama ||23||






                  30


garuḍa uwāca||

sakhyaṃ me'stu twayā dewa yathecchasi puraṃdara |
balaṃ tu mama jānīhi mahaccāsahyamewa ca ||1||

kāmaṃ naitatpraśaṃsanti santaḥ swabalasaṃstawam |
guṇasaṅkīrtanaṃ cāpi swayamewa śatakrato ||2||

sakheti kṛtwā tu sakhe pṛṣṭo wakṣyāmyahaṃ twayā |
na hyātmastawasaṃyuktaṃ waktawyamanimittataḥ ||3||

saparwatawanāmurwīṃ sasāgarawanāmimām |
pakṣanāḍyaikayā śakra twāṃ caiwātrāwalambinam ||4||

sarwānsampiṇḍitānwāpi lokānsasthāṇujaṅgamān |
waheyamapariśrānto widdhīdaṃ me mahadbalam ||5||

sūta uwāca||

ityuktawacanaṃ wīraṃ kirīṭī śrīmatāṃ waraḥ |
āha śaunaka dewendraḥ sarwabhūtahitaḥ prabhuḥ ||6||

pratigṛhyatāmidānīṃ me sakhyamānantyamuttamam |
na kāryaṃ tawa somena mama somaḥ pradīyatām ||7||

asmāṃste hi prabādheyuryebhyo dadyādbhawānimam ||7||

garuḍa uwāca||

kiñcitkāraṇamuddiśya somo'yaṃ nīyate mayā |
na dāsyāmi samādātuṃ somaṃ kasmaicidapyaham ||8||

yatremaṃ tu sahasrākṣa nikṣipeyamahaṃ swayam |
twamādāya tatastūrṇaṃ harethāstridaśeśwara ||9||

śakra uwāca||

wākyenānena tuṣṭo'haṃ yattwayoktamihāṇḍaja |
yadicchasi waraṃ mattastadgṛhāṇa khagottama ||10||

sūta uwāca||

ityuktaḥ pratyuwācedaṃ kadrūputrānanusmaran |
smṛtwā caiwopadhikṛtaṃ māturdāsyanimittataḥ ||11||

īśo'hamapi sarwasya kariṣyāmi tu te'rthitām |
bhaweyurbhujagāḥ śakra mama bhakṣyā mahābalāḥ ||12||

tathetyuktwānwagacchattaṃ tato dānawasūdanaḥ |
hariṣyāmi winikṣiptaṃ somamityanubhāṣya tam ||13||

ājagāma tatastūrṇaṃ suparṇo māturantikam |
atha sarpānuwācedaṃ sarwānparamahṛṣṭawat ||14||

idamānītamamṛtaṃ nikṣepsyāmi kuśeṣu waḥ |
snātā maṅgalasaṃyuktāstataḥ prāśnīta pannagāḥ ||15||

adāsī caiwa māteyamadyaprabhṛti cāstu me |
yathoktaṃ bhawatāmetadwaco me pratipāditam ||16||

tataḥ snātuṃ gatāḥ sarpāḥ pratyuktwā taṃ tathetyuta |
śakro'pyamṛtamākṣipya jagāma tridiwaṃ punaḥ ||17||

athāgatāstamuddeśaṃ sarpāḥ somārthinastadā |
snātāśca kṛtajapyāśca prahṛṣṭāḥ kṛtamaṅgalāḥ ||18||

tadwijñāya hṛtaṃ sarpāḥ pratimāyākṛtaṃ ca tat |
somasthānamidaṃ ceti darbhāṃste lilihustadā ||19||

tato dwaidhīkṛtā jihwā sarpāṇāṃ tena karmaṇā |
abhawaṃścāmṛtasparśāddarbhāste'tha pawitriṇaḥ ||20||

tataḥ suparṇaḥ paramaprahṛṣṭawā; nwihṛtya mātrā saha tatra kānane |
bhujaṅgabhakṣaḥ paramārcitaḥ khagai; rahīnakīrtirwinatāmanandayat ||21||

imāṃ kathāṃ yaḥ śṛṇuyānnaraḥ sadā; paṭheta wā dwijajanamukhyasaṃsadi |
asaṃśayaṃ tridiwamiyātsa puṇyabhā; ṅmahātmanaḥ patagapateḥ prakīrtanāt ||22||






                  31


śaunaka uwāca||

bhujaṅgamānāṃ śāpasya mātrā caiwa sutena ca |
winatāyāstwayā proktaṃ kāraṇaṃ sūtanandana ||1||

warapradānaṃ bhartrā ca kadrūwinatayostathā |
nāmanī caiwa te prokte pakṣiṇorwainateyayoḥ ||2||

pannagānāṃ tu nāmāni na kīrtayasi sūtaja |
prādhānyenāpi nāmāni śrotumicchāmahe wayam ||3||

sūta uwāca||

bahutwānnāmadheyāni bhujagānāṃ tapodhana |
na kīrtayiṣye sarweṣāṃ prādhānyena tu me śṛṇu ||4||

śeṣaḥ prathamato jāto wāsukistadanantaram |
airāwatastakṣakaśca karkoṭakadhanañjayau ||5||

kāliyo maṇināgaśca nāgaścāpūraṇastathā |
nāgastathā piñjaraka elāpatro'tha wāmanaḥ ||6||

nīlānīlau tathā nāgau kalmāṣaśabalau tathā |
āryakaścādikaścaiwa nāgaśca śalapotakaḥ ||7||

sumanomukho dadhimukhastathā wimalapiṇḍakaḥ |
āptaḥ koṭanakaścaiwa śaṅkho wālaśikhastathā ||8||

niṣṭhyūnako hemaguho nahuṣaḥ piṅgalastathā |
bāhyakarṇo hastipadastathā mudgarapiṇḍakaḥ ||9||

kambalāśwatarau cāpi nāgaḥ kālīyakastathā |
wṛttasaṃwartakau nāgau dwau ca padmāwiti śrutau ||10||

nāgaḥ śaṅkhanakaścaiwa tathā ca sphaṇḍako'paraḥ |
kṣemakaśca mahānāgo nāgaḥ piṇḍārakastathā ||11||

karawīraḥ puṣpadaṃṣṭra eळko bilwapāṇḍukaḥ |
mūṣakādaḥ śaṅkhaśirāḥ pūrṇadaṃṣṭro haridrakaḥ ||12||

aparājito jyotikaśca pannagaḥ śrīwahastathā |
kaurawyo dhṛtarāṣṭraśca puṣkaraḥ śalyakastathā ||13||

wirajāśca subāhuśca śālipiṇḍaśca wīryawān |
hastibhadraḥ piṭharako mukharaḥ koṇawāsanaḥ ||14||

kuñjaraḥ kuraraścaiwa tathā nāgaḥ prabhākaraḥ |
kumudaḥ kumudākṣaśca tittirirhalikastathā ||15||

karkarākarkarau cobhau kuṇḍodaramahodarau ||15||

ete prādhānyato nāgāḥ kīrtitā dwijasattama |
bahutwānnāmadheyānāmitare na prakīrtitāḥ ||16||

eteṣāṃ prasawo yaśca prasawasya ca santatiḥ |
asaṅkhyeyeti matwā tānna brawīmi dwijottama ||17||

bahūnīha sahasrāṇi prayutānyarbudāni ca |
aśakyānyewa saṅkhyātuṃ bhujagānāṃ tapodhana ||18||






                  32


śaunaka uwāca||

jātā wai bhujagāstāta wīryawanto durāsadāḥ |
śāpaṃ taṃ twatha wijñāya kṛtawanto nu kiṃ param ||1||

sūta uwāca||

teṣāṃ tu bhagawāñśeṣastyaktwā kadrūṃ mahāyaśāḥ |
tapo wipulamātasthe wāyubhakṣo yatawrataḥ ||2||

gandhamādanamāsādya badaryāṃ ca taporataḥ |
gokarṇe puṣkarāraṇye tathā himawatastaṭe ||3||

teṣu teṣu ca puṇyeṣu tīrtheṣwāyataneṣu ca |
ekāntaśīlī niyataḥ satataṃ wijitendriyaḥ ||4||

tapyamānaṃ tapo ghoraṃ taṃ dadarśa pitāmahaḥ |
pariśuṣkamāṃsatwaksnāyuṃ jaṭācīradharaṃ prabhum ||5||

tamabrawītsatyadhṛtiṃ tapyamānaṃ pitāmahaḥ |
kimidaṃ kuruṣe śeṣa prajānāṃ swasti wai kuru ||6||

twaṃ hi tīwreṇa tapasā prajāstāpayase'nagha |
brūhi kāmaṃ ca me śeṣa yatte hṛdi ciraṃ sthitam ||7||

śeṣa uwāca||

sodaryā mama sarwe hi bhrātaro mandacetasaḥ |
saha tairnotsahe wastuṃ tadbhawānanumanyatām ||8||

abhyasūyanti satataṃ parasparamamitrawat |
tato'haṃ tapa ātiṣṭhe naitānpaśyeyamityuta ||9||

na marṣayanti satataṃ winatāṃ sasutāṃ ca te |
asmākaṃ cāparo bhrātā wainateyaḥ pitāmaha ||10||

taṃ ca dwiṣanti te'tyarthaṃ sa cāpi sumahābalaḥ |
warapradānātsa pituḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ ||11||

so'haṃ tapaḥ samāsthāya mokṣyāmīdaṃ kalewaram |
kathaṃ me pretyabhāwe'pi na taiḥ syātsaha saṅgamaḥ ||12||

brahmowāca||

jānāmi śeṣa sarweṣāṃ bhrātṛṇāṃ te wiceṣṭitam |
mātuścāpyaparādhādwai bhrātṛṇāṃ te mahadbhayam ||13||

kṛto'tra parihāraśca pūrwamewa bhujaṅgama |
bhrātṛṇāṃ tawa sarweṣāṃ na śokaṃ kartumarhasi ||14||

wṛṇīṣwa ca waraṃ mattaḥ śeṣa yatte'bhikāṅkṣitam |
ditsāmi hi waraṃ te'dya prītirme paramā twayi ||15||

diṣṭyā ca buddhirdharme te niwiṣṭā pannagottama |
ato bhūyaśca te buddhirdharme bhawatu susthirā ||16||

śeṣa uwāca||

eṣa ewa waro me'dya kāṅkṣitaḥ prapitāmaha |
dharme me ramatāṃ buddhiḥ śame tapasi ceśwara ||17||

brahmowāca||

prīto'smyanena te śeṣa damena praśamena ca |
twayā twidaṃ wacaḥ kāryaṃ manniyogātprajāhitam ||18||

imāṃ mahīṃ śailawanopapannāṃ; sasāgarāṃ sākarapattanāṃ ca |
twaṃ śeṣa samyakcalitāṃ yathāwa; tsaṅgṛhya tiṣṭhaswa yathācalā syāt ||19||

śeṣa uwāca||

yathāha dewo waradaḥ prajāpati; rmahīpatirbhūtapatirjagatpatiḥ |
tathā mahīṃ dhārayitāsmi niścalāṃ; prayaccha tāṃ me śirasi prajāpate ||20||

brahmowāca||

adho mahīṃ gaccha bhujaṅgamottama; swayaṃ tawaiṣā wiwaraṃ pradāsyati |
imāṃ dharāṃ dhārayatā twayā hi me; mahatpriyaṃ śeṣa kṛtaṃ bhawiṣyati ||21||

sūta uwāca||

tatheti kṛtwā wiwaraṃ prawiśya sa; prabhurbhuwo bhujagawarāgrajaḥ sthitaḥ |
bibharti dewīṃ śirasā mahīmimāṃ; samudranemiṃ parigṛhya sarwataḥ ||22||

brahmowāca||

śeṣo'si nāgottama dharmadewo; mahīmimāṃ dhārayase yadekaḥ |
anantabhogaḥ parigṛhya sarwāṃ; yathāhamewaṃ balabhidyathā wā ||23||

sūta uwāca||

adho bhūmerwasatyewaṃ nāgo'nantaḥ pratāpawān |
dhārayanwasudhāmekaḥ śāsanādbrahmaṇo wibhuḥ ||24||

suparṇaṃ ca sakhāyaṃ wai bhagawānamarottamaḥ |
prādādanantāya tadā wainateyaṃ pitāmahaḥ ||25||






                  33


sūta uwāca||

mātuḥ sakāśāttaṃ śāpaṃ śrutwā pannagasattamaḥ |
wāsukiścintayāmāsa śāpo'yaṃ na bhawetkatham ||1||

tataḥ sa mantrayāmāsa bhrātṛbhiḥ saha sarwaśaḥ |
airāwataprabhṛtibhirye sma dharmaparāyaṇāḥ ||2||

wāsukiruwāca||

ayaṃ śāpo yathoddiṣṭo widitaṃ wastathānaghāḥ |
tasya śāpasya mokṣārthaṃ mantrayitwā yatāmahe ||3||

sarweṣāmewa śāpānāṃ pratighāto hi widyate |
na tu mātrābhiśaptānāṃ mokṣo widyeta pannagāḥ ||4||

awyayasyāprameyasya satyasya ca tathāgrataḥ |
śaptā ityewa me śrutwā jāyate hṛdi wepathuḥ ||5||

nūnaṃ sarwawināśo'yamasmākaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ |
na hyenāṃ so'wyayo dewaḥ śapantīṃ pratyaṣedhayat ||6||

tasmātsaṃmantrayāmo'tra bhujagānāmanāmayam |
yathā bhaweta sarweṣāṃ mā naḥ kālo'tyagādayam ||7||

api mantrayamāṇā hi hetuṃ paśyāma mokṣaṇe |
yathā naṣṭaṃ purā dewā gūḍhamagniṃ guhāgatam ||8||

yathā sa yajño na bhawedyathā wāpi parābhawet |
janamejayasya sarpāṇāṃ wināśakaraṇāya hi ||9||

sūta uwāca||

tathetyuktwā tu te sarwe kādraweyāḥ samāgatāḥ |
samayaṃ cakrire tatra mantrabuddhiwiśāradāḥ ||10||

eke tatrābruwannāgā wayaṃ bhūtwā dwijarṣabhāḥ |
janamejayaṃ taṃ bhikṣāmo yajñaste na bhawediti ||11||

apare twabruwannāgāstatra paṇḍitamāninaḥ |
mantriṇo'sya wayaṃ sarwe bhawiṣyāmaḥ susaṃmatāḥ ||12||

sa naḥ prakṣyati sarweṣu kāryeṣwarthawiniścayam |
tatra buddhiṃ prawakṣyāmo yathā yajño niwartate ||13||

sa no bahumatānrājā buddhwā buddhimatāṃ waraḥ |
yajñārthaṃ prakṣyati wyaktaṃ neti wakṣyāmahe wayam ||14||

darśayanto bahūndoṣānpretya ceha ca dāruṇān |
hetubhiḥ kāraṇaiścaiwa yathā yajño bhawenna saḥ ||15||

athawā ya upādhyāyaḥ kratau tasminbhawiṣyati |
sarpasatrawidhānajño rājakāryahite rataḥ ||16||

taṃ gatwā daśatāṃ kaścidbhujagaḥ sa mariṣyati |
tasminhate yajñakare kratuḥ sa na bhawiṣyati ||17||

ye cānye sarpasatrajñā bhawiṣyantyasya ṛtwijaḥ |
tāṃśca sarwāndaśiṣyāmaḥ kṛtamewaṃ bhawiṣyati ||18||

tatrāpare'mantrayanta dharmātmāno bhujaṅgamāḥ |
abuddhireṣā yuṣmākaṃ brahmahatyā na śobhanā ||19||

samyaksaddharmamūlā hi wyasane śāntiruttamā |
adharmottaratā nāma kṛtsnaṃ wyāpādayejjagat ||20||

apare twabruwannāgāḥ samiddhaṃ jātawedasam |
warṣairnirwāpayiṣyāmo meghā bhūtwā sawidyutaḥ ||21||

srugbhāṇḍaṃ niśi gatwā wā apare bhujagottamāḥ |
pramattānāṃ harantwāśu wighna ewaṃ bhawiṣyati ||22||

yajñe wā bhujagāstasmiñśataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ |
janaṃ daśantu wai sarwamewaṃ trāso bhawiṣyati ||23||

athawā saṃskṛtaṃ bhojyaṃ dūṣayantu bhujaṅgamāḥ |
swena mūtrapurīṣeṇa sarwabhojyawināśinā ||24||

apare twabruwaṃstatra ṛtwijo'sya bhawāmahe |
yajñawighnaṃ kariṣyāmo dīyatāṃ dakṣiṇā iti ||25||

waśyatāṃ ca gato'sau naḥ kariṣyati yathepṣitam ||25||

apare twabruwaṃstatra jale prakrīḍitaṃ nṛpam |
gṛhamānīya badhnīmaḥ kraturewaṃ bhawenna saḥ ||26||

apare twabruwaṃstatra nāgāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ |
daśāmainaṃ pragṛhyāśu kṛtamewaṃ bhawiṣyati ||27||

chinnaṃ mūlamanarthānāṃ mṛte tasminbhawiṣyati ||27||

eṣā wai naiṣṭhikī buddhiḥ sarweṣāmewa saṃmatā |
yathā wā manyase rājaṃstatkṣipraṃ saṃwidhīyatām ||28||

ityuktwā samudaikṣanta wāsukiṃ pannageśwaram |
wāsukiścāpi sañcintya tānuwāca bhujaṅgamān ||29||

naiṣā wo naiṣṭhikī buddhirmatā kartuṃ bhujaṅgamāḥ |
sarweṣāmewa me buddhiḥ pannagānāṃ na rocate ||30||

kiṃ twatra saṃwidhātawyaṃ bhawatāṃ yadbhaweddhitam |
anenāhaṃ bhṛśaṃ tapye guṇadoṣau madāśrayau ||31||






                  34


sūta uwāca||

śrutwā tu wacanaṃ teṣāṃ sarweṣāmiti ceti ca |
wāsukeśca wacaḥ śrutwā elāpatro'brawīdidam ||1||

na sa yajño na bhawitā na sa rājā tathāwidhaḥ |
janamejayaḥ pāṇḍaweyo yato'smākaṃ mahābhayam ||2||

daiwenopahato rājanyo bhawediha pūruṣaḥ |
sa daiwamewāśrayate nānyattatra parāyaṇam ||3||

tadidaṃ daiwamasmākaṃ bhayaṃ pannagasattamāḥ |
daiwamewāśrayāmo'tra śṛṇudhwaṃ ca waco mama ||4||

ahaṃ śāpe samutsṛṣṭe samaśrauṣaṃ wacastadā |
māturutsaṅgamārūḍho bhayātpannagasattamāḥ ||5||

dewānāṃ pannagaśreṣṭhāstīkṣṇāstīkṣṇā iti prabho |
pitāmahamupāgamya duḥkhārtānāṃ mahādyute ||6||

dewā ūcuḥ||

kā hi labdhwā priyānputrāñśapedewaṃ pitāmaha |
ṛte kadrūṃ tīkṣṇarūpāṃ dewadewa tawāgrataḥ ||7||

tatheti ca wacastasyāstwayāpyuktaṃ pitāmaha |
etadicchāma wijñātuṃ kāraṇaṃ yanna wāritā ||8||

brahmowāca||

bahawaḥ pannagāstīkṣṇā bhīmawīryā wiṣolbaṇāḥ |
prajānāṃ hitakāmo'haṃ na niwāritawāṃstadā ||9||

ye dandaśūkāḥ kṣudrāśca pāpacārā wiṣolbaṇāḥ |
teṣāṃ wināśo bhawitā na tu ye dharmacāriṇaḥ ||10||

yannimittaṃ ca bhawitā mokṣasteṣāṃ mahābhayāt |
pannagānāṃ nibodhadhwaṃ tasminkāle tathāgate ||11||

yāyāwarakule dhīmānbhawiṣyati mahānṛṣiḥ |
jaratkāruriti khyātastejaswī niyatendriyaḥ ||12||

tasya putro jaratkārorutpatsyati mahātapāḥ |
āstīko nāma yajñaṃ sa pratiṣetsyati taṃ tadā ||13||

tatra mokṣyanti bhujagā ye bhawiṣyanti dhārmikāḥ ||13||

dewā ūcuḥ||

sa muniprawaro dewa jaratkārurmahātapāḥ |
kasyāṃ putraṃ mahātmānaṃ janayiṣyati wīryawān ||14||

brahmowāca||

sanāmāyāṃ sanāmā sa kanyāyāṃ dwijasattamaḥ |
apatyaṃ wīryawāndewā wīryawajjanayiṣyati ||15||

elāpatra uwāca||

ewamastwiti taṃ dewāḥ pitāmahamathābruwan |
uktwā caiwaṃ gatā dewāḥ sa ca dewaḥ pitāmahaḥ ||16||

so'hamewaṃ prapaśyāmi wāsuke bhaginīṃ tawa |
jaratkāruriti khyātāṃ tāṃ tasmai pratipādaya ||17||

bhaikṣawadbhikṣamāṇāya nāgānāṃ bhayaśāntaye |
ṛṣaye suwratāya twameṣa mokṣaḥ śruto mayā ||18||






                  35


sūta uwāca||

elāpatrasya tu wacaḥ śrutwā nāgā dwijottama |
sarwe prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ sādhu sādhwityapūjayan ||1||

tataḥ prabhṛti tāṃ kanyāṃ wāsukiḥ paryarakṣata |
jaratkāruṃ swasāraṃ wai paraṃ harṣamawāpa ca ||2||

tato nātimahānkālaḥ samatīta iwābhawat |
atha dewāsurāḥ sarwe mamanthurwaruṇālayam ||3||

tatra netramabhūnnāgo wāsukirbalināṃ waraḥ |
samāpyaiwa ca tatkarma pitāmahamupāgaman ||4||

dewā wāsukinā sārdhaṃ pitāmahamathābruwan |
bhagawañśāpabhīto'yaṃ wāsukistapyate bhṛśam ||5||

tasyedaṃ mānasaṃ śalyaṃ samuddhartuṃ twamarhasi |
jananyāḥ śāpajaṃ dewa jñātīnāṃ hitakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ||6||

hito hyayaṃ sadāsmākaṃ priyakārī ca nāgarāṭ |
kuru prasādaṃ deweśa śamayāsya manojwaram ||7||

brahmowāca||

mayaiwaitadwitīrṇaṃ wai wacanaṃ manasāmarāḥ |
elāpatreṇa nāgena yadasyābhihitaṃ purā ||8||

tatkarotweṣa nāgendraḥ prāptakālaṃ wacastathā |
winaśiṣyanti ye pāpā na tu ye dharmacāriṇaḥ ||9||

utpannaḥ sa jaratkārustapasyugre rato dwijaḥ |
tasyaiṣa bhaginīṃ kāle jaratkāruṃ prayacchatu ||10||

yadelāpatreṇa wacastadoktaṃ bhujagena ha |
pannagānāṃ hitaṃ dewāstattathā na tadanyathā ||11||

sūta uwāca||

etacchrutwā sa nāgendraḥ pitāmahawacastadā |
sarpānbahūñjaratkārau nityayuktānsamādadhat ||12||

jaratkāruryadā bhāryāmicchedwarayituṃ prabhuḥ |
śīghrametya mamākhyeyaṃ tannaḥ śreyo bhawiṣyati ||13||






                  36


śaunaka uwāca||

jaratkāruriti proktaṃ yattwayā sūtanandana |
icchāmyetadahaṃ tasya ṛṣeḥ śrotuṃ mahātmanaḥ ||1||

kiṃ kāraṇaṃ jaratkārornāmaitatprathitaṃ bhuwi |
jaratkāruniruktaṃ twaṃ yathāwadwaktumarhasi ||2||

sūta uwāca||

jareti kṣayamāhurwai dāruṇaṃ kārusañjñitam |
śarīraṃ kāru tasyāsīttatsa dhīmāñśanaiḥ śanaiḥ ||3||

kṣapayāmāsa tīwreṇa tapasetyata ucyate |
jaratkāruriti brahmanwāsukerbhaginī tathā ||4||

ewamuktastu dharmātmā śaunakaḥ prāhasattadā |
ugraśrawasamāmantrya upapannamiti bruwan ||5||

sūta uwāca||

atha kālasya mahataḥ sa muniḥ saṃśitawrataḥ |
tapasyabhirato dhīmānna dārānabhyakāṅkṣata ||6||

sa ūrdhwaretāstapasi prasaktaḥ; swādhyāyawānwītabhayaklamaḥ san |
cacāra sarwāṃ pṛthiwīṃ mahātmā; na cāpi dārānmanasāpyakāṅkṣat ||7||

tato'parasminsamprāpte kāle kasmiṃścidewa tu |
parikṣiditi wikhyāto rājā kaurawawaṃśabhṛt ||8||

yathā pāṇḍurmahābāhurdhanurdharawaro bhuwi |
babhūwa mṛgayāśīlaḥ purāsya prapitāmahaḥ ||9||

mṛgānwidhyanwarāhāṃśca tarakṣūnmahiṣāṃstathā |
anyāṃśca wiwidhānwanyāṃścacāra pṛthiwīpatiḥ ||10||

sa kadācinmṛgaṃ widdhwā bāṇena nataparwaṇā |
pṛṣṭhato dhanurādāya sasāra gahane wane ||11||

yathā hi bhagawānrudro widdhwā yajñamṛgaṃ diwi |
anwagacchaddhanuṣpāṇiḥ paryanweṣaṃstatastataḥ ||12||

na hi tena mṛgo widdho jīwangacchati wai wanam |
pūrwarūpaṃ tu tannūnamāsītswargagatiṃ prati ||13||

parikṣitastasya rājño widdho yannaṣṭawānmṛgaḥ ||13||

dūraṃ cāpahṛtastena mṛgeṇa sa mahīpatiḥ |
pariśrāntaḥ pipāsārta āsasāda muniṃ wane ||14||

gawāṃ pracāreṣwāsīnaṃ watsānāṃ mukhaniḥsṛtam |
bhūyiṣṭhamupayuñjānaṃ phenamāpibatāṃ payaḥ ||15||

tamabhidrutya wegena sa rājā saṃśitawratam |
apṛcchaddhanurudyamya taṃ muniṃ kṣucchramānwitaḥ ||16||

bho bho brahmannahaṃ rājā parikṣidabhimanyujaḥ |
mayā widdho mṛgo naṣṭaḥ kaccittwaṃ dṛṣṭawānasi ||17||

sa munistasya nowāca kiñcinmaunawrate sthitaḥ |
tasya skandhe mṛtaṃ sarpaṃ kruddho rājā samāsajat ||18||

dhanuṣkoṭyā samutkṣipya sa cainaṃ samudaikṣata |
na ca kiñciduwācainaṃ śubhaṃ wā yadi wāśubham ||19||

sa rājā krodhamutsṛjya wyathitastaṃ tathāgatam |
dṛṣṭwā jagāma nagaramṛṣistwāste tathaiwa saḥ ||20||

taruṇastasya putro'bhūttigmatejā mahātapāḥ |
śṛṅgī nāma mahākrodho duṣprasādo mahāwrataḥ ||21||

sa dewaṃ paramīśānaṃ sarwabhūtahite ratam |
brahmāṇamupatasthe wai kāle kāle susaṃyataḥ ||22||

sa tena samanujñāto brahmaṇā gṛhameyiwān ||22||

sakhyoktaḥ krīḍamānena sa tatra hasatā kila |
saṃrambhī kopano'tīwa wiṣakalpa ṛṣeḥ sutaḥ ||23||

ṛṣiputreṇa narmārthaṃ kṛśena dwijasattama ||23||

tejaswinastawa pitā tathaiwa ca tapaswinaḥ |
śawaṃ skandhena wahati mā śṛṅgingarwito bhawa ||24||

wyāharatswṛṣiputreṣu mā sma kiñcidwaco wadīḥ |
asmadwidheṣu siddheṣu brahmawitsu tapaswiṣu ||25||

kwa te puruṣamānitwaṃ kwa te wācastathāwidhāḥ |
darpajāḥ pitaraṃ yastwaṃ draṣṭā śawadharaṃ tathā ||26||






                  37


sūta uwāca||

ewamuktaḥ sa tejaswī śṛṅgī kopasamanwitaḥ |
mṛtadhāraṃ guruṃ śrutwā paryatapyata manyunā ||1||

sa taṃ kṛśamabhipreṣkya sūnṛtāṃ wācamutsṛjan |
apṛcchata kathaṃ tātaḥ sa me'dya mṛtadhārakaḥ ||2||

kṛśa uwāca||

rājñā parikṣitā tāta mṛgayāṃ paridhāwatā |
awasaktaḥ pituste'dya mṛtaḥ skandhe bhujaṅgamaḥ ||3||

śṛṅgyuwāca||

kiṃ me pitrā kṛtaṃ tasya rājño'niṣṭaṃ durātmanaḥ |
brūhi twaṃ kṛśa tattwena paśya me tapaso balam ||4||

kṛśa uwāca||

sa rājā mṛgayāṃ yātaḥ parikṣidabhimanyujaḥ |
sasāra mṛgamekākī widdhwā bāṇena patriṇā ||5||

na cāpaśyanmṛgaṃ rājā caraṃstasminmahāwane |
pitaraṃ te sa dṛṣṭwaiwa papracchānabhibhāṣiṇam ||6||

taṃ sthāṇubhūtaṃ tiṣṭhantaṃ kṣutpipāsāśramāturaḥ |
punaḥ punarmṛgaṃ naṣṭaṃ papraccha pitaraṃ tawa ||7||

sa ca maunawratopeto naiwa taṃ pratyabhāṣata |
tasya rājā dhanuṣkoṭyā sarpaṃ skandhe samāsṛjat ||8||

śṛṅgiṃstawa pitādyāsau tathaiwāste yatawrataḥ |
so'pi rājā swanagaraṃ pratiyāto gajāhwayam ||9||

sūta uwāca||

śrutwaiwamṛṣiputrastu diwaṃ stabdhwewa wiṣṭhitaḥ |
kopasaṃraktanayanaḥ prajwalanniwa manyunā ||10||

āwiṣṭaḥ sa tu kopena śaśāpa nṛpatiṃ tadā |
wāryupaspṛśya tejaswī krodhawegabalātkṛtaḥ ||11||

śṛṅgyuwāca||

yo'sau wṛddhasya tātasya tathā kṛcchragatasya ca |
skandhe mṛtamawāsrākṣītpannagaṃ rājakilbiṣī ||12||

taṃ pāpamatisaṅkruddhastakṣakaḥ pannagottamaḥ |
āśīwiṣastigmatejā madwākyabalacoditaḥ ||13||

saptarātrādito netā yamasya sadanaṃ prati |
dwijānāmawamantāraṃ kurūṇāmayaśaskaram ||14||

sūta uwāca||

iti śaptwā nṛpaṃ kruddhaḥ śṛṅgī pitaramabhyayāt |
āsīnaṃ gocare tasminwahantaṃ śawapannagam ||15||

sa tamālakṣya pitaraṃ śṛṅgī skandhagatena wai |
śawena bhujagenāsīdbhūyaḥ krodhasamanwitaḥ ||16||

duḥkhāccāśrūṇi mumuce pitaraṃ cedamabrawīt |
śrutwemāṃ dharṣaṇāṃ tāta tawa tena durātmanā ||17||

rājñā parikṣitā kopādaśapaṃ tamahaṃ nṛpam |
yathārhati sa ewograṃ śāpaṃ kurukulādhamaḥ ||18||

saptame'hani taṃ pāpaṃ takṣakaḥ pannagottamaḥ |
waiwaswatasya bhawanaṃ netā paramadāruṇam ||19||

tamabrawītpitā brahmaṃstathā kopasamanwitam |
na me priyaṃ kṛtaṃ tāta naiṣa dharmastapaswinām ||20||

wayaṃ tasya narendrasya wiṣaye niwasāmahe |
nyāyato rakṣitāstena tasya pāpaṃ na rocaye ||21||

sarwathā wartamānasya rājño hyasmadwidhaiḥ sadā |
kṣantawyaṃ putra dharmo hi hato hanti na saṃśayaḥ ||22||

yadi rājā na rakṣeta pīḍā wai naḥ parā bhawet |
na śaknuyāma carituṃ dharmaṃ putra yathāsukham ||23||

rakṣyamāṇā wayaṃ tāta rājabhiḥ śāstradṛṣṭibhiḥ |
carāmo wipulaṃ dharmaṃ teṣāṃ cāṃśo'sti dharmataḥ ||24||

parikṣittu wiśeṣeṇa yathāsya prapitāmahaḥ |
rakṣatyasmānyathā rājñā rakṣitawyāḥ prajāstathā ||25||

teneha kṣudhitenādya śrāntena ca tapaswinā |
ajānatā wratamidaṃ kṛtametadasaṃśayam ||26||

tasmādidaṃ twayā bālyātsahasā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam |
na hyarhati nṛpaḥ śāpamasmattaḥ putra sarwathā ||27||






                  38


śṛṅgyuwāca||

yadyetatsāhasaṃ tāta yadi wā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam |
priyaṃ wāpyapriyaṃ wā te wāguktā na mṛṣā mayā ||1||

naiwānyathedaṃ bhawitā pitareṣa brawīmi te |
nāhaṃ mṛṣā prabrawīmi swaireṣwapi kutaḥ śapan ||2||

śamīka uwāca||

jānāmyugraprabhāwaṃ twāṃ putra satyagiraṃ tathā |
nānṛtaṃ hyuktapūrwaṃ te naitanmithyā bhawiṣyati ||3||

pitrā putro wayaḥstho'pi satataṃ wācya ewa tu |
yathā syādguṇasaṃyuktaḥ prāpnuyācca mahadyaśaḥ ||4||

kiṃ punarbāla ewa twaṃ tapasā bhāwitaḥ prabho |
wardhate ca prabhawatāṃ kopo'tīwa mahātmanām ||5||

so'haṃ paśyāmi waktawyaṃ twayi dharmabhṛtāṃ wara |
putratwaṃ bālatāṃ caiwa tawāwekṣya ca sāhasam ||6||

sa twaṃ śamayuto bhūtwā wanyamāhāramāharan |
cara krodhamimaṃ tyaktwā naiwaṃ dharmaṃ prahāsyasi ||7||

krodho hi dharmaṃ harati yatīnāṃ duḥkhasañcitam |
tato dharmawihīnānāṃ gatiriṣṭā na widyate ||8||

śama ewa yatīnāṃ hi kṣamiṇāṃ siddhikārakaḥ |
kṣamāwatāmayaṃ lokaḥ paraścaiwa kṣamāwatām ||9||

tasmāccarethāḥ satataṃ kṣamāśīlo jitendriyaḥ |
kṣamayā prāpsyase lokānbrahmaṇaḥ samanantarān ||10||

mayā tu śamamāsthāya yacchakyaṃ kartumadya wai |
tatkariṣye'dya tātāhaṃ preṣayiṣye nṛpāya wai ||11||

mama putreṇa śapto'si bālenākṛtabuddhinā |
mamemāṃ dharṣaṇāṃ twattaḥ prekṣya rājannamarṣiṇā ||12||

sūta uwāca||

ewamādiśya śiṣyaṃ sa preṣayāmāsa suwrataḥ |
parikṣite nṛpataye dayāpanno mahātapāḥ ||13||

saṃdiśya kuśalapraśnaṃ kāryawṛttāntamewa ca |
śiṣyaṃ gauramukhaṃ nāma śīlawantaṃ samāhitam ||14||

so'bhigamya tataḥ śīghraṃ narendraṃ kuruwardhanam |
wiweśa bhawanaṃ rājñaḥ pūrwaṃ dwāḥsthairniweditaḥ ||15||

pūjitaśca narendreṇa dwijo gauramukhastataḥ |
ācakhyau pariwiśrānto rājñe sarwamaśeṣataḥ ||16||

śamīkawacanaṃ ghoraṃ yathoktaṃ mantrisaṃnidhau ||16||

śamīko nāma rājendra wiṣaye wartate tawa |
ṛṣiḥ paramadharmātmā dāntaḥ śānto mahātapāḥ ||17||

tasya twayā narawyāghra sarpaḥ prāṇairwiyojitaḥ |
awasakto dhanuṣkoṭyā skandhe bharatasattama ||18||

kṣāntawāṃstawa tatkarma putrastasya na cakṣame ||18||

tena śapto'si rājendra piturajñātamadya wai |
takṣakaḥ saptarātreṇa mṛtyuste wai bhawiṣyati ||19||

tatra rakṣāṃ kuruṣweti punaḥ punarathābrawīt |
tadanyathā na śakyaṃ ca kartuṃ kenacidapyuta ||20||

na hi śaknoti saṃyantuṃ putraṃ kopasamanwitam |
tato'haṃ preṣitastena tawa rājanhitārthinā ||21||

iti śrutwā waco ghoraṃ sa rājā kurunandanaḥ |
paryatapyata tatpāpaṃ kṛtwā rājā mahātapāḥ ||22||

taṃ ca maunawratadharaṃ śrutwā muniwaraṃ tadā |
bhūya ewābhawadrājā śokasantaptamānasaḥ ||23||

anukrośātmatāṃ tasya śamīkasyāwadhārya tu |
paryatapyata bhūyo'pi kṛtwā tatkilbiṣaṃ muneḥ ||24||

na hi mṛtyuṃ tathā rājā śrutwā wai so'nwatapyata |
aśocadamaraprakhyo yathā kṛtweha karma tat ||25||

tatastaṃ preṣayāmāsa rājā gauramukhaṃ tadā |
bhūyaḥ prasādaṃ bhagawānkarotwiti mameti wai ||26||

tasmiṃśca gatamātre wai rājā gauramukhe tadā |
mantribhirmantrayāmāsa saha saṃwignamānasaḥ ||27||

niścitya mantribhiścaiwa sahito mantratattwawit |
prāsādaṃ kārayāmāsa ekastambhaṃ surakṣitam ||28||

rakṣāṃ ca widadhe tatra bhiṣajaścauṣadhāni ca |
brāhmaṇānsiddhamantrāṃśca sarwato wai nyaweśayat ||29||

rājakāryāṇi tatrasthaḥ sarwāṇyewākarocca saḥ |
mantribhiḥ saha dharmajñaḥ samantātparirakṣitaḥ ||30||

prāpte tu diwase tasminsaptame dwijasattama |
kāśyapo'bhyāgamadwidwāṃstaṃ rājānaṃ cikitsitum ||31||

śrutaṃ hi tena tadabhūdadya taṃ rājasattamam |
takṣakaḥ pannagaśreṣṭho neṣyate yamasādanam ||32||

taṃ daṣṭaṃ pannagendreṇa kariṣye'hamapajwaram |
tatra me'rthaśca dharmaśca bhawiteti wicintayan ||33||

taṃ dadarśa sa nāgendrastakṣakaḥ kāśyapaṃ pathi |
gacchantamekamanasaṃ dwijo bhūtwā wayotigaḥ ||34||

tamabrawītpannagendraḥ kāśyapaṃ munipuṅgawam |
kwa bhawāṃstwarito yāti kiṃ ca kāryaṃ cikīrṣati ||35||

kāśyapa uwāca||

nṛpaṃ kurukulotpannaṃ parikṣitamariṃdamam |
takṣakaḥ pannagaśreṣṭhastejasādya pradhakṣyati ||36||

taṃ daṣṭaṃ pannagendreṇa tenāgnisamatejasā |
pāṇḍawānāṃ kulakaraṃ rājānamamitaujasam ||37||

gacchāmi saumya twaritaṃ sadyaḥ kartumapajwaram ||37||

takṣaka uwāca||

ahaṃ sa takṣako brahmaṃstaṃ dhakṣyāmi mahīpatim |
niwartaswa na śaktastwaṃ mayā daṣṭaṃ cikitsitum ||38||

kāśyapa uwāca||

ahaṃ taṃ nṛpatiṃ nāga twayā daṣṭamapajwaram |
kariṣya iti me buddhirwidyābalamupāśritaḥ ||39||






                  39


takṣaka uwāca||

daṣṭaṃ yadi mayeha twaṃ śaktaḥ kiñciccikitsitum |
tato wṛkṣaṃ mayā daṣṭamimaṃ jīwaya kāśyapa ||1||

paraṃ mantrabalaṃ yatte taddarśaya yataswa ca |
nyagrodhamenaṃ dhakṣyāmi paśyataste dwijottama ||2||

kāśyapa uwāca||

daśa nāgendra wṛkṣaṃ twaṃ yamenamabhimanyase |
ahamenaṃ twayā daṣṭaṃ jīwayiṣye bhujaṅgama ||3||

sūta uwāca||

ewamuktaḥ sa nāgendraḥ kāśyapena mahātmanā |
adaśadwṛkṣamabhyetya nyagrodhaṃ pannagottamaḥ ||4||

sa wṛkṣastena daṣṭaḥ sansadya ewa mahādyute |
āśīwiṣawiṣopetaḥ prajajwāla samantataḥ ||5||

taṃ dagdhwā sa nagaṃ nāgaḥ kāśyapaṃ punarabrawīt |
kuru yatnaṃ dwijaśreṣṭha jīwayainaṃ wanaspatim ||6||

bhasmībhūtaṃ tato wṛkṣaṃ pannagendrasya tejasā |
bhasma sarwaṃ samāhṛtya kāśyapo wākyamabrawīt ||7||

widyābalaṃ pannagendra paśya me'sminwanaspatau |
ahaṃ sañjīwayāmyenaṃ paśyataste bhujaṅgama ||8||

tataḥ sa bhagawānwidwānkāśyapo dwijasattamaḥ |
bhasmarāśīkṛtaṃ wṛkṣaṃ widyayā samajīwayat ||9||

aṅkuraṃ taṃ sa kṛtawāṃstataḥ parṇadwayānwitam |
palāśinaṃ śākhinaṃ ca tathā wiṭapinaṃ punaḥ ||10||

taṃ dṛṣṭwā jīwitaṃ wṛkṣaṃ kāśyapena mahātmanā |
uwāca takṣako brahmannetadatyadbhutaṃ twayi ||11||

wiprendra yadwiṣaṃ hanyā mama wā madwidhasya wā |
kaṃ twamarthamabhiprepsuryāsi tatra tapodhana ||12||

yatte'bhilaṣitaṃ prāptuṃ phalaṃ tasmānnṛpottamāt |
ahamewa pradāsyāmi tatte yadyapi durlabham ||13||

wipraśāpābhibhūte ca kṣīṇāyuṣi narādhipe |
ghaṭamānasya te wipra siddhiḥ saṃśayitā bhawet ||14||

tato yaśaḥ pradīptaṃ te triṣu lokeṣu wiśrutam |
wiraśmiriwa gharmāṃśurantardhānamito wrajet ||15||

kāśyapa uwāca||

dhanārthī yāmyahaṃ tatra tanme ditsa bhujaṅgama |
tato'haṃ winiwartiṣye gṛhāyoragasattama ||16||

takṣaka uwāca||

yāwaddhanaṃ prārthayase tasmādrājñastato'dhikam |
ahaṃ te'dya pradāsyāmi niwartaswa dwijottama ||17||

sūta uwāca||

takṣakasya wacaḥ śrutwā kāśyapo dwijasattamaḥ |
pradadhyau sumahātejā rājānaṃ prati buddhimān ||18||

diwyajñānaḥ sa tejaswī jñātwā taṃ nṛpatiṃ tadā |
kṣīṇāyuṣaṃ pāṇḍaweyamapāwartata kāśyapaḥ ||19||

labdhwā wittaṃ muniwarastakṣakādyāwadīpsitam ||19||

niwṛtte kāśyape tasminsamayena mahātmani |
jagāma takṣakastūrṇaṃ nagaraṃ nāgasāhwayam ||20||

atha śuśrāwa gacchansa takṣako jagatīpatim |
mantrāgadairwiṣaharai rakṣyamāṇaṃ prayatnataḥ ||21||

sa cintayāmāsa tadā māyāyogena pārthiwaḥ |
mayā wañcayitawyo'sau ka upāyo bhawediti ||22||

tatastāpasarūpeṇa prāhiṇotsa bhujaṅgamān |
phalapatrodakaṃ gṛhya rājñe nāgo'tha takṣakaḥ ||23||

takṣaka uwāca||

gacchadhwaṃ yūyamawyagrā rājānaṃ kāryawattayā |
phalapatrodakaṃ nāma pratigrāhayituṃ nṛpam ||24||

sūta uwāca||

te takṣakasamādiṣṭāstathā cakrurbhujaṅgamāḥ |
upaninyustathā rājñe darbhānāpaḥ phalāni ca ||25||

tacca sarwaṃ sa rājendraḥ pratijagrāha wīryawān |
kṛtwā ca teṣāṃ kāryāṇi gamyatāmityuwāca tān ||26||

gateṣu teṣu nāgeṣu tāpasacchadmarūpiṣu |
amātyānsuhṛdaścaiwa prowāca sa narādhipaḥ ||27||

bhakṣayantu bhawanto wai swādūnīmāni sarwaśaḥ |
tāpasairupanītāni phalāni sahitā mayā ||28||

tato rājā sasaciwaḥ phalānyādātumaicchata |
yadgṛhītaṃ phalaṃ rājñā tatra kṛmirabhūdaṇuḥ ||29||

hraswakaḥ kṛṣṇanayanastāmro warṇena śaunaka ||29||

sa taṃ gṛhya nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ saciwānidamabrawīt |
astamabhyeti sawitā wiṣādadya na me bhayam ||30||

satyawāgastu sa muniḥ kṛmiko māṃ daśatwayam |
takṣako nāma bhūtwā wai tathā parihṛtaṃ bhawet ||31||

te cainamanwawartanta mantriṇaḥ kālacoditāḥ |
ewamuktwā sa rājendro grīwāyāṃ saṃniweśya ha ||32||

kṛmikaṃ prāhasattūrṇaṃ mumūrṣurnaṣṭacetanaḥ ||32||

hasannewa ca bhogena takṣakeṇābhiweṣṭitaḥ |
tasmātphalādwiniṣkramya yattadrājñe niweditam ||33||






                  40


sūta uwāca||

taṃ tathā mantriṇo dṛṣṭwā bhogena pariweṣṭitam |
wiwarṇawadanāḥ sarwe rurudurbhṛśaduḥkhitāḥ ||1||

taṃ tu nādaṃ tataḥ śrutwā mantriṇaste pradudruwuḥ |
apaśyaṃścaiwa te yāntamākāśe nāgamadbhutam ||2||

sīmantamiwa kurwāṇaṃ nabhasaḥ padmawarcasam |
takṣakaṃ pannagaśreṣṭhaṃ bhṛśaṃ śokaparāyaṇāḥ ||3||

tatastu te tadgṛhamagninā wṛtaṃ; pradīpyamānaṃ wiṣajena bhoginaḥ |
bhayātparityajya diśaḥ prapedire; papāta taccāśanitāḍitaṃ yathā ||4||

tato nṛpe takṣakatejasā hate; prayujya sarwāḥ paralokasatkriyāḥ |
śucirdwijo rājapurohitastadā; tathaiwa te tasya nṛpasya mantriṇaḥ ||5||

nṛpaṃ śiśuṃ tasya sutaṃ pracakrire; sametya sarwe purawāsino janāḥ |
nṛpaṃ yamāhustamamitraghātinaṃ; kuruprawīraṃ janamejayaṃ janāḥ ||6||

sa bāla ewāryamatirnṛpottamaḥ; sahaiwa tairmantripurohitaistadā |
śaśāsa rājyaṃ kurupuṅgawāgrajo; yathāsya wīraḥ prapitāmahastathā ||7||

tatastu rājānamamitratāpanaṃ; samīkṣya te tasya nṛpasya mantriṇaḥ |
suwarṇawarmāṇamupetya kāśipaṃ; wapuṣṭamārthaṃ warayāṃ pracakramuḥ ||8||

tataḥ sa rājā pradadau wapuṣṭamāṃ; kuruprawīrāya parīkṣya dharmataḥ |
sa cāpi tāṃ prāpya mudā yuto'bhawa; nna cānyanārīṣu mano dadhe kwacit ||9||

saraḥsu phulleṣu waneṣu caiwa ha; prasannacetā wijahāra wīryawān |
tathā sa rājanyawaro wijahriwā; nyathorwaśīṃ prāpya purā purūrawāḥ ||10||

wapuṣṭamā cāpi waraṃ patiṃ tadā; pratītarūpaṃ samawāpya bhūmipam |
bhāwena rāmā ramayāṃ babhūwa wai; wihārakāleṣwawarodhasundarī ||11||






                  41


sūta uwāca||

etasminnewa kāle tu jaratkārurmahātapāḥ |
cacāra pṛthiwīṃ kṛtsnāṃ yatrasāyaṅgṛho muniḥ ||1||

carandīkṣāṃ mahātejā duścarāmakṛtātmabhiḥ |
