tīrtheṣwāplawanaṃ kurwanpuṇyeṣu wicacāra ha ||2||

wāyubhakṣo nirāhāraḥ śuṣyannaharaharmuniḥ |
sa dadarśa pitṛngarte lambamānānadhomukhān ||3||

ekatantwawaśiṣṭaṃ wai wīraṇastambamāśritān |
taṃ ca tantuṃ śanairākhumādadānaṃ bilāśrayam ||4||

nirāhārānkṛśāndīnāngarte''rtāṃstrāṇamicchataḥ |
upasṛtya sa tāndīnāndīnarūpo'bhyabhāṣata ||5||

ke bhawanto'walambante wīraṇastambamāśritāḥ |
durbalaṃ khāditairmūlairākhunā bilawāsinā ||6||

wīraṇastambake mūlaṃ yadapyekamiha sthitam |
tadapyayaṃ śanairākhurādatte daśanaiḥ śitaiḥ ||7||

chetsyate'lpāwaśiṣṭatwādetadapyacirādiwa |
tataḥ stha patitāro'tra garte asminnadhomukhāḥ ||8||

tato me duḥkhamutpannaṃ dṛṣṭwā yuṣmānadhomukhān |
kṛcchrāmāpadamāpannānpriyaṃ kiṃ karawāṇi waḥ ||9||

tapaso'sya caturthena tṛtīyenāpi wā punaḥ |
ardhena wāpi nistartumāpadaṃ brūta māciram ||10||

athawāpi samagreṇa tarantu tapasā mama |
bhawantaḥ sarwa ewāsmātkāmamewaṃ widhīyatām ||11||

pitara ūcuḥ||

ṛddho bhawānbrahmacārī yo nastrātumihecchati |
na tu wiprāgrya tapasā śakyametadwyapohitum ||12||

asti nastāta tapasaḥ phalaṃ prawadatāṃ wara |
santānaprakṣayādbrahmanpatāmo niraye'śucau ||13||

lambatāmiha nastāta na jñānaṃ pratibhāti wai |
yena twāṃ nābhijānīmo loke wikhyātapauruṣam ||14||

ṛddho bhawānmahābhāgo yo naḥ śocyānsuduḥkhitān |
śocasyupetya kāruṇyācchṛṇu ye wai wayaṃ dwija ||15||

yāyāwarā nāma wayamṛṣayaḥ saṃśitawratāḥ |
lokātpuṇyādiha bhraṣṭāḥ santānaprakṣayādwibho ||16||

pranaṣṭaṃ nastapaḥ puṇyaṃ na hi nastanturasti wai |
asti tweko'dya nastantuḥ so'pi nāsti yathā tathā ||17||

mandabhāgyo'lpabhāgyānāṃ bandhuḥ sa kila naḥ kule |
jaratkāruriti khyāto wedawedāṅgapāragaḥ ||18||

niyatātmā mahātmā ca suwrataḥ sumahātapāḥ ||18||

tena sma tapaso lobhātkṛcchramāpāditā wayam |
na tasya bhāryā putro wā bāndhawo wāsti kaścana ||19||

tasmāllambāmahe garte naṣṭasañjñā hyanāthawat |
sa waktawyastwayā dṛṣṭwā asmākaṃ nāthawattayā ||20||

pitaraste'walambante garte dīnā adhomukhāḥ |
sādhu dārānkuruṣweti prajāyasweti cābhibho ||21||

kulatanturhi naḥ śiṣṭastwamewaikastapodhana ||21||

yaṃ tu paśyasi no brahmanwīraṇastambamāśritān |
eṣo'smākaṃ kulastamba āsītswakulawardhanaḥ ||22||

yāni paśyasi wai brahmanmūlānīhāsya wīrudhaḥ |
ete nastantawastāta kālena paribhakṣitāḥ ||23||

yattwetatpaśyasi brahmanmūlamasyārdhabhakṣitam |
tatra lambāmahe sarwe so'pyekastapa āsthitaḥ ||24||

yamākhuṃ paśyasi brahmankāla eṣa mahābalaḥ |
sa taṃ taporataṃ mandaṃ śanaiḥ kṣapayate tudan ||25||

jaratkāruṃ tapolubdhaṃ mandātmānamacetasam ||25||

na hi nastattapastasya tārayiṣyati sattama |
chinnamūlānparibhraṣṭānkālopahatacetasaḥ ||26||

narakapratiṣṭhānpaśyāsmānyathā duṣkṛtinastathā ||26||

asmāsu patiteṣwatra saha pūrwaiḥ pitāmahaiḥ |
chinnaḥ kālena so'pyatra gantā wai narakaṃ tataḥ ||27||

tapo wāpyathawā yajño yaccānyatpāwanaṃ mahat |
tatsarwaṃ na samaṃ tāta santatyeti satāṃ matam ||28||

sa tāta dṛṣṭwā brūyāstwaṃ jaratkāruṃ tapaswinam |
yathādṛṣṭamidaṃ cāsmai twayākhyeyamaśeṣataḥ ||29||

yathā dārānprakuryātsa putrāṃścotpādayedyathā |
tathā brahmaṃstwayā wācyaḥ so'smākaṃ nāthawattayā ||30||






                  42


sūta uwāca||

etacchrutwā jaratkārurduḥkhaśokaparāyaṇaḥ |
uwāca swānpitṛnduḥkhādbāṣpasaṃdigdhayā girā ||1||

ahamewa jaratkāruḥ kilbiṣī bhawatāṃ sutaḥ |
taddaṇḍaṃ dhārayata me duṣkṛterakṛtātmanaḥ ||2||

pitara ūcuḥ||

putra diṣṭyāsi samprāpta imaṃ deśaṃ yadṛcchayā |
kimarthaṃ ca twayā brahmanna kṛto dārasaṅgrahaḥ ||3||

jaratkāruruwāca||

mamāyaṃ pitaro nityaṃ hṛdyarthaḥ pariwartate |
ūrdhwaretāḥ śarīraṃ wai prāpayeyamamutra wai ||4||

ewaṃ dṛṣṭwā tu bhawataḥ śakuntāniwa lambataḥ |
mayā niwartitā buddhirbrahmacaryātpitāmahāḥ ||5||

kariṣye waḥ priyaṃ kāmaṃ niwekṣye nātra saṃśayaḥ |
sanāmnīṃ yadyahaṃ kanyāmupalapsye kadācana ||6||

bhawiṣyati ca yā kācidbhaikṣawatswayamudyatā |
pratigrahītā tāmasmi na bhareyaṃ ca yāmaham ||7||

ewaṃwidhamahaṃ kuryāṃ niweśaṃ prāpnuyāṃ yadi |
anyathā na kariṣye tu satyametatpitāmahāḥ ||8||

sūta uwāca||

ewamuktwā tu sa pitṛṃścacāra pṛthiwīṃ muniḥ |
na ca sma labhate bhāryāṃ wṛddho'yamiti śaunaka ||9||

yadā nirwedamāpannaḥ pitṛbhiścoditastathā |
tadāraṇyaṃ sa gatwoccaiścukrośa bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ ||10||

yāni bhūtāni santīha sthāwarāṇi carāṇi ca |
antarhitāni wā yāni tāni śṛṇwantu me wacaḥ ||11||

ugre tapasi wartantaṃ pitaraścodayanti mām |
niwiśasweti duḥkhārtāsteṣāṃ priyacikīrṣayā ||12||

niweśārthyakhilāṃ bhūmiṃ kanyābhaikṣaṃ carāmi bhoḥ |
daridro duḥkhaśīlaśca pitṛbhiḥ saṃniyojitaḥ ||13||

yasya kanyāsti bhūtasya ye mayeha prakīrtitāḥ |
te me kanyāṃ prayacchantu carataḥ sarwatodiśam ||14||

mama kanyā sanāmnī yā bhaikṣawaccodyatā bhawet |
bhareyaṃ caiwa yāṃ nāhaṃ tāṃ me kanyāṃ prayacchata ||15||

tataste pannagā ye wai jaratkārau samāhitāḥ |
tāmādāya prawṛttiṃ te wāsukeḥ pratyawedayan ||16||

teṣāṃ śrutwā sa nāgendraḥ kanyāṃ tāṃ samalaṅkṛtām |
pragṛhyāraṇyamagamatsamīpaṃ tasya pannagaḥ ||17||

tatra tāṃ bhaikṣawatkanyāṃ prādāttasmai mahātmane |
nāgendro wāsukirbrahmanna sa tāṃ pratyagṛhṇata ||18||

asanāmeti wai matwā bharaṇe cāwicārite |
mokṣabhāwe sthitaścāpi dwandwībhūtaḥ parigrahe ||19||

tato nāma sa kanyāyāḥ papraccha bhṛgunandana |
wāsuke bharaṇaṃ cāsyā na kuryāmityuwāca ha ||20||






                  43


sūta uwāca||

wāsukistwabrawīdwākyaṃ jaratkārumṛṣiṃ tadā |
sanāmā tawa kanyeyaṃ swasā me tapasānwitā ||1||

bhariṣyāmi ca te bhāryāṃ pratīcchemāṃ dwijottama |
rakṣaṇaṃ ca kariṣye'syāḥ sarwaśaktyā tapodhana ||2||

pratiśrute tu nāgena bhariṣye bhaginīmiti |
jaratkārustadā weśma bhujagasya jagāma ha ||3||

tatra mantrawidāṃ śreṣṭhastapowṛddho mahāwrataḥ |
jagrāha pāṇiṃ dharmātmā widhimantrapuraskṛtam ||4||

tato wāsagṛhaṃ śubhraṃ pannagendrasya saṃmatam |
jagāma bhāryāmādāya stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ ||5||

śayanaṃ tatra wai kḷptaṃ spardhyāstaraṇasaṃwṛtam |
tatra bhāryāsahāyaḥ sa jaratkāruruwāsa ha ||6||

sa tatra samayaṃ cakre bhāryayā saha sattamaḥ |
wipriyaṃ me na kartawyaṃ na ca wācyaṃ kadācana ||7||

tyajeyamapriye hi twāṃ kṛte wāsaṃ ca te gṛhe |
etadgṛhāṇa wacanaṃ mayā yatsamudīritam ||8||

tataḥ paramasaṃwignā swasā nāgapatestu sā |
atiduḥkhānwitā wācaṃ tamuwācaiwamastwiti ||9||

tathaiwa sā ca bhartāraṃ duḥkhaśīlamupācarat |
upāyaiḥ śwetakākīyaiḥ priyakāmā yaśaswinī ||10||

ṛtukāle tataḥ snātā kadācidwāsukeḥ swasā |
bhartāraṃ taṃ yathānyāyamupatasthe mahāmunim ||11||

tatra tasyāḥ samabhawadgarbho jwalanasaṃnibhaḥ |
atīwa tapasā yukto waiśwānarasamadyutiḥ ||12||

śuklapakṣe yathā somo wyawardhata tathaiwa saḥ ||12||

tataḥ katipayāhasya jaratkārurmahātapāḥ |
utsaṅge'syāḥ śiraḥ kṛtwā suṣwāpa parikhinnawat ||13||

tasmiṃśca supte wiprendre sawitāstamiyādgirim |
ahnaḥ parikṣaye brahmaṃstataḥ sācintayattadā ||14||

wāsukerbhaginī bhītā dharmalopānmanaswinī ||14||

kiṃ nu me sukṛtaṃ bhūyādbharturutthāpanaṃ na wā |
duḥkhaśīlo hi dharmātmā kathaṃ nāsyāparādhnuyām ||15||

kopo wā dharmaśīlasya dharmalopo'tha wā punaḥ |
dharmalopo garīyānwai syādatretyakaronmanaḥ ||16||

utthāpayiṣye yadyenaṃ dhruwaṃ kopaṃ kariṣyati |
dharmalopo bhawedasya sandhyātikramaṇe dhruwam ||17||

iti niścitya manasā jaratkārurbhujaṅgamā |
tamṛṣiṃ dīptatapasaṃ śayānamanalopamam ||18||

uwācedaṃ wacaḥ ślakṣṇaṃ tato madhurabhāṣiṇī ||18||

uttiṣṭha twaṃ mahābhāga sūryo'stamupagacchati |
sandhyāmupāsswa bhagawannapaḥ spṛṣṭwā yatawrataḥ ||19||

prāduṣkṛtāgnihotro'yaṃ muhūrto ramyadāruṇaḥ |
sandhyā prawartate ceyaṃ paścimāyāṃ diśi prabho ||20||

ewamuktaḥ sa bhagawāñjaratkārurmahātapāḥ |
bhāryāṃ prasphuramāṇoṣṭha idaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||21||

awamānaḥ prayukto'yaṃ twayā mama bhujaṅgame |
samīpe te na watsyāmi gamiṣyāmi yathāgatam ||22||

na hi tejo'sti wāmoru mayi supte wibhāwasoḥ |
astaṃ gantuṃ yathākālamiti me hṛdi wartate ||23||

na cāpyawamatasyeha wastuṃ roceta kasyacit |
kiṃ punardharmaśīlasya mama wā madwidhasya wā ||24||

ewamuktā jaratkārurbhartrā hṛdayakampanam |
abrawīdbhaginī tatra wāsukeḥ saṃniweśane ||25||

nāwamānātkṛtawatī tawāhaṃ pratibodhanam |
dharmalopo na te wipra syādityetatkṛtaṃ mayā ||26||

uwāca bhāryāmityukto jaratkārurmahātapāḥ |
ṛṣiḥ kopasamāwiṣṭastyaktukāmo bhujaṅgamām ||27||

na me wāganṛtaṃ prāha gamiṣye'haṃ bhujaṅgame |
samayo hyeṣa me pūrwaṃ twayā saha mithaḥ kṛtaḥ ||28||

sukhamasmyuṣito bhadre brūyāstwaṃ bhrātaraṃ śubhe |
ito mayi gate bhīru gataḥ sa bhagawāniti ||29||

twaṃ cāpi mayi niṣkrānte na śokaṃ kartumarhasi ||29||

ityuktā sānawadyāṅgī pratyuwāca patiṃ tadā |
jaratkāruṃ jaratkāruścintāśokaparāyaṇā ||30||

bāṣpagadgadayā wācā mukhena pariśuṣyatā |
kṛtāñjalirwarārohā paryaśrunayanā tataḥ ||31||

dhairyamālambya wāmorūrhṛdayena prawepatā ||31||

na māmarhasi dharmajña parityaktumanāgasam |
dharme sthitāṃ sthito dharme sadā priyahite ratām ||32||

pradāne kāraṇaṃ yacca mama tubhyaṃ dwijottama |
tadalabdhawatīṃ mandāṃ kiṃ māṃ wakṣyati wāsukhiḥ ||33||

mātṛśāpābhibhūtānāṃ jñātīnāṃ mama sattama |
apatyamīpṣitaṃ twattastacca tāwanna dṛśyate ||34||

twatto hyapatyalābhena jñātīnāṃ me śiwaṃ bhawet |
samprayogo bhawennāyaṃ mama moghastwayā dwija ||35||

jñātīnāṃ hitamicchantī bhagawaṃstwāṃ prasādaye |
imamawyaktarūpaṃ me garbhamādhāya sattama ||36||

kathaṃ tyaktwā mahātmā sangantumicchasyanāgasam ||36||

ewamuktastu sa munirbhāryāṃ wacanamabrawīt |
yadyuktamanurūpaṃ ca jaratkārustapodhanaḥ ||37||

astyeṣa garbhaḥ subhage tawa waiśwānaropamaḥ |
ṛṣiḥ paramadharmātmā wedawedāṅgapāragaḥ ||38||

ewamuktwā sa dharmātmā jaratkārurmahānṛṣiḥ |
ugrāya tapase bhūyo jagāma kṛtaniścayaḥ ||39||






                  44


sūta uwāca||

gatamātraṃ tu bhartāraṃ jaratkārurawedayat |
bhrātustwaritamāgamya yathātathyaṃ tapodhana ||1||

tataḥ sa bhujagaśreṣṭhaḥ śrutwā sumahadapriyam |
uwāca bhaginīṃ dīnāṃ tadā dīnataraḥ swayam ||2||

jānāsi bhadre yatkāryaṃ pradāne kāraṇaṃ ca yat |
pannagānāṃ hitārthāya putraste syāttato yadi ||3||

sa sarpasatrātkila no mokṣayiṣyati wīryawān |
ewaṃ pitāmahaḥ pūrwamuktawānmāṃ suraiḥ saha ||4||

apyasti garbhaḥ subhage tasmātte munisattamāt |
na cecchāmyaphalaṃ tasya dārakarma manīṣiṇaḥ ||5||

kāmaṃ ca mama na nyāyyaṃ praṣṭuṃ twāṃ kāryamīdṛśam |
kiṃ tu kāryagarīyastwāttatastwāhamacūcudam ||6||

durwāsatāṃ widitwā ca bhartuste'titapaswinaḥ |
nainamanwāgamiṣyāmi kadāciddhi śapetsa mām ||7||

ācakṣwa bhadre bhartustwaṃ sarwamewa wiceṣṭitam |
śalyamuddhara me ghoraṃ bhadre hṛdi cirasthitam ||8||

jaratkārustato wākyamityuktā pratyabhāṣata |
āśwāsayantī santaptaṃ wāsukiṃ pannageśwaram ||9||

pṛṣṭo mayāpatyahetoḥ sa mahātmā mahātapāḥ |
astītyudaramuddiśya mamedaṃ gatawāṃśca saḥ ||10||

swaireṣwapi na tenāhaṃ smarāmi witathaṃ kwacit |
uktapūrwaṃ kuto rājansāmparāye sa wakṣyati ||11||

na santāpastwayā kāryaḥ kāryaṃ prati bhujaṅgame |
utpatsyati hi te putro jwalanārkasamadyutiḥ ||12||

ityuktwā hi sa māṃ bhrātargato bhartā tapowanam |
tasmādwyetu paraṃ duḥkhaṃ tawedaṃ manasi sthitam ||13||

etacchrutwā sa nāgendro wāsukiḥ parayā mudā |
ewamastwiti tadwākyaṃ bhaginyāḥ pratyagṛhṇata ||14||

sāntwamānārthadānaiśca pūjayā cānurūpayā |
sodaryāṃ pūjayāmāsa swasāraṃ pannagottamaḥ ||15||

tataḥ sa wawṛdhe garbho mahātejā rawiprabhaḥ |
yathā somo dwijaśreṣṭha śuklapakṣodito diwi ||16||

yathākālaṃ tu sā brahmanprajajñe bhujagaswasā |
kumāraṃ dewagarbhābhaṃ pitṛmātṛbhayāpaham ||17||

wawṛdhe sa ca tatraiwa nāgarājaniweśane |
wedāṃścādhijage sāṅgānbhārgawāccyawanātmajāt ||18||

caritawrato bāla ewa buddhisattwaguṇānwitaḥ |
nāma cāsyābhawatkhyātaṃ lokeṣwāstīka ityuta ||19||

astītyuktwā gato yasmātpitā garbhasthamewa tam |
wanaṃ tasmādidaṃ tasya nāmāstīketi wiśrutam ||20||

sa bāla ewa tatrasthaścarannamitabuddhimān |
gṛhe pannagarājasya prayatnātparyarakṣyata ||21||

bhagawāniwa deweśaḥ śūlapāṇirhiraṇyadaḥ |
wiwardhamānaḥ sarwāṃstānpannagānabhyaharṣayat ||22||






                  45


śaunaka uwāca||

yadapṛcchattadā rājā mantriṇo janamejayaḥ |
pituḥ swargagatiṃ tanme wistareṇa punarwada ||1||

sūta uwāca||

śṛṇu brahmanyathā pṛṣṭā mantriṇo nṛpatestadā |
ākhyātawantaste sarwe nidhanaṃ tatparikṣitaḥ ||2||

janamejaya uwāca||

jānanti tu bhawantastadyathāwṛttaḥ pitā mama |
āsīdyathā ca nidhanaṃ gataḥ kāle mahāyaśāḥ ||3||

śrutwā bhawatsakāśāddhi piturwṛttamaśeṣataḥ |
kalyāṇaṃ pratipatsyāmi wiparītaṃ na jātu cit ||4||

sūta uwāca||

mantriṇo'thābruwanwākyaṃ pṛṣṭāstena mahātmanā |
sarwadharmawidaḥ prājñā rājānaṃ janamejayam ||5||

dharmātmā ca mahātmā ca prajāpālaḥ pitā tawa |
āsīdiha yathāwṛttaḥ sa mahātmā śṛṇuṣwa tat ||6||

cāturwarṇyaṃ swadharmasthaṃ sa kṛtwā paryarakṣata |
dharmato dharmawidrājā dharmo wigrahawāniwa ||7||

rarakṣa pṛthiwīṃ dewīṃ śrīmānatulawikramaḥ |
dweṣṭārastasya naiwāsansa ca na dweṣṭi kañcana ||8||

samaḥ sarweṣu bhūteṣu prajāpatiriwābhawat ||8||

brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā waiśyāḥ śūdrāścaiwa swakarmasu |
sthitāḥ sumanaso rājaṃstena rājñā swanuṣṭhitāḥ ||9||

widhawānāthakṛpaṇānwikalāṃśca babhāra saḥ |
sudarśaḥ sarwabhūtānāmāsītsoma iwāparaḥ ||10||

tuṣṭapuṣṭajanaḥ śrīmānsatyawāgdṛḍhawikramaḥ |
dhanurwede ca śiṣyo'bhūnnṛpaḥ śāradwatasya saḥ ||11||

gowindasya priyaścāsītpitā te janamejaya |
lokasya caiwa sarwasya priya āsīnmahāyaśāḥ ||12||

parikṣīṇeṣu kuruṣu uttarāyāmajāyata |
parikṣidabhawattena saubhadrasyātmajo balī ||13||

rājadharmārthakuśalo yuktaḥ sarwaguṇairnṛpaḥ |
jitendriyaścātmawāṃśca medhāwī wṛddhasewitaḥ ||14||

ṣaḍwargawinmahābuddhirnītidharmawiduttamaḥ |
prajā imāstawa pitā ṣaṣṭiṃ warṣāṇyapālayat ||15||

tato diṣṭāntamāpannaḥ sarpeṇānatiwartitam ||15||

tatastwaṃ puruṣaśreṣṭha dharmeṇa pratipediwān |
idaṃ warṣasahasrāya rājyaṃ kurukulāgatam ||16||

bāla ewābhijāto'si sarwabhūtānupālakaḥ ||16||

janamejaya uwāca||

nāsminkule jātu babhūwa rājā; yo na prajānāṃ hitakṛtpriyaśca |
wiśeṣataḥ prekṣya pitāmahānāṃ; wṛttaṃ mahadwṛttaparāyaṇānām ||17||

kathaṃ nidhanamāpannaḥ pitā mama tathāwidhaḥ |
ācakṣadhwaṃ yathāwanme śrotumicchāmi tattwataḥ ||18||

sūta uwāca||

ewaṃ sañcoditā rājñā mantriṇaste narādhipam |
ūcuḥ sarwe yathāwṛttaṃ rājñaḥ priyahite ratāḥ ||19||

babhūwa mṛgayāśīlastawa rājanpitā sadā |
yathā pāṇḍurmahābhāgo dhanurdharawaro yudhi ||20||

asmāswāsajya sarwāṇi rājakāryāṇyaśeṣataḥ ||20||

sa kadācidwanacaro mṛgaṃ wiwyādha patriṇā |
widdhwā cānwasarattūrṇaṃ taṃ mṛgaṃ gahane wane ||21||

padātirbaddhanistriṃśastatāyudhakalāpawān |
na cāsasāda gahane mṛgaṃ naṣṭaṃ pitā tawa ||22||

pariśrānto wayaḥsthaśca ṣaṣṭiwarṣo jarānwitaḥ |
kṣudhitaḥ sa mahāraṇye dadarśa munimantike ||23||

sa taṃ papraccha rājendro muniṃ maunawratānwitam |
na ca kiñciduwācainaṃ sa muniḥ pṛcchato'pi san ||24||

tato rājā kṣucchramārtastaṃ muniṃ sthāṇuwatsthitam |
maunawratadharaṃ śāntaṃ sadyo manyuwaśaṃ yayau ||25||

na bubodha hi taṃ rājā maunawratadharaṃ munim |
sa taṃ manyusamāwiṣṭo dharṣayāmāsa te pitā ||26||

mṛtaṃ sarpaṃ dhanuṣkoṭyā samutkṣipya dharātalāt |
tasya śuddhātmanaḥ prādātskandhe bharatasattama ||27||

na cowāca sa medhāwī tamatho sādhwasādhu wā |
tasthau tathaiwa cākrudhyansarpaṃ skandhena dhārayan ||28||






                  46


mantriṇa ūcuḥ||

tataḥ sa rājā rājendra skandhe tasya bhujaṅgamam |
muneḥ kṣutkṣāma āsajya swapuraṃ punarāyayau ||1||

ṛṣestasya tu putro'bhūdgawi jāto mahāyaśāḥ |
śṛṅgī nāma mahātejāstigmawīryo'tikopanaḥ ||2||

brahmāṇaṃ so'bhyupāgamya muniḥ pūjāṃ cakāra ha |
anujñāto gatastatra śṛṅgī śuśrāwa taṃ tadā ||3||

sakhyuḥ sakāśātpitaraṃ pitrā te dharṣitaṃ tathā ||3||

mṛtaṃ sarpaṃ samāsaktaṃ pitrā te janamejaya |
wahantaṃ kuruśārdūla skandhenānapakāriṇam ||4||

tapaswinamatīwātha taṃ muniprawaraṃ nṛpa |
jitendriyaṃ wiśuddhaṃ ca sthitaṃ karmaṇyathādbhute ||5||

tapasā dyotitātmānaṃ sweṣwaṅgeṣu yataṃ tathā |
śubhācāraṃ śubhakathaṃ susthiraṃ tamalolupam ||6||

akṣudramanasūyaṃ ca wṛddhaṃ maunawrate sthitam |
śaraṇyaṃ sarwabhūtānāṃ pitrā wiprakṛtaṃ tawa ||7||

śaśāpātha sa tacchrutwā pitaraṃ te ruṣānwitaḥ |
ṛṣeḥ putro mahātejā bālo'pi sthawirairwaraḥ ||8||

sa kṣipramudakaṃ spṛṣṭwā roṣādidamuwāca ha |
pitaraṃ te'bhisandhāya tejasā prajwalanniwa ||9||

anāgasi gurau yo me mṛtaṃ sarpamawāsṛjat |
taṃ nāgastakṣakaḥ kruddhastejasā sādayiṣyati ||10||

saptarātrāditaḥ pāpaṃ paśya me tapaso balam ||10||

ityuktwā prayayau tatra pitā yatrāsya so'bhawat |
dṛṣṭwā ca pitaraṃ tasmai śāpaṃ taṃ pratyawedayat ||11||

sa cāpi muniśārdūlaḥ preṣayāmāsa te pituḥ |
śapto'si mama putreṇa yatto bhawa mahīpate ||12||

takṣakastwāṃ mahārāja tejasā sādayiṣyati ||12||

śrutwā tu tadwaco ghoraṃ pitā te janamejaya |
yatto'bhawatparitrastastakṣakātpannagottamāt ||13||

tatastasmiṃstu diwase saptame samupasthite |
rājñaḥ samīpaṃ brahmarṣiḥ kāśyapo gantumaicchata ||14||

taṃ dadarśātha nāgendraḥ kāśyapaṃ takṣakastadā |
tamabrawītpannagendraḥ kāśyapaṃ twaritaṃ wrajan ||15||

kwa bhawāṃstwarito yāti kiṃ ca kāryaṃ cikīrṣati ||15||

kāśyapa uwāca||

yatra rājā kuruśreṣṭhaḥ parikṣinnāma wai dwija |
takṣakeṇa bhujaṅgena dhakṣyate kila tatra wai ||16||

gacchāmyahaṃ taṃ twaritaḥ sadyaḥ kartumapajwaram |
mayābhipannaṃ taṃ cāpi na sarpo dharṣayiṣyati ||17||

takṣaka uwāca||

kimarthaṃ taṃ mayā daṣṭaṃ sañjīwayitumicchasi |
brūhi kāmamahaṃ te'dya dadmi swaṃ weśma gamyatām ||18||

mantriṇa ūcuḥ||

dhanalipsurahaṃ tatra yāmītyuktaśca tena saḥ |
tamuwāca mahātmānaṃ mānayañślakṣṇayā girā ||19||

yāwaddhanaṃ prārthayase tasmādrājñastato'dhikam |
gṛhāṇa matta ewa twaṃ saṃniwartaswa cānagha ||20||

sa ewamukto nāgena kāśyapo dwipadāṃ waraḥ |
labdhwā wittaṃ niwawṛte takṣakādyāwadīpsitam ||21||

tasminpratigate wipre chadmanopetya takṣakaḥ |
taṃ nṛpaṃ nṛpatiśreṣṭha pitaraṃ dhārmikaṃ tawa ||22||

prāsādasthaṃ yattamapi dagdhawānwiṣawahninā |
tatastwaṃ puruṣawyāghra wijayāyābhiṣecitaḥ ||23||

etaddṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ cāpi yathāwannṛpasattama |
asmābhirnikhilaṃ sarwaṃ kathitaṃ te sudāruṇam ||24||

śrutwā caitaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha pārthiwasya parābhawam |
asya carṣeruttaṅkasya widhatswa yadanantaram ||25||

janamejaya uwāca||

etattu śrotumicchāmi aṭawyāṃ nirjane wane |
saṃwādaṃ pannagendrasya kāśyapasya ca yattadā ||26||

kena dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ cāpi bhawatāṃ śrotramāgatam |
śrutwā cātha widhāsyāmi pannagāntakarīṃ matim ||27||

mantriṇa ūcuḥ||

śṛṇu rājanyathāsmākaṃ yenaitatkathitaṃ purā |
samāgamaṃ dwijendrasya pannagendrasya cādhwani ||28||

tasminwṛkṣe naraḥ kaścidindhanārthāya pārthiwa |
wicinwanpūrwamārūḍhaḥ śuṣkaśākhaṃ wanaspatim ||29||

abudhyamānau taṃ tatra wṛkṣasthaṃ pannagadwijau ||29||

sa tu tenaiwa wṛkṣeṇa bhasmībhūto'bhawattadā |
dwijaprabhāwādrājendra jīwitaḥ sawanaspatiḥ ||30||

tena gatwā nṛpaśreṣṭha nagare'sminniweditam |
yathāwṛttaṃ tu tatsarwaṃ takṣakasya dwijasya ca ||31||

etatte kathitaṃ rājanyathāwṛttaṃ yathāśrutam |
śrutwā tu nṛpaśārdūla prakuruṣwa yathepsitam ||32||

sūta uwāca||

mantriṇāṃ tu wacaḥ śrutwā sa rājā janamejayaḥ |
paryatapyata duḥkhārtaḥ pratyapiṃṣatkare karam ||33||

niḥśwāsamuṣṇamasakṛddīrghaṃ rājīwalocanaḥ |
mumocāśrūṇi ca tadā netrābhyāṃ pratataṃ nṛpaḥ ||34||

uwāca ca mahīpālo duḥkhaśokasamanwitaḥ ||34||

śrutwaitadbhawatāṃ wākyaṃ piturme swargatiṃ prati |
niściteyaṃ mama matiryā wai tāṃ me nibodhata ||35||

anantaramahaṃ manye takṣakāya durātmane |
pratikartawyamityewa yena me hiṃsitaḥ pitā ||36||

ṛṣerhi śṛṅgerwacanaṃ kṛtwā dagdhwā ca pārthiwam |
yadi gacchedasau pāpo nanu jīwetpitā mama ||37||

parihīyeta kiṃ tasya yadi jīwetsa pārthiwaḥ |
kāśyapasya prasādena mantriṇāṃ sunayena ca ||38||

sa tu wāritawānmohātkāśyapaṃ dwijasattamam |
sañjijīwayiṣuṃ prāptaṃ rājānamaparājitam ||39||

mahānatikramo hyeṣa takṣakasya durātmanaḥ |
dwijasya yo'dadaddrawyaṃ mā nṛpaṃ jīwayediti ||40||

uttaṅkasya priyaṃ kurwannātmanaśca mahatpriyam |
bhawatāṃ caiwa sarweṣāṃ yāsyāmyapacitiṃ pituḥ ||41||






                  47


sūta uwāca||

ewamuktwā tataḥ śrīmānmantribhiścānumoditaḥ |
āruroha pratijñāṃ sa sarpasatrāya pārthiwaḥ ||1||

brahmanbharataśārdūlo rājā pārikṣitastadā ||1||

purohitamathāhūya ṛtwijaṃ wasudhādhipaḥ |
abrawīdwākyasampannaḥ sampadarthakaraṃ wacaḥ ||2||

yo me hiṃsitawāṃstātaṃ takṣakaḥ sa durātmawān |
pratikuryāṃ yathā tasya tadbhawanto bruwantu me ||3||

api tatkarma widitaṃ bhawatāṃ yena pannagam |
takṣakaṃ sampradīpte'gnau prāpsye'haṃ sahabāndhawam ||4||

yathā tena pitā mahyaṃ pūrwaṃ dagdho wiṣāgninā |
tathāhamapi taṃ pāpaṃ dagdhumicchāmi pannagam ||5||

ṛtwija ūcuḥ||

asti rājanmahatsatraṃ twadarthaṃ dewanirmitam |
sarpasatramiti khyātaṃ purāṇe kathyate nṛpa ||6||

āhartā tasya satrasya twannānyo'sti narādhipa |
iti paurāṇikāḥ prāhurasmākaṃ cāsti sa kratuḥ ||7||

sūta uwāca||

ewamuktaḥ sa rājarṣirmene sarpaṃ hi takṣakam |
hutāśanamukhaṃ dīptaṃ prawiṣṭamiti sattama ||8||

tato'brawīnmantrawidastānrājā brāhmaṇāṃstadā |
āhariṣyāmi tatsatraṃ sambhārāḥ sambhriyantu me ||9||

tataste ṛtwijastasya śāstrato dwijasattama |
deśaṃ taṃ māpayāmāsuryajñāyatanakāraṇāt ||10||

yathāwajjñānawiduṣaḥ sarwe buddhyā paraṃ gatāḥ ||10||

ṛddhyā paramayā yuktamiṣṭaṃ dwijagaṇāyutam |
prabhūtadhanadhānyāḍhyamṛtwigbhiḥ suniweśitam ||11||

nirmāya cāpi widhiwadyajñāyatanamīpsitam |
rājānaṃ dīkṣayāmāsuḥ sarpasatrāptaye tadā ||12||

idaṃ cāsīttatra pūrwaṃ sarpasatre bhawiṣyati |
nimittaṃ mahadutpannaṃ yajñawighnakaraṃ tadā ||13||

yajñasyāyatane tasminkriyamāṇe waco'brawīt |
sthapatirbuddhisampanno wāstuwidyāwiśāradaḥ ||14||

ityabrawītsūtradhāraḥ sūtaḥ paurāṇikastadā |
yasmindeśe ca kāle ca māpaneyaṃ prawartitā ||15||

brāhmaṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ kṛtwā nāyaṃ saṃsthāsyate kratuḥ ||15||

etacchrutwā tu rājā sa prāgdīkṣākālamabrawīt |
kṣattāraṃ neha me kaścidajñātaḥ prawiśediti ||16||

tataḥ karma prawawṛte sarpasatre widhānataḥ |
paryakrāmaṃśca widhiwatswe swe karmaṇi yājakāḥ ||17||

paridhāya kṛṣṇawāsāṃsi dhūmasaṃraktalocanāḥ |
juhuwurmantrawaccaiwa samiddhaṃ jātawedasam ||18||

kampayantaśca sarweṣāmuragāṇāṃ manāṃsi te |
sarpānājuhuwustatra sarwānagnimukhe tadā ||19||

tataḥ sarpāḥ samāpetuḥ pradīpte hawyawāhane |
wiweṣṭamānāḥ kṛpaṇā āhwayantaḥ parasparam ||20||

wisphurantaḥ śwasantaśca weṣṭayantastathā pare |
pucchaiḥ śirobhiśca bhṛśaṃ citrabhānuṃ prapedire ||21||

śwetāḥ kṛṣṇāśca nīlāśca sthawirāḥ śiśawastathā |
ruwanto bhairawānnādānpeturdīpte wibhāwasau ||22||

ewaṃ śatasahasrāṇi prayutānyarbudāni ca |
awaśāni winaṣṭāni pannagānāṃ dwijottama ||23||

indurā iwa tatrānye hastihastā iwāpare |
mattā iwa ca mātaṅgā mahākāyā mahābalāḥ ||24||

uccāwacāśca bahawo nānāwarṇā wiṣolbaṇāḥ |
ghorāśca parighaprakhyā dandaśūkā mahābalāḥ ||25||

prapeturagnāwuragā mātṛwāgdaṇḍapīḍitāḥ ||25||






                  48


śaunaka uwāca||

sarpasatre tadā rājñaḥ pāṇḍaweyasya dhīmataḥ |
janamejayasya ke twāsannṛtwijaḥ paramarṣayaḥ ||1||

ke sadasyā babhūwuśca sarpasatre sudāruṇe |
wiṣādajanane'tyarthaṃ pannagānāṃ mahābhaye ||2||

sarwaṃ wistaratastāta bhawāñśaṃsitumarhati |
sarpasatrawidhānajñā wijñeyāste hi sūtaja ||3||

sūta uwāca||

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi nāmānīha manīṣiṇām |
ye ṛtwijaḥ sadasyāśca tasyāsannṛpatestadā ||4||

tatra hotā babhūwātha brāhmaṇaścaṇḍabhārgawaḥ |
cyawanasyānwaye jātaḥ khyāto wedawidāṃ waraḥ ||5||

udgātā brāhmaṇo wṛddho widwānkautsāryajaiminiḥ |
brahmābhawacchārṅgarawo adhwaryurbodhapiṅgalaḥ ||6||

sadasyaścābhawadwyāsaḥ putraśiṣyasahāyawān |
uddālakaḥ śamaṭhakaḥ śwetaketuśca pañcamaḥ ||7||

asito dewalaścaiwa nāradaḥ parwatastathā |
ātreyaḥ kuṇḍajaṭharo dwijaḥ kuṭighaṭastathā ||8||

wātsyaḥ śrutaśrawā wṛddhastapaḥswādhyāyaśīlawān |
kahoḍo dewaśarmā ca maudgalyaḥ śamasaubharaḥ ||9||

ete cānye ca bahawo brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśitawratāḥ |
sadasyā abhawaṃstatra satre pārikṣitasya ha ||10||

juhwatswṛtwikṣwatha tadā sarpasatre mahākratau |
ahayaḥ prāpataṃstatra ghorāḥ prāṇibhayāwahāḥ ||11||

wasāmedowahāḥ kulyā nāgānāṃ samprawartitāḥ |
wawau gandhaśca tumulo dahyatāmaniśaṃ tadā ||12||

patatāṃ caiwa nāgānāṃ dhiṣṭhitānāṃ tathāmbare |
aśrūyatāniśaṃ śabdaḥ pacyatāṃ cāgninā bhṛśam ||13||

takṣakastu sa nāgendraḥ puraṃdaraniweśanam |
gataḥ śrutwaiwa rājānaṃ dīkṣitaṃ janamejayam ||14||

tataḥ sarwaṃ yathāwṛttamākhyāya bhujagottamaḥ |
agacchaccharaṇaṃ bhīta āgaskṛtwā puraṃdaram ||15||

tamindraḥ prāha suprīto na tawāstīha takṣaka |
bhayaṃ nāgendra tasmādwai sarpasatrātkathañcana ||16||

prasādito mayā pūrwaṃ tawārthāya pitāmahaḥ |
tasmāttawa bhayaṃ nāsti wyetu te mānaso jwaraḥ ||17||

ewamāśwāsitastena tataḥ sa bhujagottamaḥ |
uwāsa bhawane tatra śakrasya muditaḥ sukhī ||18||

ajasraṃ nipatatswagnau nāgeṣu bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ |
alpaśeṣaparīwāro wāsukiḥ paryatapyata ||19||

kaśmalaṃ cāwiśadghoraṃ wāsukiṃ pannageśwaram |
sa ghūrṇamānahṛdayo bhaginīmidamabrawīt ||20||

dahyante'ṅgāni me bhadre diśo na pratibhānti ca |
sīdāmīwa ca saṃmohādghūrṇatīwa ca me manaḥ ||21||

dṛṣṭirbhramati me'tīwa hṛdayaṃ dīryatīwa ca |
patiṣyāmyawaśo'dyāhaṃ tasmindīpte wibhāwasau ||22||

pārikṣitasya yajño'sau wartate'smajjighāṃsayā |
wyaktaṃ mayāpi gantawyaṃ pitṛrājaniweśanam ||23||

ayaṃ sa kālaḥ samprāpto yadarthamasi me swasaḥ |
jaratkāroḥ purā dattā sā trāhyasmānsabāndhawān ||24||

āstīkaḥ kila yajñaṃ taṃ wartantaṃ bhujagottame |
pratiṣetsyati māṃ pūrwaṃ swayamāha pitāmahaḥ ||25||

tadwatse brūhi watsaṃ swaṃ kumāraṃ wṛddhasaṃmatam |
mamādya twaṃ sabhṛtyasya mokṣārthaṃ wedawittamam ||26||






                  49


sūta uwāca||

tata āhūya putraṃ swaṃ jaratkārurbhujaṅgamā |
wāsukernāgarājasya wacanādidamabrawīt ||1||

ahaṃ tawa pituḥ putra bhrātrā dattā nimittataḥ |
kālaḥ sa cāyaṃ samprāptastatkuruṣwa yathātatham ||2||

āstīka uwāca||

kiṃnimittaṃ mama piturdattā twaṃ mātulena me |
tanmamācakṣwa tattwena śrutwā kartāsmi tattathā ||3||

sūta uwāca||

tata ācaṣṭa sā tasmai bāndhawānāṃ hitaiṣiṇī |
bhaginī nāgarājasya jaratkārurawiklawā ||4||

bhujagānāmaśeṣāṇāṃ mātā kadrūriti śrutiḥ |
tayā śaptā ruṣitayā sutā yasmānnibodha tat ||5||

ucchaiḥśrawāḥ so'śwarājo yanmithyā na kṛto mama |
winatānimittaṃ paṇite dāsabhāwāya putrakāḥ ||6||

janamejayasya wo yajñe dhakṣyatyanilasārathiḥ |
tatra pañcatwamāpannāḥ pretalokaṃ gamiṣyatha ||7||

tāṃ ca śaptawatīmewaṃ sākṣāllokapitāmahaḥ |
ewamastwiti tadwākyaṃ prowācānumumoda ca ||8||

wāsukiścāpi tacchrutwā pitāmahawacastadā |
amṛte mathite tāta dewāñśaraṇamīyiwān ||9||

siddhārthāśca surāḥ sarwe prāpyāmṛtamanuttamam |
bhrātaraṃ me puraskṛtya prajāpatimupāgaman ||10||

te taṃ prasādayāmāsurdewāḥ sarwe pitāmaham |
rājñā wāsukinā sārdhaṃ sa śāpo na bhawediti ||11||

wāsukirnāgarājo'yaṃ duḥkhito jñātikāraṇāt |
abhiśāpaḥ sa mātrāsya bhagawanna bhawediti ||12||

brahmowāca||

jaratkārurjaratkāruṃ yāṃ bhāryāṃ samawāpsyati |
tatra jāto dwijaḥ śāpādbhujagānmokṣayiṣyati ||13||

jaratkāruruwāca||

etacchrutwā tu wacanaṃ wāsukiḥ pannageśwaraḥ |
prādānmāmamaraprakhya tawa pitre mahātmane ||14||

prāgewānāgate kāle tatra twaṃ mayyajāyathāḥ ||14||

ayaṃ sa kālaḥ samprāpto bhayānnastrātumarhasi |
bhrātaraṃ caiwa me tasmāttrātumarhasi pāwakāt ||15||

amoghaṃ naḥ kṛtaṃ tatsyādyadahaṃ tawa dhīmate |
pitre dattā wimokṣārthaṃ kathaṃ wā putra manyase ||16||

sūta uwāca||

ewamuktastathetyuktwā so'stīko mātaraṃ tadā |
abrawīdduḥkhasantaptaṃ wāsukiṃ jīwayanniwa ||17||

ahaṃ twāṃ mokṣayiṣyāmi wāsuke pannagottama |
tasmācchāpānmahāsattwa satyametadbrawīmi te ||18||

bhawa swasthamanā nāga na hi te widyate bhayam |
prayatiṣye tathā saumya yathā śreyo bhawiṣyati ||19||

na me wāganṛtaṃ prāha swaireṣwapi kuto'nyathā ||19||

taṃ wai nṛpawaraṃ gatwā dīkṣitaṃ janamejayam |
wāgbhirmaṅgalayuktābhistoṣayiṣye'dya mātula ||20||

yathā sa yajño nṛpaternirwartiṣyati sattama ||20||

sa sambhāwaya nāgendra mayi sarwaṃ mahāmate |
na te mayi mano jātu mithyā bhawitumarhati ||21||

wāsukiruwāca||

āstīka parighūrṇāmi hṛdayaṃ me widīryate |
diśaśca na prajānāmi brahmadaṇḍanipīḍitaḥ ||22||

āstīka uwāca||

na santāpastwayā kāryaḥ kathañcitpannagottama |
dīptādagneḥ samutpannaṃ nāśayiṣyāmi te bhayam ||23||

brahmadaṇḍaṃ mahāghoraṃ kālāgnisamatejasam |
nāśayiṣyāmi mātra twaṃ bhayaṃ kārṣīḥ kathañcana ||24||

sūta uwāca||

tataḥ sa wāsukerghoramapanīya manojwaram |
ādhāya cātmano'ṅgeṣu jagāma twarito bhṛśam ||25||

janamejayasya taṃ yajñaṃ sarwaiḥ samuditaṃ guṇaiḥ |
mokṣāya bhujagendrāṇāmāstīko dwijasattamaḥ ||26||

sa gatwāpaśyadāstīko yajñāyatanamuttamam |
wṛtaṃ sadasyairbahubhiḥ sūryawahnisamaprabhaiḥ ||27||

sa tatra wārito dwāḥsthaiḥ prawiśandwijasattamaḥ |
abhituṣṭāwa taṃ yajñaṃ praweśārthī dwijottamaḥ ||28||






                  50


āstīka uwāca||

somasya yajño waruṇasya yajñaḥ; prajāpateryajña āsītprayāge |
tathā yajño'yaṃ tawa bhāratāgrya; pārikṣita swasti no'stu priyebhyaḥ ||1||

śakrasya yajñaḥ śatasaṅkhya ukta; stathāparastulyasaṅkhyaḥ śataṃ wai |
tathā yajño'yaṃ tawa bhāratāgrya; pārikṣita swasti no'stu priyebhyaḥ ||2||

yamasya yajño harimedhasaśca; yathā yajño rantidewasya rājñaḥ |
tathā yajño'yaṃ tawa bhāratāgrya; pārikṣita swasti no'stu priyebhyaḥ ||3||

gayasya yajñaḥ śaśabindośca rājño; yajñastathā waiśrawaṇasya rājñaḥ |
tathā yajño'yaṃ tawa bhāratāgrya; pārikṣita swasti no'stu priyebhyaḥ ||4||

nṛgasya yajñastwajamīḍhasya cāsī; dyathā yajño dāśaratheśca rājñaḥ |
tathā yajño'yaṃ tawa bhāratāgrya; pārikṣita swasti no'stu priyebhyaḥ ||5||

yajñaḥ śruto no diwi dewasūno; ryudhiṣṭhirasyājamīḍhasya rājñaḥ |
tathā yajño'yaṃ tawa bhāratāgrya; pārikṣita swasti no'stu priyebhyaḥ ||6||

kṛṣṇasya yajñaḥ satyawatyāḥ sutasya; swayaṃ ca karma pracakāra yatra |
tathā yajño'yaṃ tawa bhāratāgrya; pārikṣita swasti no'stu priyebhyaḥ ||7||

ime hi te sūryahutāśawarcasaḥ; samāsate wṛtrahaṇaḥ kratuṃ yathā |
naiṣāṃ jñānaṃ widyate jñātumadya; dattaṃ yebhyo na praṇaśyetkathañcit ||8||

ṛtwiksamo nāsti lokeṣu caiwa; dwaipāyaneneti winiścitaṃ me |
etasya śiṣyā hi kṣitiṃ caranti; sarwartwijaḥ karmasu sweṣu dakṣāḥ ||9||

wibhāwasuścitrabhānurmahātmā; hiraṇyaretā wiśwabhukkṛṣṇawartmā |
pradakṣiṇāwartaśikhaḥ pradīpto; hawyaṃ tawedaṃ hutabhugwaṣṭi dewaḥ ||10||

neha twadanyo widyate jīwaloke; samo nṛpaḥ pālayitā prajānām |
dhṛtyā ca te prītamanāḥ sadāhaṃ; twaṃ wā rājā dharmarājo yamo wā ||11||

śakraḥ sākṣādwajrapāṇiryatheha; trātā loke'smiṃstwaṃ tatheha prajānām |
matastwaṃ naḥ puruṣendreha loke; na ca twadanyo gṛhapatirasti yajñe ||12||

khaṭwāṅganābhāgadilīpakalpo; yayātimāndhātṛsamaprabhāwaḥ |
ādityatejaḥpratimānatejā; bhīṣmo yathā bhrājasi suwratastwam ||13||

wālmīkiwatte nibhṛtaṃ sudhairyaṃ; wasiṣṭhawatte niyataśca kopaḥ |
prabhutwamindreṇa samaṃ mataṃ me; dyutiśca nārāyaṇawadwibhāti ||14||

yamo yathā dharmawiniścayajñaḥ; kṛṣṇo yathā sarwaguṇopapannaḥ |
śriyāṃ niwāso'si yathā wasūnāṃ; nidhānabhūto'si tathā kratūnām ||15||

dambhodbhawenāsi samo balena; rāmo yathā śastrawidastrawicca |
aurwatritābhyāmasi tulyatejā; duṣprekṣaṇīyo'si bhagīratho wā ||16||

sūta uwāca||

ewaṃ stutāḥ sarwa ewa prasannā; rājā sadasyā ṛtwijo hawyawāhaḥ |
teṣāṃ dṛṣṭwā bhāwitānīṅgitāni; prowāca rājā janamejayo'tha ||17||






                  51


janamejaya uwāca||

bālo wākyaṃ sthawira iwa prabhāṣate; nāyaṃ bālaḥ sthawiro'yaṃ mato me |
icchāmyahaṃ waramasmai pradātuṃ; tanme wiprā witaradhwaṃ sametāḥ ||1||

sadasyā ūcuḥ||

bālo'pi wipro mānya eweha rājñāṃ; yaścāwidwānyaśca widwānyathāwat |
sarwānkāmāṃstwatta eṣo'rhate'dya; yathā ca nastakṣaka eti śīghram ||2||

sūta uwāca||

wyāhartukāme warade nṛpe dwijaṃ; waraṃ wṛṇīṣweti tato'bhyuwāca |
hotā wākyaṃ nātihṛṣṭāntarātmā; karmaṇyasmiṃstakṣako naiti tāwat ||3||

janamejaya uwāca||

yathā cedaṃ karma samāpyate me; yathā ca nastakṣaka eti śīghram |
tathā bhawantaḥ prayatantu sarwe; paraṃ śaktyā sa hi me widwiṣāṇaḥ ||4||

ṛtwija ūcuḥ||

yathā śāstrāṇi naḥ prāhuryathā śaṃsati pāwakaḥ |
indrasya bhawane rājaṃstakṣako bhayapīḍitaḥ ||5||

sūta uwāca||

yathā sūto lohitākṣo mahātmā; paurāṇiko weditawānpurastāt |
sa rājānaṃ prāha pṛṣṭastadānīṃ; yathāhurwiprāstadwadetannṛdewa ||6||

purāṇamāgamya tato brawīmyahaṃ; dattaṃ tasmai waramindreṇa rājan |
waseha twaṃ matsakāśe sugupto; na pāwakastwāṃ pradahiṣyatīti ||7||

etacchrutwā dīkṣitastapyamāna; āste hotāraṃ codayankarmakāle |
hotā ca yattaḥ sa juhāwa mantrai; ratho indraḥ swayamewājagāma ||8||

wimānamāruhya mahānubhāwaḥ; sarwairdewaiḥ parisaṃstūyamānaḥ |
balāhakaiścāpyanugamyamāno; widyādharairapsarasāṃ gaṇaiśca ||9||

tasyottarīye nihitaḥ sa nāgo; bhayodwignaḥ śarma naiwābhyagacchat |
tato rājā mantrawido'brawītpunaḥ; kruddho wākyaṃ takṣakasyāntamicchan ||10||

indrasya bhawane wiprā yadi nāgaḥ sa takṣakaḥ |
tamindreṇaiwa sahitaṃ pātayadhwaṃ wibhāwasau ||11||

ṛtwija ūcuḥ||

ayamāyāti wai tūrṇaṃ takṣakaste waśaṃ nṛpa |
śrūyate'sya mahānnādo ruwato bhairawaṃ bhayāt ||12||

nūnaṃ mukto wajrabhṛtā sa nāgo; bhraṣṭaścāṅkānmantrawisrastakāyaḥ |
ghūrṇannākāśe naṣṭasañjño'bhyupaiti; tīwrānniḥśwāsānniḥśwasanpannagendraḥ ||13||

wartate tawa rājendra karmaitadwidhiwatprabho |
asmai tu dwijamukhyāya waraṃ twaṃ dātumarhasi ||14||

janamejaya uwāca||

bālābhirūpasya tawāprameya; waraṃ prayacchāmi yathānurūpam |
wṛṇīṣwa yatte'bhimataṃ hṛdi sthitaṃ; tatte pradāsyāmyapi cedadeyam ||15||

sūta uwāca||

patiṣyamāṇe nāgendre takṣake jātawedasi |
idamantaramityewaṃ tadāstīko'bhyacodayat ||16||

waraṃ dadāsi cenmahyaṃ wṛṇomi janamejaya |
satraṃ te wiramatwetanna pateyurihoragāḥ ||17||

ewamuktastato rājā brahmanpārikṣitastadā |
nātihṛṣṭamanā wākyamāstīkamidamabrawīt ||18||

suwarṇaṃ rajataṃ gāśca yaccānyanmanyase wibho |
tatte dadyāṃ waraṃ wipra na niwartetkraturmama ||19||

āstīka uwāca||

suwarṇaṃ rajataṃ gāśca na twāṃ rājanwṛṇomyaham |
satraṃ te wiramatwetatswasti mātṛkulasya naḥ ||20||

sūta uwāca||

āstīkenaiwamuktastu rājā pārikṣitastadā |
punaḥ punaruwācedamāstīkaṃ wadatāṃ waram ||21||

anyaṃ waraya bhadraṃ te waraṃ dwijawarottama |
ayācata na cāpyanyaṃ waraṃ sa bhṛgunandana ||22||

tato wedawidastatra sadasyāḥ sarwa ewa tam |
rājānamūcuḥ sahitā labhatāṃ brāhmaṇo waram ||23||






                  52


śaunaka uwāca||

ye sarpāḥ sarpasatre'sminpatitā hawyawāhane |
teṣāṃ nāmāni sarweṣāṃ śrotumicchāmi sūtaja ||1||

sūta uwāca||

sahasrāṇi bahūnyasminprayutānyarbudāni ca |
na śakyaṃ parisaṅkhyātuṃ bahutwādwedawittama ||2||

yathāsmṛti tu nāmāni pannagānāṃ nibodha me |
ucyamānāni mukhyānāṃ hutānāṃ jātawedasi ||3||

wāsukeḥ kulajāṃstāwatprādhānyena nibodha me |
nīlaraktānsitānghorānmahākāyānwiṣolbaṇān ||4||

koṭiko mānasaḥ pūrṇaḥ sahaḥ pailo halīsakaḥ |
picchilaḥ koṇapaścakraḥ koṇawegaḥ prakālanaḥ ||5||

hiraṇyawāhaḥ śaraṇaḥ kakṣakaḥ kāladantakaḥ |
ete wāsukijā nāgāḥ prawiṣṭā hawyawāhanam ||6||

takṣakasya kule jātānprawakṣyāmi nibodha tān |
pucchaṇḍako maṇḍalakaḥ piṇḍabhettā rabheṇakaḥ ||7||

ucchikhaḥ suraso draṅgo balaheḍo wirohaṇaḥ |
śilīśalakaro mūkaḥ sukumāraḥ prawepanaḥ ||8||

mudgaraḥ śaśaromā ca sumanā wegawāhanaḥ |
ete takṣakajā nāgāḥ prawiṣṭā hawyawāhanam ||9||

pārāwataḥ pāriyātraḥ pāṇḍaro hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ |
wihaṅgaḥ śarabho modaḥ pramodaḥ saṃhatāṅgadaḥ ||10||

airāwatakulādete praiwiṣṭā hawyawāhanam |
kaurawyakulajānnāgāñśṛṇu me dwijasattama ||11||

aiṇḍilaḥ kuṇḍalo muṇḍo weṇiskandhaḥ kumārakaḥ |
bāhukaḥ śṛṅgawegaśca dhūrtakaḥ pātapātarau ||12||

dhṛtarāṣṭrakule jātāñśṛṇu nāgānyathātatham |
kīrtyamānānmayā brahmanwātawegānwiṣolbaṇān ||13||

śaṅkukarṇaḥ piṅgalakaḥ kuṭhāramukhamecakau |
pūrṇāṅgadaḥ pūrṇamukhaḥ prahasaḥ śakunirhariḥ ||14||

āmāhaṭhaḥ komaṭhakaḥ śwasano mānawo waṭaḥ |
bhairawo muṇḍawedāṅgaḥ piśaṅgaścodrapāragaḥ ||15||

ṛṣabho wegawānnāma piṇḍārakamahāhanū |
raktāṅgaḥ sarwasāraṅgaḥ samṛddhaḥ pāṭarākṣasau ||16||

warāhako wāraṇakaḥ sumitraścitrawedikaḥ |
parāśarastaruṇako maṇiskandhastathāruṇiḥ ||17||

iti nāgā mayā brahmankīrtitāḥ kīrtiwardhanāḥ |
prādhānyena bahutwāttu na sarwe parikīrtitāḥ ||18||

eteṣāṃ putrapautrāstu prasawasya ca santatiḥ |
na śakyāḥ parisaṅkhyātuṃ ye dīptaṃ pāwakaṃ gatāḥ ||19||

saptaśīrṣā dwiśīrṣāśca pañcaśīrṣāstathāpare |
kālānalawiṣā ghorā hutāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ||20||

mahākāyā mahāwīryāḥ śailaśṛṅgasamucchrayāḥ |
yojanāyāmawistārā dwiyojanasamāyatāḥ ||21||

kāmarūpāḥ kāmagamā dīptānalawiṣolbaṇāḥ |
dagdhāstatra mahāsatre brahmadaṇḍanipīḍitāḥ ||22||






                  53


sūta uwāca||

idamatyadbhutaṃ cānyadāstīkasyānuśuśrumaḥ |
tathā waraiśchandyamāne rājñā pārikṣitena ha ||1||

indrahastāccyuto nāgaḥ kha ewa yadatiṣṭhata |
tataścintāparo rājā babhūwa janamejayaḥ ||2||

hūyamāne bhṛśaṃ dīpte widhiwatpāwake tadā |
na sma sa prāpatadwahnau takṣako bhayapīḍitaḥ ||3||

śaunaka uwāca||

kiṃ sūta teṣāṃ wiprāṇāṃ mantragrāmo manīṣiṇām |
na pratyabhāttadāgnau yanna papāta sa takṣakaḥ ||4||

sūta uwāca||

tamindrahastādwisrastaṃ wisañjñaṃ pannagottamam |
āstīkastiṣṭha tiṣṭheti wācastisro'bhyudairayat ||5||

witasthe so'ntarikṣe'tha hṛdayena widūyatā |
yathā tiṣṭheta wai kaścidgocakrasyāntarā naraḥ ||6||

tato rājābrawīdwākyaṃ sadasyaiścodito bhṛśam |
kāmametadbhawatwewaṃ yathāstīkasya bhāṣitam ||7||

samāpyatāmidaṃ karma pannagāḥ santwanāmayāḥ |
prīyatāmayamāstīkaḥ satyaṃ sūtawaco'stu tat ||8||

tato halahalāśabdaḥ prītijaḥ samawartata |
āstīkasya ware datte tathaiwopararāma ca ||9||

sa yajñaḥ pāṇḍaweyasya rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya ha |
prītimāṃścābhawadrājā bhārato janamejayaḥ ||10||

ṛtwigbhyaḥ sasadasyebhyo ye tatrāsansamāgatāḥ |
tebhyaśca pradadau wittaṃ śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ||11||

lohitākṣāya sūtāya tathā sthapataye wibhuḥ |
yenoktaṃ tatra satrāgre yajñasya winiwartanam ||12||

nimittaṃ brāhmaṇa iti tasmai wittaṃ dadau bahu |
tataścakārāwabhṛthaṃ widhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ||13||

āstīkaṃ preṣayāmāsa gṛhānewa susatkṛtam |
rājā prītamanāḥ prītaṃ kṛtakṛtyaṃ manīṣiṇam ||14||

punarāgamanaṃ kāryamiti cainaṃ waco'brawīt |
bhawiṣyasi sadasyo me wājimedhe mahākratau ||15||

tathetyuktwā pradudrāwa sa cāstīko mudā yutaḥ |
kṛtwā swakāryamatulaṃ toṣayitwā ca pārthiwam ||16||

sa gatwā paramaprīto mātaraṃ mātulaṃ ca tam |
abhigamyopasaṅgṛhya yathāwṛttaṃ nyawedayat ||17||

etacchrutwā prīyamāṇāḥ sametā; ye tatrāsanpannagā wītamohāḥ |
te''stīke wai prītimanto babhūwu; rūcuścainaṃ waramiṣṭaṃ wṛṇīṣwa ||18||

bhūyo bhūyaḥ sarwaśaste'bruwaṃstaṃ; kiṃ te priyaṃ karawāmo'dya widwan |
prītā wayaṃ mokṣitāścaiwa sarwe; kāmaṃ kiṃ te karawāmo'dya watsa ||19||

āstīka uwāca||

sāyaṃ prātaḥ suprasannātmarūpā; loke wiprā mānawāścetare'pi |
dharmākhyānaṃ ye wadeyurmamedaṃ; teṣāṃ yuṣmadbhyo naiwa kiñcidbhayaṃ syāt ||20||

sūta uwāca||

taiścāpyukto bhāgineyaḥ prasannai; retatsatyaṃ kāmamewaṃ carantaḥ |
prītyā yuktā īpsitaṃ sarwaśaste; kartāraḥ sma prawaṇā bhāgineya ||21||

jaratkārorjaratkārwāṃ samutpanno mahāyaśāḥ |
āstīkaḥ satyasandho māṃ pannagebhyo'bhirakṣatu ||22||

asitaṃ cārtimantaṃ ca sunīthaṃ cāpi yaḥ smaret |
diwā wā yadi wā rātrau nāsya sarpabhayaṃ bhawet ||23||

sūta uwāca||

mokṣayitwā sa bhujagānsarpasatrāddwijottamaḥ |
jagāma kāle dharmātmā diṣṭāntaṃ putrapautrawān ||24||

ityākhyānaṃ mayāstīkaṃ yathāwatkīrtitaṃ tawa |
yatkīrtayitwā sarpebhyo na bhayaṃ widyate kwacit ||25||

śrutwā dharmiṣṭhamākhyānamāstīkaṃ puṇyawardhanam |
āstīkasya kawerwipra śrīmaccaritamāditaḥ ||26||

śaunaka uwāca||

bhṛguwaṃśātprabhṛtyewa twayā me kathitaṃ mahat |
ākhyānamakhilaṃ tāta saute prīto'smi tena te ||27||

prakṣyāmi caiwa bhūyastwāṃ yathāwatsūtanandana |
yāṃ kathāṃ wyāsasampannāṃ tāṃ ca bhūyaḥ pracakṣwa me ||28||

tasminparamaduṣprāpe sarpasatre mahātmanām |
karmāntareṣu widhiwatsadasyānāṃ mahākawe ||29||

yā babhūwuḥ kathāścitrā yeṣwartheṣu yathātatham |
twatta icchāmahe śrotuṃ saute twaṃ wai wicakṣaṇaḥ ||30||

sūta uwāca||

karmāntareṣwakathayandwijā wedāśrayāḥ kathāḥ |
wyāsastwakathayannityamākhyānaṃ bhārataṃ mahat ||31||

śaunaka uwāca||

mahābhāratamākhyānaṃ pāṇḍawānāṃ yaśaskaram |
janamejayena yatpṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇadwaipāyanastadā ||32||

śrāwayāmāsa widhiwattadā karmāntareṣu saḥ |
tāmahaṃ widhiwatpuṇyāṃ śrotumicchāmi wai kathām ||33||

manaḥsāgarasambhūtāṃ maharṣeḥ puṇyakarmaṇaḥ |
kathayaswa satāṃ śreṣṭha na hi tṛpyāmi sūtaja ||34||

sūta uwāca||

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi mahadākhyānamuttamam |
kṛṣṇadwaipāyanamataṃ mahābhāratamāditaḥ ||35||

tajjuṣaswottamamate kathyamānaṃ mayā dwija |
śaṃsituṃ tanmanoharṣo mamāpīha prawartate ||36||






              ādiwaṃśāwataraṇaparwa
                  54


sūta uwāca||

śrutwā tu sarpasatrāya dīkṣitaṃ janamejayam |
abhyāgacchadṛṣirwidwānkṛṣṇadwaipāyanastadā ||1||

janayāmāsa yaṃ kālī śakteḥ putrātparāśarāt |
kanyaiwa yamunādwīpe pāṇḍawānāṃ pitāmaham ||2||

jātamātraśca yaḥ sadya iṣṭyā dehamawīwṛdhat |
wedāṃścādhijage sāṅgānsetihāsānmahāyaśāḥ ||3||

yaṃ nātitapasā kaścinna wedādhyayanena ca |
na wratairnopawāsaiśca na prasūtyā na manyunā ||4||

wiwyāsaikaṃ caturdhā yo wedaṃ wedawidāṃ waraḥ |
parāwarajño brahmarṣiḥ kawiḥ satyawrataḥ śuciḥ ||5||

yaḥ pāṇḍuṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca widuraṃ cāpyajījanat |
śantanoḥ santatiṃ tanwanpuṇyakīrtirmahāyaśāḥ ||6||

janamejayasya rājarṣeḥ sa tadyajñasadastadā |
wiweśa śiṣyaiḥ sahito wedawedāṅgapāragaiḥ ||7||

tatra rājānamāsīnaṃ dadarśa janamejayam |
wṛtaṃ sadasyairbahubhirdewairiwa puraṃdaram ||8||

tathā mūrdhāwasiktaiśca nānājanapadeśwaraiḥ |
ṛtwigbhirdewakalpaiśca kuśalairyajñasaṃstare ||9||

janamejayastu rājarṣirdṛṣṭwā tamṛṣimāgatam |
sagaṇo'byudyayau tūrṇaṃ prītyā bharatasattamaḥ ||10||

kāñcanaṃ wiṣṭaraṃ tasmai sadasyānumate prabhuḥ |
āsanaṃ kalpayāmāsa yathā śakro bṛhaspateḥ ||11||

tatropawiṣṭaṃ waradaṃ dewarṣigaṇapūjitam |
pūjayāmāsa rājendraḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā ||12||

pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca arghyaṃ gāṃ ca widhānataḥ |
pitāmahāya kṛṣṇāya tadarhāya nyawedayat ||13||

pratigṛhya ca tāṃ pūjāṃ pāṇḍawājjanamejayāt |
gāṃ caiwa samanujñāya wyāsaḥ prīto'bhawattadā ||14||

tathā sampūjayitwā taṃ yatnena prapitāmaham |
upopawiśya prītātmā paryapṛcchadanāmayam ||15||

bhagawānapi taṃ dṛṣṭwā kuśalaṃ pratiwedya ca |
sadasyaiḥ pūjitaḥ sarwaiḥ sadasyānabhyapūjayat ||16||

tatastaṃ satkṛtaṃ sarwaiḥ sadasyairjanamejayaḥ |
idaṃ paścāddwijaśreṣṭhaṃ paryapṛcchatkṛtāñjaliḥ ||17||

kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍawānāṃ ca bhawānpratyakṣadarśiwān |
teṣāṃ caritamicchāmi kathyamānaṃ twayā dwija ||18||

kathaṃ samabhawadbhedasteṣāmakliṣṭakarmaṇām |
tacca yuddhaṃ kathaṃ wṛttaṃ bhūtāntakaraṇaṃ mahat ||19||

pitāmahānāṃ sarweṣāṃ daiwenāwiṣṭacetasām |
kārtsnyenaitatsamācakṣwa bhagawankuśalo hyasi ||20||

tasya tadwacanaṃ śrutwā kṛṣṇadwaipāyanastadā |
śaśāsa śiṣyamāsīnaṃ waiśampāyanamantike ||21||

kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍawānāṃ ca yathā bhedo'bhawatpurā |
tadasmai sarwamācakṣwa yanmattaḥ śrutawānasi ||22||

gurorwacanamājñāya sa tu wiprarṣabhastadā |
ācacakṣe tataḥ sarwamitihāsaṃ purātanam ||23||

tasmai rājñe sadasyebhyaḥ kṣatriyebhyaśca sarwaśaḥ |
bhedaṃ rājyawināśaṃ ca kurupāṇḍawayostadā ||24||






                  55


waiśampāyana uwāca||

gurawe prāṅnamaskṛtya manobuddhisamādhibhiḥ |
sampūjya ca dwijānsarwāṃstathānyānwiduṣo janān ||1||

maharṣeḥ sarwalokeṣu wiśrutasyāsya dhīmataḥ |
prawakṣyāmi mataṃ kṛtsnaṃ wyāsasyāmitatejasaḥ ||2||

śrotuṃ pātraṃ ca rājaṃstwaṃ prāpyemāṃ bhāratīṃ kathām |
gurorwaktuṃ parispando mudā protsāhatīwa mām ||3||

śṛṇu rājanyathā bhedaḥ kurupāṇḍawayorabhūt |
rājyārthe dyūtasambhūto wanawāsastathaiwa ca ||4||

yathā ca yuddhamabhawatpṛthiwīkṣayakārakam |
tatte'haṃ samprawakṣyāmi pṛcchate bharatarṣabha ||5||

mṛte pitari te wīrā wanādetya swamandiram |
nacirādiwa widwāṃso wede dhanuṣi cābhawan ||6||

tāṃstathā rūpawīryaujaḥsampannānpaurasaṃmatān |
nāmṛṣyankurawo dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍawāñśrīyaśobhṛtaḥ ||7||

tato duryodhanaḥ krūraḥ karṇaśca sahasaubalaḥ |
teṣāṃ nigrahanirwāsānwiwidhāṃste samācaran ||8||

dadāwatha wiṣaṃ pāpo bhīmāya dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ |
jarayāmāsa tadwīraḥ sahānnena wṛkodaraḥ ||9||

pramāṇakoṭyāṃ saṃsuptaṃ punarbaddhwā wṛkodaram |
toyeṣu bhīmaṃ gaṅgāyāḥ prakṣipya puramāwrajat ||10||

yadā prabuddhaḥ kaunteyastadā sañchidya bandhanam |
udatiṣṭhanmahārāja bhīmaseno gatawyathaḥ ||11||

āśīwiṣaiḥ kṛṣṇasarpaiḥ suptaṃ cainamadaṃśayat |
sarweṣwewāṅgadeśeṣu na mamāra ca śatruhā ||12||

teṣāṃ tu wiprakāreṣu teṣu teṣu mahāmatiḥ |
mokṣaṇe pratighāte ca widuro'wahito'bhawat ||13||

swargastho jīwalokasya yathā śakraḥ sukhāwahaḥ |
pāṇḍawānāṃ tathā nityaṃ widuro'pi sukhāwahaḥ ||14||

yadā tu wiwidhopāyaiḥ saṃwṛtairwiwṛtairapi |
nāśaknodwinihantuṃ tāndaiwabhāwyartharakṣitān ||15||

tataḥ saṃmantrya saciwairwṛṣaduḥśāsanādibhiḥ |
dhṛtarāṣṭramanujñāpya jātuṣaṃ gṛhamādiśat ||16||

tatra tānwāsayāmāsa pāṇḍawānamitaujasaḥ |
adāhayacca wisrabdhānpāwakena punastadā ||17||

widurasyaiwa wacanātkhanitrī wihitā tataḥ |
mokṣayāmāsa yogena te muktāḥ prādrawanbhayāt ||18||

tato mahāwane ghore hiḍimbaṃ nāma rākṣasam |
bhīmaseno'wadhītkruddho bhuwi bhīmaparākramaḥ ||19||

atha sandhāya te wīrā ekacakrāṃ wrajaṃstadā |
brahmarūpadharā bhūtwā mātrā saha parantapāḥ ||20||

tatra te brāhmaṇārthāya bakaṃ hatwā mahābalam |
brāhmaṇaiḥ sahitā jagmuḥ pāñcālānāṃ puraṃ tataḥ ||21||

te tatra draupadīṃ labdhwā parisaṃwatsaroṣitāḥ |
widitā hāstinapuraṃ pratyājagmurariṃdamāḥ ||22||

ta uktā dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa rājñā śāntanawena ca |
bhrātṛbhirwigrahastāta kathaṃ wo na bhawediti ||23||

asmābhiḥ khāṇḍawaprasthe yuṣmadwāso'nucintitaḥ ||23||

tasmājjanapadopetaṃ suwibhaktamahāpatham |
wāsāya khāṇḍawaprasthaṃ wrajadhwaṃ gatamanyawaḥ ||24||

tayoste wacanājjagmuḥ saha sarwaiḥ suhṛjjanaiḥ |
nagaraṃ khāṇḍawaprasthaṃ ratnānyādāya sarwaśaḥ ||25||

tatra te nyawasanrājansaṃwatsaragaṇānbahūn |
waśe śastrapratāpena kurwanto'nyānmahīkṣitaḥ ||26||

ewaṃ dharmapradhānāste satyawrataparāyaṇāḥ |
apramattotthitāḥ kṣāntāḥ pratapanto'hitāṃstadā ||27||

ajayadbhīmasenastu diśaṃ prācīṃ mahābalaḥ |
udīcīmarjuno wīraḥ pratīcīṃ nakulastathā ||28||

dakṣiṇāṃ sahadewastu wijigye parawīrahā |
ewaṃ cakrurimāṃ sarwe waśe kṛtsnāṃ wasundharām ||29||

pañcabhiḥ sūryasaṅkāśaiḥ sūryeṇa ca wirājatā |
ṣaṭsūryewābabhau pṛthwī pāṇḍawaiḥ satyawikramaiḥ ||30||

tato nimitte kasmiṃściddharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
wanaṃ prasthāpayāmāsa bhrātaraṃ wai dhanañjayam ||31||

sa wai saṃwatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ māsaṃ caikaṃ wane'wasat |
tato'gacchaddhṛṣīkeśaṃ dwārawatyāṃ kadācana ||32||

labdhawāṃstatra bībhatsurbhāryāṃ rājīwalocanām |
anujāṃ wāsudewasya subhadrāṃ bhadrabhāṣiṇīm ||33||

sā śacīwa mahendreṇa śrīḥ kṛṣṇenewa saṅgatā |
subhadrā yuyuje prītā pāṇḍawenārjunena ha ||34||

atarpayacca kaunteyaḥ khāṇḍawe hawyawāhanam |
bībhatsurwāsudewena sahito nṛpasattama ||35||

nātibhāro hi pārthasya keśawenābhawatsaha |
wyawasāyasahāyasya wiṣṇoḥ śatruwadheṣwiwa ||36||

pārthāyāgnirdadau cāpi gāṇḍīwaṃ dhanuruttamam |
iṣudhī cākṣayairbāṇai rathaṃ ca kapilakṣaṇam ||37||

mokṣayāmāsa bībhatsurmayaṃ tatra mahāsuram |
sa cakāra sabhāṃ diwyāṃ sarwaratnasamācitām ||38||

tasyāṃ duryodhano mando lobhaṃ cakre sudurmatiḥ |
tato'kṣairwañcayitwā ca saubalena yudhiṣṭhiram ||39||

wanaṃ prasthāpayāmāsa sapta warṣāṇi pañca ca |
ajñātamekaṃ rāṣṭre ca tathā warṣaṃ trayodaśam ||40||

tataścaturdaśe warṣe yācamānāḥ swakaṃ wasu |
nālabhanta mahārāja tato yuddhamawartata ||41||

tataste sarwamutsādya hatwā duryodhanaṃ nṛpam |
rājyaṃ widrutabhūyiṣṭhaṃ pratyapadyanta pāṇḍawāḥ ||42||

ewametatpurāwṛttaṃ teṣāmakliṣṭakarmaṇām |
bhedo rājyawināśaśca jayaśca jayatāṃ wara ||43||






                  56


janamejaya uwāca||

kathitaṃ wai samāsena twayā sarwaṃ dwijottama |
mahābhāratamākhyānaṃ kurūṇāṃ caritaṃ mahat ||1||

kathāṃ twanagha citrārthāmimāṃ kathayati twayi |
wistaraśrawaṇe jātaṃ kautūhalamatīwa me ||2||

sa bhawānwistareṇemāṃ punarākhyātumarhati |
na hi tṛpyāmi pūrweṣāṃ śṛṇwānaścaritaṃ mahat ||3||

na tatkāraṇamalpaṃ hi dharmajñā yatra pāṇḍawāḥ |
awadhyānsarwaśo jaghnuḥ praśasyante ca mānawaiḥ ||4||

kimarthaṃ te narawyāghrāḥ śaktāḥ santo hyanāgasaḥ |
prayujyamānānsaṅkleśānkṣāntawanto durātmanām ||5||

kathaṃ nāgāyutaprāṇo bāhuśālī wṛkodaraḥ |
parikliśyannapi krodhaṃ dhṛtawānwai dwijottama ||6||

kathaṃ sā draupadī kṛṣṇā kliśyamānā durātmabhiḥ |
śaktā satī dhārtarāṣṭrānnādahadghoracakṣuṣā ||7||

kathaṃ wyatikramandyūte pārthau mādrīsutau tathā |
anuwrajannarawyāghraṃ wañcyamānaṃ durātmabhiḥ ||8||

kathaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ suto dharmasya dharmawit |
anarhaḥ paramaṃ kleśaṃ soḍhawānsa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||9||

kathaṃ ca bahulāḥ senāḥ pāṇḍawaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ |
asyanneko'nayatsarwāḥ pitṛlokaṃ dhanañjayaḥ ||10||

etadācakṣwa me sarwaṃ yathāwṛttaṃ tapodhana |
yadyacca kṛtawantaste tatra tatra mahārathāḥ ||11||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

maharṣeḥ sarwalokeṣu pūjitasya mahātmanaḥ |
prawakṣyāmi mataṃ kṛtsnaṃ wyāsasyāmitatejasaḥ ||12||

idaṃ śatasahasraṃ hi ślokānāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām |
satyawatyātmajeneha wyākhyātamamitaujasā ||13||

ya idaṃ śrāwayedwidwānyaścedaṃ śṛṇuyānnaraḥ |
te brahmaṇaḥ sthānametya prāpnuyurdewatulyatām ||14||

idaṃ hi wedaiḥ samitaṃ pawitramapi cottamam |
śrāwyāṇāmuttamaṃ cedaṃ purāṇamṛṣisaṃstutam ||15||

asminnarthaśca dharmaśca nikhilenopadiśyate |
itihāse mahāpuṇye buddhiśca parinaiṣṭhikī ||16||

akṣudrāndānaśīlāṃśca satyaśīlānanāstikān |
kārṣṇaṃ wedamimaṃ widwāñśrāwayitwārthamaśnute ||17||

bhrūṇahatyākṛtaṃ cāpi pāpaṃ jahyādasaṃśayam |
itihāsamimaṃ śrutwā puruṣo'pi sudāruṇaḥ ||18||

jayo nāmetihāso'yaṃ śrotawyo wijigīṣuṇā |
mahīṃ wijayate sarwāṃ śatrūṃścāpi parājayet ||19||

idaṃ puṃsawanaṃ śreṣṭhamidaṃ swastyayanaṃ mahat |
mahiṣīyuwarājābhyāṃ śrotawyaṃ bahuśastathā ||20||

arthaśāstramidaṃ puṇyaṃ dharmaśāstramidaṃ param |
mokṣaśāstramidaṃ proktaṃ wyāsenāmitabuddhinā ||21||

sampratyācakṣate caiwa ākhyāsyanti tathāpare |
putrāḥ śuśrūṣawaḥ santi preṣyāśca priyakāriṇaḥ ||22||

śarīreṇa kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ wācā ca manasaiwa ca |
sarwaṃ tattyajati kṣipramidaṃ śṛṇwannaraḥ sadā ||23||

bhāratānāṃ mahajjanma śṛṇwatāmanasūyatām |
nāsti wyādhibhayaṃ teṣāṃ paralokabhayaṃ kutaḥ ||24||

dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ swargyaṃ puṇyaṃ tathaiwa ca |
kṛṣṇadwaipāyanenedaṃ kṛtaṃ puṇyacikīrṣuṇā ||25||

kīrtiṃ prathayatā loke pāṇḍawānāṃ mahātmanām |
anyeṣāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca bhūridrawiṇatejasām ||26||

yathā samudro bhagawānyathā ca himawāngiriḥ |
khyātāwubhau ratnanidhī tathā bhāratamucyate ||27||

ya idaṃ śrāwayedwidwānbrāhmaṇāniha parwasu |
dhūtapāpmā jitaswargo brahmabhūyaṃ sa gacchati ||28||

yaścedaṃ śrāwayecchrāddhe brāhmaṇānpādamantataḥ |
akṣayyaṃ tasya tacchrāddhamupatiṣṭhetpitṛnapi ||29||

ahnā yadenaścājñānātprakaroti naraścaran |
tanmahābhāratākhyānaṃ śrutwaiwa prawilīyate ||30||

bhāratānāṃ mahajjanma mahābhāratamucyate |
niruktamasya yo weda sarwapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||31||

tribhirwarṣaiḥ sadotthāyī kṛṣṇadwaipāyano muniḥ |
mahābhāratamākhyānaṃ kṛtawānidamuttamam ||32||

dharme cārthe ca kāme ca mokṣe ca bharatarṣabha |
yadihāsti tadanyatra yannehāsti na tatkwacit ||33||






                  57


waiśampāyana uwāca||

rājoparicaro nāma dharmanityo mahīpatiḥ |
babhūwa mṛgayāṃ gantuṃ sa kadāciddhṛtawrataḥ ||1||

sa cediwiṣayaṃ ramyaṃ wasuḥ paurawanandanaḥ |
indropadeśājjagrāha grahaṇīyaṃ mahīpatiḥ ||2||

tamāśrame nyastaśastraṃ niwasantaṃ taporatim |
dewaḥ sākṣātswayaṃ wajrī samupāyānmahīpatim ||3||

indratwamarho rājāyaṃ tapasetyanucintya wai |
taṃ sāntwena nṛpaṃ sākṣāttapasaḥ saṃnyawartayat ||4||

indra uwāca||

na saṅkīryeta dharmo'yaṃ pṛthiwyāṃ pṛthiwīpate |
taṃ pāhi dharmo hi dhṛtaḥ kṛtsnaṃ dhārayate jagat ||5||

lokyaṃ dharmaṃ pālaya twaṃ nityayuktaḥ samāhitaḥ |
dharmayuktastato lokānpuṇyānāpsyasi śāśwatān ||6||

diwiṣṭhasya bhuwiṣṭhastwaṃ sakhā bhūtwā mama priyaḥ |
ūdhaḥ pṛthiwyā yo deśastamāwasa narādhipa ||7||

paśawyaścaiwa puṇyaśca susthiro dhanadhānyawān |
swārakṣyaścaiwa saumyaśca bhogyairbhūmiguṇairyutaḥ ||8||

atyanyāneṣa deśo hi dhanaratnādibhiryutaḥ |
wasupūrṇā ca wasudhā wasa cediṣu cedipa ||9||

dharmaśīlā janapadāḥ susantoṣāśca sādhawaḥ |
na ca mithyāpralāpo'tra swaireṣwapi kuto'nyathā ||10||

na ca pitrā wibhajyante narā guruhite ratāḥ |
yuñjate dhuri no gāśca kṛśāḥ sandhukṣayanti ca ||11||

sarwe warṇāḥ swadharmasthāḥ sadā cediṣu mānada |
na te'styawiditaṃ kiñcittriṣu lokeṣu yadbhawet ||12||

dewopabhogyaṃ diwyaṃ ca ākāśe sphāṭikaṃ mahat |
ākāśagaṃ twāṃ maddattaṃ wimānamupapatsyate ||13||

twamekaḥ sarwamartyeṣu wimānawaramāsthitaḥ |
cariṣyasyuparistho wai dewo wigrahawāniwa ||14||

dadāmi te waijayantīṃ mālāmamlānapaṅkajām |
dhārayiṣyati saṅgrāme yā twāṃ śastrairawikṣatam ||15||

lakṣaṇaṃ caitadeweha bhawitā te narādhipa |
indramāleti wikhyātaṃ dhanyamapratimaṃ mahat ||16||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

yaṣṭiṃ ca waiṇawīṃ tasmai dadau wṛtraniṣūdanaḥ |
iṣṭapradānamuddiśya śiṣṭānāṃ paripālinīm ||17||

tasyāḥ śakrasya pūjārthaṃ bhūmau bhūmipatistadā |
praweśaṃ kārayāmāsa gate saṃwatsare tadā ||18||

tataḥ prabhṛti cādyāpi yaṣṭyāḥ kṣitipasattamaiḥ |
praweśaḥ kriyate rājanyathā tena prawartitaḥ ||19||

aparedyustathā cāsyāḥ kriyate ucchrayo nṛpaiḥ |
alaṅkṛtāyāḥ piṭakairgandhairmālyaiśca bhūṣaṇaiḥ ||20||

mālyadāmaparikṣiptā widhiwatkriyate'pi ca ||20||

bhagawānpūjyate cātra hāsyarūpeṇa śaṅkaraḥ |
swayamewa gṛhītena wasoḥ prītyā mahātmanaḥ ||21||

etāṃ pūjāṃ mahendrastu dṛṣṭwā dewa kṛtāṃ śubhām |
wasunā rājamukhyena prītimānabrawīdwibhuḥ ||22||

ye pūjayiṣyanti narā rājānaśca mahaṃ mama |
kārayiṣyanti ca mudā yathā cedipatirnṛpaḥ ||23||

teṣāṃ śrīrwijayaścaiwa sarāṣṭrāṇāṃ bhawiṣyati |
tathā sphīto janapado muditaśca bhawiṣyati ||24||

ewaṃ mahātmanā tena mahendreṇa narādhipa |
wasuḥ prītyā maghawatā mahārājo'bhisatkṛtaḥ ||25||

utsawaṃ kārayiṣyanti sadā śakrasya ye narāḥ |
bhūmidānādibhirdānairyathā pūtā bhawanti wai ||26||

waradānamahāyajñaistathā śakrotsawena te ||26||

sampūjito maghawatā wasuścedipatistadā |
pālayāmāsa dharmeṇa cedisthaḥ pṛthiwīmimām ||27||

indraprītyā bhūmipatiścakārendramahaṃ wasuḥ ||27||

putrāścāsya mahāwīryāḥ pañcāsannamitaujasaḥ |
nānārājyeṣu ca sutānsa samrāḍabhyaṣecayat ||28||

mahāratho magadharāḍwiśruto yo bṛhadrathaḥ |
pratyagrahaḥ kuśāmbaśca yamāhurmaṇiwāhanam ||29||

macchillaśca yaduścaiwa rājanyaścāparājitaḥ ||29||

ete tasya sutā rājanrājarṣerbhūritejasaḥ |
nyaweśayannāmabhiḥ swaiste deśāṃśca purāṇi ca ||30||

wāsawāḥ pañca rājānaḥ pṛthagwaṃśāśca śāśwatāḥ ||30||

wasantamindraprāsāde ākāśe sphāṭike ca tam |
upatasthurmahātmānaṃ gandharwāpsaraso nṛpam ||31||

rājoparicaretyewaṃ nāma tasyātha wiśrutam ||31||

puropawāhinīṃ tasya nadīṃ śuktimatīṃ giriḥ |
arautsīccetanāyuktaḥ kāmātkolāhalaḥ kila ||32||

giriṃ kolāhalaṃ taṃ tu padā wasuratāḍayat |
niścakrāma nadī tena prahārawiwareṇa sā ||33||

tasyāṃ nadyāmajanayanmithunaṃ parwataḥ swayam |
tasmādwimokṣaṇātprītā nadī rājñe nyawedayat ||34||

yaḥ pumānabhawattatra taṃ sa rājarṣisattamaḥ |
wasurwasupradaścakre senāpatimariṃdamam ||35||

cakāra patnīṃ kanyāṃ tu dayitāṃ girikāṃ nṛpaḥ ||35||

wasoḥ patnī tu girikā kāmātkāle nyawedayat |
ṛtukālamanuprāptaṃ snātā puṃsawane śuciḥ ||36||

tadahaḥ pitaraścainamūcurjahi mṛgāniti |
taṃ rājasattamaṃ prītāstadā matimatāṃ waram ||37||

sa pitṛṇāṃ niyogaṃ tamawyatikramya pārthiwaḥ |
cacāra mṛgayāṃ kāmī girikāmewa saṃsmaran ||38||

atīwa rūpasampannāṃ sākṣācchriyamiwāparām ||38||

tasya retaḥ pracaskanda carato rucire wane |
skannamātraṃ ca tadreto wṛkṣapatreṇa bhūmipaḥ ||39||

pratijagrāha mithyā me na skandedreta ityuta |
ṛtuśca tasyāḥ patnyā me na moghaḥ syāditi prabhuḥ ||40||

sañcintyaiwaṃ tadā rājā wicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ |
amoghatwaṃ ca wijñāya retaso rājasattamaḥ ||41||

śukraprasthāpane kālaṃ mahiṣyāḥ prasamīkṣya saḥ |
abhimantryātha tacchukramārāttiṣṭhantamāśugam ||42||

sūkṣmadharmārthatattwajño jñātwā śyenaṃ tato'brawīt ||42||

matpriyārthamidaṃ saumya śukraṃ mama gṛhaṃ naya |
girikāyāḥ prayacchāśu tasyā hyārtawamadya wai ||43||

gṛhītwā tattadā śyenastūrṇamutpatya wegawān |
jawaṃ paramamāsthāya pradudrāwa wihaṅgamaḥ ||44||

tamapaśyadathāyāntaṃ śyenaṃ śyenastathāparaḥ |
abhyadrawacca taṃ sadyo dṛṣṭwaiwāmiṣaśaṅkayā ||45||

tuṇḍayuddhamathākāśe tāwubhau sampracakratuḥ |
yudhyatorapatadretastaccāpi yamunāmbhasi ||46||

tatrādriketi wikhyātā brahmaśāpādwarāpsarāḥ |
mīnabhāwamanuprāptā babhūwa yamunācarī ||47||

śyenapādaparibhraṣṭaṃ tadwīryamatha wāsawam |
jagrāha tarasopetya sādrikā matsyarūpiṇī ||48||

kadācidatha matsīṃ tāṃ babandhurmatsyajīwinaḥ |
māse ca daśame prāpte tadā bharatasattama ||49||

ujjahrurudarāttasyāḥ strīpumāṃsaṃ ca mānuṣam ||49||

āścaryabhūtaṃ matwā tadrājñaste pratyawedayan |
kāye matsyā imau rājansambhūtau mānuṣāwiti ||50||

tayoḥ pumāṃsaṃ jagrāha rājoparicarastadā |
sa matsyo nāma rājāsīddhārmikaḥ satyasaṅgaraḥ ||51||

sāpsarā muktaśāpā ca kṣaṇena samapadyata |
puroktā yā bhagawatā tiryagyonigatā śubhe ||52||

mānuṣau janayitwā twaṃ śāpamokṣamawāpsyasi ||52||

tataḥ sā janayitwā tau wiśastā matsyaghātinā |
santyajya matsyarūpaṃ sā diwyaṃ rūpamawāpya ca ||53||

siddharṣicāraṇapathaṃ jagāmātha warāpsarāḥ ||53||

yā kanyā duhitā tasyā matsyā matsyasagandhinī |
rājñā dattātha dāśāya iyaṃ tawa bhawatwiti ||54||

rūpasattwasamāyuktā sarwaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥ ||54||

sā tu satyawatī nāma matsyaghātyabhisaṃśrayāt |
āsīnmatsyasagandhaiwa kañcitkālaṃ śucismitā ||55||

śuśrūṣārthaṃ piturnāwaṃ tāṃ tu wāhayatīṃ jale |
tīrthayātrāṃ parikrāmannapaśyadwai parāśaraḥ ||56||

atīwa rūpasampannāṃ siddhānāmapi kāṅkṣitām |
dṛṣṭwaiwa ca sa tāṃ dhīmāṃścakame cārudarśanām ||57||

widwāṃstāṃ wāsawīṃ kanyāṃ kāryawānmunipuṅgawaḥ ||57||

sābrawītpaśya bhagawanpārāwāre ṛṣīnsthitān |
āwayordṛśyatorebhiḥ kathaṃ nu syātsamāgamaḥ ||58||

ewaṃ tayokto bhagawānnīhāramasṛjatprabhuḥ |
yena deśaḥ sa sarwastu tamobhūta iwābhawat ||59||

dṛṣṭwā sṛṣṭaṃ tu nīhāraṃ tatastaṃ paramarṣiṇā |
wismitā cābrawītkanyā wrīḍitā ca manaswinī ||60||

widdhi māṃ bhagawankanyāṃ sadā pitṛwaśānugām |
twatsaṃyogācca duṣyeta kanyābhāwo mamānagha ||61||

kanyātwe dūṣite cāpi kathaṃ śakṣye dwijottama |
gantuṃ gṛhaṃ gṛhe cāhaṃ dhīmanna sthātumutsahe ||62||

etatsañcintya bhagawanwidhatswa yadanantaram ||62||

ewamuktawatīṃ tāṃ tu prītimānṛṣisattamaḥ |
uwāca matpriyaṃ kṛtwā kanyaiwa twaṃ bhawiṣyasi ||63||

wṛṇīṣwa ca waraṃ bhīru yaṃ twamicchasi bhāmini |
wṛthā hi na prasādo me bhūtapūrwaḥ śucismite ||64||

ewamuktā waraṃ wawre gātrasaugandhyamuttamam |
sa cāsyai bhagawānprādānmanasaḥ kāṅkṣitaṃ prabhuḥ ||65||

tato labdhawarā prītā strībhāwaguṇabhūṣitā |
jagāma saha saṃsargamṛṣiṇādbhutakarmaṇā ||66||

tena gandhawatītyewa nāmāsyāḥ prathitaṃ bhuwi |
tasyāstu yojanādgandhamājighranti narā bhuwi ||67||

tato yojanagandheti tasyā nāma pariśrutam |
parāśaro'pi bhagawāñjagāma swaṃ niweśanam ||68||

iti satyawatī hṛṣṭā labdhwā waramanuttamam |
parāśareṇa saṃyuktā sadyo garbhaṃ suṣāwa sā ||69||

jajñe ca yamunādwīpe pārāśaryaḥ sa wīryawān ||69||

sa mātaramupasthāya tapasyewa mano dadhe |
smṛto'haṃ darśayiṣyāmi kṛtyeṣwiti ca so'brawīt ||70||

ewaṃ dwaipāyano jajñe satyawatyāṃ parāśarāt |
dwīpe nyastaḥ sa yadbālastasmāddwaipāyano'bhawat ||71||

pādāpasāriṇaṃ dharmaṃ widwānsa tu yuge yuge |
āyuḥ śaktiṃ ca martyānāṃ yugānugamawekṣya ca ||72||

brahmaṇo brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tathānugrahakāmyayā |
wiwyāsa wedānyasmācca tasmādwyāsa iti smṛtaḥ ||73||

wedānadhyāpayāmāsa mahābhāratapañcamān |
sumantuṃ jaiminiṃ pailaṃ śukaṃ caiwa swamātmajam ||74||

prabhurwariṣṭho warado waiśampāyanamewa ca |
saṃhitāstaiḥ pṛthaktwena bhāratasya prakāśitāḥ ||75||

tathā bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawo gaṅgāyāmamitadyutiḥ |
wasuwīryātsamabhawanmahāwīryo mahāyaśāḥ ||76||

śūle protaḥ purāṇarṣiracoraścoraśaṅkayā |
aṇīmāṇḍawya iti wai wikhyātaḥ sumahāyaśāḥ ||77||

sa dharmamāhūya purā maharṣiridamuktawān |
iṣīkayā mayā bālyādekā widdhā śakuntikā ||78||

tatkilbiṣaṃ smare dharma nānyatpāpamahaṃ smare |
tanme sahasrasamitaṃ kasmānnehājayattapaḥ ||79||

garīyānbrāhmaṇawadhaḥ sarwabhūtawadhādyataḥ |
tasmāttwaṃ kilbiṣādasmācchūdrayonau janiṣyasi ||80||

tena śāpena dharmo'pi śūdrayonāwajāyata |
widwānwidurarūpeṇa dhārmī tanurakilbiṣī ||81||

sañjayo munikalpastu jajñe sūto gawalgaṇāt |
sūryācca kuntikanyāyāṃ jajñe karṇo mahārathaḥ ||82||

sahajaṃ kawacaṃ bibhratkuṇḍaloddyotitānanaḥ ||82||

anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ wiṣṇurlokanamaskṛtaḥ |
wasudewāttu dewakyāṃ prādurbhūto mahāyaśāḥ ||83||

anādinidhano dewaḥ sa kartā jagataḥ prabhuḥ |
awyaktamakṣaraṃ brahma pradhānaṃ nirguṇātmakam ||84||

ātmānamawyayaṃ caiwa prakṛtiṃ prabhawaṃ param |
puruṣaṃ wiśwakarmāṇaṃ sattwayogaṃ dhruwākṣaram ||85||

anantamacalaṃ dewaṃ haṃsaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum |
dhātāramajaraṃ nityaṃ tamāhuḥ paramawyayam ||86||

puruṣaḥ sa wibhuḥ kartā sarwabhūtapitāmahaḥ |
dharmasaṃwardhanārthāya prajajñe'ndhakawṛṣṇiṣu ||87||

astrajñau tu mahāwīryau sarwaśastrawiśāradau |
sātyakiḥ kṛtawarmā ca nārāyaṇamanuwratau ||88||

satyakāddhṛdikāccaiwa jajñāte'strawiśāradau ||88||

bharadwājasya ca skannaṃ droṇyāṃ śukramawardhata |
maharṣerugratapasastasmāddroṇo wyajāyata ||89||

gautamānmithunaṃ jajñe śarastambāccharadwataḥ |
aśwatthāmnaśca jananī kṛpaścaiwa mahābalaḥ ||90||

aśwatthāmā tato jajñe droṇādastrabhṛtāṃ waraḥ ||90||

tathaiwa dhṛṣṭadyumno'pi sākṣādagnisamadyutiḥ |
waitāne karmaṇi tate pāwakātsamajāyata ||91||

wīro droṇawināśāya dhanuṣā saha wīryawān ||91||

tathaiwa wedyāṃ kṛṣṇāpi jajñe tejaswinī śubhā |
wibhrājamānā wapuṣā bibhratī rūpamuttamam ||92||

prahrādaśiṣyo nagnajitsubalaścābhawattataḥ |
tasya prajā dharmahantrī jajñe dewaprakopanāt ||93||

gāndhārarājaputro'bhūcchakuniḥ saubalastathā |
duryodhanasya mātā ca jajñāte'rthawidāwubhau ||94||

kṛṣṇadwaipāyanājjajñe dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśwaraḥ |
kṣetre wicitrawīryasya pāṇḍuścaiwa mahābalaḥ ||95||

pāṇḍostu jajñire pañca putrā dewasamāḥ pṛthak |
dwayoḥ striyorguṇajyeṣṭhasteṣāmāsīdyudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||96||

dharmādyudhiṣṭhiro jajñe mārutāttu wṛkodaraḥ |
indrāddhanañjayaḥ śrīmānsarwaśastrabhṛtāṃ waraḥ ||97||

jajñāte rūpasampannāwaświbhyāṃ tu yamāwubhau |
nakulaḥ sahadewaśca guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratau ||98||

tathā putraśataṃ jajñe dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥ |
duryodhanaprabhṛtayo yuyutsuḥ karaṇastathā ||99||

abhimanyuḥ subhadrāyāmarjunādabhyajāyata |
swasrīyo wāsudewasya pautraḥ pāṇḍormahātmanaḥ ||100||

pāṇḍawebhyo'pi pañcabhyaḥ kṛṣṇāyāṃ pañca jajñire |
kumārā rūpasampannāḥ sarwaśastrawiśāradāḥ ||101||

pratiwindhyo yudhiṣṭhirātsutasomo wṛkodarāt |
arjunācchrutakīrtistu śatānīkastu nākuliḥ ||102||

tathaiwa sahadewācca śrutasenaḥ pratāpawān |
hiḍimbāyāṃ ca bhīmena wane jajñe ghaṭotkacaḥ ||103||

śikhaṇḍī drupadājjajñe kanyā putratwamāgatā |
yāṃ yakṣaḥ puruṣaṃ cakre sthūṇaḥ priyacikīrṣayā ||104||

kurūṇāṃ wigrahe tasminsamāgacchanbahūnyatha |
rājñāṃ śatasahasrāṇi yotsyamānāni saṃyuge ||105||

teṣāmaparimeyāni nāmadheyāni sarwaśaḥ |
na śakyaṃ parisaṅkhyātuṃ warṣāṇāmayutairapi ||106||

ete tu kīrtitā mukhyā yairākhyānamidaṃ tatam ||106||






                  58


janamejaya uwāca||

ya ete kīrtitā brahmanye cānye nānukīrtitāḥ |
samyaktāñśrotumicchāmi rājñaścānyānsuwarcasaḥ ||1||

yadarthamiha sambhūtā dewakalpā mahārathāḥ |
bhuwi tanme mahābhāga samyagākhyātumarhasi ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

rahasyaṃ khalwidaṃ rājandewānāmiti naḥ śrutam |
tattu te kathayiṣyāmi namaskṛtwā swayambhuwe ||3||

triḥsaptakṛtwaḥ pṛthiwīṃ kṛtwā niḥkṣatriyāṃ purā |
jāmadagnyastapastepe mahendre parwatottame ||4||

tadā niḥkṣatriye loke bhārgaweṇa kṛte sati |
brāhmaṇānkṣatriyā rājangarbhārthinyo'bhicakramuḥ ||5||

tābhiḥ saha samāpeturbrāhmaṇāḥ saṃśitawratāḥ |
ṛtāwṛtau narawyāghra na kāmānnānṛtau tathā ||6||

tebhyastu lebhire garbhānkṣatriyāstāḥ sahasraśaḥ |
tataḥ suṣuwire rājankṣatriyānwīryasaṃmatān ||7||

kumārāṃśca kumārīśca punaḥ kṣatrābhiwṛddhaye ||7||

ewaṃ tadbrāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatraṃ kṣatriyāsu tapaswibhiḥ |
jātamṛdhyata dharmeṇa sudīrgheṇāyuṣānwitam ||8||

catwāro'pi tadā warṇā babhūwurbrāhmaṇottarāḥ ||8||

abhyagacchannṛtau nārīṃ na kāmānnānṛtau tathā |
tathaiwānyāni bhūtāni tiryagyonigatānyapi ||9||

ṛtau dārāṃśca gacchanti tadā sma bharatarṣabha ||9||

tato'wardhanta dharmeṇa sahasraśatajīwinaḥ |
tāḥ prajāḥ pṛthiwīpāla dharmawrataparāyaṇāḥ ||10||

ādhibhirwyādhibhiścaiwa wimuktāḥ sarwaśo narāḥ ||10||

athemāṃ sāgarāpāṅgāṃ gāṃ gajendragatākhilām |
adhyatiṣṭhatpunaḥ kṣatraṃ saśailawanakānanām ||11||

praśāsati punaḥ kṣatre dharmeṇemāṃ wasundharām |
brāhmaṇādyāstadā warṇā lebhire mudamuttamām ||12||

kāmakrodhodbhawāndoṣānnirasya ca narādhipāḥ |
daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu dharmeṇa praṇayanto'nwapālayan ||13||

tathā dharmapare kṣatre sahasrākṣaḥ śatakratuḥ |
swādu deśe ca kāle ca wawarṣāpyāyayanprajāḥ ||14||

na bāla ewa mriyate tadā kaścinnarādhipa |
na ca striyaṃ prajānāti kaścidaprāptayauwanaḥ ||15||

ewamāyuṣmatībhistu prajābhirbharatarṣabha |
iyaṃ sāgaraparyantā samāpūryata medinī ||16||

ījire ca mahāyajñaiḥ kṣatriyā bahudakṣiṇaiḥ |
sāṅgopaniṣadānwedānwiprāścādhīyate tadā ||17||

na ca wikrīṇate brahma brāhmaṇāḥ sma tadā nṛpa |
na ca śūdrasamābhyāśe wedānuccārayantyuta ||18||

kārayantaḥ kṛṣiṃ gobhistathā waiśyāḥ kṣitāwiha |
na gāmayuñjanta dhuri kṛśāṅgāścāpyajīwayan ||19||

phenapāṃśca tathā watsānna duhanti sma mānawāḥ |
na kūṭamānairwaṇijaḥ paṇyaṃ wikrīṇate tadā ||20||

karmāṇi ca narawyāghra dharmopetāni mānawāḥ |
dharmamewānupaśyantaścakrurdharmaparāyaṇāḥ ||21||

swakarmaniratāścāsansarwe warṇā narādhipa |
ewaṃ tadā narawyāghra dharmo na hrasate kwacit ||22||

kāle gāwaḥ prasūyante nāryaśca bharatarṣabha |
phalantyṛtuṣu wṛkṣāśca puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca ||23||

ewaṃ kṛtayuge samyagwartamāne tadā nṛpa |
āpūryata mahī kṛtsnā prāṇibhirbahubhirbhṛśam ||24||

tataḥ samudite loke mānuṣe bharatarṣabha |
asurā jajñire kṣetre rājñāṃ manujapuṅgawa ||25||

ādityairhi tadā daityā bahuśo nirjitā yudhi |
aiśwaryādbhraṃśitāścāpi sambabhūwuḥ kṣitāwiha ||26||

iha dewatwamicchanto mānuṣeṣu manaswinaḥ |
jajñire bhuwi bhūteṣu teṣu teṣwasurā wibho ||27||

goṣwaśweṣu ca rājendra kharoṣṭramahiṣeṣu ca |
krawyādeṣu ca bhūteṣu gajeṣu ca mṛgeṣu ca ||28||

jātairiha mahīpāla jāyamānaiśca tairmahī |
na śaśākātmanātmānamiyaṃ dhārayituṃ dharā ||29||

atha jātā mahīpālāḥ kecidbalasamanwitāḥ |
diteḥ putrā danoścaiwa tasmāllokādiha cyutāḥ ||30||

wīryawanto'waliptāste nānārūpadharā mahīm |
imāṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ parīyurarimardanāḥ ||31||

brāhmaṇānkṣatriyānwaiśyāñśūdrāṃścaiwāpyapīḍayan |
anyāni caiwa bhūtāni pīḍayāmāsurojasā ||32||

trāsayanto winighnantastāṃstānbhūtagaṇāṃśca te |
wiceruḥ sarwato rājanmahīṃ śatasahasraśaḥ ||33||

āśramasthānmaharṣīṃśca dharṣayantastatastataḥ |
abrahmaṇyā wīryamadā mattā madabalena ca ||34||

ewaṃ wīryabalotsiktairbhūriyaṃ tairmahāsuraiḥ |
pīḍyamānā mahīpāla brahmāṇamupacakrame ||35||

na hīmāṃ pawano rājanna nāgā na nagā mahīm |
tadā dhārayituṃ śekurākrāntāṃ dānawairbalāt ||36||

tato mahī mahīpāla bhārārtā bhayapīḍitā |
jagāma śaraṇaṃ dewaṃ sarwabhūtapitāmaham ||37||

sā saṃwṛtaṃ mahābhāgairdewadwijamaharṣibhiḥ |
dadarśa dewaṃ brahmāṇaṃ lokakartāramawyayam ||38||

gandharwairapsarobhiśca bandikarmasu niṣṭhitaiḥ |
wandyamānaṃ mudopetairwawande cainametya sā ||39||

atha wijñāpayāmāsa bhūmistaṃ śaraṇārthinī |
saṃnidhau lokapālānāṃ sarweṣāmewa bhārata ||40||

tatpradhānātmanastasya bhūmeḥ kṛtyaṃ swayambhuwaḥ |
pūrwamewābhawadrājanwiditaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ||41||

sraṣṭā hi jagataḥ kasmānna sambudhyeta bhārata |
surāsurāṇāṃ lokānāmaśeṣeṇa manogatam ||42||

tamuwāca mahārāja bhūmiṃ bhūmipatirwibhuḥ |
prabhawaḥ sarwabhūtānāmīśaḥ śambhuḥ prajāpatiḥ ||43||

yadarthamasi samprāptā matsakāśaṃ wasundhare |
tadarthaṃ saṃniyokṣyāmi sarwānewa diwaukasaḥ ||44||

ityuktwā sa mahīṃ dewo brahmā rājanwisṛjya ca |
ādideśa tadā sarwānwibudhānbhūtakṛtswayam ||45||

asyā bhūmernirasituṃ bhāraṃ bhāgaiḥ pṛthakpṛthak |
asyāmewa prasūyadhwaṃ wirodhāyeti cābrawīt ||46||

tathaiwa ca samānīya gandharwāpsarasāṃ gaṇān |
uwāca bhagawānsarwānidaṃ wacanamuttamam ||47||

swairaṃśaiḥ samprasūyadhwaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ mānuṣeṣwiti ||47||

atha śakrādayaḥ sarwe śrutwā suragurorwacaḥ |
tathyamarthyaṃ ca pathyaṃ ca tasya te jagṛhustadā ||48||

atha te sarwaśoṃ'śaiḥ swairgantuṃ bhūmiṃ kṛtakṣaṇāḥ |
nārāyaṇamamitraghnaṃ waikuṇṭhamupacakramuḥ ||49||

yaḥ sa cakragadāpāṇiḥ pītawāsāsitaprabhaḥ |
padmanābhaḥ surārighnaḥ pṛthucārwañcitekṣaṇaḥ ||50||

taṃ bhuwaḥ śodhanāyendra uwāca puruṣottamam |
aṃśenāwatarasweti tathetyāha ca taṃ hariḥ ||51||






                  59


waiśampāyana uwāca||

atha nārāyaṇenendraścakāra saha saṃwidam |
awatartuṃ mahīṃ swargādaṃśataḥ sahitaḥ suraiḥ ||1||

ādiśya ca swayaṃ śakraḥ sarwānewa diwaukasaḥ |
nirjagāma punastasmātkṣayānnārāyaṇasya ha ||2||

te'marāriwināśāya sarwalokahitāya ca |
awateruḥ krameṇemāṃ mahīṃ swargāddiwaukasaḥ ||3||

tato brahmarṣiwaṃśeṣu pārthiwarṣikuleṣu ca |
jajñire rājaśārdūla yathākāmaṃ diwaukasaḥ ||4||

dānawānrākṣasāṃścaiwa gandharwānpannagāṃstathā |
puruṣādāni cānyāni jaghnuḥ sattwānyanekaśaḥ ||5||

dānawā rākṣasāścaiwa gandharwāḥ pannagāstathā |
na tānbalasthānbālye'pi jaghnurbharatasattama ||6||

janamejaya uwāca||

dewadānawasaṅghānāṃ gandharwāpsarasāṃ tathā |
mānawānāṃ ca sarweṣāṃ tathā wai yakṣarakṣasām ||7||

śrotumicchāmi tattwena sambhawaṃ kṛtsnamāditaḥ |
prāṇināṃ caiwa sarweṣāṃ sarwaśaḥ sarwawiddhyasi ||8||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi namaskṛtwā swayambhuwe |
surādīnāmahaṃ samyaglokānāṃ prabhawāpyayam ||9||

brahmaṇo mānasāḥ putrā widitāḥ ṣaṇmaharṣayaḥ |
marīciratryaṅgirasau pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ||10||

marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ putraḥ kaśyapāttu imāḥ prajāḥ |
prajajñire mahābhāgā dakṣakanyāstrayodaśa ||11||

aditirditirdanuḥ kālā anāyuḥ siṃhikā muniḥ |
krodhā prāwā ariṣṭā ca winatā kapilā tathā ||12||

kadrūśca manujawyāghra dakṣakanyaiwa bhārata |
etāsāṃ wīryasampannaṃ putrapautramanantakam ||13||

adityāṃ dwādaśādityāḥ sambhūtā bhuwaneśwarāḥ |
ye rājannāmatastāṃste kīrtayiṣyāmi bhārata ||14||

dhātā mitro'ryamā śakro waruṇaścāṃśa ewa ca |
bhago wiwaswānpūṣā ca sawitā daśamastathā ||15||

ekādaśastathā twaṣṭā wiṣṇurdwādaśa ucyate |
jaghanyajaḥ sa sarweṣāmādityānāṃ guṇādhikaḥ ||16||

eka ewa diteḥ putro hiraṇyakaśipuḥ smṛtaḥ |
nāmnā khyātāstu tasyeme putrāḥ pañca mahātmanaḥ ||17||

prahrādaḥ pūrwajasteṣāṃ saṃhrādastadanantaram |
anuhrādastṛtīyo'bhūttasmācca śibibāṣkalau ||18||

prahrādasya trayaḥ putrāḥ khyātāḥ sarwatra bhārata |
wirocanaśca kumbhaśca nikumbhaśceti wiśrutāḥ ||19||

wirocanasya putro'bhūdbalirekaḥ pratāpawān |
baleśca prathitaḥ putro bāṇo nāma mahāsuraḥ ||20||

catwāriṃśaddanoḥ putrāḥ khyātāḥ sarwatra bhārata |
teṣāṃ prathamajo rājā wipracittirmahāyaśāḥ ||21||

śambaro namuciścaiwa pulomā ceti wiśrutaḥ |
asilomā ca keśī ca durjayaścaiwa dānawaḥ ||22||

ayaḥśirā aśwaśirā ayaḥśaṅkuśca wīryawān |
tathā gaganamūrdhā ca wegawānketumāṃśca yaḥ ||23||

swarbhānuraśwo'śwapatirwṛṣaparwājakastathā |
aśwagrīwaśca sūkṣmaśca tuhuṇḍaśca mahāsuraḥ ||24||

isṛpā ekacakraśca wirūpākṣo harāharau |
nicandraśca nikumbhaśca kupathaḥ kāpathastathā ||25||

śarabhaḥ śalabhaścaiwa sūryācandramasau tathā |
iti khyātā danorwaṃśe dānawāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||26||

anyau tu khalu dewānāṃ sūryācandramasau smṛtau ||26||

ime ca waṃśe prathitāḥ sattwawanto mahābalāḥ |
danuputrā mahārāja daśa dānawapuṅgawāḥ ||27||

ekākṣo mṛtapā wīraḥ pralambanarakāwapi |
wātāpiḥ śatrutapanaḥ śaṭhaścaiwa mahāsuraḥ ||28||

gawiṣṭhaśca danāyuśca dīrghajihwaśca dānawaḥ |
asaṅkhyeyāḥ smṛtāsteṣāṃ putrāḥ pautrāśca bhārata ||29||

siṃhikā suṣuwe putraṃ rāhuṃ candrārkamardanam |
sucandraṃ candrahantāraṃ tathā candrawimardanam ||30||

krūraswabhāwaṃ krūrāyāḥ putrapautramanantakam |
gaṇaḥ krodhawaśo nāma krūrakarmārimardanaḥ ||31||

anāyuṣaḥ punaḥ putrāścatwāro'surapuṅgawāḥ |
wikṣaro balawīrau ca wṛtraścaiwa mahāsuraḥ ||32||

kālāyāḥ prathitāḥ putrāḥ kālakalpāḥ prahāriṇaḥ |
bhuwi khyātā mahāwīryā dānaweṣu parantapāḥ ||33||

wināśanaśca krodhaśca hantā krodhasya cāparaḥ |
krodhaśatrustathaiwānyaḥ kāleyā iti wiśrutāḥ ||34||

asurāṇāmupādhyāyaḥ śukrastwṛṣisuto'bhawat |
khyātāścośanasaḥ putrāścatwāro'surayājakāḥ ||35||

twaṣṭāwarastathātriśca dwāwanyau mantrakarmiṇau |
tejasā sūryasaṅkāśā brahmalokaprabhāwanāḥ ||36||

ityeṣa waṃśaprabhawaḥ kathitaste taraswinām |
asurāṇāṃ surāṇāṃ ca purāṇe saṃśruto mayā ||37||

eteṣāṃ yadapatyaṃ tu na śakyaṃ tadaśeṣataḥ |
prasaṅkhyātuṃ mahīpāla guṇabhūtamanantakam ||38||

tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiśca tathaiwa garuḍāruṇau |
āruṇirwāruṇiścaiwa wainateyā iti smṛtāḥ ||39||

śeṣo'nanto wāsukiśca takṣakaśca bhujaṅgamaḥ |
kūrmaśca kulikaścaiwa kādraweyā mahābalāḥ ||40||

bhīmasenograsenau ca suparṇo waruṇastathā |
gopatirdhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryawarcāśca saptamaḥ ||41||

patrawānarkaparṇaśca prayutaścaiwa wiśrutaḥ |
bhīmaścitrarathaścaiwa wikhyātaḥ sarwawidwaśī ||42||

tathā śāliśirā rājanpradyumnaśca caturdaśaḥ |
kaliḥ pañcadaśaścaiwa nāradaścaiwa ṣoḍaśaḥ ||43||

ityete dewagandharwā mauneyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||43||

atastu bhūtānyanyāni kīrtayiṣyāmi bhārata |
anawadyāmanuwaśāmanūnāmaruṇāṃ priyām ||44||

anūpāṃ subhagāṃ bhāsīmiti prāwā wyajāyata ||44||

siddhaḥ pūrṇaśca barhī ca pūrṇāśaśca mahāyaśāḥ |
brahmacārī ratiguṇaḥ suparṇaścaiwa saptamaḥ ||45||

wiśwāwasuśca bhānuśca sucandro daśamastathā |
ityete dewagandharwāḥ prāweyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||46||

imaṃ twapsarasāṃ waṃśaṃ widitaṃ puṇyalakṣaṇam |
prāwāsūta mahābhāgā dewī dewarṣitaḥ purā ||47||

alambusā miśrakeṣī widyutparṇā tulānaghā |
aruṇā rakṣitā caiwa rambhā tadwanmanoramā ||48||

asitā ca subāhuśca suwratā subhujā tathā |
supriyā cātibāhuśca wikhyātau ca hahāhuhū ||49||

tumburuśceti catwāraḥ smṛtā gandharwasattamāḥ ||49||

amṛtaṃ brāhmaṇā gāwo gandharwāpsarasastathā |
apatyaṃ kapilāyāstu purāṇe parikīrtitam ||50||

iti te sarwabhūtānāṃ sambhawaḥ kathito mayā |
yathāwatparisaṅkhyāto gandharwāpsarasāṃ tathā ||51||

bhujagānāṃ suparṇānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ marutāṃ tathā |
gawāṃ ca brāhmaṇānāṃ ca śrīmatāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ||52||

āyuṣyaścaiwa puṇyaśca dhanyaḥ śrutisukhāwahaḥ |
śrotawyaścaiwa satataṃ śrāwyaścaiwānasūyatā ||53||

imaṃ tu waṃśaṃ niyamena yaḥ paṭhe; nmahātmanāṃ brāhmaṇadewasaṃnidhau |
apatyalābhaṃ labhate sa puṣkalaṃ; śriyaṃ yaśaḥ pretya ca śobhanāṃ gatim ||54||






                  60


waiśampāyana uwāca||

brahmaṇo mānasāḥ putrā widitāḥ ṣaṇmaharṣayaḥ |
ekādaśa sutāḥ sthāṇoḥ khyātāḥ paramamānasāḥ ||1||

mṛgawyādhaśca śarwaśca nirṛtiśca mahāyaśāḥ |
ajaikapādahirbudhnyaḥ pinākī ca parantapaḥ ||2||

dahano'theśwaraścaiwa kapālī ca mahādyutiḥ |
sthāṇurbhawaśca bhagawānrudrā ekādaśa smṛtāḥ ||3||

marīciraṅgirā atriḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ |
ṣaḍete brahmaṇaḥ putrā wīryawanto maharṣayaḥ ||4||

trayastwaṅgirasaḥ putrā loke sarwatra wiśrutāḥ |
bṛhaspatirutathyaśca saṃwartaśca dhṛtawratāḥ ||5||

atrestu bahawaḥ putrāḥ śrūyante manujādhipa |
sarwe wedawidaḥ siddhāḥ śāntātmāno maharṣayaḥ ||6||

rākṣasāstu pulastyasya wānarāḥ kiṃnarāstathā |
pulahasya mṛgāḥ siṃhā wyāghrāḥ kimpuruṣāstathā ||7||

kratoḥ kratusamāḥ putrāḥ pataṅgasahacāriṇaḥ |
wiśrutāstriṣu lokeṣu satyawrataparāyaṇāḥ ||8||

dakṣastwajāyatāṅguṣṭhāddakṣiṇādbhagawānṛṣiḥ |
brahmaṇaḥ pṛthiwīpāla putraḥ putrawatāṃ waraḥ ||9||

wāmādajāyatāṅguṣṭhādbhāryā tasya mahātmanaḥ |
tasyāṃ pañcāśataṃ kanyāḥ sa ewājanayanmuniḥ ||10||

tāḥ sarwāstwanawadyāṅgyaḥ kanyāḥ kamalalocanāḥ |
putrikāḥ sthāpayāmāsa naṣṭaputraḥ prajāpatiḥ ||11||

dadau sa daśa dharmāya saptawiṃśatimindawe |
diwyena widhinā rājankaśyapāya trayodaśa ||12||

nāmato dharmapatnyastāḥ kīrtyamānā nibodha me |
kīrtirlakṣmīrdhṛtirmedhā puṣṭiḥ śraddhā kriyā tathā ||13||

buddhirlajjā matiścaiwa patnyo dharmasya tā daśa |
dwārāṇyetāni dharmasya wihitāni swayambhuwā ||14||

saptawiṃśati somasya patnyo loke pariśrutāḥ |
kālasya nayane yuktāḥ somapatnyaḥ śubhawratāḥ ||15||

sarwā nakṣatrayoginyo lokayātrāwidhau sthitāḥ ||15||

pitāmaho munirdewastasya putraḥ prajāpatiḥ |
tasyāṣṭau wasawaḥ putrāsteṣāṃ wakṣyāmi wistaram ||16||

dharo dhruwaśca somaśca ahaścaiwānilo'nalaḥ |
pratyūṣaśca prabhāsaśca wasawo'ṣṭāwiti smṛtāḥ ||17||

dhūmrāyāśca dharaḥ putro brahmawidyo dhruwastathā |
candramāstu manaswinyāḥ śwasāyāḥ śwasanastathā ||18||

ratāyāścāpyahaḥ putraḥ śāṇḍilyāśca hutāśanaḥ |
pratyūṣaśca prabhāsaśca prabhātāyāḥ sutau smṛtau ||19||

dharasya putro drawiṇo hutahawyawahastathā |
dhruwasya putro bhagawānkālo lokaprakālanaḥ ||20||

somasya tu suto warcā warcaswī yena jāyate |
manoharāyāḥ śiśiraḥ prāṇo'tha ramaṇastathā ||21||

ahnaḥ sutaḥ smṛto jyotiḥ śramaḥ śāntastathā muniḥ |
agneḥ putraḥ kumārastu śrīmāñśarawaṇālayaḥ ||22||

tasya śākho wiśākhaśca naigameśaśca pṛṣṭhajaḥ |
kṛttikābhyupapatteśca kārttikeya iti smṛtaḥ ||23||

anilasya śiwā bhāryā tasyāḥ putraḥ purojawaḥ |
awijñātagatiścaiwa dwau putrāwanilasya tu ||24||

pratyūṣasya widuḥ putramṛṣiṃ nāmnātha dewalam |
dwau putrau dewalasyāpi kṣamāwantau manīṣiṇau ||25||

bṛhaspatestu bhaginī warastrī brahmacāriṇī |
yogasiddhā jagatsarwamasaktaṃ wicaratyuta ||26||

prabhāsasya tu bhāryā sā wasūnāmaṣṭamasya ha ||26||

wiśwakarmā mahābhāgo jajñe śilpaprajāpatiḥ |
kartā śilpasahasrāṇāṃ tridaśānāṃ ca wardhakiḥ ||27||

bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca sarweṣāṃ kartā śilpawatāṃ waraḥ |
yo diwyāni wimānāni dewatānāṃ cakāra ha ||28||

manuṣyāścopajīwanti yasya śilpaṃ mahātmanaḥ |
pūjayanti ca yaṃ nityaṃ wiśwakarmāṇamawyayam ||29||

stanaṃ tu dakṣiṇaṃ bhittwā brahmaṇo narawigrahaḥ |
niḥsṛto bhagawāndharmaḥ sarwalokasukhāwahaḥ ||30||

trayastasya warāḥ putrāḥ sarwabhūtamanoharāḥ |
śamaḥ kāmaśca harṣaśca tejasā lokadhāriṇaḥ ||31||

kāmasya tu ratirbhāryā śamasya prāptiraṅganā |
nandī tu bhāryā harṣasya yatra lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ||32||

marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ putraḥ kaśyapasya surāsurāḥ |
jajñire nṛpaśārdūla lokānāṃ prabhawastu saḥ ||33||

twāṣṭrī tu sawiturbhāryā waḍawārūpadhāriṇī |
asūyata mahābhāgā sāntarikṣe'śwināwubhau ||34||

dwādaśaiwāditeḥ putrāḥ śakramukhyā narādhipa |
teṣāmawarajo wiṣṇuryatra lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ||35||

trayastriṃśata ityete dewāsteṣāmahaṃ tawa |
anwayaṃ samprawakṣyāmi pakṣaiśca kulato gaṇān ||36||

rudrāṇāmaparaḥ pakṣaḥ sādhyānāṃ marutāṃ tathā |
wasūnāṃ bhārgawaṃ widyādwiśwedewāṃstathaiwa ca ||37||

wainateyastu garuḍo balawānaruṇastathā |
bṛhaspatiśca bhagawānādityeṣwewa gaṇyate ||38||

aświbhyāṃ guhyakānwiddhi sarwauṣadhyastathā paśūn |
eṣa dewagaṇo rājankīrtitaste'nupūrwaśaḥ ||39||

yaṃ kīrtayitwā manujaḥ sarwapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||39||

brahmaṇo hṛdayaṃ bhittwā niḥsṛto bhagawānbhṛguḥ |
bhṛgoḥ putraḥ kawirwidwāñśukraḥ kawisuto grahaḥ ||40||

trailokyaprāṇayātrārthe warṣāwarṣe bhayābhaye |
swayambhuwā niyuktaḥ sanbhuwanaṃ paridhāwati ||41||

yogācāryo mahābuddhirdaityānāmabhawadguruḥ |
surāṇāṃ cāpi medhāwī brahmacārī yatawrataḥ ||42||

tasminniyukte wibhunā yogakṣemāya bhārgawe |
anyamutpādayāmāsa putraṃ bhṛguraninditam ||43||

cyawanaṃ dīptatapasaṃ dharmātmānaṃ manīṣiṇam |
yaḥ sa roṣāccyuto garbhānmāturmokṣāya bhārata ||44||

āruṣī tu manoḥ kanyā tasya patnī manīṣiṇaḥ |
aurwastasyāṃ samabhawadūruṃ bhittwā mahāyaśāḥ ||45||

mahātapā mahātejā bāla ewa guṇairyutaḥ ||45||

ṛcīkastasya putrastu jamadagnistato'bhawat |
jamadagnestu catwāra āsanputrā mahātmanaḥ ||46||

rāmasteṣāṃ jaghanyo'bhūdajaghanyairguṇairyutaḥ |
sarwaśastrāstrakuśalaḥ kṣatriyāntakaro waśī ||47||

aurwasyāsītputraśataṃ jamadagnipurogamam |
teṣāṃ putrasahasrāṇi babhūwurbhṛguwistaraḥ ||48||

dwau putrau brahmaṇastwanyau yayostiṣṭhati lakṣaṇam |
loke dhātā widhātā ca yau sthitau manunā saha ||49||

tayorewa swasā dewī lakṣmīḥ padmagṛhā śubhā |
tasyāstu mānasāḥ putrāsturagā wyomacāriṇaḥ ||50||

waruṇasya bhāryā jyeṣṭhā tu śukrāddewī wyajāyata |
tasyāḥ putraṃ balaṃ widdhi surāṃ ca suranandinīm ||51||

prajānāmannakāmānāmanyonyaparibhakṣaṇāt |
adharmastatra sañjātaḥ sarwabhūtawināśanaḥ ||52||

tasyāpi nirṛtirbhāryā nairṛtā yena rākṣasāḥ |
ghorāstasyāstrayaḥ putrāḥ pāpakarmaratāḥ sadā ||53||

bhayo mahābhayaścaiwa mṛtyurbhūtāntakastathā ||53||

kākīṃ śyenīṃ ca bhāsīṃ ca dhṛtarāṣṭrīṃ tathā śukīm |
tāmrā tu suṣuwe dewī pañcaitā lokawiśrutāḥ ||54||

ulūkānsuṣuwe kākī śyenī śyenānwyajāyata |
bhāsī bhāsānajanayadgṛdhrāṃścaiwa janādhipa ||55||

dhṛtarāṣṭrī tu haṃsāṃśca kalahaṃsāṃśca sarwaśaḥ |
cakrawākāṃśca bhadraṃ te prajajñe sā tu bhāminī ||56||

śukī wijajñe dharmajña śukānewa manaswinī |
kalyāṇaguṇasampannā sarwalakṣaṇapūjitā ||57||

nawa krodhawaśā nārīḥ prajajñe'pyātmasambhawāḥ |
mṛgīṃ ca mṛgamandāṃ ca hariṃ bhadramanāmapi ||58||

mātaṅgīmatha śārdūlīṃ śwetāṃ surabhimewa ca |
sarwalakṣaṇasampannāṃ surasāṃ ca yaśaswinīm ||59||

apatyaṃ tu mṛgāḥ sarwe mṛgyā narawarātmaja |
ṛkṣāśca mṛgamandāyāḥ sṛmarāścamarā api ||60||

tatastwairāwataṃ nāgaṃ jajñe bhadramanā sutam |
airāwataḥ sutastasyā dewanāgo mahāgajaḥ ||61||

haryāśca harayo'patyaṃ wānarāśca taraswinaḥ |
golāṅgūlāṃśca bhadraṃ te haryāḥ putrānpracakṣate ||62||

prajajñe twatha śārdūlī siṃhānwyāghrāṃśca bhārata |
dwīpinaśca mahābhāga sarwānewa na saṃśayaḥ ||63||

mātaṅgyāstwatha mātaṅgā apatyāni narādhipa |
diśāgajaṃ tu śwetākhyaṃ śwetājanayadāśugam ||64||

tathā duhitarau rājansurabhirwai wyajāyata |
rohiṇīṃ caiwa bhadraṃ te gandharwīṃ ca yaśaswinīm ||65||

rohiṇyāṃ jajñire gāwo gandharwyāṃ wājinaḥ sutāḥ ||65||

surasājanayannāgānrājankadrūśca pannagān |
sapta piṇḍaphalānwṛkṣānanalāpi wyajāyata ||66||

analāyāḥ śukī putrī kadrwāstu surasā sutā ||66||

aruṇasya bhāryā śyenī tu wīryawantau mahābalau |
sampātiṃ janayāmāsa tathaiwa ca jaṭāyuṣam ||67||

dwau putrau winatāyāstu wikhyātau garuḍāruṇau ||67||

ityeṣa sarwabhūtānāṃ mahatāṃ manujādhipa |
prabhawaḥ kīrtitaḥ samyaṅmayā matimatāṃ wara ||68||

yaṃ śrutwā puruṣaḥ samyakpūto bhawati pāpmanaḥ |
sarwajñatāṃ ca labhate gatimagryāṃ ca windati ||69||






                  61


janamejaya uwāca||

dewānāṃ dānawānāṃ ca yakṣāṇāmatha rakṣasām |
anyeṣāṃ caiwa bhūtānāṃ sarweṣāṃ bhagawannaham ||1||

śrotumicchāmi tattwena mānuṣeṣu mahātmanām |
janma karma ca bhūtānāmeteṣāmanupūrwaśaḥ ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

mānuṣeṣu manuṣyendra sambhūtā ye diwaukasaḥ |
prathamaṃ dānawāṃścaiwa tāṃste wakṣyāmi sarwaśaḥ ||3||

wipracittiriti khyāto ya āsīddānawarṣabhaḥ |
jarāsandha iti khyātaḥ sa āsīnmanujarṣabhaḥ ||4||

diteḥ putrastu yo rājanhiraṇyakaśipuḥ smṛtaḥ |
sa jajñe mānuṣe loke śiśupālo nararṣabhaḥ ||5||

saṃhrāda iti wikhyātaḥ prahrādasyānujastu yaḥ |
sa śalya iti wikhyāto jajñe bāhlīkapuṅgawaḥ ||6||

anuhrādastu tejaswī yo'bhūtkhyāto jaghanyajaḥ |
dhṛṣṭaketuriti khyātaḥ sa āsīnmanujeśwaraḥ ||7||

yastu rājañśibirnāma daiteyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |
druma ityabhiwikhyātaḥ sa āsīdbhuwi pārthiwaḥ ||8||

bāṣkalo nāma yasteṣāmāsīdasurasattamaḥ |
bhagadatta iti khyātaḥ sa āsīnmanujeśwaraḥ ||9||
