ayaḥśirā aśwaśirā ayaḥśaṅkuśca wīryawān |
tathā gaganamūrdhā ca wegawāṃścātra pañcamaḥ ||10||

pañcaite jajñire rājanwīryawanto mahāsurāḥ |
kekayeṣu mahātmānaḥ pārthiwarṣabhasattamāḥ ||11||

ketumāniti wikhyāto yastato'nyaḥ pratāpawān |
amitaujā iti khyātaḥ pṛthiwyāṃ so'bhawannnṛpaḥ ||12||

swarbhānuriti wikhyātaḥ śrīmānyastu mahāsuraḥ |
ugrasena iti khyāta ugrakarmā narādhipaḥ ||13||

yastwaśwa iti wikhyātaḥ śrīmānāsīnmahāsuraḥ |
aśoko nāma rājāsīnmahāwīryaparākramaḥ ||14||

tasmādawarajo yastu rājannaśwapatiḥ smṛtaḥ |
daiteyaḥ so'bhawadrājā hārdikyo manujarṣabhaḥ ||15||

wṛṣaparweti wikhyātaḥ śrīmānyastu mahāsuraḥ |
dīrghaprajña iti khyātaḥ pṛthiwyāṃ so'bhawannṛpaḥ ||16||

ajakastwanujo rājanya āsīdwṛṣaparwaṇaḥ |
sa malla iti wikhyātaḥ pṛthiwyāmabhawannṛpaḥ ||17||

aśwagrīwa iti khyātaḥ sattwawānyo mahāsuraḥ |
rocamāna iti khyātaḥ pṛthiwyāṃ so'bhawannṛpaḥ ||18||

sūkṣmastu matimānrājankīrtimānyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |
bṛhanta iti wikhyātaḥ kṣitāwāsītsa pārthiwaḥ ||19||

tuhuṇḍa iti wikhyāto ya āsīdasurottamaḥ |
senābinduriti khyātaḥ sa babhūwa narādhipaḥ ||20||

isṛpā nāma yasteṣāmasurāṇāṃ balādhikaḥ |
pāpajinnāma rājāsīdbhuwi wikhyātawikramaḥ ||21||

ekacakra iti khyāta āsīdyastu mahāsuraḥ |
pratiwindhya iti khyāto babhūwa prathitaḥ kṣitau ||22||

wirūpākṣastu daiteyaścitrayodhī mahāsuraḥ |
citrawarmeti wikhyātaḥ kṣitāwāsītsa pārthiwaḥ ||23||

harastwariharo wīra āsīdyo dānawottamaḥ |
suwāsturiti wikhyātaḥ sa jajñe manujarṣabhaḥ ||24||

aharastu mahātejāḥ śatrupakṣakṣayaṅkaraḥ |
bāhlīko nāma rājā sa babhūwa prathitaḥ kṣitau ||25||

nicandraścandrawaktraśca ya āsīdasurottamaḥ |
muñjakeśa iti khyātaḥ śrīmānāsītsa pārthiwaḥ ||26||

nikumbhastwajitaḥ saṅkhye mahāmatirajāyata |
bhūmau bhūmipatiḥ śreṣṭho dewādhipa iti smṛtaḥ ||27||

śarabho nāma yasteṣāṃ daiteyānāṃ mahāsuraḥ |
paurawo nāma rājarṣiḥ sa babhūwa nareṣwiha ||28||

dwitīyaḥ śalabhasteṣāmasurāṇāṃ babhūwa yaḥ |
prahrādo nāma bāhlīkaḥ sa babhūwa narādhipaḥ ||29||

candrastu ditijaśreṣṭho loke tārādhipopamaḥ |
ṛṣiko nāma rājarṣirbabhūwa nṛpasattamaḥ ||30||

mṛtapā iti wikhyāto ya āsīdasurottamaḥ |
paścimānūpakaṃ widdhi taṃ nṛpaṃ nṛpasattama ||31||

gawiṣṭhastu mahātejā yaḥ prakhyāto mahāsuraḥ |
drumasena iti khyātaḥ pṛthiwyāṃ so'bhawannṛpaḥ ||32||

mayūra iti wikhyātaḥ śrīmānyastu mahāsuraḥ |
sa wiśwa iti wikhyāto babhūwa pṛthiwīpatiḥ ||33||

suparṇa iti wikhyātastasmādawarajastu yaḥ |
kālakīrtiriti khyātaḥ pṛthiwyāṃ so'bhawannṛpaḥ ||34||

candrahanteti yasteṣāṃ kīrtitaḥ prawaro'suraḥ |
śunako nāma rājarṣiḥ sa babhūwa narādhipaḥ ||35||

wināśanastu candrasya ya ākhyāto mahāsuraḥ |
jānakirnāma rājarṣiḥ sa babhūwa narādhipaḥ ||36||

dīrghajihwastu kaurawya ya ukto dānawarṣabhaḥ |
kāśirāja iti khyātaḥ pṛthiwyāṃ pṛthiwīpatiḥ ||37||

grahaṃ tu suṣuwe yaṃ taṃ siṃhī candrārkamardanam |
krātha ityabhiwikhyātaḥ so'bhawanmanujādhipaḥ ||38||

anāyuṣastu putrāṇāṃ caturṇāṃ prawaro'suraḥ |
wikṣaro nāma tejaswī wasumitro'bhawannṛpaḥ ||39||

dwitīyo wikṣarādyastu narādhipa mahāsuraḥ |
pāṃsurāṣṭrādhipa iti wiśrutaḥ so'bhawannṛpaḥ ||40||

balawīra iti khyāto yastwāsīdasurottamaḥ |
pauṇḍramatsyaka ityewa sa babhūwa narādhipaḥ ||41||

wṛtra ityabhiwikhyāto yastu rājanmahāsuraḥ |
maṇimānnāma rājarṣiḥ sa babhūwa narādhipaḥ ||42||

krodhahanteti yastasya babhūwāwarajo'suraḥ |
daṇḍa ityabhiwikhyātaḥ sa āsīnnṛpatiḥ kṣitau ||43||

krodhawardhana ityewa yastwanyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |
daṇḍadhāra iti khyātaḥ so'bhawanmanujeśwaraḥ ||44||

kālakāyāstu ye putrāsteṣāmaṣṭau narādhipāḥ |
jajñire rājaśārdūla śārdūlasamawikramāḥ ||45||

magadheṣu jayatsenaḥ śrīmānāsītsa pārthiwaḥ |
aṣṭānāṃ prawarasteṣāṃ kāleyānāṃ mahāsuraḥ ||46||

dwitīyastu tatasteṣāṃ śrīmānharihayopamaḥ |
aparājita ityewa sa babhūwa narādhipaḥ ||47||

tṛtīyastu mahārāja mahābāhurmahāsuraḥ |
niṣādādhipatirjajñe bhuwi bhīmaparākramaḥ ||48||

teṣāmanyatamo yastu caturthaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |
śreṇimāniti wikhyātaḥ kṣitau rājarṣisattamaḥ ||49||

pañcamastu babhūwaiṣāṃ prawaro yo mahāsuraḥ |
mahaujā iti wikhyāto babhūweha parantapaḥ ||50||

ṣaṣṭhastu matimānyo wai teṣāmāsīnmahāsuraḥ |
abhīruriti wikhyātaḥ kṣitau rājarṣisattamaḥ ||51||

samudrasenaśca nṛpasteṣāmewābhawadgaṇāt |
wiśrutaḥ sāgarāntāyāṃ kṣitau dharmārthatattwawit ||52||

bṛhannāmāṣṭamasteṣāṃ kāleyānāṃ parantapaḥ |
babhūwa rājandharmātmā sarwabhūtahite rataḥ ||53||

gaṇaḥ krodhawaśo nāma yaste rājanprakīrtitaḥ |
tataḥ sañjajñire wīrāḥ kṣitāwiha narādhipāḥ ||54||

nandikaḥ karṇaweṣṭaśca siddhārthaḥ kīṭakastathā |
suwīraśca subāhuśca mahāwīro'tha bāhlikaḥ ||55||

krodho wicityaḥ surasaḥ śrīmānnīlaśca bhūmipaḥ |
wīradhāmā ca kaurawya bhūmipālaśca nāmataḥ ||56||

dantawaktraśca nāmāsīddurjayaścaiwa nāmataḥ |
rukmī ca nṛpaśārdūlo rājā ca janamejayaḥ ||57||

āṣāḍho wāyuwegaśca bhūritejāstathaiwa ca |
ekalawyaḥ sumitraśca wāṭadhāno'tha gomukhaḥ ||58||

kārūṣakāśca rājānaḥ kṣemadhūrtistathaiwa ca |
śrutāyuruddhawaścaiwa bṛhatsenastathaiwa ca ||59||

kṣemogratīrthaḥ kuharaḥ kaliṅgeṣu narādhipaḥ |
matimāṃśca manuṣyendra īśwaraśceti wiśrutaḥ ||60||

gaṇātkrodhawaśādewaṃ rājapūgo'bhawatkṣitau |
jātaḥ purā mahārāja mahākīrtirmahābalaḥ ||61||

yastwāsīddewako nāma dewarājasamadyutiḥ |
sa gandharwapatirmukhyaḥ kṣitau jajñe narādhipaḥ ||62||

bṛhaspaterbṛhatkīrterdewarṣerwiddhi bhārata |
aṃśāddroṇaṃ samutpannaṃ bhāradwājamayonijam ||63||

dhanwināṃ nṛpaśārdūla yaḥ sa sarwāstrawittamaḥ |
bṛhatkīrtirmahātejāḥ sañjajñe manujeṣwiha ||64||

dhanurwede ca wede ca yaṃ taṃ wedawido widuḥ |
wariṣṭhamindrakarmāṇaṃ droṇaṃ swakulawardhanam ||65||

mahādewāntakābhyāṃ ca kāmātkrodhācca bhārata |
ekatwamupapannānāṃ jajñe śūraḥ parantapaḥ ||66||

aśwatthāmā mahāwīryaḥ śatrupakṣakṣayaṅkaraḥ |
wīraḥ kamalapatrākṣaḥ kṣitāwāsīnnarādhipa ||67||

jajñire wasawastwaṣṭau gaṅgāyāṃ śantanoḥ sutāḥ |
wasiṣṭhasya ca śāpena niyogādwāsawasya ca ||68||

teṣāmawarajo bhīṣmaḥ kurūṇāmabhayaṅkaraḥ |
matimānwedawidwāgmī śatrupakṣakṣayaṅkaraḥ ||69||

jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa yaḥ sa sarwawidāṃ waraḥ |
ayudhyata mahātejā bhārgaweṇa mahātmanā ||70||

yastu rājankṛpo nāma brahmarṣirabhawatkṣitau |
rudrāṇāṃ taṃ gaṇādwiddhi sambhūtamatipauruṣam ||71||

śakunirnāma yastwāsīdrājā loke mahārathaḥ |
dwāparaṃ widdhi taṃ rājansambhūtamarimardanam ||72||

sātyakiḥ satyasandhastu yo'sau wṛṣṇikulodwahaḥ |
pakṣātsa jajñe marutāṃ dewānāmarimardanaḥ ||73||

drupadaścāpi rājarṣistata ewābhawadgaṇāt |
mānuṣe nṛpa loke'sminsarwaśastrabhṛtāṃ waraḥ ||74||

tataśca kṛtawarmāṇaṃ widdhi rājañjanādhipam |
jātamapratikarmāṇaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhasattamam ||75||

marutāṃ tu gaṇādwiddhi sañjātamarimardanam |
wirāṭaṃ nāma rājarṣiṃ pararāṣṭrapratāpanam ||76||

ariṣṭāyāstu yaḥ putro haṃsa ityabhiwiśrutaḥ |
sa gandharwapatirjajñe kuruwaṃśawiwardhanaḥ ||77||

dhṛtarāṣṭra iti khyātaḥ kṛṣṇadwaipāyanādapi |
dīrghabāhurmahātejāḥ prajñācakṣurnarādhipaḥ ||78||

māturdoṣādṛṣeḥ kopādandha ewa wyajāyata ||78||

atrestu sumahābhāgaṃ putraṃ putrawatāṃ waram |
widuraṃ widdhi loke'smiñjātaṃ buddhimatāṃ waram ||79||

kaleraṃśāttu sañjajñe bhuwi duryodhano nṛpaḥ |
durbuddhirdurmatiścaiwa kurūṇāmayaśaskaraḥ ||80||

jagato yaḥ sa sarwasya widwiṣṭaḥ kalipūruṣaḥ |
yaḥ sarwāṃ ghātayāmāsa pṛthiwīṃ puruṣādhamaḥ ||81||

yena wairaṃ samuddīptaṃ bhūtāntakaraṇaṃ mahat ||81||

paulastyā bhrātaraḥ sarwe jajñire manujeṣwiha |
śataṃ duḥśāsanādīnāṃ sarweṣāṃ krūrakarmaṇām ||82||

durmukho duḥsahaścaiwa ye cānye nānuśabditāḥ |
duryodhanasahāyāste paulastyā bharatarṣabha ||83||

dharmasyāṃśaṃ tu rājānaṃ widdhi rājanyudhiṣṭhiram |
bhīmasenaṃ tu wātasya dewarājasya cārjunam ||84||

aświnostu tathaiwāṃśau rūpeṇāpratimau bhuwi |
nakulaḥ sahadewaśca sarwalokamanoharau ||85||

yaḥ suwarcā iti khyātaḥ somaputraḥ pratāpawān |
abhimanyurbṛhatkīrtirarjunasya suto'bhawat ||86||

agneraṃśaṃ tu widdhi twaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāratham |
śikhaṇḍinamatho rājanstrīpuṃsaṃ widdhi rākṣasam ||87||

draupadeyāśca ye pañca babhūwurbharatarṣabha |
wiśwedewagaṇānrājaṃstānwiddhi bharatarṣabha ||88||

āmuktakawacaḥ karṇo yastu jajñe mahārathaḥ |
diwākarasya taṃ widdhi dewasyāṃśamanuttamam ||89||

yastu nārāyaṇo nāma dewadewaḥ sanātanaḥ |
tasyāṃśo mānuṣeṣwāsīdwāsudewaḥ pratāpawān ||90||

śeṣasyāṃśastu nāgasya baladewo mahābalaḥ |
sanatkumāraṃ pradyumnaṃ widdhi rājanmahaujasam ||91||

ewamanye manuṣyendra bahawoṃ'śā diwaukasām |
jajñire wasudewasya kule kulawiwardhanāḥ ||92||

gaṇastwapsarasāṃ yo wai mayā rājanprakīrtitaḥ |
tasya bhāgaḥ kṣitau jajñe niyogādwāsawasya ca ||93||

tāni ṣoḍaśa dewīnāṃ sahasrāṇi narādhipa |
babhūwurmānuṣe loke nārāyaṇaparigrahaḥ ||94||

śriyastu bhāgaḥ sañjajñe ratyarthaṃ pṛthiwītale |
drupadasya kule kanyā wedimadhyādaninditā ||95||

nātihraswā na mahatī nīlotpalasugandhinī |
padmāyatākṣī suśroṇī asitāyatamūrdhajā ||96||

sarwalakṣaṇasampannā waiḍūryamaṇisaṃnibhā |
pañcānāṃ puruṣendrāṇāṃ cittapramathinī rahaḥ ||97||

siddhirdhṛtiśca ye dewyau pañcānāṃ mātarau tu te |
kuntī mādrī ca jajñāte matistu subalātmajā ||98||

iti dewāsurāṇāṃ te gandharwāpsarasāṃ tathā |
aṃśāwataraṇaṃ rājanrākṣasānāṃ ca kīrtitam ||99||

ye pṛthiwyāṃ samudbhūtā rājāno yuddhadurmadāḥ |
mahātmāno yadūnāṃ ca ye jātā wipule kule ||100||

dhanyaṃ yaśasyaṃ putrīyamāyuṣyaṃ wijayāwaham |
idamaṃśāwataraṇaṃ śrotawyamanasūyatā ||101||

aṃśāwataraṇaṃ śrutwā dewagandharwarakṣasām |
prabhawāpyayawitprājño na kṛcchreṣwawasīdati ||102||






              saṃbhawaparwa
              śaṃkutalopākhyānam
                  62


janamejaya uwāca||

twattaḥ śrutamidaṃ brahmandewadānawarakṣasām |
aṃśāwataraṇaṃ samyaggandharwāpsarasāṃ tathā ||1||

imaṃ tu bhūya icchāmi kurūṇāṃ waṃśamāditaḥ |
kathyamānaṃ twayā wipra wiprarṣigaṇasaṃnidhau ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

paurawāṇāṃ waṃśakaro duḥṣanto nāma wīryawān |
pṛthiwyāścaturantāyā goptā bharatasattama ||3||

caturbhāgaṃ bhuwaḥ kṛtsnaṃ sa bhuṅkte manujeśwaraḥ |
samudrāwaraṇāṃścāpi deśānsa samitiñjayaḥ ||4||

āmlecchāṭawikānsarwānsa bhuṅkte ripumardanaḥ |
ratnākarasamudrāntāṃścāturwarṇyajanāwṛtān ||5||

na warṇasaṅkarakaro nākṛṣyakarakṛjjanaḥ |
na pāpakṛtkaścidāsīttasminrājani śāsati ||6||

dharmyāṃ ratiṃ sewamānā dharmārthāwabhipedire |
tadā narā narawyāghra tasmiñjanapadeśware ||7||

nāsīccorabhayaṃ tāta na kṣudhābhayamaṇwapi |
nāsīdwyādhibhayaṃ cāpi tasmiñjanapadeśware ||8||

swairdharmai remire warṇā daiwe karmaṇi niḥspṛhāḥ |
tamāśritya mahīpālamāsaṃścaiwākutobhayāḥ ||9||

kālawarṣī ca parjanyaḥ sasyāni phalawanti ca |
sarwaratnasamṛddhā ca mahī wasumatī tadā ||10||

sa cādbhutamahāwīryo wajrasaṃhanano yuwā |
udyamya mandaraṃ dorbhyāṃ haretsawanakānanam ||11||

dhanuṣyatha gadāyuddhe tsarupraharaṇeṣu ca |
nāgapṛṣṭhe'śwapṛṣṭhe ca babhūwa pariniṣṭhitaḥ ||12||

bale wiṣṇusamaścāsīttejasā bhāskaropamaḥ |
akṣubdhatwe'rṇawasamaḥ sahiṣṇutwe dharāsamaḥ ||13||

saṃmataḥ sa mahīpālaḥ prasannapurarāṣṭrawān |
bhūyo dharmaparairbhāwairwiditaṃ janamāwasat ||14||






                  63


waiśampāyana uwāca||

sa kadācinmahābāhuḥ prabhūtabalawāhanaḥ |
wanaṃ jagāma gahanaṃ hayanāgaśatairwṛtaḥ ||1||

khaḍgaśaktidharairwīrairgadāmusalapāṇibhiḥ |
prāsatomarahastaiśca yayau yodhaśatairwṛtaḥ ||2||

siṃhanādaiśca yodhānāṃ śaṅkhadundubhiniswanaiḥ |
rathanemiswanaiścāpi sanāgawarabṛṃhitaiḥ ||3||

heṣitaswanamiśraiśca kṣweḍitāsphoṭitaswanaiḥ |
āsītkilakilāśabdastasmingacchati pārthiwe ||4||

prāsādawaraśṛṅgasthāḥ parayā nṛpaśobhayā |
dadṛśustaṃ striyastatra śūramātmayaśaskaram ||5||

śakropamamamitraghnaṃ parawāraṇawāraṇam |
paśyantaḥ strīgaṇāstatra śastrapāṇiṃ sma menire ||6||

ayaṃ sa puruṣawyāghro raṇe'dbhutaparākramaḥ |
yasya bāhubalaṃ prāpya na bhawantyasuhṛdgaṇāḥ ||7||

iti wāco bruwantyastāḥ striyaḥ premṇā narādhipam |
tuṣṭuwuḥ puṣpawṛṣṭīśca sasṛjustasya mūrdhani ||8||

tatra tatra ca wiprendraiḥ stūyamānaḥ samantataḥ |
niryayau parayā prītyā wanaṃ mṛgajighāṃsayā ||9||

sudūramanujagmustaṃ paurajānapadāstadā |
nyawartanta tataḥ paścādanujñātā nṛpeṇa ha ||10||

suparṇapratimenātha rathena wasudhādhipaḥ |
mahīmāpūrayāmāsa ghoṣeṇa tridiwaṃ tathā ||11||

sa gacchandadṛśe dhīmānnandanapratimaṃ wanam |
bilwārkakhadirākīrṇaṃ kapitthadhawasaṅkulam ||12||

wiṣamaṃ parwataprasthairaśmabhiśca samāwṛtam |
nirjalaṃ nirmanuṣyaṃ ca bahuyojanamāyatam ||13||

mṛgasaṅghairwṛtaṃ ghorairanyaiścāpi wanecaraiḥ ||13||

tadwanaṃ manujawyāghraḥ sabhṛtyabalawāhanaḥ |
loḍayāmāsa duḥṣantaḥ sūdayanwiwidhānmṛgān ||14||

bāṇagocarasamprāptāṃstatra wyāghragaṇānbahūn |
pātayāmāsa duḥṣanto nirbibheda ca sāyakaiḥ ||15||

dūrasthānsāyakaiḥ kāṃścidabhinatsa nararṣabhaḥ |
abhyāśamāgatāṃścānyānkhaḍgena nirakṛntata ||16||

kāṃścideṇānsa nirjaghne śaktyā śaktimatāṃ waraḥ |
gadāmaṇḍalatattwajñaścacārāmitawikramaḥ ||17||

tomarairasibhiścāpi gadāmusalakarpaṇaiḥ |
cacāra sa winighnanwai wanyāṃstatra mṛgadwijān ||18||

rājñā cādbhutawīryeṇa yodhaiśca samarapriyaiḥ |
loḍyamānaṃ mahāraṇyaṃ tatyajuśca mahāmṛgāḥ ||19||

tatra widrutasaṅghāni hatayūthapatīni ca |
mṛgayūthānyathautsukyācchabdaṃ cakrustatastataḥ ||20||

śuṣkāṃ cāpi nadīṃ gatwā jalanairāśyakarśitāḥ |
wyāyāmaklāntahṛdayāḥ patanti sma wicetasaḥ ||21||

kṣutpipāsāparītāśca śrāntāśca patitā bhuwi |
kecittatra narawyāghrairabhakṣyanta bubhukṣitaiḥ ||22||

kecidagnimathotpādya samidhya ca wanecarāḥ |
bhakṣayanti sma māṃsāni prakuṭya widhiwattadā ||23||

tatra kecidgajā mattā balinaḥ śastrawikṣatāḥ |
saṅkocyāgrakarānbhītāḥ pradrawanti sma wegitāḥ ||24||

śakṛnmūtraṃ sṛjantaśca kṣarantaḥ śoṇitaṃ bahu |
wanyā gajawarāstatra mamṛdurmanujānbahūn ||25||

tadwanaṃ balameghena śaradhāreṇa saṃwṛtam |
wyarocanmahiṣākīrṇaṃ rājñā hatamahāmṛgam ||26||






                  64


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato mṛgasahasrāṇi hatwā wipulawāhanaḥ |
rājā mṛgaprasaṅgena wanamanyadwiweśa ha ||1||

eka ewottamabalaḥ kṣutpipāsāsamanwitaḥ |
sa wanasyāntamāsādya mahadīriṇamāsadat ||2||

taccāpyatītya nṛpatiruttamāśramasaṃyutam |
manaḥprahlādajananaṃ dṛṣṭikāntamatīwa ca ||3||

śītamārutasaṃyuktaṃ jagāmānyanmahadwanam ||3||

puṣpitaiḥ pādapaiḥ kīrṇamatīwa sukhaśādwalam |
wipulaṃ madhurārāwairnāditaṃ wihagaistathā ||4||

prawṛddhawiṭapairwṛkṣaiḥ sukhacchāyaiḥ samāwṛtam |
ṣaṭpadāghūrṇitalataṃ lakṣmyā paramayā yutam ||5||

nāpuṣpaḥ pādapaḥ kaścinnāphalo nāpi kaṇṭakī |
ṣaṭpadairwāpyanākīrṇastasminwai kānane'bhawat ||6||

wihagairnāditaṃ puṣpairalaṅkṛtamatīwa ca |
sarwartukusumairwṛkṣairatīwa sukhaśādwalam ||7||

manoramaṃ maheṣwāso wiweśa wanamuttamam ||7||

mārutāgalitāstatra drumāḥ kusumaśālinaḥ |
puṣpawṛṣṭiṃ wicitrāṃ sma wyasṛjaṃste punaḥ punaḥ ||8||

diwaspṛśo'tha saṅghuṣṭāḥ pakṣibhirmadhuraswaraiḥ |
wirejuḥ pādapāstatra wicitrakusumāmbarāḥ ||9||

teṣāṃ tatra prawāleṣu puṣpabhārāwanāmiṣu |
ruwanti rāwaṃ wihagāḥ ṣaṭpadaiḥ sahitā mṛdu ||10||

tatra pradeśāṃśca bahūnkusumotkaramaṇḍitān |
latāgṛhaparikṣiptānmanasaḥ prītiwardhanān ||11||

sampaśyansa mahātejā babhūwa muditastadā ||11||

parasparāśliṣṭaśākhaiḥ pādapaiḥ kusumācitaiḥ |
aśobhata wanaṃ tattairmahendradhwajasaṃnibhaiḥ ||12||

sukhaśītaḥ sugandhī ca puṣpareṇuwaho'nilaḥ |
parikrāmanwane wṛkṣānupaitīwa riraṃsayā ||13||

ewaṅguṇasamāyuktaṃ dadarśa sa wanaṃ nṛpaḥ |
nadīkacchodbhawaṃ kāntamucchritadhwajasaṃnibham ||14||

prekṣamāṇo wanaṃ tattu suprahṛṣṭawihaṅgamam |
āśramaprawaraṃ ramyaṃ dadarśa ca manoramam ||15||

nānāwṛkṣasamākīrṇaṃ samprajwalitapāwakam |
yatibhirwālakhilyaiśca wṛtaṃ munigaṇānwitam ||16||

agnyāgāraiśca bahubhiḥ puṣpasaṃstarasaṃstṛtam |
mahākacchairbṛhadbhiśca wibhrājitamatīwa ca ||17||

mālinīmabhito rājannadīṃ puṇyāṃ sukhodakām |
naikapakṣigaṇākīrṇāṃ tapowanamanoramām ||18||

tatra wyālamṛgānsaumyānpaśyanprītimawāpa saḥ ||18||

taṃ cāpyatirathaḥ śrīmānāśramaṃ pratyapadyata |
dewalokapratīkāśaṃ sarwataḥ sumanoharam ||19||

nadīmāśramasaṃśliṣṭāṃ puṇyatoyāṃ dadarśa saḥ |
sarwaprāṇabhṛtāṃ tatra jananīmiwa wiṣṭhitām ||20||

sacakrawākapulināṃ puṣpaphenaprawāhinīm |
sakiṃnaragaṇāwāsāṃ wānararkṣaniṣewitām ||21||

puṇyaswādhyāyasaṅghuṣṭāṃ pulinairupaśobhitām |
mattawāraṇaśārdūlabhujagendraniṣewitām ||22||

nadīmāśramasambaddhāṃ dṛṣṭwāśramapadaṃ tathā |
cakārābhipraweśāya matiṃ sa nṛpatistadā ||23||

alaṅkṛtaṃ dwīpawatyā mālinyā ramyatīrayā |
naranārāyaṇasthānaṃ gaṅgayewopaśobhitam ||24||

mattabarhiṇasaṅghuṣṭaṃ prawiweśa mahadwanam ||24||

tatsa caitrarathaprakhyaṃ samupetya nareśwaraḥ |
atīwa guṇasampannamanirdeśyaṃ ca warcasā ||25||

maharṣiṃ kāśyapaṃ draṣṭumatha kaṇwaṃ tapodhanam ||25||

rathinīmaśwasambādhāṃ padātigaṇasaṅkulām |
awasthāpya wanadwāri senāmidamuwāca saḥ ||26||

muniṃ wirajasaṃ draṣṭuṃ gamiṣyāmi tapodhanam |
kāśyapaṃ sthīyatāmatra yāwadāgamanaṃ mama ||27||

tadwanaṃ nandanaprakhyamāsādya manujeśwaraḥ |
kṣutpipāse jahau rājā harṣaṃ cāwāpa puṣkalam ||28||

sāmātyo rājaliṅgāni so'panīya narādhipaḥ |
purohitasahāyaśca jagāmāśramamuttamam ||29||

didṛkṣustatra tamṛṣiṃ taporāśimathāwyayam ||29||

brahmalokapratīkāśamāśramaṃ so'bhiwīkṣya ca |
ṣaṭpadodgītasaṅghuṣṭaṃ nānādwija gaṇāyutam ||30||

ṛco bahwṛcamukhyaiśca preryamāṇāḥ padakramaiḥ |
śuśrāwa manujawyāghro witateṣwiha karmasu ||31||

yajñawidyāṅgawidbhiśca kramadbhiśca kramānapi |
amitātmabhiḥ suniyataiḥ śuśubhe sa tadāśramaḥ ||32||

atharwawedaprawarāḥ pūgayājñika saṃmatāḥ |
saṃhitāmīrayanti sma padakramayutāṃ tu te ||33||

śabdasaṃskārasaṃyuktaṃ bruwadbhiścāparairdwijaiḥ |
nāditaḥ sa babhau śrīmānbrahmaloka iwāśramaḥ ||34||

yajñasaṃskārawidbhiśca kramaśikṣā wiśāradaiḥ |
nyāyatattwārthawijñānasampannairwedapāragaiḥ ||35||

nānāwākyasamāhārasamawāyawiśāradaiḥ |
wiśeṣakāryawidbhiśca mokṣadharmaparāyaṇaiḥ ||36||

sthāpanākṣepasiddhāntaparamārthajñatāṃ gataiḥ |
lokāyatikamukhyaiśca samantādanunāditam ||37||

tatra tatra ca wiprendrānniyatānsaṃśitawratān |
japahomaparānsiddhāndadarśa parawīrahā ||38||

āsanāni wicitrāṇi puṣpawanti mahīpatiḥ |
prayatnopahitāni sma dṛṣṭwā wismayamāgamat ||39||

dewatāyatanānāṃ ca pūjāṃ prekṣya kṛtāṃ dwijaiḥ |
brahmalokasthamātmānaṃ mene sa nṛpasattamaḥ ||40||

sa kāśyapatapoguptamāśramaprawaraṃ śubham |
nātṛpyatprekṣamāṇo wai tapodhanagaṇairyutam ||41||

sa kāśyapasyāyatanaṃ mahāwratai; rwṛtaṃ samantādṛṣibhistapodhanaiḥ |
wiweśa sāmātyapurohito'rihā; wiwiktamatyarthamanoharaṃ śiwam ||42||






                  65


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato gacchanmahābāhureko'mātyānwisṛjya tān |
nāpaśyadāśrame tasmiṃstamṛṣiṃ saṃśitawratam ||1||

so'paśyamānastamṛṣiṃ śūnyaṃ dṛṣṭwā tamāśramam |
uwāca ka ihetyuccairwanaṃ saṃnādayanniwa ||2||

śrutwātha tasya taṃ śabdaṃ kanyā śrīriwa rūpiṇī |
niścakrāmāśramāttasmāttāpasīweṣadhāriṇī ||3||

sā taṃ dṛṣṭwaiwa rājānaṃ duḥṣantamasitekṣaṇā |
swāgataṃ ta iti kṣipramuwāca pratipūjya ca ||4||

āsanenārcayitwā ca pādyenārghyeṇa caiwa hi |
papracchānāmayaṃ rājankuśalaṃ ca narādhipam ||5||

yathāwadarcayitwā sā pṛṣṭwā cānāmayaṃ tadā |
uwāca smayamānewa kiṃ kāryaṃ kriyatāmiti ||6||

tāmabrawīttato rājā kanyāṃ madhurabhāṣiṇīm |
dṛṣṭwā sarwānawadyāṅgīṃ yathāwatpratipūjitaḥ ||7||

āgato'haṃ mahābhāgamṛṣiṃ kaṇwamupāsitum |
kwa gato bhagawānbhadre tanmamācakṣwa śobhane ||8||

śakuntalowāca||

gataḥ pitā me bhagawānphalānyāhartumāśramāt |
muhūrtaṃ sampratīkṣaswa drakṣyasyenamihāgatam ||9||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

apaśyamānastamṛṣiṃ tayā coktastathā nṛpaḥ |
tāṃ ca dṛṣṭwā warārohāṃ śrīmatīṃ cāruhāsinīm ||10||

wibhrājamānāṃ wapuṣā tapasā ca damena ca |
rūpayauwanasampannāmityuwāca mahīpatiḥ ||11||

kāsi kasyāsi suśroṇi kimarthaṃ cāgatā wanam |
ewaṃrūpaguṇopetā kutastwamasi śobhane ||12||

darśanādewa hi śubhe twayā me'pahṛtaṃ manaḥ |
icchāmi twāmahaṃ jñātuṃ tanmamācakṣwa śobhane ||13||

ewamuktā tadā kanyā tena rājñā tadāśrame |
uwāca hasatī wākyamidaṃ sumadhurākṣaram ||14||

kaṇwaṣyāhaṃ bhagawato duḥṣanta duhitā matā |
tapaswino dhṛtimato dharmajñasya yaśaswinaḥ ||15||

duḥṣanta uwāca||

ūrdhwaretā mahābhāgo bhagawāṃllokapūjitaḥ |
caleddhi wṛttāddharmo'pi na caletsaṃśitawrataḥ ||16||

kathaṃ twaṃ tasya duhitā sambhūtā warawarṇinī |
saṃśayo me mahānatra taṃ me chettumihārhasi ||17||

śakuntalowāca||

yathāyamāgamo mahyaṃ yathā cedamabhūtpurā |
śṛṇu rājanyathātattwaṃ yathāsmi duhitā muneḥ ||18||

ṛṣiḥ kaścidihāgamya mama janmābhyacodayat |
tasmai prowāca bhagawānyathā tacchṛṇu pārthiwa ||19||

tapyamānaḥ kila purā wiśwāmitro mahattapaḥ |
subhṛśaṃ tāpayāmāsa śakraṃ suragaṇeśwaram ||20||

tapasā dīptawīryo'yaṃ sthānānmāṃ cyāwayediti |
bhītaḥ puraṃdarastasmānmenakāmidamabrawīt ||21||

guṇairdiwyairapsarasāṃ menake twaṃ wiśiṣyase |
śreyo me kuru kalyāṇi yattwāṃ wakṣyāmi tacchṛṇu ||22||

asāwādityasaṅkāśo wiśwāmitro mahātapāḥ |
tapyamānastapo ghoraṃ mama kampayate manaḥ ||23||

menake tawa bhāro'yaṃ wiśwāmitraḥ sumadhyame |
saṃśitātmā sudurdharṣa ugre tapasi wartate ||24||

sa māṃ na cyāwayetsthānāttaṃ wai gatwā pralobhaya |
cara tasya tapowighnaṃ kuru me priyamuttamam ||25||

rūpayauwanamādhuryaceṣṭitasmitabhāṣitaiḥ |
lobhayitwā warārohe tapasaḥ saṃniwartaya ||26||

menakowāca||

mahātejāḥ sa bhagawānsadaiwa ca mahātapāḥ |
kopanaśca tathā hyenaṃ jānāti bhagawānapi ||27||

tejasastapasaścaiwa kopasya ca mahātmanaḥ |
twamapyudwijase yasya nodwijeyamahaṃ katham ||28||

mahābhāgaṃ wasiṣṭhaṃ yaḥ putrairiṣṭairwyayojayat |
kṣatre jātaśca yaḥ pūrwamabhawadbrāhmaṇo balāt ||29||

śaucārthaṃ yo nadīṃ cakre durgamāṃ bahubhirjalaiḥ |
yāṃ tāṃ puṇyatamāṃ loke kauśikīti widurjanāḥ ||30||

babhāra yatrāsya purā kāle durge mahātmanaḥ |
dārānmataṅgo dharmātmā rājarṣirwyādhatāṃ gataḥ ||31||

atītakāle durbhikṣe yatraitya punarāśramam |
muniḥ pāreti nadyā wai nāma cakre tadā prabhuḥ ||32||

mataṅgaṃ yājayāṃ cakre yatra prītamanāḥ swayam |
twaṃ ca somaṃ bhayādyasya gataḥ pātuṃ śureśwara ||33||

ati nakṣatrawaṃśāṃśca kruddho nakṣatrasampadā |
prati śrawaṇapūrwāṇi nakṣatrāṇi sasarja yaḥ ||34||

etāni yasya karmāṇi tasyāhaṃ bhṛśamudwije |
yathā māṃ na dahetkruddhastathājñāpaya māṃ wibho ||35||

tejasā nirdahellokānkampayeddharaṇīṃ padā |
saṅkṣipecca mahāmeruṃ tūrṇamāwartayettathā ||36||

tādṛśaṃ tapasā yuktaṃ pradīptamiwa pāwakam |
kathamasmadwidhā bālā jitendriyamabhispṛśet ||37||

hutāśanamukhaṃ dīptaṃ sūryacandrākṣitārakam |
kālajihwaṃ suraśreṣṭha kathamasmadwidhā spṛśet ||38||

yamaśca somaśca maharṣayaśca; sādhyā wiśwe wālakhilyāśca sarwe |
ete'pi yasyodwijante prabhāwā; tkasmāttasmānmādṛśī nodwijeta ||39||

twayaiwamuktā ca kathaṃ samīpa; mṛṣerna gaccheyamahaṃ surendra |
rakṣāṃ tu me cintaya dewarāja; yathā twadarthaṃ rakṣitāhaṃ careyam ||40||

kāmaṃ tu me mārutastatra wāsaḥ; prakrīḍitāyā wiwṛṇotu dewa |
bhawecca me manmathastatra kārye; sahāyabhūtastawa dewaprasādāt ||41||

wanācca wāyuḥ surabhiḥ prawāye; ttasminkāle tamṛṣiṃ lobhayantyāḥ |
tathetyuktwā wihite caiwa tasmiṃ; stato yayau sāśramaṃ kauśikasya ||42||






                  66


śakuntalowāca||

ewamuktastayā śakraḥ saṃdideśa sadāgatim |
prātiṣṭhata tadā kāle menakā wāyunā saha ||1||

athāpaśyadwarārohā tapasā dagdhakilbiṣam |
wiśwāmitraṃ tapasyantaṃ menakā bhīrurāśrame ||2||

abhiwādya tataḥ sā taṃ prākrīḍadṛṣisaṃnidhau |
apowāha ca wāso'syā mārutaḥ śaśisaṃnibham ||3||

sāgacchattwaritā bhūmiṃ wāsastadabhiliṅgatī |
utsmayantīwa sawrīḍaṃ mārutaṃ warawarṇinī ||4||

gṛddhāṃ wāsasi sambhrāntāṃ menakāṃ munisattamaḥ |
anirdeśyawayorūpāmapaśyadwiwṛtāṃ tadā ||5||

tasyā rūpaguṇaṃ dṛṣṭwā sa tu wiprarṣabhastadā |
cakāra bhāwaṃ saṃsarge tayā kāmawaśaṃ gataḥ ||6||

nyamantrayata cāpyenāṃ sā cāpyaicchadaninditā |
tau tatra suciraṃ kālaṃ wane wyaharatāmubhau ||7||

ramamāṇau yathākāmaṃ yathaikadiwasaṃ tathā ||7||

janayāmāsa sa munirmenakāyāṃ śakuntalām |
prasthe himawato ramye mālinīmabhito nadīm ||8||

jātamutsṛjya taṃ garbhaṃ menakā mālinīmanu |
kṛtakāryā tatastūrṇamagacchacchakrasaṃsadam ||9||

taṃ wane wijane garbhaṃ siṃhawyāghrasamākule |
dṛṣṭwā śayānaṃ śakunāḥ samantātparyawārayan ||10||

nemāṃ hiṃsyurwane bālāṃ krawyādā māṃsagṛddhinaḥ |
paryarakṣanta tāṃ tatra śakuntā menakātmajām ||11||

upaspraṣṭuṃ gataścāhamapaśyaṃ śayitāmimām |
nirjane wipine'raṇye śakuntaiḥ pariwāritām ||12||

ānayitwā tataścaināṃ duhitṛtwe nyayojayam ||12||

śarīrakṛtprāṇadātā yasya cānnāni bhuñjate |
krameṇa te trayo'pyuktāḥ pitaro dharmaniścaye ||13||

nirjane ca wane yasmācchakuntaiḥ parirakṣitā |
śakuntaleti nāmāsyāḥ kṛtaṃ cāpi tato mayā ||14||

ewaṃ duhitaraṃ widdhi mama saumya śakuntalām |
śakuntalā ca pitaraṃ manyate māmaninditā ||15||

etadācaṣṭa pṛṣṭaḥ sanmama janma maharṣaye |
sutāṃ kaṇwasya māmewaṃ widdhi twaṃ manujādhipa ||16||

kaṇwaṃ hi pitaraṃ manye pitaraṃ swamajānatī |
iti te kathitaṃ rājanyathāwṛttaṃ śrutaṃ mayā ||17||






                  67


duḥṣanta uwāca||

suwyaktaṃ rājaputrī twaṃ yathā kalyāṇi bhāṣase |
bhāryā me bhawa suśroṇi brūhi kiṃ karawāṇi te ||1||

suwarṇamālā wāsāṃsi kuṇḍale parihāṭake |
nānāpattanaje śubhre maṇiratne ca śobhane ||2||

āharāmi tawādyāhaṃ niṣkādīnyajināni ca |
sarwaṃ rājyaṃ tawādyāstu bhāryā me bhawa śobhane ||3||

gāndharweṇa ca māṃ bhīru wiwāhenaihi sundari |
wiwāhānāṃ hi rambhoru gāndharwaḥ śreṣṭha ucyate ||4||

śakuntalowāca||

phalāhāro gato rājanpitā me ita āśramāt |
taṃ muhūrtaṃ pratīkṣaswa sa māṃ tubhyaṃ pradāsyati ||5||

duḥṣanta uwāca||

icchāmi twāṃ warārohe bhajamānāmanindite |
twadarthaṃ māṃ sthitaṃ widdhi twadgataṃ hi mano mama ||6||

ātmano bandhurātmaiwa gatirātmaiwa cātmanaḥ |
ātmanaiwātmano dānaṃ kartumarhasi dharmataḥ ||7||

aṣṭāwewa samāsena wiwāhā dharmataḥ smṛtāḥ |
brāhmo daiwastathaiwārṣaḥ prājāpatyastathāsuraḥ ||8||

gāndharwo rākṣasaścaiwa paiśācaścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ |
teṣāṃ dharmānyathāpūrwaṃ manuḥ swāyambhuwo'brawīt ||9||

praśastāṃścaturaḥ pūrwānbrāhmaṇasyopadhāraya |
ṣaḍānupūrwyā kṣatrasya widdhi dharmyānanindite ||10||

rājñāṃ tu rākṣaso'pyukto wiṭśūdreṣwāsuraḥ smṛtaḥ |
pañcānāṃ tu trayo dharmyā dwāwadharmyau smṛtāwiha ||11||

paiśācaścāsuraścaiwa na kartawyau kathañcana |
anena widhinā kāryo dharmasyaiṣā gatiḥ smṛtā ||12||

gāndharwarākṣasau kṣatre dharmyau tau mā wiśaṅkithāḥ |
pṛthagwā yadi wā miśrau kartawyau nātra saṃśayaḥ ||13||

sā twaṃ mama sakāmasya sakāmā warawarṇini |
gāndharweṇa wiwāhena bhāryā bhawitumarhasi ||14||

śakuntalowāca||

yadi dharmapathastweṣa yadi cātmā prabhurmama |
pradāne paurawaśreṣṭha śṛṇu me samayaṃ prabho ||15||

satyaṃ me pratijānīhi yattwāṃ wakṣyāmyahaṃ rahaḥ |
mama jāyeta yaḥ putraḥ sa bhawettwadanantaram ||16||

yuwarājo mahārāja satyametadbrawīhi me |
yadyetadewaṃ duḥṣanta astu me saṅgamastwayā ||17||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamastwiti tāṃ rājā pratyuwācāwicārayan |
api ca twāṃ nayiṣyāmi nagaraṃ swaṃ śucismite ||18||

yathā twamarhā suśroṇi satyametadbrawīmi te ||18||

ewamuktwā sa rājarṣistāmaninditagāminīm |
jagrāha widhiwatpāṇāwuwāsa ca tayā saha ||19||

wiśwāsya caināṃ sa prāyādabrawīcca punaḥ punaḥ |
preṣayiṣye tawārthāya wāhinīṃ caturaṅgiṇīm ||20||

tayā twāmānayiṣyāmi niwāsaṃ swaṃ śucismite ||20||

iti tasyāḥ pratiśrutya sa nṛpo janamejaya |
manasā cintayanprāyātkāśyapaṃ prati pārthiwaḥ ||21||

bhagawāṃstapasā yuktaḥ śrutwā kiṃ nu kariṣyati |
ewaṃ sañcintayannewa prawiweśa swakaṃ puram ||22||

muhūrtayāte tasmiṃstu kaṇwo'pyāśramamāgamat |
śakuntalā ca pitaraṃ hriyā nopajagāma tam ||23||

wijñāyātha ca tāṃ kaṇwo diwyajñāno mahātapāḥ |
uwāca bhagawānprītaḥ paśyandiwyena cakṣuṣā ||24||

twayādya rājānwayayā māmanādṛtya yatkṛtaḥ |
puṃsā saha samāyogo na sa dharmopaghātakaḥ ||25||

kṣatriyasya hi gāndharwo wiwāhaḥ śreṣṭha ucyate |
sakāmāyāḥ sakāmena nirmantro rahasi smṛtaḥ ||26||

dharmātmā ca mahātmā ca duḥṣantaḥ puruṣottamaḥ |
abhyagacchaḥ patiṃ yaṃ twaṃ bhajamānaṃ śakuntale ||27||

mahātmā janitā loke putrastawa mahābalaḥ |
ya imāṃ sāgarāpāṅgāṃ kṛtsnāṃ bhokṣyati medinīm ||28||

paraṃ cābhiprayātasya cakraṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ |
bhawiṣyatyapratihataṃ satataṃ cakrawartinaḥ ||29||

tataḥ prakṣālya pādau sā wiśrāntaṃ munimabrawīt |
winidhāya tato bhāraṃ saṃnidhāya phalāni ca ||30||

mayā patirwṛto yo'sau duḥṣantaḥ puruṣottamaḥ |
tasmai sasaciwāya twaṃ prasādaṃ kartumarhasi ||31||

kaṇwa uwāca||

prasanna ewa tasyāhaṃ twatkṛte warawarṇini |
gṛhāṇa ca waraṃ mattastatkṛte yadabhīpsitam ||32||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato dharmiṣṭhatāṃ wawre rājyāccāskhalanaṃ tathā |
śakuntalā paurawāṇāṃ duḥṣantahitakāmyayā ||33||






                  68


waiśampāyana uwāca||

pratijñāya tu duḥṣante pratiyāte śakuntalā |
garbhaṃ suṣāwa wāmoruḥ kumāramamitaujasam ||1||

triṣu warṣeṣu pūrṇeṣu diptānalasamadyutim |
rūpaudāryaguṇopetaṃ dauḥṣantiṃ janamejaya ||2||

jātakarmādisaṃskāraṃ kaṇwaḥ puṇyakṛtāṃ waraḥ |
tasyātha kārayāmāsa wardhamānasya dhīmataḥ ||3||

dantaiḥ śuklaiḥ śikharibhiḥ siṃhasaṃhanano yuwā |
cakrāṅkitakaraḥ śrīmānmahāmūrdhā mahābalaḥ ||4||

kumāro dewagarbhābhaḥ sa tatrāśu wyawardhata ||4||

ṣaḍwarṣa ewa bālaḥ sa kaṇwāśramapadaṃ prati |
wyāghrānsiṃhānwarāhāṃśca gajāṃśca mahiṣāṃstathā ||5||

baddhwā wṛkṣeṣu balawānāśramasya samantataḥ |
ārohandamayaṃścaiwa krīḍaṃśca paridhāwati ||6||

tato'sya nāma cakruste kaṇwāśramaniwāsinaḥ |
astwayaṃ sarwadamanaḥ sarwaṃ hi damayatyayam ||7||

sa sarwadamano nāma kumāraḥ samapadyata |
wikrameṇaujasā caiwa balena ca samanwitaḥ ||8||

taṃ kumāramṛṣirdṛṣṭwā karma cāsyātimānuṣam |
samayo yauwarājyāyetyabrawīcca śakuntalām ||9||

tasya tadbalamājñāya kaṇwaḥ śiṣyānuwāca ha |
śakuntalāmimāṃ śīghraṃ sahaputrāmito''śramāt ||10||

bhartre prāpayatādyaiwa sarwalakṣaṇapūjitām ||10||

nārīṇāṃ cirawāso hi bāndhaweṣu na rocate |
kīrticāritradharmaghnastasmānnayata māciram ||11||

tathetyuktwā tu te sarwe prātiṣṭhantāmitaujasaḥ |
śakuntalāṃ puraskṛtya saputrāṃ gajasāhwayam ||12||

gṛhītwāmaragarbhābhaṃ putraṃ kamalalocanam |
ājagāma tataḥ śubhrā duḥṣantawiditādwanāt ||13||

abhisṛtya ca rājānaṃ widitā sā praweśitā |
saha tenaiwa putreṇa taruṇādityawarcasā ||14||

pūjayitwā yathānyāyamabrawīttaṃ śakuntalā |
ayaṃ putrastwayā rājanyauwarājye'bhiṣicyatām ||15||

twayā hyayaṃ suto rājanmayyutpannaḥ suropamaḥ |
yathāsamayametasminwartaswa puruṣottama ||16||

yathā samāgame pūrwaṃ kṛtaḥ sa samayastwayā |
taṃ smaraswa mahābhāga kaṇwāśramapadaṃ prati ||17||

so'tha śrutwaiwa tadwākyaṃ tasyā rājā smarannapi |
abrawīnna smarāmīti kasya twaṃ duṣṭatāpasi ||18||

dharmakāmārthasambandhaṃ na smarāmi twayā saha |
gaccha wā tiṣṭha wā kāmaṃ yadwāpīcchasi tatkuru ||19||

saiwamuktā warārohā wrīḍitewa manaswinī |
wisañjñewa ca duḥkhena tasthau sthāṇuriwācalā ||20||

saṃrambhāmarṣatāmrākṣī sphuramāṇoṣṭhasampuṭā |
kaṭākṣairnirdahantīwa tiryagrājānamaikṣata ||21||

ākāraṃ gūhamānā ca manyunābhisamīritā |
tapasā sambhṛtaṃ tejo dhārayāmāsa wai tadā ||22||

sā muhūrtamiwa dhyātwā duḥkhāmarṣasamanwitā |
bhartāramabhisamprekṣya kruddhā wacanamabrawīt ||23||

jānannapi mahārāja kasmādewaṃ prabhāṣase |
na jānāmīti niḥsaṅgaṃ yathānyaḥ prākṛtastathā ||24||

atra te hṛdayaṃ weda satyasyaiwānṛtasya ca |
kalyāṇa bata sākṣī twaṃ mātmānamawamanyathāḥ ||25||

yo'nyathā santamātmānamanyathā pratipadyate |
kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇātmāpahāriṇā ||26||

eko'hamasmīti ca manyase twaṃ; na hṛcchayaṃ wetsi muniṃ purāṇam |
yo weditā karmaṇaḥ pāpakasya; tasyāntike twaṃ wṛjinaṃ karoṣi ||27||

manyate pāpakaṃ kṛtwā na kaścidwetti māmiti |
widanti cainaṃ dewāśca swaścaiwāntarapūruṣaḥ ||28||

ādityacandrāwanilānalau ca; dyaurbhūmirāpo hṛdayaṃ yamaśca |
ahaśca rātriśca ubhe ca sandhye; dharmaśca jānāti narasya wṛttam ||29||

yamo waiwaswatastasya niryātayati duṣkṛtam |
hṛdi sthitaḥ karmasākṣī kṣetrajño yasya tuṣyati ||30||

na tu tuṣyati yasyaiṣa puruṣasya durātmanaḥ |
taṃ yamaḥ pāpakarmāṇaṃ niryātayati duṣkṛtam ||31||

awamanyātmanātmānamanyathā pratipadyate |
dewā na tasya śreyāṃso yasyātmāpi na kāraṇam ||32||

swayaṃ prāpteti māmewaṃ māwamaṃsthāḥ patiwratām |
arghyārhāṃ nārcayasi māṃ swayaṃ bhāryāmupasthitām ||33||

kimarthaṃ māṃ prākṛtawadupaprekṣasi saṃsadi |
na khalwahamidaṃ śūnye raumi kiṃ na śṛṇoṣi me ||34||

yadi me yācamānāyā wacanaṃ na kariṣyasi |
duḥṣanta śatadhā mūrdhā tataste'dya phaliṣyati ||35||

bhāryāṃ patiḥ samprawiśya sa yasmājjāyate punaḥ |
jāyāyā iti jāyātwaṃ purāṇāḥ kawayo widuḥ ||36||

yadāgamawataḥ puṃsastadapatyaṃ prajāyate |
tattārayati santatyā pūrwapretānpitāmahān ||37||

punnāmno narakādyasmātpitaraṃ trāyate sutaḥ |
tasmātputra iti proktaḥ swayamewa swayambhuwā ||38||

sā bhāryā yā gṛhe dakṣā sā bhāryā yā prajāwatī |
sā bhāryā yā patiprāṇā sā bhāryā yā patiwratā ||39||

ardhaṃ bhāryā manuṣyasya bhāryā śreṣṭhatamaḥ sakhā |
bhāryā mūlaṃ triwargasya bhāryā mitraṃ mariṣyataḥ ||40||

bhāryāwantaḥ kriyāwantaḥ sabhāryā gṛhamedhinaḥ |
bhāryāwantaḥ pramodante bhāryāwantaḥ śriyānwitāḥ ||41||

sakhāyaḥ prawiwikteṣu bhawantyetāḥ priyaṃwadāḥ |
pitaro dharmakāryeṣu bhawantyārtasya mātaraḥ ||42||

kāntāreṣwapi wiśrāmo narasyādhwanikasya wai |
yaḥ sadāraḥ sa wiśwāsyastasmāddārāḥ parā gatiḥ ||43||

saṃsarantamapi pretaṃ wiṣameṣwekapātinam |
bhāryaiwānweti bhartāraṃ satataṃ yā patiwratā ||44||

prathamaṃ saṃsthitā bhāryā patiṃ pretya pratīkṣate |
pūrwaṃ mṛtaṃ ca bhartāraṃ paścātsādhwyanugacchati ||45||

etasmātkāraṇādrājanpāṇigrahaṇamiṣyate |
yadāpnoti patirbhāryāmiha loke paratra ca ||46||

ātmātmanaiwa janitaḥ putra ityucyate budhaiḥ |
tasmādbhāryāṃ naraḥ paśyenmātṛwatputramātaram ||47||

bhāryāyāṃ janitaṃ putramādarśe swamiwānanam |
hlādate janitā preṣkya swargaṃ prāpyewa puṇyakṛt ||48||

dahyamānā manoduḥkhairwyādhibhiścāturā narāḥ |
hlādante sweṣu dāreṣu gharmārtāḥ salileṣwiwa ||49||

susaṃrabdho'pi rāmāṇāṃ na brūyādapriyaṃ budhaḥ |
ratiṃ prītiṃ ca dharmaṃ ca tāswāyattamawekṣya ca ||50||

ātmano janmanaḥ kṣetraṃ puṇyaṃ rāmāḥ sanātanam |
ṛṣīṇāmapi kā śaktiḥ sraṣṭuṃ rāmāmṛte prajāḥ ||51||

paripatya yadā sūnurdharaṇīreṇuguṇṭhitaḥ |
piturāśliṣyate'ṅgāni kimiwāstyadhikaṃ tataḥ ||52||

sa twaṃ swayamanuprāptaṃ sābhilāṣamimaṃ sutam |
prekṣamāṇaṃ ca kākṣeṇa kimarthamawamanyase ||53||

aṇḍāni bibhrati swāni na bhindanti pipīlikāḥ |
na bharethāḥ kathaṃ nu twaṃ dharmajñaḥ sanswamātmajam ||54||

na wāsasāṃ na rāmāṇāṃ nāpāṃ sparśastathā sukhaḥ |
śiśorāliṅgyamānasya sparśaḥ sūnoryathā sukhaḥ ||55||

brāhmaṇo dwipadāṃ śreṣṭho gaurwariṣṭhā catuṣpadām |
gururgarīyasāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ putraḥ sparśawatāṃ waraḥ ||56||

spṛśatu twāṃ samāśliṣya putro'yaṃ priyadarśanaḥ |
putrasparśātsukhataraḥ sparśo loke na widyate ||57||

triṣu warṣeṣu pūrṇeṣu prajātāhamariṃdama |
imaṃ kumāraṃ rājendra tawa śokapraṇāśanam ||58||

āhartā wājimedhasya śatasaṅkhyasya paurawa |
iti wāgantarikṣe māṃ sūtake'bhyawadatpurā ||59||

nanu nāmāṅkamāropya snehādgrāmāntaraṃ gatāḥ |
mūrdhni putrānupāghrāya pratinandanti mānawāḥ ||60||

wedeṣwapi wadantīmaṃ mantrawādaṃ dwijātayaḥ |
jātakarmaṇi putrāṇāṃ tawāpi widitaṃ tathā ||61||

aṅgādaṅgātsambhawasi hṛdayādabhijāyase |
ātmā wai putranāmāsi sa jīwa śaradaḥ śatam ||62||

poṣo hi twadadhīno me santānamapi cākṣayam |
tasmāttwaṃ jīwa me watsa susukhī śaradāṃ śatam ||63||

twadaṅgebhyaḥ prasūto'yaṃ puruṣātpuruṣo'paraḥ |
sarasīwāmale''tmānaṃ dwitīyaṃ paśya me sutam ||64||

yathā hyāhawanīyo'gnirgārhapatyātpraṇīyate |
tathā twattaḥ prasūto'yaṃ twamekaḥ sandwidhā kṛtaḥ ||65||

mṛgāpakṛṣṭena hi te mṛgayāṃ paridhāwatā |
ahamāsāditā rājankumārī piturāśrame ||66||

urwaśī pūrwacittiśca sahajanyā ca menakā |
wiśwācī ca ghṛtācī ca ṣaḍewāpsarasāṃ warāḥ ||67||

tāsāṃ māṃ menakā nāma brahmayonirwarāpsarāḥ |
diwaḥ samprāpya jagatīṃ wiśwāmitrādajījanat ||68||

sā māṃ himawataḥ pṛṣṭhe suṣuwe menakāpsarāḥ |
awakīrya ca māṃ yātā parātmajamiwāsatī ||69||

kiṃ nu karmāśubhaṃ pūrwaṃ kṛtawatyasmi janmani |
yadahaṃ bāndhawaistyaktā bālye samprati ca twayā ||70||

kāmaṃ twayā parityaktā gamiṣyāmyahamāśramam |
imaṃ tu bālaṃ santyaktuṃ nārhasyātmajamātmanā ||71||

duḥṣanta uwāca||

na putramabhijānāmi twayi jātaṃ śakuntale |
asatyawacanā nāryaḥ kaste śraddhāsyate wacaḥ ||72||

menakā niranukrośā bandhakī jananī tawa |
yayā himawataḥ pṛṣṭhe nirmālyewa praweritā ||73||

sa cāpi niranukrośaḥ kṣatrayoniḥ pitā tawa |
wiśwāmitro brāhmaṇatwe lubdhaḥ kāmaparāyaṇaḥ ||74||

menakāpsarasāṃ śreṣṭhā maharṣīṇāṃ ca te pitā |
tayorapatyaṃ kasmāttwaṃ puṃścalīwābhidhāsyasi ||75||

aśraddheyamidaṃ wākyaṃ kathayantī na lajjase |
wiśeṣato matsakāśe duṣṭatāpasi gamyatām ||76||

kwa maharṣiḥ sadaiwograḥ sāpsarā kwa ca menakā |
kwa ca twamewaṃ kṛpaṇā tāpasīweṣadhāriṇī ||77||

atikāyaśca putraste bālo'pi balawānayam |
kathamalpena kālena śālaskandha iwodgataḥ ||78||

sunikṛṣṭā ca yoniste puṃścalī pratibhāsi me |
yadṛcchayā kāmarāgājjātā menakayā hyasi ||79||

sarwametatparokṣaṃ me yattwaṃ wadasi tāpasi |
nāhaṃ twāmabhijānāmi yatheṣṭaṃ gamyatāṃ twayā ||80||






                  69


śakuntalowāca||

rājansarṣapamātrāṇi paracchidrāṇi paśyasi |
ātmano bilwamātrāṇi paśyannapi na paśyasi ||1||

menakā tridaśeṣwewa tridaśāścānu menakām |
mamaiwodricyate janma duḥṣanta tawa janmataḥ ||2||

kṣitāwaṭasi rājaṃstwamantarikṣe carāmyaham |
āwayorantaraṃ paśya merusarṣapayoriwa ||3||

mahendrasya kuberasya yamasya waruṇasya ca |
bhawanānyanusaṃyāmi prabhāwaṃ paśya me nṛpa ||4||

satyaścāpi prawādo'yaṃ yaṃ prawakṣyāmi te'nagha |
nidarśanārthaṃ na dweṣāttacchrutwā kṣantumarhasi ||5||

wirūpo yāwadādarśe nātmanaḥ paśyate mukham |
manyate tāwadātmānamanyebhyo rūpawattaram ||6||

yadā tu mukhamādarśe wikṛtaṃ so'bhiwīkṣate |
tadetaraṃ wijānāti ātmānaṃ netaraṃ janam ||7||

atīwa rūpasampanno na kiñcidawamanyate |
atīwa jalpandurwāco bhawatīha wiheṭhakaḥ ||8||

mūrkho hi jalpatāṃ puṃsāṃ śrutwā wācaḥ śubhāśubhāḥ |
aśubhaṃ wākyamādatte purīṣamiwa sūkaraḥ ||9||

prājñastu jalpatāṃ puṃsāṃ śrutwā wācaḥ śubhāśubhāḥ |
guṇawadwākyamādatte haṃsaḥ kṣīramiwāmbhasaḥ ||10||

anyānpariwadansādhuryathā hi paritapyate |
tathā pariwadannanyāṃstuṣṭo bhawati durjanaḥ ||11||

abhiwādya yathā wṛddhānsanto gacchanti nirwṛtim |
ewaṃ sajjanamākruśya mūrkho bhawati nirwṛtaḥ ||12||

sukhaṃ jīwantyadoṣajñā mūrkhā doṣānudarśinaḥ |
yatra wācyāḥ paraiḥ santaḥ parānāhustathāwidhān ||13||

ato hāsyataraṃ loke kiñcidanyanna widyate |
yatra durjana ityāha durjanaḥ sajjanaṃ swayam ||14||

satyadharmacyutātpuṃsaḥ kruddhādāśīwiṣādiwa |
anāstiko'pyudwijate janaḥ kiṃ punarāstikaḥ ||15||

swayamutpādya wai putraṃ sadṛśaṃ yo'wamanyate |
tasya dewāḥ śriyaṃ ghnanti na ca lokānupāśnute ||16||

kulawaṃśapratiṣṭhāṃ hi pitaraḥ putramabruwan |
uttamaṃ sarwadharmāṇāṃ tasmātputraṃ na santyajet ||17||

swapatnīprabhawānpañca labdhānkrītānwiwardhitān |
kṛtānanyāsu cotpannānputrānwai manurabrawīt ||18||

dharmakīrtyāwahā nṛṇāṃ manasaḥ prītiwardhanāḥ |
trāyante narakājjātāḥ putrā dharmaplawāḥ pitṛn ||19||

sa twaṃ nṛpatiśārdūla na putraṃ tyaktumarhasi |
ātmānaṃ satyadharmau ca pālayāno mahīpate ||20||

narendrasiṃha kapaṭaṃ na woḍhuṃ twamihārhasi ||20||

waraṃ kūpaśatādwāpī waraṃ wāpīśatātkratuḥ |
waraṃ kratuśatātputraḥ satyaṃ putraśatādwaram ||21||

aśwamedhasahasraṃ ca satyaṃ ca tulayā dhṛtam |
aśwamedhasahasrāddhi satyamewa wiśiṣyate ||22||

sarwawedādhigamanaṃ sarwatīrthāwagāhanam |
satyaṃ ca wadato rājansamaṃ wā syānna wā samam ||23||

nāsti satyātparo dharmo na satyādwidyate param |
na hi tīwrataraṃ kiñcidanṛtādiha widyate ||24||

rājansatyaṃ paraṃ brahma satyaṃ ca samayaḥ paraḥ |
mā tyākṣīḥ samayaṃ rājansatyaṃ saṅgatamastu te ||25||

anṛte cetprasaṅgaste śraddadhāsi na cetswayam |
ātmano hanta gacchāmi twādṛśe nāsti saṅgatam ||26||

ṛte'pi twayi duḥṣanta śailarājāwataṃsakām |
caturantāmimāmurwīṃ putro me pālayiṣyati ||27||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

etāwaduktwā wacanaṃ prātiṣṭhata śakuntalā |
athāntarikṣe duḥṣantaṃ wāguwācāśarīriṇī ||28||

ṛtwikpurohitācāryairmantribhiścāwṛtaṃ tadā ||28||

bhastrā mātā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa ewa saḥ |
bharaswa putraṃ duḥṣanta māwamaṃsthāḥ śakuntalām ||29||

retodhāḥ putra unnayati naradewa yamakṣayāt |
twaṃ cāsya dhātā garbhasya satyamāha śakuntalā ||30||

jāyā janayate putramātmano'ṅgaṃ dwidhā kṛtam |
tasmādbharaswa duḥṣanta putraṃ śākuntalaṃ nṛpa ||31||

abhūtireṣā kastyajyājjīwañjīwantamātmajam |
śākuntalaṃ mahātmānaṃ dauḥṣantiṃ bhara paurawa ||32||

bhartawyo'yaṃ twayā yasmādasmākaṃ wacanādapi |
tasmādbhawatwayaṃ nāmnā bharato nāma te sutaḥ ||33||

tacchrutwā paurawo rājā wyāhṛtaṃ wai diwaukasām |
purohitamamātyāṃśca samprahṛṣṭo'brawīdidam ||34||

śṛṇwantwetadbhawanto'sya dewadūtasya bhāṣitam |
ahamapyewamewainaṃ jānāmi swayamātmajam ||35||

yadyahaṃ wacanādewa gṛhṇīyāmimamātmajam |
bhaweddhi śaṅkā lokasya naiwaṃ śuddho bhawedayam ||36||

taṃ wiśodhya tadā rājā dewadūtena bhārata |
hṛṣṭaḥ pramuditaścāpi pratijagrāha taṃ sutam ||37||

mūrdhni cainamupāghrāya sasnehaṃ pariṣaswaje |
sabhājyamāno wipraiśca stūyamānaśca bandibhiḥ ||38||

sa mudaṃ paramāṃ lebhe putrasaṃsparśajāṃ nṛpaḥ ||38||

tāṃ caiwa bhāryāṃ dharmajñaḥ pūjayāmāsa dharmataḥ |
abrawīccaiwa tāṃ rājā sāntwapūrwamidaṃ wacaḥ ||39||

kṛto lokaparokṣo'yaṃ sambandho wai twayā saha |
tasmādetanmayā dewi twacchuddhyarthaṃ wicāritam ||40||

manyate caiwa lokaste strībhāwānmayi saṅgatam |
putraścāyaṃ wṛto rājye mayā tasmādwicāritam ||41||

yacca kopitayātyarthaṃ twayokto'smyapriyaṃ priye |
praṇayinyā wiśālākṣi tatkṣāntaṃ te mayā śubhe ||42||

tāmewamuktwā rājarṣirduḥṣanto mahiṣīṃ priyām |
wāsobhirannapānaiśca pūjayāmāsa bhārata ||43||

duḥṣantaśca tato rājā putraṃ śākuntalaṃ tadā |
bharataṃ nāmataḥ kṛtwā yauwarājye'bhyaṣecayat ||44||

tasya tatprathitaṃ cakraṃ prāwartata mahātmanaḥ |
bhāswaraṃ diwyamajitaṃ lokasaṃnādanaṃ mahat ||45||

sa wijitya mahīpālāṃścakāra waśawartinaḥ |
cacāra ca satāṃ dharmaṃ prāpa cānuttamaṃ yaśaḥ ||46||

sa rājā cakrawartyāsītsārwabhaumaḥ pratāpawān |
īje ca bahubhiryajñairyathā śakro marutpatiḥ ||47||

yājayāmāsa taṃ kaṇwo dakṣawadbhūridakṣiṇam |
śrīmāngowitataṃ nāma wājimedhamawāpa saḥ ||48||

yasminsahasraṃ padmānāṃ kaṇwāya bharato dadau ||48||

bharatādbhāratī kīrtiryenedaṃ bhārataṃ kulam |
apare ye ca pūrwe ca bhāratā iti wiśrutāḥ ||49||

bharatasyānwawāye hi dewakalpā mahaujasaḥ |
babhūwurbrahmakalpāśca bahawo rājasattamāḥ ||50||

yeṣāmaparimeyāni nāmadheyāni sarwaśaḥ |
teṣāṃ tu te yathāmukhyaṃ kīrtayiṣyāmi bhārata ||51||

mahābhāgāndewakalpānsatyārjawaparāyaṇān ||51||






              yayātyupākhyānam
                  70


waiśampāyana uwāca||

prajāpatestu dakṣasya manorwaiwaswatasya ca |
bharatasya kuroḥ pūrorajamīḍhasya cānwaye ||1||

yādawānāmimaṃ waṃśaṃ paurawāṇāṃ ca sarwaśaḥ |
tathaiwa bhāratānāṃ ca puṇyaṃ swastyayanaṃ mahat ||2||

dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ kīrtayiṣyāmi te'nagha ||2||

tejobhiruditāḥ sarwe maharṣisamatejasaḥ |
daśa pracetasaḥ putrāḥ santaḥ pūrwajanāḥ smṛtāḥ ||3||

meghajenāgninā ye te pūrwaṃ dagdhā mahaujasaḥ ||3||

tebhyaḥ prācetaso jajñe dakṣo dakṣādimāḥ prajāḥ |
sambhūtāḥ puruṣawyāghra sa hi lokapitāmahaḥ ||4||

wīriṇyā saha saṅgamya dakṣaḥ prācetaso muniḥ |
ātmatulyānajanayatsahasraṃ saṃśitawratān ||5||

sahasrasaṅkhyānsamitānsutāndakṣasya nāradaḥ |
mokṣamadhyāpayāmāsa sāṅkhyajñānamanuttamam ||6||

tataḥ pañcāśataṃ kanyāḥ putrikā abhisaṃdadhe |
prajāpatiḥ prajā dakṣaḥ sisṛkṣurjanamejaya ||7||

dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa |
kālasya nayane yuktāḥ saptawiṃśatimindawe ||8||

trayodaśānāṃ patnīnāṃ yā tu dākṣāyaṇī warā |
mārīcaḥ kaśyapastasyāmādityānsamajījanat ||9||

indrādīnwīryasampannānwiwaswantamathāpi ca ||9||

wiwaswataḥ suto jajñe yamo waiwaswataḥ prabhuḥ |
mārtaṇḍaśca yamasyāpi putro rājannajāyata ||10||

mārtaṇḍasya manurdhīmānajāyata sutaḥ prabhuḥ |
manorwaṃśo mānawānāṃ tato'yaṃ prathito'bhawat ||11||

brahmakṣatrādayastasmānmanorjātāstu mānawāḥ ||11||

tatrābhawattadā rājanbrahma kṣatreṇa saṅgatam |
brāhmaṇā mānawāsteṣāṃ sāṅgaṃ wedamadīdharan ||12||

wenaṃ dhṛṣṇuṃ nariṣyantaṃ nābhāgekṣwākumewa ca |
karūṣamatha śaryātiṃ tathaiwātrāṣṭamīmilām ||13||

pṛṣadhranawamānāhuḥ kṣatradharmaparāyaṇān |
nābhāgāriṣṭadaśamānmanoḥ putrānmahābalān ||14||

pañcāśataṃ manoḥ putrāstathaiwānye'bhawankṣitau |
anyonyabhedātte sarwe wineśuriti naḥ śrutam ||15||

purūrawāstato widwānilāyāṃ samapadyata |
sā wai tasyābhawanmātā pitā ceti hi naḥ śrutam ||16||

trayodaśa samudrasya dwīpānaśnanpurūrawāḥ |
amānuṣairwṛtaḥ sattwairmānuṣaḥ sanmahāyaśāḥ ||17||

wipraiḥ sa wigrahaṃ cakre wīryonmattaḥ purūrawāḥ |
jahāra ca sa wiprāṇāṃ ratnānyutkrośatāmapi ||18||

sanatkumārastaṃ rājanbrahmalokādupetya ha |
anudarśayāṃ tataścakre pratyagṛhṇānna cāpyasau ||19||

tato maharṣibhiḥ kruddhaiḥ śaptaḥ sadyo wyanaśyata |
lobhānwito madabalānnaṣṭasañjño narādhipaḥ ||20||

sa hi gandharwalokastha urwaśyā sahito wirāṭ |
ānināya kriyārthe'gnīnyathāwadwihitāṃstridhā ||21||

ṣaṭputrā jajñire'thailādāyurdhīmānamāwasuḥ |
dṛḍhāyuśca wanāyuśca śrutāyuścorwaśīsutāḥ ||22||

nahuṣaṃ wṛddhaśarmāṇaṃ rajiṃ rambhamanenasam |
swarbhānawīsutānetānāyoḥ putrānpracakṣate ||23||

āyuṣo nahuṣaḥ putro dhīmānsatyaparākramaḥ |
rājyaṃ śaśāsa sumahaddharmeṇa pṛthiwīpatiḥ ||24||

pitṛndewānṛṣīnwiprāngandharworagarākṣasān |
nahuṣaḥ pālayāmāsa brahmakṣatramatho wiśaḥ ||25||

sa hatwā dasyusaṅghātānṛṣīnkaramadāpayat |
paśuwaccaiwa tānpṛṣṭhe wāhayāmāsa wīryawān ||26||

kārayāmāsa cendratwamabhibhūya diwaukasaḥ |
tejasā tapasā caiwa wikrameṇaujasā tathā ||27||

yatiṃ yayātiṃ saṃyātimāyātiṃ pāñcamuddhawam |
nahuṣo janayāmāsa ṣaṭputrānpriyawāsasi ||28||

yayātirnāhuṣaḥ samrāḍāsītsatyaparākramaḥ |
sa pālayāmāsa mahīmīje ca wiwidhaiḥ sawaiḥ ||29||

atiśaktyā pitṛnarcandewāṃśca prayataḥ sadā |
anwagṛhṇātprajāḥ sarwā yayātiraparājitaḥ ||30||

tasya putrā maheṣwāsāḥ sarwaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥ |
dewayānyāṃ mahārāja śarmiṣṭhāyāṃ ca jajñire ||31||

dewayānyāmajāyetāṃ yadusturwasurewa ca |
druhyuścānuśca pūruśca śarmiṣṭhāyāṃ prajajñire ||32||

sa śāśwatīḥ samā rājanprajā dharmeṇa pālayan |
jarāmārchanmahāghorāṃ nāhuṣo rūpanāśinīm ||33||

jarābhibhūtaḥ putrānsa rājā wacanamabrawīt |
yaduṃ pūruṃ turwasuṃ ca druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca bhārata ||34||

yauwanena carankāmānyuwā yuwatibhiḥ saha |
wihartumahamicchāmi sāhyaṃ kuruta putrakāḥ ||35||

taṃ putro dewayāneyaḥ pūrwajo yadurabrawīt |
kiṃ kāryaṃ bhawataḥ kāryamasmābhiryauwanena ca ||36||

yayātirabrawīttaṃ wai jarā me pratigṛhyatām |
yauwanena twadīyena careyaṃ wiṣayānaham ||37||

yajato dīrghasatrairme śāpāccośanaso muneḥ |
kāmārthaḥ parihīṇo me tapye'haṃ tena putrakāḥ ||38||

māmakena śarīreṇa rājyamekaḥ praśāstu waḥ |
ahaṃ tanwābhinawayā yuwā kāmānawāpnuyām ||39||

na te tasya pratyagṛhṇanyaduprabhṛtayo jarām |
tamabrawīttataḥ pūruḥ kanīyānsatyawikramaḥ ||40||

rājaṃścarābhinawayā tanwā yauwanagocaraḥ |
ahaṃ jarāṃ samāsthāya rājye sthāsyāmi te''jñayā ||41||

ewamuktaḥ sa rājarṣistapowīryasamāśrayāt |
sañcārayāmāsa jarāṃ tadā putre mahātmani ||42||

pauraweṇātha wayasā rājā yauwanamāsthitaḥ |
yāyātenāpi wayasā rājyaṃ pūrurakārayat ||43||

tato warṣasahasrānte yayātiraparājitaḥ |
atṛpta ewa kāmānāṃ pūruṃ putramuwāca ha ||44||

twayā dāyādawānasmi twaṃ me waṃśakaraḥ sutaḥ |
paurawo waṃśa iti te khyātiṃ loke gamiṣyati ||45||

tataḥ sa nṛpaśārdūlaḥ pūruṃ rājye'bhiṣicya ca |
kālena mahatā paścātkāladharmamupeyiwān ||46||






                  71


janamejaya uwāca||

yayātiḥ pūrwako'smākaṃ daśamo yaḥ prajāpateḥ |
kathaṃ sa śukratanayāṃ lebhe paramadurlabhām ||1||

etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ wistareṇa dwijottama |
ānupūrwyā ca me śaṃsa pūrorwaṃśakarānpṛthak ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

yayātirāsīdrājarṣirdewarājasamadyutiḥ |
taṃ śukrawṛṣaparwāṇau wawrāte wai yathā purā ||3||

tatte'haṃ samprawakṣyāmi pṛcchato janamejaya |
dewayānyāśca saṃyogaṃ yayāternāhuṣasya ca ||4||

surāṇāmasurāṇāṃ ca samajāyata wai mithaḥ |
aiśwaryaṃ prati saṅgharṣastrailokye sacarācare ||5||

jigīṣayā tato dewā wawrire''ṅgirasaṃ munim |
paurohityena yājyārthe kāwyaṃ tūśanasaṃ pare ||6||

brāhmaṇau tāwubhau nityamanyonyaspardhinau bhṛśam ||6||

tatra dewā nijaghnuryāndānawānyudhi saṅgatān |
tānpunarjīwayāmāsa kāwyo widyābalāśrayāt ||7||

tataste punarutthāya yodhayāṃ cakrire surān ||7||

asurāstu nijaghnuryānsurānsamaramūrdhani |
na tānsañjīwayāmāsa bṛhaspatirudāradhīḥ ||8||

na hi weda sa tāṃ widyāṃ yāṃ kāwyo weda wīryawān |
sañjīwanīṃ tato dewā wiṣādamagamanparam ||9||

te tu dewā bhayodwignāḥ kāwyāduśanasastadā |
ūcuḥ kacamupāgamya jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ bṛhaspateḥ ||10||

bhajamānānbhajaswāsmānkuru naḥ sāhyamuttamam |
yāsau widyā niwasati brāhmaṇe'mitatejasi ||11||

śukre tāmāhara kṣipraṃ bhāgabhāṅno bhawiṣyasi ||11||

wṛṣaparwasamīpe sa śakyo draṣṭuṃ twayā dwijaḥ |
rakṣate dānawāṃstatra na sa rakṣatyadānawān ||12||

tamārādhayituṃ śakto bhawānpūrwawayāḥ kawim |
dewayānīṃ ca dayitāṃ sutāṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ ||13||

twamārādhayituṃ śakto nānyaḥ kaścana widyate |
śīladākṣiṇyamādhuryairācāreṇa damena ca ||14||

dewayānyāṃ hi tuṣṭāyāṃ widyāṃ tāṃ prāpsyasi dhruwam ||14||

tathetyuktwā tataḥ prāyādbṛhaspatisutaḥ kacaḥ |
tadābhipūjito dewaiḥ samīpaṃ wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ ||15||

sa gatwā twarito rājandewaiḥ sampreṣitaḥ kacaḥ |
asurendrapure śukraṃ dṛṣṭwā wākyamuwāca ha ||16||

ṛṣeraṅgirasaḥ pautraṃ putraṃ sākṣādbṛhaspateḥ |
nāmnā kaca iti khyātaṃ śiṣyaṃ gṛhṇātu māṃ bhawān ||17||

brahmacaryaṃ cariṣyāmi twayyahaṃ paramaṃ gurau |
anumanyaswa māṃ brahmansahasraṃ pariwatsarān ||18||

śukra uwāca||

kaca suswāgataṃ te'stu pratigṛhṇāmi te wacaḥ |
arcayiṣye'hamarcyaṃ twāmarcito'stu bṛhaspatiḥ ||19||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

kacastu taṃ tathetyuktwā pratijagrāha tadwratam |
ādiṣṭaṃ kawiputreṇa śukreṇośanasā swayam ||20||

wratasya wratakālaṃ sa yathoktaṃ pratyagṛhṇata |
ārādhayannupādhyāyaṃ dewayānīṃ ca bhārata ||21||

nityamārādhayiṣyaṃstāṃ yuwā yauwanago''mukhe |
gāyannṛtyanwādayaṃśca dewayānīmatoṣayat ||22||

saṃśīlayandewayānīṃ kanyāṃ samprāptayauwanām |
puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ preṣaṇaiśca toṣayāmāsa bhārata ||23||

dewayānyapi taṃ wipraṃ niyamawratacāriṇam |
anugāyamānā lalanā rahaḥ paryacarattadā ||24||

pañca warṣaśatānyewaṃ kacasya carato wratam |
tatrātīyuratho buddhwā dānawāstaṃ tataḥ kacam ||25||

gā rakṣantaṃ wane dṛṣṭwā rahasyekamamarṣitāḥ |
jaghnurbṛhaspaterdweṣādwidyārakṣārthamewa ca ||26||

hatwā śālāwṛkebhyaśca prāyacchaṃstilaśaḥ kṛtam ||26||

tato gāwo niwṛttāstā agopāḥ swaṃ niweśanam |
tā dṛṣṭwā rahitā gāstu kacenābhyāgatā wanāt ||27||

uwāca wacanaṃ kāle dewayānyatha bhārata ||27||

ahutaṃ cāgnihotraṃ te sūryaścāstaṃ gataḥ prabho |
agopāścāgatā gāwaḥ kacastāta na dṛśyate ||28||

wyaktaṃ hato mṛto wāpi kacastāta bhawiṣyati |
taṃ winā na ca jīweyaṃ kacaṃ satyaṃ brawīmi te ||29||

śukra uwāca||

ayamehīti śabdena mṛtaṃ sañjīwayāmyaham |
waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ sañjīwanīṃ widyāṃ prayujya kacamāhwayat |
āhūtaḥ prādurabhawatkaco'riṣṭo'tha widyayā ||31||

hato'hamiti cācakhyau pṛṣṭo brāhmaṇakanyayā ||31||

sa punardewayānyoktaḥ puṣpāhāro yadṛcchayā |
wanaṃ yayau tato wipro dadṛśurdānawāśca tam ||32||

tato dwitīyaṃ hatwā taṃ dagdhwā kṛtwā ca cūrṇaśaḥ |
prāyacchanbrāhmaṇāyaiwa surāyāmasurāstadā ||33||

dewayānyatha bhūyo'pi wākyaṃ pitaramabrawīt |
puṣpāhāraḥ preṣaṇakṛtkacastāta na dṛśyate ||34||

śukra uwāca||

bṛhaspateḥ sutaḥ putri kacaḥ pretagatiṃ gataḥ |
widyayā jīwito'pyewaṃ hanyate karawāṇi kim ||35||

maiwaṃ śuco mā ruda dewayāni; na twādṛśī martyamanupraśocet |
surāśca wiśwe ca jagacca sarwa; mupasthitāṃ waikṛtimānamanti ||36||

dewayānyuwāca||

yasyāṅgirā wṛddhatamaḥ pitāmaho; bṛhaspatiścāpi pitā tapodhanaḥ |
ṛṣeḥ putraṃ tamatho wāpi pautraṃ; kathaṃ na śoceyamahaṃ na rudyām ||37||

sa brahmacārī ca tapodhanaśca; sadotthitaḥ karmasu caiwa dakṣaḥ |
kacasya mārgaṃ pratipatsye na bhokṣye; priyo hi me tāta kaco'bhirūpaḥ ||38||

śukra uwāca||

asaṃśayaṃ māmasurā dwiṣanti; ye me śiṣyaṃ nāgasaṃ sūdayanti |
abrāhmaṇaṃ kartumicchanti raudrā; ste māṃ yathā prastutaṃ dānawairhi ||39||

apyasya pāpasya bhawedihāntaḥ; kaṃ brahmahatyā na dahedapīndram ||39||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

sañcodito dewayānyā maharṣiḥ punarāhwayat |
saṃrambheṇaiwa kāwyo hi bṛhaspatisutaṃ kacam ||40||

gurorbhīto widyayā copahūtaḥ; śanairwācaṃ jaṭhare wyājahāra |
tamabrawītkena pathopanīto; mamodare tiṣṭhasi brūhi wipra ||41||

kaca uwāca||

bhawatprasādānna jahāti māṃ smṛtiḥ; smare ca sarwaṃ yacca yathā ca wṛttam |
na twewaṃ syāttapaso wyayo me; tataḥ kleśaṃ ghoramimaṃ sahāmi ||42||

asuraiḥ surāyāṃ bhawato'smi datto; hatwā dagdhwā cūrṇayitwā ca kāwya |
brāhmīṃ māyāmāsurī caiwa māyā; twayi sthite kathamewātiwartet ||43||

śukra uwāca||

kiṃ te priyaṃ karawāṇyadya watse; wadhena me jīwitaṃ syātkacasya |
nānyatra kukṣermama bhedanena; dṛśyetkaco madgato dewayāni ||44||

dewayānyuwāca||

dwau māṃ śokāwagnikalpau dahetāṃ; kacasya nāśastawa caiwopaghātaḥ |
kacasya nāśe mama nāsti śarma; tawopaghāte jīwituṃ nāsmi śaktā ||45||

śukra uwāca||

saṃsiddharūpo'si bṛhaspateḥ suta; yattwāṃ bhaktaṃ bhajate dewayānī |
widyāmimāṃ prāpnuhi jīwanīṃ twaṃ; na cedindraḥ kacarūpī twamadya ||46||

na niwartetpunarjīwankaścidanyo mamodarāt |
brāhmaṇaṃ warjayitwaikaṃ tasmādwidyāmawāpnuhi ||47||

putro bhūtwā bhāwaya bhāwito mā; masmāddehādupaniṣkramya tāta |
samīkṣethā dharmawatīmawekṣāṃ; guroḥ sakāśātprāpya widyāṃ sawidyaḥ ||48||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

guroḥ sakāśātsamawāpya widyāṃ; bhittwā kukṣiṃ nirwicakrāma wipraḥ |
kaco'bhirūpo dakṣiṇaṃ brāhmaṇasya; śuklātyaye paurṇamāsyāmiwenduḥ ||49||

dṛṣṭwā ca taṃ patitaṃ brahmarāśi; mutthāpayāmāsa mṛtaṃ kaco'pi |
widyāṃ siddhāṃ tāmawāpyābhiwādya; tataḥ kacastaṃ gurumityuwāca ||50||

ṛtasya dātāramanuttamasya; nidhiṃ nidhīnāṃ caturanwayānām |
ye nādriyante gurumarcanīyaṃ; pāpāṃllokāṃste wrajantyapratiṣṭhān ||51||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

surāpānādwañcanāṃ prāpayitwā; sañjñānāśaṃ caiwa tathātighoram |
dṛṣṭwā kacaṃ cāpi tathābhirūpaṃ; pītaṃ tadā surayā mohitena ||52||

samanyurutthāya mahānubhāwa; stadośanā wiprahitaṃ cikīrṣuḥ |
kāwyaḥ swayaṃ wākyamidaṃ jagāda; surāpānaṃ prati wai jātaśaṅkaḥ ||53||

yo brāhmaṇo'dya prabhṛtīha kaści; nmohātsurāṃ pāsyati mandabuddhiḥ |
apetadharmo brahmahā caiwa sa syā; dasmiṃlloke garhitaḥ syātpare ca ||54||

mayā cemāṃ wipradharmoktisīmāṃ; maryādāṃ wai sthāpitāṃ sarwaloke |
santo wiprāḥ śuśruwāṃso gurūṇāṃ; dewā lokāścopaśṛṇwantu sarwe ||55||

itīdamuktwā sa mahānubhāwa; staponidhīnāṃ nidhiraprameyaḥ |
tāndānawāndaiwawimūḍhabuddhī; nidaṃ samāhūya waco'bhyuwāca ||56||

ācakṣe wo dānawā bāliśāḥ stha; siddhaḥ kaco watsyati matsakāśe |
sañjīwanīṃ prāpya widyāṃ mahārthāṃ; tulyaprabhāwo brahmaṇā brahmabhūtaḥ ||57||

guroruṣya sakāśe tu daśa warṣaśatāni saḥ |
anujñātaḥ kaco gantumiyeṣa tridaśālayam ||58||






                  72


waiśampāyana uwāca||

samāwṛttawrataṃ taṃ tu wisṛṣṭaṃ guruṇā tadā |
prasthitaṃ tridaśāwāsaṃ dewayānyabrawīdidam ||1||

ṛṣeraṅgirasaḥ pautra wṛttenābhijanena ca |
bhrājase widyayā caiwa tapasā ca damena ca ||2||

ṛṣiryathāṅgirā mānyaḥ piturmama mahāyaśāḥ |
tathā mānyaśca pūjyaśca bhūyo mama bṛhaspatiḥ ||3||

ewaṃ jñātwā wijānīhi yadbrawīmi tapodhana |
wratasthe niyamopete yathā wartāmyahaṃ twayi ||4||

sa samāwṛttawidyo māṃ bhaktāṃ bhajitumarhasi |
gṛhāṇa pāṇiṃ widhiwanmama mantrapuraskṛtam ||5||

kaca uwāca||

pūjyo mānyaśca bhagawānyathā tawa pitā mama |
tathā twamanawadyāṅgi pūjanīyatarā mama ||6||

ātmaprāṇaiḥ priyatamā bhārgawasya mahātmanaḥ |
twaṃ bhadre dharmataḥ pūjyā guruputrī sadā mama ||7||

yathā mama gururnityaṃ mānyaḥ śukraḥ pitā tawa |
dewayāni tathaiwa twaṃ naiwaṃ māṃ waktumarhasi ||8||

dewayānyuwāca||

guruputrasya putro wai na tu twamasi me pituḥ |
tasmānmānyaśca pūjyaśca mamāpi twaṃ dwijottama ||9||

asurairhanyamāne ca kaca twayi punaḥ punaḥ |
tadā prabhṛti yā prītistāṃ twamewa smaraswa me ||10||

sauhārde cānurāge ca wettha me bhaktimuttamām |
na māmarhasi dharmajña tyaktuṃ bhaktāmanāgasam ||11||

kaca uwāca||

aniyojye niyoge māṃ niyunakṣi śubhawrate |
prasīda subhru twaṃ mahyaṃ gurorgurutarī śubhe ||12||

yatroṣitaṃ wiśālākṣi twayā candranibhānane |
tatrāhamuṣito bhadre kukṣau kāwyasya bhāmini ||13||

bhaginī dharmato me twaṃ maiwaṃ wocaḥ śubhānane |
sukhamasmyuṣito bhadre na manyurwidyate mama ||14||

āpṛcche twāṃ gamiṣyāmi śiwamāśaṃsa me pathi |
awirodhena dharmasya smartawyo'smi kathāntare ||15||

apramattotthitā nityamārādhaya guruṃ mama ||15||

dewayānyuwāca||

yadi māṃ dharmakāmārthe pratyākhyāsyasi coditaḥ |
tataḥ kaca na te widyā siddhimeṣā gamiṣyati ||16||

kaca uwāca||

guruputrīti kṛtwāhaṃ pratyācakṣe na doṣataḥ |
guruṇā cābhyanujñātaḥ kāmamewaṃ śapaswa mām ||17||

ārṣaṃ dharmaṃ bruwāṇo'haṃ dewayāni yathā twayā |
śapto nārho'smi śāpasya kāmato'dya na dharmataḥ ||18||

tasmādbhawatyā yaḥ kāmo na tathā sa bhawiṣyati |
ṛṣiputro na te kaścijjātu pāṇiṃ grahīṣyati ||19||

phaliṣyati na te widyā yattwaṃ māmāttha tattathā |
adhyāpayiṣyāmi tu yaṃ tasya widyā phaliṣyati ||20||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktwā dwijaśreṣṭho dewayānīṃ kacastadā |
tridaśeśālayaṃ śīghraṃ jagāma dwijasattamaḥ ||21||

tamāgatamabhiprekṣya dewā indrapurogamāḥ |
bṛhaspatiṃ sabhājyedaṃ kacamāhurmudānwitāḥ ||22||

yattwamasmaddhitaṃ karma cakartha paramādbhutam |
na te yaśaḥ praṇaśitā bhāgabhāṅno bhawiṣyasi ||23||






                  73


waiśampāyana uwāca||

kṛtawidye kace prāpte hṛṣṭarūpā diwaukasaḥ |
kacādadhītya tāṃ widyāṃ kṛtārthā bharatarṣabha ||1||

sarwa ewa samāgamya śatakratumathābruwan |
kālaste wikramasyādya jahi śatrūnpuraṃdara ||2||

ewamuktastu sahitaistridaśairmaghawāṃstadā |
tathetyuktwopacakrāma so'paśyata wane striyaḥ ||3||

krīḍantīnāṃ tu kanyānāṃ wane caitrarathopame |
wāyubhūtaḥ sa wastrāṇi sarwāṇyewa wyamiśrayat ||4||

tato jalātsamuttīrya kanyāstāḥ sahitāstadā |
wastrāṇi jagṛhustāni yathāsannānyanekaśaḥ ||5||

tatra wāso dewayānyāḥ śarmiṣṭhā jagṛhe tadā |
wyatimiśramajānantī duhitā wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ ||6||

tatastayormithastatra wirodhaḥ samajāyata |
dewayānyāśca rājendra śarmiṣṭhāyāśca tatkṛte ||7||

dewayānyuwāca||

kasmādgṛhṇāsi me wastraṃ śiṣyā bhūtwā mamāsuri |
samudācārahīnāyā na te śreyo bhawiṣyati ||8||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

āsīnaṃ ca śayānaṃ ca pitā te pitaraṃ mama |
stauti wandati cābhīkṣṇaṃ nīcaiḥ sthitwā winītawat ||9||

yācatastwaṃ hi duhitā stuwataḥ pratigṛhṇataḥ |
sutāhaṃ stūyamānasya dadato'pratigṛhṇataḥ ||10||

anāyudhā sāyudhāyā riktā kṣubhyasi bhikṣuki |
lapsyase pratiyoddhāraṃ na hi twāṃ gaṇayāmyaham ||11||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

samucchrayaṃ dewayānīṃ gatāṃ saktāṃ ca wāsasi |
śarmiṣṭhā prākṣipatkūpe tataḥ swapuramāwrajat ||12||

hateyamiti wijñāya śarmiṣṭhā pāpaniścayā |
anawekṣya yayau weśma krodhawegaparāyaṇā ||13||

atha taṃ deśamabhyāgādyayātirnahuṣātmajaḥ |
śrāntayugyaḥ śrāntahayo mṛgalipsuḥ pipāsitaḥ ||14||

sa nāhuṣaḥ prekṣamāṇa udapānaṃ gatodakam |
dadarśa kanyāṃ tāṃ tatra dīptāmagniśikhāmiwa ||15||

tāmapṛcchatsa dṛṣṭwaiwa kanyāmamarawarṇinīm |
sāntwayitwā nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ sāmnā paramawalgunā ||16||

kā twaṃ tāmranakhī śyāmā sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalā |
dīrghaṃ dhyāyasi cātyarthaṃ kasmācchwasiṣi cāturā ||17||

kathaṃ ca patitāsyasminkūpe wīruttṛṇāwṛte |
duhitā caiwa kasya twaṃ wada sarwaṃ sumadhyame ||18||

dewayānyuwāca||

yo'sau dewairhatāndaityānutthāpayati widyayā |
tasya śukrasya kanyāhaṃ sa māṃ nūnaṃ na budhyate ||19||

eṣa me dakṣiṇo rājanpāṇistāmranakhāṅguliḥ |
samuddhara gṛhītwā māṃ kulīnastwaṃ hi me mataḥ ||20||

jānāmi hi twāṃ saṃśāntaṃ wīryawantaṃ yaśaswinam |
tasmānmāṃ patitāmasmātkūpāduddhartumarhasi ||21||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tāmatha brāhmaṇīṃ strīṃ ca wijñāya nahuṣātmajaḥ |
gṛhītwā dakṣiṇe pāṇāwujjahāra tato'waṭāt ||22||

uddhṛtya caināṃ tarasā tasmātkūpānnarādhipaḥ |
āmantrayitwā suśroṇīṃ yayātiḥ swapuraṃ yayau ||23||

dewayānyuwāca||

twaritaṃ ghūrṇike gaccha sarwamācakṣwa me pituḥ |
nedānīṃ hi prawekyāmi nagaraṃ wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ ||24||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

sā tu wai twaritaṃ gatwā ghūrṇikāsuramandiram |
dṛṣṭwā kāwyamuwācedaṃ sambhramāwiṣṭacetanā ||25||

ācakṣe te mahāprājña dewayānī wane hatā |
śarmiṣṭhayā mahābhāga duhitrā wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ ||26||

śrutwā duhitaraṃ kāwyastatra śarmiṣṭhayā hatām |
twarayā niryayau duḥkhānmārgamāṇaḥ sutāṃ wane ||27||

dṛṣṭwā duhitaraṃ kāwyo dewayānīṃ tato wane |
bāhubhyāṃ sampariṣwajya duḥkhito wākyamabrawīt ||28||

ātmadoṣairniyacchanti sarwe duḥkhasukhe janāḥ |
manye duścaritaṃ te'sti yasyeyaṃ niṣkṛtiḥ kṛtā ||29||

dewayānyuwāca||

niṣkṛtirme'stu wā māstu śṛṇuṣwāwahito mama |
śarmiṣṭhayā yaduktāsmi duhitrā wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ ||30||

satyaṃ kilaitatsā prāha daityānāmasi gāyanaḥ ||30||

ewaṃ hi me kathayati śarmiṣṭhā wārṣaparwaṇī |
wacanaṃ tīkṣṇaparuṣaṃ krodharaktekṣaṇā bhṛśam ||31||

stuwato duhitā hi twaṃ yācataḥ pratigṛhṇataḥ |
sutāhaṃ stūyamānasya dadato'pratigṛhṇataḥ ||32||

iti māmāha śarmiṣṭhā duhitā wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ |
krodhasaṃraktanayanā darpapūrṇā punaḥ punaḥ ||33||

yadyahaṃ stuwatastāta duhitā pratigṛhṇataḥ |
prasādayiṣye śarmiṣṭhāmityuktā hi sakhī mayā ||34||

śukra uwāca||

stuwato duhitā na twaṃ bhadre na pratigṛhṇataḥ |
astotuḥ stūyamānasya duhitā dewayānyasi ||35||

wṛṣaparwaiwa tadweda śakro rājā ca nāhuṣaḥ |
acintyaṃ brahma nirdwandwamaiśwaraṃ hi balaṃ mama ||36||






                  74


śukra uwāca||

yaḥ pareṣāṃ naro nityamatiwādāṃstitikṣati |
dewayāni wijānīhi tena sarwamidaṃ jitam ||1||

yaḥ samutpatitaṃ krodhaṃ nigṛhṇāti hayaṃ yathā |
sa yantetyucyate sadbhirna yo raśmiṣu lambate ||2||

yaḥ samutpatitaṃ krodhamakrodhena nirasyati |
dewayāni wijānīhi tena sarwamidaṃ jitam ||3||

yaḥ samutpatitaṃ krodhaṃ kṣamayeha nirasyati |
yathoragastwacaṃ jīrṇāṃ sa wai puruṣa ucyate ||4||

yaḥ sandhārayate manyuṃ yo'tiwādāṃstitikṣati |
yaśca tapto na tapati dṛḍhaṃ so'rthasya bhājanam ||5||

yo yajedapariśrānto māsi māsi śataṃ samāḥ |
na krudhyedyaśca sarwasya tayorakrodhano'dhikaḥ ||6||

yatkumārāḥ kumāryaśca wairaṃ kuryuracetasaḥ |
na tatprājño'nukurwīta widuste na balābalam ||7||

dewayānyuwāca||

wedāhaṃ tāta bālāpi dharmāṇāṃ yadihāntaram |
akrodhe cātiwāde ca weda cāpi balābalam ||8||

śiṣyasyāśiṣyawṛtterhi na kṣantawyaṃ bubhūṣatā |
tasmātsaṅkīrṇawṛtteṣu wāso mama na rocate ||9||

pumāṃso ye hi nindanti wṛttenābhijanena ca |
na teṣu niwasetprājñaḥ śreyorthī pāpabuddhiṣu ||10||

ye twenamabhijānanti wṛttenābhijanena ca |
teṣu sādhuṣu wastawyaṃ sa wāsaḥ śreṣṭha ucyate ||11||

wāgduruktaṃ mahāghoraṃ duhiturwṛṣaparwaṇaḥ |
na hyato duṣkarataraṃ manye lokeṣwapi triṣu ||12||

yaḥ sapatnaśriyaṃ dīptāṃ hīnaśrīḥ paryupāsate ||12||






                  75


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ kāwyo bhṛguśreṣṭhaḥ samanyurupagamya ha |
wṛṣaparwāṇamāsīnamityuwācāwicārayan ||1||

nādharmaścarito rājansadyaḥ phalati gauriwa |
putreṣu wā naptṛṣu wā na cedātmani paśyati ||2||

phalatyewa dhruwaṃ pāpaṃ gurubhuktamiwodare ||2||

yadaghātayathā wipraṃ kacamāṅgirasaṃ tadā |
apāpaśīlaṃ dharmajñaṃ śuśrūṣuṃ madgṛhe ratam ||3||

wadhādanarhatastasya wadhācca duhiturmama |
wṛṣaparwannibodhedaṃ tyakṣyāmi twāṃ sabāndhawam ||4||

sthātuṃ twadwiṣaye rājanna śakṣyāmi twayā saha ||4||

aho māmabhijānāsi daitya mithyāpralāpinam |
yathemamātmano doṣaṃ na niyacchasyupekṣase ||5||

wṛṣaparwowāca||

nādharmaṃ na mṛṣāwādaṃ twayi jānāmi bhārgawa |
twayi dharmaśca satyaṃ ca tatprasīdatu no bhawān ||6||

yadyasmānapahāya twamito gacchasi bhārgawa |
samudraṃ samprawekṣyāmo nānyadasti parāyaṇam ||7||

śukra uwāca||

samudraṃ prawiśadhwaṃ wā diśo wā drawatāsurāḥ |
duhiturnāpriyaṃ soḍhuṃ śakto'haṃ dayitā hi me ||8||

prasādyatāṃ dewayānī jīwitaṃ hyatra me sthitam |
yogakṣemakaraste'hamindrasyewa bṛhaspatiḥ ||9||

wṛṣaparwowāca||

yatkiñcidasurendrāṇāṃ widyate wasu bhārgawa |
bhuwi hastigawāśwaṃ wā tasya twaṃ mama ceśwaraḥ ||10||

śukra uwāca||

yatkiñcidasti drawiṇaṃ daityendrāṇāṃ mahāsura |
tasyeśwaro'smi yadi te dewayānī prasādyatām ||11||

dewayānyuwāca||

yadi twamīśwarastāta rājño wittasya bhārgawa |
nābhijānāmi tatte'haṃ rājā tu wadatu swayam ||12||

wṛṣaparwowāca||

yaṃ kāmamabhikāmāsi dewayāni śucismite |
tatte'haṃ sampradāsyāmi yadi cedapi durlabham ||13||

dewayānyuwāca||

dāsīṃ kanyāsahasreṇa śarmiṣṭhāmabhikāmaye |
anu māṃ tatra gacchetsā yatra dāsyati me pitā ||14||

wṛṣaparwowāca||

uttiṣṭha he saṅgrahītri śarmiṣṭhāṃ śīghramānaya |
yaṃ ca kāmayate kāmaṃ dewayānī karotu tam ||15||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato dhātrī tatra gatwā śarmiṣṭhāṃ wākyamabrawīt |
uttiṣṭha bhadre śarmiṣṭhe jñātīnāṃ sukhamāwaha ||16||

tyajati brāhmaṇaḥ śiṣyāndewayānyā pracoditaḥ |
sā yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ sa kāryo'dya twayānaghe ||17||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

sā yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ karawāṇyahamadya tam |
mā twewāpagamacchukro dewayānī ca matkṛte ||18||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ kanyāsahasreṇa wṛtā śibikayā tadā |
piturniyogāttwaritā niścakrāma purottamāt ||19||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

ahaṃ kanyāsahasreṇa dāsī te paricārikā |
anu twāṃ tatra yāsyāmi yatra dāsyati te pitā ||20||

dewayānyuwāca||

stuwato duhitā te'haṃ bandinaḥ pratigṛhṇataḥ |
stūyamānasya duhitā kathaṃ dāsī bhawiṣyasi ||21||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

yena kenacidārtānāṃ jñātīnāṃ sukhamāwahet |
atastwāmanuyāsyāmi yatra dāsyati te pitā ||22||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

pratiśrute dāsabhāwe duhitrā wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ |
dewayānī nṛpaśreṣṭha pitaraṃ wākyamabrawīt ||23||

prawiśāmi puraṃ tāta tuṣṭāsmi dwijasattama |
amoghaṃ tawa wijñānamasti widyābalaṃ ca te ||24||

ewamukto duhitrā sa dwijaśreṣṭho mahāyaśāḥ |
prawiweśa puraṃ hṛṣṭaḥ pūjitaḥ sarwadānawaiḥ ||25||






                  76


waiśampāyana uwāca||

atha dīrghasya kālasya dewayānī nṛpottama |
wanaṃ tadewa niryātā krīḍārthaṃ warawarṇinī ||1||

tena dāsīsahasreṇa sārdhaṃ śarmiṣṭhayā tadā |
tamewa deśaṃ samprāptā yathākāmaṃ cacāra sā ||2||

tābhiḥ sakhībhiḥ sahitā sarwābhirmuditā bhṛśam ||2||

krīḍantyo'bhiratāḥ sarwāḥ pibantyo madhumādhawīm |
khādantyo wiwidhānbhakṣyānwidaśantyaḥ phalāni ca ||3||

punaśca nāhuṣo rājā mṛgalipsuryadṛcchayā |
tamewa deśaṃ samprāpto jalārthī śramakarśitaḥ ||4||

dadṛśe dewayānīṃ ca śarmiṣṭhāṃ tāśca yoṣitaḥ |
pibantīrlalamānāśca diwyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ||5||

upawiṣṭāṃ ca dadṛśe dewayānīṃ śucismitām |
rūpeṇāpratimāṃ tāsāṃ strīṇāṃ madhye warāṅganām ||6||

śarmiṣṭhayā sewyamānāṃ pādasaṃwāhanādibhiḥ ||6||

yayātiruwāca||

dwābhyāṃ kanyāsahasrābhyāṃ dwe kanye pariwārite |
gotre ca nāmanī caiwa dwayoḥ pṛcchāmi wāmaham ||7||

dewayānyuwāca||

ākhyāsyāmyahamādatswa wacanaṃ me narādhipa |
śukro nāmāsuraguruḥ sutāṃ jānīhi tasya mām ||8||

iyaṃ ca me sakhī dāsī yatrāhaṃ tatra gāminī |
duhitā dānawendrasya śarmiṣṭhā wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ ||9||

yayātiruwāca||

kathaṃ nu te sakhī dāsī kanyeyaṃ warawarṇinī |
asurendrasutā subhru paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ||10||

dewayānyuwāca||

sarwa ewa narawyāghra widhānamanuwartate |
widhānawihitaṃ matwā mā wicitrāḥ kathāḥ kṛthāḥ ||11||

rājawadrūpaweṣau te brāhmīṃ wācaṃ bibharṣi ca |
kiṃnāmā twaṃ kutaścāsi kasya putraśca śaṃsa me ||12||

yayātiruwāca||

brahmacaryeṇa kṛtsno me wedaḥ śrutipathaṃ gataḥ |
rājāhaṃ rājaputraśca yayātiriti wiśrutaḥ ||13||

dewayānyuwāca||

kenāsyarthena nṛpate imaṃ deśamupāgataḥ |
jighṛkṣurwārijaṃ kiñcidatha wā mṛgalipsayā ||14||

yayātiruwāca||

mṛgalipsurahaṃ bhadre pānīyārthamupāgataḥ |
bahu cāpyanuyukto'smi tanmānujñātumarhasi ||15||

dewayānyuwāca||

dwābhyāṃ kanyāsahasrābhyāṃ dāsyā śarmiṣṭhayā saha |
twadadhīnāsmi bhadraṃ te sakhā bhartā ca me bhawa ||16||

yayātiruwāca||

widdhyauśanasi bhadraṃ te na twāmarho'smi bhāmini |
awiwāhyā hi rājāno dewayāni pitustawa ||17||

dewayānyuwāca||

saṃsṛṣṭaṃ brahmaṇā kṣatraṃ kṣatraṃ ca brahmasaṃhitam |
ṛṣiśca ṛṣiputraśca nāhuṣāṅga wahaswa mām ||18||

yayātiruwāca||

ekadehodbhawā warṇāścatwāro'pi warāṅgane |
pṛthagdharmāḥ pṛthakṣaucāsteṣāṃ tu brāhmaṇo waraḥ ||19||

dewayānyuwāca||

pāṇidharmo nāhuṣāyaṃ na pumbhiḥ sewitaḥ purā |
taṃ me twamagrahīragre wṛṇomi twāmahaṃ tataḥ ||20||

kathaṃ nu me manaswinyāḥ pāṇimanyaḥ pumānspṛśet |
gṛhītamṛṣiputreṇa swayaṃ wāpyṛṣiṇā twayā ||21||

yayātiruwāca||

kruddhādāśīwiṣātsarpājjwalanātsarwatomukhāt |
durādharṣataro wipraḥ puruṣeṇa wijānatā ||22||

dewayānyuwāca||

kathamāśīwiṣātsarpājjwalanātsarwatomukhāt |
durādharṣataro wipra ityāttha puruṣarṣabha ||23||

yayātiruwāca||

ekamāśīwiṣo hanti śastreṇaikaśca wadhyate |
hanti wipraḥ sarāṣṭrāṇi purāṇyapi hi kopitaḥ ||24||

durādharṣataro wiprastasmādbhīru mato mama |
ato'dattāṃ ca pitrā twāṃ bhadre na wiwahāmyaham ||25||

dewayānyuwāca||

dattāṃ wahaswa pitrā māṃ twaṃ hi rājanwṛto mayā |
ayācato bhayaṃ nāsti dattāṃ ca pratigṛhṇataḥ ||26||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

twaritaṃ dewayānyātha preṣitaṃ piturātmanaḥ |
śrutwaiwa ca sa rājānaṃ darśayāmāsa bhārgawaḥ ||27||

dṛṣṭwaiwa cāgataṃ śukraṃ yayātiḥ pṛthiwīpatiḥ |
wawande brāhmaṇaṃ kāwyaṃ prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ sthitaḥ ||28||

dewayānyuwāca||

rājāyaṃ nāhuṣastāta durge me pāṇimagrahīt |
namaste dehi māmasmai nānyaṃ loke patiṃ wṛṇe ||29||

śukra uwāca||

wṛto'nayā patirwīra sutayā twaṃ mameṣṭayā |
gṛhāṇemāṃ mayā dattāṃ mahiṣīṃ nahuṣātmaja ||30||

yayātiruwāca||

adharmo na spṛśedewaṃ mahānmāmiha bhārgawa |
warṇasaṅkarajo brahmanniti twāṃ prawṛṇomyaham ||31||

śukra uwāca||

adharmāttwāṃ wimuñcāmi warayaswa yathepṣitam |
asminwiwāhe mā glāsīrahaṃ pāpaṃ nudāmi te ||32||

wahaswa bhāryāṃ dharmeṇa dewayānīṃ sumadhyamām |
anayā saha samprītimatulāṃ samawāpsyasi ||33||

iyaṃ cāpi kumārī te śarmiṣṭhā wārṣaparwaṇī |
sampūjyā satataṃ rājanmā caināṃ śayane hwayeḥ ||34||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamukto yayātistu śukraṃ kṛtwā pradakṣiṇam |
jagāma swapuraṃ hṛṣṭo anujñāto mahātmanā ||35||






                  77


waiśampāyana uwāca||

yayātiḥ swapuraṃ prāpya mahendrapurasaṃnibham |
prawiśyāntaḥpuraṃ tatra dewayānīṃ nyaweśayat ||1||

dewayānyāścānumate tāṃ sutāṃ wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ |
aśokawanikābhyāśe gṛhaṃ kṛtwā nyaweśayat ||2||

wṛtāṃ dāsīsahasreṇa śarmiṣṭhāmāsurāyaṇīm |
wāsobhirannapānaiśca saṃwibhajya susatkṛtām ||3||

dewayānyā tu sahitaḥ sa nṛpo nahuṣātmajaḥ |
wijahāra bahūnabdāndewawanmudito bhṛśam ||4||

ṛtukāle tu samprāpte dewayānī warāṅganā |
lebhe garbhaṃ prathamataḥ kumāraṃ ca wyajāyata ||5||

gate warṣasahasre tu śarmiṣṭhā wārṣaparwaṇī |
dadarśa yauwanaṃ prāptā ṛtuṃ sā cānwacintayat ||6||

ṛtukālaśca samprāpto na ca me'sti patirwṛtaḥ |
kiṃ prāptaṃ kiṃ nu kartawyaṃ kiṃ wā kṛtwā kṛtaṃ bhawet ||7||

dewayānī prajātāsau wṛthāhaṃ prāptayauwanā |
yathā tayā wṛto bhartā tathaiwāhaṃ wṛṇomi tam ||8||

rājñā putraphalaṃ deyamiti me niścitā matiḥ |
apīdānīṃ sa dharmātmā iyānme darśanaṃ rahaḥ ||9||

atha niṣkramya rājāsau tasminkāle yadṛcchayā |
aśokawanikābhyāśe śarmiṣṭhāṃ prāpya wiṣṭhitaḥ ||10||

tamekaṃ rahite dṛṣṭwā śarmiṣṭhā cāruhāsinī |
pratyudgamyāñjaliṃ kṛtwā rājānaṃ wākyamabrawīt ||11||

somasyendrasya wiṣṇorwā yamasya waruṇasya wā |
tawa wā nāhuṣa kule kaḥ striyaṃ spraṣṭumarhati ||12||

rūpābhijanaśīlairhi twaṃ rājanwettha māṃ sadā |
sā twāṃ yāce prasādyāhamṛtuṃ dehi narādhipa ||13||

yayātiruwāca||

wedmi twāṃ śīlasampannāṃ daityakanyāmaninditām |
rūpe ca te na paśyāmi sūcyagramapi ninditam ||14||

abrawīduśanā kāwyo dewayānīṃ yadāwaham |
neyamāhwayitawyā te śayane wārṣaparwaṇī ||15||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

na narmayuktaṃ wacanaṃ hinasti; na strīṣu rājanna wiwāhakāle |
prāṇātyaye sarwadhanāpahāre; pañcānṛtānyāhurapātakāni ||16||

pṛṣṭaṃ tu sākṣye prawadantamanyathā; wadanti mithyopahitaṃ narendra |
ekārthatāyāṃ tu samāhitāyāṃ; mithyā wadantamanṛtaṃ hinasti ||17||

yayātiruwāca||

rājā pramāṇaṃ bhūtānāṃ sa naśyeta mṛṣā wadan |
arthakṛcchramapi prāpya na mithyā kartumutsahe ||18||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

samāwetau matau rājanpatiḥ sakhyāśca yaḥ patiḥ |
samaṃ wiwāhamityāhuḥ sakhyā me'si patirwṛtaḥ ||19||

yayātiruwāca||

dātawyaṃ yācamānebhya iti me wratamāhitam |
twaṃ ca yācasi māṃ kāmaṃ brūhi kiṃ karawāṇi te ||20||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

adharmāttrāhi māṃ rājandharmaṃ ca pratipādaya |
twatto'patyawatī loke careyaṃ dharmamuttamam ||21||

traya ewādhanā rājanbhāryā dāsastathā sutaḥ |
yatte samadhigacchanti yasya te tasya taddhanam ||22||

dewayānyā bhujiṣyāsmi waśyā ca tawa bhārgawī |
sā cāhaṃ ca twayā rājanbharaṇīye bhajaswa mām ||23||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastu rājā sa tathyamityewa jajñiwān |
pūjayāmāsa śarmiṣṭhāṃ dharmaṃ ca pratyapādayat ||24||

samāgamya ca śarmiṣṭhāṃ yathākāmamawāpya ca |
anyonyamabhisampūjya jagmatustau yathāgatam ||25||

tasminsamāgame subhrūḥ śarmiṣṭhā cāruhāsinī |
lebhe garbhaṃ prathamatastasmānnṛpatisattamāt ||26||

prajajñe ca tataḥ kāle rājanrājīwalocanā |
kumāraṃ dewagarbhābhaṃ rājīwanibhalocanam ||27||






                  78


waiśampāyana uwāca||

śrutwā kumāraṃ jātaṃ tu dewayānī śucismitā |
cintayāmāsa duḥkhārtā śarmiṣṭhāṃ prati bhārata ||1||

abhigamya ca śarmiṣṭhāṃ dewayānyabrawīdidam |
kimidaṃ wṛjinaṃ subhru kṛtaṃ te kāmalubdhayā ||2||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

ṛṣirabhyāgataḥ kaściddharmātmā wedapāragaḥ |
sa mayā waradaḥ kāmaṃ yācito dharmasaṃhitam ||3||

nāhamanyāyataḥ kāmamācarāmi śucismite |
tasmādṛṣermamāpatyamiti satyaṃ brawīmi te ||4||

dewayānyuwāca||

śobhanaṃ bhīru satyaṃ cedatha sa jñāyate dwijaḥ |
gotranāmābhijanato wettumicchāmi taṃ dwijam ||5||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

ojasā tejasā caiwa dīpyamānaṃ rawiṃ yathā |
taṃ dṛṣṭwā mama sampraṣṭuṃ śaktirnāsīcchucismite ||6||

dewayānyuwāca||

yadyetadewaṃ śarmiṣṭhe na manyurwidyate mama |
apatyaṃ yadi te labdhaṃ jyeṣṭhācchreṣṭhācca wai dwijāt ||7||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

anyonyamewamuktwā ca samprahasya ca te mithaḥ |
jagāma bhārgawī weśma tathyamityewa jajñuṣī ||8||

yayātirdewayānyāṃ tu putrāwajanayannṛpaḥ |
yaduṃ ca turwasuṃ caiwa śakrawiṣṇū iwāparau ||9||

tasmādewa tu rājarṣeḥ śarmiṣṭhā wārṣaparwaṇī |
druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca trīnkumārānajījanat ||10||

tataḥ kāle tu kasmiṃściddewayānī śucismitā |
yayātisahitā rājannirjagāma mahāwanam ||11||

dadarśa ca tadā tatra kumārāndewarūpiṇaḥ |
krīḍamānānsuwiśrabdhānwismitā cedamabrawīt ||12||

kasyaite dārakā rājandewaputropamāḥ śubhāḥ |
warcasā rūpataścaiwa sadṛśā me matāstawa ||13||

ewaṃ pṛṣṭwā tu rājānaṃ kumārānparyapṛcchata |
kiṃnāmadheyagotro waḥ putrakā brāhmaṇaḥ pitā ||14||

wibrūta me yathātathyaṃ śrotumicchāmi taṃ hyaham ||14||

te'darśayanpradeśinyā tamewa nṛpasattamam |
śarmiṣṭhāṃ mātaraṃ caiwa tasyācakhyuśca dārakāḥ ||15||

ityuktwā sahitāste tu rājānamupacakramuḥ |
nābhyanandata tānrājā dewayānyāstadāntike ||16||

rudantaste'tha śarmiṣṭhāmabhyayurbālakāstataḥ ||16||

dṛṣṭwā tu teṣāṃ bālānāṃ praṇayaṃ pārthiwaṃ prati |
buddhwā ca tattwato dewī śarmiṣṭhāmidamabrawīt ||17||

madadhīnā satī kasmādakārṣīrwipriyaṃ mama |
tamewāsuradharmaṃ twamāsthitā na bibheṣi kim ||18||

śarmiṣṭhowāca||

yaduktamṛṣirityewa tatsatyaṃ cāruhāsini |
nyāyato dharmataścaiwa carantī na bibhemi te ||19||

yadā twayā wṛto rājā wṛta ewa tadā mayā |
sakhībhartā hi dharmeṇa bhartā bhawati śobhane ||20||

pūjyāsi mama mānyā ca jyeṣṭhā śreṣṭhā ca brāhmaṇī |
twatto'pi me pūjyatamo rājarṣiḥ kiṃ na wettha tat ||21||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

śrutwā tasyāstato wākyaṃ dewayānyabrawīdidam |
rājannādyeha watsyāmi wipriyaṃ me kṛtaṃ twayā ||22||

sahasotpatitāṃ śyāmāṃ dṛṣṭwā tāṃ sāśrulocanām |
twaritaṃ sakāśaṃ kāwyasya prasthitāṃ wyathitastadā ||23||

anuwawrāja sambhrāntaḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ sāntwayannṛpaḥ |
nyawartata na caiwa sma krodhasaṃraktalocanā ||24||

awibruwantī kiñcittu rājānaṃ cārulocanā |
acirādiwa samprāptā kāwyasyośanaso'ntikam ||25||

sā tu dṛṣṭwaiwa pitaramabhiwādyāgrataḥ sthitā |
anantaraṃ yayātistu pūjayāmāsa bhārgawam ||26||

dewayānyuwāca||

adharmeṇa jito dharmaḥ prawṛttamadharottaram |
śarmiṣṭhayātiwṛttāsmi duhitrā wṛṣaparwaṇaḥ ||27||

trayo'syāṃ janitāḥ putrā rājñānena yayātinā |
durbhagāyā mama dwau tu putrau tāta brawīmi te ||28||

dharmajña iti wikhyāta eṣa rājā bhṛgūdwaha |
atikrāntaśca maryādāṃ kāwyaitatkathayāmi te ||29||

śukra uwāca||

dharmajñaḥ sanmahārāja yo'dharmamakṛthāḥ priyam |
tasmājjarā twāmacirāddharṣayiṣyati durjayā ||30||

yayātiruwāca||

ṛtuṃ wai yācamānāyā bhagawannānyacetasā |
duhiturdānawendrasya dharmyametatkṛtaṃ mayā ||31||

ṛtuṃ wai yācamānāyā na dadāti pumānwṛtaḥ |
bhrūṇahetyucyate brahmansa iha brahmawādibhiḥ ||32||

abhikāmāṃ striyaṃ yastu gamyāṃ rahasi yācitaḥ |
nopaiti sa ca dharmeṣu bhrūṇahetyucyate budhaiḥ ||33||

ityetāni samīkṣyāhaṃ kāraṇāni bhṛgūdwaha |
adharmabhayasaṃwignaḥ śarmiṣṭhāmupajagmiwān ||34||

śukra uwāca||

nanwahaṃ pratyawekṣyaste madadhīno'si pārthiwa |
mithyācārasya dharmeṣu cauryaṃ bhawati nāhuṣa ||35||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

kruddhenośanasā śapto yayātirnāhuṣastadā |
pūrwaṃ wayaḥ parityajya jarāṃ sadyo'nwapadyata ||36||

yayātiruwāca||

atṛpto yauwanasyāhaṃ dewayānyāṃ bhṛgūdwaha |
prasādaṃ kuru me brahmañjareyaṃ mā wiśeta mām ||37||

śukra uwāca||

nāhaṃ mṛṣā brawīmyetajjarāṃ prāpto'si bhūmipa |
jarāṃ twetāṃ twamanyasmai saṅkrāmaya yadīcchasi ||38||

yayātiruwāca||

rājyabhāksa bhawedbrahmanpuṇyabhākkīrtibhāktathā |
yo me dadyādwayaḥ putrastadbhawānanumanyatām ||39||

śukra uwāca||

saṅkrāmayiṣyasi jarāṃ yatheṣṭaṃ nahuṣātmaja |
māmanudhyāya bhāwena na ca pāpamawāpsyasi ||40||

wayo dāsyati te putro yaḥ sa rājā bhawiṣyati |
āyuṣmānkīrtimāṃścaiwa bahwapatyastathaiwa ca ||41||






                  79


waiśampāyana uwāca||

jarāṃ prāpya yayātistu swapuraṃ prāpya caiwa ha |
putraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ wariṣṭhaṃ ca yadumityabrawīdwacaḥ ||1||

jarā walī ca māṃ tāta palitāni ca paryaguḥ |
kāwyasyośanasaḥ śāpānna ca tṛpto'smi yauwane ||2||

twaṃ yado pratipadyaswa pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha |
yauwanena twadīyena careyaṃ wiṣayānaham ||3||

pūrṇe warṣasahasre tu punaste yauwanaṃ twaham |
dattwā swaṃ pratipatsyāmi pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ||4||

yaduruwāca||

sitaśmaśruśirā dīno jarayā śithilīkṛtaḥ |
walīsantatagātraśca durdarśo durbalaḥ kṛśaḥ ||5||

aśaktaḥ kāryakaraṇe paribhūtaḥ sa yauwanaiḥ |
sahopajīwibhiścaiwa tāṃ jarāṃ nābhikāmaye ||6||

yayātiruwāca||

yattwaṃ me hṛdayājjāto wayaḥ swaṃ na prayacchasi |
tasmādarājyabhāktāta prajā te wai bhawiṣyati ||7||

turwaso pratipadyaswa pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha |
yauwanena careyaṃ wai wiṣayāṃstawa putraka ||8||

pūrṇe warṣasahasre tu punardāsyāmi yauwanam |
swaṃ caiwa pratipatsyāmi pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ||9||

turwasuruwāca||

na kāmaye jarāṃ tāta kāmabhogapraṇāśinīm |
balarūpāntakaraṇīṃ buddhiprāṇawināśinīm ||10||

yayātiruwāca||

yattwaṃ me hṛdayājjāto wayaḥ swaṃ na prayacchasi |
tasmātprajā samucchedaṃ turwaso tawa yāsyati ||11||

saṅkīrṇācāradharmeṣu pratilomacareṣu ca |
piśitāśiṣu cāntyeṣu mūḍha rājā bhawiṣyasi ||12||

gurudāraprasakteṣu tiryagyonigateṣu ca |
paśudharmiṣu pāpeṣu mleccheṣu prabhawiṣyasi ||13||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ sa turwasuṃ śaptwā yayātiḥ sutamātmanaḥ |
śarmiṣṭhāyāḥ sutaṃ druhyumidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||14||

druhyo twaṃ pratipadyaswa warṇarūpawināśinīm |
jarāṃ warṣasahasraṃ me yauwanaṃ swaṃ dadaswa ca ||15||

pūrṇe warṣasahasre tu pratidāsyāmi yauwanam |
swaṃ cādāsyāmi bhūyo'haṃ pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ||16||

druhyuruwāca||

na gajaṃ na rathaṃ nāśwaṃ jīrṇo bhuṅkte na ca striyam |
wāgbhaṅgaścāsya bhawati tajjarāṃ nābhikāmaye ||17||

yayātiruwāca||

yattwaṃ me hṛdayājjāto wayaḥ swaṃ na prayacchasi |
tasmāddruhyo priyaḥ kāmo na te sampatsyate kwacit ||18||

uḍupaplawasantāro yatra nityaṃ bhawiṣyati |
arājā bhojaśabdaṃ twaṃ tatrāwāpsyasi sānwayaḥ ||19||

ano twaṃ pratipadyaswa pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha |
ekaṃ warṣasahasraṃ tu careyaṃ yauwanena te ||20||

anuruwāca||

jīrṇaḥ śiśuwadādatte'kāle'nnamaśuciryathā |
na juhoti ca kāle'gniṃ tāṃ jarāṃ nābhikāmaye ||21||

yayātiruwāca||

yattwaṃ me hṛdayājjāto wayaḥ swaṃ na prayacchasi |
jarādoṣastwayokto'yaṃ tasmāttwaṃ pratipatsyase ||22||

prajāśca yauwanaprāptā winaśiṣyantyano tawa |
agnipraskandanaparastwaṃ cāpyewaṃ bhawiṣyasi ||23||

pūro twaṃ me priyaḥ putrastwaṃ warīyānbhawiṣyasi |
jarā walī ca me tāta palitāni ca paryaguḥ ||24||

kāwyasyośanasaḥ śāpānna ca tṛpto'smi yauwane ||24||

pūro twaṃ pratipadyaswa pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha |
kañcitkālaṃ careyaṃ wai wiṣayānwayasā tawa ||25||

pūrṇe warṣasahasre tu pratidāsyāmi yauwanam |
swaṃ caiwa pratipatsyāmi pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ||26||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktaḥ pratyuwāca pūruḥ pitaramañjasā |
yathāttha māṃ mahārāja tatkariṣyāmi te wacaḥ ||27||

pratipatsyāmi te rājanpāpmānaṃ jarayā saha |
gṛhāṇa yauwanaṃ mattaścara kāmānyathepsitān ||28||

jarayāhaṃ praticchanno wayorūpadharastawa |
yauwanaṃ bhawate dattwā cariṣyāmi yathāttha mām ||29||

yayātiruwāca||

pūro prīto'smi te watsa prītaścedaṃ dadāmi te |
sarwakāmasamṛddhā te prajā rājye bhawiṣyati ||30||






                  80


waiśampāyana uwāca||

pauraweṇātha wayasā yayātirnahuṣātmajaḥ |
prītiyukto nṛpaśreṣṭhaścacāra wiṣayānpriyān ||1||

yathākāmaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathākālaṃ yathāsukham |
dharmāwiruddhānrājendro yathārhati sa ewa hi ||2||

dewānatarpayadyajñaiḥ śrāddhaistadwatpitṛnapi |
dīnānanugrahairiṣṭaiḥ kāmaiśca dwijasattamān ||3||

atithīnannapānaiśca wiśaśca paripālanaiḥ |
ānṛśaṃsyena śūdrāṃśca dasyūnsaṃnigraheṇa ca ||4||

dharmeṇa ca prajāḥ sarwā yathāwadanurañjayan |
yayātiḥ pālayāmāsa sākṣādindra iwāparaḥ ||5||

sa rājā siṃhawikrānto yuwā wiṣayagocaraḥ |
awirodhena dharmasya cacāra sukhamuttamam ||6||

sa samprāpya śubhānkāmāṃstṛptaḥ khinnaśca pārthiwaḥ |
kālaṃ warṣasahasrāntaṃ sasmāra manujādhipaḥ ||7||

parisaṅkhyāya kālajñaḥ kalāḥ kāṣṭhāśca wīryawān |
pūrṇaṃ matwā tataḥ kālaṃ pūruṃ putramuwāca ha ||8||

yathākāmaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathākālamariṃdama |
sewitā wiṣayāḥ putra yauwanena mayā tawa ||9||

pūro prīto'smi bhadraṃ te gṛhāṇedaṃ swayauwanam |
rājyaṃ caiwa gṛhāṇedaṃ twaṃ hi me priyakṛtsutaḥ ||10||

pratipede jarāṃ rājā yayātirnāhuṣastadā |
yauwanaṃ pratipede ca pūruḥ swaṃ punarātmanaḥ ||11||

abhiṣektukāmaṃ nṛpatiṃ pūruṃ putraṃ kanīyasam |
brāhmaṇapramukhā warṇā idaṃ wacanamabruwan ||12||

kathaṃ śukrasya naptāraṃ dewayānyāḥ sutaṃ prabho |
jyeṣṭhaṃ yadumatikramya rājyaṃ pūroḥ pradāsyasi ||13||

yadurjyeṣṭhastawa suto jātastamanu turwasuḥ |
śarmiṣṭhāyāḥ suto druhyustato'nuḥ pūrurewa ca ||14||

kathaṃ jyeṣṭhānatikramya kanīyānrājyamarhati |
etatsambodhayāmastwāṃ dharmaṃ twamanupālaya ||15||

yayātiruwāca||

brāhmaṇapramukhā warṇāḥ sarwe śṛṇwantu me wacaḥ |
jyeṣṭhaṃ prati yathā rājyaṃ na deyaṃ me kathañcana ||16||

mama jyeṣṭhena yadunā niyogo nānupālitaḥ |
pratikūlaḥ pituryaśca na sa putraḥ satāṃ mataḥ ||17||

mātāpitrorwacanakṛddhitaḥ pathyaśca yaḥ sutaḥ |
sa putraḥ putrawadyaśca wartate pitṛmātṛṣu ||18||

yadunāhamawajñātastathā turwasunāpi ca |
druhyunā cānunā caiwa mayyawajñā kṛtā bhṛśam ||19||

pūruṇā me kṛtaṃ wākyaṃ mānitaśca wiśeṣataḥ |
