kanīyānmama dāyādo jarā yena dhṛtā mama ||20||

mama kāmaḥ sa ca kṛtaḥ pūruṇā putrarūpiṇā ||20||

śukreṇa ca waro dattaḥ kāwyenośanasā swayam |
putro yastwānuwarteta sa rājā pṛthiwīpatiḥ ||21||

bhawato'nunayāmyewaṃ pūrū rājye'bhiṣicyatām ||21||

prakṛtaya ūcuḥ||

yaḥ putro guṇasampanno mātāpitrorhitaḥ sadā |
sarwamarhati kalyāṇaṃ kanīyānapi sa prabho ||22||

arhaḥ pūruridaṃ rājyaṃ yaḥ sutaḥ priyakṛttawa |
waradānena śukrasya na śakyaṃ waktumuttaram ||23||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

paurajānapadaistuṣṭairityukto nāhuṣastadā |
abhyaṣiñcattataḥ pūruṃ rājye swe sutamātmajam ||24||

dattwā ca pūrawe rājyaṃ wanawāsāya dīkṣitaḥ |
purātsa niryayau rājā brāhmaṇaistāpasaiḥ saha ||25||

yadostu yādawā jātāsturwasoryawanāḥ sutāḥ |
druhyorapi sutā bhojā anostu mlecchajātayaḥ ||26||

pūrostu paurawo waṃśo yatra jāto'si pārthiwa |
idaṃ warṣasahasrāya rājyaṃ kārayituṃ waśī ||27||






              uttarayāyātam
                  81


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ sa nāhuṣo rājā yayātiḥ putramīpsitam |
rājye'bhiṣicya mudito wānaprastho'bhawanmuniḥ ||1||

uṣitwā ca wane wāsaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha saṃśritaḥ |
phalamūlāśano dānto yathā swargamito gataḥ ||2||

sa gataḥ surawāsaṃ taṃ niwasanmuditaḥ sukham |
kālasya nātimahataḥ punaḥ śakreṇa pātitaḥ ||3||

nipatanpracyutaḥ swargādaprāpto medinītalam |
sthita āsīdantarikṣe sa tadeti śrutaṃ mayā ||4||

tata ewa punaścāpi gataḥ swargamiti śrutiḥ |
rājñā wasumatā sārdhamaṣṭakena ca wīryawān ||5||

pratardanena śibinā sametya kila saṃsadi ||5||

janamejaya uwāca||

karmaṇā kena sa diwaṃ punaḥ prāpto mahīpatiḥ |
sarwametadaśeṣeṇa śrotumicchāmi tattwataḥ ||6||

kathyamānaṃ twayā wipra wiprarṣigaṇasaṃnidhau ||6||

dewarājasamo hyāsīdyayātiḥ pṛthiwīpatiḥ |
wardhanaḥ kuruwaṃśasya wibhāwasusamadyutiḥ ||7||

tasya wistīrṇayaśasaḥ satyakīrtermahātmanaḥ |
caritaṃ śrotumicchāmi diwi ceha ca sarwaśaḥ ||8||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi yayāteruttarāṃ kathām |
diwi ceha ca puṇyārthāṃ sarwapāpapraṇāśinīm ||9||

yayātirnāhuṣo rājā pūruṃ putraṃ kanīyasam |
rājye'bhiṣicya muditaḥ prawawrāja wanaṃ tadā ||10||

anteṣu sa winikṣipya putrānyadupurogamān |
phalamūlāśano rājā wane saṃnyawasacciram ||11||

saṃśitātmā jitakrodhastarpayanpitṛdewatāḥ |
agnīṃśca widhiwajjuhwanwānaprasthawidhānataḥ ||12||

atithīnpūjayāmāsa wanyena hawiṣā wibhuḥ |
śiloñchawṛttimāsthāya śeṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ ||13||

pūrṇaṃ warṣasahasraṃ sa ewaṃwṛttirabhūnnṛpaḥ |
abbhakṣaḥ śaradastriṃśadāsīnniyatawāṅmanāḥ ||14||

tataśca wāyubhakṣo'bhūtsaṃwatsaramatandritaḥ |
pañcāgnimadhye ca tapastepe saṃwatsaraṃ nṛpaḥ ||15||

ekapādasthitaścāsītṣaṇmāsānanilāśanaḥ |
puṇyakīrtistataḥ swargaṃ jagāmāwṛtya rodasī ||16||






                  82


waiśampāyana uwāca||

swargataḥ sa tu rājendro niwasandewasadmani |
pūjitastridaśaiḥ sādhyairmarudbhirwasubhistathā ||1||

dewalokādbrahmalokaṃ sañcaranpuṇyakṛdwaśī |
awasatpṛthiwīpālo dīrghakālamiti śrutiḥ ||2||

sa kadācinnṛpaśreṣṭho yayātiḥ śakramāgamat |
kathānte tatra śakreṇa pṛṣṭaḥ sa pṛthiwīpatiḥ ||3||

śakra uwāca||

yadā sa pūrustawa rūpeṇa rāja; ñjarāṃ gṛhītwā pracacāra bhūmau |
tadā rājyaṃ sampradāyaiwa tasmai; twayā kimuktaḥ kathayeha satyam ||4||

yayātiruwāca||

gaṅgāyamunayormadhye kṛtsno'yaṃ wiṣayastawa |
madhye pṛthiwyāstwaṃ rājā bhrātaro'ntyādhipāstawa ||5||

akrodhanaḥ krodhanebhyo wiśiṣṭa; stathā titikṣuratitikṣorwiśiṣṭaḥ |
amānuṣebhyo mānuṣāśca pradhānā; widwāṃstathaiwāwiduṣaḥ pradhānaḥ ||6||

ākruśyamāno nākrośenmanyurewa titikṣataḥ |
ākroṣṭāraṃ nirdahati sukṛtaṃ cāsya windati ||7||

nāruntudaḥ syānna nṛśaṃsawādī; na hīnataḥ paramabhyādadīta |
yayāsya wācā para udwijeta; na tāṃ wadedruśatīṃ pāpalokyām ||8||

aruntudaṃ puruṣaṃ rūkṣawācaṃ; wākkaṇṭakairwitudantaṃ manuṣyān |
widyādalakṣmīkatamaṃ janānāṃ; mukhe nibaddhāṃ nirṛtiṃ wahantam ||9||

sadbhiḥ purastādabhipūjitaḥ syā; tsadbhistathā pṛṣṭhato rakṣitaḥ syāt |
sadāsatāmatiwādāṃstitikṣe; tsatāṃ wṛttaṃ cādadītāryawṛttaḥ ||10||

wāksāyakā wadanānniṣpatanti; yairāhataḥ śocati rātryahāni |
parasya wā marmasu ye patanti; tānpaṇḍito nāwasṛjetpareṣu ||11||

na hīdṛśaṃ saṃwananaṃ triṣu lokeṣu widyate |
yathā maitrī ca bhūteṣu dānaṃ ca madhurā ca wāk ||12||

tasmātsāntwaṃ sadā wācyaṃ na wācyaṃ paruṣaṃ kwacit |
pūjyānsampūjayeddadyānna ca yācetkadācana ||13||






                  83


indra uwāca||

sarwāṇi karmāṇi samāpya rāja; ngṛhānparityajya wanaṃ gato'si |
tattwāṃ pṛcchāmi nahuṣasya putra; kenāsi tulyastapasā yayāte ||1||

yayātiruwāca||

nāhaṃ dewamanuṣyeṣu na gandharwamaharṣiṣu |
ātmanastapasā tulyaṃ kañcitpaśyāmi wāsawa ||2||

indra uwāca||

yadāwamaṃsthāḥ sadṛśaḥ śreyasaśca; pāpīyasaścāwiditaprabhāwaḥ |
tasmāllokā antawantastaweme; kṣīṇe puṇye patitāsyadya rājan ||3||

yayātiruwāca||

surarṣigandharwanarāwamānā; tkṣayaṃ gatā me yadi śakra lokāḥ |
iccheyaṃ wai suralokādwihīnaḥ; satāṃ madhye patituṃ dewarāja ||4||

indra uwāca||

satāṃ sakāśe patitāsi rājaṃ; ścyutaḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ yatra labdhāsi bhūyaḥ |
ewaṃ widitwā tu punaryayāte; na te'wamānyāḥ sadṛśaḥ śreyasaśca ||5||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ prahāyāmararājajuṣṭā; npuṇyāṃllokānpatamānaṃ yayātim |
samprekṣya rājarṣiwaro'ṣṭakasta; muwāca saddharmawidhānagoptā ||6||

kastwaṃ yuwā wāsawatulyarūpaḥ; swatejasā dīpyamāno yathāgniḥ |
patasyudīrṇāmbudharāndhakārā; tkhātkhecarāṇāṃ prawaro yathārkaḥ ||7||

dṛṣṭwā ca twāṃ sūryapathātpatantaṃ; waiśwānarārkadyutimaprameyam |
kiṃ nu swidetatpatatīti sarwe; witarkayantaḥ parimohitāḥ smaḥ ||8||

dṛṣṭwā ca twāṃ wiṣṭhitaṃ dewamārge; śakrārkawiṣṇupratimaprabhāwam |
abhyudgatāstwāṃ wayamadya sarwe; tattwaṃ pāte tawa jijñāsamānāḥ ||9||

na cāpi twāṃ dhṛṣṇumaḥ praṣṭumagre; na ca twamasmānpṛcchasi ye wayaṃ smaḥ |
tattwāṃ pṛcchāmaḥ spṛhaṇīyarūpaṃ; kasya twaṃ wā kiṃnimittaṃ twamāgāḥ ||10||

bhayaṃ tu te wyetu wiṣādamohau; tyajāśu dewendrasamānarūpa |
twāṃ wartamānaṃ hi satāṃ sakāśe; nālaṃ prasoḍhuṃ balahāpi śakraḥ ||11||

santaḥ pratiṣṭhā hi sukhacyutānāṃ; satāṃ sadaiwāmararājakalpa |
te saṅgatāḥ sthāwarajaṅgameśāḥ; pratiṣṭhitastwaṃ sadṛśeṣu satsu ||12||

prabhuragniḥ pratapane bhūmirāwapane prabhuḥ |
prabhuḥ sūryaḥ prakāśitwe satāṃ cābhyāgataḥ prabhuḥ ||13||






                  84


yayātiruwāca||

ahaṃ yayātirnahuṣasya putraḥ; pūroḥ pitā sarwabhūtāwamānāt |
prabhraṃśitaḥ surasiddharṣilokā; tparicyutaḥ prapatāmyalpapuṇyaḥ ||1||

ahaṃ hi pūrwo wayasā bhawadbhya; stenābhiwādaṃ bhawatāṃ na prayuñje |
yo widyayā tapasā janmanā wā; wṛddhaḥ sa pūjyo bhawati dwijānām ||2||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

awādīścedwayasā yaḥ sa wṛddha; iti rājannābhyawadaḥ kathañcit |
yo wai widwānwayasā sansma wṛddhaḥ; sa ewa pūjyo bhawati dwijānām ||3||

yayātiruwāca||

pratikūlaṃ karmaṇāṃ pāpamāhu; stadwartate'prawaṇe pāpalokyam |
santo'satāṃ nānuwartanti caita; dyathā ātmaiṣāmanukūlawādī ||4||

abhūddhanaṃ me wipulaṃ mahadwai; wiceṣṭamāno nādhigantā tadasmi |
ewaṃ pradhāryātmahite niwiṣṭo; yo wartate sa wijānāti jīwan ||5||

nānābhāwā bahawo jīwaloke; daiwādhīnā naṣṭaceṣṭādhikārāḥ |
tattatprāpya na wihanyeta dhīro; diṣṭaṃ balīya iti matwātmabuddhyā ||6||

sukhaṃ hi janturyadi wāpi duḥkhaṃ; daiwādhīnaṃ windati nātmaśaktyā |
tasmāddiṣṭaṃ balawanmanyamāno; na sañjwarennāpi hṛṣyetkadācit ||7||

duḥkhe na tapyenna sukhena hṛṣye; tsamena warteta sadaiwa dhīraḥ |
diṣṭaṃ balīya iti manyamāno; na sañjwarennāpi hṛṣyetkadācit ||8||

bhaye na muhyāmyaṣṭakāhaṃ kadā ci; tsantāpo me mānaso nāsti kaścit |
dhātā yathā māṃ widadhāti loke; dhruwaṃ tathāhaṃ bhawiteti matwā ||9||

saṃswedajā aṇḍajā udbhidāśca; sarīsṛpāḥ kṛmayo'thāpsu matsyāḥ |
tathāśmānastṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca sarwaṃ; diṣṭakṣaye swāṃ prakṛtiṃ bhajante ||10||

anityatāṃ sukhaduḥkhasya buddhwā; kasmātsantāpamaṣṭakāhaṃ bhajeyam |
kiṃ kuryāṃ wai kiṃ ca kṛtwā na tapye; tasmātsantāpaṃ warjayāmyapramattaḥ ||11||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

ye ye lokāḥ pārthiwendra pradhānā; stwayā bhuktā yaṃ ca kālaṃ yathā ca |
tanme rājanbrūhi sarwaṃ yathāwa; tkṣetrajñawadbhāṣase twaṃ hi dharmān ||12||

yayātiruwāca||

rājāhamāsamiha sārwabhauma; stato lokānmahato ajayaṃ wai |
tatrāwasaṃ warṣasahasramātraṃ; tato lokaṃ paramasmyabhyupetaḥ ||13||

tataḥ purīṃ puruhūtasya ramyāṃ; sahasradwārāṃ śatayojanāyatām |
adhyāwasaṃ warṣasahasramātraṃ; tato lokaṃ paramasmyabhyupetaḥ ||14||

tato diwyamajaraṃ prāpya lokaṃ; prajāpaterlokapaterdurāpam |
tatrāwasaṃ warṣasahasramātraṃ; tato lokaṃ paramasmyabhyupetaḥ ||15||

dewasya dewasya niweśane ca; wijitya lokānawasaṃ yatheṣṭam |
sampūjyamānastridaśaiḥ samastai; stulyaprabhāwadyutirīśwarāṇām ||16||

tathāwasaṃ nandane kāmarūpī; saṃwatsarāṇāmayutaṃ śatānām |
sahāpsarobhirwiharanpuṇyagandhā; npaśyannagānpuṣpitāṃścārurūpān ||17||

tatrasthaṃ māṃ dewasukheṣu saktaṃ; kāle'tīte mahati tato'timātram |
dūto dewānāmabrawīdugrarūpo; dhwaṃsetyuccaistriḥ plutena swareṇa ||18||

etāwanme widitaṃ rājasiṃha; tato bhraṣṭo'haṃ nandanātkṣīṇapuṇyaḥ |
wāco'śrauṣaṃ cāntarikṣe surāṇā; manukrośācchocatāṃ mānawendra ||19||

aho kaṣṭaṃ kṣīṇapuṇyo yayātiḥ; patatyasau puṇyakṛtpuṇyakīrtiḥ |
tānabruwaṃ patamānastato'haṃ; satāṃ madhye nipateyaṃ kathaṃ nu ||20||

tairākhyātā bhawatāṃ yajñabhūmiḥ; samīkṣya caināṃ twaritamupāgato'smi |
hawirgandhaṃ deśikaṃ yajñabhūme; rdhūmāpāṅgaṃ pratigṛhya pratītaḥ ||21||






                  85


aṣṭaka uwāca||

yadāwaso nandane kāmarūpī; saṃwatsarāṇāmayutaṃ śatānām |
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ kārtayugapradhāna; hitwā tattwaṃ wasudhāmanwapadyaḥ ||1||

yayātiruwāca||

jñātiḥ suhṛtswajano yo yatheha; kṣīṇe witte tyajyate mānawairhi |
tathā tatra kṣīṇapuṇyaṃ manuṣyaṃ; tyajanti sadyaḥ seśwarā dewasaṅghāḥ ||2||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

kathaṃ tasminkṣīṇapuṇyā bhawanti; saṃmuhyate me'tra mano'timātram |
kiṃwiśiṣṭāḥ kasya dhāmopayānti; tadwai brūhi kṣetrawittwaṃ mato me ||3||

yayātiruwāca||

imaṃ bhaumaṃ narakaṃ te patanti; lālapyamānā naradewa sarwe |
te kaṅkagomāyubalāśanārthaṃ; kṣīṇā wiwṛddhiṃ bahudhā wrajanti ||4||

tasmādetadwarjanīyaṃ nareṇa; duṣṭaṃ loke garhaṇīyaṃ ca karma |
ākhyātaṃ te pārthiwa sarwameta; dbhūyaścedānīṃ wada kiṃ te wadāmi ||5||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

yadā tu tānwitudante wayāṃsi; tathā gṛdhrāḥ śitikaṇṭhāḥ pataṅgāḥ |
kathaṃ bhawanti kathamābhawanti; na bhaumamanyaṃ narakaṃ śṛṇomi ||6||

yayātiruwāca||

ūrdhwaṃ dehātkarmaṇo jṛmbhamāṇā; dwyaktaṃ pṛthiwyāmanusañcaranti |
imaṃ bhaumaṃ narakaṃ te patanti; nāwekṣante warṣapūgānanekān ||7||

ṣaṣṭiṃ sahasrāṇi patanti wyomni; tathā aśītiṃ pariwatsarāṇi |
tānwai tudanti prapatataḥ prapātaṃ; bhīmā bhaumā rākṣasāstīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāḥ ||8||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

yadenasaste patatastudanti; bhīmā bhaumā rākṣasāstīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāḥ |
kathaṃ bhawanti kathamābhawanti; kathambhūtā garbhabhūtā bhawanti ||9||

yayātiruwāca||

asraṃ retaḥ puṣpaphalānupṛkta; manweti tadwai puruṣeṇa sṛṣṭam |
sa wai tasyā raja āpadyate wai; sa garbhabhūtaḥ samupaiti tatra ||10||

wanaspatīṃścauṣadhīścāwiśanti; apo wāyuṃ pṛthiwīṃ cāntarikṣam |
catuṣpadaṃ dwipadaṃ cāpi sarwa; mewambhūtā garbhabhūtā bhawanti ||11||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

anyadwapurwidadhātīha garbha; utāho switswena kāmena yāti |
āpadyamāno narayonimetā; mācakṣwa me saṃśayātprabrawīmi ||12||

śarīradehādisamucchrayaṃ ca; cakṣuḥśrotre labhate kena sañjñām |
etattattwaṃ sarwamācakṣwa pṛṣṭaḥ; kṣetrajñaṃ twāṃ tāta manyāma sarwe ||13||

yayātiruwāca||

wāyuḥ samutkarṣati garbhayoni; mṛtau retaḥ puṣparasānupṛktam |
sa tatra tanmātrakṛtādhikāraḥ; krameṇa saṃwardhayatīha garbham ||14||

sa jāyamāno wigṛhītagātraḥ; ṣaḍjñānaniṣṭhāyatano manuṣyaḥ |
sa śrotrābhyāṃ wedayatīha śabdaṃ; sarwaṃ rūpaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā ca ||15||

ghrāṇena gandhaṃ jihwayātho rasaṃ ca; twacā sparśaṃ manasā weda bhāwam |
ityaṣṭakehopacitiṃ ca widdhi; mahātmanaḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ śarīre ||16||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

yaḥ saṃsthitaḥ puruṣo dahyate wā; nikhanyate wāpi nighṛṣyate wā |
abhāwabhūtaḥ sa wināśametya; kenātmānaṃ cetayate purastāt ||17||

yayātiruwāca||

hitwā so'sūnsuptawanniṣṭanitwā; purodhāya sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ ca |
anyāṃ yoniṃ pawanāgrānusārī; hitwā dehaṃ bhajate rājasiṃha ||18||

puṇyāṃ yoniṃ puṇyakṛto wrajanti; pāpāṃ yoniṃ pāpakṛto wrajanti |
kīṭāḥ pataṅgāśca bhawanti pāpā; na me wiwakṣāsti mahānubhāwa ||19||

catuṣpadā dwipadāḥ ṣaṭpadāśca; tathābhūtā garbhabhūtā bhawanti |
ākhyātametannikhilena sarwaṃ; bhūyastu kiṃ pṛcchasi rājasiṃha ||20||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

kiṃ switkṛtwā labhate tāta lokā; nmartyaḥ śreṣṭhāṃstapasā widyayā wā |
tanme pṛṣṭaḥ śaṃsa sarwaṃ yathāwa; cchubhāṃllokānyena gacchetkrameṇa ||21||

yayātiruwāca||

tapaśca dānaṃ ca śamo damaśca; hrīrārjawaṃ sarwabhūtānukampā |
naśyanti mānena tamo'bhibhūtāḥ; puṃsaḥ sadaiweti wadanti santaḥ ||22||

adhīyānaḥ paṇḍitaṃ manyamāno; yo widyayā hanti yaśaḥ pareṣām |
tasyāntawantaśca bhawanti lokā; na cāsya tadbrahma phalaṃ dadāti ||23||

catwāri karmāṇyabhayaṅkarāṇi; bhayaṃ prayacchantyayathākṛtāni |
mānāgnihotramuta mānamaunaṃ; mānenādhītamuta mānayajñaḥ ||24||

na mānyamāno mudamādadīta; na santāpaṃ prāpnuyāccāwamānāt |
santaḥ sataḥ pūjayantīha loke; nāsādhawaḥ sādhubuddhiṃ labhante ||25||

iti dadyāditi yajedityadhīyīta me wratam |
ityasminnabhayānyāhustāni warjyāni nityaśaḥ ||26||

yenāśrayaṃ wedayante purāṇaṃ; manīṣiṇo mānasamānabhaktam |
tanniḥśreyastaijasaṃ rūpametya; parāṃ śāntiṃ prāpnuyuḥ pretya ceha ||27||






                  86


aṣṭaka uwāca||

carangṛhasthaḥ kathameti dewā; nkathaṃ bhikṣuḥ kathamācāryakarmā |
wānaprasthaḥ satpathe saṃniwiṣṭo; bahūnyasminsamprati wedayanti ||1||

yayātiruwāca||

āhūtādhyāyī gurukarmaswacodyaḥ; pūrwotthāyī caramaṃ copaśāyī |
mṛdurdānto dhṛtimānapramattaḥ; swādhyāyaśīlaḥ sidhyati brahmacārī ||2||

dharmāgataṃ prāpya dhanaṃ yajeta; dadyātsadaiwātithīnbhojayecca |
anādadānaśca parairadattaṃ; saiṣā gṛhasthopaniṣatpurāṇī ||3||

swawīryajīwī wṛjinānniwṛtto; dātā parebhyo na paropatāpī |
tādṛṅmuniḥ siddhimupaiti mukhyāṃ; wasannaraṇye niyatāhāraceṣṭaḥ ||4||

aśilpajīwī nagṛhaśca nityaṃ; jitendriyaḥ sarwato wipramuktaḥ |
anokasārī laghuralpacāra; ścarandeśānekacaraḥ sa bhikṣuḥ ||5||

rātryā yayā cābhijitāśca lokā; bhawanti kāmā wijitāḥ sukhāśca |
tāmewa rātriṃ prayateta widwā; naraṇyasaṃstho bhawituṃ yatātmā ||6||

daśaiwa pūrwāndaśa cāparāṃstu; jñātīnsahātmānamathaikawiṃśam |
araṇyawāsī sukṛte dadhāti; wimucyāraṇye swaśarīradhātūn ||7||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

kati swidewa munayo maunāni kati cāpyuta |
bhawantīti tadācakṣwa śrotumicchāmahe wayam ||8||

yayātiruwāca||

araṇye wasato yasya grāmo bhawati pṛṣṭhataḥ |
grāme wā wasato'raṇyaṃ sa muniḥ syājjanādhipa ||9||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

kathaṃ swidwasato'raṇye grāmo bhawati pṛṣṭhataḥ |
grāme wā wasato'raṇyaṃ kathaṃ bhawati pṛṣṭhataḥ ||10||

yayātiruwāca||

na grāmyamupayuñjīta ya āraṇyo munirbhawet |
tathāsya wasato'raṇye grāmo bhawati pṛṣṭhataḥ ||11||

anagniraniketaśca agotracaraṇo muniḥ |
kaupīnācchādanaṃ yāwattāwadicchecca cīwaram ||12||

yāwatprāṇābhisandhānaṃ tāwadicchecca bhojanam |
tathāsya wasato grāme'raṇyaṃ bhawati pṛṣṭhataḥ ||13||

yastu kāmānparityajya tyaktakarmā jitendriyaḥ |
ātiṣṭheta munirmaunaṃ sa loke siddhimāpnuyāt ||14||

dhautadantaṃ kṛttanakhaṃ sadā snātamalaṅkṛtam |
asitaṃ sitakarmasthaṃ kastaṃ nārcitumarhati ||15||

tapasā karśitaḥ kṣāmaḥ kṣīṇamāṃsāsthiśoṇitaḥ |
yadā bhawati nirdwandwo munirmaunaṃ samāsthitaḥ ||16||

atha lokamimaṃ jitwā lokaṃ wijayate param ||16||

āsyena tu yadāhāraṃ gowanmṛgayate muniḥ |
athāsya lokaḥ pūrwo yaḥ so'mṛtatwāya kalpate ||17||






                  87


aṣṭaka uwāca||

katarastwetayoḥ pūrwaṃ dewānāmeti sātmyatām |
ubhayordhāwato rājansūryācandramasoriwa ||1||

yayātiruwāca||

aniketo gṛhastheṣu kāmawṛtteṣu saṃyataḥ |
grāma ewa wasanbhikṣustayoḥ pūrwataraṃ gataḥ ||2||

aprāpya dīrghamāyustu yaḥ prāpto wikṛtiṃ caret |
tapyeta yadi tatkṛtwā caretso'nyattatastapaḥ ||3||

yadwai nṛśaṃsaṃ tadapathyamāhu; ryaḥ sewate dharmamanarthabuddhiḥ |
aswo'pyanīśaśca tathaiwa rājaṃ; stadārjawaṃ sa samādhistadāryam ||4||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

kenāsi dūtaḥ prahito'dya rāja; nyuwā sragwī darśanīyaḥ suwarcāḥ |
kuta āgataḥ katarasyāṃ diśi twa; mutāho switpārthiwaṃ sthānamasti ||5||

yayātiruwāca||

imaṃ bhaumaṃ narakaṃ kṣīṇapuṇyaḥ; praweṣṭumurwīṃ gaganādwiprakīrṇaḥ |
uktwāhaṃ waḥ prapatiṣyāmyanantaraṃ; twaranti māṃ brāhmaṇā lokapālāḥ ||6||

satāṃ sakāśe tu wṛtaḥ prapāta; ste saṅgatā guṇawantaśca sarwe |
śakrācca labdho hi waro mayaiṣa; patiṣyatā bhūmitale narendra ||7||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

pṛcchāmi twāṃ mā prapata prapātaṃ; yadi lokāḥ pārthiwa santi me'tra |
yadyantarikṣe yadi wā diwi śritāḥ; kṣetrajñaṃ twāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ||8||

yayātiruwāca||

yāwatpṛthiwyāṃ wihitaṃ gawāśwaṃ; sahāraṇyaiḥ paśubhiḥ parwataiśca |
tāwallokā diwi te saṃsthitā wai; tathā wijānīhi narendrasiṃha ||9||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

tāṃste dadāmi mā prapata prapātaṃ; ye me lokā diwi rājendra santi |
yadyantarikṣe yadi wā diwi śritā; stānākrama kṣipramamitrasāha ||10||

yayātiruwāca||

nāsmadwidho'brāhmaṇo brahmawicca; pratigrahe wartate rājamukhya |
yathā pradeyaṃ satataṃ dwijebhya; stathādadaṃ pūrwamahaṃ narendra ||11||

nābrāhmaṇaḥ kṛpaṇo jātu jīwe; dyā cāpi syādbrāhmaṇī wīrapatnī |
so'haṃ yadaiwākṛtapūrwaṃ careyaṃ; wiwitsamānaḥ kimu tatra sādhu ||12||

pratardana uwāca||

pṛcchāmi twāṃ spṛhaṇīyarūpa; pratardano'haṃ yadi me santi lokāḥ |
yadyantarikṣe yadi wā diwi śritāḥ; kṣetrajñaṃ twāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ||13||

yayātiruwāca||

santi lokā bahawaste narendra; apyekaikaḥ sapta saptāpyahāni |
madhucyuto ghṛtapṛktā wiśokā; ste nāntawantaḥ pratipālayanti ||14||

pratardana uwāca||

tāṃste dadāmi mā prapata prapātaṃ; ye me lokāstawa te wai bhawantu |
yadyantarikṣe yadi wā diwi śritā; stānākrama kṣipramapetamohaḥ ||15||

yayātiruwāca||

na tulyatejāḥ sukṛtaṃ kāmayeta; yogakṣemaṃ pārthiwa pārthiwaḥ san |
daiwādeśādāpadaṃ prāpya widwāṃ; ścarennṛśaṃsaṃ na hi jātu rājā ||16||

dharmyaṃ mārgaṃ cetayāno yaśasyaṃ; kuryānnṛpo dharmamawekṣamāṇaḥ |
na madwidho dharmabuddhiḥ prajāna; nkuryādewaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ māṃ yathāttha ||17||

kuryāmapūrwaṃ na kṛtaṃ yadanyai; rwiwitsamānaḥ kimu tatra sādhu |
bruwāṇamewaṃ nṛpatiṃ yayātiṃ; nṛpottamo wasumanābrawīttam ||18||






                  88


wasumanā uwāca||

pṛcchāmi twāṃ wasumanā rauśadaświ; ryadyasti loko diwi mahyaṃ narendra |
yadyantarikṣe prathito mahātma; nkṣetrajñaṃ twāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ||1||

yayātiruwāca||

yadantarikṣaṃ pṛthiwī diśaśca; yattejasā tapate bhānumāṃśca |
lokāstāwanto diwi saṃsthitā wai; te nāntawantaḥ pratipālayanti ||2||

wasumanā uwāca||

tāṃste dadāmi pata mā prapātaṃ; ye me lokāstawa te wai bhawantu |
krīṇīṣwaināṃstṛṇakenāpi rāja; npratigrahaste yadi samyakpraduṣṭaḥ ||3||

yayātiruwāca||

na mithyāhaṃ wikrayaṃ wai smarāmi; wṛthā gṛhītaṃ śiśukācchaṅkamānaḥ |
kuryāṃ na caiwākṛtapūrwamanyai; rwiwitsamānaḥ kimu tatra sādhu ||4||

wasumanā uwāca||

tāṃstwaṃ lokānpratipadyaswa rāja; nmayā dattānyadi neṣṭaḥ krayaste |
ahaṃ na tānwai pratigantā narendra; sarwe lokāstawa te wai bhawantu ||5||

śibiruwāca||

pṛcchāmi twāṃ śibirauśīnaro'haṃ; mamāpi lokā yadi santīha tāta |
yadyantarikṣe yadi wā diwi śritāḥ; kṣetrajñaṃ twāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ||6||

yayātiruwāca||

na twaṃ wācā hṛdayenāpi widwa; nparīpsamānānnāwamaṃsthā narendra |
tenānantā diwi lokāḥ śritāste; widyudrūpāḥ swanawanto mahāntaḥ ||7||

śibiruwāca||

tāṃstwaṃ lokānpratipadyaswa rāja; nmayā dattānyadi neṣṭaḥ krayaste |
na cāhaṃ tānpratipatsyeha dattwā; yatra gatwā twamupāsse ha lokān ||8||

yayātiruwāca||

yathā twamindrapratimaprabhāwa; ste cāpyanantā naradewa lokāḥ |
tathādya loke na rame'nyadatte; tasmācchibe nābhinandāmi dāyam ||9||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

na cedekaikaśo rājaṃllokānnaḥ pratinandasi |
sarwe pradāya bhawate gantāro narakaṃ wayam ||10||

yayātiruwāca||

yadarhāya dadadhwaṃ tatsantaḥ satyānṛśaṃsyataḥ |
ahaṃ tu nābhidhṛṣṇomi yatkṛtaṃ na mayā purā ||11||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

kasyaite pratidṛśyante rathāḥ pañca hiraṇmayāḥ |
uccaiḥ santaḥ prakāśante jwalanto'gniśikhā iwa ||12||

yayātiruwāca||

yuṣmānete hi wakṣyanti rathāḥ pañca hiraṇmayāḥ |
uccaiḥ santaḥ prakāśante jwalanto'gniśikhā iwa ||13||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

ātiṣṭhaswa rathaṃ rājanwikramaswa wihāyasā |
wayamapyanuyāsyāmo yadā kālo bhawiṣyati ||14||

yayātiruwāca||

sarwairidānīṃ gantawyaṃ sahaswargajito wayam |
eṣa no wirajāḥ panthā dṛśyate dewasadmanaḥ ||15||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

te'dhiruhya rathānsarwe prayātā nṛpasattamāḥ |
ākramanto diwaṃ bhābhirdharmeṇāwṛtya rodasī ||16||

aṣṭaka uwāca||

ahaṃ manye pūrwameko'smi gantā; sakhā cendraḥ sarwathā me mahātmā |
kasmādewaṃ śibirauśīnaro'ya; meko'tyagātsarwawegena wāhān ||17||

yayātiruwāca||

adadāddewayānāya yāwadwittamawindata |
uśīnarasya putro'yaṃ tasmācchreṣṭho hi naḥ śibiḥ ||18||

dānaṃ tapaḥ satyamathāpi dharmo; hrīḥ śrīḥ kṣamā saumya tathā titikṣā |
rājannetānyapratimasya rājñaḥ; śibeḥ sthitānyanṛśaṃsasya buddhyā ||19||

ewaṃwṛtto hrīniṣedhaśca yasmā; ttasmācchibiratyagādwai rathena ||19||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

athāṣṭakaḥ punarewānwapṛccha; nmātāmahaṃ kautukādindrakalpam |
pṛcchāmi twāṃ nṛpate brūhi satyaṃ; kutaśca kasyāsi sutaśca kasya ||20||

kṛtaṃ twayā yaddhi na tasya kartā; loke twadanyaḥ kṣatriyo brāhmaṇo wā ||20||

yayātiruwāca||

yayātirasmi nahuṣasya putraḥ; pūroḥ pitā sārwabhaumastwihāsam |
guhyamarthaṃ māmakebhyo brawīmi; mātāmaho'haṃ bhawatāṃ prakāśaḥ ||21||

sarwāmimāṃ pṛthiwīṃ nirjigāya; prasthe baddhwā hyadadaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ |
medhyānaśwānekaśaphānsurūpāṃ; stadā dewāḥ puṇyabhājo bhawanti ||22||

adāmahaṃ pṛthiwīṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ; pūrṇāmimāmakhilāṃ wāhanasya |
gobhiḥ suwarṇena dhanaiśca mukhyai; statrāsangāḥ śatamarbudāni ||23||

satyena me dyauśca wasundharā ca; tathaiwāgnirjwalate mānuṣeṣu |
na me wṛthā wyāhṛtamewa wākyaṃ; satyaṃ hi santaḥ pratipūjayanti ||24||

sarwe ca dewā munayaśca lokāḥ; satyena pūjyā iti me manogatam ||24||

yo naḥ swargajitaḥ sarwānyathāwṛttaṃ niwedayet |
anasūyurdwijāgrebhyaḥ sa labhennaḥ salokatām ||25||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ rājā sa mahātmā hyatīwa; swairdauhitraistārito'mitrasāhaḥ |
tyaktwā mahīṃ paramodārakarmā; swargaṃ gataḥ karmabhirwyāpya pṛthwīm ||26||






              saṃbhawaparwa
                  89


janamejaya uwāca||

bhagawañśrotumicchāmi pūrorwaṃśakarānnṛpān |
yadwīryā yādṛśāścaiwa yāwanto yatparākramāḥ ||1||

na hyasmiñśīlahīno wā nirwīryo wā narādhipaḥ |
prajāwirahito wāpi bhūtapūrwaḥ kadācana ||2||

teṣāṃ prathitawṛttānāṃ rājñāṃ wijñānaśālinām |
caritaṃ śrotumicchāmi wistareṇa tapodhana ||3||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi yanmāṃ twaṃ paripṛcchasi |
pūrorwaṃśadharānwīrāñśakrapratimatejasaḥ ||4||

prawīreśwararaudrāśwāstrayaḥ putrā mahārathāḥ |
pūroḥ pauṣṭyāmajāyanta prawīrastatra waṃśakṛt ||5||

manasyurabhawattasmācchūraḥ śyenīsutaḥ prabhuḥ |
pṛthiwyāścaturantāyā goptā rājīwalocanaḥ ||6||

subhrūḥ saṃhanano wāgmī sauwīrītanayāstrayaḥ |
manasyorabhawanputrāḥ śūrāḥ sarwe mahārathāḥ ||7||

raudrāśwasya maheṣwāsā daśāpsarasi sūnawaḥ |
yajwāno jajñire śūrāḥ prajāwanto bahuśrutāḥ ||8||

sarwe sarwāstrawidwāṃsaḥ sarwe dharmaparāyaṇāḥ ||8||

ṛcepuratha kakṣepuḥ kṛkaṇepuśca wīryawān |
sthaṇḍilepurwanepuśca sthalepuśca mahārathaḥ ||9||

tejepurbalawāndhīmānsatyepuścendrawikramaḥ |
dharmepuḥ saṃnatepuśca daśamo dewawikramaḥ ||10||

anādhṛṣṭisutāstāta rājasūyāśwamedhinaḥ ||10||

matinārastato rājā widwāṃścarceputo'bhawat |
matinārasutā rājaṃścatwāro'mitawikramāḥ ||11||

taṃsurmahānatiratho druhyuścāpratimadyutiḥ ||11||

teṣāṃ taṃsurmahāwīryaḥ paurawaṃ waṃśamudwahan |
ājahāra yaśo dīptaṃ jigāya ca wasundharām ||12||

ilinaṃ tu sutaṃ taṃsurjanayāmāsa wīryawān |
so'pi kṛtsnāmimāṃ bhūmiṃ wijigye jayatāṃ waraḥ ||13||

rathantaryāṃ sutānpañca pañcabhūtopamāṃstataḥ |
ilino janayāmāsa duḥṣantaprabhṛtīnnṛpa ||14||

duḥṣantaṃ śūrabhīmau ca prapūrwaṃ wasumewa ca |
teṣāṃ jyeṣṭho'bhawadrājā duḥṣanto janamejaya ||15||

duḥṣantādbharato jajñe widwāñśākuntalo nṛpaḥ |
tasmādbharatawaṃśasya wipratasthe mahadyaśaḥ ||16||

bharatastisṛṣu strīṣu nawa putrānajījanat |
nābhyanandanta tānrājā nānurūpā mametyuta ||17||

tato mahadbhiḥ kratubhirījāno bharatastadā |
lebhe putraṃ bharadwājādbhumanyuṃ nāma bhārata ||18||

tataḥ putriṇamātmānaṃ jñātwā paurawanandanaḥ |
bhumanyuṃ bharataśreṣṭha yauwarājye'bhyaṣecayat ||19||

tatastasya mahīndrasya witathaḥ putrako'bhawat |
tataḥ sa witatho nāma bhumanyorabhawatsutaḥ ||20||

suhotraśca suhotā ca suhawiḥ suyajustathā |
puṣkariṇyāmṛcīkasya bhumanyorabhawansutāḥ ||21||

teṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ suhotrastu rājyamāpa mahīkṣitām |
rājasūyāśwamedhādyaiḥ so'yajadbahubhiḥ sawaiḥ ||22||

suhotraḥ pṛthiwīṃ sarwāṃ bubhuje sāgarāmbarām |
pūrṇāṃ hastigawāśwasya bahuratnasamākulām ||23||

mamajjewa mahī tasya bhūribhārāwapīḍitā |
hastyaśwarathasampūrṇā manuṣyakalilā bhṛśam ||24||

suhotre rājani tadā dharmataḥ śāsati prajāḥ |
caityayūpāṅkitā cāsīdbhūmiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ||25||

prawṛddhajanasasyā ca sahadewā wyarocata ||25||

aikṣwākī janayāmāsa suhotrātpṛthiwīpateḥ |
ajamīḍhaṃ sumīḍhaṃ ca purumīḍhaṃ ca bhārata ||26||

ajamīḍho warasteṣāṃ tasminwaṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ |
ṣaṭputrānso'pyajanayattisṛṣu strīṣu bhārata ||27||

ṛkṣaṃ dhūminyatho nīlī duḥṣantaparameṣṭhinau |
keśinyajanayajjahnumubhau ca janarūpiṇau ||28||

tatheme sarwapāñcālā duḥṣantaparameṣṭhinoḥ |
anwayāḥ kuśikā rājañjahnoramitatejasaḥ ||29||

janarūpiṇayorjyeṣṭhamṛkṣamāhurjanādhipam |
ṛkṣātsaṃwaraṇo jajñe rājanwaṃśakarastawa ||30||

ārkṣe saṃwaraṇe rājanpraśāsati wasundharām |
saṅkṣayaḥ sumahānāsītprajānāmiti śuśrumaḥ ||31||

wyaśīryata tato rāṣṭraṃ kṣayairnānāwidhaistathā |
kṣunmṛtyubhyāmanāwṛṣṭyā wyādhibhiśca samāhatam ||32||

abhyaghnanbhāratāṃścaiwa sapatnānāṃ balāni ca ||32||

cālayanwasudhāṃ caiwa balena caturaṅgiṇā |
abhyayāttaṃ ca pāñcālyo wijitya tarasā mahīm ||33||

akṣauhiṇībhirdaśabhiḥ sa enaṃ samare'jayat ||33||

tataḥ sadāraḥ sāmātyaḥ saputraḥ sasuhṛjjanaḥ |
rājā saṃwaraṇastasmātpalāyata mahābhayāt ||34||

sindhornadasya mahato nikuñje nyawasattadā |
nadīwiṣayaparyante parwatasya samīpataḥ ||35||

tatrāwasanbahūnkālānbhāratā durgamāśritāḥ ||35||

teṣāṃ niwasatāṃ tatra sahasraṃ pariwatsarān |
athābhyagacchadbharatānwasiṣṭho bhagawānṛṣiḥ ||36||

tamāgataṃ prayatnena pratyudgamyābhiwādya ca |
arghyamabhyāharaṃstasmai te sarwe bhāratāstadā ||37||

niwedya sarwamṛṣaye satkāreṇa suwarcase ||37||

taṃ samāmaṣṭamīmuṣṭaṃ rājā wawre swayaṃ tadā |
purohito bhawānno'stu rājyāya prayatāmahe ||38||

omityewaṃ wasiṣṭho'pi bhāratānpratyapadyata ||38||

athābhyaṣiñcatsāmrājye sarwakṣatrasya paurawam |
wiṣāṇabhūtaṃ sarwasyāṃ pṛthiwyāmiti naḥ śrutam ||39||

bharatādhyuṣitaṃ pūrwaṃ so'dhyatiṣṭhatpurottamam |
punarbalibhṛtaścaiwa cakre sarwamahīkṣitaḥ ||40||

tataḥ sa pṛthiwīṃ prāpya punarīje mahābalaḥ |
ājamīḍho mahāyajñairbahubhirbhūridakṣiṇaiḥ ||41||

tataḥ saṃwaraṇātsaurī suṣuwe tapatī kurum |
rājatwe taṃ prajāḥ sarwā dharmajña iti wawrire ||42||

tasya nāmnābhiwikhyātaṃ pṛthiwyāṃ kurujāṅgalam |
kurukṣetraṃ sa tapasā puṇyaṃ cakre mahātapāḥ ||43||

aśwawantamabhiṣwantaṃ tathā citrarathaṃ munim |
janamejayaṃ ca wikhyātaṃ putrāṃścāsyānuśuśrumaḥ ||44||

pañcaitānwāhinī putrānwyajāyata manaswinī ||44||

abhiṣwataḥ parikṣittu śabalāśwaśca wīryawān |
abhirājo wirājaśca śalmalaśca mahābalaḥ ||45||

uccaiḥśrawā bhadrakāro jitāriścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ |
eteṣāmanwawāye tu khyātāste karmajairguṇaiḥ ||46||

janamejayādayaḥ sapta tathaiwānye mahābalāḥ |
parikṣito'bhawanputrāḥ sarwe dharmārthakowidāḥ ||47||

kakṣasenograsenau ca citrasenaśca wīryawān |
indrasenaḥ suṣeṇaśca bhīmasenaśca nāmataḥ ||48||

janamejayasya tanayā bhuwi khyātā mahābalāḥ |
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ prathamajaḥ pāṇḍurbāhlīka ewa ca ||49||

niṣadhaśca mahātejāstathā jāmbūnado balī |
kuṇḍodaraḥ padātiśca wasātiścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||50||

sarwe dharmārthakuśalāḥ sarwe bhūtahite ratāḥ ||50||

dhṛtarāṣṭro'tha rājāsīttasya putro'tha kuṇḍikaḥ |
hastī witarkaḥ krāthaśca kuṇḍalaścāpi pañcamaḥ ||51||

hawiḥśrawāstathendrābhaḥ sumanyuścāparājitaḥ ||51||

pratīpasya trayaḥ putrā jajñire bharatarṣabha |
dewāpiḥ śantanuścaiwa bāhlīkaśca mahārathaḥ ||52||

dewāpistu prawawrāja teṣāṃ dharmaparīpsayā |
śantanuśca mahīṃ lebhe bāhlīkaśca mahārathaḥ ||53||

bharatasyānwaye jātāḥ sattwawanto mahārathāḥ |
dewarṣikalpā nṛpate bahawo rājasattamāḥ ||54||

ewaṃwidhāścāpyapare dewakalpā mahārathāḥ |
jātā manoranwawāye ailawaṃśawiwardhanāḥ ||55||






                  90


janamejaya uwāca||

śrutastwatto mayā wipra pūrweṣāṃ sambhawo mahān |
udārāścāpi waṃśe'sminrājāno me pariśrutāḥ ||1||

kiṃ tu laghwarthasaṃyuktaṃ priyākhyānaṃ na māmati |
prīṇātyato bhawānbhūyo wistareṇa brawītu me ||2||

etāmewa kathāṃ diwyāmā prajāpatito manoḥ |
teṣāmājananaṃ puṇyaṃ kasya na prītimāwahet ||3||

saddharmaguṇamāhātmyairabhiwardhitamuttamam |
wiṣṭabhya lokāṃstrīneṣāṃ yaśaḥ sphītamawasthitam ||4||

guṇaprabhāwawīryaujaḥsattwotsāhawatāmaham |
na tṛpyāmi kathāṃ śṛṇwannamṛtāswādasaṃmitām ||5||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

śṛṇu rājanpurā samyaṅmayā dwaipāyanācchrutam |
procyamānamidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ swawaṃśajananaṃ śubham ||6||

dakṣasyāditiḥ |
aditerwiwaswān |
wiwaswato manuḥ |
manorilā |
ilāyāḥ purūrawāḥ |
purūrawasa āyuḥ |
āyuṣo nahuṣaḥ |
nahuṣasya yayātiḥ | 007 |
yayāterdwe bhārye babhūwatuḥ |
uśanaso duhitā dewayānī wṛṣaparwaṇaśca duhitā śarmiṣṭhā nāma |
atrānuwaṃśo bhawati | 008 |

yaduṃ ca turwasuṃ caiwa dewayānī wyajāyata |
druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca śarmiṣṭhā wārṣaparwaṇī ||9||

tatra yadoryādawāḥ |
pūroḥ paurawāḥ | 010 |
pūrorbhāryā kausalyā nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe janamejayo nāma |
yastrīnaśwamedhānājahāra |
wiśwajitā ceṣṭwā wanaṃ prawiweśa | 011 |
janamejayaḥ khalwanantāṃ nāmopayeme mādhawīm |
tasyāmasya jajñe prācinwān |
yaḥ prācīṃ diśaṃ jigāya yāwatsūryodayāt |
tatastasya prācinwatwam | 012 |
prācinwānkhalwaśmakīmupayeme |
tasyāmasya jajñe saṃyātiḥ | 013 |
saṃyātiḥ khalu dṛṣadwato duhitaraṃ warāṅgīṃ nāmopayeme |
tasyāmasya jajñe ahampātiḥ | 014 |
ahampātistu khalu kṛtawīryaduhitaramupayeme bhānumatīṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe sārwabhaumaḥ | 015 |
sārwabhaumaḥ khalu jitwājahāra kaikeyīṃ sunandāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe jayatsenaḥ | 016 |
jayatsenaḥ khalu waidarbhīmupayeme suṣuwāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe arācīnaḥ | 017 |
arācīno'pi waidarbhīmewāparāmupayeme maryādāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe mahābhaumaḥ | 018 |
mahābhaumaḥ khalu prāsenajitīmupayeme suyajñāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe ayutanāyī |
yaḥ puruṣamedhānāmayutamānayat |
tadasyāyutanāyitwam | 019 |
ayutanāyī khalu pṛthuśrawaso duhitaramupayeme bhāsāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe akrodhanaḥ | 020 |
akrodhanaḥ khalu kāliṅgīṃ karaṇḍuṃ nāmopayeme |
tasyāmasya jajñe dewātithiḥ | 021 |
dewātithiḥ khalu waidehīmupayeme maryādāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe ṛcaḥ | 022 |
ṛcaḥ khalwāṅgeyīmupayeme sudewāṃ nāma |
tasyāṃ putramajanayadṛkṣam | 023 |
ṛkṣaḥ khalu takṣakaduhitaramupayeme jwālāṃ nāma |
tasyāṃ putraṃ matināraṃ nāmotpādayāmāsa | 024 |
matināraḥ khalu saraswatyāṃ dwādaśawārṣikaṃ satramājahāra | 025 |
niwṛtte ca satre saraswatyabhigamya taṃ bhartāraṃ warayāmāsa |
tasyāṃ putramajanayattaṃsuṃ nāma | 026 |
atrānuwaṃśo bhawati | 027 |

taṃsuṃ saraswatī putraṃ matinārādajījanat |
ilinaṃ janayāmāsa kālindyāṃ taṃsurātmajam ||28||

ilinastu rathantaryāṃ duḥṣantādyānpañca putrānajanayat | 029 |
duḥṣantaḥ khalu wiśwāmitraduhitaraṃ śakuntalāṃ nāmopayeme |
tasyāmasya jajñe bharataḥ |
tatra ślokau bhawataḥ | 030 |

mātā bhastrā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa ewa saḥ |
bharaswa putraṃ duḥṣanta māwamaṃsthāḥ śakuntalām ||31||

retodhāḥ putra unnayati naradewa yamakṣayāt |
twaṃ cāsya dhātā garbhasya satyamāha śakuntalā ||32||

tato'sya bharatatwam | 033 |
bharataḥ khalu kāśeyīmupayeme sārwasenīṃ sunandāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe bhumanyuḥ | 034 |
bhumanyuḥ khalu dāśārhīmupayeme jayāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe suhotraḥ | 035 |
suhotraḥ khalwikṣwākukanyāmupayeme suwarṇāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe hastī |
ya idaṃ hāstinapuraṃ māpayāmāsa |
etadasya hāstinapuratwam | 036 |
hastī khalu traigartīmupayeme yaśodharāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe wikuṇṭhanaḥ | 037 |
wikuṇṭhanaḥ khalu dāśārhīmupayeme sudewāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe'jamīḍhaḥ | 038 |
ajamīḍhasya caturwiṃśaṃ putraśataṃ babhūwa kaikeyyāṃ nāgāyāṃ gāndhāryāṃ wimalāyāmṛkṣāyāṃ ceti |
pṛthakpṛthagwaṃśakarā nṛpatayaḥ |
tatra waṃśakaraḥ saṃwaraṇaḥ | 039 |
saṃwaraṇaḥ khalu waiwaswatīṃ tapatīṃ nāmopayeme |
tasyāmasya jajñe kuruḥ | 040 |
kuruḥ khalu dāśārhīmupayeme śubhāṅgīṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe wiḍūrathaḥ | 041 |
wiḍūrathastu māgadhīmupayeme sampriyāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe'rugwānnāma | 042 |
arugwānkhalu māgadhīmupayeme'mṛtāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe parikṣit | 043 |
parikṣitkhalu bāhudāmupayeme suyaśāṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe bhīmasenaḥ | 044 |
bhīmasenaḥ khalu kaikeyīmupayeme sukumārīṃ nāma |
tasyāmasya jajñe paryaśrawāḥ |
yamāhuḥ pratīpaṃ nāma | 045 |
pratīpaḥ khalu śaibyāmupayeme sunandāṃ nāma |
tasyāṃ putrānutpādayāmāsa dewāpiṃ śantanuṃ bāhlīkaṃ ceti | 046 |
dewāpiḥ khalu bāla ewāraṇyaṃ prawiweśa |
śantanustu mahīpālo'bhawat |
atrānuwaṃśo bhawati | 047 |

yaṃ yaṃ karābhyāṃ spṛśati jīrṇaṃ sa sukhamaśnute |
punaryuwā ca bhawati tasmāttaṃ śantanuṃ widuḥ ||48||

tadasya śantanutwam | 049 |
śantanuḥ khalu gaṅgāṃ bhāgīrathīmupayeme |
tasyāmasya jajñe dewawrataḥ |
yamāhurbhīṣma iti | 050 |
bhīṣmaḥ khalu pituḥ priyacikīrṣayā satyawatīmudawahanmātaram |
yāmāhurgandhakālīti | 051 |
tasyāṃ kānīno garbhaḥ parāśarāddwaipāyanaḥ |
tasyāmewa śantanordwau putrau babhūwatuḥ |
citrāṅgado wicitrawīryaśca | 052 |
tayoraprāptayauwana ewa citrāṅgado gandharweṇa hataḥ |
wicitrawīryastu rājā samabhawat | 053 |
wicitrawīryaḥ khalu kausalyātmaje'mbikāmbālike kāśirājaduhitarāwupayeme | 054 |
wicitrawīryastwanapatya ewa widehatwaṃ prāptaḥ | 055 |
tataḥ satyawatī cintayāmāsa |
dauḥṣanto waṃśa ucchidyate iti | 056 |
sā dwaipāyanamṛṣiṃ cintayāmāsa | 057 |
sa tasyāḥ purataḥ sthitaḥ kiṃ karawāṇīti | 058 |
sā tamuwāca |
bhrātā tawānapatya ewa swaryāto wicitrawīryaḥ |
sādhwapatyaṃ tasyotpādayeti | 059 |
sa paramityuktwā trīnputrānutpādayāmāsa dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ pāṇḍuṃ widuraṃ ceti | 060 |
tatra dhṛtarāṣṭrasya rājñaḥ putraśataṃ babhūwa gāndhāryāṃ waradānāddwaipāyanasya | 061 |
teṣāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāṇāṃ catwāraḥ pradhānā babhūwurduryodhano duḥśāsano wikarṇaścitrasena iti | 062 |
pāṇḍostu dwe bhārye babhūwatuḥ kuntī mādrī cetyubhe strīratne | 063 |
atha pāṇḍurmṛgayāṃ caranmaithunagatamṛṣimapaśyanmṛgyāṃ wartamānam |
tathaiwāplutamanāsāditakāmarasamatṛptaṃ bāṇenābhijaghāna | 064 |
sa bāṇawiddha uwāca pāṇḍum |
caratā dharmamimaṃ yena twayābhijñena kāmarasasyāhamanawāptakāmaraso'bhihatastasmāttwamapyetāmawasthāmāsādyānawāptakāmarasaḥ pañcatwamāpsyasi kṣiprameweti | 065 |
sa wiwarṇarūpaḥ pāṇḍuḥ śāpaṃ pariharamāṇo nopāsarpata bhārye | 066 |
wākyaṃ cowāca |
swacāpalyādidaṃ prāptawānaham |
śṛṇomi ca nānapatyasya lokā santīti | 067 |
sā twaṃ madarthe putrānutpādayeti kuntīmuwāca | 068 |
sā tatra putrānutpādayāmāsa dharmādyudhiṣṭhiraṃ mārutādbhīmasenaṃ śakrādarjunamiti | 069 |
sa tāṃ hṛṣṭarūpaḥ pāṇḍuruwāca |
iyaṃ te sapatnyanapatyā |
sādhwasyāmapatyamutpādyatāmiti | 070 |
sa ewamastwityuktaḥ kuntyā | 071 |
tato mādryāmaświbhyāṃ nakulasahadewāwutpāditau | 072 |
mādrīṃ khalwalaṅkṛtāṃ dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍurbhāwaṃ cakre | 073 |
sa tāṃ spṛṣṭwaiwa widehatwaṃ prāptaḥ | 074 |
tatrainaṃ citāsthaṃ mādrī samanwāruroha | 075 |
uwāca kuntīm |
yamayorāryayāpramattayā bhawitawyamiti | 076 |
tataste pañca pāṇḍawāḥ kuntyā sahitā hāstinapuramānīya tāpasairbhīṣmasya widurasya ca niweditāḥ | 077 |
tatrāpi jatugṛhe dagdhuṃ samārabdhā na śakitā widuramantritena | 078 |
tataśca hiḍimbamantarā hatwā ekacakrāṃ gatāḥ | 079 |
tasyāmapyekacakrāyāṃ bakaṃ nāma rākṣasaṃ hatwā pāñcālanagaramabhigatāḥ | 080 |
tasmāddraupadīṃ bhāryāmawindanswawiṣayaṃ cājagmuḥ kuśalinaḥ | 081 |
putrāṃścotpādayāmāsuḥ |
pratiwindhyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
sutasomaṃ wṛkodaraḥ |
śrutakīrtimarjunaḥ |
śatānīkaṃ nakulaḥ |
śrutakarmāṇaṃ sahadewa iti | 082 |
yudhiṣṭhirastu gowāsanasya śaibyasya dewikāṃ nāma kanyāṃ swayaṃware lebhe |
tasyāṃ putraṃ janayāmāsa yaudheyaṃ nāma | 083 |
bhīmaseno'pi kāśyāṃ baladharāṃ nāmopayeme wīryaśulkām |
tasyāṃ putraṃ sarwagaṃ nāmotpādayāmāsa | 084 |
arjunaḥ khalu dwārawatīṃ gatwā bhaginīṃ wāsudewasya subhadrāṃ nāma bhāryāmudawahat |
tasyāṃ putramabhimanyuṃ nāma janayāmāsa | 085 |
nakulastu caidyāṃ kareṇuwatīṃ nāma bhāryāmudawahat |
tasyāṃ putraṃ niramitraṃ nāmājanayat | 086 |
sahadewo'pi mādrīmewa swayaṃware wijayāṃ nāmopayeme |
tasyāṃ putramajanayatsuhotraṃ nāma | 087 |
bhīmasenastu pūrwamewa hiḍimbāyāṃ rākṣasyāṃ ghaṭotkacaṃ nāma putraṃ janayāmāsa | 088 |
ityete ekādaśa pāṇḍawānāṃ putrāḥ | 089 |
wirāṭasya duhitaramuttarāṃ nāmābhimanyurupayeme |
tasyāmasya parāsurgarbho'jāyata | 090 |
tamutsaṅgena pratijagrāha pṛthā niyogātpuruṣottamasya wāsudewasya |
ṣāṇmāsikaṃ garbhamahamenaṃ jīwayiṣyāmīti | 091 |
sañjīwayitwā cainamuwāca |
parikṣīṇe kule jāto bhawatwayaṃ parikṣinnāmeti | 092 |
parikṣittu khalu mādrawatīṃ nāmopayeme |
tasyāmasya janamejayaḥ | 093 |
janamejayāttu wapuṣṭamāyāṃ dwau putrau śatānīkaḥ śaṅkuśca | 094 |
śatānīkastu khalu waidehīmupayeme |
tasyāmasya jajñe putro'śwamedhadattaḥ | 095 |

ityeṣa pūrorwaṃśastu pāṇḍawānāṃ ca kīrtitaḥ |
pūrorwaṃśamimaṃ śrutwā sarwapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||96||






                  91


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ikṣwākuwaṃśaprabhawo rājāsītpṛthiwīpatiḥ |
mahābhiṣa iti khyātaḥ satyawāksatyawikramaḥ ||1||

so'śwamedhasahasreṇa wājapeyaśatena ca |
toṣayāmāsa dewendraṃ swargaṃ lebhe tataḥ prabhuḥ ||2||

tataḥ kadācidbrahmāṇamupāsāṃ cakrire surāḥ |
tatra rājarṣayo āsansa ca rājā mahābhiṣaḥ ||3||

atha gaṅgā saricchreṣṭhā samupāyātpitāmaham |
tasyā wāsaḥ samuddhūtaṃ mārutena śaśiprabham ||4||

tato'bhawansuragaṇāḥ sahasāwāṅmukhāstadā |
mahābhiṣastu rājarṣiraśaṅko dṛṣṭawānnadīm ||5||

apadhyāto bhagawatā brahmaṇā sa mahābhiṣaḥ |
uktaśca jāto martyeṣu punarlokānawāpsyasi ||6||

sa cintayitwā nṛpatirnṛpānsarwāṃstapodhanān |
pratīpaṃ rocayāmāsa pitaraṃ bhūriwarcasam ||7||

mahābhiṣaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭwā nadī dhairyāccyutaṃ nṛpam |
tamewa manasādhyāyamupāwartatsaridwarā ||8||

sā tu widhwastawapuṣaḥ kaśmalābhihataujasaḥ |
dadarśa pathi gacchantī wasūndewāndiwaukasaḥ ||9||

tathārūpāṃśca tāndṛṣṭwā papraccha saritāṃ warā |
kimidaṃ naṣṭarūpāḥ stha kaccitkṣemaṃ diwaukasām ||10||

tāmūcurwasawo dewāḥ śaptāḥ smo wai mahānadi |
alpe'parādhe saṃrambhādwasiṣṭhena mahātmanā ||11||

wimūḍhā hi wayaṃ sarwe pracchannamṛṣisattamam |
sandhyāṃ wasiṣṭhamāsīnaṃ tamatyabhisṛtāḥ purā ||12||

tena kopādwayaṃ śaptā yonau sambhawateti ha |
na śakyamanyathā kartuṃ yaduktaṃ brahmawādinā ||13||

twaṃ tasmānmānuṣī bhūtwā sūṣwa putrānwasūnbhuwi |
na mānuṣīṇāṃ jaṭharaṃ prawiśemāśubhaṃ wayam ||14||

ityuktā tānwasūngaṅgā tathetyuktwābrawīdidam |
martyeṣu puruṣaśreṣṭhaḥ ko waḥ kartā bhawiṣyati ||15||

wasawa ūcuḥ||

pratīpasya suto rājā śantanurnāma dhārmikaḥ |
bhawitā mānuṣe loke sa naḥ kartā bhawiṣyati ||16||

gaṅgowāca||

mamāpyewaṃ mataṃ dewā yathāwadata mānaghāḥ |
priyaṃ tasya kariṣyāmi yuṣmākaṃ caitadīpśitam ||17||

wasawa ūcuḥ||

jātānkumārānswānapsu prakṣeptuṃ wai twamarhasi |
yathā nacirakālaṃ no niṣkṛtiḥ syāttrilokage ||18||

gaṅgowāca||

ewametatkariṣyāmi putrastasya widhīyatām |
nāsya moghaḥ saṅgamaḥ syātputrahetormayā saha ||19||

wasawa ūcuḥ||

turīyārdhaṃ pradāsyāmo wīryasyaikaikaśo wayam |
tena wīryeṇa putraste bhawitā tasya cepsitaḥ ||20||

na sampatsyati martyeṣu punastasya tu santatiḥ |
tasmādaputraḥ putraste bhawiṣyati sa wīryawān ||21||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ te samayaṃ kṛtwā gaṅgayā wasawaḥ saha |
jagmuḥ prahṛṣṭamanaso yathāsaṅkalpamañjasā ||22||






                  92


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ pratīpo rājā sa sarwabhūtahite rataḥ |
niṣasāda samā bahwīrgaṅgātīragato japan ||1||

tasya rūpaguṇopetā gaṅgā śrīriwa rūpiṇī |
uttīrya salilāttasmāllobhanīyatamākṛtiḥ ||2||

adhīyānasya rājarṣerdiwyarūpā manaswinī |
dakṣiṇaṃ śālasaṅkāśamūruṃ bheje śubhānanā ||3||

pratīpastu mahīpālastāmuwāca manaswinīm |
karawāṇi kiṃ te kalyāṇi priyaṃ yatte'bhikāṅkṣitam ||4||

stryuwāca||

twāmahaṃ kāmaye rājankuruśreṣṭha bhajaswa mām |
tyāgaḥ kāmawatīnāṃ hi strīṇāṃ sadbhirwigarhitaḥ ||5||

pratīpa uwāca||

nāhaṃ parastriyaṃ kāmādgaccheyaṃ warawarṇini |
na cāsawarṇāṃ kalyāṇi dharmyaṃ tadwiddhi me wratam ||6||

stryuwāca||

nāśreyasyasmi nāgamyā na waktawyā ca karhicit |
bhaja māṃ bhajamānāṃ twaṃ rājankanyāṃ warastriyam ||7||

pratīpa uwāca||

mayātiwṛttametatte yanmāṃ codayasi priyam |
anyathā pratipannaṃ māṃ nāśayeddharmawiplawaḥ ||8||

prāpya dakṣiṇamūruṃ me twamāśliṣṭā warāṅgane |
apatyānāṃ snuṣāṇāṃ ca bhīru widdhyetadāsanam ||9||

sawyataḥ kāminībhāgastwayā sa ca wiwarjitaḥ |
tasmādahaṃ nācariṣye twayi kāmaṃ warāṅgane ||10||

snuṣā me bhawa kalyāṇi putrārthe twāṃ wṛṇomyaham |
snuṣāpakṣaṃ hi wāmoru twamāgamya samāśritā ||11||

stryuwāca||

ewamapyastu dharmajña saṃyujyeyaṃ sutena te |
twadbhaktyaiwa bhajiṣyāmi prakhyātaṃ bhārataṃ kulam ||12||

pṛthiwyāṃ pārthiwā ye ca teṣāṃ yūyaṃ parāyaṇam |
guṇā na hi mayā śakyā waktuṃ warṣaśatairapi ||13||

kulasya ye waḥ prasthitāstatsādhutwamanuttamam ||13||

sa me nābhijanajñaḥ syādācareyaṃ ca yadwibho |
tatsarwamewa putraste na mīmāṃseta karhicit ||14||

ewaṃ wasantī putre te wardhayiṣyāmyahaṃ priyam |
putraiḥ puṇyaiḥ priyaiścāpi swargaṃ prāpsyati te sutaḥ ||15||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tathetyuktwā tu sā rājaṃstatraiwāntaradhīyata |
putrajanma pratīkṣaṃstu sa rājā tadadhārayat ||16||

etasminnewa kāle tu pratīpaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ |
tapastepe sutasyārthe sabhāryaḥ kurunandana ||17||

tayoḥ samabhawatputro wṛddhayoḥ sa mahābhiṣaḥ |
śāntasya jajñe santānastasmādāsītsa śantanuḥ ||18||

saṃsmaraṃścākṣayāṃllokānwijitānswena karmaṇā |
puṇyakarmakṛdewāsīcchantanuḥ kurusattama ||19||

pratīpaḥ śantanuṃ putraṃ yauwanasthaṃ tato'nwaśāt |
purā māṃ strī samabhyāgācchantano bhūtaye tawa ||20||

twāmāwrajedyadi rahaḥ sā putra warawarṇinī |
kāmayānābhirūpāḍhyā diwyā strī putrakāmyayā ||21||

sā twayā nānuyoktawyā kāsi kasyāsi wāṅgane ||21||

yacca kuryānna tatkāryaṃ praṣṭawyā sā twayānagha |
manniyogādbhajantīṃ tāṃ bhajethā ityuwāca tam ||22||

ewaṃ saṃdiśya tanayaṃ pratīpaḥ śantanuṃ tadā |
swe ca rājye'bhiṣicyainaṃ wanaṃ rājā wiweśa ha ||23||

sa rājā śantanurdhīmānkhyātaḥ pṛthwyāṃ dhanurdharaḥ |
babhūwa mṛgayāśīlaḥ satataṃ wanagocaraḥ ||24||

sa mṛgānmahiṣāṃścaiwa winighnanrājasattamaḥ |
gaṅgāmanucacāraikaḥ siddhacāraṇasewitām ||25||

sa kadācinmahārāja dadarśa paramastriyam |
jājwalyamānāṃ wapuṣā sākṣātpadmāmiwa śriyam ||26||

sarwānawadyāṃ sudatīṃ diwyābharaṇabhūṣitām |
sūkṣmāmbaradharāmekāṃ padmodarasamaprabhām ||27||

tāṃ dṛṣṭwā hṛṣṭaromābhūdwismito rūpasampadā |
pibanniwa ca netrābhyāṃ nātṛpyata narādhipaḥ ||28||

sā ca dṛṣṭwaiwa rājānaṃ wicarantaṃ mahādyutim |
snehādāgatasauhārdā nātṛpyata wilāsinī ||29||

tāmuwāca tato rājā sāntwayañślakṣṇayā girā |
dewī wā dānawī wā twaṃ gandharwī yadi wāpsarāḥ ||30||

yakṣī wā pannagī wāpi mānuṣī wā sumadhyame |
yā wā twaṃ suragarbhābhe bhāryā me bhawa śobhane ||31||

etacchrutwā waco rājñaḥ sasmitaṃ mṛdu walgu ca |
wasūnāṃ samayaṃ smṛtwā abhyagacchadaninditā ||32||

uwāca caiwa rājñaḥ sā hlādayantī mano girā |
bhawiṣyāmi mahīpāla mahiṣī te waśānugā ||33||

yattu kuryāmahaṃ rājañśubhaṃ wā yadi wāśubham |
na tadwārayitawyāsmi na waktawyā tathāpriyam ||34||

ewaṃ hi wartamāne'haṃ twayi watsyāmi pārthiwa |
wāritā wipriyaṃ coktā tyajeyaṃ twāmasaṃśayam ||35||

tatheti rājñā sā tūktā tadā bharatasattama |
praharṣamatulaṃ lebhe prāpya taṃ pārthiwottamam ||36||

āsādya śantanustāṃ ca bubhuje kāmato waśī |
na praṣṭawyeti manwāno na sa tāṃ kiñcidūciwān ||37||

sa tasyāḥ śīlawṛttena rūpaudāryaguṇena ca |
upacāreṇa ca rahastutoṣa jagatīpatiḥ ||38||

diwyarūpā hi sā dewī gaṅgā tripathagā nadī |
mānuṣaṃ wigrahaṃ śrīmatkṛtwā sā warawarṇinī ||39||

bhāgyopanatakāmasya bhāryewopasthitābhawat |
śantano rājasiṃhasya dewarājasamadyuteḥ ||40||

sambhogasnehacāturyairhāwalāsyairmanoharaiḥ |
rājānaṃ ramayāmāsa yathā reme tathaiwa saḥ ||41||

sa rājā ratisaktatwāduttamastrīguṇairhṛtaḥ |
saṃwatsarānṛtūnmāsānna bubodha bahūngatān ||42||

ramamāṇastayā sārdhaṃ yathākāmaṃ janeśwaraḥ |
aṣṭāwajanayatputrāṃstasyāmamarawarṇinaḥ ||43||

jātaṃ jātaṃ ca sā putraṃ kṣipatyambhasi bhārata |
prīṇāmi twāhamityuktwā gaṅgāsrotasyamajjayat ||44||

tasya tanna priyaṃ rājñaḥ śantanorabhawattadā |
na ca tāṃ kiñcanowāca tyāgādbhīto mahīpatiḥ ||45||

atha tāmaṣṭame putre jāte prahasitāmiwa |
uwāca rājā duḥkhārtaḥ parīpsanputramātmanaḥ ||46||

mā wadhīḥ kāsi kasyāsi kiṃ hiṃsasi sutāniti |
putraghni sumahatpāpaṃ mā prāpastiṣṭha garhite ||47||

stryuwāca||

putrakāma na te hanmi putraṃ putrawatāṃ wara |
jīrṇastu mama wāso'yaṃ yathā sa samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ||48||

ahaṃ gaṅgā jahnusutā maharṣigaṇasewitā |
dewakāryārthasiddhyarthamuṣiṭāhaṃ twayā saha ||49||

aṣṭeme wasawo dewā mahābhāgā mahaujasaḥ |
wasiṣṭhaśāpadoṣeṇa mānuṣatwamupāgatāḥ ||50||

teṣāṃ janayitā nānyastwadṛte bhuwi widyate |
madwidhā mānuṣī dhātrī na caiwāstīha kācana ||51||

tasmāttajjananīhetormānuṣatwamupāgatā |
janayitwā wasūnaṣṭau jitā lokāstwayākṣayāḥ ||52||

dewānāṃ samayastweṣa wasūnāṃ saṃśruto mayā |
jātaṃ jātaṃ mokṣayiṣye janmato mānuṣāditi ||53||

tatte śāpādwinirmuktā āpawasya mahātmanaḥ |
swasti te'stu gamiṣyāmi putraṃ pāhi mahāwratam ||54||

eṣa paryāyawāso me wasūnāṃ saṃnidhau kṛtaḥ |
matprasūtaṃ wijānīhi gaṅgādattamimaṃ sutam ||55||






                  93


śantanuruwāca||

āpawo nāma ko nweṣa wasūnāṃ kiṃ ca duṣkṛtam |
yasyābhiśāpātte sarwe mānuṣīṃ tanumāgatāḥ ||1||

anena ca kumāreṇa gaṅgādattena kiṃ kṛtam |
yasya caiwa kṛtenāyaṃ mānuṣeṣu niwatsyati ||2||

īśānāḥ sarwalokasya wasawaste ca wai katham |
mānuṣeṣūdapadyanta tanmamācakṣwa jāhnawi ||3||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

saiwamuktā tato gaṅgā rājānamidamabrawīt |
bhartāraṃ jāhnawī dewī śantanuṃ puruṣarṣabham ||4||

yaṃ lebhe waruṇaḥ putraṃ purā bharatasattama |
wasiṣṭho nāma sa muniḥ khyāta āpawa ityuta ||5||

tasyāśramapadaṃ puṇyaṃ mṛgapakṣigaṇānwitam |
meroḥ pārśwe nagendrasya sarwartukusumāwṛtam ||6||

sa wāruṇistapastepe tasminbharatasattama |
wane puṇyakṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ swādumūlaphalodake ||7||

dakṣasya duhitā yā tu surabhītyatigarwitā |
gāṃ prajātā tu sā dewī kaśyapādbharatarṣabha ||8||

anugrahārthaṃ jagataḥ sarwakāmadughāṃ warām |
tāṃ lebhe gāṃ tu dharmātmā homadhenuṃ sa wāruṇiḥ ||9||

sā tasmiṃstāpasāraṇye wasantī munisewite |
cacāra ramye dharmye ca gaurapetabhayā tadā ||10||

atha tadwanamājagmuḥ kadācidbharatarṣabha |
pṛthwādyā wasawaḥ sarwe dewadewarṣisewitam ||11||

te sadārā wanaṃ tacca wyacaranta samantataḥ |
remire ramaṇīyeṣu parwateṣu waneṣu ca ||12||

tatraikasya tu bhāryā wai wasorwāsawawikrama |
sā carantī wane tasmingāṃ dadarśa sumadhyamā ||13||

yā sā wasiṣṭhasya muneḥ sarwakāmadhuguttamā ||13||

sā wismayasamāwiṣṭā śīladrawiṇasampadā |
diwe wai darśayāmāsa tāṃ gāṃ gowṛṣabhekṣaṇa ||14||

swāpīnāṃ ca sudogdhrīṃ ca suwāladhimukhāṃ śubhām |
upapannāṃ guṇaiḥ sarwaiḥ śīlenānuttamena ca ||15||

ewaṅguṇasamāyuktāṃ wasawe wasunandinī |
darśayāmāsa rājendra purā paurawanandana ||16||

dyaustadā tāṃ tu dṛṣṭwaiwa gāṃ gajendrendrawikrama |
uwāca rājaṃstāṃ dewīṃ tasyā rūpaguṇānwadan ||17||

eṣā gauruttamā dewi wāruṇerasitekṣaṇe |
ṛṣestasya warārohe yasyedaṃ wanamuttamam ||18||

asyāḥ kṣīraṃ pibenmartyaḥ swādu yo wai sumadhyame |
daśa warṣasahasrāṇi sa jīwetsthirayauwanaḥ ||19||

etacchrutwā tu sā dewī nṛpottama sumadhyamā |
tamuwācānawadyāṅgī bhartāraṃ dīptatejasam ||20||

asti me mānuṣe loke naradewātmajā sakhī |
nāmnā jinawatī nāma rūpayauwanaśālinī ||21||

uśīnarasya rājarṣeḥ satyasandhasya dhīmataḥ |
duhitā prathitā loke mānuṣe rūpasampadā ||22||

tasyā hetormahābhāga sawatsāṃ gāṃ mamepsitām |
ānayaswāmaraśreṣṭha twaritaṃ puṇyawardhana ||23||

yāwadasyāḥ payaḥ pītwā sā sakhī mama mānada |
mānuṣeṣu bhawatwekā jarārogawiwarjitā ||24||

etanmama mahābhāga kartumarhasyanindita |
priyaṃ priyataraṃ hyasmānnāsti me'nyatkathañcana ||25||

etacchrutwā wacastasyā dewyāḥ priyacikīrṣayā |
pṛthwādyairbhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ dyaustadā tāṃ jahāra gām ||26||

tayā kamalapatrākṣyā niyukto dyaustadā nṛpa |
ṛṣestasya tapastīwraṃ na śaśāka nirīkṣitum ||27||

hṛtā gauḥ sā tadā tena prapātastu na tarkitaḥ ||27||

athāśramapadaṃ prāptaḥ phalānyādāya wāruṇiḥ |
na cāpaśyata gāṃ tatra sawatsāṃ kānanottame ||28||

tataḥ sa mṛgayāmāsa wane tasmiṃstapodhanaḥ |
nādhyagacchacca mṛgayaṃstāṃ gāṃ munirudāradhīḥ ||29||

jñātwā tathāpanītāṃ tāṃ wasubhirdiwyadarśanaḥ |
yayau krodhawaśaṃ sadyaḥ śaśāpa ca wasūṃstadā ||30||

yasmānme wasawo jahrurgāṃ wai dogdhrīṃ suwāladhim |
tasmātsarwe janiṣyanti mānuṣeṣu na saṃśayaḥ ||31||

ewaṃ śaśāpa bhagawānwasūṃstānmunisattamaḥ |
waśaṃ kopasya samprāpta āpawo bharatarṣabha ||32||

śaptwā ca tānmahābhāgastapasyewa mano dadhe |
ewaṃ sa śaptawānrājanwasūnaṣṭau tapodhanaḥ ||33||

mahāprabhāwo brahmarṣirdewānroṣasamanwitaḥ ||33||

athāśramapadaṃ prāpya taṃ sma bhūyo mahātmanaḥ |
śaptāḥ sma iti jānanta ṛṣiṃ tamupacakramuḥ ||34||

prasādayantastamṛṣiṃ wasawaḥ pārthiwarṣabha |
na lebhire ca tasmātte prasādamṛṣisattamāt ||35||

āpawātpuruṣawyāghra sarwadharmawiśāradāt ||35||

uwāca ca sa dharmātmā sapta yūyaṃ dharādayaḥ |
anu saṃwatsarācchāpamokṣaṃ wai samawāpsyatha ||36||

ayaṃ tu yatkṛte yūyaṃ mayā śaptāḥ sa watsyati |
dyaustadā mānuṣe loke dīrghakālaṃ swakarmaṇā ||37||

nānṛtaṃ taccikīrṣāmi yuṣmānkruddho yadabruwam |
na prajāsyati cāpyeṣa mānuṣeṣu mahāmanāḥ ||38||

bhawiṣyati ca dharmātmā sarwaśāstrawiśāradaḥ |
pituḥ priyahite yuktaḥ strībhogānwarjayiṣyati ||39||

ewamuktwā wasūnsarwāñjagāma bhagawānṛṣiḥ ||39||

tato māmupajagmuste samastā wasawastadā |
ayācanta ca māṃ rājanwaraṃ sa ca mayā kṛtaḥ ||40||

jātāñjātānprakṣipāsmānswayaṃ gaṅge twamambhasi ||40||

ewaṃ teṣāmahaṃ samyakṣaptānāṃ rājasattama |
mokṣārthaṃ mānuṣāllokādyathāwatkṛtawatyaham ||41||

ayaṃ śāpādṛṣestasya eka ewa nṛpottama |
dyau rājanmānuṣe loke ciraṃ watsyati bhārata ||42||

etadākhyāya sā dewī tatraiwāntaradhīyata |
ādāya ca kumāraṃ taṃ jagāmātha yathepsitam ||43||

sa tu dewawrato nāma gāṅgeya iti cābhawat |
dwināmā śantanoḥ putraḥ śantanoradhiko guṇaiḥ ||44||

śantanuścāpi śokārto jagāma swapuraṃ tataḥ |
tasyāhaṃ kīrtayiṣyāmi śantanoramitānguṇān ||45||

mahābhāgyaṃ ca nṛpaterbhāratasya yaśaswinaḥ |
yasyetihāso dyutimānmahābhāratamucyate ||46||






                  94


waiśampāyana uwāca||

sa ewaṃ śantanurdhīmāndewarājarṣisatkṛtaḥ |
dharmātmā sarwalokeṣu satyawāgiti wiśrutaḥ ||1||

damo dānaṃ kṣamā buddhirhrīrdhṛtisteja uttamam |
nityānyāsanmahāsattwe śantanau puruṣarṣabhe ||2||

ewaṃ sa guṇasampanno dharmārthakuśalo nṛpaḥ |
āsīdbharatawaṃśasya goptā sādhujanasya ca ||3||

kambugrīwaḥ pṛthuwyaṃso mattawāraṇawikramaḥ |
dharma ewa paraḥ kāmādarthācceti wyawasthitaḥ ||4||

etānyāsanmahāsattwe śantanau bharatarṣabha |
na cāsya sadṛśaḥ kaścitkṣatriyo dharmato'bhawat ||5||

wartamānaṃ hi dharme swe sarwadharmawidāṃ waram |
taṃ mahīpā mahīpālaṃ rājarājye'bhyaṣecayan ||6||

wītaśokabhayābādhāḥ sukhaswapnawibodhanāḥ |
prati bhāratagoptāraṃ samapadyanta bhūmipāḥ ||7||

śantanupramukhairgupte loke nṛpatibhistadā |
niyamātsarwawarṇānāṃ brahmottaramawartata ||8||

brahma paryacaratkṣatraṃ wiśaḥ kṣatramanuwratāḥ |
brahmakṣatrānuraktāśca śūdrāḥ paryacaranwiśaḥ ||9||

sa hāstinapure ramye kurūṇāṃ puṭabhedane |
wasansāgaraparyantāmanwaśādwai wasundharām ||10||

sa dewarājasadṛśo dharmajñaḥ satyawāgṛjuḥ |
dānadharmatapoyogācchriyā paramayā yutaḥ ||11||

arāgadweṣasaṃyuktaḥ somawatpriyadarśanaḥ |
tejasā sūryasaṅkāśo wāyuwegasamo jawe ||12||

antakapratimaḥ kope kṣamayā pṛthiwīsamaḥ ||12||

wadhaḥ paśuwarāhāṇāṃ tathaiwa mṛgapakṣiṇām |
śantanau pṛthiwīpāle nāwartata wṛthā nṛpa ||13||

dharmabrahmottare rājye śantanurwinayātmawān |
samaṃ śaśāsa bhūtāni kāmarāgawiwarjitaḥ ||14||

dewarṣipitṛyajñārthamārabhyanta tadā kriyāḥ |
na cādharmeṇa keṣāñcitprāṇināmabhawadwadhaḥ ||15||

asukhānāmanāthānāṃ tiryagyoniṣu wartatām |
sa ewa rājā bhūtānāṃ sarweṣāmabhawatpitā ||16||

tasminkurupatiśreṣṭhe rājarājeśware sati |
śritā wāgabhawatsatyaṃ dānadharmāśritaṃ manaḥ ||17||

sa samāḥ ṣoḍaśāṣṭau ca catasro'ṣṭau tathāparāḥ |
ratimaprāpnuwanstrīṣu babhūwa wanagocaraḥ ||18||

tathārūpastathācārastathāwṛttastathāśrutaḥ |
gāṅgeyastasya putro'bhūnnāmnā dewawrato wasuḥ ||19||

sarwāstreṣu sa niṣṇātaḥ pārthiweṣwitareṣu ca |
mahābalo mahāsattwo mahāwīryo mahārathaḥ ||20||

sa kadācinmṛgaṃ widdhwā gaṅgāmanusarannadīm |
bhāgīrathīmalpajalāṃ śantanurdṛṣṭawānnṛpaḥ ||21||

tāṃ dṛṣṭwā cintayāmāsa śantanuḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ |
syandate kiṃ nwiyaṃ nādya saricchreṣṭhā yathā purā ||22||

tato nimittamanwicchandadarśa sa mahāmanāḥ |
kumāraṃ rūpasampannaṃ bṛhantaṃ cārudarśanam ||23||

diwyamastraṃ wikurwāṇaṃ yathā dewaṃ puraṃdaram |
kṛtsnāṃ gaṅgāṃ samāwṛtya śaraistīkṣṇairawasthitam ||24||

tāṃ śarairāwṛtāṃ dṛṣṭwā nadīṃ gaṅgāṃ tadantike |
abhawadwismito rājā karma dṛṣṭwātimānuṣam ||25||

jātamātraṃ purā dṛṣṭaṃ taṃ putraṃ śantanustadā |
nopalebhe smṛtiṃ dhīmānabhijñātuṃ tamātmajam ||26||

sa tu taṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭwā mohayāmāsa māyayā |
saṃmohya tu tataḥ kṣipraṃ tatraiwāntaradhīyata ||27||

tadadbhutaṃ tadā dṛṣṭwā tatra rājā sa śantanuḥ |
śaṅkamānaḥ sutaṃ gaṅgāmabrawīddarśayeti ha ||28||

darśayāmāsa taṃ gaṅgā bibhratī rūpamuttamam |
gṛhītwā dakṣiṇe pāṇau taṃ kumāramalaṅkṛtam ||29||

alaṅkṛtāmābharaṇairarajombaradhāriṇīm |
dṛṣṭapūrwāmapi satīṃ nābhyajānātsa śantanuḥ ||30||

gaṅgowāca||

yaṃ putramaṣṭamaṃ rājaṃstwaṃ purā mayyajāyithāḥ |
sa te'yaṃ puruṣawyāghra nayaswainaṃ gṛhāntikam ||31||

wedānadhijage sāṅgānwasiṣṭhādewa wīryawān |
kṛtāstraḥ parameṣwāso dewarājasamo yudhi ||32||

surāṇāṃ saṃmato nityamasurāṇāṃ ca bhārata |
uśanā weda yacchāstramayaṃ tadweda sarwaśaḥ ||33||

tathaiwāṅgirasaḥ putraḥ surāsuranamaskṛtaḥ |
yadweda śāstraṃ taccāpi kṛtsnamasminpratiṣṭhitam ||34||

tawa putre mahābāhau sāṅgopāṅgaṃ mahātmani ||34||

ṛṣiḥ parairanādhṛṣyo jāmadagnyaḥ pratāpawān |
yadastraṃ weda rāmaśca tadapyasminpratiṣṭhitam ||35||

maheṣwāsamimaṃ rājanrājadharmārthakowidam |
mayā dattaṃ nijaṃ putraṃ wīraṃ wīra gṛhānnaya ||36||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tayaiwaṃ samanujñātaḥ putramādāya śantanuḥ |
bhrājamānaṃ yathādityamāyayau swapuraṃ prati ||37||

paurawaḥ swapuraṃ gatwā puraṃdarapuropamam |
sarwakāmasamṛddhārthaṃ mene ātmānamātmanā ||38||

pauraweṣu tataḥ putraṃ yauwarājye'bhyaṣecayat ||38||

paurawāñśantanoḥ putraḥ pitaraṃ ca mahāyaśāḥ |
rāṣṭraṃ ca rañjayāmāsa wṛttena bharatarṣabha ||39||

sa tathā saha putreṇa ramamāṇo mahīpatiḥ |
wartayāmāsa warṣāṇi catwāryamitawikramaḥ ||40||

sa kadācidwanaṃ yāto yamunāmabhito nadīm |
mahīpatiranirdeśyamājighradgandhamuttamam ||41||

tasya prabhawamanwicchanwicacāra samantataḥ |
sa dadarśa tadā kanyāṃ dāśānāṃ dewarūpiṇīm ||42||

tāmapṛcchatsa dṛṣṭwaiwa kanyāmasitalocanām |
kasya twamasi kā cāsi kiṃ ca bhīru cikīrṣasi ||43||

sābrawīddāśakanyāsmi dharmārthaṃ wāhaye tarīm |
piturniyogādbhadraṃ te dāśarājño mahātmanaḥ ||44||

rūpamādhuryagandhaistāṃ saṃyuktāṃ dewarūpiṇīm |
samīkṣya rājā dāśeyīṃ kāmayāmāsa śantanuḥ ||45||

sa gatwā pitaraṃ tasyā warayāmāsa tāṃ tadā |
paryapṛcchattatastasyāḥ pitaraṃ cātmakāraṇāt ||46||

sa ca taṃ pratyuwācedaṃ dāśarājo mahīpatim |
jātamātraiwa me deyā warāya warawarṇinī ||47||

hṛdi kāmastu me kaścittaṃ nibodha janeśwara ||47||

yadīmāṃ dharmapatnīṃ twaṃ mattaḥ prārthayase'nagha |
satyawāgasi satyena samayaṃ kuru me tataḥ ||48||

samayena pradadyāṃ te kanyāmahamimāṃ nṛpa |
na hi me twatsamaḥ kaścidwaro jātu bhawiṣyati ||49||

śantanuruwāca||

śrutwā tawa waraṃ dāśa wyawasyeyamahaṃ na wā |
dātawyaṃ cetpradāsyāmi na twadeyaṃ kathañcana ||50||

dāśa uwāca||

asyāṃ jāyeta yaḥ putraḥ sa rājā pṛthiwīpatiḥ |
twadūrdhwamabhiṣektawyo nānyaḥ kaścana pārthiwa ||51||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

nākāmayata taṃ dātuṃ waraṃ dāśāya śantanuḥ |
śarīrajena tīwreṇa dahyamāno'pi bhārata ||52||

sa cintayannewa tadā dāśakanyāṃ mahīpatiḥ |
pratyayāddhāstinapuraṃ śokopahatacetanaḥ ||53||

tataḥ kadācicchocantaṃ śantanuṃ dhyānamāsthitam |
putro dewawrato'bhyetya pitaraṃ wākyamabrawīt ||54||

sarwato bhawataḥ kṣemaṃ widheyāḥ sarwapārthiwāḥ |
tatkimarthamihābhīkṣṇaṃ pariśocasi duḥkhitaḥ ||55||

dhyāyanniwa ca kiṃ rājannābhibhāṣasi kiñcana ||55||

ewamuktaḥ sa putreṇa śantanuḥ pratyabhāṣata |
asaṃśayaṃ dhyānaparaṃ yathā māttha tathāsmyuta ||56||

apatyaṃ nastwamewaikaḥ kule mahati bhārata |
anityatā ca martyānāmataḥ śocāmi putraka ||57||

kathañcittawa gāṅgeya wipattau nāsti naḥ kulam |
asaṃśayaṃ twamewaikaḥ śatādapi waraḥ sutaḥ ||58||

na cāpyahaṃ wṛthā bhūyo dārānkartumihotsahe |
santānasyāwināśāya kāmaye bhadramastu te ||59||

anapatyataikaputratwamityāhurdharmawādinaḥ ||59||

agnihotraṃ trayo wedā yajñāśca sahadakṣiṇāḥ |
sarwāṇyetānyapatyasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ||60||

ewamewa manuṣyeṣu syācca sarwaprajāswapi |
yadapatyaṃ mahāprājña tatra me nāsti saṃśayaḥ ||61||

eṣā trayī purāṇānāmuttamānāṃ ca śāśwatī ||61||

twaṃ ca śūraḥ sadāmarṣī śastranityaśca bhārata |
nānyatra śastrāttasmātte nidhanaṃ widyate'nagha ||62||

so'smi saṃśayamāpannastwayi śānte kathaṃ bhawet |
iti te kāraṇaṃ tāta duḥkhasyoktamaśeṣataḥ ||63||

tatastatkāraṇaṃ jñātwā kṛtsnaṃ caiwamaśeṣataḥ |
dewawrato mahābuddhiḥ prayayāwanucintayan ||64||

abhyagacchattadaiwāśu wṛddhāmātyaṃ piturhitam |
tamapṛcchattadābhyetya pitustacchokakāraṇam ||65||

tasmai sa kurumukhyāya yathāwatparipṛcchate |
waraṃ śaśaṃsa kanyāṃ tāmuddiśya bharatarṣabha ||66||

tato dewawrato wṛddhaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ sahitastadā |
abhigamya dāśarājānaṃ kanyāṃ wawre pituḥ swayam ||67||

taṃ dāśaḥ pratijagrāha widhiwatpratipūjya ca |
abrawīccainamāsīnaṃ rājasaṃsadi bhārata ||68||

twamewa nāthaḥ paryāptaḥ śantanoḥ puruṣarṣabha |
putraḥ putrawatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kiṃ nu wakṣyāmi te wacaḥ ||69||

ko hi sambandhakaṃ ślāghyamīpsitaṃ yaunamīdṛśam |
atikrāmanna tapyeta sākṣādapi śatakratuḥ ||70||

apatyaṃ caitadāryasya yo yuṣmākaṃ samo guṇaiḥ |
yasya śukrātsatyawatī prādurbhūtā yaśaswinī ||71||

tena me bahuśastāta pitā te parikīrtitaḥ |
arhaḥ satyawatīṃ woḍhuṃ sarwarājasu bhārata ||72||

asito hyapi dewarṣiḥ pratyākhyātaḥ purā mayā |
satyawatyā bhṛśaṃ hyarthī sa āsīdṛṣisattamaḥ ||73||

kanyāpitṛtwātkiñcittu wakṣyāmi bharatarṣabha |
balawatsapatnatāmatra doṣaṃ paśyāmi kewalam ||74||

yasya hi twaṃ sapatnaḥ syā gandharwasyāsurasya wā |
na sa jātu sukhaṃ jīwettwayi kruddhe parantapa ||75||

etāwānatra doṣo hi nānyaḥ kaścana pārthiwa |
etajjānīhi bhadraṃ te dānādāne parantapa ||76||

ewamuktastu gāṅgeyastadyuktaṃ pratyabhāṣata |
śṛṇwatāṃ bhūmipālānāṃ piturarthāya bhārata ||77||

idaṃ me matamādatswa satyaṃ satyawatāṃ wara |
naiwa jāto na wājāta īdṛśaṃ waktumutsahet ||78||

ewametatkariṣyāmi yathā twamanubhāṣase |
yo'syāṃ janiṣyate putraḥ sa no rājā bhawiṣyati ||79||

ityuktaḥ punarewātha taṃ dāśaḥ pratyabhāṣata |
cikīrṣurduṣkaraṃ karma rājyārthe bharatarṣabha ||80||

twamewa nāthaḥ paryāptaḥ śantanoramitadyuteḥ |
kanyāyāścaiwa dharmātmanprabhurdānāya ceśwaraḥ ||81||

idaṃ tu wacanaṃ saumya kāryaṃ caiwa nibodha me |
kaumārikāṇāṃ śīlena wakṣyāmyahamariṃdama ||82||

yattwayā satyawatyarthe satyadharmaparāyaṇa |
rājamadhye pratijñātamanurūpaṃ tawaiwa tat ||83||

nānyathā tanmahābāho saṃśayo'tra na kaścana |
tawāpatyaṃ bhawedyattu tatra naḥ saṃśayo mahān ||84||

tasya tanmatamājñāya satyadharmaparāyaṇaḥ |
pratyajānāttadā rājanpituḥ priyacikīrṣayā ||85||

dewawrata uwāca||

dāśarāja nibodhedaṃ wacanaṃ me nṛpottama |
śṛṇwatāṃ bhūmipālānāṃ yadbrawīmi pituḥ kṛte ||86||

rājyaṃ tāwatpūrwamewa mayā tyaktaṃ narādhipa |
apatyahetorapi ca karomyeṣa winiścayam ||87||

adya prabhṛti me dāśa brahmacaryaṃ bhawiṣyati |
aputrasyāpi me lokā bhawiṣyantyakṣayā diwi ||88||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tasya tadwacanaṃ śrutwā samprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ |
dadānītyewa taṃ dāśo dharmātmā pratyabhāṣata ||89||

tato'ntarikṣe'psaraso dewāḥ sarṣigaṇāstathā |
abhyawarṣanta kusumairbhīṣmo'yamiti cābruwan ||90||

tataḥ sa piturarthāya tāmuwāca yaśaswinīm |
adhiroha rathaṃ mātargacchāwaḥ swagṛhāniti ||91||

ewamuktwā tu bhīṣmastāṃ rathamāropya bhāminīm |
āgamya hāstinapuraṃ śantanoḥ saṃnyawedayat ||92||

tasya tadduṣkaraṃ karma praśaśaṃsurnarādhipāḥ |
sametāśca pṛthakcaiwa bhīṣmo'yamiti cābruwan ||93||

taddṛṣṭwā duṣkaraṃ karma kṛtaṃ bhīṣmeṇa śantanuḥ |
swacchandamaraṇaṃ tasmai dadau tuṣṭaḥ pitā swayam ||94||






                  95


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato wiwāhe nirwṛtte sa rājā śantanurnṛpaḥ |
tāṃ kanyāṃ rūpasampannāṃ swagṛhe saṃnyaweśayat ||1||

tataḥ śāntanawo dhīmānsatyawatyāmajāyata |
wīraścitrāṅgado nāma wīryeṇa manujānati ||2||

athāparaṃ maheṣwāsaṃ satyawatyāṃ punaḥ prabhuḥ |
wicitrawīryaṃ rājānaṃ janayāmāsa wīryawān ||3||

aprāptawati tasmiṃśca yauwanaṃ bharatarṣabha |
sa rājā śantanurdhīmānkāladharmamupeyiwān ||4||

swargate śantanau bhīṣmaścitrāṅgadamariṃdamam |
sthāpayāmāsa wai rājye satyawatyā mate sthitaḥ ||5||

sa tu citrāṅgadaḥ śauryātsarwāṃścikṣepa pārthiwān |
manuṣyaṃ na hi mene sa kañcitsadṛśamātmanaḥ ||6||

taṃ kṣipantaṃ surāṃścaiwa manuṣyānasurāṃstathā |
gandharwarājo balawāṃstulyanāmābhyayāttadā ||7||

tenāsya sumahadyuddhaṃ kurukṣetre babhūwa ha ||7||

tayorbalawatostatra gandharwakurumukhyayoḥ |
nadyāstīre hiraṇwatyāḥ samāstisro'bhawadraṇaḥ ||8||

tasminwimarde tumule śastrawṛṣṭisamākule |
māyādhiko'wadhīdwīraṃ gandharwaḥ kurusattamam ||9||

citrāṅgadaṃ kuruśreṣṭhaṃ wicitraśarakārmukam |
antāya kṛtwā gandharwo diwamācakrame tataḥ ||10||

tasminnṛpatiśārdūle nihate bhūriwarcasi |
bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawo rājanpretakāryāṇyakārayat ||11||

wicitrawīryaṃ ca tadā bālamaprāptayauwanam |
kururājye mahābāhurabhyaṣiñcadanantaram ||12||

wicitrawīryastu tadā bhīṣmasya wacane sthitaḥ |
anwaśāsanmahārāja pitṛpaitāmahaṃ padam ||13||

sa dharmaśāstrakuśalo bhīṣmaṃ śāntanawaṃ nṛpaḥ |
pūjayāmāsa dharmeṇa sa cainaṃ pratyapālayat ||14||






                  96


waiśampāyana uwāca||

hate citrāṅgade bhīṣmo bāle bhrātari cānagha |
pālayāmāsa tadrājyaṃ satyawatyā mate sthitaḥ ||1||

samprāptayauwanaṃ paśyanbhrātaraṃ dhīmatāṃ waram |
bhīṣmo wicitrawīryasya wiwāhāyākaronmatim ||2||

atha kāśipaterbhīṣmaḥ kanyāstisro'psaraḥsamāḥ |
śuśrāwa sahitā rājanwṛṇwatīrwai swayaṃ waram ||3||

tataḥ sa rathināṃ śreṣṭho rathenaikena warmabhṛt |
jagāmānumate mātuḥ purīṃ wārāṇasīṃ prati ||4||

tatra rājñaḥ samuditānsarwataḥ samupāgatān |
dadarśa kanyāstāścaiwa bhīṣmaḥ śantanunandanaḥ ||5||

kīrtyamāneṣu rājñāṃ tu nāmaswatha sahasraśaḥ |
bhīṣmaḥ swayaṃ tadā rājanwarayāmāsa tāḥ prabhuḥ ||6||

uwāca ca mahīpālānrājañjaladaniḥswanaḥ |
rathamāropya tāḥ kanyā bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ waraḥ ||7||

āhūya dānaṃ kanyānāṃ guṇawadbhyaḥ smṛtaṃ budhaiḥ |
alaṅkṛtya yathāśakti pradāya ca dhanānyapi ||8||

prayacchantyapare kanyāṃ mithunena gawāmapi |
wittena kathitenānye balenānye'numānya ca ||9||

pramattāmupayāntyanye swayamanye ca windate |
aṣṭamaṃ tamatho witta wiwāhaṃ kawibhiḥ smṛtam ||10||

swayaṃwaraṃ tu rājanyāḥ praśaṃsantyupayānti ca |
pramathya tu hṛtāmāhurjyāyasīṃ dharmawādinaḥ ||11||

tā imāḥ pṛthiwīpālā jihīrṣāmi balāditaḥ |
te yatadhwaṃ paraṃ śaktyā wijayāyetarāya wā ||12||

sthito'haṃ pṛthiwīpālā yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ ||12||

ewamuktwā mahīpālānkāśirājaṃ ca wīryawān |
sarwāḥ kanyāḥ sa kaurawyo rathamāropayatswakam ||13||

āmantrya ca sa tānprāyācchīghraṃ kanyāḥ pragṛhya tāḥ ||13||

tataste pārthiwāḥ sarwe samutpeturamarṣitāḥ |
saṃspṛśantaḥ swakānbāhūndaśanto daśanacchadān ||14||

teṣāmābharaṇānyāśu twaritānāṃ wimuñcatām |
āmuñcatāṃ ca warmāṇi sambhramaḥ sumahānabhūt ||15||

tārāṇāmiwa sampāto babhūwa janamejaya |
bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca śubhrāṇāṃ kawacānāṃ ca sarwaśaḥ ||16||

sawarmabhirbhūṣaṇaiste drāgbhrājadbhiritastataḥ |
sakrodhāmarṣajihmabhrūsakaṣāyadṛśastathā ||17||

sūtopakḷptānrucirānsadaśwodyatadhūrgatān |
rathānāsthāya te wīrāḥ sarwapraharaṇānwitāḥ ||18||

prayāntamekaṃ kaurawyamanusasrurudāyudhāḥ ||18||

tataḥ samabhawadyuddhaṃ teṣāṃ tasya ca bhārata |
ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ||19||

te twiṣūndaśasāhasrāṃstasmai yugapadākṣipan |
aprāptāṃścaiwa tānāśu bhīṣmaḥ sarwāṃstadācchinat ||20||

tataste pārthiwāḥ sarwe sarwataḥ pariwārayan |
wawarṣuḥ śarawarṣeṇa warṣeṇewādrimambudāḥ ||21||

sa tadbāṇamayaṃ warṣaṃ śarairāwārya sarwataḥ |
tataḥ sarwānmahīpālānpratyawidhyattribhistribhiḥ ||22||

tasyāti puruṣānanyāṃllāghawaṃ rathacāriṇaḥ |
rakṣaṇaṃ cātmanaḥ saṅkhye śatrawo'pyabhyapūjayan ||23||

tānwinirjitya tu raṇe sarwaśastrawiśāradaḥ |
kanyābhiḥ sahitaḥ prāyādbhārato bhāratānprati ||24||

tatastaṃ pṛṣṭhato rājañśālwarājo mahārathaḥ |
abhyāhanadameyātmā bhīṣmaṃ śāntanawaṃ raṇe ||25||

wāraṇaṃ jaghane nighnandantābhyāmaparo yathā |
wāśitāmanusamprāpto yūthapo balināṃ waraḥ ||26||

strīkāma tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti bhīṣmamāha sa pārthiwaḥ |
śālwarājo mahābāhuramarṣeṇābhicoditaḥ ||27||

tataḥ sa puruṣawyāghro bhīṣmaḥ parabalārdanaḥ |
tadwākyākulitaḥ krodhādwidhūmo'gniriwa jwalan ||28||

kṣatradharmaṃ samāsthāya wyapetabhayasambhramaḥ |
niwartayāmāsa rathaṃ śālwaṃ prati mahārathaḥ ||29||

niwartamānaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭwā rājānaḥ sarwa ewa te |
prekṣakāḥ samapadyanta bhīṣmaśālwasamāgame ||30||

tau wṛṣāwiwa nardantau balinau wāśitāntare |
anyonyamabhiwartetāṃ balawikramaśālinau ||31||

tato bhīṣmaṃ śāntanawaṃ śaraiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ |
śālwarājo naraśreṣṭhaḥ samawākiradāśugaiḥ ||32||

pūrwamabhyarditaṃ dṛṣṭwā bhīṣmaṃ śālwena te nṛpāḥ |
wismitāḥ samapadyanta sādhu sādhwiti cābruwan ||33||

lāghawaṃ tasya te dṛṣṭwā saṃyuge sarwapārthiwāḥ |
apūjayanta saṃhṛṣṭā wāgbhiḥ śālwaṃ narādhipāḥ ||34||

kṣatriyāṇāṃ tadā wācaḥ śrutwā parapurañjayaḥ |
kruddhaḥ śāntanawo bhīṣmastiṣṭha tiṣṭhetyabhāṣata ||35||

sārathiṃ cābrawītkruddho yāhi yatraiṣa pārthiwaḥ |
yāwadenaṃ nihanmyadya bhujaṅgamiwa pakṣirāṭ ||36||

tato'straṃ wāruṇaṃ samyagyojayāmāsa kaurawaḥ |
tenāśwāṃścaturo'mṛdnācchālwarājño narādhipa ||37||

astrairastrāṇi saṃwārya śālwarājñaḥ sa kaurawaḥ |
bhīṣmo nṛpatiśārdūla nyawadhīttasya sārathim ||38||

astreṇa cāpyathaikena nyawadhītturagottamān ||38||

kanyāhetornaraśreṣṭha bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawastadā |
jitwā wisarjayāmāsa jīwantaṃ nṛpasattamam ||39||

tataḥ śālwaḥ swanagaraṃ prayayau bharatarṣabha ||39||

rājāno ye ca tatrāsanswayaṃwaradidṛkṣawaḥ |
swānyewa te'pi rāṣṭrāṇi jagmuḥ parapurañjaya ||40||

ewaṃ wijitya tāḥ kanyā bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ waraḥ |
prayayau hāstinapuraṃ yatra rājā sa kaurawaḥ ||41||

so'cireṇaiwa kālena atyakrāmannarādhipa |
wanāni saritaścaiwa śailāṃśca wiwidhadrumān ||42||

akṣataḥ kṣapayitwārīnsaṅkhye'saṅkhyeyawikramaḥ |
ānayāmāsa kāśyasya sutāḥ sāgaragāsutaḥ ||43||

snuṣā iwa sa dharmātmā bhaginya iwa cānujāḥ |
yathā duhitaraścaiwa pratigṛhya yayau kurūn ||44||

tāḥ sarwā guṇasampannā bhrātā bhrātre yawīyase |
bhīṣmo wicitrawīryāya pradadau wikramāhṛtāḥ ||45||

satāṃ dharmeṇa dharmajñaḥ kṛtwā karmātimānuṣam |
bhrāturwicitrawīryasya wiwāhāyopacakrame ||46||

satyawatyā saha mithaḥ kṛtwā niścayamātmawān ||46||

wiwāhaṃ kārayiṣyantaṃ bhīṣmaṃ kāśipateḥ sutā |
jyeṣṭhā tāsāmidaṃ wākyamabrawīddha satī tadā ||47||

mayā saubhapatiḥ pūrwaṃ manasābhiwṛtaḥ patiḥ |
tena cāsmi wṛtā pūrwameṣa kāmaśca me pituḥ ||48||

mayā warayitawyo'bhūcchālwastasminswayaṃware |
etadwijñāya dharmajña tatastwaṃ dharmamācara ||49||

ewamuktastayā bhīṣmaḥ kanyayā wiprasaṃsadi |
cintāmabhyagamadwīro yuktāṃ tasyaiwa karmaṇaḥ ||50||

sa winiścitya dharmajño brāhmaṇairwedapāragaiḥ |
anujajñe tadā jyeṣṭāmambāṃ kāśipateḥ sutām ||51||

ambikāmbālike bhārye prādādbhrātre yawīyase |
bhīṣmo wicitrawīryāya widhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ||52||

tayoḥ pāṇiṃ gṛhītwā sa rūpayauwanadarpitaḥ |
wicitrawīryo dharmātmā kāmātmā samapadyata ||53||

te cāpi bṛhatī śyāme nīlakuñcitamūrdhaje |
raktatuṅganakhopete pīnaśroṇipayodhare ||54||

ātmanaḥ pratirūpo'sau labdhaḥ patiriti sthite |
wicitrawīryaṃ kalyāṇaṃ pūjayāmāsatustu te ||55||

sa cāświrūpasadṛśo dewasattwaparākramaḥ |
sarwāsāmewa nārīṇāṃ cittapramathano'bhawat ||56||

tābhyāṃ saha samāḥ sapta wiharanpṛthiwīpatiḥ |
wicitrawīryastaruṇo yakṣmāṇaṃ samapadyata ||57||

suhṛdāṃ yatamānānāmāptaiḥ saha cikitsakaiḥ |
jagāmāstamiwādityaḥ kaurawyo yamasādanam ||58||

pretakāryāṇi sarwāṇi tasya samyagakārayat |
rājño wicitrawīryasya satyawatyā mate sthitaḥ ||59||

ṛtwigbhiḥ sahito bhīṣmaḥ sarwaiśca kurupuṅgawaiḥ ||59||






                  97


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ satyawatī dīnā kṛpaṇā putragṛddhinī |
putrasya kṛtwā kāryāṇi snuṣābhyāṃ saha bhārata ||1||

dharmaṃ ca pitṛwaṃśaṃ ca mātṛwaṃśaṃ ca māninī |
prasamīkṣya mahābhāgā gāṅgeyaṃ wākyamabrawīt ||2||

śantanordharmanityasya kaurawyasya yaśaswinaḥ |
twayi piṇḍaśca kīrtiśca santānaṃ ca pratiṣṭhitam ||3||

yathā karma śubhaṃ kṛtwā swargopagamanaṃ dhruwam |
yathā cāyurdhruwaṃ satye twayi dharmastathā dhruwaḥ ||4||

wettha dharmāṃśca dharmajña samāsenetareṇa ca |
wiwidhāstwaṃ śrutīrwettha wettha wedāṃśca sarwaśaḥ ||5||

wyawasthānaṃ ca te dharme kulācāraṃ ca lakṣaye |
pratipattiṃ ca kṛcchreṣu śukrāṅgirasayoriwa ||6||

tasmātsubhṛśamāśwasya twayi dharmabhṛtāṃ wara |
kārye twāṃ winiyokṣyāmi tacchrutwā kartumarhasi ||7||

mama putrastawa bhrātā wīryawānsupriyaśca te |
bāla ewa gataḥ swargamaputraḥ puruṣarṣabha ||8||

ime mahiṣyau bhrātuste kāśirājasute śubhe |
rūpayauwanasampanne putrakāme ca bhārata ||9||

tayorutpādayāpatyaṃ santānāya kulasya naḥ |
manniyogānmahābhāga dharmaṃ kartumihārhasi ||10||

rājye caiwābhiṣicyaswa bhāratānanuśādhi ca |
dārāṃśca kuru dharmeṇa mā nimajjīḥ pitāmahān ||11||

tathocyamāno mātrā ca suhṛdbhiśca parantapaḥ |
pratyuwāca sa dharmātmā dharmyamewottaraṃ wacaḥ ||12||

asaṃśayaṃ paro dharmastwayā mātarudāhṛtaḥ |
twamapatyaṃ prati ca me pratijñāṃ wettha wai parām ||13||

jānāsi ca yathāwṛttaṃ śulkahetostwadantare |
sa satyawati satyaṃ te pratijānāmyahaṃ punaḥ ||14||

parityajeyaṃ trailokyaṃ rājyaṃ deweṣu wā punaḥ |
yadwāpyadhikametābhyāṃ na tu satyaṃ kathañcana ||15||

tyajecca pṛthiwī gandhamāpaśca rasamātmanaḥ |
jyotistathā tyajedrūpaṃ wāyuḥ sparśaguṇaṃ tyajet ||16||

prabhāṃ samutsṛjedarko dhūmaketustathoṣṇatām |
tyajecchabdaṃ tathākāśaḥ somaḥ śītāṃśutāṃ tyajet ||17||

wikramaṃ wṛtrahā jahyāddharmaṃ jahyācca dharmarāṭ |
na twahaṃ satyamutsraṣṭuṃ wyawaseyaṃ kathañcana ||18||

ewamuktā tu putreṇa bhūridrawiṇatejasā |
mātā satyawatī bhīṣmamuwāca tadanantaram ||19||

jānāmi te sthitiṃ satye parāṃ satyaparākrama |
icchansṛjethāstrīṃllokānanyāṃstwaṃ swena tejasā ||20||

jānāmi caiwa satyaṃ tanmadarthaṃ yadabhāṣathāḥ |
āpaddharmamawekṣaswa waha paitāmahīṃ dhuram ||21||

yathā te kulatantuśca dharmaśca na parābhawet |
suhṛdaśca prahṛṣyeraṃstathā kuru parantapa ||22||

lālapyamānāṃ tāmewaṃ kṛpaṇāṃ putragṛddhinīm |
dharmādapetaṃ bruwatīṃ bhīṣmo bhūyo'brawīdidam ||23||

rājñi dharmānawekṣaswa mā naḥ sarwānwyanīnaśaḥ |
satyāccyutiḥ kṣatriyasya na dharmeṣu praśasyate ||24||

śantanorapi santānaṃ yathā syādakṣayaṃ bhuwi |
tatte dharmaṃ prawakṣyāmi kṣātraṃ rājñi sanātanam ||25||

śrutwā taṃ pratipadyethāḥ prājñaiḥ saha purohitaiḥ |
āpaddharmārthakuśalairlokatantramawekṣya ca ||26||






                  98


bhīṣma uwāca||

jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa piturwadhamamṛṣyatā |
kruddhena ca mahābhāge haihayādhipatirhataḥ ||1||

śatāni daśa bāhūnāṃ nikṛttānyarjunasya wai ||1||

punaśca dhanurādāya mahāstrāṇi pramuñcatā |
nirdagdhaṃ kṣatramasakṛdrathena jayatā mahīm ||2||

ewamuccāwacairastrairbhārgaweṇa mahātmanā |
triḥsaptakṛtwaḥ pṛthiwī kṛtā niḥkṣatriyā purā ||3||

tataḥ sambhūya sarwābhiḥ kṣatriyābhiḥ samantataḥ |
utpāditānyapatyāni brāhmaṇairniyatātmabhiḥ ||4||

pāṇigrāhasya tanaya iti wedeṣu niścitam |
dharmaṃ manasi saṃsthāpya brāhmaṇāṃstāḥ samabhyayuḥ ||5||

loke'pyācarito dṛṣṭaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ punarbhawaḥ ||5||

athotathya iti khyāta āsīddhīmānṛṣiḥ purā |
mamatā nāma tasyāsīdbhāryā paramasaṃmatā ||6||

utathyasya yawīyāṃstu purodhāstridiwaukasām |
bṛhaspatirbṛhattejā mamatāṃ so'nwapadyata ||7||

uwāca mamatā taṃ tu dewaraṃ wadatāṃ waram |
antarwatnī ahaṃ bhrātrā jyeṣṭhenāramyatāmiti ||8||

ayaṃ ca me mahābhāga kukṣāwewa bṛhaspate |
autathyo wedamatraiwa ṣaḍaṅgaṃ pratyadhīyata ||9||

amogharetāstwaṃ cāpi nūnaṃ bhawitumarhasi |
tasmādewaṅgate'dya twamupāramitumarhasi ||10||

ewamuktastayā samyagbṛhattejā bṛhaspatiḥ |
kāmātmānaṃ tadātmānaṃ na śaśāka niyacchitum ||11||

sambabhūwa tataḥ kāmī tayā sārdhamakāmayā |
utsṛjantaṃ tu taṃ retaḥ sa garbhastho'bhyabhāṣata ||12||

bhostāta kanyasa wade dwayornāstyatra sambhawaḥ |
amoghaśukraśca bhawānpūrwaṃ cāhamihāgataḥ ||13||

śaśāpa taṃ tataḥ kruddha ewamukto bṛhaspatiḥ |
utathyaputraṃ garbhasthaṃ nirbhartsya bhagawānṛṣiḥ ||14||

yasmāttwamīdṛśe kāle sarwabhūtepsite sati |
ewamāttha wacastasmāttamo dīrghaṃ prawekṣyasi ||15||

sa wai dīrghatamā nāma śāpādṛṣirajāyata |
bṛhaspaterbṛhatkīrterbṛhaspatiriwaujasā ||16||

sa putrāñjanayāmāsa gautamādīnmahāyaśāḥ |
ṛṣerutathyasya tadā santānakulawṛddhaye ||17||

lobhamohābhibhūtāste putrāstaṃ gautamādayaḥ |
kāṣṭhe samudge prakṣipya gaṅgāyāṃ samawāsṛjan ||18||

na syādandhaśca wṛddhaśca bhartawyo'yamiti sma te |
cintayitwā tataḥ krūrāḥ pratijagmuratho gṛhān ||19||

so'nusrotastadā rājanplawamāna ṛṣistataḥ |
jagāma subahūndeśānandhastenoḍupena ha ||20||

taṃ tu rājā balirnāma sarwadharmawiśāradaḥ |
apaśyanmajjanagataḥ srotasābhyāśamāgatam ||21||

jagrāha cainaṃ dharmātmā baliḥ satyaparākramaḥ |
jñātwā cainaṃ sa wawre'tha putrārthaṃ manujarṣabha ||22||

santānārthaṃ mahābhāga bhāryāsu mama mānada |
putrāndharmārthakuśalānutpādayitumarhasi ||23||

ewamuktaḥ sa tejaswī taṃ tathetyuktawānṛṣiḥ |
tasmai sa rājā swāṃ bhāryāṃ sudeṣṇāṃ prāhiṇottadā ||24||

andhaṃ wṛddhaṃ ca taṃ matwā na sā dewī jagāma ha |
swāṃ tu dhātreyikāṃ tasmai wṛddhāya prāhiṇottadā ||25||

tasyāṃ kākṣīwadādīnsa śūdrayonāwṛṣirwaśī |
janayāmāsa dharmātmā putrānekādaśaiwa tu ||26||

kākṣīwadādīnputrāṃstāndṛṣṭwā sarwānadhīyataḥ |
uwāca tamṛṣiṃ rājā mamaita iti wīryawān ||27||

netyuwāca maharṣistaṃ mamaiwaita iti bruwan |
śūdrayonau mayā hīme jātāḥ kākṣīwadādayaḥ ||28||

andhaṃ wṛddhaṃ ca māṃ matwā sudeṣṇā mahiṣī tawa |
awamanya dadau mūḍhā śūdrāṃ dhātreyikāṃ hi me ||29||

tataḥ prasādayāmāsa punastamṛṣisattamam |
baliḥ sudeṣṇāṃ bhāryāṃ ca tasmai tāṃ prāhiṇotpunaḥ ||30||

tāṃ sa dīrghatamāṅgeṣu spṛṣṭwā dewīmathābrawīt |
bhawiṣyati kumāraste tejaswī satyawāgiti ||31||

tatrāṅgo nāma rājarṣiḥ sudeṣṇāyāmajāyata |
ewamanye maheṣwāsā brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyā bhuwi ||32||

jātāḥ paramadharmajñā wīryawanto mahābalāḥ |
etacchrutwā twamapyatra mātaḥ kuru yathepsitam ||33||






                  99


bhīṣma uwāca||

punarbharatawaṃśasya hetuṃ santānawṛddhaye |
wakṣyāmi niyataṃ mātastanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu ||1||

brāhmaṇo guṇawānkaściddhanenopanimantryatām |
wicitrawīryakṣetreṣu yaḥ samutpādayetprajāḥ ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ satyawatī bhīṣmaṃ wācā saṃsajjamānayā |
wihasantīwa sawrīḍamidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||3||

satyametanmahābāho yathā wadasi bhārata |
wiśwāsātte prawakṣyāmi santānāya kulasya ca ||4||

na te śakyamanākhyātumāpaddhīyaṃ tathāwidhā ||4||

twamewa naḥ kule dharmastwaṃ satyaṃ twaṃ parā gatiḥ |
tasmānniśamya wākyaṃ me kuruṣwa yadanantaram ||5||

dharmayuktasya dharmātmanpiturāsīttarī mama |
sā kadācidahaṃ tatra gatā prathamayauwane ||6||

atha dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ paramarṣiḥ parāśaraḥ |
ājagāma tarīṃ dhīmāṃstariṣyanyamunāṃ nadīm ||7||

sa tāryamāṇo yamunāṃ māmupetyābrawīttadā |
sāntwapūrwaṃ muniśreṣṭhaḥ kāmārto madhuraṃ bahu ||8||

tamahaṃ śāpabhītā ca piturbhītā ca bhārata |
warairasulabhairuktā na pratyākhyātumutsahe ||9||

abhibhūya sa māṃ bālāṃ tejasā waśamānayat |
tamasā lokamāwṛtya naugatāmewa bhārata ||10||

matsyagandho mahānāsītpurā mama jugupsitaḥ |
tamapāsya śubhaṃ gandhamimaṃ prādātsa me muniḥ ||11||

tato māmāha sa munirgarbhamutsṛjya māmakam |
dwīpe'syā ewa saritaḥ kanyaiwa twaṃ bhawiṣyasi ||12||

pārāśaryo mahāyogī sa babhūwa mahānṛṣiḥ |
kanyāputro mama purā dwaipāyana iti smṛtaḥ ||13||

yo wyasya wedāṃścaturastapasā bhagawānṛṣiḥ |
loke wyāsatwamāpede kārṣṇyātkṛṣṇatwamewa ca ||14||

satyawādī śamaparastapaswī dagdhakilbiṣaḥ |
sa niyukto mayā wyaktaṃ twayā ca amitadyute ||15||

bhrātuḥ kṣetreṣu kalyāṇamapatyaṃ janayiṣyati ||15||

sa hi māmuktawāṃstatra smareḥ kṛtyeṣu māmiti |
taṃ smariṣye mahābāho yadi bhīṣma twamicchasi ||16||

tawa hyanumate bhīṣma niyataṃ sa mahātapāḥ |
wicitrawīryakṣetreṣu putrānutpādayiṣyati ||17||

maharṣeḥ kīrtane tasya bhīṣmaḥ prāñjalirabrawīt |
dharmamarthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca trīnetānyo'nupaśyati ||18||

arthamarthānubandhaṃ ca dharmaṃ dharmānubandhanam |
kāmaṃ kāmānubandhaṃ ca wiparītānpṛthakpṛthak ||19||

yo wicintya dhiyā samyagwyawasyati sa buddhimān ||19||

tadidaṃ dharmayuktaṃ ca hitaṃ caiwa kulasya naḥ |
uktaṃ bhawatyā yacchreyaḥ paramaṃ rocate mama ||20||

tatastasminpratijñāte bhīṣmeṇa kurunandana |
kṛṣṇadwaipāyanaṃ kālī cintayāmāsa wai munim ||21||

sa wedānwibruwandhīmānmāturwijñāya cintitam |
prādurbabhūwāwiditaḥ kṣaṇena kurunandana ||22||

tasmai pūjāṃ tadā dattwā sutāya widhipūrwakam |
pariṣwajya ca bāhubhyāṃ prasnawairabhiṣicya ca ||23||

mumoca bāṣpaṃ dāśeyī putraṃ dṛṣṭwā cirasya tam ||23||

tāmadbhiḥ pariṣicyārtāṃ maharṣirabhiwādya ca |
mātaraṃ pūrwajaḥ putro wyāso wacanamabrawīt ||24||

bhawatyā yadabhipretaṃ tadahaṃ kartumāgataḥ |
śādhi māṃ dharmatattwajñe karawāṇi priyaṃ tawa ||25||

tasmai pūjāṃ tato'kārṣītpurodhāḥ paramarṣaye |
sa ca tāṃ pratijagrāha widhiwanmantrapūrwakam ||26||

tamāsanagataṃ mātā pṛṣṭwā kuśalamawyayam |
satyawatyabhiwīkṣyainamuwācedamanantaram ||27||

mātāpitroḥ prajāyante putrāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ kawe |
teṣāṃ pitā yathā swāmī tathā mātā na saṃśayaḥ ||28||

widhātṛwihitaḥ sa twaṃ yathā me prathamaḥ sutaḥ |
wicitrawīryo brahmarṣe tathā me'warajaḥ sutaḥ ||29||

yathaiwa pitṛto bhīṣmastathā twamapi mātṛtaḥ |
bhrātā wicitrawīryasya yathā wā putra manyase ||30||

ayaṃ śāntanawaḥ satyaṃ pālayansatyawikramaḥ |
buddhiṃ na kurute'patye tathā rājyānuśāsane ||31||

sa twaṃ wyapekṣayā bhrātuḥ santānāya kulasya ca |
bhīṣmasya cāsya wacanānniyogācca mamānagha ||32||

anukrośācca bhūtānāṃ sarweṣāṃ rakṣaṇāya ca |
ānṛśaṃsyena yadbrūyāṃ tacchrutwā kartumarhasi ||33||

yawīyasastawa bhrāturbhārye surasutopame |
rūpayauwanasampanne putrakāme ca dharmataḥ ||34||

tayorutpādayāpatyaṃ samartho hyasi putraka |
anurūpaṃ kulasyāsya santatyāḥ prasawasya ca ||35||

wyāsa uwāca||

wettha dharmaṃ satyawati paraṃ cāparamewa ca |
yathā ca tawa dharmajñe dharme praṇihitā matiḥ ||36||

tasmādahaṃ twanniyogāddharmamuddiśya kāraṇam |
īpsitaṃ te kariṣyāmi dṛṣṭaṃ hyetatpurātanam ||37||

bhrātuḥ putrānpradāsyāmi mitrāwaruṇayoḥ samān |
wrataṃ caretāṃ te dewyau nirdiṣṭamiha yanmayā ||38||

saṃwatsaraṃ yathānyāyaṃ tataḥ śuddhe bhawiṣyataḥ |
na hi māmawratopetā upeyātkācidaṅganā ||39||

satyawatyuwāca||

yathā sadyaḥ prapadyeta dewī garbhaṃ tathā kuru |
arājakeṣu rāṣṭreṣu nāsti wṛṣṭirna dewatāḥ ||40||

kathamarājakaṃ rāṣṭraṃ śakyaṃ dhārayituṃ prabho |
tasmādgarbhaṃ samādhatswa bhīṣmastaṃ wardhayiṣyati ||41||

wyāsa uwāca||

yadi putraḥ pradātawyo mayā kṣipramakālikam |
wirūpatāṃ me sahatāmetadasyāḥ paraṃ wratam ||42||

yadi me sahate gandhaṃ rūpaṃ weṣaṃ tathā wapuḥ |
adyaiwa garbhaṃ kausalyā wiśiṣṭaṃ pratipadyatām ||43||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

samāgamanamākāṅkṣanniti so'ntarhito muniḥ |
tato'bhigamya sā dewī snuṣāṃ rahasi saṅgatām ||44||

dharmyamarthasamāyuktamuwāca wacanaṃ hitam ||44||

kausalye dharmatantraṃ yadbrawīmi twāṃ nibodha me |
bharatānāṃ samucchedo wyaktaṃ madbhāgyasaṅkṣayāt ||45||

wyathitāṃ māṃ ca samprekṣya pitṛwaṃśaṃ ca pīḍitam |
bhīṣmo buddhimadānme'tra dharmasya ca wiwṛddhaye ||46||

sā ca buddhistawādhīnā putri jñātaṃ mayeti ha |
naṣṭaṃ ca bhārataṃ waṃśaṃ punarewa samuddhara ||47||

putraṃ janaya suśroṇi dewarājasamaprabham |
sa hi rājyadhuraṃ gurwīmudwakṣyati kulasya naḥ ||48||

sā dharmato'nunīyaināṃ kathañciddharmacāriṇīm |
bhojayāmāsa wiprāṃśca dewarṣīnatithīṃstathā ||49||






                  100


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ satyawatī kāle wadhūṃ snātāmṛtau tadā |
saṃweśayantī śayane śanakairwākyamabrawīt ||1||

kausalye dewaraste'sti so'dya twānuprawekṣyati |
apramattā pratīkṣainaṃ niśīthe āgamiṣyati ||2||

śwaśrwāstadwacanaṃ śrutwā śayānā śayane śubhe |
sācintayattadā bhīṣmamanyāṃśca kurupuṅgawān ||3||

tato'mbikāyāṃ prathamaṃ niyuktaḥ satyawāgṛṣiḥ |
dīpyamāneṣu dīpeṣu śayanaṃ prawiweśa ha ||4||

tasya kṛṣṇasya kapilā jaṭā dīpte ca locane |
babhrūṇi caiwa śmaśrūṇi dṛṣṭwā dewī nyamīlayat ||5||

sambabhūwa tayā rātrau mātuḥ priyacikīrṣayā |
bhayātkāśisutā taṃ tu nāśaknodabhiwīkṣitum ||6||

tato niṣkrāntamāsādya mātā putramathābrawīt |
apyasyāṃ guṇawānputra rājaputro bhawiṣyati ||7||

niśamya tadwaco māturwyāsaḥ paramabuddhimān |
prowācātīndriyajñāno widhinā sampracoditaḥ ||8||

nāgāyutasamaprāṇo widwānrājarṣisattamaḥ |
mahābhāgo mahāwīryo mahābuddhirbhawiṣyati ||9||

tasya cāpi śataṃ putrā bhawiṣyanti mahābalāḥ |
kiṃ tu mātuḥ sa waiguṇyādandha ewa bhawiṣyati ||10||

tasya tadwacanaṃ śrutwā mātā putramathābrawīt |
nāndhaḥ kurūṇāṃ nṛpatiranurūpastapodhana ||11||

jñātiwaṃśasya goptāraṃ pitṛṇāṃ waṃśawardhanam |
dwitīyaṃ kuruwaṃśasya rājānaṃ dātumarhasi ||12||

sa tatheti pratijñāya niścakrāma mahātapāḥ |
sāpi kālena kausalyā suṣuwe'ndhaṃ tamātmajam ||13||

punarewa tu sā dewī paribhāṣya snuṣāṃ tataḥ |
ṛṣimāwāhayatsatyā yathāpūrwamaninditā ||14||

tatastenaiwa widhinā maharṣistāmapadyata |
ambālikāmathābhyāgādṛṣiṃ dṛṣṭwā ca sāpi tam ||15||

wiṣaṇṇā pāṇḍusaṅkāśā samapadyata bhārata ||15||

tāṃ bhītāṃ pāṇḍusaṅkāśāṃ wiṣaṇṇāṃ prekṣya pārthiwa |
wyāsaḥ satyawatīputra idaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||16||

yasmātpāṇḍutwamāpannā wirūpaṃ prekṣya māmapi |
tasmādeṣa sutastubhyaṃ pāṇḍurewa bhawiṣyati ||17||

nāma cāsya tadeweha bhawiṣyati śubhānane |
ityuktwā sa nirākrāmadbhagawānṛṣisattamaḥ ||18||

tato niṣkrāntamālokya satyā putramabhāṣata |
śaśaṃsa sa punarmātre tasya bālasya pāṇḍutām ||19||

taṃ mātā punarewānyamekaṃ putramayācata |
tatheti ca maharṣistāṃ mātaraṃ pratyabhāṣata ||20||

tataḥ kumāraṃ sā dewī prāptakālamajījanat |
pāṇḍuṃ lakṣaṇasampannaṃ dīpyamānamiwa śriyā ||21||
