tasya putrā maheṣwāsā jajñire pañca pāṇḍawāḥ ||21||

ṛtukāle tato jyeṣṭhāṃ wadhūṃ tasmai nyayojayat |
sā tu rūpaṃ ca gandhaṃ ca maharṣeḥ prawicintya tam ||22||

nākarodwacanaṃ dewyā bhayātsurasutopamā ||22||

tataḥ swairbhūṣaṇairdāsīṃ bhūṣayitwāpsaropamām |
preṣayāmāsa kṛṣṇāya tataḥ kāśipateḥ sutā ||23||

dāsī ṛṣimanuprāptaṃ pratyudgamyābhiwādya ca |
saṃwiweśābhyanujñātā satkṛtyopacacāra ha ||24||

kāmopabhogena tu sa tasyāṃ tuṣṭimagādṛṣiḥ |
tayā sahoṣito rātriṃ maharṣiḥ prīyamāṇayā ||25||

uttiṣṭhannabrawīdenāmabhujiṣyā bhawiṣyasi |
ayaṃ ca te śubhe garbhaḥ śrīmānudaramāgataḥ ||26||

dharmātmā bhawitā loke sarwabuddhimatāṃ waraḥ ||26||

sa jajñe widuro nāma kṛṣṇadwaipāyanātmajaḥ |
dhṛtarāṣṭrasya ca bhrātā pāṇḍoścāmitabuddhimān ||27||

dharmo widurarūpeṇa śāpāttasya mahātmanaḥ |
māṇḍawyasyārthatattwajñaḥ kāmakrodhawiwarjitaḥ ||28||

sa dharmasyānṛṇo bhūtwā punarmātrā sametya ca |
tasyai garbhaṃ samāwedya tatraiwāntaradhīyata ||29||

ewaṃ wicitrawīryasya kṣetre dwaipāyanādapi |
jajñire dewagarbhābhāḥ kuruwaṃśawiwardhanāḥ ||30||






                  101


janamejaya uwāca||

kiṃ kṛtaṃ karma dharmeṇa yena śāpamupeyiwān |
kasya śāpācca brahmarṣe śūdrayonāwajāyata ||1||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

babhūwa brāhmaṇaḥ kaścinmāṇḍawya iti wiśrutaḥ |
dhṛtimānsarwadharmajñaḥ satye tapasi ca sthitaḥ ||2||

sa āśramapadadwāri wṛkṣamūle mahātapāḥ |
ūrdhwabāhurmahāyogī tasthau maunawratānwitaḥ ||3||

tasya kālena mahatā tasmiṃstapasi tiṣṭhataḥ |
tamāśramapadaṃ prāptā dasyawo loptrahāriṇaḥ ||4||

anusāryamāṇā bahubhī rakṣibhirbharatarṣabha ||4||

te tasyāwasathe loptraṃ nidadhuḥ kurusattama |
nidhāya ca bhayāllīnāstatraiwānwāgate bale ||5||

teṣu līneṣwatho śīghraṃ tatastadrakṣiṇāṃ balam |
ājagāma tato'paśyaṃstamṛṣiṃ taskarānugāḥ ||6||

tamapṛcchaṃstato rājaṃstathāwṛttaṃ tapodhanam |
katareṇa pathā yātā dasyawo dwijasattama ||7||

tena gacchāmahe brahmanpathā śīghrataraṃ wayam ||7||

tathā tu rakṣiṇāṃ teṣāṃ bruwatāṃ sa tapodhanaḥ |
na kiñcidwacanaṃ rājannawadatsādhwasādhu wā ||8||

tataste rājapuruṣā wicinwānāstadāśramam |
dadṛśustatra saṃlīnāṃstāṃścorāndrawyamewa ca ||9||

tataḥ śaṅkā samabhawadrakṣiṇāṃ taṃ muniṃ prati |
saṃyamyainaṃ tato rājñe dasyūṃścaiwa nyawedayan ||10||

taṃ rājā saha taiścorairanwaśādwadhyatāmiti |
sa wadhyaghātairajñātaḥ śūle proto mahātapāḥ ||11||

tataste śūlamāropya taṃ muniṃ rakṣiṇastadā |
pratijagmurmahīpālaṃ dhanānyādāya tānyatha ||12||

śūlasthaḥ sa tu dharmātmā kālena mahatā tataḥ |
nirāhāro'pi wiprarṣirmaraṇaṃ nābhyupāgamat ||13||

dhārayāmāsa ca prāṇānṛṣīṃśca samupānayat ||13||

śūlāgre tapyamānena tapastena mahātmanā |
santāpaṃ paramaṃ jagmurmunayo'tha parantapa ||14||

te rātrau śakunā bhūtwā saṃnyawartanta sarwataḥ |
darśayanto yathāśakti tamapṛcchandwijottamam ||15||

śrotumicchāmahe brahmankiṃ pāpaṃ kṛtawānasi ||15||

tataḥ sa muniśārdūlastānuwāca tapodhanān |
doṣataḥ kaṃ gamiṣyāmi na hi me'nyo'parādhyati ||16||

rājā ca tamṛṣiṃ śrutwā niṣkramya saha mantribhiḥ |
prasādayāmāsa tadā śūlasthamṛṣisattamam ||17||

yanmayāpakṛtaṃ mohādajñānādṛṣisattama |
prasādaye twāṃ tatrāhaṃ na me twaṃ kroddhumarhasi ||18||

ewamuktastato rājñā prasādamakaronmuniḥ |
kṛtaprasādo rājā taṃ tataḥ samawatārayat ||19||

awatārya ca śūlāgrāttacchūlaṃ niścakarṣa ha |
aśaknuwaṃśca niṣkraṣṭuṃ śūlaṃ mūle sa cicchide ||20||

sa tathāntargatenaiwa śūlena wyacaranmuniḥ |
sa tena tapasā lokānwijigye durlabhānparaiḥ ||21||

aṇīmāṇḍawya iti ca tato lokeṣu kathyate ||21||

sa gatwā sadanaṃ wipro dharmasya paramārthawit |
āsanasthaṃ tato dharmaṃ dṛṣṭwopālabhata prabhuḥ ||22||

kiṃ nu tadduṣkṛtaṃ karma mayā kṛtamajānatā |
yasyeyaṃ phalanirwṛttirīdṛśyāsāditā mayā ||23||

śīghramācakṣwa me tattwaṃ paśya me tapaso balam ||23||

dharma uwāca||

pataṅgakānāṃ puccheṣu twayeṣīkā praweśitā |
karmaṇastasya te prāptaṃ phalametattapodhana ||24||

aṇīmāṇḍawya uwāca||

alpe'parādhe wipulo mama daṇḍastwayā kṛtaḥ |
śūdrayonāwato dharma mānuṣaḥ sambhawiṣyasi ||25||

maryādāṃ sthāpayāmyadya loke dharmaphalodayām |
ā caturdaśamādwarṣānna bhawiṣyati pātakam ||26||

pareṇa kurwatāmewaṃ doṣa ewa bhawiṣyati ||26||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

etena twaparādhena śāpāttasya mahātmanaḥ |
dharmo widurarūpeṇa śūdrayonāwajāyata ||27||

dharme cārthe ca kuśalo lobhakrodhawiwarjitaḥ |
dīrghadarśī śamaparaḥ kurūṇāṃ ca hite rataḥ ||28||






                  102


waiśampāyana uwāca||

teṣu triṣu kumāreṣu jāteṣu kurujāṅgalam |
kurawo'tha kurukṣetraṃ trayametadawardhata ||1||

ūrdhwasasyābhawadbhūmiḥ sasyāni phalawanti ca |
yathartuwarṣī parjanyo bahupuṣpaphalā drumāḥ ||2||

wāhanāni prahṛṣṭāni muditā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ |
gandhawanti ca mālyāni rasawanti phalāni ca ||3||

waṇigbhiścāwakīryanta nagarāṇyatha śilpibhiḥ |
śūrāśca kṛtawidyāśca santaśca sukhino'bhawan ||4||

nābhawandasyawaḥ kecinnādharmarucayo janāḥ |
pradeśeṣwapi rāṣṭrāṇāṃ kṛtaṃ yugamawartata ||5||

dānakriyādharmaśīlā yajñawrataparāyaṇāḥ |
anyonyaprītisaṃyuktā wyawardhanta prajāstadā ||6||

mānakrodhawihīnāśca janā lobhawiwarjitāḥ |
anyonyamabhyawardhanta dharmottaramawartata ||7||

tanmahodadhiwatpūrṇaṃ nagaraṃ wai wyarocata |
dwāratoraṇaniryūhairyuktamabhracayopamaiḥ ||8||

prāsādaśatasambādhaṃ mahendrapurasaṃnibham ||8||

nadīṣu wanakhaṇḍeṣu wāpīpalwalasānuṣu |
kānaneṣu ca ramyeṣu wijahrurmuditā janāḥ ||9||

uttaraiḥ kurubhiḥ sārdhaṃ dakṣiṇāḥ kurawastadā |
wispardhamānā wyacaraṃstathā siddharṣicāraṇaiḥ ||10||

nābhawatkṛpaṇaḥ kaścinnābhawanwidhawāḥ striyaḥ ||10||

tasmiñjanapade ramye bahawaḥ kurubhiḥ kṛtāḥ |
kūpārāmasabhāwāpyo brāhmaṇāwasathāstathā ||11||

bhīṣmeṇa śāstrato rājansarwataḥ parirakṣite ||11||

babhūwa ramaṇīyaśca caityayūpaśatāṅkitaḥ |
sa deśaḥ pararāṣṭrāṇi pratigṛhyābhiwardhitaḥ ||12||

bhīṣmeṇa wihitaṃ rāṣṭre dharmacakramawartata ||12||

kriyamāṇeṣu kṛtyeṣu kumārāṇāṃ mahātmanām |
paurajānapadāḥ sarwe babhūwuḥ satatotsawāḥ ||13||

gṛheṣu kurumukhyānāṃ paurāṇāṃ ca narādhipa |
dīyatāṃ bhujyatāṃ ceti wāco'śrūyanta sarwaśaḥ ||14||

dhṛtarāṣṭraśca pāṇḍuśca widuraśca mahāmatiḥ |
janmaprabhṛti bhīṣmeṇa putrawatparipālitāḥ ||15||

saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtāste tu wratādhyayanasaṃyutāḥ |
śramawyāyāmakuśalāḥ samapadyanta yauwanam ||16||

dhanurwede'śwapṛṣṭhe ca gadāyuddhe'sicarmaṇi |
tathaiwa gajaśikṣāyāṃ nītiśāstre ca pāragāḥ ||17||

itihāsapurāṇeṣu nānāśikṣāsu cābhibho |
wedawedāṅgatattwajñāḥ sarwatra kṛtaniśramāḥ ||18||

pāṇḍurdhanuṣi wikrānto narebhyo'bhyadhiko'bhawat |
atyanyānbalawānāsīddhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥ ||19||

triṣu lokeṣu na twāsītkaścidwidurasaṃmitaḥ |
dharmanityastato rājandharme ca paramaṃ gataḥ ||20||

pranaṣṭaṃ śantanorwaṃśaṃ samīkṣya punaruddhṛtam |
tato nirwacanaṃ loke sarwarāṣṭreṣwawartata ||21||

wīrasūnāṃ kāśisute deśānāṃ kurujāṅgalam |
sarwadharmawidāṃ bhīṣmaḥ purāṇāṃ gajasāhwayam ||22||

dhṛtarāṣṭrastwacakṣuṣṭwādrājyaṃ na pratyapadyata |
karaṇatwācca widuraḥ pāṇḍurāsīnmahīpatiḥ ||23||






                  103


bhīṣma uwāca||

guṇaiḥ samuditaṃ samyagidaṃ naḥ prathitaṃ kulam |
atyanyānpṛthiwīpālānpṛthiwyāmadhirājyabhāk ||1||

rakṣitaṃ rājabhiḥ pūrwairdharmawidbhirmahātmabhiḥ |
notsādamagamaccedaṃ kadācidiha naḥ kulam ||2||

mayā ca satyawatyā ca kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā |
samawasthāpitaṃ bhūyo yuṣmāsu kulatantuṣu ||3||

wardhate tadidaṃ putra kulaṃ sāgarawadyathā |
tathā mayā widhātawyaṃ twayā caiwa wiśeṣataḥ ||4||

śrūyate yādawī kanyā anurūpā kulasya naḥ |
subalasyātmajā caiwa tathā madreśwarasya ca ||5||

kulīnā rūpawatyaśca nāthawatyaśca sarwaśaḥ |
ucitāścaiwa sambandhe te'smākaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ ||6||

manye warayitawyāstā ityahaṃ dhīmatāṃ wara |
santānārthaṃ kulasyāsya yadwā widura manyase ||7||

widura uwāca||

bhawānpitā bhawānmātā bhawānnaḥ paramo guruḥ |
tasmātswayaṃ kulasyāsya wicārya kuru yaddhitam ||8||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

atha śuśrāwa wiprebhyo gāndhārīṃ subalātmajām |
ārādhya waradaṃ dewaṃ bhaganetraharaṃ haram ||9||

gāndhārī kila putrāṇāṃ śataṃ lebhe waraṃ śubhā ||9||

iti śrutwā ca tattwena bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥ |
tato gāndhārarājasya preṣayāmāsa bhārata ||10||

acakṣuriti tatrāsītsubalasya wicāraṇā |
kulaṃ khyātiṃ ca wṛttaṃ ca buddhyā tu prasamīkṣya saḥ ||11||

dadau tāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya gāndhārīṃ dharmacāriṇīm ||11||

gāndhārī twapi śuśrāwa dhṛtarāṣṭramacakṣuṣam |
ātmānaṃ ditsitaṃ cāsmai pitrā mātrā ca bhārata ||12||

tataḥ sā paṭṭamādāya kṛtwā bahuguṇaṃ śubhā |
babandha netre swe rājanpatiwrataparāyaṇā ||13||

nātyaśnīyāṃ patimahamityewaṃ kṛtaniścayā ||13||

tato gāndhārarājasya putraḥ śakunirabhyayāt |
swasāraṃ parayā lakṣmyā yuktāmādāya kaurawān ||14||

dattwā sa bhaginīṃ wīro yathārhaṃ ca paricchadam |
punarāyātswanagaraṃ bhīṣmeṇa pratipūjitaḥ ||15||

gāndhāryapi warārohā śīlācārawiceṣṭitaiḥ |
tuṣṭiṃ kurūṇāṃ sarweṣāṃ janayāmāsa bhārata ||16||

wṛttenārādhya tānsarwānpatiwrataparāyaṇā |
wācāpi puruṣānanyānsuwratā nānwakīrtayat ||17||






                  104


waiśampāyana uwāca||

śūro nāma yaduśreṣṭho wasudewapitābhawat |
tasya kanyā pṛthā nāma rūpeṇāsadṛśī bhuwi ||1||

paitṛṣwaseyāya sa tāmanapatyāya wīryawān |
agryamagre pratijñāya swasyāpatyasya wīryawān ||2||

agrajāteti tāṃ kanyāmagryānugrahakāṅkṣiṇe |
pradadau kuntibhojāya sakhā sakhye mahātmane ||3||

sā niyuktā piturgehe dewatātithipūjane |
ugraṃ paryacaradghoraṃ brāhmaṇaṃ saṃśitawratam ||4||

nigūḍhaniścayaṃ dharme yaṃ taṃ durwāsasaṃ widuḥ |
tamugraṃ saṃśitātmānaṃ sarwayatnairatoṣayat ||5||

tasyai sa pradadau mantramāpaddharmānwawekṣayā |
abhicārābhisaṃyuktamabrawīccaiwa tāṃ muniḥ ||6||

yaṃ yaṃ dewaṃ twametena mantreṇāwāhayiṣyasi |
tasya tasya prasādena putrastawa bhawiṣyati ||7||

tathoktā sā tu wipreṇa tena kautūhalāttadā |
kanyā satī dewamarkamājuhāwa yaśaswinī ||8||

sā dadarśa tamāyāntaṃ bhāskaraṃ lokabhāwanam |
wismitā cānawadyāṅgī dṛṣṭwā tanmahadadbhutam ||9||

prakāśakarmā tapanastasyāṃ garbhaṃ dadhau tataḥ |
ajījanattato wīraṃ sarwaśastrabhṛtāṃ waram ||10||

āmuktakawacaḥ śrīmāndewagarbhaḥ śriyāwṛtaḥ ||10||

sahajaṃ kawacaṃ bibhratkuṇḍaloddyotitānanaḥ |
ajāyata sutaḥ karṇaḥ sarwalokeṣu wiśrutaḥ ||11||

prādācca tasyāḥ kanyātwaṃ punaḥ sa paramadyutiḥ |
dattwā ca dadatāṃ śreṣṭho diwamācakrame tataḥ ||12||

gūhamānāpacāraṃ taṃ bandhupakṣabhayāttadā |
utsasarja jale kuntī taṃ kumāraṃ salakṣaṇam ||13||

tamutsṛṣṭaṃ tadā garbhaṃ rādhābhartā mahāyaśāḥ |
putratwe kalpayāmāsa sabhāryaḥ sūtanandanaḥ ||14||

nāmadheyaṃ ca cakrāte tasya bālasya tāwubhau |
wasunā saha jāto'yaṃ wasuṣeṇo bhawatwiti ||15||

sa wardhamāno balawānsarwāstreṣūdyato'bhawat |
ā pṛṣṭhatāpādādityamupatasthe sa wīryawān ||16||

yasminkāle japannāste sa wīraḥ satyasaṅgaraḥ |
nādeyaṃ brāhmaṇeṣwāsīttasminkāle mahātmanaḥ ||17||

tamindro brāhmaṇo bhūtwā bhikṣārthaṃ bhūtabhāwanaḥ |
kuṇḍale prārthayāmāsa kawacaṃ ca mahādyutiḥ ||18||

utkṛtya wimanāḥ swāṅgātkawacaṃ rudhirasrawam |
karṇastu kuṇḍale chittwā prāyacchatsa kṛtāñjaliḥ ||19||

śaktiṃ tasmai dadau śakraḥ wismito wākyamabrawīt |
dewāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ gandharworagarakṣasām ||20||

yasmai kṣepsyasi ruṣṭaḥ sanso'nayā na bhawiṣyati ||20||

purā nāma tu tasyāsīdwasuṣeṇa iti śrutam |
tato waikartanaḥ karṇaḥ karmaṇā tena so'bhawat ||21||






                  105


waiśampāyana uwāca||

rūpasattwaguṇopetā dharmārāmā mahāwratā |
duhitā kuntibhojasya kṛte pitrā swayaṃware ||1||

siṃhadaṃṣṭraṃ gajaskandhamṛṣabhākṣaṃ mahābalam |
bhūmipālasahasrāṇāṃ madhye pāṇḍumawindata ||2||

sa tayā kuntibhojasya duhitrā kurunandanaḥ |
yuyuje'mitasaubhāgyaḥ paulomyā maghawāniwa ||3||

yātwā dewawratenāpi madrāṇāṃ puṭabhedanam |
wiśrutā triṣu lokeṣu mādrī madrapateḥ sutā ||4||

sarwarājasu wikhyātā rūpeṇāsadṛśī bhuwi |
pāṇḍorarthe parikrītā dhanena mahatā tadā ||5||

wiwāhaṃ kārayāmāsa bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍormahātmanaḥ ||5||

siṃhoraskaṃ gajaskandhamṛṣabhākṣaṃ manaswinam |
pāṇḍuṃ dṛṣṭwā narawyāghraṃ wyasmayanta narā bhuwi ||6||

kṛtodwāhastataḥ pāṇḍurbalotsāhasamanwitaḥ |
jigīṣamāṇo wasudhāṃ yayau śatrūnanekaśaḥ ||7||

pūrwamāgaskṛto gatwā daśārṇāḥ samare jitāḥ |
pāṇḍunā narasiṃhena kaurawāṇāṃ yaśobhṛtā ||8||

tataḥ senāmupādāya pāṇḍurnānāwidhadhwajām |
prabhūtahastyaśwarathāṃ padātigaṇasaṅkulām ||9||

āgaskṛtsarwawīrāṇāṃ wairī sarwamahībhṛtām |
goptā magadharāṣṭrasya dārwo rājagṛhe hataḥ ||10||

tataḥ kośaṃ samādāya wāhanāni balāni ca |
pāṇḍunā mithilāṃ gatwā widehāḥ samare jitāḥ ||11||

tathā kāśiṣu suhmeṣu puṇḍreṣu bharatarṣabha |
swabāhubalawīryeṇa kurūṇāmakarodyaśaḥ ||12||

taṃ śaraughamahājwālamastrārciṣamariṃdamam |
pāṇḍupāwakamāsādya wyadahyanta narādhipāḥ ||13||

te sasenāḥ sasenena widhwaṃsitabalā nṛpāḥ |
pāṇḍunā waśagāḥ kṛtwā karakarmasu yojitāḥ ||14||

tena te nirjitāḥ sarwe pṛthiwyāṃ sarwapārthiwāḥ |
tamekaṃ menire śūraṃ deweṣwiwa puraṃdaram ||15||

taṃ kṛtāñjalayaḥ sarwe praṇatā wasudhādhipāḥ |
upājagmurdhanaṃ gṛhya ratnāni wiwidhāni ca ||16||

maṇimuktāprawālaṃ ca suwarṇaṃ rajataṃ tathā |
goratnānyaśwaratnāni ratharatnāni kuñjarān ||17||

kharoṣṭramahiṣāṃścaiwa yacca kiñcidajāwikam |
tatsarwaṃ pratijagrāha rājā nāgapurādhipaḥ ||18||

tadādāya yayau pāṇḍuḥ punarmuditawāhanaḥ |
harṣayiṣyanswarāṣṭrāṇi puraṃ ca gajasāhwayam ||19||

śantano rājasiṃhasya bharatasya ca dhīmataḥ |
pranaṣṭaḥ kīrtijaḥ śabdaḥ pāṇḍunā punaruddhṛtaḥ ||20||

ye purā kururāṣṭrāṇi jahruḥ kurudhanāni ca |
te nāgapurasiṃhena pāṇḍunā karadāḥ kṛtāḥ ||21||

ityabhāṣanta rājāno rājāmātyāśca saṅgatāḥ |
pratītamanaso hṛṣṭāḥ paurajānapadaiḥ saha ||22||

pratyudyayustaṃ samprāptaṃ sarwe bhīṣmapurogamāḥ |
te nadūramiwādhwānaṃ gatwā nāgapurālayāḥ ||23||

āwṛtaṃ dadṛśurlokaṃ hṛṣṭā bahuwidhairjanaiḥ ||23||

nānāyānasamānītai ratnairuccāwacaistathā |
hastyaśwaratharatnaiśca gobhiruṣṭrairathāwikaiḥ ||24||

nāntaṃ dadṛśurāsādya bhīṣmeṇa saha kaurawāḥ ||24||

so'bhiwādya pituḥ pādau kausalyānandawardhanaḥ |
yathārhaṃ mānayāmāsa paurajānapadānapi ||25||

pramṛdya pararāṣṭrāṇi kṛtārthaṃ punarāgatam |
putramāsādya bhīṣmastu harṣādaśrūṇyawartayat ||26||

sa tūryaśatasaṅghānāṃ bherīṇāṃ ca mahāswanaiḥ |
harṣayansarwaśaḥ paurānwiweśa gajasāhwayam ||27||






                  106


waiśampāyana uwāca||

dhṛtarāṣṭrābhyanujñātaḥ swabāhuwijitaṃ dhanam |
bhīṣmāya satyawatyai ca mātre copajahāra saḥ ||1||

widurāya ca wai pāṇḍuḥ preṣayāmāsa taddhanam |
suhṛdaścāpi dharmātmā dhanena samatarpayat ||2||

tataḥ satyawatīṃ bhīṣmaḥ kausalyāṃ ca yaśaswinīm |
śubhaiḥ pāṇḍujitai ratnaistoṣayāmāsa bhārata ||3||

nananda mātā kausalyā tamapratimatejasam |
jayantamiwa paulomī pariṣwajya nararṣabham ||4||

tasya wīrasya wikrāntaiḥ sahasraśatadakṣiṇaiḥ |
aśwamedhaśatairīje dhṛtarāṣṭro mahāmakhaiḥ ||5||

samprayuktaśca kuntyā ca mādryā ca bharatarṣabha |
jitatandrīstadā pāṇḍurbabhūwa wanagocaraḥ ||6||

hitwā prāsādanilayaṃ śubhāni śayanāni ca |
araṇyanityaḥ satataṃ babhūwa mṛgayāparaḥ ||7||

sa carandakṣiṇaṃ pārśwaṃ ramyaṃ himawato gireḥ |
uwāsa giripṛṣṭheṣu mahāśālawaneṣu ca ||8||

rarāja kuntyā mādryā ca pāṇḍuḥ saha wane wasan |
kareṇworiwa madhyasthaḥ śrīmānpauraṃdaro gajaḥ ||9||

bhārataṃ saha bhāryābhyāṃ bāṇakhaḍgadhanurdharam |
wicitrakawacaṃ wīraṃ paramāstrawidaṃ nṛpam ||10||

dewo'yamityamanyanta carantaṃ wanawāsinaḥ ||10||

tasya kāmāṃśca bhogāṃśca narā nityamatandritāḥ |
upajahrurwanānteṣu dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa coditāḥ ||11||

atha pāraśawīṃ kanyāṃ dewakasya mahīpateḥ |
rūpayauwanasampannāṃ sa śuśrāwāpagāsutaḥ ||12||

tatastu warayitwā tāmānāyya puruṣarṣabhaḥ |
wiwāhaṃ kārayāmāsa widurasya mahāmateḥ ||13||

tasyāṃ cotpādayāmāsa widuraḥ kurunandanaḥ |
putrānwinayasampannānātmanaḥ sadṛśānguṇaiḥ ||14||






                  107


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ putraśataṃ jajñe gāndhāryāṃ janamejaya |
dhṛtarāṣṭrasya waiśyāyāmekaścāpi śatātparaḥ ||1||

pāṇḍoḥ kuntyāṃ ca mādryāṃ ca pañca putrā mahārathāḥ |
dewebhyaḥ samapadyanta santānāya kulasya wai ||2||

janamejaya uwāca||

kathaṃ putraśataṃ jajñe gāndhāryāṃ dwijasattama |
kiyatā caiwa kālena teṣāmāyuśca kiṃ param ||3||

kathaṃ caikaḥ sa waiśyāyāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasuto'bhawat |
kathaṃ ca sadṛśīṃ bhāryāṃ gāndhārīṃ dharmacāriṇīm ||4||

ānukūlye wartamānāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro'tyawartata ||4||

kathaṃ ca śaptasya sataḥ pāṇḍostena mahātmanā |
samutpannā daiwatebhyaḥ pañca putrā mahārathāḥ ||5||

etadwidwanyathāwṛttaṃ wistareṇa tapodhana |
kathayaswa na me tṛptiḥ kathyamāneṣu bandhuṣu ||6||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

kṣucchramābhipariglānaṃ dwaipāyanamupasthitam |
toṣayāmāsa gāndhārī wyāsastasyai waraṃ dadau ||7||

sā wawre sadṛśaṃ bhartuḥ putrāṇāṃ śatamātmanaḥ |
tataḥ kālena sā garbhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrādathāgrahīt ||8||

saṃwatsaradwayaṃ taṃ tu gāndhārī garbhamāhitam |
aprajā dhārayāmāsa tatastāṃ duḥkhamāwiśat ||9||

śrutwā kuntīsutaṃ jātaṃ bālārkasamatejasam |
udarasyātmanaḥ sthairyamupalabhyānwacintayat ||10||

ajñātaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya yatnena mahatā tataḥ |
sodaraṃ pātayāmāsa gāndhārī duḥkhamūrcchitā ||11||

tato jajñe māṃsapeśī lohāṣṭhīlewa saṃhatā |
dwiwarṣasambhṛtāṃ kukṣau tāmutsraṣṭuṃ pracakrame ||12||

atha dwaipāyano jñātwā twaritaḥ samupāgamat |
tāṃ sa māṃsamayīṃ peśīṃ dadarśa japatāṃ waraḥ ||13||

tato'brawītsaubaleyīṃ kimidaṃ te cikīrṣitam |
sā cātmano mataṃ satyaṃ śaśaṃsa paramarṣaye ||14||

jyeṣṭhaṃ kuntīsutaṃ jātaṃ śrutwā rawisamaprabham |
duḥkhena parameṇedamudaraṃ pātitaṃ mayā ||15||

śataṃ ca kila putrāṇāṃ witīrṇaṃ me twayā purā |
iyaṃ ca me māṃsapeśī jātā putraśatāya wai ||16||

wyāsa uwāca||

ewametatsaubaleyi naitajjātwanyathā bhawet |
witathaṃ noktapūrwaṃ me swaireṣwapi kuto'nyathā ||17||

ghṛtapūrṇaṃ kuṇḍaśataṃ kṣipramewa widhīyatām |
śītābhiradbhiraṣṭhīlāmimāṃ ca pariṣiñcata ||18||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

sā sicyamānā aṣṭhīlā abhawacchatadhā tadā |
aṅguṣṭhaparwamātrāṇāṃ garbhāṇāṃ pṛthagewa tu ||19||

ekādhikaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ yathāyogaṃ wiśāṃ pate |
māṃsapeśyāstadā rājankramaśaḥ kālaparyayāt ||20||

tatastāṃsteṣu kuṇḍeṣu garbhānawadadhe tadā |
swanugupteṣu deśeṣu rakṣāṃ ca wyadadhāttataḥ ||21||

śaśāsa caiwa bhagawānkālenaitāwatā punaḥ |
wighaṭṭanīyānyetāni kuṇḍānīti sma saubalīm ||22||

ityuktwā bhagawānwyāsastathā pratiwidhāya ca |
jagāma tapase dhīmānhimawantaṃ śiloccayam ||23||

jajñe krameṇa caitena teṣāṃ duryodhano nṛpaḥ |
janmatastu pramāṇena jyeṣṭho rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||24||

jātamātre sute tasmindhṛtarāṣṭro'brawīdidam |
samānīya bahūnwiprānbhīṣmaṃ widuramewa ca ||25||

yudhiṣṭhiro rājaputro jyeṣṭho naḥ kulawardhanaḥ |
prāptaḥ swaguṇato rājyaṃ na tasminwācyamasti naḥ ||26||

ayaṃ twanantarastasmādapi rājā bhawiṣyati |
etaddhi brūta me satyaṃ yadatra bhawitā dhruwam ||27||

wākyasyaitasya nidhane dikṣu sarwāsu bhārata |
krawyādāḥ prāṇadanghorāḥ śiwāścāśiwaśaṃsinaḥ ||28||

lakṣayitwā nimittāni tāni ghorāṇi sarwaśaḥ |
te'bruwanbrāhmaṇā rājanwiduraśca mahāmatiḥ ||29||

wyaktaṃ kulāntakaraṇo bhawitaiṣa sutastawa |
tasya śāntiḥ parityāge puṣṭyā twapanayo mahān ||30||

śatamekonamapyastu putrāṇāṃ te mahīpate |
ekena kuru wai kṣemaṃ lokasya ca kulasya ca ||31||

tyajedekaṃ kulasyārthe grāmasyārthe kulaṃ tyajet |
grāmaṃ janapadasyārthe ātmārthe pṛthiwīṃ tyajet ||32||

sa tathā widureṇoktastaiśca sarwairdwijottamaiḥ |
na cakāra tathā rājā putrasnehasamanwitaḥ ||33||

tataḥ putraśataṃ sarwaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya pārthiwa |
māsamātreṇa sañjajñe kanyā caikā śatādhikā ||34||

gāndhāryāṃ kliśyamānāyāmudareṇa wiwardhatā |
dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahābāhuṃ waiśyā paryacaratkila ||35||

tasminsaṃwatsare rājandhṛtarāṣṭrānmahāyaśāḥ |
jajñe dhīmāṃstatastasyāṃ yuyutsuḥ karaṇo nṛpa ||36||

ewaṃ putraśataṃ jajñe dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥ |
mahārathānāṃ wīrāṇāṃ kanyā caikātha duḥśalā ||37||






                  108


janamejaya uwāca||

jyeṣṭhānujyeṣṭhatāṃ teṣāṃ nāmadheyāni cābhibho |
dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāṇāmānupūrwyeṇa kīrtaya ||1||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

duryodhano yuyutsuśca rājanduḥśāsanastathā |
duḥsaho duḥśalaścaiwa jalasandhaḥ samaḥ sahaḥ ||2||

windānuwindau durdharṣaḥ subāhurduṣpradharṣaṇaḥ |
durmarṣaṇo durmukhaśca duṣkarṇaḥ karṇa ewa ca ||3||

wiwiṃśatirwikarṇaśca jalasandhaḥ sulocanaḥ |
citropacitrau citrākṣaścārucitraḥ śarāsanaḥ ||4||

durmado duṣpragāhaśca wiwitsurwikaṭaḥ samaḥ |
ūrṇanābhaḥ sunābhaśca tathā nandopanandakau ||5||

senāpatiḥ suṣeṇaśca kuṇḍodaramahodarau |
citrabāṇaścitrawarmā suwarmā durwimocanaḥ ||6||

ayobāhurmahābāhuścitrāṅgaścitrakuṇḍalaḥ |
bhīmawego bhīmabalo balākī balawardhanaḥ ||7||

ugrāyudho bhīmakarmā kanakāyurdṛḍhāyudhaḥ |
dṛḍhawarmā dṛḍhakṣatraḥ somakīrtiranūdaraḥ ||8||

dṛḍhasandho jarāsandhaḥ satyasandhaḥ sadaḥsuwāk |
ugraśrawā aśwasenaḥ senānīrduṣparājayaḥ ||9||

aparājitaḥ paṇḍitako wiśālākṣo durāwaraḥ |
dṛḍhahastaḥ suhastaśca wātawegasuwarcasau ||10||

ādityaketurbahwāśī nāgadantograyāyinau |
kawacī niṣaṅgī pāśī ca daṇḍadhāro dhanurgrahaḥ ||11||

ugro bhīmaratho wīro wīrabāhuralolupaḥ |
abhayo raudrakarmā ca tathā dṛḍharathastrayaḥ ||12||

anādhṛṣyaḥ kuṇḍabhedī wirāwī dīrghalocanaḥ |
dīrghabāhurmahābāhurwyūḍhoruḥ kanakadhwajaḥ ||13||

kuṇḍāśī wirajāścaiwa duḥśalā ca śatādhikā |
etadekaśataṃ rājankanyā caikā prakīrtitā ||14||

nāmadheyānupūrwyeṇa widdhi janmakramaṃ nṛpa |
sarwe twatirathāḥ śūrāḥ sarwe yuddhawiśāradāḥ ||15||

sarwe wedawidaścaiwa rājaśāstreṣu kowidāḥ |
sarwe saṃsargawidyāsu widyābhijanaśobhinaḥ ||16||

sarweṣāmanurūpāśca kṛtā dārā mahīpate |
dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa samaye samīkṣya widhiwattadā ||17||

duḥśalāṃ samaye rājā sindhurājāya bhārata |
jayadrathāya pradadau saubalānumate tadā ||18||






                  109


janamejaya uwāca||

kathito dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāmārṣaḥ sambhawa uttamaḥ |
amānuṣo mānuṣāṇāṃ bhawatā brahmawittama ||1||

nāmadheyāni cāpyeṣāṃ kathyamānāni bhāgaśaḥ |
twattaḥ śrutāni me brahmanpāṇḍawānāṃ tu kīrtaya ||2||

te hi sarwe mahātmāno dewarājaparākramāḥ |
twayaiwāṃśāwataraṇe dewabhāgāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||3||

tasmādicchāmyahaṃ śrotumatimānuṣakarmaṇām |
teṣāmājananaṃ sarwaṃ waiśampāyana kīrtaya ||4||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

rājā pāṇḍurmahāraṇye mṛgawyālaniṣewite |
wane maithunakālasthaṃ dadarśa mṛgayūthapam ||5||

tatastāṃ ca mṛgīṃ taṃ ca rukmapuṅkhaiḥ supatribhiḥ |
nirbibheda śaraistīkṣṇaiḥ pāṇḍuḥ pañcabhirāśugaiḥ ||6||

sa ca rājanmahātejā ṛṣiputrastapodhanaḥ |
bhāryayā saha tejaswī mṛgarūpeṇa saṅgataḥ ||7||

saṃsaktastu tayā mṛgyā mānuṣīmīrayangiram |
kṣaṇena patito bhūmau wilalāpākulendriyaḥ ||8||

mṛga uwāca||

kāmamanyuparītāpi buddhyaṅgarahitāpi ca |
warjayanti nṛśaṃsāni pāpeṣwabhiratā narāḥ ||9||

na widhiṃ grasate prajñā prajñāṃ tu grasate widhiḥ |
widhiparyāgatānarthānprajñā na pratipadyate ||10||

śaśwaddharmātmanāṃ mukhye kule jātasya bhārata |
kāmalobhābhibhūtasya kathaṃ te calitā matiḥ ||11||

pāṇḍuruwāca||

śatrūṇāṃ yā wadhe wṛttiḥ sā mṛgāṇāṃ wadhe smṛtā |
rājñāṃ mṛga na māṃ mohāttwaṃ garhayitumarhasi ||12||

acchadmanāmāyayā ca mṛgāṇāṃ wadha iṣyate |
sa ewa dharmo rājñāṃ tu tadwidwānkiṃ nu garhase ||13||

agastyaḥ satramāsīnaścacāra mṛgayāmṛṣiḥ |
āraṇyānsarwadaiwatyānmṛgānprokṣya mahāwane ||14||

pramāṇadṛṣṭadharmeṇa kathamasmānwigarhase |
agastyasyābhicāreṇa yuṣmākaṃ wai wapā hutā ||15||

mṛga uwāca||

na ripūnwai samuddiśya wimuñcanti purā śarān |
randhra eṣāṃ wiśeṣeṇa wadhakālaḥ praśasyate ||16||

pāṇḍuruwāca||

pramattamapramattaṃ wā wiwṛtaṃ ghnanti caujasā |
upāyairiṣubhistīkṣṇaiḥ kasmānmṛga wigarhase ||17||

mṛga uwāca||

nāhaṃ ghnantaṃ mṛgānrājanwigarhe ātmakāraṇāt |
maithunaṃ tu pratīkṣyaṃ me syāttwayehānṛśaṃsataḥ ||18||

sarwabhūtahite kāle sarwabhūtepsite tathā |
ko hi widwānmṛgaṃ hanyāccarantaṃ maithunaṃ wane ||19||

puruṣārthaphalaṃ kāntaṃ yattwayā witathaṃ kṛtam ||19||

paurawāṇāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca teṣāmakliṣṭakarmaṇām |
waṃśe jātasya kaurawya nānurūpamidaṃ tawa ||20||

nṛśaṃsaṃ karma sumahatsarwalokawigarhitam |
aswargyamayaśasyaṃ ca adharmiṣṭhaṃ ca bhārata ||21||

strībhogānāṃ wiśeṣajñaḥ śāstradharmārthatattwawit |
nārhastwaṃ surasaṅkāśa kartumaswargyamīdṛśam ||22||

twayā nṛśaṃsakartāraḥ pāpācārāśca mānawāḥ |
nigrāhyāḥ pārthiwaśreṣṭha triwargapariwarjitāḥ ||23||

kiṃ kṛtaṃ te naraśreṣṭha nighnato māmanāgasam |
muniṃ mūlaphalāhāraṃ mṛgaweṣadharaṃ nṛpa ||24||

wasamānamaraṇyeṣu nityaṃ śamaparāyaṇam ||24||

twayāhaṃ hiṃsito yasmāttasmāttwāmapyasaṃśayam |
dwayornṛśaṃsakartāramawaśaṃ kāmamohitam ||25||

jīwitāntakaro bhāwa ewamewāgamiṣyati ||25||

ahaṃ hi kiṃdamo nāma tapasāpratimo muniḥ |
wyapatrapanmanuṣyāṇāṃ mṛgyāṃ maithunamācaram ||26||

mṛgo bhūtwā mṛgaiḥ sārdhaṃ carāmi gahane wane |
na tu te brahmahatyeyaṃ bhawiṣyatyawijānataḥ ||27||

mṛgarūpadharaṃ hatwā māmewaṃ kāmamohitam ||27||

asya tu twaṃ phalaṃ mūḍha prāpsyasīdṛśamewa hi |
priyayā saha saṃwāsaṃ prāpya kāmawimohitaḥ ||28||

twamapyasyāmawasthāyāṃ pretalokaṃ gamiṣyasi ||28||

antakāle ca saṃwāsaṃ yayā gantāsi kāntayā |
pretarājawaśaṃ prāptaṃ sarwabhūtaduratyayam ||29||

bhaktyā matimatāṃ śreṣṭha saiwa twāmanuyāsyati ||29||

wartamānaḥ sukhe duḥkhaṃ yathāhaṃ prāpitastwayā |
tathā sukhaṃ twāṃ samprāptaṃ duḥkhamabhyāgamiṣyati ||30||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktwā suduḥkhārto jīwitātsa wyayujyata |
mṛgaḥ pāṇḍuśca śokārtaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyata ||31||






                  110


waiśampāyana uwāca||

taṃ wyatītamatikramya rājā swamiwa bāndhawam |
sabhāryaḥ śokaduḥkhārtaḥ paryadewayadāturaḥ ||1||

pāṇḍuruwāca||

satāmapi kule jātāḥ karmaṇā bata durgatim |
prāpnuwantyakṛtātmānaḥ kāmajālawimohitāḥ ||2||

śaśwaddharmātmanā jāto bāla ewa pitā mama |
jīwitāntamanuprāptaḥ kāmātmaiweti naḥ śrutam ||3||

tasya kāmātmanaḥ kṣetre rājñaḥ saṃyatawāgṛṣiḥ |
kṛṣṇadwaipāyanaḥ sākṣādbhagawānmāmajījanat ||4||

tasyādya wyasane buddhiḥ sañjāteyaṃ mamādhamā |
tyaktasya dewairanayānmṛgayāyāṃ durātmanaḥ ||5||

mokṣamewa wyawasyāmi bandho hi wyasanaṃ mahat |
suwṛttimanuwartiṣye tāmahaṃ piturawyayām ||6||

atīwa tapasātmānaṃ yojayiṣyāmyasaṃśayam ||6||

tasmādeko'hamekāhamekaikasminwanaspatau |
caranbhaikṣaṃ munirmuṇḍaścariṣyāmi mahīmimām ||7||

pāṃsunā samawacchannaḥ śūnyāgārapratiśrayaḥ |
wṛkṣamūlaniketo wā tyaktasarwapriyāpriyaḥ ||8||

na śocanna prahṛṣyaṃśca tulyanindātmasaṃstutiḥ |
nirāśīrnirnamaskāro nirdwandwo niṣparigrahaḥ ||9||

na cāpyawahasankañcinna kurwanbhrukuṭīṃ kwacit |
prasannawadano nityaṃ sarwabhūtahite rataḥ ||10||

jaṅgamājaṅgamaṃ sarwamawihiṃsaṃścaturwidham |
swāsu prajāswiwa sadā samaḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ prati ||11||

ekakālaṃ caranbhaikṣaṃ kulāni dwe ca pañca ca |
asambhawe wā bhaikṣasya carannanaśanānyapi ||12||

alpamalpaṃ yathābhojyaṃ pūrwalābhena jātu cit |
nityaṃ nāticaraṃllābhe alābhe sapta pūrayan ||13||

wāsyaikaṃ takṣato bāhuṃ candanenaikamukṣataḥ |
nākalyāṇaṃ na kalyāṇaṃ pradhyāyannubhayostayoḥ ||14||

na jijīwiṣuwatkiñcinna mumūrṣuwadācaran |
maraṇaṃ jīwitaṃ caiwa nābhinandanna ca dwiṣan ||15||

yāḥ kāścijjīwatā śakyāḥ kartumabhyudayakriyāḥ |
tāḥ sarwāḥ samatikramya nimeṣādiṣwawasthitaḥ ||16||

tāsu sarwāswawasthāsu tyaktasarwendriyakriyaḥ |
samparityaktadharmātmā sunirṇiktātmakalmaṣaḥ ||17||

nirmuktaḥ sarwapāpebhyo wyatītaḥ sarwawāgurāḥ |
na waśe kasyacittiṣṭhansadharmā mātariśwanaḥ ||18||

etayā satataṃ wṛttyā carannewamprakārayā |
dehaṃ sandhārayiṣyāmi nirbhayaṃ mārgamāsthitaḥ ||19||

nāhaṃ śwācarite mārge awīryakṛpaṇocite |
swadharmātsatatāpete rameyaṃ wīryawarjitaḥ ||20||

satkṛto'saktṛto wāpi yo'nyāṃ kṛpaṇacakṣuṣā |
upaiti wṛttiṃ kāmātmā sa śunāṃ wartate pathi ||21||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktwā suduḥkhārto niḥśwāsaparamo nṛpaḥ |
awekṣamāṇaḥ kuntīṃ ca mādrīṃ ca samabhāṣata ||22||

kausalyā widuraḥ kṣattā rājā ca saha bandhubhiḥ |
āryā satyawatī bhīṣmaste ca rājapurohitāḥ ||23||

brāhmaṇāśca mahātmānaḥ somapāḥ saṃśitawratāḥ |
paurawṛddhāśca ye tatra niwasantyasmadāśrayāḥ ||24||

prasādya sarwe waktawyāḥ pāṇḍuḥ prawrajito wanam ||24||

niśamya wacanaṃ bharturwanawāse dhṛtātmanaḥ |
tatsamaṃ wacanaṃ kuntī mādrī ca samabhāṣatām ||25||

anye'pi hyāśramāḥ santi ye śakyā bharatarṣabha |
āwābhyāṃ dharmapatnībhyāṃ saha taptwā tapo mahat ||26||

twamewa bhawitā sārthaḥ swargasyāpi na saṃśayaḥ ||26||

praṇidhāyendriyagrāmaṃ bhartṛlokaparāyaṇe |
tyaktakāmasukhe hyāwāṃ tapsyāwo wipulaṃ tapaḥ ||27||

yadi āwāṃ mahāprājña tyakṣyasi twaṃ wiśāṃ pate |
adyaiwāwāṃ prahāsyāwo jītiwaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ||28||

pāṇḍuruwāca||

yadi wyawasitaṃ hyetadyuwayordharmasaṃhitam |
swawṛttimanuwartiṣye tāmahaṃ piturawyayām ||29||

tyaktagrāmyasukhācārastapyamāno mahattapaḥ |
walkalī phalamūlāśī cariṣyāmi mahāwane ||30||

agniṃ juhwannubhau kālāwubhau kālāwupaspṛśan |
kṛśaḥ parimitāhāraścīracarmajaṭādharaḥ ||31||

śītawātātapasahaḥ kṣutpipāsāśramānwitaḥ |
tapasā duścareṇedaṃ śarīramupaśoṣayan ||32||

ekāntaśīlī wimṛśanpakwāpakwena wartayan |
pitṛndewāṃśca wanyena wāgbhiradbhiśca tarpayan ||33||

wānaprasthajanasyāpi darśanaṃ kulawāsinām |
nāpriyāṇyācarañjātu kiṃ punargrāmawāsinām ||34||

ewamāraṇyaśāstrāṇāmugramugrataraṃ widhim |
kāṅkṣamāṇo'hamāsiṣye dehasyāsya samāpanāt ||35||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ityewamuktwā bhārye te rājā kaurawawaṃśajaḥ |
tataścūḍāmaṇiṃ niṣkamaṅgade kuṇḍalāni ca ||36||

wāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi strīṇāmābharaṇāni ca ||36||

pradāya sarwaṃ wiprebhyaḥ pāṇḍuḥ punarabhāṣata |
gatwā nāgapuraṃ wācyaṃ pāṇḍuḥ prawrajito wanam ||37||

arthaṃ kāmaṃ sukhaṃ caiwa ratiṃ ca paramātmikām |
pratasthe sarwamutsṛjya sabhāryaḥ kurupuṅgawaḥ ||38||

tatastasyānuyātrāṇi te caiwa paricārakāḥ |
śrutwā bharatasiṃhasya wiwidhāḥ karuṇā giraḥ ||39||

bhīmamārtaswaraṃ kṛtwā hāheti paricukruśuḥ ||39||

uṣṇamaśru wimuñcantastaṃ wihāya mahīpatim |
yayurnāgapuraṃ tūrṇaṃ sarwamādāya tadwacaḥ ||40||

śrutwā ca tebhyastatsarwaṃ yathāwṛttaṃ mahāwane |
dhṛtarāṣṭro naraśreṣṭhaḥ pāṇḍumewānwaśocata ||41||

rājaputrastu kaurawyaḥ pāṇḍurmūlaphalāśanaḥ |
jagāma saha bhāryābhyāṃ tato nāgasabhaṃ girim ||42||

sa caitrarathamāsādya wāriṣeṇamatītya ca |
himawantamatikramya prayayau gandhamādanam ||43||

rakṣyamāṇo mahābhūtaiḥ siddhaiśca paramarṣibhiḥ |
uwāsa sa tadā rājā sameṣu wiṣameṣu ca ||44||

indradyumnasaraḥ prāpya haṃsakūṭamatītya ca |
śataśṛṅge mahārāja tāpasaḥ samapadyata ||45||






                  111


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tatrāpi tapasi śreṣṭhe wartamānaḥ sa wīryawān |
siddhacāraṇasaṅghānāṃ babhūwa priyadarśanaḥ ||1||

śuśrūṣuranahaṃwādī saṃyatātmā jitendriyaḥ |
swargaṃ gantuṃ parākrāntaḥ swena wīryeṇa bhārata ||2||

keṣāñcidabhawadbhrātā keṣāñcidabhawatsakhā |
ṛṣayastwapare cainaṃ putrawatparyapālayan ||3||

sa tu kālena mahatā prāpya niṣkalmaṣaṃ tapaḥ |
brahmarṣisadṛśaḥ pāṇḍurbabhūwa bharatarṣabha ||4||

swargapāraṃ titīrṣansa śataśṛṅgādudaṅmukhaḥ |
pratasthe saha patnībhyāmabruwaṃstatra tāpasāḥ ||5||

uparyupari gacchantaḥ śailarājamudaṅmukhāḥ ||5||

dṛṣṭawanto girerasya durgāndeśānbahūnwayam |
ākrīḍabhūtāndewānāṃ gandharwāpsarasāṃ tathā ||6||

udyānāni kuberasya samāni wiṣamāṇi ca |
mahānadīnitambāṃśca durgāṃśca girigahwarān ||7||

santi nityahimā deśā nirwṛkṣamṛgapakṣiṇaḥ |
santi kecinmahāwarṣā durgāḥ keciddurāsadāḥ ||8||

atikrāmenna pakṣī yānkuta ewetare mṛgāḥ |
wāyureko'tigādyatra siddhāśca paramarṣayaḥ ||9||

gacchantyau śailarāje'sminrājaputryau kathaṃ twime |
na sīdetāmaduḥkhārhe mā gamo bharatarṣabha ||10||

pāṇḍuruwāca||

aprajasya mahābhāgā na dwāraṃ paricakṣate |
swarge tenābhitapto'hamaprajastadbrawīmi waḥ ||11||

ṛṇaiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktā jāyante manujā bhuwi |
pitṛdewarṣimanujadeyaiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ||12||

etāni tu yathākālaṃ yo na budhyati mānawaḥ |
na tasya lokāḥ santīti dharmawidbhiḥ pratiṣṭhitam ||13||

yajñaiśca dewānprīṇāti swādhyāyatapasā munīn |
putraiḥ śrāddhaiḥ pitṛṃścāpi ānṛśaṃsyena mānawān ||14||

ṛṣidewamanuṣyāṇāṃ parimukto'smi dharmataḥ |
pitryādṛṇādanirmuktastena tapye tapodhanāḥ ||15||

dehanāśe dhruwo nāśaḥ pitṛṇāmeṣa niścayaḥ |
iha tasmātprajāhetoḥ prajāyante narottamāḥ ||16||

yathaiwāhaṃ pituḥ kṣetre sṛṣṭastena mahātmanā |
tathaiwāsminmama kṣetre kathaṃ wai sambhawetprajā ||17||

tāpasā ūcuḥ||

asti wai tawa dharmātmanwidma dewopamaṃ śubham |
apatyamanaghaṃ rājanwayaṃ diwyena cakṣuṣā ||18||

daiwadiṣṭaṃ narawyāghra karmaṇehopapādaya |
akliṣṭaṃ phalamawyagro windate buddhimānnaraḥ ||19||

tasmindṛṣṭe phale tāta prayatnaṃ kartumarhasi |
apatyaṃ guṇasampannaṃ labdhwā prītimawāpsyasi ||20||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tacchrutwā tāpasawacaḥ pāṇḍuścintāparo'bhawat |
ātmano mṛgaśāpena jānannupahatāṃ kriyām ||21||

so'brawīdwijane kuntīṃ dharmapatnīṃ yaśaswinīm |
apatyotpādane yogamāpadi prasamarthayan ||22||

apatyaṃ nāma lokeṣu pratiṣṭhā dharmasaṃhitā |
iti kunti widurdhīrāḥ śāśwataṃ dharmamāditaḥ ||23||

iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ tapastaptaṃ niyamaśca swanuṣṭhitaḥ |
sarwamewānapatyasya na pāwanamihocyate ||24||

so'hamewaṃ widitwaitatprapaśyāmi śucismite |
anapatyaḥ śubhāṃllokānnāwāpsyāmīti cintayan ||25||

mṛgābhiśāpānnaṣṭaṃ me prajanaṃ hyakṛtātmanaḥ |
nṛśaṃsakāriṇo bhīru yathaiwopahataṃ tathā ||26||

ime wai bandhudāyādāḥ ṣaṭputrā dharmadarśane |
ṣaḍewābandhudāyādāḥ putrāstāñśṛṇu me pṛthe ||27||

swayañjātaḥ praṇītaśca parikrītaśca yaḥ sutaḥ |
paunarbhawaśca kānīnaḥ swairiṇyāṃ yaśca jāyate ||28||

dattaḥ krītaḥ kṛtrimaśca upagacchetswayaṃ ca yaḥ |
sahoḍho jātaretāśca hīnayonidhṛtaśca yaḥ ||29||

pūrwapūrwatamābhāwe matwā lipseta wai sutam |
uttamādawarāḥ puṃsaḥ kāṅkṣante putramāpadi ||30||

apatyaṃ dharmaphaladaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ windanti sādhawaḥ |
ātmaśukrādapi pṛthe manuḥ swāyambhuwo'brawīt ||31||

tasmātpraheṣyāmyadya twāṃ hīnaḥ prajananātswayam |
sadṛśācchreyaso wā twaṃ widdhyapatyaṃ yaśaswini ||32||

śṛṇu kunti kathāṃ cemāṃ śāradaṇḍāyanīṃ prati |
yā wīrapatnī gurubhirniyuktāpatyajanmani ||33||

puṣpeṇa prayatā snātā niśi kunti catuṣpathe |
warayitwā dwijaṃ siddhaṃ hutwā puṃsawane'nalam ||34||

karmaṇyawasite tasminsā tenaiwa sahāwasat |
tatra trīñjanayāmāsa durjayādīnmahārathān ||35||

tathā twamapi kalyāṇi brāhmaṇāttapasādhikāt |
manniyogādyata kṣipramapatyotpādanaṃ prati ||36||






                  112


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktā mahārāja kuntī pāṇḍumabhāṣata |
kurūṇāmṛṣabhaṃ wīraṃ tadā bhūmipatiṃ patim ||1||

na māmarhasi dharmajña waktumewaṃ kathañcana |
dharmapatnīmabhiratāṃ twayi rājīwalocana ||2||

twamewa tu mahābāho mayyapatyāni bhārata |
wīra wīryopapannāni dharmato janayiṣyasi ||3||

swargaṃ manujaśārdūla gaccheyaṃ sahitā twayā |
apatyāya ca māṃ gaccha twamewa kurunandana ||4||

na hyahaṃ manasāpyanyaṃ gaccheyaṃ twadṛte naram |
twattaḥ pratiwiśiṣṭaśca ko'nyo'sti bhuwi mānawaḥ ||5||

imāṃ ca tāwaddharmyāṃ twaṃ paurāṇīṃ śṛṇu me kathām |
pariśrutāṃ wiśālākṣa kīrtayiṣyāmi yāmaham ||6||

wyuṣitāśwa iti khyāto babhūwa kila pārthiwaḥ |
purā paramadharmiṣṭhaḥ pūrorwaṃśawiwardhanaḥ ||7||

tasmiṃśca yajamāne wai dharmātmani mahātmani |
upāgamaṃstato dewāḥ sendrāḥ saha maharṣibhiḥ ||8||

amādyadindraḥ somena dakṣiṇābhirdwijātayaḥ |
wyuṣitāśwasya rājarṣestato yajñe mahātmanaḥ ||9||

wyuṣitāśwastato rājannati martyānwyarocata |
sarwabhūtānyati yathā tapanaḥ śiśirātyaye ||10||

sa wijitya gṛhītwā ca nṛpatīnrājasattamaḥ |
prācyānudīcyānmadhyāṃśca dakṣiṇātyānakālayat ||11||

aśwamedhe mahāyajñe wyuṣitāśwaḥ pratāpawān |
babhūwa sa hi rājendro daśanāgabalānwitaḥ ||12||

apyatra gāthāṃ gāyanti ye purāṇawido janāḥ |
wyuṣitāśwaḥ samudrāntāṃ wijityemāṃ wasundharām ||13||

apālayatsarwawarṇānpitā putrāniwaurasān ||13||

yajamāno mahāyajñairbrāhmaṇebhyo dadau dhanam |
anantaratnānyādāya ājahāra mahākratūn ||14||

suṣāwa ca bahūnsomānsomasaṃsthāstatāna ca ||14||

āsītkākṣīwatī cāsya bhāryā paramasaṃmatā |
bhadrā nāma manuṣyendra rūpeṇāsadṛśī bhuwi ||15||

kāmayāmāsatustau tu parasparamiti śrutiḥ |
sa tasyāṃ kāmasaṃmatto yakṣmāṇaṃ samapadyata ||16||

tenācireṇa kālena jagāmāstamiwāṃśumān |
tasminprete manuṣyendre bhāryāsya bhṛśaduḥkhitā ||17||

aputrā puruṣawyāghra wilalāpeti naḥ śrutam |
bhadrā paramaduḥkhārtā tannibodha narādhipa ||18||

nārī paramadharmajña sarwā putrawinākṛtā |
patiṃ winā jīwati yā na sā jīwati duḥkhitā ||19||

patiṃ winā mṛtaṃ śreyo nāryāḥ kṣatriyapuṅgawa |
twadgatiṃ gantumicchāmi prasīdaswa nayaswa mām ||20||

twayā hīnā kṣaṇamapi nāhaṃ jīwitumutsahe |
prasādaṃ kuru me rājannitastūrṇaṃ nayaswa mām ||21||

pṛṣṭhato'nugamiṣyāmi sameṣu wiṣameṣu ca |
twāmahaṃ naraśārdūla gacchantamaniwartinam ||22||

chāyewānapagā rājansatataṃ waśawartinī |
bhawiṣyāmi narawyāghra nityaṃ priyahite ratā ||23||

adya prabhṛti māṃ rājankaṣṭā hṛdayaśoṣaṇāḥ |
ādhayo'bhibhawiṣyanti twadṛte puṣkarekṣaṇa ||24||

abhāgyayā mayā nūnaṃ wiyuktāḥ sahacāriṇaḥ |
saṃyogā wiprayuktā wā pūrwadeheṣu pārthiwa ||25||

tadidaṃ karmabhiḥ pāpaiḥ pūrwadeheṣu sañcitam |
duḥkhaṃ māmanusamprāptaṃ rājaṃstwadwiprayogajam ||26||

adya prabhṛtyahaṃ rājankuśaprastaraśāyinī |
bhawiṣyāmyasukhāwiṣṭā twaddarśanaparāyaṇā ||27||

darśayaswa narawyāghra sādhu māmasukhānwitām |
dīnāmanāthāṃ kṛpaṇāṃ wilapantīṃ nareśwara ||28||

ewaṃ bahuwidhaṃ tasyāṃ wilapantyāṃ punaḥ punaḥ |
taṃ śawaṃ sampariṣwajya wākkilāntarhitābrawīt ||29||

uttiṣṭha bhadre gaccha twaṃ dadānīha waraṃ tawa |
janayiṣyāmyapatyāni twayyahaṃ cāruhāsini ||30||

ātmīye ca warārohe śayanīye caturdaśīm |
aṣṭamīṃ wā ṛtusnātā saṃwiśethā mayā saha ||31||

ewamuktā tu sā dewī tathā cakre patiwratā |
yathoktamewa tadwākyaṃ bhadrā putrārthinī tadā ||32||

sā tena suṣuwe dewī śawena manujādhipa |
trīñśālwāṃścaturo madrānsutānbharatasattama ||33||

tathā twamapi mayyewa manasā bharatarṣabha |
śakto janayituṃ putrāṃstapoyogabalānwayāt ||34||






                  113


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastayā rājā tāṃ dewīṃ punarabrawīt |
dharmawiddharmasaṃyuktamidaṃ wacanamuttamam ||1||

ewametatpurā kunti wyuṣitāśwaścakāra ha |
yathā twayoktaṃ kalyāṇi sa hyāsīdamaropamaḥ ||2||

atha twimaṃ prawakṣyāmi dharmaṃ twetaṃ nibodha me |
purāṇamṛṣibhirdṛṣṭaṃ dharmawidbhirmahātmabhiḥ ||3||

anāwṛtāḥ kila purā striya āsanwarānane |
kāmacārawihāriṇyaḥ swatantrāścārulocane ||4||

tāsāṃ wyuccaramāṇānāṃ kaumārātsubhage patīn |
nādharmo'bhūdwarārohe sa hi dharmaḥ purābhawat ||5||

taṃ caiwa dharmaṃ paurāṇaṃ tiryagyonigatāḥ prajāḥ |
adyāpyanuwidhīyante kāmadweṣawiwarjitāḥ ||6||

purāṇadṛṣṭo dharmo'yaṃ pūjyate ca maharṣibhiḥ ||6||

uttareṣu ca rambhoru kuruṣwadyāpi wartate |
strīṇāmanugrahakaraḥ sa hi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ||7||

asmiṃstu loke nacirānmaryādeyaṃ śucismite |
sthāpitā yena yasmācca tanme wistarataḥ śṛṇu ||8||

babhūwoddālako nāma maharṣiriti naḥ śrutam |
śwetaketuriti khyātaḥ putrastasyābhawanmuniḥ ||9||

maryādeyaṃ kṛtā tena mānuṣeṣwiti naḥ śrutam |
kopātkamalapatrākṣi yadarthaṃ tannibodha me ||10||

śwetaketoḥ kila purā samakṣaṃ mātaraṃ pituḥ |
jagrāha brāhmaṇaḥ pāṇau gacchāwa iti cābrawīt ||11||

ṛṣiputrastataḥ kopaṃ cakārāmarṣitastadā |
mātaraṃ tāṃ tathā dṛṣṭwā nīyamānāṃ balādiwa ||12||

kruddhaṃ taṃ tu pitā dṛṣṭwā śwetaketumuwāca ha |
mā tāta kopaṃ kārṣīstwameṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ||13||

anāwṛtā hi sarweṣāṃ warṇānāmaṅganā bhuwi |
yathā gāwaḥ sthitāstāta swe swe warṇe tathā prajāḥ ||14||

ṛṣiputro'tha taṃ dharmaṃ śwetaketurna cakṣame |
cakāra caiwa maryādāmimāṃ strīpuṃsayorbhuwi ||15||

mānuṣeṣu mahābhāge na twewānyeṣu jantuṣu |
tadā prabhṛti maryādā sthiteyamiti naḥ śrutam ||16||

wyuccarantyāḥ patiṃ nāryā adya prabhṛti pātakam |
bhrūṇahatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhawiṣyatyasukhāwaham ||17||

bhāryāṃ tathā wyuccarataḥ kaumārīṃ brahmacāriṇīm |
patiwratāmetadewa bhawitā pātakaṃ bhuwi ||18||

patyā niyuktā yā caiwa patnyapatyārthamewa ca |
na kariṣyati tasyāśca bhawiṣyatyetadewa hi ||19||

iti tena purā bhīru maryādā sthāpitā balāt |
uddālakasya putreṇa dharmyā wai śwetaketunā ||20||

saudāsena ca rambhoru niyuktāpatyajanmani |
madayantī jagāmarṣiṃ wasiṣṭhamiti naḥ śrutam ||21||

tasmāllebhe ca sā putramaśmakaṃ nāma bhāminī |
bhāryā kalmāṣapādasya bhartuḥ priyacikīrṣayā ||22||

asmākamapi te janma widitaṃ kamalekṣaṇe |
kṛṣṇadwaipāyanādbhīru kurūṇāṃ waṃśawṛddhaye ||23||

ata etāni sarwāṇi kāraṇāni samīkṣya wai |
mamaitadwacanaṃ dharmyaṃ kartumarhasyanindite ||24||

ṛtāwṛtau rājaputri striyā bhartā yatawrate |
nātiwartawya ityewaṃ dharmaṃ dharmawido widuḥ ||25||

śeṣeṣwanyeṣu kāleṣu swātantryaṃ strī kilārhati |
dharmametaṃ janāḥ santaḥ purāṇaṃ paricakṣate ||26||

bhartā bhāryāṃ rājaputri dharmyaṃ wādharmyamewa wā |
yadbrūyāttattathā kāryamiti dharmawido widuḥ ||27||

wiśeṣataḥ putragṛddhī hīnaḥ prajananātswayam |
yathāhamanawadyāṅgi putradarśanalālasaḥ ||28||

tathā raktāṅgulitalaḥ padmapatranibhaḥ śubhe |
prasādārthaṃ mayā te'yaṃ śirasyabhyudyato'ñjaliḥ ||29||

manniyogātsukeśānte dwijātestapasādhikāt |
putrānguṇasamāyuktānutpādayitumarhasi ||30||

twatkṛte'haṃ pṛthuśroṇi gaccheyaṃ putriṇāṃ gatim ||30||

ewamuktā tataḥ kuntī pāṇḍuṃ parapurañjayam |
pratyuwāca warārohā bhartuḥ priyahite ratā ||31||

pitṛweśmanyahaṃ bālā niyuktātithipūjane |
ugraṃ paryacaraṃ tatra brāhmaṇaṃ saṃśitawratam ||32||

nigūḍhaniścayaṃ dharme yaṃ taṃ durwāsasaṃ widuḥ |
tamahaṃ saṃśitātmānaṃ sarwayatnairatoṣayam ||33||

sa me'bhicārasaṃyuktamācaṣṭa bhagawānwaram |
mantragrāmaṃ ca me prādādabrawīccaiwa māmidam ||34||

yaṃ yaṃ dewaṃ twametena mantreṇāwāhayiṣyasi |
akāmo wā sakāmo wā sa te waśamupaiṣyati ||35||

ityuktāhaṃ tadā tena pitṛweśmani bhārata |
brāhmaṇena wacastathyaṃ tasya kālo'yamāgataḥ ||36||

anujñātā twayā dewamāhwayeyamahaṃ nṛpa |
tena mantreṇa rājarṣe yathā syānnau prajā wibho ||37||

āwāhayāmi kaṃ dewaṃ brūhi tattwawidāṃ wara |
twatto'nujñāpratīkṣāṃ māṃ widdhyasminkarmaṇi sthitām ||38||

pāṇḍuruwāca||

adyaiwa twaṃ warārohe prayataswa yathāwidhi |
dharmamāwāhaya śubhe sa hi deweṣu puṇyabhāk ||39||

adharmeṇa na no dharmaḥ saṃyujyeta kathañcana |
lokaścāyaṃ warārohe dharmo'yamiti maṃsyate ||40||

dhārmikaśca kurūṇāṃ sa bhawiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ |
dattasyāpi ca dharmeṇa nādharme raṃsyate manaḥ ||41||

tasmāddharmaṃ puraskṛtya niyatā twaṃ śucismite |
upacārābhicārābhyāṃ dharmamārādhayaswa wai ||42||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

sā tathoktā tathetyuktwā tena bhartrā warāṅganā |
abhiwādyābhyanujñātā pradakṣiṇamawartata ||43||






                  114


waiśampāyana uwāca||

saṃwatsarāhite garbhe gāndhāryā janamejaya |
āhwayāmāsa wai kuntī garbhārthaṃ dharmamacyutam ||1||

sā baliṃ twaritā dewī dharmāyopajahāra ha |
jajāpa japyaṃ widhiwaddattaṃ durwāsasā purā ||2||

saṅgamya sā tu dharmeṇa yogamūrtidhareṇa wai |
lebhe putraṃ warārohā sarwaprāṇabhṛtāṃ waram ||3||

aindre candrasamāyukte muhūrte'bhijite'ṣṭame |
diwā madhyagate sūrye tithau puṇye'bhipūjite ||4||

samṛddhayaśasaṃ kuntī suṣāwa samaye sutam |
jātamātre sute tasminwāguwācāśarīriṇī ||5||

eṣa dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho bhawiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ |
yudhiṣṭhira iti khyātaḥ pāṇḍoḥ prathamajaḥ sutaḥ ||6||

bhawitā prathito rājā triṣu lokeṣu wiśrutaḥ |
yaśasā tejasā caiwa wṛttena ca samanwitaḥ ||7||

dhārmikaṃ taṃ sutaṃ labdhwā pāṇḍustāṃ punarabrawīt |
prāhuḥ kṣatraṃ balajyeṣṭhaṃ balajyeṣṭhaṃ sutaṃ wṛṇu ||8||

tatastathoktā patyā tu wāyumewājuhāwa sā |
tasmājjajñe mahābāhurbhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ ||9||

tamapyatibalaṃ jātaṃ wāgabhyawadadacyutam |
sarweṣāṃ balināṃ śreṣṭho jāto'yamiti bhārata ||10||

idamatyadbhutaṃ cāsījjātamātre wṛkodare |
yadaṅkātpatito mātuḥ śilāṃ gātrairacūrṇayat ||11||

kuntī wyāghrabhayodwignā sahasotpatitā kila |
nānwabudhyata saṃsuptamutsaṅge swe wṛkodaram ||12||

tataḥ sa wajrasaṅghātaḥ kumāro'bhyapatadgirau |
patatā tena śatadhā śilā gātrairwicūrṇitā ||13||

tāṃ śilāṃ cūrṇitāṃ dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍurwismayamāgamat ||13||

yasminnahani bhīmastu jajñe bharatasattama |
duryodhano'pi tatraiwa prajajñe wasudhādhipa ||14||

jāte wṛkodare pāṇḍuridaṃ bhūyo'nwacintayat |
kathaṃ nu me waraḥ putro lokaśreṣṭho bhawediti ||15||

daiwe puruṣakāre ca loko'yaṃ hi pratiṣṭhitaḥ |
tatra daiwaṃ tu widhinā kālayuktena labhyate ||16||

indro hi rājā dewānāṃ pradhāna iti naḥ śrutam |
aprameyabalotsāho wīryawānamitadyutiḥ ||17||

taṃ toṣayitwā tapasā putraṃ lapsye mahābalam |
yaṃ dāsyati sa me putraṃ sa warīyānbhawiṣyati ||18||

karmaṇā manasā wācā tasmāttapsye mahattapaḥ ||18||

tataḥ pāṇḍurmahātejā mantrayitwā maharṣibhiḥ |
dideśa kuntyāḥ kaurawyo wrataṃ sāṃwatsaraṃ śubham ||19||

ātmanā ca mahābāhurekapādasthito'bhawat |
ugraṃ sa tapa ātasthe parameṇa samādhinā ||20||

ārirādhayiṣurdewaṃ tridaśānāṃ tamīśwaram |
sūryeṇa saha dharmātmā paryawartata bhārata ||21||

taṃ tu kālena mahatā wāsawaḥ pratyabhāṣata |
putraṃ tawa pradāsyāmi triṣu lokeṣu wiśrutam ||22||

dewānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca suhṛdāṃ cārthasādhakam |
sutaṃ te'gryaṃ pradāsyāmi sarwāmitrawināśanam ||23||

ityuktaḥ kaurawo rājā wāsawena mahātmanā |
uwāca kuntīṃ dharmātmā dewarājawacaḥ smaran ||24||

nītimantaṃ mahātmānamādityasamatejasam |
durādharṣaṃ kriyāwantamatīwādbhutadarśanam ||25||

putraṃ janaya suśroṇi dhāma kṣatriyatejasām |
labdhaḥ prasādo dewendrāttamāhwaya śucismite ||26||

ewamuktā tataḥ śakramājuhāwa yaśaswinī |
athājagāma dewendro janayāmāsa cārjunam ||27||

jātamātre kumāre tu wāguwācāśarīriṇī |
mahāgambhīranirghoṣā nabho nādayatī tadā ||28||

kārtawīryasamaḥ kunti śibitulyaparākramaḥ |
eṣa śakra iwājeyo yaśaste prathayiṣyati ||29||

adityā wiṣṇunā prītiryathābhūdabhiwardhitā |
tathā wiṣṇusamaḥ prītiṃ wardhayiṣyati te'rjunaḥ ||30||

eṣa madrānwaśe kṛtwā kurūṃśca saha kekayaiḥ |
cedikāśikarūṣāṃśca kurulakṣma sudhāsyati ||31||

etasya bhujawīryeṇa khāṇḍawe hawyawāhanaḥ |
medasā sarwabhūtānāṃ tṛptiṃ yāsyati wai parām ||32||

grāmaṇīśca mahīpālāneṣa jitwā mahābalaḥ |
bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito wīrastrīnmedhānāhariṣyati ||33||

jāmadagnyasamaḥ kunti wiṣṇutulyaparākramaḥ |
eṣa wīryawatāṃ śreṣṭho bhawiṣyatyaparājitaḥ ||34||

tathā diwyāni cāstrāṇi nikhilānyāhariṣyati |
wipranaṣṭāṃ śriyaṃ cāyamāhartā puruṣarṣabhaḥ ||35||

etāmatyadbhutāṃ wācaṃ kuntīputrasya sūtake |
uktawānwāyurākāśe kuntī śuśrāwa cāsya tām ||36||

wācamuccāritāmuccaistāṃ niśamya tapaswinām |
babhūwa paramo harṣaḥ śataśṛṅganiwāsinām ||37||

tathā dewaṛṣīṇāṃ ca sendrāṇāṃ ca diwaukasām |
ākāśe dundubhīnāṃ ca babhūwa tumulaḥ swanaḥ ||38||

udatiṣṭhanmahāghoṣaḥ puṣpawṛṣṭibhirāwṛtaḥ |
samawetya ca dewānāṃ gaṇāḥ pārthamapūjayan ||39||

kādraweyā wainateyā gandharwāpsarasastathā |
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarwe sapta caiwa maharṣayaḥ ||40||

bharadwājaḥ kaśyapo gautamaśca; wiśwāmitro jamadagnirwasiṣṭhaḥ |
yaścodito bhāskare'bhūtpranaṣṭe; so'pyatrātrirbhagawānājagāma ||41||

marīciraṅgirāścaiwa pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ |
dakṣaḥ prajāpatiścaiwa gandharwāpsarasastathā ||42||

diwyamālyāmbaradharāḥ sarwālaṅkārabhūṣitāḥ |
upagāyanti bībhatsumupanṛtyanti cāpsarāḥ ||43||

gandharwaiḥ sahitaḥ śrīmānprāgāyata ca tumburuḥ ||43||

bhīmasenograsenau ca ūrṇāyuranaghastathā |
gopatirdhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryawarcāśca saptamaḥ ||44||

yugapastṛṇapaḥ kārṣṇirnandiścitrarathastathā |
trayodaśaḥ śāliśirāḥ parjanyaśca caturdaśaḥ ||45||

kaliḥ pañcadaśaścātra nāradaścaiwa ṣoḍaśaḥ |
sadwā bṛhadwā bṛhakaḥ karālaśca mahāyaśāḥ ||46||

brahmacārī bahuguṇaḥ suparṇaśceti wiśrutaḥ |
wiśwāwasurbhumanyuśca sucandro daśamastathā ||47||

gītamādhuryasampannau wikhyātau ca hahāhuhū |
ityete dewagandharwā jagustatra nararṣabham ||48||

tathaiwāpsaraso hṛṣṭāḥ sarwālaṅkārabhūṣitāḥ |
nanṛturwai mahābhāgā jaguścāyatalocanāḥ ||49||

anūnā cānawadyā ca priyamukhyā guṇāwarā |
adrikā ca tathā sācī miśrakeśī alambusā ||50||

marīciḥ śicukā caiwa widyutparṇā tilottamā |
agnikā lakṣaṇā kṣemā dewī rambhā manoramā ||51||

asitā ca subāhuśca supriyā suwapustathā |
puṇḍarīkā sugandhā ca surathā ca pramāthinī ||52||

kāmyā śāradwatī caiwa nanṛtustatra saṅghaśaḥ |
menakā sahajanyā ca parṇikā puñjikasthalā ||53||

kratusthalā ghṛtācī ca wiśwācī pūrwacittyapi |
umlocetyabhiwikhyātā pramloceti ca tā daśa ||54||

urwaśyekādaśītyetā jagurāyatalocanāḥ ||54||

dhātāryamā ca mitraśca waruṇoṃ'śo bhagastathā |
indro wiwaswānpūṣā ca twaṣṭā ca sawitā tathā ||55||

parjanyaścaiwa wiṣṇuśca ādityāḥ pāwakārciṣaḥ |
mahimānaṃ pāṇḍawasya wardhayanto'mbare sthitāḥ ||56||

mṛgawyādhaśca śarwaśca nirṛtiśca mahāyaśāḥ |
ajaikapādahirbudhnyaḥ pinākī ca parantapaḥ ||57||

dahano'theśwaraścaiwa kapālī ca wiśāṃ pate |
sthāṇurbhawaśca bhagawānrudrāstatrāwatasthire ||58||

aświnau wasawaścāṣṭau marutaśca mahābalāḥ |
wiśwedewāstathā sādhyāstatrāsanparisaṃsthitāḥ ||59||

karkoṭako'tha śeṣaśca wāsukiśca bhujaṅgamaḥ |
kacchapaścāpakuṇḍaśca takṣakaśca mahoragaḥ ||60||

āyayustejasā yuktā mahākrodhā mahābalāḥ |
ete cānye ca bahawastatra nāgā wyawasthitāḥ ||61||

tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiśca garuḍaścāsitadhwajaḥ |
aruṇaścāruṇiścaiwa wainateyā wyawasthitāḥ ||62||

taddṛṣṭwā mahadāścaryaṃ wismitā munisattamāḥ |
adhikāṃ sma tato wṛttimawartanpāṇḍawānprati ||63||

pāṇḍustu punarewaināṃ putralobhānmahāyaśāḥ |
prāhiṇoddarśanīyāṅgīṃ kuntī twenamathābrawīt ||64||

nātaścaturthaṃ prasawamāpatswapi wadantyuta |
ataḥ paraṃ cāriṇī syātpañcame bandhakī bhawet ||65||

sa twaṃ widwandharmamimaṃ buddhigamyaṃ kathaṃ nu mām |
apatyārthaṃ samutkramya pramādādiwa bhāṣase ||66||






                  115


waiśampāyana uwāca||

kuntīputreṣu jāteṣu dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajeṣu ca |
madrarājasutā pāṇḍuṃ raho wacanamabrawīt ||1||

na me'sti twayi santāpo wiguṇe'pi parantapa |
nāwaratwe warārhāyāḥ sthitwā cānagha nityadā ||2||

gāndhāryāścaiwa nṛpate jātaṃ putraśataṃ tathā |
śrutwā na me tathā duḥkhamabhawatkurunandana ||3||

idaṃ tu me mahadduḥkhaṃ tulyatāyāmaputratā |
diṣṭyā twidānīṃ bharturme kuntyāmapyasti santatiḥ ||4||

yadi twapatyasantānaṃ kuntirājasutā mayi |
kuryādanugraho me syāttawa cāpi hitaṃ bhawet ||5||

stambho hi me sapatnītwādwaktuṃ kuntisutāṃ prati |
yadi tu twaṃ prasanno me swayamenāṃ pracodaya ||6||

pāṇḍuruwāca||

mamāpyeṣa sadā mādri hṛdyarthaḥ pariwartate |
na tu twāṃ prasahe waktumiṣṭāniṣṭawiwakṣayā ||7||

tawa twidaṃ mataṃ jñātwā prayatiṣyāmyataḥ param |
manye dhruwaṃ mayoktā sā waco me pratipatsyate ||8||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ kuntīṃ punaḥ pāṇḍurwiwikta idamabrawīt |
kulasya mama santānaṃ lokasya ca kuru priyam ||9||

mama cāpiṇḍanāśāya pūrweṣāmapi cātmanaḥ |
matpriyārthaṃ ca kalyāṇi kuru kalyāṇamuttamam ||10||

yaśaso'rthāya caiwa twaṃ kuru karma suduṣkaram |
prāpyādhipatyamindreṇa yajñairiṣṭaṃ yaśorthinā ||11||

tathā mantrawido wiprāstapastaptwā suduṣkaram |
gurūnabhyupagacchanti yaśaso'rthāya bhāmini ||12||

tathā rājarṣayaḥ sarwe brāhmaṇāśca tapodhanāḥ |
cakruruccāwacaṃ karma yaśaso'rthāya duṣkaram ||13||

sā twaṃ mādrīṃ plawenewa tārayemāmanindite |
apatyasaṃwibhāgena parāṃ kīrtimawāpnuhi ||14||

ewamuktābrawīnmādrīṃ sakṛccintaya daiwatam |
tasmātte bhawitāpatyamanurūpamasaṃśayam ||15||

tato mādrī wicāryaiwa jagāma manasāświnau |
tāwāgamya sutau tasyāṃ janayāmāsaturyamau ||16||

nakulaṃ sahadewaṃ ca rūpeṇāpratimau bhuwi |
tathaiwa tāwapi yamau wāguwācāśarīriṇī ||17||

rūpasattwaguṇopetāwetāwanyāñjanānati |
bhāsatastejasātyarthaṃ rūpadrawiṇasampadā ||18||

nāmāni cakrire teṣāṃ śataśṛṅganiwāsinaḥ |
bhaktyā ca karmaṇā caiwa tathāśīrbhirwiśāṃ pate ||19||

jyeṣṭhaṃ yudhiṣṭhiretyāhurbhīmaseneti madhyamam |
arjuneti tṛtīyaṃ ca kuntīputrānakalpayan ||20||

pūrwajaṃ nakuletyewaṃ sahadeweti cāparam |
mādrīputrāwakathayaṃste wiprāḥ prītamānasāḥ ||21||

anusaṃwatsaraṃ jātā api te kurusattamāḥ ||21||

kuntīmatha punaḥ pāṇḍurmādryarthe samacodayat |
tamuwāca pṛthā rājanrahasyuktā satī sadā ||22||

uktā sakṛddwandwameṣā lebhe tenāsmi wañcitā |
bibhemyasyāḥ paribhawānnārīṇāṃ gatirīdṛśī ||23||

nājñāsiṣamahaṃ mūḍhā dwandwāhwāne phaladwayam |
tasmānnāhaṃ niyoktawyā twayaiṣo'stu waro mama ||24||

ewaṃ pāṇḍoḥ sutāḥ pañca dewadattā mahābalāḥ |
sambhūtāḥ kīrtimantaste kuruwaṃśawiwardhanāḥ ||25||

śubhalakṣaṇasampannāḥ somawatpriyadarśanāḥ |
siṃhadarpā maheṣwāsāḥ siṃhawikrāntagāminaḥ ||26||

siṃhagrīwā manuṣyendrā wawṛdhurdewawikramāḥ ||26||

wiwardhamānāste tatra puṇye haimawate girau |
wismayaṃ janayāmāsurmaharṣīṇāṃ sameyuṣām ||27||

te ca pañca śataṃ caiwa kuruwaṃśawiwardhanāḥ |
sarwe wawṛdhuralpena kālenāpswiwa nīrajāḥ ||28||






                  116


waiśampāyana uwāca||

darśanīyāṃstataḥ putrānpāṇḍuḥ pañca mahāwane |
tānpaśyanparwate reme swabāhubalapālitān ||1||

supuṣpitawane kāle kadācinmadhumādhawe |
bhūtasaṃmohane rājā sabhāryo wyacaradwanam ||2||

palāśaistilakaiścūtaiścampakaiḥ pāribhadrakaiḥ |
anyaiśca bahubhirwṛkṣaiḥ phalapuṣpasamṛddhibhiḥ ||3||

jalasthānaiśca wiwidhaiḥ padminībhiśca śobhitam |
pāṇḍorwanaṃ tu samprekṣya prajajñe hṛdi manmathaḥ ||4||

prahṛṣṭamanasaṃ tatra wiharantaṃ yathāmaram |
taṃ mādryanujagāmaikā wasanaṃ bibhratī śubham ||5||

samīkṣamāṇaḥ sa tu tāṃ wayaḥsthāṃ tanuwāsasam |
tasya kāmaḥ prawawṛdhe gahane'gniriwotthitaḥ ||6||

rahasyātmasamāṃ dṛṣṭwā rājā rājīwalocanām |
na śaśāka niyantuṃ taṃ kāmaṃ kāmabalātkṛtaḥ ||7||

tata enāṃ balādrājā nijagrāha rahogatām |
wāryamāṇastayā dewyā wisphurantyā yathābalam ||8||

sa tu kāmaparītātmā taṃ śāpaṃ nānwabudhyata |
mādrīṃ maithunadharmeṇa gacchamāno balādiwa ||9||

jīwitāntāya kaurawyo manmathasya waśaṃ gataḥ |
śāpajaṃ bhayamutsṛjya jagāmaiwa balātpriyām ||10||

tasya kāmātmano buddhiḥ sākṣātkālena mohitā |
sampramathyendriyagrāmaṃ pranaṣṭā saha cetasā ||11||

sa tayā saha saṅgamya bhāryayā kurunandana |
pāṇḍuḥ paramadharmātmā yuyuje kāladharmaṇā ||12||

tato mādrī samāliṅgya rājānaṃ gatacetasam |
mumoca duḥkhajaṃ śabdaṃ punaḥ punaratīwa ha ||13||

saha putraistataḥ kuntī mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍawau |
ājagmuḥ sahitāstatra yatra rājā tathāgataḥ ||14||

tato mādryabrawīdrājannārtā kuntīmidaṃ wacaḥ |
ekaiwa twamihāgaccha tiṣṭhantwatraiwa dārakāḥ ||15||

tacchrutwā wacanaṃ tasyāstatraiwāwārya dārakān |
hatāhamiti wikruśya sahasopajagāma ha ||16||

dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍuṃ ca mādrīṃ ca śayānau dharaṇītale |
kuntī śokaparītāṅgī wilalāpa suduḥkhitā ||17||

rakṣyamāṇo mayā nityaṃ wīraḥ satatamātmawān |
kathaṃ twamabhyatikrāntaḥ śāpaṃ jānanwanaukasaḥ ||18||

nanu nāma twayā mādri rakṣitawyo janādhipaḥ |
sā kathaṃ lobhitawatī wijane twaṃ narādhipam ||19||

kathaṃ dīnasya satataṃ twāmāsādya rahogatām |
taṃ wicintayataḥ śāpaṃ praharṣaḥ samajāyata ||20||

dhanyā twamasi bāhlīki matto bhāgyatarā tathā |
dṛṣṭawatyasi yadwaktraṃ prahṛṣṭasya mahīpateḥ ||21||

mādryuwāca||

wilobhyamānena mayā wāryamāṇena cāsakṛt |
ātmā na wārito'nena satyaṃ diṣṭaṃ cikīrṣuṇā ||22||

kuntyuwāca||

ahaṃ jyeṣṭhā dharmapatnī jyeṣṭhaṃ dharmaphalaṃ mama |
awaśyaṃ bhāwino bhāwānmā māṃ mādri niwartaya ||23||

anweṣyāmīha bhartāramahaṃ pretawaśaṃ gatam |
uttiṣṭha twaṃ wisṛjyainamimānrakṣaswa dārakān ||24||

mādryuwāca||

ahamewānuyāsyāmi bhartāramapalāyinam |
na hi tṛptāsmi kāmānāṃ tajjyeṣṭhā anumanyatām ||25||

māṃ cābhigamya kṣīṇo'yaṃ kāmādbharatasattamaḥ |
tamucchindyāmasya kāmaṃ kathaṃ nu yamasādane ||26||

na cāpyahaṃ wartayantī nirwiśeṣaṃ suteṣu te |
wṛttimārye cariṣyāmi spṛśedenastathā hi mām ||27||

tasmānme sutayoḥ kunti wartitawyaṃ swaputrawat |
māṃ hi kāmayamāno'yaṃ rājā pretawaśaṃ gataḥ ||28||

rājñaḥ śarīreṇa saha mamāpīdaṃ kalewaram |
dagdhawyaṃ supraticchannametadārye priyaṃ kuru ||29||

dārakeṣwapramattā ca bhawethāśca hitā mama |
ato'nyanna prapaśyāmi saṃdeṣṭawyaṃ hi kiñcana ||30||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ityuktwā taṃ citāgnisthaṃ dharmapatnī nararṣabham |
madrarājātmajā tūrṇamanwārohadyaśaswinī ||31||






                  117


waiśampāyana uwāca||

pāṇḍorawabhṛthaṃ kṛtwā dewakalpā maharṣayaḥ |
tato mantramakurwanta te sametya tapaswinaḥ ||1||

hitwā rājyaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca sa mahātmā mahātapāḥ |
asminsthāne tapastaptuṃ tāpasāñśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ||2||

sa jātamātrānputrāṃśca dārāṃśca bhawatāmiha |
pradāyopanidhiṃ rājā pāṇḍuḥ swargamito gataḥ ||3||

te parasparamāmantrya sarwabhūtahite ratāḥ |
pāṇḍoḥ putrānpuraskṛtya nagaraṃ nāgasāhwayam ||4||

udāramanasaḥ siddhā gamane cakrire manaḥ |
bhīṣmāya pāṇḍawāndātuṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya caiwa hi ||5||

tasminnewa kṣaṇe sarwe tānādāya pratasthire |
pāṇḍordārāṃśca putrāṃśca śarīraṃ caiwa tāpasāḥ ||6||

sukhinī sā purā bhūtwā satataṃ putrawatsalā |
prapannā dīrghamadhwānaṃ saṅkṣiptaṃ tadamanyata ||7||

sā nadīrgheṇa kālena samprāptā kurujāṅgalam |
wardhamānapuradwāramāsasāda yaśaswinī ||8||

taṃ cāraṇasahasrāṇāṃ munīnāmāgamaṃ tadā |
śrutwā nāgapure nṛṇāṃ wismayaḥ samajāyata ||9||

muhūrtodita āditye sarwe dharmapuraskṛtāḥ |
sadārāstāpasāndraṣṭuṃ niryayuḥ purawāsinaḥ ||10||

strīsaṅghāḥ kṣatrasaṅghāśca yānasaṅghānsamāsthitāḥ |
brāhmaṇaiḥ saha nirjagmurbrāhmaṇānāṃ ca yoṣitaḥ ||11||

tathā wiṭśūdrasaṅghānāṃ mahānwyatikaro'bhawat |
na kaścidakarodīrṣyāmabhawandharmabuddhayaḥ ||12||

tathā bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawaḥ somadatto'tha bāhlikaḥ |
prajñācakṣuśca rājarṣiḥ kṣattā ca widuraḥ swayam ||13||

sā ca satyawatī dewī kausalyā ca yaśaswinī |
rājadāraiḥ pariwṛtā gāndhārī ca winiryayau ||14||

dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dāyādā duryodhanapurogamāḥ |
bhūṣitā bhūṣaṇaiścitraiḥ śatasaṅkhyā winiryayuḥ ||15||

tānmaharṣigaṇānsarwāñśirobhirabhiwādya ca |
upopawiwiśuḥ sarwe kaurawyāḥ sapurohitāḥ ||16||

tathaiwa śirasā bhūmāwabhiwādya praṇamya ca |
upopawiwiśuḥ sarwe paurajānapadā api ||17||

tamakūjamiwājñāya janaughaṃ sarwaśastadā |
bhīṣmo rājyaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca maharṣibhyo nyawedayat ||18||

teṣāmatho wṛddhatamaḥ pratyutthāya jaṭājinī |
maharṣimatamājñāya maharṣiridamabrawīt ||19||

yaḥ sa kaurawyadāyādaḥ pāṇḍurnāma narādhipaḥ |
kāmabhogānparityajya śataśṛṅgamito gataḥ ||20||

brahmacaryawratasthasya tasya diwyena hetunā |
sākṣāddharmādayaṃ putrastasya jāto yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||21||

tathemaṃ balināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tasya rājño mahātmanaḥ |
mātariśwā dadau putraṃ bhīmaṃ nāma mahābalam ||22||

puruhūtādayaṃ jajñe kuntyāṃ satyaparākramaḥ |
yasya kīritrmaheṣwāsānsarwānabhibhawiṣyati ||23||

yau tu mādrī maheṣwāsāwasūta kurusattamau |
aświbhyāṃ manujawyāghrāwimau tāwapi tiṣṭhataḥ ||24||

caratā dharmanityena wanawāsaṃ yaśaswinā |
eṣa paitāmaho waṃśaḥ pāṇḍunā punaruddhṛtaḥ ||25||

putrāṇāṃ janma wṛddhiṃ ca waidikādhyayanāni ca |
paśyataḥ satataṃ pāṇḍoḥ śaśwatprītirawardhata ||26||

wartamānaḥ satāṃ wṛtte putralābhamawāpya ca |
pitṛlokaṃ gataḥ pāṇḍuritaḥ saptadaśe'hani ||27||

taṃ citāgatamājñāya waiśwānaramukhe hutam |
prawiṣṭā pāwakaṃ mādrī hitwā jīwitamātmanaḥ ||28||

sā gatā saha tenaiwa patilokamanuwratā |
tasyāstasya ca yatkāryaṃ kriyatāṃ tadanantaram ||29||

ime tayoḥ śarīre dwe sutāśceme tayorwarāḥ |
kriyābhiranugṛhyantāṃ saha mātrā parantapāḥ ||30||

pretakārye ca nirwṛtte pitṛmedhaṃ mahāyaśāḥ |
labhatāṃ sarwadharmajñaḥ pāṇḍuḥ kurukulodwahaḥ ||31||

ewamuktwā kurūnsarwānkurūṇāmewa paśyatām |
kṣaṇenāntarhitāḥ sarwe cāraṇā guhyakaiḥ saha ||32||

gandharwanagarākāraṃ tatraiwāntarhitaṃ punaḥ |
ṛṣisiddhagaṇaṃ dṛṣṭwā wismayaṃ te paraṃ yayuḥ ||33||






                  118


dhṛtarāṣṭra uwāca||

pāṇḍorwidura sarwāṇi pretakāryāṇi kāraya |
rājawadrājasiṃhasya mādryāścaiwa wiśeṣataḥ ||1||

paśūnwāsāṃsi ratnāni dhanāni wiwidhāni ca |
pāṇḍoḥ prayaccha mādryāśca yebhyo yāwacca wāñchitam ||2||

yathā ca kuntī satkāraṃ kuryānmādryāstathā kuru |
yathā na wāyurnādityaḥ paśyetāṃ tāṃ susaṃwṛtām ||3||

na śocyaḥ pāṇḍuranaghaḥ praśasyaḥ sa narādhipaḥ |
yasya pañca sutā wīrā jātāḥ surasutopamāḥ ||4||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

widurastaṃ tathetyuktwā bhīṣmeṇa saha bhārata |
pāṇḍuṃ saṃskārayāmāsa deśe paramasaṃwṛte ||5||

tatastu nagarāttūrṇamājyahomapuraskṛtāḥ |
nirhṛtāḥ pāwakā dīptāḥ pāṇḍo rājapurohitaiḥ ||6||

athainamārtawairgandhairmālyaiśca wiwidhairwaraiḥ |
śibikāṃ samalañcakrurwāsasācchādya sarwaśaḥ ||7||

tāṃ tathā śobhitāṃ mālyairwāsobhiśca mahādhanaiḥ |
amātyā jñātayaścaiwa suhṛdaścopatasthire ||8||

nṛsiṃhaṃ narayuktena paramālaṅkṛtena tam |
awahanyānamukhyena saha mādryā susaṃwṛtam ||9||

pāṇḍureṇātapatreṇa cāmarawyajanena ca |
sarwawāditranādaiśca samalañcakrire tataḥ ||10||

ratnāni cāpyupādāya bahūni śataśo narāḥ |
pradaduḥ kāṅkṣamāṇebhyaḥ pāṇḍostatraurdhwadehikam ||11||

atha chatrāṇi śubhrāṇi pāṇḍurāṇi bṛhanti ca |
ājahruḥ kaurawasyārthe wāsāṃsi rucirāṇi ca ||12||

yājakaiḥ śuklawāsobhirhūyamānā hutāśanāḥ |
agacchannagratastasya dīpyamānāḥ swalaṅkṛtāḥ ||13||

brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā waiśyāḥ śūdrāścaiwa sahasraśaḥ |
rudantaḥ śokasantaptā anujagmurnarādhipam ||14||

ayamasmānapāhāya duḥkhe cādhāya śāśwate |
kṛtwānāthānparo nāthaḥ kwa yāsyati narādhipaḥ ||15||

krośantaḥ pāṇḍawāḥ sarwe bhīṣmo widura ewa ca |
ramaṇīye wanoddeśe gaṅgātīre same śubhe ||16||

nyāsayāmāsuratha tāṃ śibikāṃ satyawādinaḥ |
sabhāryasya nṛsiṃhasya pāṇḍorakliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ ||17||

tatastasya śarīraṃ tatsarwagandhaniṣewitam |
śucikālīyakādigdhaṃ mukhyasnānādhiwāsitam ||18||

paryaṣiñcajjalenāśu śātakumbhamayairghaṭaiḥ ||18||

candanena ca mukhyena śuklena samalepayan |
kālāguruwimiśreṇa tathā tuṅgarasena ca ||19||

athainaṃ deśajaiḥ śuklairwāsobhiḥ samayojayan |
ācchannaḥ sa tu wāsobhirjīwanniwa nararṣabhaḥ ||20||

śuśubhe puruṣawyāghro mahārhaśayanocitaḥ ||20||

yājakairabhyanujñātaṃ pretakarmaṇi niṣṭhitaiḥ |
ghṛtāwasiktaṃ rājānaṃ saha mādryā swalaṅkṛtam ||21||

tuṅgapadmakamiśreṇa candanena sugandhinā |
anyaiśca wiwidhairgandhairanalpaiḥ samadāhayan ||22||

tatastayoḥ śarīre te dṛṣṭwā mohawaśaṃ gatā |
hāhā putreti kausalyā papāta sahasā bhuwi ||23||

tāṃ prekṣya patitāmārtāṃ paurajānapado janaḥ |
ruroda saswanaṃ sarwo rājabhaktyā kṛpānwitaḥ ||24||

klāntānīwārtanādena sarwāṇi ca wicukruśuḥ |
mānuṣaiḥ saha bhūtāni tiryagyonigatānyapi ||25||

tathā bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawo widuraśca mahāmatiḥ |
sarwaśaḥ kaurawāścaiwa prāṇadanbhṛśaduḥkhitāḥ ||26||

tato bhīṣmo'tha widuro rājā ca saha bandhubhiḥ |
udakaṃ cakrire tasya sarwāśca kuruyoṣitaḥ ||27||

kṛtodakāṃstānādāya pāṇḍawāñśokakarśitān |
sarwāḥ prakṛtayo rājañśocantyaḥ paryawārayan ||28||

yathaiwa pāṇḍawā bhūmau suṣupuḥ saha bāndhawaiḥ |
tathaiwa nāgarā rājañśiśyire brāhmaṇādayaḥ ||29||

tadanānandamaswasthamākumāramahṛṣṭawat |
babhūwa pāṇḍawaiḥ sārdhaṃ nagaraṃ dwādaśa kṣapāḥ ||30||






                  119


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ kṣattā ca rājā ca bhīṣmaśca saha bandhubhiḥ |
daduḥ śrāddhaṃ tadā pāṇḍoḥ swadhāmṛtamayaṃ tadā ||1||

kurūṃśca wipramukhyāṃśca bhojayitwā sahasraśaḥ |
ratnaughāndwijamukhyebhyo dattwā grāmawarānapi ||2||

kṛtaśaucāṃstatastāṃstu pāṇḍawānbharatarṣabhān |
ādāya wiwiśuḥ paurāḥ puraṃ wāraṇasāhwayam ||3||

satataṃ smānwatapyanta tamewa bharatarṣabham |
paurajānapadāḥ sarwe mṛtaṃ swamiwa bāndhawam ||4||

śrāddhāwasāne tu tadā dṛṣṭwā taṃ duḥkhitaṃ janam |
saṃmūḍhāṃ duḥkhaśokārtāṃ wyāso mātaramabrawīt ||5||

atikrāntasukhāḥ kālāḥ pratyupasthitadāruṇāḥ |
śwaḥ śwaḥ pāpīyadiwasāḥ pṛthiwī gatayauwanā ||6||

bahumāyāsamākīrṇo nānādoṣasamākulaḥ |
luptadharmakriyācāro ghoraḥ kālo bhawiṣyati ||7||

gaccha twaṃ tyāgamāsthāya yuktā wasa tapowane |
mā drakṣyasi kulasyāsya ghoraṃ saṅkṣayamātmanaḥ ||8||

tatheti samanujñāya sā prawiśyābrawītsnuṣām |
ambike tawa putrasya durnayātkila bhāratāḥ ||9||

sānubandhā winaṅkṣyanti pautrāścaiweti naḥ śrutam ||9||

tatkausalyāmimāmārtāṃ putraśokābhipīḍitām |
wanamādāya bhadraṃ te gacchāwo yadi manyase ||10||

tathetyukte ambikayā bhīṣmamāmantrya suwratā |
wanaṃ yayau satyawatī snuṣābhyāṃ saha bhārata ||11||

tāḥ sughoraṃ tapaḥ kṛtwā dewyo bharatasattama |
dehaṃ tyaktwā mahārāja gatimiṣṭāṃ yayustadā ||12||

awāpnuwanta wedoktānsaṃskārānpāṇḍawāstadā |
awardhanta ca bhogāṃste bhuñjānāḥ pitṛweśmani ||13||

dhārtarāṣṭraiśca sahitāḥ krīḍantaḥ pitṛweśmani |
bālakrīḍāsu sarwāsu wiśiṣṭāḥ pāṇḍawābhawan ||14||

jawe lakṣyābhiharaṇe bhojye pāṃsuwikarṣaṇe |
dhārtarāṣṭrānbhīmasenaḥ sarwānsa parimardati ||15||

harṣādetānkrīḍamānāngṛhya kākanilīyane |
śiraḥsu ca nigṛhyainānyodhayāmāsa pāṇḍawaḥ ||16||

śatamekottaraṃ teṣāṃ kumārāṇāṃ mahaujasām |
eka ewa wimṛdnāti nātikṛcchrādwṛkodaraḥ ||17||

pādeṣu ca nigṛhyainānwinihatya balādbalī |
cakarṣa krośato bhūmau ghṛṣṭajānuśirokṣikān ||18||

daśa bālāñjale krīḍanbhujābhyāṃ parigṛhya saḥ |
āste sma salile magnaḥ pramṛtāṃśca wimuñcati ||19||

phalāni wṛkṣamāruhya pracinwanti ca te yadā |
tadā pādaprahāreṇa bhīmaḥ kampayate drumam ||20||

prahārawegābhihatāddrumādwyāghūrṇitāstataḥ |
saphalāḥ prapatanti sma drutaṃ srastāḥ kumārakāḥ ||21||

na te niyuddhe na jawe na yogyāsu kadācana |
kumārā uttaraṃ cakruḥ spardhamānā wṛkodaram ||22||

ewaṃ sa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ spardhamāno wṛkodaraḥ |
apriye'tiṣṭhadatyantaṃ bālyānna drohacetasā ||23||

tato balamatikhyātaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ pratāpawān |
bhīmasenasya tajjñātwā duṣṭabhāwamadarśayat ||24||

tasya dharmādapetasya pāpāni paripaśyataḥ |
mohādaiśwaryalobhācca pāpā matirajāyata ||25||

ayaṃ balawatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kuntīputro wṛkodaraḥ |
madhyamaḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ nikṛtyā saṃnihanyatām ||26||

atha tasmādawarajaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ caiwa yudhiṣṭhiram |
prasahya bandhane baddhwā praśāsiṣye wasundharām ||27||

ewaṃ sa niścayaṃ pāpaḥ kṛtwā duryodhanastadā |
nityamewāntaraprekṣī bhīmasyāsīnmahātmanaḥ ||28||

tato jalawihārārthaṃ kārayāmāsa bhārata |
celakambalaweśmāni wicitrāṇi mahānti ca ||29||

pramāṇakoṭyāmuddeśaṃ sthalaṃ kiñcidupetya ca |
krīḍāwasāne sarwe te śuciwastrāḥ swalaṅkṛtāḥ ||30||

sarwakāmasamṛddhaṃ tadannaṃ bubhujire śanaiḥ ||30||

diwasānte pariśrāntā wihṛtya ca kurūdwahāḥ |
wihārāwasatheṣwewa wīrā wāsamarocayan ||31||

khinnastu balawānbhīmo wyāyāmābhyadhikastadā |
wāhayitwā kumārāṃstāñjalakrīḍāgatānwibhuḥ ||32||

pramāṇakoṭyāṃ wāsārthī suṣwāpāruhya tatsthalam ||32||

śītaṃ wāsaṃ samāsādya śrānto madawimohitaḥ |
niśceṣṭaḥ pāṇḍawo rājansuṣwāpa mṛtakalpawat ||33||

tato baddhwā latāpāśairbhīmaṃ duryodhanaḥ śanaiḥ |
gambhīraṃ bhīmawegaṃ ca sthalājjalamapātayat ||34||

tataḥ prabuddhaḥ kaunteyaḥ sarwaṃ sañchidya bandhanam |
udatiṣṭhajjalādbhūyo bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ waraḥ ||35||

suptaṃ cāpi punaḥ sarpaistīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrairmahāwiṣaiḥ |
kupitairdaṃśayāmāsa sarweṣwewāṅgamarmasu ||36||

daṃṣṭrāśca daṃṣṭriṇāṃ teṣāṃ marmaswapi nipātitāḥ |
twacaṃ naiwāsya bibhiduḥ sāratwātpṛthuwakṣasaḥ ||37||

pratibuddhastu bhīmastānsarwānsarpānapothayat |
sārathiṃ cāsya dayitamapahastena jaghniwān ||38||

bhojane bhīmasenasya punaḥ prākṣepayadwiṣam |
kālakūṭaṃ nawaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ sambhṛtaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ||39||

waiśyāputrastadācaṣṭa pārthānāṃ hitakāmyayā |
taccāpi bhuktwājarayadawikāro wṛkodaraḥ ||40||

wikāraṃ na hyajanayatsutīkṣṇamapi tadwiṣam |
bhīmasaṃhanano bhīmastadapyajarayattataḥ ||41||

ewaṃ duryodhanaḥ karṇaḥ śakuniścāpi saubalaḥ |
anekairabhyupāyaistāñjighāṃsanti sma pāṇḍawān ||42||

pāṇḍawāścāpi tatsarwaṃ pratyajānannariṃdamāḥ |
udbhāwanamakurwanto widurasya mate sthitāḥ ||43||






                  120


janamejaya uwāca||

kṛpasyāpi mahābrahmansambhawaṃ waktumarhasi |
śarastambhātkathaṃ jajñe kathaṃ cāstrāṇyawāptawān ||1||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

maharṣergautamasyāsīccharadwānnāma nāmataḥ |
putraḥ kila mahārāja jātaḥ saha śarairwibho ||2||

na tasya wedādhyayane tathā buddhirajāyata |
yathāsya buddhirabhawaddhanurwede parantapa ||3||

adhijagmuryathā wedāṃstapasā brahmawādinaḥ |
tathā sa tapasopetaḥ sarwāṇyastrāṇyawāpa ha ||4||

dhanurwedaparatwācca tapasā wipulena ca |
bhṛśaṃ santāpayāmāsa dewarājaṃ sa gautamaḥ ||5||

tato jālapadīṃ nāma dewakanyāṃ sureśwaraḥ |
prāhiṇottapaso wighnaṃ kuru tasyeti kaurawa ||6||

sābhigamyāśramapadaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ śaradwataḥ |
dhanurbāṇadharaṃ bālā lobhayāmāsa gautamam ||7||

tāmekawasanāṃ dṛṣṭwā gautamo'psarasaṃ wane |
loke'pratimasaṃsthānāmutphullanayano'bhawat ||8||

dhanuśca hi śarāścāsya karābhyāṃ prāpatanbhuwi |
wepathuścāsya tāṃ dṛṣṭwā śarīre samajāyata ||9||

sa tu jñānagarīyastwāttapasaśca samanwayāt |
awatasthe mahāprājño dhairyeṇa parameṇa ha ||10||

yastwasya sahasā rājanwikāraḥ samapadyata |
tena susrāwa reto'sya sa ca tannāwabudhyata ||11||

sa wihāyāśramaṃ taṃ ca tāṃ caiwāpsarasaṃ muniḥ |
jagāma retastattasya śarastambe papāta ha ||12||

śarastambe ca patitaṃ dwidhā tadabhawannṛpa |
tasyātha mithunaṃ jajñe gautamasya śaradwataḥ ||13||

mṛgayāṃ carato rājñaḥ śantanostu yadṛcchayā |
kaścitsenācaro'raṇye mithunaṃ tadapaśyata ||14||

dhanuśca saśaraṃ dṛṣṭwā tathā kṛṣṇājināni ca |
wyawasya brāhmaṇāpatyaṃ dhanurwedāntagasya tat ||15||

sa rājñe darśayāmāsa mithunaṃ saśaraṃ tadā ||15||

sa tadādāya mithunaṃ rājātha kṛpayānwitaḥ |
ājagāma gṛhānewa mama putrāwiti bruwan ||16||

tataḥ saṃwardhayāmāsa saṃskāraiścāpyayojayat |
gautamo'pi tadāpetya dhanurwedaparo'bhawat ||17||

kṛpayā yanmayā bālāwimau saṃwardhitāwiti |
tasmāttayornāma cakre tadewa sa mahīpatiḥ ||18||

nihitau gautamastatra tapasā tāwawindata |
āgamya cāsmai gotrādi sarwamākhyātawāṃstadā ||19||

caturwidhaṃ dhanurwedamastrāṇi wiwidhāni ca |
nikhilenāsya tatsarwaṃ guhyamākhyātawāṃstadā ||20||

so'cireṇaiwa kālena paramācāryatāṃ gataḥ ||20||

tato'dhijagmuḥ sarwe te dhanurwedaṃ mahārathāḥ |
dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajāścaiwa pāṇḍawāśca mahābalāḥ ||21||

wṛṣṇayaśca nṛpāścānye nānādeśasamāgatāḥ ||21||






                  121


waiśampāyana uwāca||

wiśeṣārthī tato bhīṣmaḥ pautrāṇāṃ winayepsayā |
iṣwastrajñānparyapṛcchadācāryānwīryasaṃmatān ||1||

nālpadhīrnāmahābhāgastathānānāstrakowidaḥ |
nādewasattwo winayetkurūnastre mahābalān ||2||

maharṣistu bharadwājo hawirdhāne caranpurā |
dadarśāpsarasaṃ sākṣādghṛtācīmāplutāmṛṣiḥ ||3||

tasyā wāyuḥ samuddhūto wasanaṃ wyapakarṣata |
tato'sya retaścaskanda tadṛṣirdroṇa ādadhe ||4||

tasminsamabhawaddroṇaḥ kalaśe tasya dhīmataḥ |
adhyagīṣṭa sa wedāṃśca wedāṅgāni ca sarwaśaḥ ||5||

agniweśyaṃ mahābhāgaṃ bharadwājaḥ pratāpawān |
pratyapādayadāgneyamastraṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ waraḥ ||6||

agniṣṭujjātaḥ sa munistato bharatasattama |
bhāradwājaṃ tadāgneyaṃ mahāstraṃ pratyapādayat ||7||

bharadwājasakhā cāsītpṛṣato nāma pārthiwaḥ |
tasyāpi drupado nāma tadā samabhawatsutaḥ ||8||

sa nityamāśramaṃ gatwā droṇena saha pārṣataḥ |
cikrīḍādhyayanaṃ caiwa cakāra kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ ||9||

tato wyatīte pṛṣate sa rājā drupado'bhawat |
pāñcāleṣu mahābāhuruttareṣu nareśwaraḥ ||10||

bharadwājo'pi bhagawānāruroha diwaṃ tadā |
tataḥ pitṛniyuktātmā putralobhānmahāyaśāḥ ||11||

śāradwatīṃ tato droṇaḥ kṛpīṃ bhāryāmawindata ||11||

agnihotre ca dharme ca dame ca satataṃ ratā |
alabhadgautamī putramaśwatthāmānamewa ca ||12||

sa jātamātro wyanadadyathaiwoccaiḥśrawā hayaḥ |
tacchrutwāntarhitaṃ bhūtamantarikṣasthamabrawīt ||13||

aśwasyewāsya yatsthāma nadataḥ pradiśo gatam |
aśwatthāmaiwa bālo'yaṃ tasmānnāmnā bhawiṣyati ||14||

sutena tena suprīto bhāradwājastato'bhawat |
tatraiwa ca wasandhīmāndhanurwedaparo'bhawat ||15||

sa śuśrāwa mahātmānaṃ jāmadagnyaṃ parantapam |
brāhmaṇebhyastadā rājanditsantaṃ wasu sarwaśaḥ ||16||

wanaṃ tu prasthitaṃ rāmaṃ bhāradwājastadābrawīt |
āgataṃ wittakāmaṃ māṃ widdhi droṇaṃ dwijarṣabham ||17||

rāma uwāca||

hiraṇyaṃ mama yaccānyadwasu kiñcana widyate |
brāhmaṇebhyo mayā dattaṃ sarwamewa tapodhana ||18||

tathaiweyaṃ dharā dewī sāgarāntā sapattanā |
kaśyapāya mayā dattā kṛtsnā nagaramālinī ||19||

śarīramātramewādya mayedamawaśeṣitam |
astrāṇi ca mahārhāṇi śastrāṇi wiwidhāni ca ||20||

wṛṇīṣwa kiṃ prayacchāmi tubhyaṃ droṇa wadāśu tat ||20||

droṇa uwāca||

astrāṇi me samagrāṇi sasaṃhārāṇi bhārgawa |
saprayogarahasyāni dātumarhasyaśeṣataḥ ||21||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tathetyuktwā tatastasmai prādādastrāṇi bhārgawaḥ |
sarahasyawrataṃ caiwa dhanurwedamaśeṣataḥ ||22||

pratigṛhya tu tatsarwaṃ kṛtāstro dwijasattamaḥ |
priyaṃ sakhāyaṃ suprīto jagāma drupadaṃ prati ||23||






                  122


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato drupadamāsādya bhāradwājaḥ pratāpawān |
abrawītpārṣataṃ rājansakhāyaṃ widdhi māmiti ||1||

drupada uwāca||

akṛteyaṃ tawa prajñā brahmannātisamañjasī |
yanmāṃ brawīṣi prasabhaṃ sakhā te'hamiti dwija ||2||

na hi rājñāmudīrṇānāmewaṃ bhūtairnaraiḥ kwacit |
sakhyaṃ bhawati mandātmañśriyā hīnairdhanacyutaiḥ ||3||

sauhṛdānyapi jīryante kālena parijīryatām |
sauhṛdaṃ me twayā hyāsītpūrwaṃ sāmarthyabandhanam ||4||

na sakhyamajaraṃ loke jātu dṛśyeta karhicit |
kāmo wainaṃ wiharati krodhaścainaṃ prawṛścati ||5||

maiwaṃ jīrṇamupāsiṣṭhāḥ sakhyaṃ nawamupākuru |
āsītsakhyaṃ dwijaśreṣṭha twayā me'rthanibandhanam ||6||

na daridro wasumato nāwidwānwiduṣaḥ sakhā |
śūrasya na sakhā klībaḥ sakhipūrwaṃ kimiṣyate ||7||

yayorewa samaṃ wittaṃ yayorewa samaṃ kulam |
tayoḥ sakhyaṃ wiwāhaśca na tu puṣṭawipuṣṭayoḥ ||8||

nāśrotriyaḥ śrotriyasya nārathī rathinaḥ sakhā |
nārājñā saṅgataṃ rājñaḥ sakhipūrwaṃ kimiṣyate ||9||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

drupadenaiwamuktastu bhāradwājaḥ pratāpawān |
muhūrtaṃ cintayāmāsa manyunābhipariplutaḥ ||10||

sa winiścitya manasā pāñcālaṃ prati buddhimān |
jagāma kurumukhyānāṃ nagaraṃ nāgasāhwayam ||11||

kumārāstwatha niṣkramya sametā gajasāhwayāt |
krīḍanto wīṭayā tatra wīrāḥ paryacaranmudā ||12||

papāta kūpe sā wīṭā teṣāṃ wai krīḍatāṃ tadā |
na ca te pratyapadyanta karma wīṭopalabdhaye ||13||

atha droṇaḥ kumārāṃstāndṛṣṭwā kṛtyawatastadā |
prahasya mandaṃ paiśalyādabhyabhāṣata wīryawān ||14||

aho nu dhigbalaṃ kṣātraṃ dhigetāṃ waḥ kṛtāstratām |
bharatasyānwaye jātā ye wīṭāṃ nādhigacchata ||15||

eṣa muṣṭiriṣīkāṇāṃ mayāstreṇābhimantritaḥ |
asya wīryaṃ nirīkṣadhwaṃ yadanyasya na widyate ||16||

wetsyāmīṣīkayā wīṭāṃ tāmiṣīkāmathānyayā |
tāmanyayā samāyogo wīṭāyā grahaṇe mama ||17||

tadapaśyankumārāste wismayotphullalocanāḥ |
aweṣkya coddhṛtāṃ wīṭāṃ wīṭāweddhāramabruwan ||18||

abhiwādayāmahe brahmannaitadanyeṣu widyate |
ko'si kaṃ twābhijānīmo wayaṃ kiṃ karawāmahe ||19||

droṇa uwāca||

ācakṣadhwaṃ ca bhīṣmāya rūpeṇa ca guṇaiśca mām |
sa ewa sumahābuddhiḥ sāmprataṃ pratipatsyate ||20||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tathetyuktwā tu te sarwe bhīṣmamūcuḥ pitāmaham |
brāhmaṇasya wacastathyaṃ tacca karmawiśeṣawat ||21||

bhīṣmaḥ śrutwā kumārāṇāṃ droṇaṃ taṃ pratyajānata |
yuktarūpaḥ sa hi gururityewamanucintya ca ||22||

athainamānīya tadā swayamewa susatkṛtam |
paripapraccha nipuṇaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ waraḥ ||23||

hetumāgamane tasya droṇaḥ sarwaṃ nyawedayat ||23||

maharṣeragniweśyasya sakāśamahamacyuta |
astrārthamagamaṃ pūrwaṃ dhanurwedajighṛkṣayā ||24||

brahmacārī winītātmā jaṭilo bahulāḥ samāḥ |
awasaṃ tatra suciraṃ dhanurwedacikīrṣayā ||25||

pāñcālarājaputrastu yajñaseno mahābalaḥ |
mayā sahākarodwidyāṃ guroḥ śrāmyansamāhitaḥ ||26||

sa me tatra sakhā cāsīdupakārī priyaśca me |
tenāhaṃ saha saṅgamya ratawānsuciraṃ bata ||27||

bālyātprabhṛti kaurawya sahādhyayanamewa ca ||27||

sa samāsādya māṃ tatra priyakārī priyaṃwadaḥ |
abrawīditi māṃ bhīṣma wacanaṃ prītiwardhanam ||28||

ahaṃ priyatamaḥ putraḥ piturdroṇa mahātmanaḥ |
abhiṣekṣyati māṃ rājye sa pāñcālyo yadā tadā ||29||

twadbhojyaṃ bhawitā rājyaṃ sakhe satyena te śape |
mama bhogāśca wittaṃ ca twadadhīnaṃ sukhāni ca ||30||

ewamuktaḥ prawawrāja kṛtāstro'haṃ dhanepsayā |
abhiṣiktaṃ ca śrutwainaṃ kṛtārtho'smīti cintayan ||31||

priyaṃ sakhāyaṃ suprīto rājyasthaṃ punarāwrajam |
saṃsmaransaṅgamaṃ caiwa wacanaṃ caiwa tasya tat ||32||

tato drupadamāgamya sakhipūrwamahaṃ prabho |
abruwaṃ puruṣawyāghra sakhāyaṃ widdhi māmiti ||33||

upasthitaṃ tu drupadaḥ sakhiwaccābhisaṅgatam |
sa māṃ nirākāramiwa prahasannidamabrawīt ||34||

akṛteyaṃ tawa prajñā brahmannātisamañjasī |
yadāttha māṃ twaṃ prasabhaṃ sakhā te'hamiti dwija ||35||

na hi rājñāmudīrṇānāmewambhūtairnaraiḥ kwacit |
sakhyaṃ bhawati mandātmañśriyā hīnairdhanacyutaiḥ ||36||

nāśrotriyaḥ śrotriyasya nārathī rathinaḥ sakhā |
nārājā pārthiwasyāpi sakhipūrwaṃ kimiṣyate ||37||

drupadenaiwamukto'haṃ manyunābhipariplutaḥ |
abhyāgacchaṃ kurūnbhīṣma śiṣyairarthī guṇānwitaiḥ ||38||

pratijagrāha taṃ bhīṣmo guruṃ pāṇḍusutaiḥ saha |
pautrānādāya tānsarwānwasūni wiwidhāni ca ||39||

śiṣyā iti dadau rājandroṇāya widhipūrwakam |
sa ca śiṣyānmaheṣwāsaḥ pratijagrāha kaurawān ||40||

pratigṛhya ca tānsarwāndroṇo wacanamabrawīt |
rahasyekaḥ pratītātmā kṛtopasadanāṃstadā ||41||

kāryaṃ me kāṅkṣitaṃ kiñciddhṛdi sampariwartate |
kṛtāstraistatpradeyaṃ me tadṛtaṃ wadatānaghāḥ ||42||

tacchrutwā kauraweyāste tūṣṇīmāsanwiśāṃ pate |
arjunastu tataḥ sarwaṃ pratijajñe parantapaḥ ||43||

tato'rjunaṃ mūrdhni tadā samāghrāya punaḥ punaḥ |
prītipūrwaṃ pariṣwajya praruroda mudā tadā ||44||

tato droṇaḥ pāṇḍuputrānastrāṇi wiwidhāni ca |
grāhayāmāsa diwyāni mānuṣāṇi ca wīryawān ||45||

rājaputrāstathaiwānye sametya bharatarṣabha |
abhijagmustato droṇamastrārthe dwijasattamam ||46||

wṛṣṇayaścāndhakāścaiwa nānādeśyāśca pārthiwāḥ ||46||

sūtaputraśca rādheyo guruṃ droṇamiyāttadā |
spardhamānastu pārthena sūtaputro'tyamarṣaṇaḥ ||47||

duryodhanamupāśritya pāṇḍawānatyamanyata ||47||






                  123


waiśampāyana uwāca||

arjunastu paraṃ yatnamātasthe gurupūjane |
astre ca paramaṃ yogaṃ priyo droṇasya cābhawat ||1||

droṇena tu tadāhūya rahasyukto'nnasādhakaḥ |
andhakāre'rjunāyānnaṃ na deyaṃ te kathañcana ||2||

tataḥ kadācidbhuñjāne prawawau wāyurarjune |
tena tatra pradīpaḥ sa dīpyamāno niwāpitaḥ ||3||

bhuṅkta ewārjuno bhaktaṃ na cāsyāsyādwyamuhyata |
hastastejaswino nityamannagrahaṇakāraṇāt ||4||

tadabhyāsakṛtaṃ matwā rātrāwabhyasta pāṇḍawaḥ ||4||

tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ droṇaḥ śuśrāwa bhārata |
upetya cainamutthāya pariṣwajyedamabrawīt ||5||

prayatiṣye tathā kartuṃ yathā nānyo dhanurdharaḥ |
twatsamo bhawitā loke satyametadbrawīmi te ||6||

tato droṇo'rjunaṃ bhūyo ratheṣu ca gajeṣu ca |
aśweṣu bhūmāwapi ca raṇaśikṣāmaśikṣayat ||7||

gadāyuddhe'sicaryāyāṃ tomaraprāsaśaktiṣu |
droṇaḥ saṅkīrṇayuddheṣu śikṣayāmāsa pāṇḍawam ||8||

tasya tatkauśalaṃ dṛṣṭwā dhanurwedajighṛkṣawaḥ |
rājāno rājaputrāśca samājagmuḥ sahasraśaḥ ||9||

tato niṣādarājasya hiraṇyadhanuṣaḥ sutaḥ |
ekalawyo mahārāja droṇamabhyājagāma ha ||10||

na sa taṃ pratijagrāha naiṣādiriti cintayan |
śiṣyaṃ dhanuṣi dharmajñasteṣāmewānwawekṣayā ||11||

sa tu droṇasya śirasā pādau gṛhya parantapaḥ |
araṇyamanusamprāptaḥ kṛtwā droṇaṃ mahīmayam ||12||

tasminnācāryawṛttiṃ ca paramāmāsthitastadā |
iṣwastre yogamātasthe paraṃ niyamamāsthitaḥ ||13||

parayā śraddhayā yukto yogena parameṇa ca |
wimokṣādānasandhāne laghutwaṃ paramāpa saḥ ||14||

atha droṇābhyanujñātāḥ kadācitkurupāṇḍawāḥ |
rathairwiniryayuḥ sarwe mṛgayāmarimardanāḥ ||15||

tatropakaraṇaṃ gṛhya naraḥ kaścidyadṛcchayā |
rājannanujagāmaikaḥ śwānamādāya pāṇḍawān ||16||

teṣāṃ wicaratāṃ tatra tattatkarma cikīrṣatām |
śwā caransa wane mūḍho naiṣādiṃ prati jagmiwān ||17||

sa kṛṣṇaṃ maladigdhāṅgaṃ kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ wane |
naiṣādiṃ śwā samālakṣya bhaṣaṃstasthau tadantike ||18||

tadā tasyātha bhaṣataḥ śunaḥ sapta śarānmukhe |
lāghawaṃ darśayannastre mumoca yugapadyathā ||19||

sa tu śwā śarapūrṇāsyaḥ pāṇḍawānājagāma ha |
taṃ dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍawā wīrā wismayaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ ||20||

lāghawaṃ śabdawedhitwaṃ dṛṣṭwā tatparamaṃ tadā |
prekṣya taṃ wrīḍitāścāsanpraśaśaṃsuśca sarwaśaḥ ||21||

taṃ tato'nweṣamāṇāste wane wananiwāsinam |
dadṛśuḥ pāṇḍawā rājannasyantamaniśaṃ śarān ||22||

na cainamabhyajānaṃste tadā wikṛtadarśanam |
athainaṃ paripapracchuḥ ko bhawānkasya wetyuta ||23||

ekalawya uwāca||

niṣādādhipaterwīrā hiraṇyadhanuṣaḥ sutam |
droṇaśiṣyaṃ ca māṃ witta dhanurwedakṛtaśramam ||24||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

te tamājñāya tattwena punarāgamya pāṇḍawāḥ |
yathāwṛttaṃ ca te sarwaṃ droṇāyācakhyuradbhutam ||25||

kaunteyastwarjuno rājannekalawyamanusmaran |
raho droṇaṃ samāgamya praṇayādidamabrawīt ||26||

nanwahaṃ parirabhyaikaḥ prītipūrwamidaṃ wacaḥ |
bhawatokto na me śiṣyastwadwiśiṣṭo bhawiṣyati ||27||

atha kasmānmadwiśiṣṭo lokādapi ca wīryawān |
astyanyo bhawataḥ śiṣyo niṣādādhipateḥ sutaḥ ||28||

muhūrtamiwa taṃ droṇaścintayitwā winiścayam |
sawyasācinamādāya naiṣādiṃ prati jagmiwān ||29||

dadarśa maladigdhāṅgaṃ jaṭilaṃ cīrawāsasam |
ekalawyaṃ dhanuṣpāṇimasyantamaniśaṃ śarān ||30||

ekalawyastu taṃ dṛṣṭwā droṇamāyāntamantikāt |
abhigamyopasaṅgṛhya jagāma śirasā mahīm ||31||

pūjayitwā tato droṇaṃ widhiwatsa niṣādajaḥ |
niwedya śiṣyamātmānaṃ tasthau prāñjaliragrataḥ ||32||

tato droṇo'brawīdrājannekalawyamidaṃ wacaḥ |
yadi śiṣyo'si me tūrṇaṃ wetanaṃ sampradīyatām ||33||

ekalawyastu tacchrutwā prīyamāṇo'brawīdidam |
kiṃ prayacchāmi bhagawannājñāpayatu māṃ guruḥ ||34||

na hi kiñcidadeyaṃ me gurawe brahmawittama |
tamabrawīttwayāṅguṣṭho dakṣiṇo dīyatāṃ mama ||35||

ekalawyastu tacchrutwā waco droṇasya dāruṇam |
pratijñāmātmano rakṣansatye ca nirataḥ sadā ||36||

tathaiwa hṛṣṭawadanastathaiwādīnamānasaḥ |
chittwāwicārya taṃ prādāddroṇāyāṅguṣṭhamātmanaḥ ||37||

tataḥ paraṃ tu naiṣādiraṅgulībhirwyakarṣata |
na tathā sa tu śīghro'bhūdyathā pūrwaṃ narādhipa ||38||

tato'rjunaḥ prītamanā babhūwa wigatajwaraḥ |
droṇaśca satyawāgāsīnnānyo'bhyabhawadarjunam ||39||

droṇasya tu tadā śiṣyau gadāyogyāṃ wiśeṣataḥ |
duryodhanaśca bhīmaśca kurūṇāmabhyagacchatām ||40||

aśwatthāmā rahasyeṣu sarweṣwabhyadhiko'bhawat |
tathāti puruṣānanyāntsārukau yamajāwubhau ||41||

yudhiṣṭhiro rathaśreṣṭhaḥ sarwatra tu dhanañjayaḥ ||41||

prathitaḥ sāgarāntāyāṃ rathayūthapayūthapaḥ |
buddhiyogabalotsāhaiḥ sarwāstreṣu ca pāṇḍawaḥ ||42||

astre gurwanurāge ca wiśiṣṭo'bhawadarjunaḥ |
tulyeṣwastropadeśeṣu sauṣṭhawena ca wīryawān ||43||

ekaḥ sarwakumārāṇāṃ babhūwātiratho'rjunaḥ ||43||

prāṇādhikaṃ bhīmasenaṃ kṛtawidyaṃ dhanañjayam |
dhārtarāṣṭrā durātmāno nāmṛṣyanta narādhipa ||44||

tāṃstu sarwānsamānīya sarwawidyāsu niṣṭhitān |
droṇaḥ praharaṇajñāne jijñāsuḥ puruṣarṣabha ||45||

kṛtrimaṃ bhāsamāropya wṛkṣāgre śilpibhiḥ kṛtam |
awijñātaṃ kumārāṇāṃ lakṣyabhūtamupādiśat ||46||

droṇa uwāca||

śīghraṃ bhawantaḥ sarwe wai dhanūṃṣyādāya satwarāḥ |
bhāsametaṃ samuddiśya tiṣṭhantāṃ saṃhiteṣawaḥ ||47||

madwākyasamakālaṃ ca śiro'sya winipātyatām |
ekaikaśo niyokṣyāmi tathā kuruta putrakāḥ ||48||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ pūrwamuwācāṅgirasāṃ waraḥ |
sandhatswa bāṇaṃ durdharṣa madwākyānte wimuñca ca ||49||

tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pūrwaṃ dhanurgṛhya mahārawam |
tasthau bhāsaṃ samuddiśya guruwākyapracoditaḥ ||50||

tato witatadhanwānaṃ droṇastaṃ kurunandanam |
sa muhūrtāduwācedaṃ wacanaṃ bharatarṣabha ||51||

paśyasyenaṃ drumāgrasthaṃ bhāsaṃ narawarātmaja |
paśyāmītyewamācāryaṃ pratyuwāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||52||

sa muhūrtādiwa punardroṇastaṃ pratyabhāṣata |
atha wṛkṣamimaṃ māṃ wā bhrātṛnwāpi prapaśyasi ||53||

tamuwāca sa kaunteyaḥ paśyāmyenaṃ wanaspatim |
bhawantaṃ ca tathā bhrātṛnbhāsaṃ ceti punaḥ punaḥ ||54||

tamuwācāpasarpeti droṇo'prītamanā iwa |
naitacchakyaṃ twayā weddhuṃ lakṣyamityewa kutsayan ||55||

tato duryodhanādīṃstāndhārtarāṣṭrānmahāyaśāḥ |
tenaiwa kramayogena jijñāsuḥ paryapṛcchata ||56||

anyāṃśca śiṣyānbhīmādīnrājñaścaiwānyadeśajān |
tathā ca sarwe sarwaṃ tatpaśyāma iti kutsitāḥ ||57||

tato dhanañjayaṃ droṇaḥ smayamāno'bhyabhāṣata |
