twayedānīṃ prahartawyametallakṣyaṃ niśamyatām ||58||

madwākyasamakālaṃ te moktawyo'tra bhaweccharaḥ |
witatya kārmukaṃ putra tiṣṭha tāwanmuhūrtakam ||59||

ewamuktaḥ sawyasācī maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ |
tasthau lakṣyaṃ samuddiśya guruwākyapracoditaḥ ||60||

muhūrtādiwa taṃ droṇastathaiwa samabhāṣata |
paśyasyenaṃ sthitaṃ bhāsaṃ drumaṃ māmapi wetyuta ||61||

paśyāmyenaṃ bhāsamiti droṇaṃ pārtho'bhyabhāṣata |
na tu wṛkṣaṃ bhawantaṃ wā paśyāmīti ca bhārata ||62||

tataḥ prītamanā droṇo muhūrtādiwa taṃ punaḥ |
pratyabhāṣata durdharṣaḥ pāṇḍawānāṃ ratharṣabham ||63||

bhāsaṃ paśyasi yadyenaṃ tathā brūhi punarwacaḥ |
śiraḥ paśyāmi bhāsasya na gātramiti so'brawīt ||64||

arjunenaiwamuktastu droṇo hṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ |
muñcaswetyabrawītpārthaṃ sa mumocāwicārayan ||65||

tatastasya nagasthasya kṣureṇa niśitena ha |
śira utkṛtya tarasā pātayāmāsa pāṇḍawaḥ ||66||

tasminkarmaṇi saṃsiddhe paryaśwajata phalgunam |
mene ca drupadaṃ saṅkhye sānubandhaṃ parājitam ||67||

kasyacittwatha kālasya saśiṣyo'ṅgirasāṃ waraḥ |
jagāma gaṅgāmabhito majjituṃ bharatarṣabha ||68||

awagāḍhamatho droṇaṃ salile salilecaraḥ |
grāho jagrāha balawāñjaṅghānte kālacoditaḥ ||69||

sa samartho'pi mokṣāya śiṣyānsarwānacodayat |
grāhaṃ hatwā mokṣayadhwaṃ māmiti twarayanniwa ||70||

tadwākyasamakālaṃ tu bībhatsurniśitaiḥ śaraiḥ |
āwāpaiḥ pañcabhirgrāhaṃ magnamambhasyatāḍayat ||71||

itare tu wisaṃmūḍhāstatra tatra prapedire ||71||

taṃ ca dṛṣṭwā kriyopetaṃ droṇo'manyata pāṇḍawam |
wiśiṣṭaṃ sarwaśiṣyebhyaḥ prītimāṃścābhawattadā ||72||

sa pārthabāṇairbahudhā khaṇḍaśaḥ parikalpitaḥ |
grāhaḥ pañcatwamāpede jaṅghāṃ tyaktwā mahātmanaḥ ||73||

athābrawīnmahātmānaṃ bhāradwājo mahāratham |
gṛhāṇedaṃ mahābāho wiśiṣṭamatidurdharam ||74||

astraṃ brahmaśiro nāma saprayoganiwartanam ||74||

na ca te mānuṣeṣwetatprayoktawyaṃ kathañcana |
jagadwinirdahedetadalpatejasi pātitam ||75||

asāmānyamidaṃ tāta lokeṣwastraṃ nigadyate |
taddhārayethāḥ prayataḥ śṛṇu cedaṃ waco mama ||76||

bādhetāmānuṣaḥ śatruryadā twāṃ wīra kaścana |
tadwadhāya prayuñjīthāstadāstramidamāhawe ||77||

tatheti tatpratiśrutya bībhatsuḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ |
jagrāha paramāstraṃ tadāha cainaṃ punarguruḥ ||78||

bhawitā twatsamo nānyaḥ pumāṃlloke dhanurdharaḥ ||78||






              jatugṛhadāhaparwa
                  124


waiśampāyana uwāca||

kṛtāstrāndhārtarāṣṭrāṃśca pāṇḍuputrāṃśca bhārata |
dṛṣṭwā droṇo'brawīdrājandhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśwaram ||1||

kṛpasya somadattasya bāhlīkasya ca dhīmataḥ |
gāṅgeyasya ca sāṃnidhye wyāsasya widurasya ca ||2||

rājansamprāptawidyāste kumarāḥ kurusattama |
te darśayeyuḥ swāṃ śikṣāṃ rājannanumate tawa ||3||

tato'brawīnmahārājaḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā |
bhāradwāja mahatkarma kṛtaṃ te dwijasattama ||4||

yadā tu manyase kālaṃ yasmindeśe yathā yathā |
tathā tathā widhānāya swayamājñāpayaswa mām ||5||

spṛhayāmyadya nirwedātpuruṣāṇāṃ sacakṣuṣām |
astrahetoḥ parākrāntānye me drakṣyanti putrakān ||6||

kṣattaryadgururācāryo brawīti kuru tattathā |
na hīdṛśaṃ priyaṃ manye bhawitā dharmawatsala ||7||

tato rājānamāmantrya widurānugato bahiḥ |
bhāradwājo mahāprājño māpayāmāsa medinīm ||8||

samāmawṛkṣāṃ nirgulmāmudakprawaṇasaṃsthitām ||8||

tasyāṃ bhūmau baliṃ cakre tithau nakṣatrapūjite |
awaghuṣṭaṃ pure cāpi tadarthaṃ wadatāṃ wara ||9||

raṅgabhūmau suwipulaṃ śāstradṛṣṭaṃ yathāwidhi |
prekṣāgāraṃ suwihitaṃ cakrustatra ca śilpinaḥ ||10||

rājñaḥ sarwāyudhopetaṃ strīṇāṃ caiwa nararṣabha ||10||

mañcāṃśca kārayāmāsustatra jānapadā janāḥ |
wipulānucchrayopetāñśibikāśca mahādhanāḥ ||11||

tasmiṃstato'hani prāpte rājā sasaciwastadā |
bhīṣmaṃ pramukhataḥ kṛtwā kṛpaṃ cācāryasattamam ||12||

muktājālaparikṣiptaṃ waiḍūryamaṇibhūṣitam |
śātakumbhamayaṃ diwyaṃ prekṣāgāramupāgamat ||13||

gāndhārī ca mahābhāgā kuntī ca jayatāṃ wara |
striyaśca sarwā yā rājñaḥ sapreṣyāḥ saparicchadāḥ ||14||

harṣādāruruhurmañcānmeruṃ dewastriyo yathā ||14||

brāhmaṇakṣatriyādyaṃ ca cāturwarṇyaṃ purāddrutam |
darśanepsu samabhyāgātkumārāṇāṃ kṛtāstratām ||15||

prawāditaiśca wāditrairjanakautūhalena ca |
mahārṇawa iwa kṣubdhaḥ samājaḥ so'bhawattadā ||16||

tataḥ śuklāmbaradharaḥ śuklayajñopawītawān |
śuklakeśaḥ sitaśmaśruḥ śuklamālyānulepanaḥ ||17||

raṅgamadhyaṃ tadācāryaḥ saputraḥ prawiweśa ha |
nabho jaladharairhīnaṃ sāṅgāraka iwāṃśumān ||18||

sa yathāsamayaṃ cakre baliṃ balawatāṃ waraḥ |
brāhmaṇāṃścātra mantrajñānwācayāmāsa maṅgalam ||19||

atha puṇyāhaghoṣasya puṇyasya tadanantaram |
wiwiśurwiwidhaṃ gṛhya śastropakaraṇaṃ narāḥ ||20||

tato baddhatanutrāṇā baddhakakṣyā mahābalāḥ |
baddhatūṇāḥ sadhanuṣo wiwiśurbharatarṣabhāḥ ||21||

anujyeṣṭhaṃ ca te tatra yudhiṣṭhirapurogamāḥ |
cakrurastraṃ mahāwīryāḥ kumārāḥ paramādbhutam ||22||

keciccharākṣepabhayācchirāṃsyawananāmire |
manujā dhṛṣṭamapare wīkṣāṃ cakruḥ sawismayāḥ ||23||

te sma lakṣyāṇi wiwidhurbāṇairnāmāṅkaśobhitaiḥ |
wiwidhairlāghawotsṛṣṭairuhyanto wājibhirdrutam ||24||

tatkumārabalaṃ tatra gṛhītaśarakārmukam |
gandharwanagarākāraṃ prekṣya te wismitābhawan ||25||

sahasā cukruśustatra narāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ |
wismayotphullanayanāḥ sādhu sādhwiti bhārata ||26||

kṛtwā dhanuṣi te mārgānrathacaryāsu cāsakṛt |
gajapṛṣṭhe'śwapṛṣṭhe ca niyuddhe ca mahābalāḥ ||27||

gṛhītakhaḍgacarmāṇastato bhūyaḥ prahāriṇaḥ |
tsarumārgānyathoddiṣṭāṃśceruḥ sarwāsu bhūmiṣu ||28||

lāghawaṃ sauṣṭhawaṃ śobhāṃ sthiratwaṃ dṛḍhamuṣṭitām |
dadṛśustatra sarweṣāṃ prayoge khaḍgacarmaṇām ||29||

atha tau nityasaṃhṛṣṭau suyodhanawṛkodarau |
awatīrṇau gadāhastāwekaśṛṅgāwiwācalau ||30||

baddhakakṣyau mahābāhū pauruṣe paryawasthitau |
bṛṃhantau wāśitāhetoḥ samadāwiwa kuñjarau ||31||

tau pradakṣiṇasawyāni maṇḍalāni mahābalau |
ceraturnirmalagadau samadāwiwa gowṛṣau ||32||

widuro dhṛtarāṣṭrāya gāndhāryai pāṇḍawāraṇiḥ |
nyawedayetāṃ tatsarwaṃ kumārāṇāṃ wiceṣṭitam ||33||






                  125


waiśampāyana uwāca||

kururāje ca raṅgasthe bhīme ca balināṃ ware |
pakṣapātakṛtasnehaḥ sa dwidhewābhawajjanaḥ ||1||

hā wīra kururājeti hā bhīmeti ca nardatām |
puruṣāṇāṃ suwipulāḥ praṇādāḥ sahasotthitāḥ ||2||

tataḥ kṣubdhārṇawanibhaṃ raṅgamālokya buddhimān |
bhāradwājaḥ priyaṃ putramaśwatthāmānamabrawīt ||3||

wārayaitau mahāwīryau kṛtayogyāwubhāwapi |
mā bhūdraṅgaprakopo'yaṃ bhīmaduryodhanodbhawaḥ ||4||

tatastāwudyatagadau guruputreṇa wāritau |
yugāntānilasaṅkṣubdhau mahāwegāwiwārṇawau ||5||

tato raṅgāṅgaṇagato droṇo wacanamabrawīt |
niwārya wāditragaṇaṃ mahāmeghanibhaswanam ||6||

yo me putrātpriyataraḥ sarwāstrawiduṣāṃ waraḥ |
aindririndrānujasamaḥ sa pārtho dṛśyatāmiti ||7||

ācāryawacanenātha kṛtaswastyayano yuwā |
baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṇaḥ pūrṇatūṇaḥ sakārmukaḥ ||8||

kāñcanaṃ kawacaṃ bibhratpratyadṛśyata phalgunaḥ |
sārkaḥ sendrāyudhataḍitsasandhya iwa toyadaḥ ||9||

tataḥ sarwasya raṅgasya samutpiñjo'bhawanmahān |
prāwādyanta ca wādyāni saśaṅkhāni samantataḥ ||10||

eṣa kuntīsutaḥ śrīmāneṣa pāṇḍawamadhyamaḥ |
eṣa putro mahendrasya kurūṇāmeṣa rakṣitā ||11||

eṣo'strawiduṣāṃ śreṣṭha eṣa dharmabhṛtāṃ waraḥ |
eṣa śīlawatāṃ cāpi śīlajñānanidhiḥ paraḥ ||12||

ityewamatulā wācaḥ śṛṇwantyāḥ prekṣakeritāḥ |
kuntyāḥ prasnawasaṃmiśrairasraiḥ klinnamuro'bhawat ||13||

tena śabdena mahatā pūrṇaśrutirathābrawīt |
dhṛtarāṣṭro naraśreṣṭho widuraṃ hṛṣṭamānasaḥ ||14||

kṣattaḥ kṣubdhārṇawanibhaḥ kimeṣa sumahāswanaḥ |
sahasaiwotthito raṅge bhindanniwa nabhastalam ||15||

widura uwāca||

eṣa pārtho mahārāja phalgunaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ |
awatīrṇaḥ sakawacastatraiṣa sumahāswanaḥ ||16||

dhṛtarāṣṭra uwāca||

dhanyo'smyanugṛhīto'smi rakṣito'smi mahāmate |
pṛthāraṇisamudbhūtaistribhiḥ pāṇḍawawahnibhiḥ ||17||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tasminsamudite raṅge kathañcitparyawasthite |
darśayāmāsa bībhatsurācāryādastralāghawam ||18||

āgneyenāsṛjadwahniṃ wāruṇenāsṛjatpayaḥ |
wāyawyenāsṛjadwāyuṃ pārjanyenāsṛjadghanān ||19||

bhaumena prāwiśadbhūmiṃ pārwatenāsṛjadgirīn |
antardhānena cāstreṇa punarantarhito'bhawat ||20||

kṣaṇātprāṃśuḥ kṣaṇāddhraswaḥ kṣaṇācca rathadhūrgataḥ |
kṣaṇena rathamadhyasthaḥ kṣaṇenāwāpatanmahīm ||21||

sukumāraṃ ca sūkṣmaṃ ca guruṃ cāpi gurupriyaḥ |
sauṣṭhawenābhisaṃyuktaḥ so'widhyadwiwidhaiḥ śaraiḥ ||22||

bhramataśca warāhasya lohasya pramukhe samam |
pañca bāṇānasaṃsaktānsa mumocaikabāṇawat ||23||

gawye wiṣāṇakośe ca cale rajjwawalambite |
nicakhāna mahāwīryaḥ sāyakānekawiṃśatim ||24||

ityewamādi sumahatkhaḍge dhanuṣi cābhawat |
gadāyāṃ śastrakuśalo darśanāni wyadarśayat ||25||

tataḥ samāptabhūyiṣṭhe tasminkarmaṇi bhārata |
mandībhūte samāje ca wāditrasya ca niswane ||26||

dwāradeśātsamudbhūto māhātmya balasūcakaḥ |
wajraniṣpeṣasadṛśaḥ śuśruwe bhujaniswanaḥ ||27||

dīryante kiṃ nu girayaḥ kiṃ swidbhūmirwidīryate |
kiṃ swidāpūryate wyoma jalabhāraghanairghanaiḥ ||28||

raṅgasyaiwaṃ matirabhūtkṣaṇena wasudhādhipa |
dwāraṃ cābhimukhāḥ sarwe babhūwuḥ prekṣakāstadā ||29||

pañcabhirbhrātṛbhiḥ pārthairdroṇaḥ pariwṛto babhau |
pañcatāreṇa saṃyuktaḥ sāwitreṇewa candramāḥ ||30||

aśwatthāmnā ca sahitaṃ bhrātṛṇāṃ śatamūrjitam |
duryodhanamamitraghnamutthitaṃ paryawārayat ||31||

sa taistadā bhrātṛbhirudyatāyudhai; rwṛto gadāpāṇirawasthitaiḥ sthitaḥ |
babhau yathā dānawasaṅkṣaye purā; puraṃdaro dewagaṇaiḥ samāwṛtaḥ ||32||






                  126


waiśampāyana uwāca||

datte'wakāśe puruṣairwismayotphullalocanaiḥ |
wiweśa raṅgaṃ wistīrṇaṃ karṇaḥ parapurañjayaḥ ||1||

sahajaṃ kawacaṃ bibhratkuṇḍaloddyotitānanaḥ |
sadhanurbaddhanistriṃśaḥ pādacārīwa parwataḥ ||2||

kanyāgarbhaḥ pṛthuyaśāḥ pṛthāyāḥ pṛthulocanaḥ |
tīkṣṇāṃśorbhāskarasyāṃśaḥ karṇo'rigaṇasūdanaḥ ||3||

siṃharṣabhagajendrāṇāṃ tulyawīryaparākramaḥ |
dīptikāntidyutiguṇaiḥ sūryendujwalanopamaḥ ||4||

prāṃśuḥ kanakatālābhaḥ siṃhasaṃhanano yuwā |
asaṅkhyeyaguṇaḥ śrīmānbhāskarasyātmasambhawaḥ ||5||

sa nirīkṣya mahābāhuḥ sarwato raṅgamaṇḍalam |
praṇāmaṃ droṇakṛpayornātyādṛtamiwākarot ||6||

sa sāmājajanaḥ sarwo niścalaḥ sthiralocanaḥ |
ko'yamityāgatakṣobhaḥ kautūhalaparo'bhawat ||7||

so'brawīnmeghadhīreṇa swareṇa wadatāṃ waraḥ |
bhrātā bhrātaramajñātaṃ sāwitraḥ pākaśāsanim ||8||

pārtha yatte kṛtaṃ karma wiśeṣawadahaṃ tataḥ |
kariṣye paśyatāṃ nṛṇāṃ mātmanā wismayaṃ gamaḥ ||9||

asamāpte tatastasya wacane wadatāṃ wara |
yantrotkṣipta iwa kṣipramuttasthau sarwato janaḥ ||10||

prītiśca puruṣawyāghra duryodhanamathāspṛśat |
hrīśca krodhaśca bībhatsuṃ kṣaṇenānwawiśacca ha ||11||

tato droṇābhyanujñātaḥ karṇaḥ priyaraṇaḥ sadā |
yatkṛtaṃ tatra pārthena taccakāra mahābalaḥ ||12||

atha duryodhanastatra bhrātṛbhiḥ saha bhārata |
karṇaṃ pariṣwajya mudā tato wacanamabrawīt ||13||

swāgataṃ te mahābāho diṣṭyā prāpto'si mānada |
ahaṃ ca kururājyaṃ ca yatheṣṭamupabhujyatām ||14||

karṇa uwāca||

kṛtaṃ sarweṇa me'nyena sakhitwaṃ ca twayā wṛṇe |
dwandwayuddhaṃ ca pārthena kartumicchāmi bhārata ||15||

duryodhana uwāca||

bhuṅkṣwa bhogānmayā sārdhaṃ bandhūnāṃ priyakṛdbhawa |
durhṛdāṃ kuru sarweṣāṃ mūrdhni pādamariṃdama ||16||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ kṣiptamiwātmānaṃ matwā pārtho'bhyabhāṣata |
karṇaṃ bhrātṛsamūhasya madhye'calamiwa sthitam ||17||

anāhūtopasṛptānāmanāhūtopajalpinām |
ye lokāstānhataḥ karṇa mayā twaṃ pratipatsyase ||18||

karṇa uwāca||

raṅgo'yaṃ sarwasāmānyaḥ kimatra tawa phalguna |
wīryaśreṣṭhāśca rājanyā balaṃ dharmo'nuwartate ||19||

kiṃ kṣepairdurbalāśwāsaiḥ śaraiḥ kathaya bhārata |
guroḥ samakṣaṃ yāwatte harāmyadya śiraḥ śaraiḥ ||20||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato droṇābhyanujñātaḥ pārthaḥ parapurañjayaḥ |
bhrātṛbhistwarayāśliṣṭo raṇāyopajagāma tam ||21||

tato duryodhanenāpi sabhrātrā samarodyataḥ |
pariṣwaktaḥ sthitaḥ karṇaḥ pragṛhya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ ||22||

tataḥ sawidyutstanitaiḥ sendrāyudhapurojawaiḥ |
āwṛtaṃ gaganaṃ meghairbalākāpaṅktihāsibhiḥ ||23||

tataḥ snehāddharihayaṃ dṛṣṭwā raṅgāwalokinam |
bhāskaro'pyanayannāśaṃ samīpopagatānghanān ||24||

meghacchāyopagūḍhastu tato'dṛśyata pāṇḍawaḥ |
sūryātapaparikṣiptaḥ karṇo'pi samadṛśyata ||25||

dhārtarāṣṭrā yataḥ karṇastasmindeśe wyawasthitāḥ |
bhāradwājaḥ kṛpo bhīṣmo yataḥ pārthastato'bhawan ||26||

dwidhā raṅgaḥ samabhawatstrīṇāṃ dwaidhamajāyata |
kuntibhojasutā mohaṃ wijñātārthā jagāma ha ||27||

tāṃ tathā mohasampannāṃ widuraḥ sarwadharmawit |
kuntīmāśwāsayāmāsa prokṣyādbhiścandanokṣitaiḥ ||28||

tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇā tāwubhāwapi daṃśitau |
putrau dṛṣṭwā susantaptā nānwapadyata kiñcana ||29||

tāwudyatamahācāpau kṛpaḥ śāradwato'brawīt |
dwandwayuddhasamācāre kuśalaḥ sarwadharmawit ||30||

ayaṃ pṛthāyāstanayaḥ kanīyānpāṇḍunandanaḥ |
kaurawo bhawatā sārdhaṃ dwandwayuddhaṃ kariṣyati ||31||

twamapyewaṃ mahābāho mātaraṃ pitaraṃ kulam |
kathayaswa narendrāṇāṃ yeṣāṃ twaṃ kulawardhanaḥ ||32||

tato widitwā pārthastwāṃ pratiyotsyati wā na wā ||32||

ewamuktasya karṇasya wrīḍāwanatamānanam |
babhau warṣāmbubhiḥ klinnaṃ padmamāgalitaṃ yathā ||33||

duryodhana uwāca||

ācārya triwidhā yonī rājñāṃ śāstrawiniścaye |
tatkulīnaśca śūraśca senāṃ yaśca prakarṣati ||34||

yadyayaṃ phalguno yuddhe nārājñā yoddhumicchati |
tasmādeṣo'ṅgawiṣaye mayā rājye'bhiṣicyate ||35||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tatastasminkṣaṇe karṇaḥ salājakusumairghaṭaiḥ |
kāñcanaiḥ kāñcane pīṭhe mantrawidbhirmahārathaḥ ||36||

abhiṣikto'ṅgarājye sa śriyā yukto mahābalaḥ ||36||

sacchatrawālawyajano jayaśabdāntareṇa ca |
uwāca kaurawaṃ rājā rājānaṃ taṃ wṛṣastadā ||37||

asya rājyapradānasya sadṛśaṃ kiṃ dadāni te |
prabrūhi rājaśārdūla kartā hyasmi tathā nṛpa ||38||

atyantaṃ sakhyamicchāmītyāha taṃ sa suyodhanaḥ ||38||

ewamuktastataḥ karṇastatheti pratyabhāṣata |
harṣāccobhau samāśliṣya parāṃ mudamawāpatuḥ ||39||






                  127


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ srastottarapaṭaḥ sapraswedaḥ sawepathuḥ |
wiweśādhiratho raṅgaṃ yaṣṭiprāṇo hwayanniwa ||1||

tamālokya dhanustyaktwā pitṛgaurawayantritaḥ |
karṇo'bhiṣekārdraśirāḥ śirasā samawandata ||2||

tataḥ pādāwawacchādya paṭāntena sasambhramaḥ |
putreti paripūrṇārthamabrawīdrathasārathiḥ ||3||

pariṣwajya ca tasyātha mūrdhānaṃ snehawiklawaḥ |
aṅgarājyābhiṣekārdramaśrubhiḥ siṣice punaḥ ||4||

taṃ dṛṣṭwā sūtaputro'yamiti niścitya pāṇḍawaḥ |
bhīmasenastadā wākyamabrawītprahasanniwa ||5||

na twamarhasi pārthena sūtaputra raṇe wadham |
kulasya sadṛśastūrṇaṃ pratodo gṛhyatāṃ twayā ||6||

aṅgarājyaṃ ca nārhastwamupabhoktuṃ narādhama |
śwā hutāśasamīpasthaṃ puroḍāśamiwādhware ||7||

ewamuktastataḥ karṇaḥ kiñcitprasphuritādharaḥ |
gaganasthaṃ winiḥśwasya diwākaramudaikṣata ||8||

tato duryodhanaḥ kopādutpapāta mahābalaḥ |
bhrātṛpadmawanāttasmānmadotkaṭa iwa dwipaḥ ||9||

so'brawīdbhīmakarmāṇaṃ bhīmasenamawasthitam |
wṛkodara na yuktaṃ te wacanaṃ waktumīdṛśam ||10||

kṣatriyāṇāṃ balaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ yoddhawyaṃ kṣatrabandhunā |
śūrāṇāṃ ca nadīnāṃ ca prabhawā durwidāḥ kila ||11||

salilādutthito wahniryena wyāptaṃ carācaram |
dadhīcasyāsthito wajraṃ kṛtaṃ dānawasūdanam ||12||

āgneyaḥ kṛttikāputro raudro gāṅgeya ityapi |
śrūyate bhagawāndewaḥ sarwaguhyamayo guhaḥ ||13||

kṣatriyābhyaśca ye jātā brāhmaṇāste ca wiśrutāḥ |
ācāryaḥ kalaśājjātaḥ śarastambādguruḥ kṛpaḥ ||14||

bhawatāṃ ca yathā janma tadapyāgamitaṃ nṛpaiḥ ||14||

sakuṇḍalaṃ sakawacaṃ diwyalakṣaṇalakṣitam |
kathamādityasaṅkāśaṃ mṛgī wyāghraṃ janiṣyati ||15||

pṛthiwīrājyamarho'yaṃ nāṅgarājyaṃ nareśwaraḥ |
anena bāhuwīryeṇa mayā cājñānuwartinā ||16||

yasya wā manujasyedaṃ na kṣāntaṃ madwiceṣṭitam |
rathamāruhya padbhyāṃ wā wināmayatu kārmukam ||17||

tataḥ sarwasya raṅgasya hāhākāro mahānabhūt |
sādhuwādānusambaddhaḥ sūryaścāstamupāgamat ||18||

tato duryodhanaḥ karṇamālambyātha kare nṛpa |
dīpikāgnikṛtālokastasmādraṅgādwiniryayau ||19||

pāṇḍawāśca sahadroṇāḥ sakṛpāśca wiśāṃ pate |
bhīṣmeṇa sahitāḥ sarwe yayuḥ swaṃ swaṃ niweśanam ||20||

arjuneti janaḥ kaścitkaścitkarṇeti bhārata |
kaścidduryodhanetyewaṃ bruwantaḥ prasthitāstadā ||21||

kuntyāśca pratyabhijñāya diwyalakṣaṇasūcitam |
putramaṅgeśwaraṃ snehācchannā prītirawardhata ||22||

duryodhanasyāpi tadā karṇamāsādya pārthiwa |
bhayamarjunasāñjātaṃ kṣipramantaradhīyata ||23||

sa cāpi wīraḥ kṛtaśastraniśramaḥ; pareṇa sāmnābhyawadatsuyodhanam |
yudhiṣṭhirasyāpyabhawattadā mati; rna karṇatulyo'sti dhanurdharaḥ kṣitau ||24||






                  128


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ śiṣyānsamānīya ācāryārthamacodayat |
droṇaḥ sarwānaśeṣeṇa dakṣiṇārthaṃ mahīpate ||1||

pāñcālarājaṃ drupadaṃ gṛhītwā raṇamūrdhani |
paryānayata bhadraṃ waḥ sā syātparamadakṣiṇā ||2||

tathetyuktwā tu te sarwe rathaistūrṇaṃ prahāriṇaḥ |
ācāryadhanadānārthaṃ droṇena sahitā yayuḥ ||3||

tato'bhijagmuḥ pāñcālānnighnantaste nararṣabhāḥ |
mamṛdustasya nagaraṃ drupadasya mahaujasaḥ ||4||

te yajñasenaṃ drupadaṃ gṛhītwā raṇamūrdhani |
upājahruḥ sahāmātyaṃ droṇāya bharatarṣabhāḥ ||5||

bhagnadarpaṃ hṛtadhanaṃ tathā ca waśamāgatam |
sa wairaṃ manasā dhyātwā droṇo drupadamabrawīt ||6||

pramṛdya tarasā rāṣṭraṃ puraṃ te mṛditaṃ mayā |
prāpya jīwanripuwaśaṃ sakhipūrwaṃ kimiṣyate ||7||

ewamuktwā prahasyainaṃ niścitya punarabrawīt |
mā bhaiḥ prāṇabhayādrājankṣamiṇo brāhmaṇā wayam ||8||

āśrame krīḍitaṃ yattu twayā bālye mayā saha |
tena saṃwardhitaḥ snehastwayā me kṣatriyarṣabha ||9||

prārthayeyaṃ twayā sakhyaṃ punarewa nararṣabha |
waraṃ dadāmi te rājanrājyasyārdhamawāpnuhi ||10||

arājā kila no rājñāṃ sakhā bhawitumarhati |
ataḥ prayatitaṃ rājye yajñasena mayā tawa ||11||

rājāsi dakṣiṇe kūle bhāgīrathyāhamuttare |
sakhāyaṃ māṃ wijānīhi pāñcāla yadi manyase ||12||

drupada uwāca||

anāścaryamidaṃ brahmanwikrānteṣu mahātmasu |
prīye twayāhaṃ twattaśca prītimicchāmi śāśwatīm ||13||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastu taṃ droṇo mokṣayāmāsa bhārata |
satkṛtya cainaṃ prītātmā rājyārdhaṃ pratyapādayat ||14||

mākandīmatha gaṅgāyāstīre janapadāyutām |
so'dhyāwasaddīnamanāḥ kāmpilyaṃ ca purottamam ||15||

dakṣiṇāṃścaiwa pāñcālānyāwaccarmaṇwatī nadī ||15||

droṇena wairaṃ drupadaḥ saṃsmaranna śaśāma ha |
kṣātreṇa ca balenāsya nāpaśyatsa parājayam ||16||

hīnaṃ widitwā cātmānaṃ brāhmaṇena balena ca |
putrajanma parīpsanwai sa rājā tadadhārayat ||17||

ahicchatraṃ ca wiṣayaṃ droṇaḥ samabhipadyata ||17||

ewaṃ rājannahicchatrā purī janapadāyutā |
yudhi nirjitya pārthena droṇāya pratipāditā ||18||






                  129


waiśampāyana uwāca||

prāṇādhikaṃ bhīmasenaṃ kṛtawidyaṃ dhanañjayam |
duryodhano lakṣayitwa paryatapyata durmatiḥ ||1||

tato waikartanaḥ karṇaḥ śakuniścāpi saubalaḥ |
anekairabhyupāyaistāñjighāṃsanti sma pāṇḍawān ||2||

pāṇḍawāścāpi tatsarwaṃ pratyajānannariṃdamāḥ |
udbhāwanamakurwanto widurasya mate sthitāḥ ||3||

guṇaiḥ samuditāndṛṣṭwā paurāḥ pāṇḍusutāṃstadā |
kathayanti sma sambhūya catwareṣu sabhāsu ca ||4||

prajñācakṣuracakṣuṣṭwāddhṛtarāṣṭro janeśwaraḥ |
rājyamaprāptawānpūrwaṃ sa kathaṃ nṛpatirbhawet ||5||

tathā bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawaḥ satyasandho mahāwrataḥ |
pratyākhyāya purā rājyaṃ nādya jātu grahīṣyati ||6||

te wayaṃ pāṇḍawaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ taruṇaṃ wṛddhaśīlinam |
abhiṣiñcāma sādhwadya satyaṃ karuṇawedinam ||7||

sa hi bhīṣmaṃ śāntanawaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca dharmawit |
saputraṃ wiwidhairbhogairyojayiṣyati pūjayan ||8||

teṣāṃ duryodhanaḥ śrutwā tāni wākyāni bhāṣatām |
yudhiṣṭhirānuraktānāṃ paryatapyata durmatiḥ ||9||

sa tapyamāno duṣṭātmā teṣāṃ wāco na cakṣame |
īrṣyayā cābhisantapto dhṛtarāṣṭramupāgamat ||10||

tato wirahitaṃ dṛṣṭwā pitaraṃ pratipūjya saḥ |
paurānurāgasantaptaḥ paścādidamabhāṣata ||11||

śrutā me jalpatāṃ tāta paurāṇāmaśiwā giraḥ |
twāmanādṛtya bhīṣmaṃ ca patimicchanti pāṇḍawam ||12||

matametacca bhīṣmasya na sa rājyaṃ bubhūṣati |
asmākaṃ tu parāṃ pīḍāṃ cikīrṣanti pure janāḥ ||13||

pitṛtaḥ prāptawānrājyaṃ pāṇḍurātmaguṇaiḥ purā |
twamapyaguṇasaṃyogātprāptaṃ rājyaṃ na labdhawān ||14||

sa eṣa pāṇḍordāyādyaṃ yadi prāpnoti pāṇḍawaḥ |
tasya putro dhruwaṃ prāptastasya tasyeti cāparaḥ ||15||

te wayaṃ rājawaṃśena hīnāḥ saha sutairapi |
awajñātā bhawiṣyāmo lokasya jagatīpate ||16||

satataṃ nirayaṃ prāptāḥ parapiṇḍopajīwinaḥ |
na bhawema yathā rājaṃstathā śīghraṃ widhīyatām ||17||

abhawiṣyaḥ sthiro rājye yadi hi twaṃ purā nṛpa |
dhruwaṃ prāpsyāma ca wayaṃ rājyamapyawaśe jane ||18||






                  130


waiśampāyana uwāca||

dhṛtarāṣṭrastu putrasya śrutwā wacanamīdṛśam |
muhūrtamiwa sañcintya duryodhanamathābrawīt ||1||

dharmanityaḥ sadā pāṇḍurmamāsītpriyakṛddhitaḥ |
sarweṣu jñātiṣu tathā mayi twāsīdwiśeṣataḥ ||2||

nāsya kiñcinna jānāmi bhojanādi cikīrṣitam |
niwedayati nityaṃ hi mama rājyaṃ dhṛtawrataḥ ||3||

tasya putro yathā pāṇḍustathā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ |
guṇawāṃllokawikhyātaḥ paurāṇāṃ ca susaṃmataḥ ||4||

sa kathaṃ śakyamasmābhirapakraṣṭuṃ balāditaḥ |
pitṛpaitāmahādrājyātsasahāyo wiśeṣataḥ ||5||

bhṛtā hi pāṇḍunāmātyā balaṃ ca satataṃ bhṛtam |
bhṛtāḥ putrāśca pautrāśca teṣāmapi wiśeṣataḥ ||6||

te purā satkṛtāstāta pāṇḍunā paurawā janāḥ |
kathaṃ yudhiṣṭhirasyārthe na no hanyuḥ sabāndhawān ||7||

duryodhana uwāca||

ewametanmayā tāta bhāwitaṃ doṣamātmani |
dṛṣṭwā prakṛtayaḥ sarwā arthamānena yojitāḥ ||8||

dhruwamasmatsahāyāste bhawiṣyanti pradhānataḥ |
arthawargaḥ sahāmātyo matsaṃstho'dya mahīpate ||9||

sa bhawānpāṇḍawānāśu wiwāsayitumarhati |
mṛdunaiwābhyupāyena nagaraṃ wāraṇāwatam ||10||

yadā pratiṣṭhitaṃ rājyaṃ mayi rājanbhawiṣyati |
tadā kuntī sahāpatyā punareṣyati bhārata ||11||

dhṛtarāṣṭra uwāca||

duryodhana mamāpyetaddhṛdi sampariwartate |
abhiprāyasya pāpatwānnaitattu wiwṛṇomyaham ||12||

na ca bhīṣmo na ca droṇo na kṣattā na ca gautamaḥ |
wiwāsyamānānkaunteyānanumaṃsyanti karhicit ||13||

samā hi kauraweyāṇāṃ wayamete ca putraka |
naite wiṣamamiccheyurdharmayuktā manaswinaḥ ||14||

te wayaṃ kauraweyāṇāmeteṣāṃ ca mahātmanām |
kathaṃ na wadhyatāṃ tāta gacchema jagatastathā ||15||

duryodhana uwāca||

madhyasthaḥ satataṃ bhīṣmo droṇaputro mayi sthitaḥ |
yataḥ putrastato droṇo bhawitā nātra sāṃśayaḥ ||16||

kṛpaḥ śāradwataścaiwa yata ete trayastataḥ |
droṇaṃ ca bhāgineyaṃ ca na sa tyakṣyati karhicit ||17||

kṣattārthabaddhastwasmākaṃ pracchannaṃ tu yataḥ pare |
na caikaḥ sa samartho'smānpāṇḍawārthe prabādhitum ||18||

sa wiśrabdhaḥ pāṇḍuputrānsaha mātrā wiwāsaya |
wāraṇāwatamadyaiwa nātra doṣo bhawiṣyati ||19||

winidrakaraṇaṃ ghoraṃ hṛdi śalyamiwārpitam |
śokapāwakamudbhūtaṃ karmaṇaitena nāśaya ||20||






                  131


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato duryodhano rājā sarwāstāḥ prakṛtīḥ śanaiḥ |
arthamānapradānābhyāṃ sañjahāra sahānujaḥ ||1||

dhṛtarāṣṭraprayuktāstu kecitkuśalamantriṇaḥ |
kathayāṃ cakrire ramyaṃ nagaraṃ wāraṇāwatam ||2||

ayaṃ samājaḥ sumahānramaṇīyatamo bhuwi |
upasthitaḥ paśupaternagare wāraṇāwate ||3||

sarwaratnasamākīrṇe puṃsāṃ deśe manorame |
ityewaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya wacanāccakrire kathāḥ ||4||

kathyamāne tathā ramye nagare wāraṇāwate |
gamane pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ jajñe tatra matirnṛpa ||5||

yadā twamanyata nṛpo jātakautūhalā iti |
uwācainānatha tadā pāṇḍawānambikāsutaḥ ||6||

mameme puruṣā nityaṃ kathayanti punaḥ punaḥ |
ramaṇīyataraṃ loke nagaraṃ wāraṇāwatam ||7||

te tāta yadi manyadhwamutsawaṃ wāraṇāwate |
sagaṇāḥ sānuyātrāśca wiharadhwaṃ yathāmarāḥ ||8||

brāhmaṇebhyaśca ratnāni gāyanebhyaśca sarwaśaḥ |
prayacchadhwaṃ yathākāmaṃ dewā iwa suwarcasaḥ ||9||

kañcitkālaṃ wihṛtyaiwamanubhūya parāṃ mudam |
idaṃ wai hāstinapuraṃ sukhinaḥ punareṣyatha ||10||

dhṛtarāṣṭrasya taṃ kāmamanubuddhwā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
ātmanaścāsahāyatwaṃ tatheti pratyuwāca tam ||11||

tato bhīṣmaṃ mahāprājñaṃ widuraṃ ca mahāmatim |
droṇaṃ ca bāhlikaṃ caiwa somadattaṃ ca kaurawam ||12||

kṛpamācāryaputraṃ ca gāndhārīṃ ca yaśaswinīm |
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śanairdīnamuwācedaṃ wacastadā ||13||

ramaṇīye janākīrṇe nagare wāraṇāwate |
sagaṇāstāta watsyāmo dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt ||14||

prasannamanasaḥ sarwe puṇyā wāco wimuñcata |
āśīrbhirwardhitānasmānna pāpaṃ prasahiṣyati ||15||

ewamuktāstu te sarwe pāṇḍuputreṇa kaurawāḥ |
prasannawadanā bhūtwā te'bhyawartanta pāṇḍawān ||16||

swastyastu waḥ pathi sadā bhūtebhyaścaiwa sarwaśaḥ |
mā ca wo'stwaśubhaṃ kiñcitsarwataḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ ||17||

tataḥ kṛtaswastyayanā rājyalābhāya pāṇḍawāḥ |
kṛtwā sarwāṇi kāryāṇi prayayurwāraṇāwatam ||18||






                  132


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamukteṣu rājñā tu pāṇḍaweṣu mahātmasu |
duryodhanaḥ paraṃ harṣamājagāma durātmawān ||1||

sa purocanamekāntamānīya bharatarṣabha |
gṛhītwā dakṣiṇe pāṇau saciwaṃ wākyamabrawīt ||2||

mameyaṃ wasusampūrṇā purocana wasundharā |
yatheyaṃ mama tadwatte sa tāṃ rakṣitumarhasi ||3||

na hi me kaścidanyo'sti waiśwāsikatarastwayā |
sahāyo yena sandhāya mantrayeyaṃ yathā twayā ||4||

saṃrakṣa tāta mantraṃ ca sapatnāṃśca mamoddhara |
nipuṇenābhyupāyena yadbrawīmi tathā kuru ||5||

pāṇḍawā dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa preṣitā wāraṇāwatam |
utsawe wihariṣyanti dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt ||6||

sa twaṃ rāsabhayuktena syandanenāśugāminā |
wāraṇāwatamadyaiwa yathā yāsi tathā kuru ||7||

tatra gatwā catuḥśālaṃ gṛhaṃ paramasaṃwṛtam |
āyudhāgāramāśritya kārayethā mahādhanam ||8||

śaṇasarjarasādīni yāni drawyāṇi kānicit |
āgneyānyuta santīha tāni sarwāṇi dāpaya ||9||

sarpiṣā ca satailena lākṣayā cāpyanalpayā |
mṛttikāṃ miśrayitwā twaṃ lepaṃ kuḍyeṣu dāpayeḥ ||10||

śaṇānwaṃśaṃ ghṛtaṃ dāru yantrāṇi wiwidhāni ca |
tasminweśmani sarwāṇi nikṣipethāḥ samantataḥ ||11||

yathā ca twāṃ na śaṅkeranparīkṣanto'pi pāṇḍawāḥ |
āgneyamiti tatkāryamiti cānye ca mānawāḥ ||12||

weśmanyewaṃ kṛte tatra kṛtwā tānparamārcitān |
wāsayeḥ pāṇḍaweyāṃśca kuntīṃ ca sasuhṛjjanām ||13||

tatrāsanāni mukhyāni yānāni śayanāni ca |
widhātawyāni pāṇḍūnāṃ yathā tuṣyeta me pitā ||14||

yathā rameranwiśrabdhā nagare wāraṇāwate |
tathā sarwaṃ widhātawyaṃ yāwatkālasya paryayaḥ ||15||

jñātwā tu tānsuwiśwastāñśayānānakutobhayān |
agnistatastwayā deyo dwāratastasya weśmanaḥ ||16||

dagdhānewaṃ swake gehe dagdhā iti tato janāḥ |
jñātayo wā wadiṣyanti pāṇḍawārthāya karhicit ||17||

tattatheti pratijñāya kaurawāya purocanaḥ |
prāyādrāsabhayuktena nagaraṃ wāraṇāwatam ||18||

sa gatwā twarito rājanduryodhanamate sthitaḥ |
yathoktaṃ rājaputreṇa sarwaṃ cakre purocanaḥ ||19||






                  133


waiśampāyana uwāca||

pāṇḍawāstu rathānyuktwā sadaśwairanilopamaiḥ |
ārohamāṇā bhīṣmasya pādau jagṛhurārtawat ||1||

rājñaśca dhṛtarāṣṭrasya droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ |
anyeṣāṃ caiwa wṛddhānāṃ widurasya kṛpasya ca ||2||

ewaṃ sarwānkurūnwṛddhānabhiwādya yatawratāḥ |
samāliṅgya samānāṃśca bālaiścāpyabhiwāditāḥ ||3||

sarwā mātṛstathāpṛṣṭwā kṛtwā caiwa pradakṣiṇam |
sarwāḥ prakṛtayaścaiwa prayayurwāraṇāwatam ||4||

widuraśca mahāprājñastathānye kurupuṅgawāḥ |
paurāśca puruṣawyāghrānanwayuḥ śokakarśitāḥ ||5||

tatra keccidbruwanti sma brāhmaṇā nirbhayāstadā |
śocamānāḥ pāṇḍuputrānatīwa bharatarṣabha ||6||

wiṣamaṃ paśyate rājā sarwathā tamasāwṛtaḥ |
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sudurbuddhirna ca dharmaṃ prapaśyati ||7||

na hi pāpamapāpātmā rocayiṣyati pāṇḍawaḥ |
bhīmo wā balināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kaunteyo wā dhanañjayaḥ ||8||

kuta ewa mahāprājñau mādrīputrau kariṣyataḥ ||8||

tadrājyaṃ pitṛtaḥ prāptaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro na mṛṣyate |
adharmamakhilaṃ kiṃ nu bhīṣmo'yamanumanyate ||9||

wiwāsyamānānasthāne kaunteyānbharatarṣabhān ||9||

pitewa hi nṛpo'smākamabhūcchāntanawaḥ purā |
wicitrawīryo rājarṣiḥ pāṇḍuśca kurunandanaḥ ||10||

sa tasminpuruṣawyāghre diṣṭabhāwaṃ gate sati |
rājaputrānimānbālāndhṛtarāṣṭro na mṛṣyate ||11||

wayametadamṛṣyantaḥ sarwa ewa purottamāt |
gṛhānwihāya gacchāmo yatra yāti yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||12||

tāṃstathāwādinaḥ paurānduḥkhitānduḥkhakarśitaḥ |
uwāca paramaprīto dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||13||

pitā mānyo guruḥ śreṣṭho yadāha pṛthiwīpatiḥ |
aśaṅkamānaistatkāryamasmābhiriti no wratam ||14||

bhawantaḥ suhṛdo'smākamasmānkṛtwā pradakṣiṇam |
āśīrbhirabhinandyāsmānniwartadhwaṃ yathāgṛham ||15||

yadā tu kāryamasmākaṃ bhawadbhirupapatsyate |
tadā kariṣyatha mama priyāṇi ca hitāni ca ||16||

te tatheti pratijñāya kṛtwā caitānpradakṣiṇam |
āśīrbhirabhinandyaināñjagmurnagaramewa hi ||17||

paureṣu tu niwṛtteṣu widuraḥ sarwadharmawit |
bodhayanpāṇḍawaśreṣṭhamidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||18||

prājñaḥ prājñaṃ pralāpajñaḥ samyagdharmārthadarśiwān ||18||

wijñāyedaṃ tathā kuryādāpadaṃ nistaredyathā |
alohaṃ niśitaṃ śastraṃ śarīraparikartanam ||19||

yo wetti na tamāghnanti pratighātawidaṃ dwiṣaḥ ||19||

kakṣaghnaḥ śiśiraghnaśca mahākakṣe bilaukasaḥ |
na dahediti cātmānaṃ yo rakṣati sa jīwati ||20||

nācakṣurwetti panthānaṃ nācakṣurwindate diśaḥ |
nādhṛtirbhūtimāpnoti budhyaswaiwaṃ prabodhitaḥ ||21||

anāptairdattamādatte naraḥ śastramalohajam |
śwāwiccharaṇamāsādya pramucyeta hutāśanāt ||22||

caranmārgānwijānāti nakṣatrairwindate diśaḥ |
ātmanā cātmanaḥ pañca pīḍayannānupīḍyate ||23||

anuśiṣṭwānugatwā ca kṛtwā cainānpradakṣiṇam |
pāṇḍawānabhyanujñāya widuraḥ prayayau gṛhān ||24||

niwṛtte widure caiwa bhīṣme paurajane tathā |
ajātaśatrumāmantrya kuntī wacanamabrawīt ||25||

kṣattā yadabrawīdwākyaṃ janamadhye'bruwanniwa |
twayā ca tattathetyukto jānīmo na ca tadwayam ||26||

yadi tacchakyamasmābhiḥ śrotuṃ na ca sadoṣawat |
śrotumicchāmi tatsarwaṃ saṃwādaṃ tawa tasya ca ||27||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

wiṣādagneśca boddhawyamiti māṃ widuro'brawīt |
panthāśca wo nāwiditaḥ kaścitsyāditi cābrawīt ||28||

jitendriyaśca wasudhāṃ prāpsyasīti ca mābrawīt |
wijñātamiti tatsarwamityukto widuro mayā ||29||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

aṣṭame'hani rohiṇyāṃ prayātāḥ phalgunasya te |
wāraṇāwatamāsādya dadṛśurnāgaraṃ janam ||30||






                  134


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ sarwāḥ prakṛtayo nagarādwāraṇāwatāt |
sarwamaṅgalasaṃyuktā yathāśāstramatandritāḥ ||1||

śrutwāgatānpāṇḍuputrānnānāyānaiḥ sahasraśaḥ |
abhijagmurnaraśreṣṭhāñśrutwaiwa parayā mudā ||2||

te samāsādya kaunteyānwāraṇāwatakā janāḥ |
kṛtwā jayāśiṣaḥ sarwe pariwāryopatasthire ||3||

tairwṛtaḥ puruṣawyāghro dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
wibabhau dewasaṅkāśo wajrapāṇiriwāmaraiḥ ||4||

satkṛtāste tu pauraiśca paurānsatkṛtya cānaghāḥ |
alaṅkṛtaṃ janākīrṇaṃ wiwiśurwāraṇāwatam ||5||

te prawiśya puraṃ wīrāstūrṇaṃ jagmuratho gṛhān |
brāhmaṇānāṃ mahīpāla ratānāṃ sweṣu karmasu ||6||

nagarādhikṛtānāṃ ca gṛhāṇi rathināṃ tathā |
upatasthurnaraśreṣṭhā waiśyaśūdragṛhānapi ||7||

arcitāśca naraiḥ pauraiḥ pāṇḍawā bharatarṣabhāḥ |
jagmurāwasathaṃ paścātpurocanapuraskṛtāḥ ||8||

tebhyo bhakṣyānnapānāni śayanāni śubhāni ca |
āsanāni ca mukhyāni pradadau sa purocanaḥ ||9||

tatra te satkṛtāstena sumahārhaparicchadāḥ |
upāsyamānāḥ puruṣairūṣuḥ puraniwāsibhiḥ ||10||

daśarātroṣitānāṃ tu tatra teṣāṃ purocanaḥ |
niwedayāmāsa gṛhaṃ śiwākhyamaśiwaṃ tadā ||11||

tatra te puruṣawyāghrā wiwiśuḥ saparicchadāḥ |
purocanasya wacanātkailāsamiwa guhyakāḥ ||12||

tattwagāramabhiprekṣya sarwadharmawiśāradaḥ |
uwācāgneyamityewaṃ bhīmasenaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||13||

jighransomya wasāgandhaṃ sarpirjatuwimiśritam ||13||

kṛtaṃ hi wyaktamāgneyamidaṃ weśma parantapa |
śaṇasarjarasaṃ wyaktamānītaṃ gṛhakarmaṇi ||14||

muñjabalwajawaṃśādi drawyaṃ sarwaṃ ghṛtokṣitam ||14||

śilpibhiḥ sukṛtaṃ hyāptairwinītairweśmakarmaṇi |
wiśwastaṃ māmayaṃ pāpo dagdhukāmaḥ purocanaḥ ||15||

imāṃ tu tāṃ mahābuddhirwiduro dṛṣṭawāṃstadā |
āpadaṃ tena māṃ pārtha sa sambodhitawānpurā ||16||

te wayaṃ bodhitāstena buddhawanto'śiwaṃ gṛham |
ācāryaiḥ sukṛtaṃ gūḍhairduryodhanawaśānugaiḥ ||17||

bhīma uwāca||

yadidaṃ gṛhamāgneyaṃ wihitaṃ manyate bhawān |
tatraiwa sādhu gacchāmo yatra pūrwoṣitā wayam ||18||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

iha yattairnirākārairwastawyamiti rocaye |
naṣṭairiwa wicinwadbhirgatimiṣṭāṃ dhruwāmitaḥ ||19||

yadi windeta cākāramasmākaṃ hi purocanaḥ |
śīghrakārī tato bhūtwā prasahyāpi daheta naḥ ||20||

nāyaṃ bibhetyupakrośādadharmādwā purocanaḥ |
tathā hi wartate mandaḥ suyodhanamate sthitaḥ ||21||

api ceha pradagdheṣu bhīṣmo'smāsu pitāmahaḥ |
kopaṃ kuryātkimarthaṃ wā kaurawānkopayeta saḥ ||22||

dharma ityewa kupyeta tathānye kurupuṅgawāḥ ||22||

wayaṃ tu yadi dāhasya bibhyataḥ pradrawema hi |
spaśairno ghātayetsārwānrājyalubdhaḥ suyodhanaḥ ||23||

apadasthānpade tiṣṭhannapakṣānpakṣasaṃsthitaḥ |
hīnakośānmahākośaḥ prayogairghātayeddhruwam ||24||

tadasmābhirimaṃ pāpaṃ taṃ ca pāpaṃ suyodhanam |
wañcayadbhirniwastawyaṃ channawāsaṃ kwacitkwacit ||25||

te wayaṃ mṛgayāśīlāścarāma wasudhāmimām |
tathā no widitā mārgā bhawiṣyanti palāyatām ||26||

bhaumaṃ ca bilamadyaiwa karawāma susaṃwṛtam |
gūḍhocchwasānna nastatra hutāśaḥ sampradhakṣyati ||27||

wasato'tra yathā cāsmānna budhyeta purocanaḥ |
pauro wāpi janaḥ kaścittathā kāryamatandritaiḥ ||28||






                  135


waiśampāyana uwāca||

widurasya suhṛtkaścitkhanakaḥ kuśalaḥ kwacit |
wiwikte pāṇḍawānrājannidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||1||

prahito widureṇāsmi khanakaḥ kuśalo bhṛśam |
pāṇḍawānāṃ priyaṃ kāryamiti kiṃ karawāṇi waḥ ||2||

pracchannaṃ widureṇoktaḥ śreyastwamiha pāṇḍawān |
pratipādaya wiśwāsāditi kiṃ karawāṇi waḥ ||3||

kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ rātrāwasya purocanaḥ |
bhawanasya tawa dwāri pradāsyati hutāśanam ||4||

mātrā saha pradagdhawyāḥ pāṇḍawāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ |
iti wyawasitaṃ pārtha dhārtarāṣṭrasya me śrutam ||5||

kiñcicca widureṇokto mlecchawācāsi pāṇḍawa |
twayā ca tattathetyuktametadwiśwāsakāraṇam ||6||

uwāca taṃ satyadhṛtiḥ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
abhijānāmi saumya twāṃ suhṛdaṃ widurasya wai ||7||

śucimāptaṃ priyaṃ caiwa sadā ca dṛḍhabhaktikam |
na widyate kaweḥ kiñcidabhijñānaprayojanam ||8||

yathā naḥ sa tathā nastwaṃ nirwiśeṣā wayaṃ twayi |
bhawataḥ sma yathā tasya pālayāsmānyathā kawiḥ ||9||

idaṃ śaraṇamāgneyaṃ madarthamiti me matiḥ |
purocanena wihitaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt ||10||

sa pāpaḥ kośawāṃścaiwa sasahāyaśca durmatiḥ |
asmānapi ca duṣṭātmā nityakālaṃ prabādhate ||11||

sa bhawānmokṣayatwasmānyatnenāsmāddhutāśanāt |
asmāswiha hi dagdheṣu sakāmaḥ syātsuyodhanaḥ ||12||

samṛddhamāyudhāgāramidaṃ tasya durātmanaḥ |
waprānte niṣpratīkāramāśliṣyedaṃ kṛtaṃ mahat ||13||

idaṃ tadaśubhaṃ nūnaṃ tasya karma cikīrṣitam |
prāgewa widuro weda tenāsmānanwabodhayat ||14||

seyamāpadanuprāptā kṣattā yāṃ dṛṣṭawānpurā |
purocanasyāwiditānasmāṃstwaṃ wipramocaya ||15||

sa tatheti pratiśrutya khanako yatnamāsthitaḥ |
parikhāmutkirannāma cakāra sumahadbilam ||16||

cakre ca weśmanastasya madhye nātimahanmukham |
kapāṭayuktamajñātaṃ samaṃ bhūmyā ca bhārata ||17||

purocanabhayāccaiwa wyadadhātsaṃwṛtaṃ mukham |
sa tatra ca gṛhadwāri wasatyaśubhadhīḥ sadā ||18||

tatra te sāyudhāḥ sarwe wasanti sma kṣapāṃ nṛpa |
diwā caranti mṛgayāṃ pāṇḍaweyā wanādwanam ||19||

wiśwastawadawiśwastā wañcayantaḥ purocanam |
atuṣṭāstuṣṭawadrājannūṣuḥ paramaduḥkhitāḥ ||20||

na cainānanwabudhyanta narā nagarawāsinaḥ |
anyatra widurāmātyāttasmātkhanakasattamāt ||21||






                  136


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tāṃstu dṛṣṭwā sumanasaḥ parisaṃwatsaroṣitān |
wiśwastāniwa saṃlakṣya harṣaṃ cakre purocanaḥ ||1||

purocane tathā hṛṣṭe kaunteyo'tha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
bhīmasenārjunau caiwa yamau cowāca dharmawit ||2||

asmānayaṃ suwiśwastānwetti pāpaḥ purocanaḥ |
wañcito'yaṃ nṛśaṃsātmā kālaṃ manye palāyane ||3||

āyudhāgāramādīpya dagdhwā caiwa purocanam |
ṣaṭprāṇino nidhāyeha drawāmo'nabhilakṣitāḥ ||4||

atha dānāpadeśena kuntī brāhmaṇabhojanam |
cakre niśi mahadrājannājagmustatra yoṣitaḥ ||5||

tā wihṛtya yathākāmaṃ bhuktwā pītwā ca bhārata |
jagmurniśi gṛhānewa samanujñāpya mādhawīm ||6||

niṣādī pañcaputrā tu tasminbhojye yadṛcchayā |
annārthinī samabhyāgātsaputrā kālacoditā ||7||

sā pītwā madirāṃ mattā saputrā madawihwalā |
saha sarwaiḥ sutai rājaṃstasminnewa niweśane ||8||

suṣwāpa wigatajñānā mṛtakalpā narādhipa ||8||

atha prawāte tumule niśi supte jane wibho |
tadupādīpayadbhīmaḥ śete yatra purocanaḥ ||9||

tataḥ pratāpaḥ sumahāñśabdaścaiwa wibhāwasoḥ |
prādurāsīttadā tena bubudhe sa janawrajaḥ ||10||

paurā ūcuḥ||

duryodhanaprayuktena pāpenākṛtabuddhinā |
gṛhamātmawināśāya kāritaṃ dāhitaṃ ca yat ||11||

aho dhigdhṛtarāṣṭrasya buddhirnātisamañjasī |
yaḥ śucīnpāṇḍawānbālāndāhayāmāsa mantriṇā ||12||

diṣṭyā twidānīṃ pāpātmā dagdho'yamatidurmatiḥ |
anāgasaḥ suwiśwastānyo dadāha narottamān ||13||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ te wilapanti sma wāraṇāwatakā janāḥ |
pariwārya gṛhaṃ tacca tasthū rātrau samantataḥ ||14||

pāṇḍawāścāpi te rājanmātrā saha suduḥkhitāḥ |
bilena tena nirgatya jagmurgūḍhamalakṣitāḥ ||15||

tena nidroparodhena sādhwasena ca pāṇḍawāḥ |
na śekuḥ sahasā gantuṃ saha mātrā parantapāḥ ||16||

bhīmasenastu rājendra bhīmawegaparākramaḥ |
jagāma bhrātṛnādāya sarwānmātaramewa ca ||17||

skandhamāropya jananīṃ yamāwaṅkena wīryawān |
pārthau gṛhītwā pāṇibhyāṃ bhrātarau sumahābalau ||18||

tarasā pādapānbhañjanmahīṃ padbhyāṃ widārayan |
sa jagāmāśu tejaswī wātaraṃhā wṛkodaraḥ ||19||






                  137


waiśampāyana uwāca||

atha rātryāṃ wyatītāyāmaśeṣo nāgaro janaḥ |
tatrājagāma twarito didṛkṣuḥ pāṇḍunandanān ||1||

nirwāpayanto jwalanaṃ te janā dadṛśustataḥ |
jātuṣaṃ tadgṛhaṃ dagdhamamātyaṃ ca purocanam ||2||

nūnaṃ duryodhanenedaṃ wihitaṃ pāpakarmaṇā |
pāṇḍawānāṃ wināśāya ityewaṃ cukruṣurjanāḥ ||3||

widite dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dhārtarāṣṭro na saṃśayaḥ |
dagdhawānpāṇḍudāyādānna hyenaṃ pratiṣiddhawān ||4||

nūnaṃ śāntanawo bhīṣmo na dharmamanuwartate |
droṇaśca widuraścaiwa kṛpaścānye ca kaurawāḥ ||5||

te wayaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya preṣayāmo durātmanaḥ |
saṃwṛttaste paraḥ kāmaḥ pāṇḍawāndagdhawānasi ||6||

tato wyapohamānāste pāṇḍawārthe hutāśanam |
niṣādīṃ dadṛśurdagdhāṃ pañcaputrāmanāgasam ||7||

khanakena tu tenaiwa weśma śodhayatā bilam |
pāṃsubhiḥ pratyapihitaṃ puruṣaistairalakṣitam ||8||

tataste preṣayāmāsurdhṛtarāṣṭrasya nāgarāḥ |
pāṇḍawānagninā dagdhānamātyaṃ ca purocanam ||9||

śrutwā tu dhṛtarāṣṭrastadrājā sumahadapriyam |
wināśaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ wilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ ||10||

adya pāṇḍurmṛto rājā bhrātā mama sudurlabhaḥ |
teṣu wīreṣu dagdheṣu mātrā saha wiśeṣataḥ ||11||

gacchantu puruṣāḥ śīghraṃ nagaraṃ wāraṇāwatam |
satkārayantu tānwīrānkuntirājasutāṃ ca tām ||12||

kārayantu ca kulyāni śubhrāṇi ca mahānti ca |
ye ca tatra mṛtāsteṣāṃ suhṛdo'rcantu tānapi ||13||

ewaṅgate mayā śakyaṃ yadyatkārayituṃ hitam |
pāṇḍawānāṃ ca kuntyāśca tatsarwaṃ kriyatāṃ dhanaiḥ ||14||

ewamuktwā tataścakre jñātibhiḥ pariwāritaḥ |
udakaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro'mbikāsutaḥ ||15||

cukruśuḥ kaurawāḥ sarwe bhṛśaṃ śokaparāyaṇāḥ |
widurastwalpaśaścakre śokaṃ weda paraṃ hi saḥ ||16||

pāṇḍawāścāpi nirgatya nagarādwāraṇāwatāt |
jawena prayayū rājandakṣiṇāṃ diśamāśritāḥ ||17||

wijñāya niśi panthānaṃ nakṣatrairdakṣiṇāmukhāḥ |
yatamānā wanaṃ rājangahanaṃ pratipedire ||18||

tataḥ śrāntāḥ pipāsārtā nidrāndhāḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ |
punarūcurmahāwīryaṃ bhīmasenamidaṃ wacaḥ ||19||

itaḥ kaṣṭataraṃ kiṃ nu yadwayaṃ gahane wane |
diśaśca na prajānīmo gantuṃ caiwa na śaknumaḥ ||20||

taṃ ca pāpaṃ na jānīmo yadi dagdhaḥ purocanaḥ |
kathaṃ nu wipramucyema bhayādasmādalakṣitāḥ ||21||

punarasmānupādāya tathaiwa wraja bhārata |
twaṃ hi no balawāneko yathā satatagastathā ||22||

ityukto dharmarājena bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ |
ādāya kuntīṃ bhrātṛṃśca jagāmāśu mahābalaḥ ||23||






                  138


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tena wikramatā tūrṇamūruwegasamīritam |
prawawāwanilo rājañśuciśukrāgame yathā ||1||

sa mṛdnanpuṣpitāṃścaiwa phalitāṃśca wanaspatīn |
ārujandārugulmāṃśca pathastasya samīpajān ||2||

tathā wṛkṣānbhañjamāno jagāmāmitawikramaḥ |
tasya wegena pāṇḍūnāṃ mūrcchewa samajāyata ||3||

asakṛccāpi santīrya dūrapāraṃ bhujaplawaiḥ |
pathi pracchannamāsedurdhārtarāṣṭrabhayāttadā ||4||

kṛcchreṇa mātaraṃ twekāṃ sukumārīṃ yaśaswinīm |
awahattatra pṛṣṭhena rodhaḥsu wiṣameṣu ca ||5||

āgamaṃste wanoddeśamalpamūlaphalodakam |
krūrapakṣimṛgaṃ ghoraṃ sāyāhne bharatarṣabhāḥ ||6||

ghorā samabhawatsandhyā dāruṇā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ |
aprakāśā diśaḥ sarwā wātairāsannanārtawaiḥ ||7||

te śrameṇa ca kaurawyāstṛṣṇayā ca prapīḍitāḥ |
nāśaknuwaṃstadā gantuṃ nidrayā ca prawṛddhayā ||8||

tato bhīmo wanaṃ ghoraṃ prawiśya wijanaṃ mahat |
nyagrodhaṃ wipulacchāyaṃ ramaṇīyamupādrawat ||9||

tatra nikṣipya tānsarwānuwāca bharatarṣabhaḥ |
pānīyaṃ mṛgayāmīha wiśramadhwamiti prabho ||10||

ete ruwanti madhuraṃ sārasā jalacāriṇaḥ |
dhruwamatra jalasthāyo mahāniti matirmama ||11||

anujñātaḥ sa gaccheti bhrātrā jyeṣṭhena bhārata |
jagāma tatra yatra sma ruwanti jalacāriṇaḥ ||12||

sa tatra pītwā pānīyaṃ snātwā ca bharatarṣabha |
uttarīyeṇa pānīyamājahāra tadā nṛpa ||13||

gawyūtimātrādāgatya twarito mātaraṃ prati |
sa suptāṃ mātaraṃ dṛṣṭwā bhrātṛṃśca wasudhātale ||14||

bhṛśaṃ duḥkhaparītātmā wilalāpa wṛkodaraḥ ||14||

śayaneṣu parārdhyeṣu ye purā wāraṇāwate |
nādhijagmustadā nidrāṃ te'dya suptā mahītale ||15||

swasāraṃ wasudewasya śatrusaṅghāwamardinaḥ |
kuntibhojasutāṃ kuntīṃ sarwalakṣaṇapūjitām ||16||

snuṣāṃ wicitrawīryasya bhāryāṃ pāṇḍormahātmanaḥ |
prāsādaśayanāṃ nityaṃ puṇḍarīkāntaraprabhām ||17||

sukumāratarāṃ strīṇāṃ mahārhaśayanocitām |
śayānāṃ paśyatādyeha pṛthiwyāmatathocitām ||18||

dharmādindrācca wāyośca suṣuwe yā sutānimān |
seyaṃ bhūmau pariśrāntā śete hyadyātathocitā ||19||

kiṃ nu duḥkhataraṃ śakyaṃ mayā draṣṭumataḥ param |
yo'hamadya narawyāghrānsuptānpaśyāmi bhūtale ||20||

triṣu lokeṣu yadrājyaṃ dharmawidyo'rhate nṛpaḥ |
so'yaṃ bhūmau pariśrāntaḥ śete prākṛtawatkatham ||21||

ayaṃ nīlāmbudaśyāmo nareṣwapratimo bhuwi |
śete prākṛtawadbhūmāwato duḥkhataraṃ nu kim ||22||

aśwināwiwa dewānāṃ yāwimau rūpasampadā |
tau prākṛtawadadyemau prasuptau dharaṇītale ||23||

jñātayo yasya naiwa syurwiṣamāḥ kulapāṃsanāḥ |
sa jīwetsusukhaṃ loke grāme druma iwaikajaḥ ||24||

eko wṛkṣo hi yo grāme bhawetparṇaphalānwitaḥ |
caityo bhawati nirjñātirarcanīyaḥ supūjitaḥ ||25||

yeṣāṃ ca bahawaḥ śūrā jñātayo dharmasaṃśritāḥ |
te jīwanti sukhaṃ loke bhawanti ca nirāmayāḥ ||26||

balawantaḥ samṛddhārthā mitrabāndhawanandanāḥ |
jīwantyanyonyamāśritya drumāḥ kānanajā iwa ||27||

wayaṃ tu dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa saputreṇa durātmanā |
wiwāsitā na dagdhāśca kathañcittasya śāsanāt ||28||

tasmānmuktā wayaṃ dāhādimaṃ wṛkṣamupāśritāḥ |
kāṃ diśaṃ pratipatsyāmaḥ prāptāḥ kleśamanuttamam ||29||

nātidūre ca nagaraṃ wanādasmāddhi lakṣaye |
jāgartawye swapantīme hanta jāgarmyahaṃ swayam ||30||

pāsyantīme jalaṃ paścātpratibuddhā jitaklamāḥ |
iti bhīmo wyawasyaiwa jajāgāra swayaṃ tadā ||31||






              hiḍimbawadhaparwa
                  139


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tatra teṣu śayāneṣu hiḍimbo nāma rākṣasaḥ |
awidūre wanāttasmācchālawṛkṣamupāśritaḥ ||1||

krūro mānuṣamāṃsādo mahāwīryo mahābalaḥ |
wirūparūpaḥ piṅgākṣaḥ karālo ghoradarśanaḥ ||2||

piśitepsuḥ kṣudhārtastānapaśyata yadṛcchayā ||2||

ūrdhwāṅguliḥ sa kaṇḍūyandhunwanrūkṣāñśiroruhān |
jṛmbhamāṇo mahāwaktraḥ punaḥ punarawekṣya ca ||3||

duṣṭo mānuṣamāṃsādo mahākāyo mahābalaḥ |
āghrāya mānuṣaṃ gandhaṃ bhaginīmidamabrawīt ||4||

upapannaścirasyādya bhakṣo mama manaḥpriyaḥ |
snehasrawānprasrawati jihwā paryeti me mukham ||5||

aṣṭau daṃṣṭrāḥ sutīkṣṇāgrāścirasyāpātaduḥsahāḥ |
deheṣu majjayiṣyāmi snigdheṣu piśiteṣu ca ||6||

ākramya mānuṣaṃ kaṇṭhamācchidya dhamanīmapi |
uṣṇaṃ nawaṃ prapāsyāmi phenilaṃ rudhiraṃ bahu ||7||

gaccha jānīhi ke twete śerate wanamāśritāḥ |
mānuṣo balawāngandho ghrāṇaṃ tarpayatīwa me ||8||

hatwaitānmānuṣānsarwānānayaswa mamāntikam |
asmadwiṣayasuptebhyo naitebhyo bhayamasti te ||9||

eṣāṃ māṃsāni saṃskṛtya mānuṣāṇāṃ yatheṣṭataḥ |
bhakṣayiṣyāwa sahitau kuru tūrṇaṃ waco mama ||10||

bhrāturwacanamājñāya twaramāṇewa rākṣasī |
jagāma tatra yatra sma pāṇḍawā bharatarṣabha ||11||

dadarśa tatra gatwā sā pāṇḍawānpṛthayā saha |
śayānānbhīmasenaṃ ca jāgrataṃ twaparājitam ||12||

dṛṣṭwaiwa bhīmasenaṃ sā śālaskandhamiwodgatam |
rākṣasī kāmayāmāsa rūpeṇāpratimaṃ bhuwi ||13||

ayaṃ śyāmo mahābāhuḥ siṃhaskandho mahādyutiḥ |
kambugrīwaḥ puṣkarākṣo bhartā yukto bhawenmama ||14||

nāhaṃ bhrātṛwaco jātu kuryāṃ krūropasaṃhitam |
patisneho'tibalawānna tathā bhrātṛsauhṛdam ||15||

muhūrtamiwa tṛptiśca bhawedbhrāturmamaiwa ca |
hatairetairahatwā tu modiṣye śāśwatiḥ samāḥ ||16||

sā kāmarūpiṇī rūpaṃ kṛtwā mānuṣamuttamam |
upatasthe mahābāhuṃ bhīmasenaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ||17||

wilajjamānewa latā diwyābharaṇabhūṣitā |
smitapūrwamidaṃ wākyaṃ bhīmasenamathābrawīt ||18||

kutastwamasi samprāptaḥ kaścāsi puruṣarṣabha |
ka ime śerate ceha puruṣā dewarūpiṇaḥ ||19||

keyaṃ ca bṛhatī śyāmā sukumārī tawānagha |
śete wanamidaṃ prāpya wiśwastā swagṛhe yathā ||20||

nedaṃ jānāti gahanaṃ wanaṃ rākṣasasewitam |
wasati hyatra pāpātmā hiḍimbo nāma rākṣasaḥ ||21||

tenāhaṃ preṣitā bhrātrā duṣṭabhāwena rakṣasā |
bibhakṣayiṣatā māṃsaṃ yuṣmākamamaropama ||22||

sāhaṃ twāmabhisamprekṣya dewagarbhasamaprabham |
nānyaṃ bhartāramicchāmi satyametadbrawīmi te ||23||

etadwijñāya dharmajña yuktaṃ mayi samācara |
kāmopahatacittāṅgīṃ bhajamānāṃ bhajaswa mām ||24||

trāsye'haṃ twāṃ mahābāho rākṣasātpuruṣādakāt |
watsyāwo giridurgeṣu bhartā bhawa mamānagha ||25||

antarikṣacarā hyasmi kāmato wicarāmi ca |
atulāmāpnuhi prītiṃ tatra tatra mayā saha ||26||

bhīma uwāca||

mātaraṃ bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ kaniṣṭhānaparānimān |
parityajeta ko nwadya prabhawanniwa rākṣasi ||27||

ko hi suptānimānbhrātṛndattwā rākṣasabhojanam |
mātaraṃ ca naro gacchetkāmārta iwa madwidhaḥ ||28||

rākṣasyuwāca||

yatte priyaṃ tatkariṣye sarwānetānprabodhaya |
mokṣayiṣyāmi waḥ kāmaṃ rākṣasātpuruṣādakāt ||29||

bhīma uwāca||

sukhasuptānwane bhrātṛnmātaraṃ caiwa rākṣasi |
na bhayādbodhayiṣyāmi bhrātustawa durātmanaḥ ||30||

na hi me rākṣasā bhīru soḍhuṃ śaktāḥ parākramam |
na manuṣyā na gandharwā na yakṣāścārulocane ||31||

gaccha wā tiṣṭha wā bhadre yadwāpīcchasi tatkuru |
taṃ wā preṣaya tanwaṅgi bhrātaraṃ puruṣādakam ||32||






                  140


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tāṃ widitwā ciragatāṃ hiḍimbo rākṣaseśwaraḥ |
awatīrya drumāttasmādājagāmātha pāṇḍawān ||1||

lohitākṣo mahābāhurūrdhwakeśo mahābalaḥ |
meghasaṅghātawarṣmā ca tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrojjwalānanaḥ ||2||

tamāpatantaṃ dṛṣṭwaiwa tathā wikṛtadarśanam |
hiḍimbowāca witrastā bhīmasenamidaṃ wacaḥ ||3||

āpatatyeṣa duṣṭātmā saṅkruddhaḥ puruṣādakaḥ |
twāmahaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ yadbrawīmi tathā kuru ||4||

ahaṃ kāmagamā wīra rakṣobalasamanwitā |
āruhemāṃ mama śroṇīṃ neṣyāmi twāṃ wihāyasā ||5||

prabodhayainānsaṃsuptānmātaraṃ ca parantapa |
sarwānewa gamiṣyāmi gṛhītwā wo wihāyasā ||6||

bhīma uwāca||

mā bhaistwaṃ wipulaśroṇi naiṣa kaścinmayi sthite |
ahamenaṃ haniṣyāmi prekṣantyāste sumadhyame ||7||

nāyaṃ pratibalo bhīru rākṣasāpasado mama |
soḍhuṃ yudhi parispandamathawā sarwarākṣasāḥ ||8||

paśya bāhū suwṛttau me hastihastanibhāwimau |
ūrū parighasaṅkāśau saṃhataṃ cāpyuro mama ||9||

wikramaṃ me yathendrasya sādya drakṣyasi śobhane |
māwamaṃsthāḥ pṛthuśroṇi matwā māmiha mānuṣam ||10||

hiḍimbowāca||

nāwamanye narawyāghra twāmahaṃ dewarūpiṇam |
dṛṣṭāpadānastu mayā mānuṣeṣwewa rākṣasaḥ ||11||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tathā sañjalpatastasya bhīmasenasya bhārata |
wācaḥ śuśrāwa tāḥ kruddho rākṣasaḥ puruṣādakaḥ ||12||

awekṣamāṇastasyāśca hiḍimbo mānuṣaṃ wapuḥ |
sragdāmapūritaśikhaṃ samagrendunibhānanam ||13||

subhrūnāsākṣikeśāntaṃ sukumāranakhatwacam |
sarwābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ susūkṣmāmbarawāsasam ||14||

tāṃ tathā mānuṣaṃ rūpaṃ bibhratīṃ sumanoharam |
puṃskāmāṃ śaṅkamānaśca cukrodha puruṣādakaḥ ||15||

saṅkruddho rākṣasastasyā bhaginyāḥ kurusattama |
utphālya wipule netre tatastāmidamabrawīt ||16||

ko hi me bhoktukāmasya wighnaṃ carati durmatiḥ |
na bibheṣi hiḍimbe kiṃ matkopādwipramohitā ||17||

dhiktwāmasati puṃskāme mama wipriyakāriṇi |
pūrweṣāṃ rākṣasendrāṇāṃ sarweṣāmayaśaskari ||18||

yānimānāśritākārṣīrapriyaṃ sumahanmama |
eṣa tānadya wai sarwānhaniṣyāmi twayā saha ||19||

ewamuktwā hiḍimbāṃ sa hiḍimbo lohitekṣaṇaḥ |
wadhāyābhipapātaināṃ dantairdantānupaspṛśan ||20||

tamāpatantaṃ samprekṣya bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ waraḥ |
bhartsayāmāsa tejaswī tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābrawīt ||21||






                  141


waiśampāyana uwāca||

bhīmasenastu taṃ dṛṣṭwā rākṣasaṃ prahasanniwa |
bhaginīṃ prati saṅkruddhamidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||1||

kiṃ te hiḍimba etairwā sukhasuptaiḥ prabodhitaiḥ |
māmāsādaya durbuddhe tarasā twaṃ narāśana ||2||

mayyewa praharaihi twaṃ na striyaṃ hantumarhasi |
wiśeṣato'napakṛte pareṇāpakṛte sati ||3||

na hīyaṃ swawaśā bālā kāmayatyadya māmiha |
coditaiṣā hyanaṅgena śarīrāntaracāriṇā ||4||

bhaginī tawa durbuddhe rākṣasānāṃ yaśohara ||4||

twanniyogena caiweyaṃ rūpaṃ mama samīkṣya ca |
kāmayatyadya māṃ bhīrurnaiṣā dūṣayate kulam ||5||

anaṅgena kṛte doṣe nemāṃ twamiha rākṣasa |
mayi tiṣṭhati duṣṭātmanna striyaṃ hantumarhasi ||6||

samāgaccha mayā sārdhamekenaiko narāśana |
ahamewa nayiṣyāmi twāmadya yamasādanam ||7||

adya te talaniṣpiṣṭaṃ śiro rākṣasa dīryatām |
kuñjarasyewa pādena winiṣpiṣṭaṃ balīyasaḥ ||8||

adya gātrāṇi krawyādāḥ śyenā gomāyawaśca te |
karṣantu bhuwi saṃhṛṣṭā nihatasya mayā mṛdhe ||9||

kṣaṇenādya kariṣye'hamidaṃ wanamakaṇṭakam |
purastāddūṣitaṃ nityaṃ twayā bhakṣayatā narān ||10||

adya twāṃ bhaginī pāpa kṛṣyamāṇaṃ mayā bhuwi |
drakṣatyadripratīkāśaṃ siṃhenewa mahādwipam ||11||

nirābādhāstwayi hate mayā rākṣasapāṃsana |
wanametaccariṣyanti puruṣā wanacāriṇaḥ ||12||

hiḍimba uwāca||

garjitena wṛthā kiṃ te katthitena ca mānuṣa |
kṛtwaitatkarmaṇā sarwaṃ katthethā mā ciraṃ kṛthāḥ ||13||

balinaṃ manyase yacca ātmānamaparākramam |
jñāsyasyadya samāgamya mayātmānaṃ balādhikam ||14||

na tāwadetānhiṃsiṣye swapantwete yathāsukham |
eṣa twāmewa durbuddhe nihanmyadyāpriyaṃwadam ||15||

pītwā tawāsṛggātrebhyastataḥ paścādimānapi |
haniṣyāmi tataḥ paścādimāṃ wipriyakāriṇīm ||16||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktwā tato bāhuṃ pragṛhya puruṣādakaḥ |
abhyadhāwata saṅkruddho bhīmasenamariṃdamam ||17||

tasyābhipatatastūrṇaṃ bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ |
wegena prahṛtaṃ bāhuṃ nijagrāha hasanniwa ||18||

nigṛhya taṃ balādbhīmo wisphurantaṃ cakarṣa ha |
tasmāddeśāddhanūṃṣyaṣṭau siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā ||19||

tataḥ sa rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ pāṇḍawena balāddhṛtaḥ |
bhīmasenaṃ samāliṅgya wyanadadbhairawaṃ rawam ||20||

punarbhīmo balādenaṃ wicakarṣa mahābalaḥ |
mā śabdaḥ sukhasuptānāṃ bhrātṛṇāṃ me bhawediti ||21||

anyonyaṃ tau samāsādya wicakarṣaturojasā |
rākṣaso bhīmasenaśca wikramaṃ cakratuḥ param ||22||

babhañjaturmahāwṛkṣāṃllatāścākarṣatustataḥ |
mattāwiwa susaṃrabdhau wāraṇau ṣaṣṭihāyanau ||23||

tayoḥ śabdena mahatā wibuddhāste nararṣabhāḥ |
saha mātrā tu dadṛśurhiḍimbāmagrataḥ sthitām ||24||






                  142


waiśampāyana uwāca||

prabuddhāste hiḍimbāyā rūpaṃ dṛṣṭwātimānuṣam |
wismitāḥ puruṣawyāghrā babhūwuḥ pṛthayā saha ||1||

tataḥ kuntī samīkṣyaināṃ wismitā rūpasampadā |
uwāca madhuraṃ wākyaṃ sāntwapūrwamidaṃ śanaiḥ ||2||

kasya twaṃ suragarbhābhe kā cāsi warawarṇini |
kena kāryeṇa suśroṇi kutaścāgamanaṃ tawa ||3||

yadi wāsya wanasyāsi dewatā yadi wāpsarāḥ |
ācakṣwa mama tatsarwaṃ kimarthaṃ ceha tiṣṭhasi ||4||

hiḍimbowāca||

yadetatpaśyasi wanaṃ nīlameghanibhaṃ mahat |
niwāso rākṣasasyaitaddhiḍimbasya mamaiwa ca ||5||

tasya māṃ rākṣasendrasya bhaginīṃ widdhi bhāmini |
bhrātrā sampreṣitāmārye twāṃ saputrāṃ jighāṃsatā ||6||

krūrabuddherahaṃ tasya wacanādāgatā iha |
adrākṣaṃ hemawarṇābhaṃ tawa putraṃ mahaujasam ||7||

tato'haṃ sarwabhūtānāṃ bhāwe wicaratā śubhe |
coditā tawa putrasya manmathena waśānugā ||8||

tato wṛto mayā bhartā tawa putro mahābalaḥ |
apanetuṃ ca yatito na caiwa śakito mayā ||9||

cirāyamāṇāṃ māṃ jñātwā tataḥ sa puruṣādakaḥ |
swayamewāgato hantumimānsarwāṃstawātmajān ||10||

sa tena mama kāntena tawa putreṇa dhīmatā |
balādito winiṣpiṣya wyapakṛṣṭo mahātmanā ||11||

wikarṣantau mahāwegau garjamānau parasparam |
paśyadhwaṃ yudhi wikrāntāwetau tau nararākṣasau ||12||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tasyāḥ śrutwaiwa wacanamutpapāta yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
arjuno nakulaścaiwa sahadewaśca wīryawān ||13||

tau te dadṛśurāsaktau wikarṣantau parasparam |
kāṅkṣamāṇau jayaṃ caiwa siṃhāwiwa raṇotkaṭau ||14||

tāwanyonyaṃ samāśliṣya wikarṣantau parasparam |
dāwāgnidhūmasadṛśaṃ cakratuḥ pārthiwaṃ rajaḥ ||15||

wasudhāreṇusaṃwītau wasudhādharasaṃnibhau |
wibhrājetāṃ yathā śailau nīhāreṇābhisaṃwṛtau ||16||

rākṣasena tathā bhīmaṃ kliśyamānaṃ nirīkṣya tu |
uwācedaṃ wacaḥ pārthaḥ prahasañśanakairiwa ||17||

bhīma mā bhairmahābāho na twāṃ budhyāmahe wayam |
sametaṃ bhīmarūpeṇa prasuptāḥ śramakarśitāḥ ||18||

sāhāyye'smi sthitaḥ pārtha yodhayiṣyāmi rākṣasam |
nakulaḥ sahadewaśca mātaraṃ gopayiṣyataḥ ||19||

bhīma uwāca||

udāsīno nirīkṣaswa na kāryaḥ sambhramastwayā |
na jātwayaṃ punarjīwenmadbāhwantaramāgataḥ ||20||

arjuna uwāca||

kimanena ciraṃ bhīma jīwatā pāparakṣasā |
gantawyaṃ na ciraṃ sthātumiha śakyamariṃdama ||21||

purā saṃrajyate prācī purā sandhyā prawartate |
raudre muhūrte rakṣāṃsi prabalāni bhawanti ca ||22||

twaraswa bhīma mā krīḍa jahi rakṣo wibhīṣaṇam |
purā wikurute māyāṃ bhujayoḥ sāramarpaya ||23||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

arjunenaiwamuktastu bhīmo bhīmasya rakṣasaḥ |
utkṣipyābhrāmayaddehaṃ tūrṇaṃ guṇaśatādhikam ||24||

bhīma uwāca||

wṛthāmāṃsairwṛthā puṣṭo wṛthā wṛddho wṛthāmatiḥ |
wṛthāmaraṇamarhastwaṃ wṛthādya na bhawiṣyasi ||25||

arjuna uwāca||

atha wā manyase bhāraṃ twamimaṃ rākṣasaṃ yudhi |
karomi tawa sāhāyyaṃ śīghramewa nihanyatām ||26||

atha wāpyahamewainaṃ haniṣyāmi wṛkodara |
kṛtakarmā pariśrāntaḥ sādhu tāwadupārama ||27||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tasya tadwacanaṃ śrutwā bhīmaseno'tyamarṣaṇaḥ |
niṣpiṣyainaṃ balādbhūmau paśumāramamārayat ||28||

sa māryamāṇo bhīmena nanāda wipulaṃ swanam |
pūrayaṃstadwanaṃ sarwaṃ jalārdra iwa dundubhiḥ ||29||

bhujābhyāṃ yoktrayitwā taṃ balawānpāṇḍunandanaḥ |
madhye bhaṅktwā sa balawānharṣayāmāsa pāṇḍawān ||30||

hiḍimbaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭwā saṃhṛṣṭāste taraswinaḥ |
apūjayannarawyāghraṃ bhīmasenamariṃdamam ||31||

abhipūjya mahātmānaṃ bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramam |
punarewārjuno wākyamuwācedaṃ wṛkodaram ||32||

nadūre nagaraṃ manye wanādasmādahaṃ prabho |
śīghraṃ gacchāma bhadraṃ te na no widyātsuyodhanaḥ ||33||

tataḥ sarwe tathetyuktwā saha mātrā parantapāḥ |
prayayuḥ puruṣawyāghrā hiḍimbā caiwa rākṣasī ||34||






              bakawadhaparwa
                  143


bhīma uwāca||

smaranti wairaṃ rakṣāṃsi māyāmāśritya mohinīm |
hiḍimbe wraja panthānaṃ twaṃ wai bhrātṛniṣewitam ||1||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

kruddho'pi puruṣawyāghra bhīma mā sma striyaṃ wadhīḥ |
śarīraguptyābhyadhikaṃ dharmaṃ gopaya pāṇḍawa ||2||

wadhābhiprāyamāyāntamawadhīstwaṃ mahābalam |
rakṣasastasya bhaginī kiṃ naḥ kruddhā kariṣyati ||3||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

hiḍimbā tu tataḥ kuntīmabhiwādya kṛtāñjaliḥ |
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca kaunteyamidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||4||

ārye jānāsi yadduḥkhamiha strīṇāmanaṅgajam |
tadidaṃ māmanuprāptaṃ bhīmasenakṛtaṃ śubhe ||5||

soḍhaṃ tatparamaṃ duḥkhaṃ mayā kālapratīkṣayā |
so'yamabhyāgataḥ kālo bhawitā me sukhāya wai ||6||

mayā hyutsṛjya suhṛdaḥ swadharmaṃ swajanaṃ tathā |
wṛto'yaṃ puruṣawyāghrastawa putraḥ patiḥ śubhe ||7||

wareṇāpi tathānena twayā cāpi yaśaswini |
tathā bruwantī hi tadā pratyākhyātā kriyāṃ prati ||8||

twaṃ māṃ mūḍheti wā matwā bhaktā wānugateti wā |
bhartrānena mahābhāge saṃyojaya sutena te ||9||

tamupādāya gaccheyaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ dewarūpiṇam |
punaścaiwāgamiṣyāmi wiśrambhaṃ kuru me śubhe ||10||

ahaṃ hi manasā dhyātā sarwānneṣyāmi waḥ sadā |
wṛjine tārayiṣyāmi durgeṣu ca nararṣabhān ||11||

pṛṣṭhena wo wahiṣyāmi śīghrāṃ gatimabhīpsataḥ |
yūyaṃ prasādaṃ kuruta bhīmaseno bhajeta mām ||12||

āpadastaraṇe prāṇāndhārayedyena yena hi |
sarwamādṛtya kartawyaṃ taddharmamanuwartatā ||13||

āpatsu yo dhārayati dhramaṃ dharmawiduttamaḥ |
wyasanaṃ hyewa dharmasya dharmiṇāmāpaducyate ||14||

puṇyaṃ prāṇāndhārayati puṇyaṃ prāṇadamucyate |
yena yenācareddharmaṃ tasmingarhā na widyate ||15||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

ewametadyathāttha twaṃ hiḍimbe nātra saṃśayaḥ |
sthātawyaṃ tu twayā dharme yathā brūyāṃ sumadhyame ||16||

snātaṃ kṛtāhnikaṃ bhadre kṛtakautukamaṅgalam |
bhīmasenaṃ bhajethāstwaṃ prāgastagamanādraweḥ ||17||

ahaḥsu wiharānena yathākāmaṃ manojawā |
ayaṃ twānayitawyaste bhīmasenaḥ sadā niśi ||18||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tatheti tatpratijñāya hiḍimbā rākṣasī tadā |
bhīmasenamupādāya ūrdhwamācakrame tataḥ ||19||

śailaśṛṅgeṣu ramyeṣu dewatāyataneṣu ca |
mṛgapakṣiwighuṣṭeṣu ramaṇīyeṣu sarwadā ||20||

kṛtwā ca paramaṃ rūpaṃ sarwābharaṇabhūṣitā |
sañjalpantī sumadhuraṃ ramayāmāsa pāṇḍawam ||21||

tathaiwa wanadurgeṣu puṣpitadrumasānuṣu |
saraḥsu ramaṇīyeṣu padmotpalayuteṣu ca ||22||

nadīdwīpapradeśeṣu waiḍūryasikatāsu ca |
sutīrthawanatoyāsu tathā girinadīṣu ca ||23||

sagarasya pradeśeṣu maṇihemaciteṣu ca |
pattaneṣu ca ramyeṣu mahāśālawaneṣu ca ||24||

dewāraṇyeṣu puṇyeṣu tathā parwatasānuṣu |
guhyakānāṃ niwāseṣu tāpasāyataneṣu ca ||25||

sarwartuphalapuṣpeṣu mānaseṣu saraḥsu ca |
bibhratī paramaṃ rūpaṃ ramayāmāsa pāṇḍawam ||26||

ramayantī tathā bhīmaṃ tatra tatra manojawā |
prajajñe rākṣasī putraṃ bhīmasenānmahābalam ||27||

wirūpākṣaṃ mahāwaktraṃ śaṅkukarṇaṃ wibhīṣaṇam |
bhīmarūpaṃ sutāmroṣṭhaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ mahābalam ||28||

maheṣwāsaṃ mahāwīryaṃ mahāsattwaṃ mahābhujam |
mahājawaṃ mahākāyaṃ mahāmāyamariṃdamam ||29||

amānuṣaṃ mānuṣajaṃ bhīmawegaṃ mahābalam |
yaḥ piśācānatīwānyānbabhūwāti sa mānuṣān ||30||

bālo'pi yauwanaṃ prāpto mānuṣeṣu wiśāṃ pate |
sarwāstreṣu paraṃ wīraḥ prakarṣamagamadbalī ||31||

sadyo hi garbhaṃ rākṣasyo labhante prasawanti ca |
kāmarūpadharāścaiwa bhawanti bahurūpiṇaḥ ||32||

praṇamya wikacaḥ pādāwagṛhṇātsa pitustadā |
mātuśca parameṣwāsastau ca nāmāsya cakratuḥ ||33||

ghaṭabhāsotkaca iti mātaraṃ so'bhyabhāṣata |
abhawattena nāmāsya ghaṭotkaca iti sma ha ||34||

anuraktaśca tānāsītpāṇḍawānsa ghaṭotkacaḥ |
teṣāṃ ca dayito nityamātmabhūto babhūwa saḥ ||35||

saṃwāsasamayo jīrṇa ityabhāṣata taṃ tataḥ |
hiḍimbā samayaṃ kṛtwā swāṃ gatiṃ pratyapadyata ||36||

kṛtyakāla upasthāsye pitṛniti ghaṭotkacaḥ |
āmantrya rākṣasaśreṣṭhaḥ pratasthe cottarāṃ diśam ||37||

sa hi sṛṣṭo maghawatā śaktihetormahātmanā |
karṇasyāpratiwīryasya wināśāya mahātmanaḥ ||38||






                  144


waiśampāyana uwāca||

te wanena wanaṃ wīrā ghnanto mṛgagaṇānbahūn |
apakramya yayū rājaṃstwaramāṇā mahārathāḥ ||1||

matsyāṃstrigartānpāñcālānkīcakānantareṇa ca |
ramaṇīyānwanoddeśānprekṣamāṇāḥ sarāṃsi ca ||2||

jaṭāḥ kṛtwātmanaḥ sarwe walkalājinawāsasaḥ |
saha kuntyā mahātmāno bibhratastāpasaṃ wapuḥ ||3||

kwacidwahanto jananīṃ twaramāṇā mahārathāḥ |
kwacicchandena gacchantaste jagmuḥ prasabhaṃ punaḥ ||4||

brāhmaṃ wedamadhīyānā wedāṅgāni ca sarwaśaḥ |
nītiśāstraṃ ca dharmajñā dadṛśuste pitāmaham ||5||

te'bhiwādya mahātmānaṃ kṛṣṇadwaipāyanaṃ tadā |
tasthuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarwe saha mātrā parantapāḥ ||6||

wyāsa uwāca||

mayedaṃ manasā pūrwaṃ widitaṃ bharatarṣabhāḥ |
yathā sthitairadharmeṇa dhārtarāṣṭrairwiwāsitāḥ ||7||

tadwiditwāsmi samprāptaścikīrṣuḥ paramaṃ hitam |
na wiṣādo'tra kartawyaḥ sarwametatsukhāya waḥ ||8||

samāste caiwa me sarwe yūyaṃ caiwa na saṃśayaḥ |
dīnato bālataścaiwa snehaṃ kurwanti bāndhawāḥ ||9||

tasmādabhyadhikaḥ sneho yuṣmāsu mama sāmpratam |
snehapūrwaṃ cikīrṣāmi hitaṃ wastannibodhata ||10||

idaṃ nagaramabhyāśe ramaṇīyaṃ nirāmayam |
wasateha praticchannā mamāgamanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ||11||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ sa tānsamāśwāsya wyāsaḥ pārthānariṃdamān |
ekacakrāmabhigataḥ kuntīmāśwāsayatprabhuḥ ||12||

jīwaputri sutaste'yaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
pṛthiwyāṃ pārthiwānsarwānpraśāsiṣyati dharmarāṭ ||13||

dharmeṇa jitwā pṛthiwīmakhilāṃ dharmawidwaśī |
bhīmasenārjunabalādbhokṣyatyayamasaṃśayaḥ ||14||

putrāstawa ca mādryāśca sarwa ewa mahārathāḥ |
swarāṣṭre wihariṣyanti sukhaṃ sumanasastadā ||15||

yakṣyanti ca narawyāghrā wijitya pṛthiwīmimām |
rājasūyāśwamedhādyaiḥ kratubhirbhūridakṣiṇaiḥ ||16||

anugṛhya suhṛdwargaṃ dhanena ca sukhena ca |
pitṛpaitāmahaṃ rājyamiha bhokṣyanti te sutāḥ ||17||

ewamuktwā niweśyainānbrāhmaṇasya niweśane |
abrawītpārthiwaśreṣṭhamṛṣirdwaipāyanastadā ||18||

iha māṃ sampratīkṣadhwamāgamiṣyāmyahaṃ punaḥ |
deśakālau widitwaiwa wetsyadhwaṃ paramāṃ mudam ||19||

sa taiḥ prāñjalibhiḥ sarwaistathetyukto narādhipa |
jagāma bhagawānwyāso yathākāmamṛṣiḥ prabhuḥ ||20||






                  145


janamejaya uwāca||

ekacakrāṃ gatāste tu kuntīputrā mahārathāḥ |
ataḥ paraṃ dwijaśreṣṭha kimakurwata pāṇḍawāḥ ||1||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ekacakrāṃ gatāste tu kuntīputrā mahārathāḥ |
ūṣurnāticiraṃ kālaṃ brāhmaṇasya niweśane ||2||

ramaṇīyāni paśyanto wanāni wiwidhāni ca |
pārthiwānapi coddeśānsaritaśca sarāṃsi ca ||3||

cerurbhaikṣaṃ tadā te tu sarwa ewa wiśāṃ pate |
babhūwurnāgarāṇāṃ ca swairguṇaiḥ priyadarśanāḥ ||4||

niwedayanti sma ca te bhaikṣaṃ kuntyāḥ sadā niśi |
tayā wibhaktānbhāgāṃste bhuñjate sma pṛthakpṛthak ||5||

ardhaṃ te bhuñjate wīrāḥ saha mātrā parantapāḥ |
ardhaṃ bhaikṣasya sarwasya bhīmo bhuṅkte mahābalaḥ ||6||

tathā tu teṣāṃ wasatāṃ tatra rājanmahātmanām |
aticakrāma sumahānkālo'tha bharatarṣabha ||7||

tataḥ kadācidbhaikṣāya gatāste bharatarṣabhāḥ |
saṅgatyā bhīmasenastu tatrāste pṛthayā saha ||8||

athārtijaṃ mahāśabdaṃ brāhmaṇasya niweśane |
bhṛśamutpatitaṃ ghoraṃ kuntī śuśrāwa bhārata ||9||

rorūyamāṇāṃstānsarwānparidewayataśca sā |
kāruṇyātsādhubhāwācca dewī rājanna cakṣame ||10||

mathyamānewa duḥkhena hṛdayena pṛthā tataḥ |
uwāca bhīmaṃ kalyāṇī kṛpānwitamidaṃ wacaḥ ||11||

wasāmaḥ susukhaṃ putra brāhmaṇasya niweśane |
ajñātā dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ satkṛtā wītamanyawaḥ ||12||

sā cintaye sadā putra brāhmaṇasyāsya kiṃ nwaham |
priyaṃ kuryāmiti gṛhe yatkuryuruṣitāḥ sukham ||13||

etāwānpuruṣastāta kṛtaṃ yasminna naśyati |
yāwacca kuryādanyo'sya kuryādabhyadhikaṃ tataḥ ||14||

tadidaṃ brāhmaṇasyāsya duḥkhamāpatitaṃ dhruwam |
tatrāsya yadi sāhāyyaṃ kuryāma sukṛtaṃ bhawet ||15||

bhīma uwāca||

jñāyatāmasya yadduḥkhaṃ yataścaiwa samutthitam |
widite wyawasiṣyāmi yadyapi syātsuduṣkaram ||16||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tathā hi kathayantau tau bhūyaḥ śuśruwatuḥ swanam |
ārtijaṃ tasya wiprasya sabhāryasya wiśāṃ pate ||17||

antaḥpuraṃ tatastasya brāhmaṇasya mahātmanaḥ |
wiweśa kuntī twaritā baddhawatsewa saurabhī ||18||

tatastaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tatra bhāryayā ca sutena ca |
duhitrā caiwa sahitaṃ dadarśa wikṛtānanam ||19||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

dhigidaṃ jīwitaṃ loke'nalasāramanarthakam |
duḥkhamūlaṃ parādhīnaṃ bhṛśamapriyabhāgi ca ||20||

jīwite paramaṃ duḥkhaṃ jīwite paramo jwaraḥ |
jīwite wartamānasya dwandwānāmāgamo dhruwaḥ ||21||

ekātmāpi hi dharmārthau kāmaṃ ca na niṣewate |
etaiśca wiprayogo'pi duḥkhaṃ paramakaṃ matam ||22||

āhuḥ kecitparaṃ mokṣaṃ sa ca nāsti kathañcana |
arthaprāptau ca narakaḥ kṛtsna ewopapadyate ||23||

arthepsutā paraṃ duḥkhamarthaprāptau tato'dhikam |
jātasnehasya cārtheṣu wiprayoge mahattaram ||24||

na hi yogaṃ prapaśyāmi yena mucyeyamāpadaḥ |
putradāreṇa wā sārdhaṃ prādraweyāmanāmayam ||25||

yatitaṃ wai mayā pūrwaṃ yathā twaṃ wettha brāhmaṇi |
yataḥ kṣemaṃ tato gantuṃ twayā tu mama na śrutam ||26||

iha jātā wiwṛddhāsmi pitā ceha mameti ca |
uktawatyasi durmedhe yācyamānā mayāsakṛt ||27||

swargato hi pitā wṛddhastathā mātā ciraṃ tawa |
bāndhawā bhūtapūrwāśca tatra wāse tu kā ratiḥ ||28||

so'yaṃ te bandhukāmāyā aśṛṇwantyā waco mama |
bandhupraṇāśaḥ samprāpto bhṛśaṃ duḥkhakaro mama ||29||

athawā madwināśo'yaṃ na hi śakṣyāmi kañcana |
parityaktumahaṃ bandhuṃ swayaṃ jīwannṛśaṃsawat ||30||

sahadharmacarīṃ dāntāṃ nityaṃ mātṛsamāṃ mama |
sakhāyaṃ wihitāṃ dewairnityaṃ paramikāṃ gatim ||31||

mātrā pitrā ca wihitāṃ sadā gārhasthyabhāginīm |
warayitwā yathānyāyaṃ mantrawatpariṇīya ca ||32||

kulīnāṃ śīlasampannāmapatyajananīṃ mama |
twāmahaṃ jīwitasyārthe sādhwīmanapakāriṇīm ||33||

parityaktuṃ na śakṣyāmi bhāryāṃ nityamanuwratām ||33||

kuta ewa parityaktuṃ sutāṃ śakṣyāmyahaṃ swayam |
bālāmaprāptawayasamajātawyañjanākṛtim ||34||

bharturarthāya nikṣiptāṃ nyāsaṃ dhātrā mahātmanā |
yasyāṃ dauhitrajāṃllokānāśaṃse pitṛbhiḥ saha ||35||

swayamutpādya tāṃ bālāṃ kathamutsraṣṭumutsahe ||35||

manyante kecidadhikaṃ snehaṃ putre piturnarāḥ |
kanyāyāṃ naiwa tu punarmama tulyāwubhau matau ||36||

yasmiṃllokāḥ prasūtiśca sthitā nityamatho sukham |
apāpāṃ tāmahaṃ bālāṃ kathamutsraṣṭumutsahe ||37||

ātmānamapi cotsṛjya tapsye pretawaśaṃ gataḥ |
tyaktā hyete mayā wyaktaṃ neha śakṣyanti jīwitum ||38||

eṣāṃ cānyatamatyāgo nṛśaṃso garhito budhaiḥ |
ātmatyāge kṛte ceme mariṣyanti mayā winā ||39||

sa kṛcchrāmahamāpanno na śaktastartumāpadam |
aho dhikkāṃ gatiṃ twadya gamiṣyāmi sabāndhawaḥ ||40||

sarwaiḥ saha mṛtaṃ śreyo na tu me jīwitaṃ kṣamam ||40||






                  146


brāhmaṇyuwāca||

na santāpastwayā kāryaḥ prākṛtenewa karhicit |
na hi santāpakālo'yaṃ waidyasya tawa widyate ||1||

awaśyaṃ nidhanaṃ sarwairgantawyamiha mānawaiḥ |
awaśyabhāwinyarthe wai santāpo neha widyate ||2||

bhāryā putro'tha duhitā sarwamātmārthamiṣyate |
wyathāṃ jahi subuddhyā twaṃ swayaṃ yāsyāmi tatra wai ||3||

etaddhi paramaṃ nāryāḥ kāryaṃ loke sanātanam |
prāṇānapi parityajya yadbhartṛhitamācaret ||4||

tacca tatra kṛtaṃ karma tawāpīha sukhāwaham |
bhawatyamutra cākṣayyaṃ loke'smiṃśca yaśaskaram ||5||

eṣa caiwa gururdharmo yaṃ prawakṣāmyahaṃ tawa |
arthaśca tawa dharmaśca bhūyānatra pradṛśyate ||6||

yadarthamiṣyate bhāryā prāptaḥ so'rthastwayā mayi |
kanyā caiwa kumāraśca kṛtāhamanṛṇā twayā ||7||

samarthaḥ poṣaṇe cāsi sutayo rakṣaṇe tathā |
na twahaṃ sutayoḥ śaktā tathā rakṣaṇapoṣaṇe ||8||

mama hi twadwihīnāyāḥ sarwakāmā na āpadaḥ |
kathaṃ syātāṃ sutau bālau bhaweyaṃ ca kathaṃ twaham ||9||

kathaṃ hi widhawānāthā bālaputrā winā twayā |
mithunaṃ jīwayiṣyāmi sthitā sādhugate pathi ||10||

ahaṅkṛtāwaliptaiśca prārthyamānāmimāṃ sutām |
ayuktaistawa sambandhe kathaṃ śakṣyāmi rakṣitum ||11||

utsṛṣṭamāmiṣaṃ bhūmau prārthayanti yathā khagāḥ |
prārthayanti janāḥ sarwe wīrahīnāṃ tathā striyam ||12||

sāhaṃ wicālyamānā wai prārthyamānā durātmabhiḥ |
sthātuṃ pathi na śakṣyāmi sajjaneṣṭe dwijottama ||13||

kathaṃ tawa kulasyaikāmimāṃ bālāmasaṃskṛtām |
pitṛpaitāmahe mārge niyoktumahamutsahe ||14||

kathaṃ śakṣyāmi bāle'sminguṇānādhātumīpṣitān |
anāthe sarwato lupte yathā twaṃ dharmadarśiwān ||15||

imāmapi ca te bālāmanāthāṃ paribhūya mām |
anarhāḥ prārthayiṣyanti śūdrā wedaśrutiṃ yathā ||16||

tāṃ cedahaṃ na ditseyaṃ twadguṇairupabṛṃhitām |
pramathyaināṃ hareyuste hawirdhwāṅkṣā iwādhwarāt ||17||

samprekṣamāṇā putraṃ te nānurūpamiwātmanaḥ |
anarhawaśamāpannāmimāṃ cāpi sutāṃ tawa ||18||

awajñātā ca lokasya tathātmānamajānatī |
awaliptairnarairbrahmanmariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ ||19||

tau wihīnau mayā bālau twayā caiwa mamātmajau |
winaśyetāṃ na saṃdeho matsyāwiwa jalakṣaye ||20||

tritayaṃ sarwathāpyewaṃ winaśiṣyatyasaṃśayam |
twayā wihīnaṃ tasmāttwaṃ māṃ parityaktumarhasi ||21||

wyuṣṭireṣā parā strīṇāṃ pūrwaṃ bhartuḥ parā gatiḥ |
na tu brāhmaṇa putrāṇāṃ wiṣaye pariwartitum ||22||

parityaktaḥ sutaścāyaṃ duhiteyaṃ tathā mayā |
bāndhawāśca parityaktāstwadarthaṃ jīwitaṃ ca me ||23||

yajñaistapobhirniyamairdānaiśca wiwidhaistathā |
wiśiṣyate striyā bharturnityaṃ priyahite sthitiḥ ||24||

tadidaṃ yaccikīrṣāmi dharmyaṃ paramasaṃmatam |
iṣṭaṃ caiwa hitaṃ caiwa tawa caiwa kulasya ca ||25||

iṣṭāni cāpyapatyāni drawyāṇi suhṛdaḥ priyāḥ |
āpaddharmawimokṣāya bhāryā cāpi satāṃ matam ||26||

ekato wā kulaṃ kṛtsnamātmā wā kulawardhana |
na samaṃ sarwameweti budhānāmeṣa niścayaḥ ||27||

sa kuruṣwa mayā kāryaṃ tārayātmānamātmanā |
anujānīhi māmārya sutau me parirakṣa ca ||28||

awadhyāḥ striya ityāhurdharmajñā dharmaniścaye |
dharmajñānrākṣasānāhurna hanyātsa ca māmapi ||29||

niḥsaṃśayo wadhaḥ puṃsāṃ strīṇāṃ saṃśayito wadhaḥ |
ato māmewa dharmajña prasthāpayitumarhasi ||30||

bhuktaṃ priyāṇyawāptāni dharmaśca carito mayā |
twatprasūtiḥ priyā prāptā na māṃ tapsyatyajīwitam ||31||

jātaputrā ca wṛddhā ca priyakāmā ca te sadā |
samīkṣyaitadahaṃ sarwaṃ wyawasāyaṃ karomyataḥ ||32||

utsṛjyāpi ca māmārya wetsyasyanyāmapi striyam |
tataḥ pratiṣṭhito dharmo bhawiṣyati punastawa ||33||

na cāpyadharmaḥ kalyāṇa bahupatnīkatā nṛṇām |
strīṇāmadharmaḥ sumahānbhartuḥ pūrwasya laṅghane ||34||

etatsarwaṃ samīkṣya twamātmatyāgaṃ ca garhitam |
ātmānaṃ tāraya mayā kulaṃ cemau ca dārakau ||35||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastayā bhartā tāṃ samāliṅgya bhārata |
mumoca bāṣpaṃ śanakaiḥ sabhāryo bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ ||36||






                  147


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tayorduḥkhitayorwākyamatimātraṃ niśamya tat |
bhṛśaṃ duḥkhaparītāṅgī kanyā tāwabhyabhāṣata ||1||

kimidaṃ bhṛśaduḥkhārtau rorawītho anāthawat |
mamāpi śrūyatāṃ kiñcicchrutwā ca kriyatāṃ kṣamam ||2||

dharmato'haṃ parityājyā yuwayornātra saṃśayaḥ |
tyaktawyāṃ māṃ parityajya trātaṃ sarwaṃ mayaikayā ||3||

ityarthamiṣyate'patyaṃ tārayiṣyati māmiti |
tasminnupasthite kāle tarataṃ plawawanmayā ||4||

iha wā tārayeddurgāduta wā pretya tārayet |
sarwathā tārayetputraḥ putra ityucyate budhaiḥ ||5||

ākāṅkṣante ca dauhitrānapi nityaṃ pitāmahāḥ |
tānswayaṃ wai paritrāsye rakṣantī jīwitaṃ pituḥ ||6||

bhrātā ca mama bālo'yaṃ gate lokamamuṃ twayi |
acireṇaiwa kālena winaśyeta na saṃśayaḥ ||7||

tāte'pi hi gate swargaṃ winaṣṭe ca mamānuje |
piṇḍaḥ pitṛṇāṃ wyucchidyettatteṣāmapriyaṃ bhawet ||8||

pitrā tyaktā tathā mātrā bhrātrā cāhamasaṃśayam |
duḥkhādduḥkhataraṃ prāpya mriyeyamatathocitā ||9||

twayi twaroge nirmukte mātā bhrātā ca me śiśuḥ |
santānaścaiwa piṇḍaśca pratiṣṭhāsyatyasaṃśayam ||10||

ātmā putraḥ sakhā bhāryā kṛcchraṃ tu duhitā kila |
sa kṛcchrānmocayātmānaṃ māṃ ca dharmeṇa yojaya ||11||

anāthā kṛpaṇā bālā yatrakwacanagāminī |
bhawiṣyāmi twayā tāta wihīnā kṛpaṇā bata ||12||

athawāhaṃ kariṣyāmi kulasyāsya wimokṣaṇam |
phalasaṃsthā bhawiṣyāmi kṛtwā karma suduṣkaram ||13||

athawā yāsyase tatra tyaktwā māṃ dwijasattama |
pīḍitāhaṃ bhawiṣyāmi tadawekṣaswa māmapi ||14||

tadasmadarthaṃ dharmārthaṃ prasawārthaṃ ca sattama |
ātmānaṃ parirakṣaswa tyaktawyāṃ māṃ ca santyaja ||15||

awaśyakaraṇīye'rthe mā twāṃ kālo'tyagādayam |
twayā dattena toyena bhawiṣyati hitaṃ ca me ||16||

kiṃ nwataḥ paramaṃ duḥkhaṃ yadwayaṃ swargate twayi |
yācamānāḥ parādannaṃ paridhāwemahi śwawat ||17||

twayi twaroge nirmukte kleśādasmātsabāndhawe |
amṛte wasatī loke bhawiṣyāmi sukhānwitā ||18||

ewaṃ bahuwidhaṃ tasyā niśamya paridewitam |
pitā mātā ca sā caiwa kanyā prarurudustrayaḥ ||19||

tataḥ praruditānsarwānniśamyātha sutastayoḥ |
utphullanayano bālaḥ kalamawyaktamabrawīt ||20||

mā rodīstāta mā mātarmā swasastwamiti bruwan |
prahasanniwa sarwāṃstānekaikaṃ so'pasarpati ||21||

tataḥ sa tṛṇamādāya prahṛṣṭaḥ punarabrawīt |
anena taṃ haniṣyāmi rākṣasaṃ puruṣādakam ||22||

tathāpi teṣāṃ duḥkhena parītānāṃ niśamya tat |
bālasya wākyamawyaktaṃ harṣaḥ samabhawanmahān ||23||

ayaṃ kāla iti jñātwā kuntī samupasṛtya tān |
gatāsūnamṛtenewa jīwayantīdamabrawīt ||24||






                  148


kuntyuwāca||

kutomūlamidaṃ duḥkhaṃ jñātumicchāmi tattwataḥ |
widitwā apakarṣeyaṃ śakyaṃ cedapakarṣitum ||1||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

upapannaṃ satāmetadyadbrawīṣi tapodhane |
na tu duḥkhamidaṃ śakyaṃ mānuṣeṇa wyapohitum ||2||

samīpe nagarasyāsya bako wasati rākṣasaḥ |
īśo janapadasyāsya purasya ca mahābalaḥ ||3||

puṣṭo mānuṣamāṃsena durbuddhiḥ puruṣādakaḥ |
rakṣatyasurarāṇnityamimaṃ janapadaṃ balī ||4||

nagaraṃ caiwa deśaṃ ca rakṣobalasamanwitaḥ |
tatkṛte paracakrācca bhūtebhyaśca na no bhayam ||5||

wetanaṃ tasya wihitaṃ śāliwāhasya bhojanam |
mahiṣau puruṣaścaiko yastadādāya gacchati ||6||

ekaikaścaiwa puruṣastatprayacchati bhojanam |
sa wāro bahubhirwarṣairbhawatyasutaro naraiḥ ||7||

tadwimokṣāya ye cāpi yatante puruṣāḥ kwacit |
saputradārāṃstānhatwā tadrakṣo bhakṣayatyuta ||8||

wetrakīyagṛhe rājā nāyaṃ nayamihāsthitaḥ |
anāmayaṃ janasyāsya yena syādadya śāśwatam ||9||

etadarhā wayaṃ nūnaṃ wasāmo durbalasya ye |
wiṣaye nityamudwignāḥ kurājānamupāśritāḥ ||10||

brāhmaṇāḥ kasya waktawyāḥ kasya wā chandacāriṇaḥ |
guṇairete hi wāsyante kāmagāḥ pakṣiṇo yathā ||11||

rājānaṃ prathamaṃ windettato bhāryāṃ tato dhanam |
trayasya sañcaye cāsya jñātīnputrāṃśca dhārayet ||12||

wiparītaṃ mayā cedaṃ trayaṃ sarwamupārjitam |
ta imāmāpadaṃ prāpya bhṛśaṃ tapsyāmahe wayam ||13||

so'yamasmānanuprāpto wāraḥ kulawināśanaḥ |
bhojanaṃ puruṣaścaikaḥ pradeyaṃ wetanaṃ mayā ||14||

na ca me widyate wittaṃ saṅkretuṃ puruṣaṃ kwacit |
suhṛjjanaṃ pradātuṃ ca na śakṣyāmi kathañcana ||15||

gatiṃ cāpi na paśyāmi tasmānmokṣāya rakṣasaḥ ||15||

so'haṃ duḥkhārṇawe magno mahatyasutare bhṛśam |
sahaiwaitairgamiṣyāmi bāndhawairadya rākṣasam ||16||

tato naḥ sahitankṣudraḥ sarwānewopabhokṣyati ||16||






                  149


kuntyuwāca||

na wiṣādastwayā kāryo bhayādasmātkathañcana |
upāyaḥ paridṛṣṭo'tra tasmānmokṣāya rakṣasaḥ ||1||

ekastawa suto bālaḥ kanyā caikā tapaswinī |
na te tayostathā patnyā gamanaṃ tatra rocaye ||2||

mama pañca sutā brahmaṃsteṣāmeko gamiṣyati |
twadarthaṃ balimādāya tasya pāpasya rakṣasaḥ ||3||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

nāhametatkariṣyāmi jīwitārthī kathañcana |
brāhmaṇasyātitheścaiwa swārthe prāṇairwiyojanam ||4||

na twetadakulīnāsu nādharmiṣṭhāsu widyate |
yadbrāhmaṇārthe wisṛjedātmānamapi cātmajam ||5||

ātmanastu mayā śreyo boddhawyamiti rocaye |
brahmawadhyātmawadhyā wā śreya ātmawadho mama ||6||

brahmawadhyā paraṃ pāpaṃ niṣkṛtirnātra widyate |
abuddhipūrwaṃ kṛtwāpi śreya ātmawadho mama ||7||

na twahaṃ wadhamākāṅkṣe swayamewātmanaḥ śubhe |
paraiḥ kṛte wadhe pāpaṃ na kiñcinmayi widyate ||8||

abhisandhikṛte tasminbrāhmaṇasya wadhe mayā |
niṣkṛtiṃ na prapaśyāmi nṛśaṃsaṃ kṣudramewa ca ||9||

āgatasya gṛhe tyāgastathaiwa śaraṇārthinaḥ |
yācamānasya ca wadho nṛśaṃsaṃ paramaṃ matam ||10||

kuryānna ninditaṃ karma na nṛśaṃsaṃ kadācana |
iti pūrwe mahātmāna āpaddharmawido widuḥ ||11||

śreyāṃstu sahadārasya wināśo'dya mama swayam |
brāhmaṇasya wadhaṃ nāhamanumaṃsye kathañcana ||12||

kuntyuwāca||

mamāpyeṣā matirbrahmanwiprā rakṣyā iti sthirā |
na cāpyaniṣṭaḥ putro me yadi putraśataṃ bhawet ||13||

na cāsau rākṣasaḥ śakto mama putrawināśane |
wīryawānmantrasiddhaśca tejaswī ca suto mama ||14||

rākṣasāya ca tatsarwaṃ prāpayiṣyati bhojanam |
mokṣayiṣyati cātmānamiti me niścitā matiḥ ||15||

samāgatāśca wīreṇa dṛṣṭapūrwāśca rākṣasāḥ |
balawanto mahākāyā nihatāścāpyanekaśaḥ ||16||

na twidaṃ keṣucidbrahmanwyāhartawyaṃ kathañcana |
widyārthino hi me putrānwiprakuryuḥ kutūhalāt ||17||

guruṇā cānanujñāto grāhayedyaṃ suto mama |
na sa kuryāttayā kāryaṃ widyayeti satāṃ matam ||18||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastu pṛthayā sa wipro bhāryayā saha |
hṛṣṭaḥ sampūjayāmāsa tadwākyamamṛtopamam ||19||

tataḥ kuntī ca wipraśca sahitāwanilātmajam |
tamabrūtāṃ kuruṣweti sa tathetyabrawīcca tau ||20||






                  150


waiśampāyana uwāca||

kariṣya iti bhīmena pratijñāte tu bhārata |
ājagmuste tataḥ sarwe bhaikṣamādāya pāṇḍawāḥ ||1||

ākāreṇaiwa taṃ jñātwā pāṇḍuputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
rahaḥ samupawiśyaikastataḥ papraccha mātaram ||2||

kiṃ cikīrṣatyayaṃ karma bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ |
bhawatyanumate kaccidayaṃ kartumihecchati ||3||

kuntyuwāca||

mamaiwa wacanādeṣa kariṣyati parantapaḥ |
brāhmaṇārthe mahatkṛtyaṃ moṣkāya nagarasya ca ||4||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

kimidaṃ sāhasaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ bhawatyā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam |
parityāgaṃ hi putrasya na praśaṃsanti sādhawaḥ ||5||

kathaṃ parasutasyārthe swasutaṃ tyaktumicchasi |
lokawṛttiwiruddhaṃ wai putratyāgātkṛtaṃ twayā ||6||

yasya bāhū samāśritya sukhaṃ sarwe swapāmahe |
rājyaṃ cāpahṛtaṃ kṣudrairājihīrṣāmahe punaḥ ||7||

yasya duryodhano wīryaṃ cintayannamitaujasaḥ |
na śete wasatīḥ sarwā duḥkhācchakuninā saha ||8||

yasya wīrasya wīryeṇa muktā jatugṛhādwayam |
anyebhyaścaiwa pāpebhyo nihataśca purocanaḥ ||9||

yasya wīryaṃ samāśritya wasupūrṇāṃ wasundharām |
imāṃ manyāmahe prāptāṃ nihatya dhṛtarāṣṭrajān ||10||

tasya wyawasitastyāgo buddhimāsthāya kāṃ twayā |
kaccinna duḥkhairbuddhiste wiplutā gatacetasaḥ ||11||

kuntyuwāca||

yudhiṣṭhira na santāpaḥ kāryaḥ prati wṛkodaram |
na cāyaṃ buddhidaurbalyādwyawasāyaḥ kṛto mayā ||12||

iha wiprasya bhawane wayaṃ putra sukhoṣitāḥ |
tasya pratikriyā tāta mayeyaṃ prasamīkṣitā ||13||

etāwānewa puruṣaḥ kṛtaṃ yasminna naśyati ||13||

dṛṣṭwā bhīṣmasya wikrāntaṃ tadā jatugṛhe mahat |
hiḍimbasya wadhāccaiwa wiśwāso me wṛkodare ||14||

bāhworbalaṃ hi bhīmasya nāgāyutasamaṃ mahat |
yena yūyaṃ gajaprakhyā nirwyūḍhā wāraṇāwatāt ||15||

wṛkodarabalo nānyo na bhūto na bhawiṣyati |
yo'bhyudīyādyudhi śreṣṭhamapi wajradharaṃ swayam ||16||

jātamātraḥ purā caiṣa mamāṅkātpatito girau |
śarīragaurawāttasya śilā gātrairwicūrṇitā ||17||

tadahaṃ prajñayā smṛtwā balaṃ bhīmasya pāṇḍawa |
pratīkāraṃ ca wiprasya tataḥ kṛtawatī matim ||18||

nedaṃ lobhānna cājñānānna ca mohādwiniścitam |
buddhipūrwaṃ tu dharmasya wyawasāyaḥ kṛto mayā ||19||

arthau dwāwapi niṣpannau yudhiṣṭhira bhawiṣyataḥ |
pratīkāraśca wāsasya dharmaśca carito mahān ||20||

yo brāhmaṇasya sāhāyyaṃ kuryādartheṣu karhicit |
kṣatriyaḥ sa śubhāṃllokānprāpnuyāditi me śrutam ||21||

kṣatriyaḥ kṣatriyasyaiwa kurwāṇo wadhamokṣaṇam |
wipulāṃ kīrtimāpnoti loke'smiṃśca paratra ca ||22||

waiśyasyaiwa tu sāhāyyaṃ kurwāṇaḥ kṣatriyo yudhi |
sa sarweṣwapi lokeṣu prajā rañjayate dhruwam ||23||

śūdraṃ tu mokṣayanrājā śaraṇārthinamāgatam |
prāpnotīha kule janma sadrawye rājasatkṛte ||24||

ewaṃ sa bhagawānwyāsaḥ purā kaurawanandana |
prowāca sutarāṃ prājñastasmādetaccikīrṣitam ||25||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

upapannamidaṃ mātastwayā yadbuddhipūrwakam |
ārtasya brāhmaṇasyaiwamanukrośādidaṃ kṛtam ||26||

dhruwameṣyati bhīmo'yaṃ nihatya puruṣādakam ||26||

yathā twidaṃ na windeyurnarā nagarawāsinaḥ |
tathāyaṃ brāhmaṇo wācyaḥ parigrāhyaśca yatnataḥ ||27||






                  151


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato rātryāṃ wyatītāyāmannamādāya pāṇḍawaḥ |
bhīmaseno yayau tatra yatrāsau puruṣādakaḥ ||1||

āsādya tu wanaṃ tasya rakṣasaḥ pāṇḍawo balī |
ājuhāwa tato nāmnā tadannamupayojayan ||2||

tataḥ sa rākṣasaḥ śrutwā bhīmasenasya tadwacaḥ |
ājagāma susaṅkruddho yatra bhīmo wyawasthitaḥ ||3||

mahākāyo mahāwego dārayanniwa medinīm |
triśikhāṃ bhṛkuṭiṃ kṛtwā saṃdaśya daśanacchadam ||4||

bhuñjānamannaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭwā bhīmasenaṃ sa rākṣasaḥ |
wiwṛtya nayane kruddha idaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||5||

ko'yamannamidaṃ bhuṅkte madarthamupakalpitam |
paśyato mama durbuddhiryiyāsuryamasādanam ||6||

bhīmasenastu tacchrutwā prahasanniwa bhārata |
rākṣasaṃ tamanādṛtya bhuṅkta ewa parāṅmukhaḥ ||7||

tataḥ sa bhairawaṃ kṛtwā samudyamya karāwubhau |
abhyadrawadbhīmasenaṃ jighāṃsuḥ puruṣādakaḥ ||8||

tathāpi paribhūyainaṃ nekṣamāṇo wṛkodaraḥ |
rākṣasaṃ bhuṅkta ewānnaṃ pāṇḍawaḥ parawīrahā ||9||

amarṣeṇa tu sampūrṇaḥ kuntīputrasya rākṣasaḥ |
jaghāna pṛṣṭhaṃ pāṇibhyāmubhābhyāṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ sthitaḥ ||10||

tathā balawatā bhīmaḥ pāṇibhyāṃ bhṛśamāhataḥ |
naiwāwalokayāmāsa rākṣasaṃ bhuṅkta ewa saḥ ||11||

tataḥ sa bhūyaḥ saṅkruddho wṛkṣamādāya rākṣasaḥ |
tāḍayiṣyaṃstadā bhīmaṃ punarabhyadrawadbalī ||12||

tato bhīmaḥ śanairbhuktwā tadannaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ |
wāryupaspṛśya saṃhṛṣṭastasthau yudhi mahābalaḥ ||13||

kṣiptaṃ kruddhena taṃ wṛkṣaṃ pratijagrāha wīryawān |
sawyena pāṇinā bhīmaḥ prahasanniwa bhārata ||14||

tataḥ sa punarudyamya wṛkṣānbahuwidhānbalī |
prāhiṇodbhīmasenāya tasmai bhīmaśca pāṇḍawaḥ ||15||

tadwṛkṣayuddhamabhawanmahīruhawināśanam |
ghorarūpaṃ mahārāja bakapāṇḍawayormahat ||16||

nāma wiśrāwya tu bakaḥ samabhidrutya pāṇḍawam |
bhujābhyāṃ parijagrāha bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam ||17||

bhīmaseno'pi tadrakṣaḥ parirabhya mahābhujaḥ |
wisphurantaṃ mahāwegaṃ wicakarṣa balādbalī ||18||

sa kṛṣyamāṇo bhīmena karṣamāṇaśca pāṇḍawam |
samayujyata tīwreṇa śrameṇa puruṣādakaḥ ||19||

tayorwegena mahatā pṛthiwī samakampata |
pādapāṃśca mahākāyāṃścūrṇayāmāsatustadā ||20||

hīyamānaṃ tu tadrakṣaḥ samīkṣya bharatarṣabha |
niṣpiṣya bhūmau pāṇibhyāṃ samājaghne wṛkodaraḥ ||21||

tato'sya jānunā pṛṣṭhamawapīḍya balādiwa |
bāhunā parijagrāha dakṣiṇena śirodharām ||22||

sawyena ca kaṭīdeśe gṛhya wāsasi pāṇḍawaḥ |
tadrakṣo dwiguṇaṃ cakre nadantaṃ bhairawānrawān ||23||

tato'sya rudhiraṃ waktrātprādurāsīdwiśāṃ pate |
bhajyamānasya bhīmena tasya ghorasya rakṣasaḥ ||24||






                  152


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tena śabdena witrasto janastasyātha rakṣasaḥ |
niṣpapāta gṛhādrājansahaiwa paricāribhiḥ ||1||

tānbhītānwigatajñānānbhīmaḥ praharatāṃ waraḥ |
sāntwayāmāsa balawānsamaye ca nyaweśayat ||2||

na hiṃsyā mānuṣā bhūyo yuṣmābhiriha karhicit |
hiṃsatāṃ hi wadhaḥ śīghramewamewa bhawediti ||3||

tasya tadwacanaṃ śrutwā tāni rakṣāṃsi bhārata |
ewamastwiti taṃ prāhurjagṛhuḥ samayaṃ ca tam ||4||

tataḥ prabhṛti rakṣāṃsi tatra saumyāni bhārata |
nagare pratyadṛśyanta narairnagarawāsibhiḥ ||5||

tato bhimastamādāya gatāsuṃ puruṣādakam |
dwāradeśe winikṣipya jagāmānupalakṣitaḥ ||6||

tataḥ sa bhīmastaṃ hatwā gatwā brāhmaṇaweśma tat |
ācacakṣe yathāwṛttaṃ rājñaḥ sarwamaśeṣataḥ ||7||

tato narā winiṣkrāntā nagarātkālyamewa tu |
dadṛśurnihataṃ bhūmau rākṣasaṃ rudhirokṣitam ||8||

tamadrikūṭasadṛśaṃ winikīrṇaṃ bhayāwaham |
ekacakrāṃ tato gatwā prawṛttiṃ pradaduḥ pare ||9||

tataḥ sahasraśo rājannarā nagarawāsinaḥ |
tatrājagmurbakaṃ draṣṭuṃ sastrīwṛddhakumārakāḥ ||10||

tataste wismitāḥ sarwe karma dṛṣṭwātimānuṣam |
daiwatānyarcayāṃ cakruḥ sarwa ewa wiśāṃ pate ||11||

tataḥ pragaṇayāmāsuḥ kasya wāro'dya bhojane |
jñātwā cāgamya taṃ wipraṃ papracchuḥ sarwa ewa tat ||12||

ewaṃ pṛṣṭastu bahuśo rakṣamāṇaśca pāṇḍawān |
uwāca nāgarānsarwānidaṃ wiprarṣabhastadā ||13||

ājñāpitaṃ māmaśane rudantaṃ saha bandhubhiḥ |
dadarśa brāhmaṇaḥ kaścinmantrasiddho mahābalaḥ ||14||

paripṛcchya sa māṃ pūrwaṃ parikleśaṃ purasya ca |
abrawīdbrāhmaṇaśreṣṭha āśwāsya prahasanniwa ||15||

prāpayiṣyāmyahaṃ tasmai idamannaṃ durātmane |
mannimittaṃ bhayaṃ cāpi na kāryamiti wīryawān ||16||

sa tadannamupādāya gato bakawanaṃ prati |
tena nūnaṃ bhawedetatkarma lokahitaṃ kṛtam ||17||

tataste brāhmaṇāḥ sarwe kṣatriyāśca suwismitāḥ |
waiśyāḥ śūdrāśca muditāścakrurbrahmamahaṃ tadā ||18||

tato jānapadāḥ sarwe ājagmurnagaraṃ prati |
tadadbhutatamaṃ draṣṭuṃ pārthāstatraiwa cāwasan ||19||






              caitrarathaparwa
                  153


janamejaya uwāca||

te tathā puruṣawyāghrā nihatya bakarākṣasam |
