ata ūrdhwaṃ tato brahmankimakurwata pāṇḍawāḥ ||1||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tatraiwa nyawasanrājannihatya bakarākṣasam |
adhīyānāḥ paraṃ brahma brāhmaṇasya niweśane ||2||

tataḥ katipayāhasya brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśitawrataḥ |
pratiśrayārthaṃ tadweśma brāhmaṇasyājagāma ha ||3||

sa samyakpūjayitwā taṃ widwānwiprarṣabhastadā |
dadau pratiśrayaṃ tasmai sadā sarwātithiwratī ||4||

tataste pāṇḍawāḥ sarwe saha kuntyā nararṣabhāḥ |
upāsāṃ cakrire wipraṃ kathayānaṃ kathāstadā ||5||

kathayāmāsa deśānsa tīrthāni wiwidhāni ca |
rājñāṃ ca wiwidhāścaryāḥ purāṇi wiwidhāni ca ||6||

sa tatrākathayadwipraḥ kathānte janamejaya |
pāñcāleṣwadbhutākāraṃ yājñasenyāḥ swayaṃwaram ||7||

dhṛṣṭadyumnasya cotpattimutpattiṃ ca śikhaṇḍinaḥ |
ayonijatwaṃ kṛṣṇāyā drupadasya mahāmakhe ||8||

tadadbhutatamaṃ śrutwā loke tasya mahātmanaḥ |
wistareṇaiwa papracchuḥ kathāṃ tāṃ puruṣarṣabhāḥ ||9||

kathaṃ drupadaputrasya dhṛṣṭadyumnasya pāwakāt |
wedimadhyācca kṛṣṇāyāḥ sambhawaḥ kathamadbhutaḥ ||10||

kathaṃ droṇānmaheṣwāsātsarwāṇyastrāṇyaśikṣata |
kathaṃ priyasakhāyau tau bhinnau kasya kṛtena ca ||11||

ewaṃ taiścodito rājansa wipraḥ puruṣarṣabhaiḥ |
kathayāmāsa tatsarwaṃ draupadīsambhawaṃ tadā ||12||






                  154


brāhmaṇa uwāca||

gaṅgādwāraṃ prati mahānbabhūwarṣirmahātapāḥ |
bharadwājo mahāprājñaḥ satataṃ saṃśitawrataḥ ||1||

so'bhiṣektuṃ gato gaṅgāṃ pūrwamewāgatāṃ satīm |
dadarśāpsarasaṃ tatra ghṛtācīmāplutāmṛṣiḥ ||2||

tasyā wāyurnadītīre wasanaṃ wyaharattadā |
apakṛṣṭāmbarāṃ dṛṣṭwā tāmṛṣiścakame tataḥ ||3||

tasyāṃ saṃsaktamanasaḥ kaumārabrahmacāriṇaḥ |
hṛṣṭasya retaścaskanda tadṛṣirdroṇa ādadhe ||4||

tataḥ samabhawaddroṇaḥ kumārastasya dhīmataḥ |
adhyagīṣṭa sa wedāṃśca wedāṅgāni ca sarwaśaḥ ||5||

bharadwājasya tu sakhā pṛṣato nāma pārthiwaḥ |
tasyāpi drupado nāma tadā samabhawatsutaḥ ||6||

sa nityamāśramaṃ gatwā droṇena saha pārṣataḥ |
cikrīḍādhyayanaṃ caiwa cakāra kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ ||7||

tatastu pṛṣate'tīte sa rājā drupado'bhawat |
droṇo'pi rāmaṃ śuśrāwa ditsantaṃ wasu sarwaśaḥ ||8||

wanaṃ tu prasthitaṃ rāmaṃ bharadwājasuto'brawīt |
āgataṃ wittakāmaṃ māṃ widdhi droṇaṃ dwijarṣabha ||9||

rāma uwāca||

śarīramātramewādya mayedamawaśeṣitam |
astrāṇi wā śarīraṃ wā brahmannanyataraṃ wṛṇu ||10||

droṇa uwāca||

astrāṇi caiwa sarwāṇi teṣāṃ saṃhāramewa ca |
prayogaṃ caiwa sarweṣāṃ dātumarhati me bhawān ||11||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

tathetyuktwā tatastasmai pradadau bhṛgunandanaḥ |
pratigṛhya tato droṇaḥ kṛtakṛtyo'bhawattadā ||12||

samprahṛṣṭamanāścāpi rāmātparamasaṃmatam |
brahmāstraṃ samanuprāpya nareṣwabhyadhiko'bhawat ||13||

tato drupadamāsādya bhāradwājaḥ pratāpawān |
abrawītpuruṣawyāghraḥ sakhāyaṃ widdhi māmiti ||14||

drupada uwāca||

nāśrotriyaḥ śrotriyasya nārathī rathinaḥ sakhā |
nārājā pārthiwasyāpi sakhipūrwaṃ kimiṣyate ||15||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

sa winiścitya manasā pāñcālyaṃ prati buddhimān |
jagāma kurumukhyānāṃ nagaraṃ nāgasāhwayam ||16||

tasmai pautrānsamādāya wasūni wiwidhāni ca |
prāptāya pradadau bhīṣmaḥ śiṣyāndroṇāya dhīmate ||17||

droṇaḥ śiṣyāṃstataḥ sarwānidaṃ wacanamabrawīt |
samānīya tadā widwāndrupadasyāsukhāya wai ||18||

ācāryawetanaṃ kiñciddhṛdi sampariwartate |
kṛtāstraistatpradeyaṃ syāttadṛtaṃ wadatānaghāḥ ||19||

yadā ca pāṇḍawāḥ sarwe kṛtāstrāḥ kṛtaniśramāḥ |
tato droṇo'brawīdbhūyo wetanārthamidaṃ wacaḥ ||20||

pārṣato drupado nāma chatrawatyāṃ nareśwaraḥ |
tasyāpakṛṣya tadrājyaṃ mama śīghraṃ pradīyatām ||21||

tataḥ pāṇḍusutāḥ pañca nirjitya drupadaṃ yudhi |
droṇāya darśayāmāsurbaddhwā sasaciwaṃ tadā ||22||

droṇa uwāca||

prārthayāmi twayā sakhyaṃ punarewa narādhipa |
arājā kila no rājñaḥ sakhā bhawitumarhati ||23||

ataḥ prayatitaṃ rājye yajñasena mayā tawa |
rājāsi dakṣiṇe kūle bhāgīrathyāhamuttare ||24||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

asatkāraḥ sa sumahānmuhūrtamapi tasya tu |
na wyeti hṛdayādrājño durmanāḥ sa kṛśo'bhawat ||25||






                  155


brāhmaṇa uwāca||

amarṣī drupado rājā karmasiddhāndwijarṣabhān |
anwicchanparicakrāma brāhmaṇāwasathānbahūn ||1||

putrajanma parīpsanwai śokopahatacetanaḥ |
nāsti śreṣṭhaṃ mamāpatyamiti nityamacintayat ||2||

jātānputrānsa nirwedāddhigbandhūniti cābrawīt |
niḥśwāsaparamaścāsīddroṇaṃ praticikīrṣayā ||3||

prabhāwaṃ winayaṃ śikṣāṃ droṇasya caritāni ca |
kṣātreṇa ca balenāsya cintayannānwapadyata ||4||

pratikartuṃ nṛpaśreṣṭho yatamāno'pi bhārata ||4||

abhitaḥ so'tha kalmāṣīṃ gaṅgākūle paribhraman |
brāhmaṇāwasathaṃ puṇyamāsasāda mahīpatiḥ ||5||

tatra nāsnātakaḥ kaścinna cāsīdawratī dwijaḥ |
tathaiwa nāmahābhāgaḥ so'paśyatsaṃśitawratau ||6||

yājopayājau brahmarṣī śāmyantau pṛṣatātmajaḥ |
saṃhitādhyayane yuktau gotrataścāpi kāśyapau ||7||

tāraṇe yuktarūpau tau brāhmaṇāwṛṣisattamau |
sa tāwāmantrayāmāsa sarwakāmairatandritaḥ ||8||

buddhwā tayorbalaṃ buddhiṃ kanīyāṃsamupahware |
prapede chandayankāmairupayājaṃ dhṛtawratam ||9||

pādaśuśrūṣaṇe yuktaḥ priyawāksarwakāmadaḥ |
arhayitwā yathānyāyamupayājamuwāca saḥ ||10||

yena me karmaṇā brahmanputraḥ syāddroṇamṛtyawe |
upayāja kṛte tasmingawāṃ dātāsmi te'rbudam ||11||

yadwā te'nyaddwijaśreṣṭha manasaḥ supriyaṃ bhawet |
sarwaṃ tatte pradātāhaṃ na hi me'styatra saṃśayaḥ ||12||

ityukto nāhamityewaṃ tamṛṣiḥ pratyuwāca ha |
ārādhayiṣyandrupadaḥ sa taṃ paryacaratpunaḥ ||13||

tataḥ saṃwatsarasyānte drupadaṃ sa dwijottamaḥ |
upayājo'brawīdrājankāle madhurayā girā ||14||

jyeṣṭho bhrātā mamāgṛhṇādwicaranwananirjhare |
aparijñātaśaucāyāṃ bhūmau nipatitaṃ phalam ||15||

tadapaśyamahaṃ bhrāturasāmpratamanuwrajan |
wimarśaṃ saṅkarādāne nāyaṃ kuryātkathañcana ||16||

dṛṣṭwā phalasya nāpaśyaddoṣā ye'syānubandhikāḥ |
wiwinakti na śaucaṃ yaḥ so'nyatrāpi kathaṃ bhawet ||17||

saṃhitādhyayanaṃ kurwanwasangurukule ca yaḥ |
bhaikṣamucchiṣṭamanyeṣāṃ bhuṅkte cāpi sadā sadā ||18||

kīrtayanguṇamannānāmaghṛṇī ca punaḥ punaḥ ||18||

tamahaṃ phalārthinaṃ manye bhrātaraṃ tarkacakṣuṣā |
taṃ wai gacchaswa nṛpate sa twāṃ saṃyājayiṣyati ||19||

jugupsamāno nṛpatirmanasedaṃ wicintayan |
upayājawacaḥ śrutwā nṛpatiḥ sarwadharmawit ||20||

abhisampūjya pūjārhamṛṣiṃ yājamuwāca ha ||20||

ayutāni dadānyaṣṭau gawāṃ yājaya māṃ wibho |
droṇawairābhisantaptaṃ twaṃ hlādayitumarhasi ||21||

sa hi brahmawidāṃ śreṣṭho brahmāstre cāpyanuttamaḥ |
tasmāddroṇaḥ parājaiṣīnmāṃ wai sa sakhiwigrahe ||22||

kṣatriyo nāsti tulyo'sya pṛthiwyāṃ kaścidagraṇīḥ |
kaurawācāryamukhyasya bhāradwājasya dhīmataḥ ||23||

droṇasya śarajālāni prāṇidehaharāṇi ca |
ṣaḍaratni dhanuścāsya dṛśyate'pratimaṃ mahat ||24||

sa hi brāhmaṇawegena kṣātraṃ wegamasaṃśayam |
pratihanti maheṣwāso bhāradwājo mahāmanāḥ ||25||

kṣatrocchedāya wihito jāmadagnya iwāsthitaḥ |
tasya hyastrabalaṃ ghoramaprasahyaṃ narairbhuwi ||26||

brāhmamuccārayaṃstejo hutāhutiriwānalaḥ |
sametya sa dahatyājau kṣatraṃ brahmapuraḥsaraḥ ||27||

brahmakṣatre ca wihite brahmatejo wiśiṣyate ||27||

so'haṃ kṣatrabalāddhīno brahmatejaḥ prapediwān |
droṇādwiśiṣṭamāsādya bhawantaṃ brahmawittamam ||28||

droṇāntakamahaṃ putraṃ labheyaṃ yudhi durjayam |
tatkarma kuru me yāja nirwapāmyarbudaṃ gawām ||29||

tathetyuktwā tu taṃ yājo yājyārthamupakalpayat |
gurwartha iti cākāmamupayājamacodayat ||30||

yājo droṇawināśāya pratijajñe tathā ca saḥ ||30||

tatastasya narendrasya upayājo mahātapāḥ |
ācakhyau karma waitānaṃ tadā putraphalāya wai ||31||

sa ca putro mahāwīryo mahātejā mahābalaḥ |
iṣyate yadwidho rājanbhawitā te tathāwidhaḥ ||32||

bhāradwājasya hantāraṃ so'bhisandhāya bhūmipaḥ |
ājahre tattathā sarwaṃ drupadaḥ karmasiddhaye ||33||

yājastu hawanasyānte dewīmāhwāpayattadā |
praihi māṃ rājñi pṛṣati mithunaṃ twāmupasthitam ||34||

dewyuwāca||

awaliptaṃ me mukhaṃ brahmanpuṇyāngandhānbibharmi ca |
sutārthenoparuddhāsmi tiṣṭha yāja mama priye ||35||

yāja uwāca||

yājena śrapitaṃ hawyamupayājena mantritam |
kathaṃ kāmaṃ na saṃdadhyātsā twaṃ wipraihi tiṣṭha wā ||36||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

ewamukte tu yājena hute hawiṣi saṃskṛte |
uttasthau pāwakāttasmātkumāro dewasaṃnibhaḥ ||37||

jwālāwarṇo ghorarūpaḥ kirīṭī warma cottamam |
bibhratsakhaḍgaḥ saśaro dhanuṣmānwinadanmuhuḥ ||38||

so'dhyārohadrathawaraṃ tena ca prayayau tadā |
tataḥ praṇeduḥ pāñcālāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ sādhu sādhwiti ||39||

bhayāpaho rājaputraḥ pāñcālānāṃ yaśaskaraḥ |
rājñaḥ śokāpaho jāta eṣa droṇawadhāya wai ||40||

ityuwāca mahadbhūtamadṛśyaṃ khecaraṃ tadā ||40||

kumārī cāpi pāñcālī wedimadhyātsamutthitā |
subhagā darśanīyāṅgī wedimadhyā manoramā ||41||

śyāmā padmapalāśākṣī nīlakuñcitamūrdhajā |
mānuṣaṃ wigrahaṃ kṛtwā sākṣādamarawarṇinī ||42||

nīlotpalasamo gandho yasyāḥ krośātprawāyati |
yā bibharti paraṃ rūpaṃ yasyā nāstyupamā bhuwi ||43||

tāṃ cāpi jātāṃ suśroṇīṃ wāguwācāśarīriṇī |
sarwayoṣidwarā kṛṣṇā kṣayaṃ kṣatraṃ ninīṣati ||44||

surakāryamiyaṃ kāle kariṣyati sumadhyamā |
asyā hetoḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahadutpatsyate bhayam ||45||

tacchrutwā sarwapāñcālāḥ praṇeduḥ siṃhasaṅghawat |
na caitānharṣasampūṇāniyaṃ sehe wasundharā ||46||

tau dṛṣṭwā pṛṣatī yājaṃ prapede wai sutārthinī |
na wai madanyāṃ jananīṃ jānīyātāmimāwiti ||47||

tathetyuwāca tāṃ yājo rājñaḥ priyacikīrṣayā |
tayośca nāmanī cakrurdwijāḥ sampūrṇamānasāḥ ||48||

dhṛṣṭatwādatidhṛṣṇutwāddharmāddyutsambhawādapi |
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kumāro'yaṃ drupadasya bhawatwiti ||49||

kṛṣṇetyewābruwankṛṣṇāṃ kṛṣṇābhūtsā hi warṇataḥ |
tathā tanmithunaṃ jajñe drupadasya mahāmakhe ||50||

dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tu pāñcālyamānīya swaṃ wiweśanam |
upākarodastrahetorbhāradwājaḥ pratāpawān ||51||

amokṣaṇīyaṃ daiwaṃ hi bhāwi matwā mahāmatiḥ |
tathā tatkṛtawāndroṇa ātmakīrtyanurakṣaṇāt ||52||






                  156


waiśampāyana uwāca||

etacchrutwā tu kaunteyāḥ śalyawiddhā iwābhawan |
sarwe cāswasthamanaso babhūwuste mahārathāḥ ||1||

tataḥ kuntī sutāndṛṣṭwā wibhrāntāngatacetasaḥ |
yudhiṣṭhiramuwācedaṃ wacanaṃ satyawādinī ||2||

cirarātroṣitāḥ smeha brāhmaṇasya niweśane |
ramamāṇāḥ pure ramye labdhabhaikṣā yudhiṣṭhira ||3||

yānīha ramaṇīyāni wanānyupawanāni ca |
sarwāṇi tāni dṛṣṭāni punaḥ punarariṃdama ||4||

punardṛṣṭāni tānyewa prīṇayanti na nastathā |
bhaikṣaṃ ca na tathā wīra labhyate kurunandana ||5||

te wayaṃ sādhu pāñcālāngacchāma yadi manyase |
apūrwadarśanaṃ tāta ramaṇīyaṃ bhawiṣyati ||6||

subhikṣāścaiwa pāñcālāḥ śrūyante śatrukarśana |
yajñasenaśca rājāsau brahmaṇya iti śuśrumaḥ ||7||

ekatra cirawāso hi kṣamo na ca mato mama |
te tatra sādhu gacchāmo yadi twaṃ putra manyase ||8||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

bhawatyā yanmataṃ kāryaṃ tadasmākaṃ paraṃ hitam |
anujāṃstu na jānāmi gaccheyurneti wā punaḥ ||9||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ kuntī bhīmasenamarjunaṃ yamajau tathā |
uwāca gamanaṃ te ca tathetyewābruwaṃstadā ||10||

tata āmantrya taṃ wipraṃ kuntī rājansutaiḥ saha |
pratasthe nagarīṃ ramyāṃ drupadasya mahātmanaḥ ||11||






                  157


waiśampāyana uwāca||

wasatsu teṣu pracchannaṃ pāṇḍaweṣu mahātmasu |
ājagāmātha tāndraṣṭuṃ wyāsaḥ satyawatīsutaḥ ||1||

tamāgatamabhiprekṣya pratyudgamya parantapāḥ |
praṇipatyābhiwādyainaṃ tasthuḥ prāñjalayastadā ||2||

samanujñāpya tānsarwānāsīnānmunirabrawīt |
prasannaḥ pūjitaḥ pārthaiḥ prītipūrwamidaṃ wacaḥ ||3||

api dharmeṇa wartadhwaṃ śāstreṇa ca parantapāḥ |
api wipreṣu waḥ pūjā pūjārheṣu na hīyate ||4||

atha dharmārthawadwākyamuktwā sa bhagawānṛṣiḥ |
wicitrāśca kathāstāstāḥ punarewedamabrawīt ||5||

āsīttapowane kācidṛṣeḥ kanyā mahātmanaḥ |
wilagnamadhyā suśroṇī subhrūḥ sarwaguṇānwitā ||6||

karmabhiḥ swakṛtaiḥ sā tu durbhagā samapadyata |
nādhyagacchatpatiṃ sā tu kanyā rūpawatī satī ||7||

tapastaptumathārebhe patyarthamasukhā tataḥ |
toṣayāmāsa tapasā sā kilogreṇa śaṅkaram ||8||

tasyāḥ sa bhagawāṃstuṣṭastāmuwāca tapaswinīm |
waraṃ waraya bhadraṃ te warado'smīti bhāmini ||9||

atheśwaramuwācedamātmanaḥ sā waco hitam |
patiṃ sarwaguṇopetamicchāmīti punaḥ punaḥ ||10||

tāmatha pratyuwācedamīśāno wadatāṃ waraḥ |
pañca te patayo bhadre bhawiṣyantīti śaṅkaraḥ ||11||

pratibruwantīmekaṃ me patiṃ dehīti śaṅkaram |
punarewābrawīddewa idaṃ wacanamuttamam ||12||

pañcakṛtwastwayā uktaḥ patiṃ dehītyahaṃ punaḥ |
dehamanyaṃ gatāyāste yathoktaṃ tadbhawiṣyati ||13||

drupadasya kule jātā kanyā sā dewarūpiṇī |
nirdiṣṭā bhawatāṃ patnī kṛṣṇā pārṣatyaninditā ||14||

pāñcālanagaraṃ tasmātprawiśadhwaṃ mahābalāḥ |
sukhinastāmanuprāpya bhawiṣyatha na saṃśayaḥ ||15||

ewamuktwā mahābhāgaḥ pāṇḍawānāṃ pitāmahaḥ |
pārthānāmantrya kuntīṃ ca prātiṣṭhata mahātapāḥ ||16||






                  158


waiśampāyana uwāca||

te pratasthuḥ puraskṛtya mātaraṃ puruṣarṣabhāḥ |
samairudaṅmukhairmārgairyathoddiṣṭaṃ parantapāḥ ||1||

te gacchantastwahorātraṃ tīrthaṃ somaśrawāyaṇam |
āseduḥ puruṣawyāghrā gaṅgāyāṃ pāṇḍunandanāḥ ||2||

ulmukaṃ tu samudyamya teṣāmagre dhanañjayaḥ |
prakāśārthaṃ yayau tatra rakṣārthaṃ ca mahāyaśāḥ ||3||

tatra gaṅgājale ramye wiwikte krīḍayanstriyaḥ |
īrṣyurgandharwarājaḥ sma jalakrīḍāmupāgataḥ ||4||

śabdaṃ teṣāṃ sa śuśrāwa nadīṃ samupasarpatām |
tena śabdena cāwiṣṭaścukrodha balawadbalī ||5||

sa dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍawāṃstatra saha mātrā parantapān |
wisphārayandhanurghoramidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||6||

sandhyā saṃrajyate ghorā pūrwarātrāgameṣu yā |
aśītibhistruṭairhīnaṃ taṃ muhūrtaṃ pracakṣate ||7||

wihitaṃ kāmacārāṇāṃ yakṣagandharwarakṣasām |
śeṣamanyanmanuṣyāṇāṃ kāmacāramiha smṛtam ||8||

lobhātpracāraṃ caratastāsu welāsu wai narān |
upakrāntā nigṛhṇīmo rākṣasaiḥ saha bāliśān ||9||

tato rātrau prāpnuwato jalaṃ brahmawido janāḥ |
garhayanti narānsarwānbalasthānnṛpatīnapi ||10||

ārāttiṣṭhata mā mahyaṃ samīpamupasarpata |
kasmānmāṃ nābhijānīta prāptaṃ bhāgīrathījalam ||11||

aṅgāraparṇaṃ gandharwaṃ witta māṃ swabalāśrayam |
ahaṃ hi mānī cerṣyuśca kuberasya priyaḥ sakhā ||12||

aṅgāraparṇamiti ca khyataṃ wanamidaṃ mama |
anu gaṅgāṃ ca wākāṃ ca citraṃ yatra wasāmyaham ||13||

na kuṇapāḥ śṛṅgiṇo wā na dewā na ca mānuṣāḥ |
idaṃ samupasarpanti tatkiṃ samupasarpatha ||14||

arjuna uwāca||

samudre himawatpārśwe nadyāmasyāṃ ca durmate |
rātrāwahani sandhau ca kasya kḷptaḥ parigrahaḥ ||15||

wayaṃ ca śaktisampannā akāle twāmadhṛṣṇumaḥ |
aśaktā hi kṣaṇe krūre yuṣmānarcanti mānawāḥ ||16||

purā himawataścaiṣā hemaśṛṅgādwiniḥsṛtā |
gaṅgā gatwā samudrāmbhaḥ saptadhā pratipadyate ||17||

iyaṃ bhūtwā caikawaprā śucirākāśagā punaḥ |
deweṣu gaṅgā gandharwa prāpnotyalakanandatām ||18||

tathā pitṛnwaitaraṇī dustarā pāpakarmabhiḥ |
gaṅgā bhawati gandharwa yathā dwaipāyano'brawīt ||19||

asambādhā dewanadī swargasampādanī śubhā |
kathamicchasi tāṃ roddhuṃ naiṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ||20||

aniwāryamasambādhaṃ tawa wācā kathaṃ wayam |
na spṛśema yathākāmaṃ puṇyaṃ bhāgīrathījalam ||21||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

aṅgāraparṇastacchrutwā kruddha ānamya kārmukam |
mumoca sāyakāndīptānahīnāśīwiṣāniwa ||22||

ulmukaṃ bhrāmayaṃstūrṇaṃ pāṇḍawaścarma cottamam |
wyapowāha śarāṃstasya sarwānewa dhanañjayaḥ ||23||

arjuna uwāca||

bibhīṣikaiṣā gandharwa nāstrajñeṣu prayujyate |
astrajñeṣu prayuktaiṣā phenawatprawilīyate ||24||

mānuṣānati gandharwānsarwāngandharwa lakṣaye |
tasmādastreṇa diwyena yotsye'haṃ na tu māyayā ||25||

purāstramidamāgneyaṃ prādātkila bṛhaspatiḥ |
bharadwājasya gandharwa guruputraḥ śatakratoḥ ||26||

bharadwājādagniweśyo agniweśyādgururmama |
sa twidaṃ mahyamadadāddroṇo brāhmaṇasattamaḥ ||27||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ityuktwā pāṇḍawaḥ kruddho gandharwāya mumoca ha |
pradīptamastramāgneyaṃ dadāhāsya rathaṃ tu tat ||28||

wirathaṃ wiplutaṃ taṃ tu sa gandharwaṃ mahābalam |
astratejaḥpramūḍhaṃ ca prapatantamawāṅmukham ||29||

śiroruheṣu jagrāha mālyawatsu dhanañjayaḥ |
bhrātṛnprati cakarṣātha so'strapātādacetasam ||30||

yudhiṣṭhiraṃ tasya bhāryā prapede śaraṇārthinī |
nāmnā kumbhīnasī nāma patitrāṇamabhīpsatī ||31||

gandharwyuwāca||

trāhi twaṃ māṃ mahārāja patiṃ cemaṃ wimuñca me |
gandharwīṃ śaraṇaṃ prāptāṃ nāmnā kumbīnasīṃ prabho ||32||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

yuddhe jitaṃ yaśohīnaṃ strīnāthamaparākramam |
ko nu hanyādripuṃ twādṛṅmuñcemaṃ ripusūdana ||33||

arjuna uwāca||

aṅgemaṃ pratipadyaswa gaccha gandharwa mā śucaḥ |
pradiśatyabhayaṃ te'dya kururājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||34||

gandharwa uwāca||

jito'haṃ pūrwakaṃ nāma muñcāmyaṅgāraparṇatām |
na ca ślāghe balenādya na nāmnā janasaṃsadi ||35||

sādhwimaṃ labdhawāṃllābhaṃ yo'haṃ diwyāstradhāriṇam |
gāndharwyā māyayā yoddhumicchāmi wayasā waram ||36||

astrāgninā wicitro'yaṃ dagdho me ratha uttamaḥ |
so'haṃ citraratho bhūtwā nāmnā dagdharatho'bhawam ||37||

sambhṛtā caiwa widyeyaṃ tapaseha purā mayā |
niwedayiṣye tāmadya prāṇadāyā mahātmane ||38||

saṃstambhitaṃ hi tarasā jitaṃ śaraṇamāgatam |
yo'riṃ saṃyojayetprāṇaiḥ kalyāṇaṃ kiṃ na so'rhati ||39||

cakṣuṣī nāma widyeyaṃ yāṃ somāya dadau manuḥ |
dadau sa wiśwāwasawe mahyaṃ wiśwāwasurdadau ||40||

seyaṃ kāpuruṣaṃ prāptā gurudattā praṇaśyati |
āgamo'syā mayā prokto wīryaṃ pratinibodha me ||41||

yaccakṣuṣā draṣṭumicchettriṣu lokeṣu kiñcana |
tatpaśyedyādṛśaṃ cecchettādṛṣaṃ draṣṭumarhati ||42||

samānapadye ṣaṇmāsānsthito widyāṃ labhedimām |
anuneṣyāmyahaṃ widyāṃ swayaṃ tubhyaṃ wrate kṛte ||43||

widyayā hyanayā rājanwayaṃ nṛbhyo wiśeṣitāḥ |
awiśiṣṭāśca dewānāmanubhāwaprawartitāḥ ||44||

gandharwajānāmaśwānāmahaṃ puruṣasattama |
bhrātṛbhyastawa pañcabhyaḥ pṛthagdātā śataṃ śatam ||45||

dewagandharwawāhāste diwyagandhā manogamāḥ |
kṣīṇāḥ kṣīṇā bhawantyete na hīyante ca raṃhasaḥ ||46||

purā kṛtaṃ mahendrasya wajraṃ wṛtranibarhaṇe |
daśadhā śatadhā caiwa tacchīrṇaṃ wṛtramūrdhani ||47||

tato bhāgīkṛto dewairwajrabhāga upāsyate |
loke yatsādhanaṃ kiñcitsā wai wajratanuḥ smṛtā ||48||

wajrapāṇirbrāhmaṇaḥ syātkṣatraṃ wajrarathaṃ smṛtam |
waiśyā wai dānawajrāśca karmawajrā yawīyasaḥ ||49||

wajraṃ kṣatrasya wājino awadhyā wājinaḥ smṛtāḥ |
rathāṅgaṃ waḍawā sūte sūtāścāśweṣu ye matāḥ ||50||

kāmawarṇāḥ kāmajawāḥ kāmataḥ samupasthitāḥ |
ime gandharwajāḥ kāmaṃ pūrayiṣyanti te hayāḥ ||51||

arjuna uwāca||

yadi prītena wā dattaṃ saṃśaye jīwitasya wā |
widyā wittaṃ śrutaṃ wāpi na tadgandharwa kāmaye ||52||

gandharwa uwāca||

saṃyogo wai prītikaraḥ saṃsatsu pratidṛśyate |
jīwitasya pradānena prīto widyāṃ dadāmi te ||53||

twatto hyahaṃ grahīṣyāmi astramāgneyamuttamam |
tathaiwa sakhyaṃ bībhatso cirāya bharatarṣabha ||54||

arjuna uwāca||

twatto'streṇa wṛṇomyaśwānsaṃyogaḥ śāśwato'stu nau |
sakhe tadbrūhi gandharwa yuṣmabhyo yadbhayaṃ tyajet ||55||






                  159


arjuna uwāca||

kāraṇaṃ brūhi gandharwa kiṃ tadyena sma dharṣitāḥ |
yānto brahmawidaḥ santaḥ sarwe rātrāwariṃdama ||1||

gandharwa uwāca||

anagnayo'nāhutayo na ca wiprapuraskṛtāḥ |
yūyaṃ tato dharṣitāḥ stha mayā pāṇḍawanandana ||2||

yakṣarākṣasagandharwāḥ piśācoragamānawāḥ |
wistaraṃ kuruwaṃśasya śrīmataḥ kathayanti te ||3||

nāradaprabhṛtīnāṃ ca dewarṣīṇāṃ mayā śrutam |
guṇānkathayatāṃ wīra pūrweṣāṃ tawa dhīmatām ||4||

swayaṃ cāpi mayā dṛṣṭaścaratā sāgarāmbarām |
imāṃ wasumatīṃ kṛtsnāṃ prabhāwaḥ swakulasya te ||5||

wede dhanuṣi cācāryamabhijānāmi te'rjuna |
wiśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu bhāradwājaṃ yaśaswinam ||6||

dharmaṃ wāyuṃ ca śakraṃ ca wijānāmyaświnau tathā |
pāṇḍuṃ ca kuruśārdūla ṣaḍetānkulawardhanān ||7||

pitṛnetānahaṃ pārtha dewamānuṣasattamān ||7||

diwyātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarwaśastrabhṛtāṃ warāḥ |
bhawanto bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ sarwe sucaritawratāḥ ||8||

uttamāṃ tu manobuddhiṃ bhawatāṃ bhāwitātmanām |
jānannapi ca waḥ pārtha kṛtawāniha dharṣaṇām ||9||

strīsakāśe ca kaurawya na pumānkṣantumarhati |
dharṣaṇāmātmanaḥ paśyanbāhudrawiṇamāśritaḥ ||10||

naktaṃ ca balamasmākaṃ bhūya ewābhiwardhate |
yatastato māṃ kaunteya sadāraṃ manyurāwiśat ||11||

so'haṃ twayeha wijitaḥ saṅkhye tāpatyawardhana |
yena teneha widhinā kīrtyamānaṃ nibodha me ||12||

brahmacaryaṃ paro dharmaḥ sa cāpi niyatastwayi |
yasmāttasmādahaṃ pārtha raṇe'sminwijitastwayā ||13||

yastu syātkṣatriyaḥ kaścitkāmawṛttaḥ parantapa |
naktaṃ ca yudhi yudhyeta na sa jīwetkathañcana ||14||

yastu syātkāmawṛtto'pi rājā tāpatya saṅgare |
jayennaktañcarānsarwānsa purohitadhūrgataḥ ||15||

tasmāttāpatya yatkiñcinnṛṇāṃ śreya ihepsitam |
tasminkarmaṇi yoktawyā dāntātmānaḥ purohitāḥ ||16||

wede ṣaḍaṅge niratāḥ śucayaḥ satyawādinaḥ |
dharmātmānaḥ kṛtātmānaḥ syurnṛpāṇāṃ purohitāḥ ||17||

jayaśca niyato rājñaḥ swargaśca syādanantaram |
yasya syāddharmawidwāgmī purodhāḥ śīlawāñśuciḥ ||18||

lābhaṃ labdhumalabdhaṃ hi labdhaṃ ca parirakṣitum |
purohitaṃ prakurwīta rājā guṇasamanwitam ||19||

purohitamate tiṣṭhedya icchetpṛthiwīṃ nṛpaḥ |
prāptuṃ meruwarottaṃsāṃ sarwaśaḥ sāgarāmbarām ||20||

na hi kewalaśauryeṇa tāpatyābhijanena ca |
jayedabrāhmaṇaḥ kaścidbhūmiṃ bhūmipatiḥ kwacit ||21||

tasmādewaṃ wijānīhi kurūṇāṃ waṃśawardhana |
brāhmaṇapramukhaṃ rājyaṃ śakyaṃ pālayituṃ ciram ||22||






              tāpasyopākhyānam
                  160


arjuna uwāca||

tāpatya iti yadwākyamuktawānasi māmiha |
tadahaṃ jñātumicchāmi tāpatyārthawiniścayam ||1||

tapatī nāma kā caiṣā tāpatyā yatkṛte wayam |
kaunteyā hi wayaṃ sādho tattwamicchāmi weditum ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktaḥ sa gandharwaḥ kuntīputraṃ dhanañjayam |
wiśrutāṃ triṣu lokeṣu śrāwayāmāsa wai kathām ||3||

gandharwa uwāca||

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi kathāmetāṃ manoramām |
yathāwadakhilāṃ pārtha dharmyāṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ wara ||4||

uktawānasmi yena twāṃ tāpatya iti yadwacaḥ |
tatte'haṃ kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇuṣwaikamanā mama ||5||

ya eṣa diwi dhiṣṇyena nākaṃ wyāpnoti tejasā |
etasya tapatī nāma babhūwāsadṛśī sutā ||6||

wiwaswato wai kaunteya sāwitryawarajā wibho |
wiśrutā triṣu lokeṣu tapatī tapasā yutā ||7||

na dewī nāsurī caiwa na yakṣī na ca rākṣasī |
nāpsarā na ca gandharwī tathārūpeṇa kācana ||8||

suwibhaktānawadyāṅgī swasitāyatalocanā |
swācārā caiwa sādhwī ca suweṣā caiwa bhāminī ||9||

na tasyāḥ sadṛśaṃ kañcittriṣu lokeṣu bhārata |
bhartāraṃ sawitā mene rūpaśīlakulaśrutaiḥ ||10||

samprāptayauwanāṃ paśyandeyāṃ duhitaraṃ tu tām |
nopalebhe tataḥ śāntiṃ sampradānaṃ wicintayan ||11||

artharkṣaputraḥ kaunteya kurūṇāmṛṣabho balī |
sūryamārādhayāmāsa nṛpaḥ saṃwaraṇaḥ sadā ||12||

arghyamālyopahāraiśca śaśwacca nṛpatiryataḥ |
niyamairupawāsaiśca tapobhirwiwidhairapi ||13||

śuśrūṣuranahaṃwādī śuciḥ paurawanandanaḥ |
aṃśumantaṃ samudyantaṃ pūjayāmāsa bhaktimān ||14||

tataḥ kṛtajñaṃ dharmajñaṃ rūpeṇāsadṛśaṃ bhuwi |
tapatyāḥ sadṛśaṃ mene sūryaḥ saṃwaraṇaṃ patim ||15||

dātumaicchattataḥ kanyāṃ tasmai saṃwaraṇāya tām |
nṛpottamāya kaurawya wiśrutābhijanāya wai ||16||

yathā hi diwi dīptāṃśuḥ prabhāsayati tejasā |
tathā bhuwi mahīpālo dīptyā saṃwaraṇo'bhawat ||17||

yathārcayanti cādityamudyantaṃ brahmawādinaḥ |
tathā saṃwaraṇaṃ pārtha brāhmaṇāwarajāḥ prajāḥ ||18||

sa somamati kāntatwādādityamati tejasā |
babhūwa nṛpatiḥ śrīmānsuhṛdāṃ durhṛdāmapi ||19||

ewaṅguṇasya nṛpatestathāwṛttasya kaurawa |
tasmai dātuṃ manaścakre tapatīṃ tapanaḥ swayam ||20||

sa kadācidatho rājā śrīmānuruyaśā bhuwi |
cacāra mṛgayāṃ pārtha parwatopawane kila ||21||

carato mṛgayāṃ tasya kṣutpipāsāśramānwitaḥ |
mamāra rājñaḥ kaunteya girāwapratimo hayaḥ ||22||

sa mṛtāśwaścaranpārtha padbhyāmewa girau nṛpaḥ |
dadarśāsadṛśīṃ loke kanyāmāyatalocanām ||23||

sa eka ekāmāsādya kanyāṃ tāmarimardanaḥ |
tasthau nṛpatiśārdūlaḥ paśyannawicalekṣaṇaḥ ||24||

sa hi tāṃ tarkayāmāsa rūpato nṛpatiḥ śriyam |
punaḥ santarkayāmāsa rawerbhraṣṭāmiwa prabhām ||25||

giriprasthe tu sā yasminsthitā swasitalocanā |
sa sawṛkṣakṣupalato hiraṇmaya iwābhawat ||26||

awamene ca tāṃ dṛṣṭwā sarwaprāṇabhṛtāṃ wapuḥ |
awāptaṃ cātmano mene sa rājā cakṣuṣaḥ phalam ||27||

janmaprabhṛti yatkiñciddṛṣṭawānsa mahīpatiḥ |
rūpaṃ na sadṛśaṃ tasyāstarkayāmāsa kiñcana ||28||

tayā baddhamanaścakṣuḥ pāśairguṇamayaistadā |
na cacāla tato deśādbubudhe na ca kiñcana ||29||

asyā nūnaṃ wiśālākṣyāḥ sadewāsuramānuṣam |
lokaṃ nirmathya dhātredaṃ rūpamāwiṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ||30||

ewaṃ sa tarkayāmāsa rūpadrawiṇasampadā |
kanyāmasadṛśīṃ loke nṛpaḥ saṃwaraṇastadā ||31||

tāṃ ca dṛṣṭwaiwa kalyāṇīṃ kalyāṇābhijano nṛpaḥ |
jagāma manasā cintāṃ kāmamārgaṇapīḍitaḥ ||32||

dahyamānaḥ sa tīwreṇa nṛpatirmanmathāgninā |
apragalbhāṃ pragalbhaḥ sa tāmuwāca yaśaswinīm ||33||

kāsi kasyāsi rambhoru kimarthaṃ ceha tiṣṭhasi |
kathaṃ ca nirjane'raṇye carasyekā śucismite ||34||

twaṃ hi sarwānawadyāṅgī sarwābharaṇabhūṣitā |
wibhūṣaṇamiwaiteṣāṃ bhūṣaṇānāmabhīpsitam ||35||

na dewīṃ nāsurīṃ caiwa na yakṣīṃ na ca rākṣasīm |
na ca bhogawatīṃ manye na gandharwīṃ na mānuṣīm ||36||

yā hi dṛṣṭā mayā kāścicchrutā wāpi warāṅganāḥ |
na tāsāṃ sadṛśīṃ manye twāmahaṃ mattakāśini ||37||

ewaṃ tāṃ sa mahīpālo babhāṣe na tu sā tadā |
kāmārtaṃ nirjane'raṇye pratyabhāṣata kiñcana ||38||

tato lālapyamānasya pārthiwasyāyatekṣaṇā |
saudāminīwa sābhreṣu tatraiwāntaradhīyata ||39||

tāmanwicchansa nṛpatiḥ paricakrāma tattadā |
wanaṃ wanajapatrākṣīṃ bhramannunmattawattadā ||40||

apaśyamānaḥ sa tu tāṃ bahu tatra wilapya ca |
niśceṣṭaḥ kaurawaśreṣṭho muhūrtaṃ sa wyatiṣṭhata ||41||






                  161


gandharwa uwāca||

atha tasyāmadṛśyāyāṃ nṛpatiḥ kāmamohitaḥ |
pātanaḥ śatrusaṅghānāṃ papāta dharaṇītale ||1||

tasminnipatite bhūmāwatha sā cāruhāsinī |
punaḥ pīnāyataśroṇī darśayāmāsa taṃ nṛpam ||2||

athābabhāṣe kalyāṇī wācā madhurayā nṛpam |
taṃ kurūṇāṃ kulakaraṃ kāmābhihatacetasam ||3||

uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha bhadraṃ te na twamarhasyariṃdama |
mohaṃ nṛpatiśārdūla gantumāwiṣkṛtaḥ kṣitau ||4||

ewamukto'tha nṛpatirwācā madhurayā tadā |
dadarśa wipulaśroṇīṃ tāmewābhimukhe sthitām ||5||

atha tāmasitāpāṅgīmābabhāṣe narādhipaḥ |
manmathāgniparītātmā saṃdigdhākṣarayā girā ||6||

sādhu māmasitāpāṅge kāmārtaṃ mattakāśini |
bhajaswa bhajamānaṃ māṃ prāṇā hi prajahanti mām ||7||

twadarthaṃ hi wiśālākṣi māmayaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ |
kāmaḥ kamalagarbhābhe pratiwidhyanna śāmyati ||8||

grastamewamanākrande bhadre kāmamahāhinā |
sā twaṃ pīnāyataśroṇi paryāpnuhi śubhānane ||9||

twayyadhīnā hi me prāṇāḥ kiṃnarodgītabhāṣiṇi |
cārusarwānawadyāṅgi padmendusadṛśānane ||10||

na hyahaṃ twadṛte bhīru śakṣye jīwitumātmanā |
tasmātkuru wiśālākṣi mayyanukrośamaṅgane ||11||

bhaktaṃ māmasitāpāṅge na parityaktumarhasi |
twaṃ hi māṃ prītiyogena trātumarhasi bhāmini ||12||

gāndharweṇa ca māṃ bhīru wiwāhenaihi sundari |
wiwāhānāṃ hi rambhoru gāndharwaḥ śreṣṭha ucyate ||13||

tapatyuwāca||

nāhamīśātmano rājankanyā pitṛmatī hyaham |
mayi cedasti te prītiryācaswa pitaraṃ mama ||14||

yathā hi te mayā prāṇāḥ saṅgṛhītā nareśwara |
darśanādewa bhūyastwaṃ tathā prāṇānmamāharaḥ ||15||

na cāhamīśā dehasya tasmānnṛpatisattama |
samīpaṃ nopagacchāmi na swatantrā hi yoṣitaḥ ||16||

kā hi sarweṣu lokeṣu wiśrutābhijanaṃ nṛpam |
kanyā nābhilaṣennāthaṃ bhartāraṃ bhaktawatsalam ||17||

tasmādewaṅgate kāle yācaswa pitaraṃ mama |
ādityaṃ praṇipātena tapasā niyamena ca ||18||

sa cetkāmayate dātuṃ tawa māmarimardana |
bhawiṣyāmyatha te rājansatataṃ waśawartinī ||19||

ahaṃ hi tapatī nāma sāwitryawarajā sutā |
asya lokapradīpasya sawituḥ kṣatriyarṣabha ||20||






                  162


gandharwa uwāca||

ewamuktwā tatastūrṇaṃ jagāmordhwamaninditā |
sa tu rājā punarbhūmau tatraiwa nipapāta ha ||1||

amātyaḥ sānuyātrastu taṃ dadarśa mahāwane |
kṣitau nipatitaṃ kāle śakradhwajamiwocchritam ||2||

taṃ hi dṛṣṭwā maheṣwāsaṃ niraśwaṃ patitaṃ kṣitau |
babhūwa so'sya saciwaḥ sampradīpta iwāgninā ||3||

twarayā copasaṅgamya snehādāgatasambhramaḥ |
taṃ samutthāpayāmāsa nṛpatiṃ kāmamohitam ||4||

bhūtalādbhūmipāleśaṃ pitewa patitaṃ sutam |
prajñayā wayasā caiwa wṛddhaḥ kīrtyā damena ca ||5||

amātyastaṃ samutthāpya babhūwa wigatajwaraḥ |
uwāca cainaṃ kalyāṇyā wācā madhurayotthitam ||6||

mā bhairmanujaśārdūla bhadraṃ cāstu tawānagha ||6||

kṣutpipāsāpariśrāntaṃ tarkayāmāsa taṃ nṛpam |
patitaṃ pātanaṃ saṅkhye śātrawāṇāṃ mahītale ||7||

wāriṇātha suśītena śirastasyābhyaṣecayat |
aspṛśanmukuṭaṃ rājñaḥ puṇḍarīkasugandhinā ||8||

tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇastadbalaṃ balawānnṛpaḥ |
sarwaṃ wisarjayāmāsa tamekaṃ saciwaṃ winā ||9||

tatastasyājñayā rājño wipratasthe mahadbalam |
sa tu rājā giriprasthe tasminpunarupāwiśat ||10||

tatastasmingiriware śucirbhūtwā kṛtāñjaliḥ |
ārirādhayiṣuḥ sūryaṃ tasthāwūrdhwabhujaḥ kṣitau ||11||

jagāma manasā caiwa wasiṣṭhamṛṣisattamam |
purohitamamitraghnastadā saṃwaraṇo nṛpaḥ ||12||

naktaṃdinamathaikasthe sthite tasmiñjanādhipe |
athājagāma wiprarṣistadā dwādaśame'hani ||13||

sa widitwaiwa nṛpatiṃ tapatyā hṛtamānasam |
diwyena widhinā jñātwā bhāwitātmā mahānṛṣiḥ ||14||

tathā tu niyatātmānaṃ sa taṃ nṛpatisattamam |
ābabhāṣe sa dharmātmā tasyaiwārthacikīrṣayā ||15||

sa tasya manujendrasya paśyato bhagawānṛṣiḥ |
ūrdhwamācakrame draṣṭuṃ bhāskaraṃ bhāskaradyutiḥ ||16||

sahasrāṃśuṃ tato wipraḥ kṛtāñjalirupasthitaḥ |
wasiṣṭho'hamiti prītyā sa cātmānaṃ nyawedayat ||17||

tamuwāca mahātejā wiwaswānmunisattamam |
maharṣe swāgataṃ te'stu kathayaswa yathecchasi ||18||






                  163


wasiṣṭha uwāca||

yaiṣā te tapatī nāma sāwitryawarajā sutā |
tāṃ twāṃ saṃwaraṇasyārthe warayāmi wibhāwaso ||1||

sa hi rājā bṛhatkīrtirdharmārthawidudāradhīḥ |
yuktaḥ saṃwaraṇo bhartā duhituste wihaṅgama ||2||

gandharwa uwāca||

ityuktaḥ sawitā tena dadānītyewa niścitaḥ |
pratyabhāṣata taṃ wipraṃ pratinandya diwākaraḥ ||3||

waraḥ saṃwaraṇo rājñāṃ twamṛṣīṇāṃ waro mune |
tapatī yoṣitāṃ śreṣṭhā kimanyatrāpawarjanāt ||4||

tataḥ sarwānawadyāgnīṃ tapatīṃ tapanaḥ swayam |
dadau saṃwaraṇasyārthe wasiṣṭhāya mahātmane ||5||

pratijagrāha tāṃ kanyāṃ maharṣistapatīṃ tadā ||5||

wasiṣṭho'tha wisṛṣṭaśca punarewājagāma ha |
yatra wikhyatakīrtiḥ sa kurūṇāmṛṣabho'bhawat ||6||

sa rājā manmathāwiṣṭastadgatenāntarātmanā |
dṛṣṭwā ca dewakanyāṃ tāṃ tapatīṃ cāruhāsinīm ||7||

wasiṣṭhena sahāyāntīṃ saṃhṛṣṭo'bhyadhikaṃ babhau ||7||

kṛcchre dwādaśarātre tu tasya rājñaḥ samāpite |
ājagāma wiśuddhātmā wasiṣṭho bhagawānṛṣiḥ ||8||

tapasārādhya waradaṃ dewaṃ gopatimīśwaram |
lebhe saṃwaraṇo bhāryāṃ wasiṣṭhasyaiwa tejasā ||9||

tatastasmingiriśreṣṭhe dewagandharwasewite |
jagrāha widhiwatpāṇiṃ tapatyāḥ sa nararṣabhaḥ ||10||

wasiṣṭhenābhyanujñātastasminnewa dharādhare |
so'kāmayata rājarṣirwihartuṃ saha bhāryayā ||11||

tataḥ pure ca rāṣṭre ca wāhaneṣu baleṣu ca |
ādideśa mahīpālastamewa saciwaṃ tadā ||12||

nṛpatiṃ twabhyanujñāya wasiṣṭho'thāpacakrame |
so'pi rājā girau tasminwijahārāmaropamaḥ ||13||

tato dwādaśa warṣāṇi kānaneṣu jaleṣu ca |
reme tasmingirau rājā tayaiwa saha bhāryayā ||14||

tasya rājñaḥ pure tasminsamā dwādaśa sarwaśaḥ |
na wawarṣa sahasrākṣo rāṣṭre caiwāsya sarwaśaḥ ||15||

tatkṣudhārtairnirānandaiḥ śawabhūtaistadā naraiḥ |
abhawatpretarājasya puraṃ pretairiwāwṛtam ||16||

tatastattādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭwā sa ewa bhagawānṛṣiḥ |
abhyapadyata dharmātmā wasiṣṭho rājasattamam ||17||

taṃ ca pārthiwaśārdūlamānayāmāsa tatpuram |
tapatyā sahitaṃ rājannuṣitaṃ dwādaśīḥ samāḥ ||18||

tataḥ prawṛṣṭastatrāsīdyathāpūrwaṃ surārihā |
tasminnṛpatiśārdūle prawiṣṭe nagaraṃ punaḥ ||19||

tataḥ sarāṣṭraṃ mumude tatpuraṃ parayā mudā |
tena pārthiwamukhyena bhāwitaṃ bhāwitātmanā ||20||

tato dwādaśa warṣāṇi punarīje narādhipaḥ |
patnyā tapatyā sahito yathā śakro marutpatiḥ ||21||

ewamāsīnmahābhāgā tapatī nāma paurwikī |
tawa waiwaswatī pārtha tāpatyastwaṃ yayā mataḥ ||22||

tasyāṃ sañjanayāmāsa kuruṃ saṃwaraṇo nṛpaḥ |
tapatyāṃ tapatāṃ śreṣṭha tāpatyastwaṃ tato'rjuna ||23||






              wāsiṣṭhopākhyānam
                  164


waiśampāyana uwāca||

sa gandharwawacaḥ śrutwā tattadā bharatarṣabha |
arjunaḥ parayā prītyā pūrṇacandra iwābabhau ||1||

uwāca ca maheṣwāso gandharwaṃ kurusattamaḥ |
jātakautūhalo'tīwa wasiṣṭhasya tapobalāt ||2||

wasiṣṭha iti yasyaitadṛṣernāma twayeritam |
etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ yathāwattadwadaswa me ||3||

ya eṣa gandharwapate pūrweṣāṃ naḥ purohitaḥ |
āsīdetanmamācakṣwa ka eṣa bhagawānṛṣiḥ ||4||

gandharwa uwāca||

tapasā nirjitau śaśwadajeyāwamarairapi |
kāmakrodhāwubhau yasya caraṇau saṃwawāhatuḥ ||5||

yastu nocchedanaṃ cakre kuśikānāmudāradhīḥ |
wiśwāmitrāparādhena dhārayanmanyumuttamam ||6||

putrawyasanasantaptaḥ śaktimānapi yaḥ prabhuḥ |
wiśwāmitrawināśāya na mene karma dāruṇam ||7||

mṛtāṃśca punarāhartuṃ yaḥ sa putrānyamakṣayāt |
kṛtāntaṃ nāticakrāma welāmiwa mahodadhiḥ ||8||

yaṃ prāpya wijitātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ narādhipāḥ |
ikṣwākawo mahīpālā lebhire pṛthiwīmimām ||9||

purohitawaraṃ prāpya wasiṣṭhamṛṣisattamam |
ījire kratubhiścāpi nṛpāste kurunandana ||10||

sa hi tānyājayāmāsa sarwānnṛpatisattamān |
brahmarṣiḥ pāṇḍawaśreṣṭha bṛhaspatiriwāmarān ||11||

tasmāddharmapradhānātmā wedadharmawidīpsitaḥ |
brāhmaṇo guṇawānkaścitpurodhāḥ prawimṛśyatām ||12||

kṣatriyeṇa hi jātena pṛthiwīṃ jetumicchatā |
pūrwaṃ purohitaḥ kāryaḥ pārtha rājyābhiwṛddhaye ||13||

mahīṃ jigīṣatā rājñā brahma kāryaṃ puraḥsaram |
tasmātpurohitaḥ kaścidguṇawānastu wo dwijaḥ ||14||






                  165


arjuna uwāca||

kiṃnimittamabhūdwairaṃ wiśwāmitrawasiṣṭhayoḥ |
wasatorāśrame puṇye śaṃsa naḥ sarwamewa tat ||1||

gandharwa uwāca||

idaṃ wāsiṣṭhamākhyānaṃ purāṇaṃ paricakṣate |
pārtha sarweṣu lokeṣu yathāwattannibodha me ||2||

kanyakubje mahānāsītpārthiwo bharatarṣabha |
gādhīti wiśruto loke satyadharmaparāyaṇaḥ ||3||

tasya dharmātmanaḥ putraḥ samṛddhabalawāhanaḥ |
wiśwāmitra iti khyāto babhūwa ripumardanaḥ ||4||

sa cacāra sahāmātyo mṛgayāṃ gahane wane |
mṛgānwidhyanwarāhāṃśca ramyeṣu marudhanwasu ||5||

wyāyāmakarśitaḥ so'tha mṛgalipsuḥ pipāsitaḥ |
ājagāma naraśreṣṭha wasiṣṭhasyāśramaṃ prati ||6||

tamāgatamabhiprekṣya wasiṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhabhāgṛṣiḥ |
wiśwāmitraṃ naraśreṣṭhaṃ pratijagrāha pūjayā ||7||

pādyārghyācamanīyena swāgatena ca bhārata |
tathaiwa pratijagrāha wanyena hawiṣā tathā ||8||

tasyātha kāmadhugdhenurwasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ |
uktā kāmānprayaccheti sā kāmānduduhe tataḥ ||9||

grāmyāraṇyā oṣadhīśca duduhe paya ewa ca |
ṣaḍrasaṃ cāmṛtarasaṃ rasāyanamanuttamam ||10||

bhojanīyāni peyāni bhakṣyāṇi wiwidhāni ca |
lehyānyamṛtakalpāni coṣyāṇi ca tathārjuna ||11||

taiḥ kāmaiḥ sarwasampūrṇaiḥ pūjitaḥ sa mahīpatiḥ |
sāmātyaḥ sabalaścaiwa tutoṣa sa bhṛśaṃ nṛpaḥ ||12||

ṣaḍāyatāṃ supārśworuṃ tripṛthuṃ pañca saṃwṛtām |
maṇḍūkanetrāṃ swākārāṃ pīnodhasamaninditām ||13||

suwāladhiṃ śaṅkukarṇāṃ cāruśṛṅgāṃ manoramām |
puṣṭāyataśirogrīwāṃ wismitaḥ so'bhiwīkṣya tām ||14||

abhinandati tāṃ nandīṃ wasiṣṭhasya payaswinīm |
abrawīcca bhṛśaṃ tuṣṭo wiśwāmitro muniṃ tadā ||15||

arbudena gawāṃ brahmanmama rājyena wā punaḥ |
nandinīṃ samprayacchaswa bhuṅkṣwa rājyaṃ mahāmune ||16||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

dewatātithipitrarthamājyārthaṃ ca payaswinī |
adeyā nandinīyaṃ me rājyenāpi tawānagha ||17||

wiśwāmitra uwāca||

kṣatriyo'haṃ bhawānwiprastapaḥswādhyāyasādhanaḥ |
brāhmaṇeṣu kuto wīryaṃ praśānteṣu dhṛtātmasu ||18||

arbudena gawāṃ yastwaṃ na dadāsi mamepsitām |
swadharmaṃ na prahāsyāmi nayiṣye te balena gām ||19||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

balasthaścāsi rājā ca bāhuwīryaśca kṣatriyaḥ |
yathecchasi tathā kṣipraṃ kuru twaṃ mā wicāraya ||20||

gandharwa uwāca||

ewamuktastadā pārtha wiśwāmitro balādiwa |
haṃsacandrapratīkāśāṃ nandinīṃ tāṃ jahāra gām ||21||

kaśādaṇḍapratihatā kālyamānā tatastataḥ |
hambhāyamānā kalyāṇī wasiṣṭhasyātha nandinī ||22||

āgamyābhimukhī pārtha tasthau bhagawadunmukhī |
bhṛśaṃ ca tāḍyamānāpi na jagāmāśramāttataḥ ||23||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

śṛṇomi te rawaṃ bhadre winadantyāḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
balāddhriyasi me nandi kṣamāwānbrāhmaṇo hyaham ||24||

gandharwa uwāca||

sā tu teṣāṃ balānnandī balānāṃ bharatarṣabha |
wiśwāmitrabhayodwignā wasiṣṭhaṃ samupāgamat ||25||

gauruwāca||

pāṣāṇadaṇḍābhihatāṃ krandantīṃ māmanāthawat |
wiśwāmitrabalairghorairbhagawankimupekṣase ||26||

gandharwa uwāca||

ewaṃ tasyāṃ tadā partha dharṣitāyāṃ mahāmuniḥ |
na cukṣubhe na dhairyācca wicacāla dhṛtawrataḥ ||27||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

kṣatriyāṇāṃ balaṃ tejo brāhmaṇānāṃ kṣamā balam |
kṣamā māṃ bhajate tasmādgamyatāṃ yadi rocate ||28||

gauruwāca||

kiṃ nu tyaktāsmi bhagawanyadewaṃ māṃ prabhāṣase |
atyaktāhaṃ twayā brahmanna śakyā nayituṃ balāt ||29||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

na twāṃ tyajāmi kalyāṇi sthīyatāṃ yadi śakyate |
dṛḍhena dāmnā baddhwaiṣa watsaste hriyate balāt ||30||

gandharwa uwāca||

sthīyatāmiti tacchrutwā wasiṣṭhasya payaswinī |
ūrdhwāñcitaśirogrīwā prababhau ghoradarśanā ||31||

krodharaktekṣaṇā sā gaurhambhārawaghanaswanā |
wiśwāmitrasya tatsainyaṃ wyadrāwayata sarwaśaḥ ||32||

kaśāgradaṇḍābhihatā kālyamānā tatastataḥ |
krodhadīptekṣaṇā krodhaṃ bhūya ewa samādadhe ||33||

āditya iwa madhyāhne krodhadīptawapurbabhau |
aṅgārawarṣaṃ muñcantī muhurwāladhito mahat ||34||

asṛjatpahlawānpucchācchakṛtaḥ śabarāñśakān |
mūtrataścāsṛjaccāpi yawanānkrodhamūrcchitā ||35||

puṇḍrānkirātāndramiḍānsiṃhalānbarbarāṃstathā |
tathaiwa daradānmlecchānphenataḥ sā sasarja ha ||36||

tairwisṛṣṭairmahatsainyaṃ nānāmlecchagaṇaistadā |
nānāwaraṇasañchannairnānāyudhadharaistathā ||37||

awākīryata saṃrabdhairwiśwāmitrasya paśyataḥ ||37||

ekaikaśca tadā yodhaḥ pañcabhiḥ saptabhirwṛtaḥ |
astrawarṣeṇa mahatā kālyamānaṃ balaṃ tataḥ ||38||

prabhagnaṃ sarwatastrastaṃ wiśwāmitrasya paśyataḥ ||38||

na ca prāṇairwiyujyanta kecitte sainikāstadā |
wiśwāmitrasya saṅkruddhairwāsiṣṭhairbharatarṣabha ||39||

wiśwāmitrasya sainyaṃ tu kālyamānaṃ triyojanam |
krośamānaṃ bhayodwignaṃ trātāraṃ nādhyagacchata ||40||

dṛṣṭwā tanmahadāścaryaṃ brahmatejobhawaṃ tadā |
wiśwāmitraḥ kṣatrabhāwānnirwiṇṇo wākyamabrawīt ||41||

dhigbalaṃ kṣatriyabalaṃ brahmatejobalaṃ balam |
balābalaṃ winiścitya tapa ewa paraṃ balam ||42||

sa rājyaṃ sphītamutsṛjya tāṃ ca dīptāṃ nṛpaśriyam |
bhogāṃśca pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtwā tapasyewa mano dadhe ||43||

sa gatwā tapasā siddhiṃ lokānwiṣṭabhya tejasā |
tatāpa sarwāndīptaujā brāhmaṇatwamawāpa ca ||44||

apibacca sutaṃ somamindreṇa saha kauśikaḥ ||44||






                  166


gandharwa uwāca||

kalmāṣapāda ityasmiṃlloke rājā babhūwa ha |
ikṣwākuwaṃśajaḥ pārtha tejasāsadṛśo bhuwi ||1||

sa kadācidwanaṃ rājā mṛgayāṃ niryayau purāt |
mṛgānwidhyanwarāhāṃśca cacāra ripumardanaḥ ||2||

sa tu rājā mahātmānaṃ wāsiṣṭhamṛṣisattamam |
tṛṣārtaśca kṣudhārtaśca ekāyanagataḥ pathi ||3||

apaśyadajitaḥ saṅkhye muniṃ pratimukhāgatam |
śaktiṃ nāma mahābhāgaṃ wasiṣṭhakulanandanam ||4||

jyeṣṭhaṃ putraśatātputraṃ wasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ ||4||

apagaccha patho'smākamityewaṃ pārthiwo'brawīt |
tathā ṛṣiruwācainaṃ sāntwayañślakṣṇayā girā ||5||

ṛṣistu nāpacakrāma tasmindharmapathe sthitaḥ |
nāpi rājā munermānātkrodhāccāpi jagāma ha ||6||

amuñcantaṃ tu panthānaṃ tamṛṣiṃ nṛpasattamaḥ |
jaghāna kaśayā mohāttadā rākṣasawanmunim ||7||

kaśāprahārābhihatastataḥ sa munisattamaḥ |
taṃ śaśāpa nṛpaśreṣṭhaṃ wāsiṣṭhaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ ||8||

haṃsi rākṣasawadyasmādrājāpasada tāpasam |
tasmāttwamadya prabhṛti puruṣādo bhawiṣyasi ||9||

manuṣyapiśite saktaścariṣyasi mahīmimām |
gaccha rājādhametyuktaḥ śaktinā wīryaśaktinā ||10||

tato yājyanimittaṃ tu wiśwāmitrawasiṣṭhayoḥ |
wairamāsīttadā taṃ tu wiśwāmitro'nwapadyata ||11||

tayorwiwadatorewaṃ samīpamupacakrame |
ṛṣirugratapāḥ pārtha wiśwāmitraḥ pratāpawān ||12||

tataḥ sa bubudhe paścāttamṛṣiṃ nṛpasattamaḥ |
ṛṣeḥ putraṃ wasiṣṭhasya wasiṣṭhamiwa tejasā ||13||

antardhāya tadātmānaṃ wiśwāmitro'pi bhārata |
tāwubhāwupacakrāma cikīrṣannātmanaḥ priyam ||14||

sa tu śaptastadā tena śaktinā wai nṛpottamaḥ |
jagāma śaraṇaṃ śaktiṃ prasādayitumarhayan ||15||

tasya bhāwaṃ widitwā sa nṛpateḥ kurunandana |
wiśwāmitrastato rakṣa ādideśa nṛpaṃ prati ||16||

sa śāpāttasya wiprarṣerwiśwāmitrasya cājñayā |
rākṣasaḥ kiṅkaro nāma wiweśa nṛpatiṃ tadā ||17||

rakṣasā tu gṛhītaṃ taṃ widitwā sa munistadā |
wiśwāmitro'pyapakrāmattasmāddeśādariṃdama ||18||

tataḥ sa nṛpatirwidwānrakṣannātmānamātmanā |
balawatpīḍyamāno'pi rakṣasāntargatena ha ||19||

dadarśa taṃ dwijaḥ kaścidrājānaṃ prasthitaṃ punaḥ |
yayāce kṣudhitaścainaṃ samāṃsaṃ bhojanaṃ tadā ||20||

tamuwācātha rājarṣirdwijaṃ mitrasahastadā |
āsswa brahmaṃstwamatraiwa muhūrtamiti sāntwayan ||21||

niwṛttaḥ pratidāsyāmi bhojanaṃ te yathepsitam |
ityuktwā prayayau rājā tasthau ca dwijasattamaḥ ||22||

antargataṃ tu tadrājñastadā brāhmaṇabhāṣitam |
so'ntaḥpuraṃ prawiśyātha saṃwiweśa narādhipaḥ ||23||

tato'rdharātra utthāya sūdamānāyya satwaram |
uwāca rājā saṃsmṛtya brāhmaṇasya pratiśrutam ||24||

gacchāmuṣminnasau deśe brāhmaṇo māṃ pratīkṣate |
annārthī twaṃ tamannena samāṃsenopapādaya ||25||

ewamuktastadā sūdaḥ so'nāsādyāmiṣaṃ kwacit |
niwedayāmāsa tadā tasmai rājñe wyathānwitaḥ ||26||

rājā tu rakṣasāwiṣṭaḥ sūdamāha gatawyathaḥ |
apyenaṃ naramāṃsena bhojayeti punaḥ punaḥ ||27||

tathetyuktwā tataḥ sūdaḥ saṃsthānaṃ wadhyaghātinām |
gatwā jahāra twarito naramāṃsamapetabhīḥ ||28||

sa tatsaṃskṛtya widhiwadannopahitamāśu wai |
tasmai prādādbrāhmaṇāya kṣudhitāya tapaswine ||29||

sa siddhacakṣuṣā dṛṣṭwā tadannaṃ dwijasattamaḥ |
abhojyamidamityāha krodhaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ ||30||

yasmādabhojyamannaṃ me dadāti sa narādhipaḥ |
tasmāttasyaiwa mūḍhasya bhawiṣyatyatra lolupā ||31||

sakto mānuṣamāṃseṣu yathoktaḥ śaktinā purā |
udwejanīyo bhūtānāṃ cariṣyati mahīmimām ||32||

dwiranuwyāhṛte rājñaḥ sa śāpo balawānabhūt |
rakṣobalasamāwiṣṭo wisañjñaścābhawattadā ||33||

tataḥ sa nṛpatiśreṣṭho rākṣasopahatendriyaḥ |
uwāca śaktiṃ taṃ dṛṣṭwā nacirādiwa bhārata ||34||

yasmādasadṛśaḥ śāpaḥ prayukto'yaṃ twayā mayi |
tasmāttwattaḥ prawartiṣye khādituṃ mānuṣānaham ||35||

ewamuktwā tataḥ sadyastaṃ prāṇairwiprayujya saḥ |
śaktinaṃ bhakṣayāmāsa wyāghraḥ paśumiwepsitam ||36||

śaktinaṃ tu hataṃ dṛṣṭwā wiśwāmitrastataḥ punaḥ |
wasiṣṭhasyaiwa putreṣu tadrakṣaḥ saṃdideśa ha ||37||

sa tāñśatāwarānputrānwasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ |
bhakṣayāmāsa saṅkruddhaḥ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgāniwa ||38||

wasiṣṭho ghātitāñśrutwā wiśwāmitreṇa tānsutān |
dhārayāmāsa taṃ śokaṃ mahādririwa medinīm ||39||

cakre cātmawināśāya buddhiṃ sa munisattamaḥ |
na twewa kuśikocchedaṃ mene matimatāṃ waraḥ ||40||

sa merukūṭādātmānaṃ mumoca bhagawānṛṣiḥ |
śirastasya śilāyāṃ ca tūlarāśāwiwāpatat ||41||

na mamāra ca pātena sa yadā tena pāṇḍawa |
tadāgnimiddhwā bhagawānsaṃwiweśa mahāwane ||42||

taṃ tadā susamiddho'pi na dadāha hutāśanaḥ |
dīpyamāno'pyamitraghna śīto'gnirabhawattataḥ ||43||

sa samudramabhipretya śokāwiṣṭo mahāmuniḥ |
baddhwā kaṇṭhe śilāṃ gurwīṃ nipapāta tadambhasi ||44||

sa samudrormiwegena sthale nyasto mahāmuniḥ |
jagāma sa tataḥ khinnaḥ punarewāśramaṃ prati ||45||






                  167


gandharwa uwāca||

tato dṛṣṭwāśramapadaṃ rahitaṃ taiḥ sutairmuniḥ |
nirjagāma suduḥkhārtaḥ punarewāśramāttataḥ ||1||

so'paśyatsaritaṃ pūrṇāṃ prāwṛṭkāle nawāmbhasā |
wṛkṣānbahuwidhānpārtha wahantīṃ tīrajānbahūn ||2||

atha cintāṃ samāpede punaḥ paurawanandana |
ambhasyasyā nimajjeyamiti duḥkhasamanwitaḥ ||3||

tataḥ pāśaistadātmānaṃ gāḍhaṃ baddhwā mahāmuniḥ |
tasyā jale mahānadyā nimamajja suduḥkhitaḥ ||4||

atha chittwā nadī pāśāṃstasyāribalamardana |
samasthaṃ tamṛṣiṃ kṛtwā wipāśaṃ samawāsṛjat ||5||

uttatāra tataḥ pāśairwimuktaḥ sa mahānṛṣiḥ |
wipāśeti ca nāmāsyā nadyāścakre mahānṛṣiḥ ||6||

śoke buddhiṃ tataścakre na caikatra wyatiṣṭhata |
so'gacchatparwatāṃścaiwa saritaśca sarāṃsi ca ||7||

tataḥ sa punarewarṣirnadīṃ haimawatīṃ tadā |
caṇḍagrāhawatīṃ dṛṣṭwā tasyāḥ srotasyawāpatat ||8||

sā tamagnisamaṃ wipramanucintya saridwarā |
śatadhā widrutā yasmācchatadruriti wiśrutā ||9||

tataḥ sthalagataṃ dṛṣṭwā tatrāpyātmānamātmanā |
martuṃ na śakyamityuktwā punarewāśramaṃ yayau ||10||

wadhwādṛśyantyānugata āśramābhimukho wrajan |
atha śuśrāwa saṅgatyā wedādhyayananiḥswanam ||11||

pṛṣṭhataḥ paripūrṇārthaiḥ ṣaḍbhiraṅgairalaṅkṛtam ||11||

anuwrajati ko nweṣa māmityewa ca so'brawīt |
ahaṃ twadṛśyatī nāmnā taṃ snuṣā pratyabhāṣata ||12||

śakterbhāryā mahābhāga tapoyuktā tapaswinī ||12||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

putri kasyaiṣa sāṅgasya wedasyādhyayanaswanaḥ |
purā sāṅgasya wedasya śakteriwa mayā śrutaḥ ||13||

adṛśyantyuwāca||

ayaṃ kukṣau samutpannaḥ śaktergarbhaḥ sutasya te |
samā dwādaśa tasyeha wedānabhyasato mune ||14||

gandharwa uwāca||

ewamuktastato hṛṣṭo wasiṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhabhāgṛṣiḥ |
asti santānamityuktwā mṛtyoḥ pārtha nyawartata ||15||

tataḥ pratiniwṛttaḥ sa tayā wadhwā sahānagha |
kalmāṣapādamāsīnaṃ dadarśa wijane wane ||16||

sa tu dṛṣṭwaiwa taṃ rājā kruddha utthāya bhārata |
āwiṣṭo rakṣasogreṇa iyeṣāttuṃ tataḥ sma tam ||17||

adṛśyantī tu taṃ dṛṣṭwā krūrakarmāṇamagrataḥ |
bhayasaṃwignayā wācā wasiṣṭhamidamabrawīt ||18||

asau mṛtyuriwogreṇa daṇḍena bhagawannitaḥ |
pragṛhītena kāṣṭhena rākṣaso'bhyeti bhīṣaṇaḥ ||19||

taṃ niwārayituṃ śakto nānyo'sti bhuwi kaścana |
twadṛte'dya mahābhāga sarwawedawidāṃ wara ||20||

trāhi māṃ bhagawanpāpādasmāddāruṇadarśanāt |
rakṣo attumiha hyāwāṃ nūnametaccikīrṣati ||21||






                  168


wasiṣṭha uwāca||

mā bhaiḥ putri na bhetawyaṃ rakṣasaste kathañcana |
naitadrakṣo bhayaṃ yasmātpaśyasi twamupasthitam ||1||

rājā kalmāṣapādo'yaṃ wīryawānprathito bhuwi |
sa eṣo'sminwanoddeśe niwasatyatibhīṣaṇaḥ ||2||

gandharwa uwāca||

tamāpatantaṃ samprekṣya wasiṣṭho bhagawānṛṣiḥ |
wārayāmāsa tejaswī huṅkareṇaiwa bhārata ||3||

mantrapūtena ca punaḥ sa tamabhyukṣya wāriṇā |
mokṣayāmāsa wai ghorādrākṣasādrājasattamam ||4||

sa hi dwādaśa warṣāṇi wasiṣṭhasyaiwa tejasā |
grasta āsīdgṛheṇewa parwakāle diwākaraḥ ||5||

rakṣasā wipramukto'tha sa nṛpastadwanaṃ mahat |
tejasā rañjayāmāsa sandhyābhramiwa bhāskaraḥ ||6||

pratilabhya tataḥ sañjñāmabhiwādya kṛtāñjaliḥ |
uwāca nṛpatiḥ kāle wasiṣṭhamṛṣisattamam ||7||

saudāso'haṃ mahābhāga yājyaste dwijasattama |
asminkāle yadiṣṭaṃ te brūhi kiṃ karawāṇi te ||8||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

wṛttametadyathākālaṃ gaccha rājyaṃ praśādhi tat |
brāhmaṇāṃśca manuṣyendra māwamaṃsthāḥ kadācana ||9||

rājowāca||

nāwamaṃsyāmyahaṃ brahmankadācidbrāhmaṇarṣabhān |
twannideśe sthitaḥ śaśwatpujayiṣyāmyahaṃ dwijān ||10||

ikṣwākūṇāṃ tu yenāhamanṛṇaḥ syāṃ dwijottama |
tattwattaḥ prāptumicchāmi waraṃ wedawidāṃ wara ||11||

apatyāyepsitāṃ mahyaṃ mahiṣīṃ gantumarhasi |
śīlarūpaguṇopetāmikṣwākukulawṛddhaye ||12||

gandharwa uwāca||

dadānītyewa taṃ tatra rājānaṃ pratyuwāca ha |
wasiṣṭhaḥ parameṣwāsaṃ satyasandho dwijottamaḥ ||13||

tataḥ pratiyayau kāle wasiṣṭhasahito'nagha |
khyātaṃ purawaraṃ lokeṣwayodhyāṃ manujeśwaraḥ ||14||

taṃ prajāḥ pratimodantyaḥ sarwāḥ pratyudyayustadā |
wipāpmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ diwaukasa iweśwaram ||15||

acirātsa manuṣyendro nagarīṃ puṇyakarmaṇām |
wiweśa sahitastena wasiṣṭhena mahātmanā ||16||

dadṛśustaṃ tato rājannayodhyāwāsino janāḥ |
puṣyeṇa sahitaṃ kāle diwākaramiwoditam ||17||

sa hi tāṃ pūrayāmāsa lakṣmyā lakṣmīwatāṃ waraḥ |
ayodhyāṃ wyoma śītāṃśuḥ śaratkāla iwoditaḥ ||18||

saṃsiktamṛṣṭapanthānaṃ patākocchrayabhūṣitam |
manaḥ prahlādayāmāsā tasya tatpuramuttamam ||19||

tuṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇā sā purī kurunandana |
aśobhata tadā tena śakreṇewāmarāwatī ||20||

tataḥ prawiṣṭe rājendre tasminrājani tāṃ purīm |
tasya rājño''jñayā dewī wasiṣṭhamupacakrame ||21||

ṛtāwatha maharṣiḥ sa sambabhūwa tayā saha |
dewyā diwyena widhinā wasiṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhabhāgṛṣiḥ ||22||

atha tasyāṃ samutpanne garbhe sa munisattamaḥ |
rājñābhiwāditastena jagāma punarāśramam ||23||

dīrghakāladhṛtaṃ garbhaṃ suṣāwa na tu taṃ yadā |
sātha dewyaśmanā kukṣiṃ nirbibheda tadā swakam ||24||

dwādaśe'tha tato warṣe sa jajñe manujarṣabha |
aśmako nāma rājarṣiḥ potanaṃ yo nyaweśayat ||25||






              aurwopākhyānam
                  169


gandharwa uwāca||

āśramasthā tataḥ putramadṛśyantī wyajāyata |
śakteḥ kulakaraṃ rājandwitīyamiwa śaktinam ||1||

jātakarmādikāstasya kriyāḥ sa munipuṅgawaḥ |
pautrasya bharataśreṣṭha cakāra bhagawānswayam ||2||

parāsuśca yatastena wasiṣṭhaḥ sthāpitastadā |
garbhasthena tato loke parāśara iti smṛtaḥ ||3||

amanyata sa dharmātmā wasiṣṭhaṃ pitaraṃ tadā |
janmaprabhṛti tasmiṃśca pitarīwa wyawartata ||4||

sa tāta iti wiprarṣiṃ wasiṣṭhaṃ pratyabhāṣata |
mātuḥ samakṣaṃ kaunteya adṛśyantyāḥ parantapa ||5||

tāteti paripūrṇārthaṃ tasya tanmadhuraṃ wacaḥ |
adṛśyantyaśrupūrṇākṣī śṛṇwantī tamuwāca ha ||6||

mā tāta tāta tāteti na te tāto mahāmuniḥ |
rakṣasā bhakṣitastāta tawa tāto wanāntare ||7||

manyase yaṃ tu tāteti naiṣa tātastawānagha |
āryastweṣa pitā tasya pitustawa mahātmanaḥ ||8||

sa ewamukto duḥkhārtaḥ satyawāgṛṣisattamaḥ |
sarwalokawināśāya matiṃ cakre mahāmanāḥ ||9||

taṃ tathā niścitātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ mahātapāḥ |
wasiṣṭho wārayāmāsa hetunā yena tacchṛṇu ||10||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

kṛtawīrya iti khyāto babhūwa nṛpatiḥ kṣitau |
yājyo wedawidāṃ loke bhṛgūṇāṃ pārthiwarṣabhaḥ ||11||

sa tānagrabhujastāta dhānyena ca dhanena ca |
somānte tarpayāmāsa wipulena wiśāṃ patiḥ ||12||

tasminnṛpatiśārdūle swaryāte'tha kadācana |
babhūwa tatkuleyānāṃ drawyakāryamupasthitam ||13||

te bhṛgūṇāṃ dhanaṃ jñātwā rājānaḥ sarwa ewa ha |
yāciṣṇawo'bhijagmustāṃstāta bhārgawasattamān ||14||

bhūmau tu nidadhuḥ kecidbhṛgawo dhanamakṣayam |
daduḥ keciddwijātibhyo jñātwā kṣatriyato bhayam ||15||

bhṛgawastu daduḥ kecitteṣāṃ wittaṃ yathepsitam |
kṣatriyāṇāṃ tadā tāta kāraṇāntaradarśanāt ||16||

tato mahītalaṃ tāta kṣatriyeṇa yadṛcchayā |
khanatādhigataṃ wittaṃ kenacidbhṛguweśmani ||17||

tadwittaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarwe sametāḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ ||17||

awamanya tataḥ kopādbhṛgūṃstāñśaraṇāgatān |
nijaghnuste maheṣwāsāḥ sarwāṃstānniśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ||18||

ā garbhādanukṛntantaśceruścaiwa wasundharām ||18||

tata ucchidyamāneṣu bhṛguṣwewaṃ bhayāttadā |
bhṛgupatnyo giriṃ tāta himawantaṃ prapedire ||19||

tāsāmanyatamā garbhaṃ bhayāddādhāra taijasam |
ūruṇaikena wāmorūrbhartuḥ kulawiwṛddhaye ||20||

dadṛśurbrāhmaṇīṃ tāṃ te dīpyamānāṃ swatejasā ||20||

atha garbhaḥ sa bhittworuṃ brāhmaṇyā nirjagāma ha |
muṣṇandṛṣṭīḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ madhyāhna iwa bhāskaraḥ ||21||

tataścakṣurwiyuktāste giridurgeṣu babhramuḥ ||21||

tataste moghasaṅkalpā bhayārtāḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ |
brahmaṇīṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmurdṛṣṭyarthaṃ tāmaninditām ||22||

ūcuścaināṃ mahābhāgāṃ kṣatriyāste wicetasaḥ |
jyotiḥprahīṇā duḥkhārtāḥ śāntārciṣa iwāgnayaḥ ||23||

bhagawatyāḥ prasādena gacchetkṣatraṃ sacakṣuṣam |
upāramya ca gacchema sahitāḥ pāpakarmaṇaḥ ||24||

saputrā twaṃ prasādaṃ naḥ sarweṣāṃ kartumarhasi |
punardṛṣṭipradānena rājñaḥ santrātumarhasi ||25||






                  170


brāhmaṇyuwāca||

nāhaṃ gṛhṇāmi wastāta dṛṣṭīrnāsti ruṣānwitā |
ayaṃ tu bhārgawo nūnamūrujaḥ kupito'dya waḥ ||1||

tena cakṣūṃṣi wastāta nūnaṃ kopānmahātmanā |
smaratā nihatānbandhūnādattāni na saṃśayaḥ ||2||

garbhānapi yadā yūyaṃ bhṛgūṇāṃ ghnata putrakāḥ |
tadāyamūruṇā garbho mayā warṣaśataṃ dhṛtaḥ ||3||

ṣaḍaṅgaścākhilo weda imaṃ garbhasthamewa hi |
wiweśa bhṛguwaṃśasya bhūyaḥ priyacikīrṣayā ||4||

so'yaṃ pitṛwadhānnūnaṃ krodhādwo hantumicchati |
tejasā yasya diwyena cakṣūṃṣi muṣitāni waḥ ||5||

tamimaṃ tāta yācadhwamaurwaṃ mama sutottamam |
ayaṃ waḥ praṇipātena tuṣṭo dṛṣṭīrwimokṣyati ||6||

gandharwa uwāca||

ewamuktāstataḥ sarwe rājānaste tamūrujam |
ūcuḥ prasīdeti tadā prasādaṃ ca cakāra saḥ ||7||

anenaiwa ca wikhyāto nāmnā lokeṣu sattamaḥ |
sa aurwa iti wiprarṣirūruṃ bhittwā wyajāyata ||8||

cakṣūṃṣi pratilabhyātha pratijagmustato nṛpāḥ |
bhārgawastu munirmene sarwalokaparābhawam ||9||

sa cakre tāta lokānāṃ wināśāya mahāmanāḥ |
sarweṣāmewa kārtsnyena manaḥ prawaṇamātmanaḥ ||10||

icchannapacitiṃ kartuṃ bhṛgūṇāṃ bhṛgusattamaḥ |
sarwalokawināśāya tapasā mahataidhitaḥ ||11||

tāpayāmāsa lokānsa sadewāsuramānuṣān |
tapasogreṇa mahatā nandayiṣyanpitāmahān ||12||

tatastaṃ pitarastāta wijñāya bhṛgusattamam |
pitṛlokādupāgamya sarwa ūcuridaṃ wacaḥ ||13||

aurwa dṛṣṭaḥ prabhāwaste tapasograsya putraka |
prasādaṃ kuru lokānāṃ niyaccha krodhamātmanaḥ ||14||

nānīśairhi tadā tāta bhṛgubhirbhāwitātmabhiḥ |
wadho'bhyupekṣitaḥ sarwaiḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ wihiṃsatām ||15||

āyuṣā hi prakṛṣṭena yadā naḥ kheda āwiśat |
tadāsmābhirwadhastāta kṣatriyairīpsitaḥ swayam ||16||

nikhātaṃ taddhi wai wittaṃ kenacidbhṛguweśmani |
wairāyaiwa tadā nyastaṃ kṣatriyānkopayiṣṇubhiḥ ||17||

kiṃ hi wittena naḥ kāryaṃ swargepsūnāṃ dwijarṣabha ||17||

yadā tu mṛtyurādātuṃ na naḥ śaknoti sarwaśaḥ |
tadāsmābhirayaṃ dṛṣṭa upāyastāta saṃmataḥ ||18||

ātmahā ca pumāṃstāta na lokāṃllabhate śubhān |
tato'smābhiḥ samīkṣyaiwaṃ nātmanātmā wināśitaḥ ||19||

na caitannaḥ priyaṃ tāta yadidaṃ kartumicchasi |
niyacchedaṃ manaḥ pāpātsarwalokaparābhawāt ||20||

na hi naḥ kṣatriyāḥ kecinna lokāḥ sapta putraka |
dūṣayanti tapastejaḥ krodhamutpatitaṃ jahi ||21||






                  171


aurwa uwāca||

uktawānasmi yāṃ krodhātpratijñāṃ pitarastadā |
sarwalokawināśāya na sā me witathā bhawet ||1||

wṛthāroṣapratijño hi nāhaṃ jīwitumutsahe |
anistīrṇo hi māṃ roṣo dahedagniriwāraṇim ||2||

yo hi kāraṇataḥ krodhaṃ sañjātaṃ kṣantumarhati |
nālaṃ sa manujaḥ samyaktriwargaṃ parirakṣitum ||3||

aśiṣṭānāṃ niyantā hi śiṣṭānāṃ parirakṣatā |
sthāne roṣaḥ prayuktaḥ syānnṛpaiḥ swargajigīṣubhiḥ ||4||

aśrauṣamahamūrustho garbhaśayyāgatastadā |
ārāwaṃ mātṛwargasya bhṛgūṇāṃ kṣatriyairwadhe ||5||

sāmarairhi yadā lokairbhṛgūṇāṃ kṣatriyādhamaiḥ |
āgarbhotsādanaṃ kṣāntaṃ tadā māṃ manyurāwiṣat ||6||

āpūrṇakośāḥ kila me mātaraḥ pitarastathā |
bhayātsarweṣu lokeṣu nādhijagmuḥ parāyaṇam ||7||

tānbhṛgūṇāṃ tadā dārānkaścinnābhyawapadyata |
yadā tadā dadhāreyamūruṇaikena māṃ śubhā ||8||

pratiṣeddhā hi pāpasya yadā lokeṣu widyate |
tadā sarweṣu lokeṣu pāpakṛnnopapadyate ||9||

yadā tu pratiṣeddhāraṃ pāpo na labhate kwacit |
tiṣṭhanti bahawo loke tadā pāpeṣu karmasu ||10||

jānannapi ca yaḥ pāpaṃ śaktimānna niyacchati |
īśaḥ sanso'pi tenaiwa karmaṇā samprayujyate ||11||

rājabhiśceśwaraiścaiwa yadi wai pitaro mama |
śaktairna śakitā trātumiṣṭaṃ matweha jīwitam ||12||

ata eṣāmahaṃ kruddho lokānāmīśwaro'dya san |
bhawatāṃ tu waco nāhamalaṃ samatiwartitum ||13||

mama cāpi bhawedetadīśwarasya sato mahat |
upekṣamāṇasya punarlokānāṃ kilbiṣādbhayam ||14||

yaścāyaṃ manyujo me'gnirlokānādātumicchati |
dahedeṣa ca māmewa nigṛhītaḥ swatejasā ||15||

bhawatāṃ ca wijānāmi sarwalokahitepsutām |
tasmādwidadhwaṃ yacchreyo lokānāṃ mama ceśwarāḥ ||16||

pitara ūcuḥ||

ya eṣa manyujaste'gnirlokānādātumicchati |
apsu taṃ muñca bhadraṃ te lokā hyapsu pratiṣṭhitāḥ ||17||

āpomayāḥ sarwarasāḥ sarwamāpomayaṃ jagat |
tasmādapsu wimuñcemaṃ krodhāgniṃ dwijasattama ||18||

ayaṃ tiṣṭhatu te wipra yadīcchasi mahodadhau |
manyujo'gnirdahannāpo lokā hyāpomayāḥ smṛtāḥ ||19||

ewaṃ pratijñā satyeyaṃ tawānagha bhawiṣyati |
na caiwa sāmarā lokā gamiṣyanti parābhawam ||20||

wasiṣṭha uwāca||

tatastaṃ krodhajaṃ tāta aurwo'gniṃ waruṇālaye |
utsasarja sa caiwāpa upayuṅkte mahodadhau ||21||

mahaddhayaśiro bhūtwā yattadwedawido widuḥ |
tamagnimudgiranwaktrātpibatyāpo mahodadhau ||22||

tasmāttwamapi bhadraṃ te na lokānhantumarhasi |
parāśara parāndharmāñjānañjñānawatāṃ wara ||23||






                  172


gandharwa uwāca||

ewamuktaḥ sa wiprarṣirwasiṣṭhena mahātmanā |
nyayacchadātmanaḥ kopaṃ sarwalokaparābhawāt ||1||

īje ca sa mahātejāḥ sarwawedawidāṃ waraḥ |
ṛṣī rākṣasasatreṇa śākteyo'tha parāśaraḥ ||2||

tato wṛddhāṃśca bālāṃśca rākṣasānsa mahāmuniḥ |
dadāha witate yajñe śakterwadhamanusmaran ||3||

na hi taṃ wārayāmāsa wasiṣṭho rakṣasāṃ wadhāt |
dwitīyāmasya mā bhāṅkṣaṃ pratijñāmiti niścayāt ||4||

trayāṇāṃ pāwakānāṃ sa satre tasminmahāmuniḥ |
āsītpurastāddīptānāṃ caturtha iwa pāwakaḥ ||5||

tena yajñena śubhreṇa hūyamānena yuktitaḥ |
tadwidīpitamākāśaṃ sūryeṇewa ghanātyaye ||6||

taṃ wasiṣṭhādayaḥ sarwe munayastatra menire |
tejasā diwi dīpyantaṃ dwitīyamiwa bhāskaram ||7||

tataḥ paramaduṣprāpamanyairṛṣirudāradhīḥ |
samāpipayiṣuḥ satraṃ tamatriḥ samupāgamat ||8||

tathā pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuścaiwa mahākratum |
upājagmuramitraghna rakṣasāṃ jīwitepsayā ||9||

pulastyastu wadhātteṣāṃ rakṣasāṃ bharatarṣabha |
uwācedaṃ wacaḥ pārtha parāśaramariṃdamam ||10||

kaccittātāpawighnaṃ te kaccinnandasi putraka |
ajānatāmadoṣāṇāṃ sarweṣāṃ rakṣasāṃ wadhāt ||11||

prajocchedamimaṃ mahyaṃ sarwaṃ somapasattama |
adharmiṣṭhaṃ wariṣṭhaḥ sankuruṣe twaṃ parāśara ||12||

rājā kalmāṣapādaśca diwamāroḍhumicchati ||12||

ye ca śaktyawarāḥ putrā wasiṣṭhasya mahāmuneḥ |
te ca sarwe mudā yuktā modante sahitāḥ suraiḥ ||13||

sarwametadwasiṣṭhasya widitaṃ wai mahāmune ||13||

rakṣasāṃ ca samuccheda eṣa tāta tapaswinām |
nimittabhūtastwaṃ cātra kratau wāsiṣṭhanandana ||14||

sa satraṃ muñca bhadraṃ te samāptamidamastu te ||14||

ewamuktaḥ pulastyena wasiṣṭhena ca dhīmatā |
tadā samāpayāmāsa satraṃ śāktiḥ parāśaraḥ ||15||

sarwarākṣasasatrāya sambhṛtaṃ pāwakaṃ muniḥ |
uttare himawatpārśwe utsasarja mahāwane ||16||

sa tatrādyāpi rakṣāṃsi wṛkṣānaśmāna ewa ca |
bhakṣayandṛśyate wahniḥ sadā parwaṇi parwaṇi ||17||






                  173


arjuna uwāca||

rājñā kalmāṣapādena gurau brahmawidāṃ ware |
kāraṇaṃ kiṃ puraskṛtya bhāryā wai saṃniyojitā ||1||

jānatā ca paraṃ dharmaṃ lokyaṃ tena mahātmanā |
agamyāgamanaṃ kasmādwasiṣṭhena mahātmanā ||2||

kṛtaṃ tena purā sarwaṃ waktumarhasi pṛcchataḥ ||2||

gandharwa uwāca||

dhanañjaya nibodhedaṃ yanmāṃ twaṃ paripṛcchasi |
wasiṣṭhaṃ prati durdharṣaṃ tathāmitrasahaṃ nṛpam ||3||

kathitaṃ te mayā pūrwaṃ yathā śaptaḥ sa pārthiwaḥ |
śaktinā bharataśreṣṭha wāsiṣṭhena mahātmanā ||4||

sa tu śāpawaśaṃ prāptaḥ krodhaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ |
nirjagāma purādrājā sahadāraḥ parantapaḥ ||5||

araṇyaṃ nirjanaṃ gatwā sadāraḥ paricakrame |
nānāmṛgagaṇākīrṇaṃ nānāsattwasamākulam ||6||

nānāgulmalatācchannaṃ nānādrumasamāwṛtam |
araṇyaṃ ghorasaṃnādaṃ śāpagrastaḥ paribhraman ||7||

sa kadācitkṣudhāwiṣṭo mṛgayanbhakṣamātmanaḥ |
dadarśa suparikliṣṭaḥ kasmiṃścidwananirjhare ||8||

brāhmaṇīṃ brāhmaṇaṃ caiwa maithunāyopasaṅgatau ||8||

tau samīkṣya tu witrastāwakṛtārthau pradhāwitau |
tayośca drawatorwipraṃ jagṛhe nṛpatirbalāt ||9||

dṛṣṭwā gṛhītaṃ bhartāramatha brāhmaṇyabhāṣata |
śṛṇu rājanwaco mahyaṃ yattwāṃ wakṣyāmi suwrata ||10||

ādityawaṃśaprabhawastwaṃ hi lokapariśrutaḥ |
apramattaḥ sthito dharme guruśuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ ||11||

śāpaṃ prāpto'si durdharṣa na pāpaṃ kartumarhasi |
ṛtukāle tu samprāpte bhartrāsmyadya samāgatā ||12||

akṛtārthā hyahaṃ bhartrā prasawārthaśca me mahān |
prasīda nṛpatiśreṣṭha bhartā me'yaṃ wisṛjyatām ||13||

ewaṃ wikrośamānāyāstasyāḥ sa sunṛśaṃsakṛt |
bhartāraṃ bhakṣayāmāsa wyāghro mṛgamiwepsitam ||14||

tasyāḥ krodhābhibhūtāyā yadaśru nyapatadbhuwi |
so'gniḥ samabhawaddīptastaṃ ca deśaṃ wyadīpayat ||15||

tataḥ sā śokasantaptā bhartṛwyasanaduḥkhitā |
kalmāṣapādaṃ rājarṣimaśapadbrāhmaṇī ruṣā ||16||

yasmānmamākṛtārthāyāstwayā kṣudra nṛśaṃsawat |
prekṣantyā bhakṣito me'dya prabhurbhartā mahāyaśāḥ ||17||

tasmāttwamapi durbuddhe macchāpapariwikṣataḥ |
patnīmṛtāwanuprāpya sadyastyakṣyasi jīwitam ||18||

yasya carṣerwasiṣṭhasya twayā putrā wināśitāḥ |
tena saṅgamya te bhāryā tanayaṃ janayiṣyati ||19||

sa te waṃśakaraḥ putro bhawiṣyati nṛpādhama ||19||

ewaṃ śaptwā tu rājānaṃ sā tamāṅgirasī śubhā |
tasyaiwa saṃnidhau dīptaṃ prawiweśa hutāśanam ||20||

wasiṣṭhaśca mahābhāgaḥ sarwametadapaśyata |
jñānayogena mahatā tapasā ca parantapa ||21||

muktaśāpaśca rājarṣiḥ kālena mahatā tataḥ |
ṛtukāle'bhipatito madayantyā niwāritaḥ ||22||

na hi sasmāra nṛpatistaṃ śāpaṃ śāpamohitaḥ |
dewyāḥ so'tha wacaḥ śrutwā sa tasyā nṛpasattamaḥ ||23||

taṃ ca śāpamanusmṛtya paryatapyadbhṛśaṃ tadā ||23||

etasmātkāraṇādrājā wasiṣṭhaṃ saṃnyayojayat |
swadāre bharataśreṣṭha śāpadoṣasamanwitaḥ ||24||






              draupadīswayaṃwaraparwa
                  174


arjuna uwāca||

asmākamanurūpo wai yaḥ syādgandharwa wedawit |
purohitastamācakṣwa sarwaṃ hi widitaṃ tawa ||1||

gandharwa uwāca||

yawīyāndewalasyaiṣa wane bhrātā tapasyati |
dhaumya utkocake tīrthe taṃ wṛṇudhwaṃ yadīcchatha ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato'rjuno'stramāgneyaṃ pradadau tadyathāwidhi |
gandharwāya tadā prīto wacanaṃ cedamabrawīt ||3||

twayyewa tāwattiṣṭhantu hayā gandharwasattama |
karmakāle grahīṣyāmi swasti te'stwiti cābrawīt ||4||

te'nyonyamabhisampūjya gandharwaḥ pāṇḍawāśca ha |
ramyādbhāgīrathīkacchādyathākāmaṃ pratasthire ||5||

tata utkocakaṃ tīrthaṃ gatwā dhaumyāśramaṃ tu te |
taṃ wawruḥ pāṇḍawā dhaumyaṃ paurohityāya bhārata ||6||

tāndhaumyaḥ pratijagrāha sarwawedawidāṃ waraḥ |
pādyena phalamūlena paurohityena caiwa ha ||7||

te tadāśaṃsire labdhāṃ śriyaṃ rājyaṃ ca pāṇḍawāḥ |
taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ puraskṛtya pāñcālyāśca swayaṃwaram ||8||

mātṛṣaṣṭhāstu te tena guruṇā saṅgatāstadā |
nāthawantamiwātmānaṃ menire bharatarṣabhāḥ ||9||

sa hi wedārthatattwajñasteṣāṃ gururudāradhīḥ |
tena dharmawidā pārthā yājyāḥ sarwawidā kṛtāḥ ||10||

wīrāṃstu sa hi tānmene prāptarājyānswadharmataḥ |
buddhiwīryabalotsāhairyuktāndewāniwāparān ||11||

kṛtaswastyayanāstena tataste manujādhipāḥ |
menire sahitā gantuṃ pāñcālyāstaṃ swayaṃwaram ||12||






                  175


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataste naraśārdūlā bhrātaraḥ pañca pāṇḍawāḥ |
prayayurdraupadīṃ draṣṭuṃ taṃ ca dewamahotsawam ||1||

te prayātā narawyāghrā mātrā saha parantapāḥ |
brāhmaṇāndadṛśurmārge gacchataḥ sagaṇānbahūn ||2||

tānūcurbrāhmaṇā rājanpāṇḍawānbrahmacāriṇaḥ |
kwa bhawanto gamiṣyanti kuto wāgacchateti ha ||3||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

āgatānekacakrāyāḥ sodaryāndewadarśinaḥ |
bhawanto hi wijānantu sahitānmātṛcāriṇaḥ ||4||

brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ||

gacchatādyaiwa pāñcālāndrupadasya niweśanam |
swayaṃwaro mahāṃstatra bhawitā sumahādhanaḥ ||5||

ekasārthaṃ prayātāḥ smo wayamapyatra gāminaḥ |
tatra hyadbhutasaṅkāśo bhawitā sumahotsawaḥ ||6||

yajñasenasya duhitā drupadasya mahātmanaḥ |
wedīmadhyātsamutpannā padmapatranibhekṣaṇā ||7||

darśanīyānawadyāṅgī sukumārī manaswinī |
dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhaginī droṇaśatroḥ pratāpinaḥ ||8||

yo jātaḥ kawacī khaḍgī saśaraḥ saśarāsanaḥ |
susamiddhe mahābāhuḥ pāwake pāwakaprabhaḥ ||9||

swasā tasyānawadyāṅgī draupadī tanumadhyamā |
nīlotpalasamo gandho yasyāḥ krośātprawāyati ||10||

tāṃ yajñasenasya sutāṃ swayaṃwarakṛtakṣaṇām |
gacchāmahe wayaṃ draṣṭuṃ taṃ ca dewamahotsawam ||11||

rājāno rājaputrāśca yajwāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ |
swādhyāyawantaḥ śucayo mahātmāno yatawratāḥ ||12||

taruṇā darśanīyāśca nānādeśasamāgatāḥ |
mahārathāḥ kṛtāstrāśca samupaiṣyanti bhūmipāḥ ||13||

te tatra wiwidhāndāyānwijayārthaṃ nareśwarāḥ |
pradāsyanti dhanaṃ gāśca bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca sarwaśaḥ ||14||

pratigṛhya ca tatsarwaṃ dṛṣṭwā caiwa swayaṃwaram |
anubhūyotsawaṃ caiwa gamiṣyāmo yathepsitam ||15||

naṭā waitālikāścaiwa nartakāḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ |
niyodhakāśca deśebhyaḥ sameṣyanti mahābalāḥ ||16||

ewaṃ kautūhalaṃ kṛtwā dṛṣṭwā ca pratigṛhya ca |
sahāsmābhirmahātmānaḥ punaḥ pratiniwartsyatha ||17||

darśanīyāṃśca waḥ sarwāndewarūpānawasthitān |
samīkṣya kṛṣṇā warayetsaṅgatyānyatamaṃ waram ||18||

ayaṃ bhrātā tawa śrīmāndarśanīyo mahābhujaḥ |
niyudhyamāno wijayetsaṅgatyā drawiṇaṃ bahu ||19||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

paramaṃ bho gamiṣyāmo draṣṭuṃ dewamahotsawam |
bhawadbhiḥ sahitāḥ sarwe kanyāyāstaṃ swayaṃwaram ||20||






                  176


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktāḥ prayātāste pāṇḍawā janamejaya |
rājñā dakṣiṇapāñcālāndrupadenābhirakṣitān ||1||

tataste taṃ mahātmānaṃ śuddhātmānamakalmaṣam |
dadṛśuḥ pāṇḍawā rājanpathi dwaipāyanaṃ tadā ||2||

tasmai yathāwatsatkāraṃ kṛtwā tena ca sāntwitāḥ |
kathānte cābhyanujñātāḥ prayayurdrupadakṣayam ||3||

paśyanto ramaṇīyāni wanāni ca sarāṃsi ca |
tatra tatra wasantaśca śanairjagmurmahārathāḥ ||4||

swādhyāyawantaḥ śucayo madhurāḥ priyawādinaḥ |
ānupūrwyeṇa samprāptāḥ pāñcālānkurunandanāḥ ||5||

te tu dṛṣṭwā puraṃ tacca skandhāwāraṃ ca pāṇḍawāḥ |
kumbhakārasya śālāyāṃ niweśaṃ cakrire tadā ||6||

tatra bhaikṣaṃ samājahrurbrāhmīṃ wṛttiṃ samāśritāḥ |
tāṃśca prāptāṃstadā wīrāñjajñire na narāḥ kwacit ||7||

yajñasenasya kāmastu pāṇḍawāya kirīṭine |
kṛṣṇāṃ dadyāmiti sadā na caitadwiwṛṇoti saḥ ||8||

so'nweṣamāṇaḥ kaunteyānpāñcālyo janamejaya |
dṛḍhaṃ dhanuranāyamyaṃ kārayāmāsa bhārata ||9||

yantraṃ waihāyasaṃ cāpi kārayāmāsa kṛtrimam |
tena yantreṇa sahitaṃ rājā lakṣyaṃ ca kāñcanam ||10||

drupada uwāca||

idaṃ sajyaṃ dhanuḥ kṛtwā sajyenānena sāyakaiḥ |
atītya lakṣyaṃ yo weddhā sa labdhā matsutāmiti ||11||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

iti sa drupado rājā sarwataḥ samaghoṣayat |
tacchrutwā pārthiwāḥ sarwe samīyustatra bhārata ||12||

ṛṣayaśca mahātmānaḥ swayaṃwaradidṛkṣayā |
duryodhanapurogāśca sakarṇāḥ kurawo nṛpa ||13||

brāhmaṇāśca mahābhāgā deśebhyaḥ samupāgaman |
te'bhyarcitā rājagaṇā drupadena mahātmanā ||14||

tataḥ paurajanāḥ sarwe sāgaroddhūtaniḥswanāḥ |
śiśumārapuraṃ prāpya nyawiśaṃste ca pārthiwāḥ ||15||

prāguttareṇa nagarādbhūmibhāge same śubhe |
samājawāṭaḥ śuśubhe bhawanaiḥ sarwato wṛtaḥ ||16||

prākāraparikhopeto dwāratoraṇamaṇḍitaḥ |
witānena wicitreṇa sarwataḥ samawastṛtaḥ ||17||

tūryaughaśatasaṅkīrṇaḥ parārdhyāgurudhūpitaḥ |
candanodakasiktaśca mālyadāmaiśca śobhitaḥ ||18||

kailāsaśikharaprakhyairnabhastalawilekhibhiḥ |
sarwataḥ saṃwṛtairnaddhaḥ prāsādaiḥ sukṛtocchritaiḥ ||19||

suwarṇajālasaṃwītairmaṇikuṭṭimabhūṣitaiḥ |
sukhārohaṇasopānairmahāsanaparicchadaiḥ ||20||

agrāmyasamawacchannairagurūttamawāsitaiḥ |
haṃsācchawarṇairbahubhirāyojanasugandhibhiḥ ||21||

asambādhaśatadwāraiḥ śayanāsanaśobhitaiḥ |
bahudhātupinaddhāṅgairhimawacchikharairiwa ||22||

tatra nānāprakāreṣu wimāneṣu swalaṅkṛtāḥ |
spardhamānāstadānyonyaṃ niṣeduḥ sarwapārthiwāḥ ||23||

tatropawiṣṭāndadṛśurmahāsattwaparākramān |
rājasiṃhānmahābhāgānkṛṣṇāguruwibhūṣitān ||24||

mahāprasādānbrahmaṇyānswarāṣṭraparirakṣiṇaḥ |
priyānsarwasya lokasya sukṛtaiḥ karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ ||25||

mañceṣu ca parārdhyeṣu paurajānapadā janāḥ |
kṛṣṇādarśanatuṣṭyarthaṃ sarwataḥ samupāwiśan ||26||

brāhmaṇaiste ca sahitāḥ pāṇḍawāḥ samupāwiśan |
ṛddhiṃ pāñcālarājasya paśyantastāmanuttamām ||27||

tataḥ samājo wawṛdhe sa rājandiwasānbahūn |
ratnapradānabahulaḥ śobhito naṭanartakaiḥ ||28||

wartamāne samāje tu ramaṇīye'hni ṣoḍaśe |
āplutāṅgī suwasanā sarwābharaṇabhūṣitā ||29||

wīrakāṃsyamupādāya kāñcanaṃ samalaṅkṛtam |
awatīrṇā tato raṅgaṃ draupadī bharatarṣabha ||30||

purohitaḥ somakānāṃ mantrawidbrāhmaṇaḥ śuciḥ |
paristīrya juhāwāgnimājyena widhinā tadā ||31||

sa tarpayitwā jwalanaṃ brāhmaṇānswasti wācya ca |
wārayāmāsa sarwāṇi wāditrāṇi samantataḥ ||32||

niḥśabde tu kṛte tasmindhṛṣṭadyumno wiśāṃ pate |
raṅgamadhyagatastatra meghagambhīrayā girā ||33||

wākyamuccairjagādedaṃ ślakṣṇamarthawaduttamam ||33||

idaṃ dhanurlakṣyamime ca bāṇāḥ; śṛṇwantu me pārthiwāḥ sarwa ewa |
yantracchidreṇābhyatikramya lakṣyaṃ; samarpayadhwaṃ khagamairdaśārdhaiḥ ||34||

etatkartā karma suduṣkaraṃ yaḥ; kulena rūpeṇa balena yuktaḥ |
tasyādya bhāryā bhaginī mameyaṃ; kṛṣṇā bhawitrī na mṛṣā brawīmi ||35||

tānewamuktwā drupadasya putraḥ; paścādidaṃ draupadīmabhyuwāca |
nāmnā ca gotreṇa ca karmaṇā ca; saṅkīrtayaṃstānnṛpatīnsametān ||36||






                  177


dhṛṣṭadyumna uwāca||

duryodhano durwiṣaho durmukho duṣpradharṣaṇaḥ |
wiwiṃśatirwikarṇaśca saho duḥśāsanaḥ samaḥ ||1||

yuyutsurwātawegaśca bhīmawegadharastathā |
ugrāyudho balākī ca kanakāyurwirocanaḥ ||2||

sukuṇḍalaścitrasenaḥ suwarcāḥ kanakadhwajaḥ |
nandako bāhuśālī ca kuṇḍajo wikaṭastathā ||3||

ete cānye ca bahawo dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābalāḥ |
karṇena sahitā wīrāstwadarthaṃ samupāgatāḥ ||4||

śatasaṅkhyā mahātmānaḥ prathitāḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ ||4||

śakuniśca balaścaiwa wṛṣako'tha bṛhadbalaḥ |
ete gāndhārarājasya sutāḥ sarwe samāgatāḥ ||5||

aśwatthāmā ca bhojaśca sarwaśastrabhṛtāṃ warau |
samawetau mahātmānau twadarthe samalaṅkṛtau ||6||

bṛhanto maṇimāṃścaiwa daṇḍadhāraśca wīryawān |
sahadewo jayatseno meghasandhiśca māgadhaḥ ||7||

wirāṭaḥ saha putrābhyāṃ śaṅkhenaiwottareṇa ca |
wārdhakṣemiḥ suwarcāśca senābinduśca pārthiwaḥ ||8||

abhibhūḥ saha putreṇa sudāmnā ca suwarcasā |
sumitraḥ sukumāraśca wṛkaḥ satyadhṛtistathā ||9||

sūryadhwajo rocamāno nīlaścitrāyudhastathā |
aṃśumāṃścekitānaśca śreṇimāṃśca mahābalaḥ ||10||

samudrasenaputraśca candrasenaḥ pratāpawān |
jalasandhaḥ pitāputrau sudaṇḍo daṇḍa ewa ca ||11||

pauṇḍrako wāsudewaśca bhagadattaśca wīryawān |
kaliṅgastāmraliptaśca pattanādhipatistathā ||12||

madrarājastathā śalyaḥ sahaputro mahārathaḥ |
rukmāṅgadena wīreṇa tathā rukmarathena ca ||13||

kaurawyaḥ somadattaśca putrāścāsya mahārathāḥ |
samawetāstrayaḥ śūrā bhūrirbhūriśrawāḥ śalaḥ ||14||

sudakṣiṇaśca kāmbojo dṛḍhadhanwā ca kaurawaḥ |
bṛhadbalaḥ suṣeṇaśca śibirauśīnarastathā ||15||

saṅkarṣaṇo wāsudewo raukmiṇeyaśca wīryawān |
sāmbaśca cārudeṣṇaśca sāraṇo'tha gadastathā ||16||

akrūraḥ sātyakiścaiwa uddhawaśca mahābalaḥ |
kṛtawarmā ca hārdikyaḥ pṛthurwipṛthurewa ca ||17||

wiḍūrathaśca kaṅkaśca samīkaḥ sāramejayaḥ |
wīro wātapatiścaiwa jhillī piṇḍārakastathā ||18||

uśīnaraśca wikrānto wṛṣṇayaste prakīrtitāḥ ||18||

bhagīratho bṛhatkṣatraḥ saindhawaśca jayadrathaḥ |
bṛhadratho bāhlikaśca śrutāyuśca mahārathaḥ ||19||

ulūkaḥ kaitawo rājā citrāṅgadaśubhāṅgadau |
watsarājaśca dhṛtimānkosalādhipatistathā ||20||

ete cānye ca bahawo nānājanapadeśwarāḥ |
twadarthamāgatā bhadre kṣatriyāḥ prathitā bhuwi ||21||

ete wetsyanti wikrāntāstwadarthaṃ lakṣyamuttamam |
widhyeta ya imaṃ lakṣyaṃ warayethāḥ śubhe'dya tam ||22||






                  178


waiśampāyana uwāca||

te'laṅkṛtāḥ kuṇḍalino yuwānaḥ; parasparaṃ spardhamānāḥ sametāḥ |
astraṃ balaṃ cātmani manyamānāḥ; sarwe samutpeturahaṅkṛtena ||1||

rūpeṇa wīryeṇa kulena caiwa; dharmeṇa caiwāpi ca yauwanena |
samṛddhadarpā madawegabhinnā; mattā yathā haimawatā gajendrāḥ ||2||

parasparaṃ spardhayā prekṣamāṇāḥ; saṅkalpajenāpi pariplutāṅgāḥ |
kṛṣṇā mamaiṣetyabhibhāṣamāṇā; nṛpāsanebhyaḥ sahasopatasthuḥ ||3||

te kṣatriyā raṅgagatāḥ sametā; jigīṣamāṇā drupadātmajāṃ tām |
cakāśire parwatarājakanyā; mumāṃ yathā dewagaṇāḥ sametāḥ ||4||

kandarpabāṇābhinipīḍitāṅgāḥ; kṛṣṇāgataiste hṛdayairnarendrāḥ |
raṅgāwatīrṇā drupadātmajārthaṃ; dweṣyānhi cakruḥ suhṛdo'pi tatra ||5||

athāyayurdewagaṇā wimānai; rudrādityā wasawo'thāświnau ca |
sādhyāśca sarwe marutastathaiwa; yamaṃ puraskṛtya dhaneśwaraṃ ca ||6||

daityāḥ suparṇāśca mahoragāśca; dewarṣayo guhyakāścāraṇāśca |
wiśwāwasurnāradaparwatau ca; gandharwamukhyāśca sahāpsarobhiḥ ||7||

halāyudhastatra ca keśawaśca; wṛṣṇyandhakāścaiwa yathā pradhānāḥ |
prekṣāṃ sma cakruryadupuṅgawāste; sthitāśca kṛṣṇasya mate babhūwuḥ ||8||

dṛṣṭwā hi tānmattagajendrarūpā; npañcābhipadmāniwa wāraṇendrān |
bhasmāwṛtāṅgāniwa hawyawāhā; npārthānpradadhyau sa yaduprawīraḥ ||9||

śaśaṃsa rāmāya yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca; bhīmaṃ ca jiṣṇuṃ ca yamau ca wīrau |
śanaiḥ śanaistāṃśca nirīkṣya rāmo; janārdanaṃ prītamanā dadarśa ||10||

anye tu nānānṛpaputrapautrāḥ; kṛṣṇāgatairnetramanaḥswabhāwaiḥ |
wyāyacchamānā dadṛśurbhramantīṃ; saṃdaṣṭadantacchadatāmrawaktrāḥ ||11||

tathaiwa pārthāḥ pṛthubāhawaste; wīrau yamau caiwa mahānubhāwau |
tāṃ draupadīṃ prekṣya tadā sma sarwe; kandarpabāṇābhihatā babhūwuḥ ||12||

dewarṣigandharwasamākulaṃ ta; tsuparṇanāgāsurasiddhajuṣṭam |
diwyena gandhena samākulaṃ ca; diwyaiśca mālyairawakīryamāṇam ||13||

mahāswanairdundubhināditaiśca; babhūwa tatsaṅkulamantarikṣam |
wimānasambādhamabhūtsamantā; tsaweṇuwīṇāpaṇawānunādam ||14||

tatastu te rājagaṇāḥ krameṇa; kṛṣṇānimittaṃ nṛpa wikramantaḥ |
tatkārmukaṃ saṃhananopapannaṃ; sajyaṃ na śekustarasāpi kartum ||15||

te wikramantaḥ sphuratā dṛḍhena; niṣkṛṣyamāṇā dhanuṣā narendrāḥ |
wiceṣṭamānā dharaṇītalasthā; dīnā adṛśyanta wibhagnacittāḥ ||16||

hāhākṛtaṃ taddhanuṣā dṛḍhena; niṣpiṣṭabhagnāṅgadakuṇḍalaṃ ca |
kṛṣṇānimittaṃ winiwṛttabhāwaṃ; rājñāṃ tadā maṇḍalamārtamāsīt ||17||

tasmiṃstu sambhrāntajane samāje; nikṣiptawādeṣu narādhipeṣu |
kuntīsuto jiṣṇuriyeṣa kartuṃ; sajyaṃ dhanustatsaśaraṃ sa wīraḥ ||18||






                  179


waiśampāyana uwāca||

yadā niwṛttā rājāno dhanuṣaḥ sajyakarmaṇi |
athodatiṣṭhadwiprāṇāṃ madhyājjiṣṇurudāradhīḥ ||1||

udakrośanwipramukhyā widhunwanto'jināni ca |
dṛṣṭwā samprasthitaṃ pārthamindraketusamaprabham ||2||

kecidāsanwimanasaḥ kecidāsanmudā yutāḥ |
āhuḥ parasparaṃ kecinnipuṇā buddhijīwinaḥ ||3||

yatkarṇaśalyapramukhaiḥ pārthiwairlokawiśrutaiḥ |
nānataṃ balawadbhirhi dhanurwedaparāyaṇaiḥ ||4||

tatkathaṃ twakṛtāstreṇa prāṇato durbalīyasā |
baṭumātreṇa śakyaṃ hi sajyaṃ kartuṃ dhanurdwijāḥ ||5||

awahāsyā bhawiṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ sarwarājasu |
karmaṇyasminnasaṃsiddhe cāpalādaparīkṣite ||6||

yadyeṣa darpāddharṣādwā yadi wā brahmacāpalāt |
prasthito dhanurāyantuṃ wāryatāṃ sādhu mā gamat ||7||

nāwahāsyā bhawiṣyāmo na ca lāghawamāsthitāḥ |
na ca widwiṣṭatāṃ loke gamiṣyāmo mahīkṣitām ||8||

kecidāhuryuwā śrīmānnāgarājakaropamaḥ |
pīnaskandhorubāhuśca dhairyeṇa himawāniwa ||9||

sambhāwyamasminkarmedamutsāhāccānumīyate |
śaktirasya mahotsāhā na hyaśaktaḥ swayaṃ wrajet ||10||

na ca tadwidyate kiñcitkarma lokeṣu yadbhawet |
brāhmaṇānāmasādhyaṃ ca triṣu saṃsthānacāriṣu ||11||

abbhakṣā wāyubhakṣāśca phalāhārā dṛḍhawratāḥ |
durbalā hi balīyāṃso wiprā hi brahmatejasā ||12||

brāhmaṇo nāwamantawyaḥ sadwāsadwā samācaran |
sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ mahaddhraswaṃ karma yatsamupāgatam ||13||

ewaṃ teṣāṃ wilapatāṃ wiprāṇāṃ wiwidhā giraḥ |
arjuno dhanuṣo'bhyāśe tasthau giririwācalaḥ ||14||

sa taddhanuḥ parikramya pradakṣiṇamathākarot |
praṇamya śirasā hṛṣṭo jagṛhe ca parantapaḥ ||15||

sajyaṃ ca cakre nimiṣāntareṇa; śarāṃśca jagrāha daśārdhasaṅkhyān |
wiwyādha lakṣyaṃ nipapāta tacca; chidreṇa bhūmau sahasātiwiddham ||16||

tato'ntarikṣe ca babhūwa nādaḥ; samājamadhye ca mahānninādaḥ |
puṣpāṇi diwyāni wawarṣa dewaḥ; pārthasya mūrdhni dwiṣatāṃ nihantuḥ ||17||

celāwedhāṃstataścakrurhāhākārāṃśca sarwaśaḥ |
nyapataṃścātra nabhasaḥ samantātpuṣpawṛṣṭayaḥ ||18||

śatāṅgāni ca tūryāṇi wādakāścāpyawādayan |
sūtamāgadhasaṅghāśca astuwaṃstatra suswanāḥ ||19||

taṃ dṛṣṭwā drupadaḥ prīto babhūwāriniṣūdanaḥ |
sahasainyaśca pārthasya sāhāyyārthamiyeṣa saḥ ||20||

tasmiṃstu śabde mahati prawṛtte; yudhiṣṭhiro dharmabhṛtāṃ wariṣṭhaḥ |
āwāsamewopajagāma śīghraṃ; sārdhaṃ yamābhyāṃ puruṣottamābhyām ||21||

widdhaṃ tu lakṣyaṃ prasamīkṣya kṛṣṇā; pārthaṃ ca śakrapratimaṃ nirīkṣya |
ādāya śuklaṃ waramālyadāma; jagāma kuntīsutamutsmayantī ||22||

sa tāmupādāya wijitya raṅge; dwijātibhistairabhipūjyamānaḥ |
raṅgānnirakrāmadacintyakarmā; patnyā tayā cāpyanugamyamānaḥ ||23||






                  180


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tasmai ditsati kanyāṃ tu brāhmaṇāya mahātmane |
kopa āsīnmahīpānāmālokyānyonyamantikāt ||1||

asmānayamatikramya tṛṇīkṛtya ca saṅgatān |
dātumicchati wiprāya draupadīṃ yoṣitāṃ warām ||2||

nihanmainaṃ durātmānaṃ yo'yamasmānna manyate |
na hyarhatyeṣa satkāraṃ nāpi wṛddhakramaṃ guṇaiḥ ||3||

hanmainaṃ saha putreṇa durācāraṃ nṛpadwiṣam |
ayaṃ hi sarwānāhūya satkṛtya ca narādhipān ||4||

guṇawadbhojayitwā ca tataḥ paścādwinindati ||4||

asminrājasamāwāye dewānāmiwa saṃnaye |
kimayaṃ sadṛśaṃ kañcinnṛpatiṃ naiwa dṛṣṭawān ||5||

na ca wipreṣwadhīkāro widyate waraṇaṃ prati |
swayaṃwaraḥ kṣatriyāṇāmitīyaṃ prathitā śrutiḥ ||6||

atha wā yadi kanyeyaṃ neha kañcidbubhūṣati |
agnāwenāṃ parikṣipya yāma rāṣṭrāṇi pārthiwāḥ ||7||

brāhmaṇo yadi wā bālyāllobhādwā kṛtawānidam |
wipriyaṃ pārthiwendrāṇāṃ naiṣa wadhyaḥ kathañcana ||8||

brāhmaṇārthaṃ hi no rājyaṃ jīwitaṃ ca wasūni ca |
putrapautraṃ ca yaccānyadasmākaṃ widyate dhanam ||9||

awamānabhayādetatswadharmasya ca rakṣaṇāt |
swayaṃwarāṇāṃ cānyeṣāṃ mā bhūdewaṃwidhā gatiḥ ||10||

ityuktwā rājaśārdūlā hṛṣṭāḥ parighabāhawaḥ |
drupadaṃ sañjighṛkṣantaḥ sāyudhāḥ samupādrawan ||11||

tāngṛhītaśarāwāpānkruddhānāpatato nṛpān |
drupado wīkṣya santrāsādbrāhmaṇāñśaraṇaṃ gataḥ ||12||

wegenāpatatastāṃstu prabhinnāniwa wāraṇān |
pāṇḍuputrau mahāwīryau pratīyaturariṃdamau ||13||

tataḥ samutpeturudāyudhāste; mahīkṣito baddhatalāṅgulitrāḥ |
jighāṃsamānāḥ kururājaputrā; wamarṣayanto'rjunabhīmasenau ||14||

tatastu bhīmo'dbhutawīryakarmā; mahābalo wajrasamānawīryaḥ |
utpāṭya dorbhyāṃ drumamekawīro; niṣpatrayāmāsa yathā gajendraḥ ||15||

taṃ wṛkṣamādāya ripupramāthī; daṇḍīwa daṇḍaṃ pitṛrāja ugram |
tasthau samīpe puruṣarṣabhasya; pārthasya pārthaḥ pṛthudīrghabāhuḥ ||16||

tatprekṣya karmātimanuṣyabuddhe; rjiṣṇoḥ sahabhrāturacintyakarmā |
dāmodaro bhrātaramugrawīryaṃ; halāyudhaṃ wākyamidaṃ babhāṣe ||17||

ya eṣa mattarṣabhatulyagāmī; mahaddhanuḥ karṣati tālamātram |
eṣo'rjuno nātra wicāryamasti; yadyasmi saṅkarṣaṇa wāsudewaḥ ||18||

ya eṣa wṛkṣaṃ tarasāwarujya; rājñāṃ wikāre sahasā niwṛttaḥ |
wṛkodaro nānya ihaitadadya; kartuṃ samartho bhuwi martyadharmā ||19||

yo'sau purastātkamalāyatākṣa; stanurmahāsiṃhagatirwinītaḥ |
gauraḥ pralambojjwalacārughoṇo; winiḥsṛtaḥ so'cyuta dharmarājaḥ ||20||

yau tau kumārāwiwa kārttikeyau; dwāwaświneyāwiti me pratarkaḥ |
muktā hi tasmājjatuweśmadāhā; nmayā śrutāḥ pāṇḍusutāḥ pṛthā ca ||21||

tamabrawīnnirmalatoyadābho; halāyudho'nantarajaṃ pratītaḥ |
prīto'smi diṣṭyā hi pitṛṣwasā naḥ; pṛthā wimuktā saha kaurawāgryaiḥ ||22||






                  181


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ajināni widhunwantaḥ karakāṃśca dwijarṣabhāḥ |
ūcustaṃ bhīrna kartawyā wayaṃ yotsyāmahe parān ||1||

tānewaṃ wadato wiprānarjunaḥ prahasanniwa |
uwāca prekṣakā bhūtwā yūyaṃ tiṣṭhata pārśwataḥ ||2||

ahamenānajihmāgraiḥ śataśo wikirañśaraiḥ |
wārayiṣyāmi saṅkruddhānmantrairāśīwiṣāniwa ||3||

iti taddhanurādāya śulkāwāptaṃ mahārathaḥ |
bhrātrā bhīmena sahitastasthau giririwācalaḥ ||4||

tataḥ karṇamukhānkruddhānkṣatriyāṃstānruṣotthitān |
sampetaturabhītau tau gajau pratigajāniwa ||5||

ūcuśca wācaḥ paruṣāste rājāno jighāṃsawaḥ |
āhawe hi dwijasyāpi wadho dṛṣṭo yuyutsataḥ ||6||

tato waikartanaḥ karṇo jagāmārjunamojasā |
yuddhārthī wāśitāhetorgajaḥ pratigajaṃ yathā ||7||

bhīmasenaṃ yayau śalyo madrāṇāmīśwaro balī |
duryodhanādayastwanye brāhmaṇaiḥ saha saṅgatāḥ ||8||

mṛdupūrwamayatnena pratyayudhyaṃstadāhawe ||8||

tato'rjunaḥ pratyawidhyadāpatantaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ |
karṇaṃ waikartanaṃ dhīmānwikṛṣya balawaddhanuḥ ||9||

teṣāṃ śarāṇāṃ wegena śitānāṃ tigmatejasām |
wimuhyamāno rādheyo yatnāttamanudhāwati ||10||

tāwubhāwapyanirdeśyau lāghawājjayatāṃ warau |
ayudhyetāṃ susaṃrabdhāwanyonyawijayaiṣiṇau ||11||

kṛte pratikṛtaṃ paśya paśya bāhubalaṃ ca me |
iti śūrārthawacanairābhāṣetāṃ parasparam ||12||

tato'rjunasya bhujayorwīryamapratimaṃ bhuwi |
jñātwā waikartanaḥ karṇaḥ saṃrabdhaḥ samayodhayat ||13||

arjunena prayuktāṃstānbāṇānwegawatastadā |
pratihatya nanādoccaiḥ sainyāstamabhipūjayan ||14||

karṇa uwāca||

tuṣyāmi te wipramukhya bhujawīryasya saṃyuge |
awiṣādasya caiwāsya śastrāstrawinayasya ca ||15||

kiṃ twaṃ sākṣāddhanurwedo rāmo wā wiprasattama |
atha sākṣāddharihayaḥ sākṣādwā wiṣṇuracyutaḥ ||16||

ātmapracchādanārthaṃ wai bāhuwīryamupāśritaḥ |
wiprarūpaṃ widhāyedaṃ tato māṃ pratiyudhyase ||17||

na hi māmāhawe kruddhamanyaḥ sākṣācchacīpateḥ |
pumānyodhayituṃ śaktaḥ pāṇḍawādwā kirīṭinaḥ ||18||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tamewaṃwādinaṃ tatra phalgunaḥ pratyabhāṣata |
nāsmi karṇa dhanurwedo nāsmi rāmaḥ pratāpawān ||19||

brāhmaṇo'smi yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sarwaśastrabhṛtāṃ waraḥ ||19||

brāhme pauraṃdare cāstre niṣṭhito guruśāsanāt |
sthito'smyadya raṇe jetuṃ twāṃ wīrāwicalo bhawa ||20||

ewamuktastu rādheyo yuddhātkarṇo nyawartata |
brahmaṃ tejastadājayyaṃ manyamāno mahārathaḥ ||21||

yuddhaṃ tūpeyatustatra rājañśalyawṛkodarau |
balinau yugapanmattau spardhayā ca balena ca ||22||

anyonyamāhwayantau tau mattāwiwa mahāgajau |
muṣṭibhirjānubhiścaiwa nighnantāwitaretaram ||23||

muhūrtaṃ tau tathānyonyaṃ samare paryakarṣatām ||23||

tato bhīmaḥ samutkṣipya bāhubhyāṃ śalyamāhawe |
nyawadhīdbalināṃ śreṣṭho jahasurbrāhmaṇāstataḥ ||24||

tatrāścaryaṃ bhīmasenaścakāra puruṣarṣabhaḥ |
yacchalyaṃ patitaṃ bhūmau nāhanadbalinaṃ balī ||25||

pātite bhīmasenena śalye karṇe ca śaṅkite |
śaṅkitāḥ sarwarājānaḥ pariwawrurwṛkodaram ||26||

ūcuśca sahitāstatra sādhwime brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥ |
wijñāyantāṃ kwajanmānaḥ kwaniwāsāstathaiwa ca ||27||

ko hi rādhāsutaṃ karmaṃ śakto yodhayituṃ raṇe |
anyatra rāmāddroṇādwā kṛpādwāpi śaradwataḥ ||28||

kṛṣṇādwā dewakīputrātphalgunādwā parantapāt |
ko wā duryodhanaṃ śaktaḥ pratiyodhayituṃ raṇe ||29||

tathaiwa madrarājānaṃ śalyaṃ balawatāṃ waram |
baladewādṛte wīrātpāṇḍawādwā wṛkodarāt ||30||

kriyatāmawahāro'smādyuddhādbrāhmaṇasaṃyutāt |
athainānupalabhyeha punaryotsyāmahe wayam ||31||

tatkarma bhīmasya samīkṣya kṛṣṇaḥ; kuntīsutau tau pariśaṅkamānaḥ |
niwārayāmāsa mahīpatīṃstā; ndharmeṇa labdhetyanunīya sarwān ||32||

ta ewaṃ saṃniwṛttāstu yuddhādyuddhawiśāradāḥ |
yathāwāsaṃ yayuḥ sarwe wismitā rājasattamāḥ ||33||

wṛtto brahmottaro raṅgaḥ pāñcālī brāhmaṇairwṛtā |
iti bruwantaḥ prayayurye tatrāsansamāgatāḥ ||34||

brāhmaṇaistu praticchannau raurawājinawāsibhiḥ |
kṛcchreṇa jagmatustatra bhīmasenadhanañjayau ||35||

wimuktau janasambādhācchatrubhiḥ pariwikṣatau |
kṛṣṇayānugatau tatra nṛwīrau tau wirejatuḥ ||36||

teṣāṃ mātā bahuwidhaṃ wināśaṃ paryacintayat |
anāgacchatsu putreṣu bhaikṣakāle'tigacchati ||37||

dhārtarāṣṭrairhatā na syurwijñāya kurupuṅgawāḥ |
māyānwitairwā rakṣobhiḥ sughorairdṛḍhawairibhiḥ ||38||

wiparītaṃ mataṃ jātaṃ wyāsasyāpi mahātmanaḥ |
ityewaṃ cintayāmāsa sutasnehānwitā pṛthā ||39||

mahatyathāparāhṇe tu ghanaiḥ sūrya iwāwṛtaḥ |
brāhmaṇaiḥ prāwiśattatra jiṣṇurbrahmapuraskṛtaḥ ||40||






                  182


waiśampāyana uwāca||

gatwā tu tāṃ bhārgawakarmaśālāṃ; pārthau pṛthāṃ prāpya mahānubhāwau |
tāṃ yājñasenīṃ paramapratītau; bhikṣetyathāwedayatāṃ narāgryau ||1||

kuṭīgatā sā twanawekṣya putrā; nuwāca bhuṅkteti sametya sarwe |
paścāttu kuntī prasamīkṣya kanyāṃ; kaṣṭaṃ mayā bhāṣitamityuwāca ||2||

sādharmabhītā hi wilajjamānā; tāṃ yājñasenīṃ paramapratītām |
pāṇau gṛhītwopajagāma kuntī; yudhiṣṭhiraṃ wākyamuwāca cedam ||3||

iyaṃ hi kanyā drupadasya rājña; stawānujābhyāṃ mayi saṃnisṛṣṭā |
yathocitaṃ putra mayāpi coktaṃ; sametya bhuṅkteti nṛpa pramādāt ||4||

kathaṃ mayā nānṛtamuktamadya; bhawetkurūṇāmṛṣabha brawīhi |
pāñcālarājasya sutāmadharmo; na copawarteta nabhūtapūrwaḥ ||5||

muhūrtamātraṃ twanucintya rājā; yudhiṣṭhiro mātaramuttamaujāḥ |
kuntīṃ samāśwāsya kuruprawīro; dhanañjayaṃ wākyamidaṃ babhāṣe ||6||
