twayā jitā pāṇḍawa yājñasenī; twayā ca toṣiṣyati rājaputrī |
prajwālyatāṃ hūyatāṃ cāpi wahni; rgṛhāṇa pāṇiṃ widhiwattwamasyāḥ ||7||

arjuna uwāca||

mā māṃ narendra twamadharmabhājaṃ; kṛthā na dharmo hyayamīpsito'nyaiḥ |
bhawānniweśyaḥ prathamaṃ tato'yaṃ; bhīmo mahābāhuracintyakarmā ||8||

ahaṃ tato nakulo'nantaraṃ me; mādrīsutaḥ sahadewo jaghanyaḥ |
wṛkodaro'haṃ ca yamau ca rāja; nniyaṃ ca kanyā bhawataḥ sma sarwe ||9||

ewaṅgate yatkaraṇīyamatra; dharmyaṃ yaśasyaṃ kuru tatpracintya |
pāñcālarājasya ca yatpriyaṃ syā; ttadbrūhi sarwe sma waśe sthitāste ||10||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

te dṛṣṭwā tatra tiṣṭhantīṃ sarwe kṛṣṇāṃ yaśaswinīm |
samprekṣyānyonyamāsīnā hṛdayaistāmadhārayan ||11||

teṣāṃ hi draupadīṃ dṛṣṭwā sarweṣāmamitaujasām |
sampramathyendriyagrāmaṃ prādurāsīnmanobhawaḥ ||12||

kāmyaṃ rūpaṃ hi pāñcālyā widhātrā wihitaṃ swayam |
babhūwādhikamanyābhyaḥ sarwabhūtamanoharam ||13||

teṣāmākārabhāwajñaḥ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
dwaipāyanawacaḥ kṛtsnaṃ saṃsmaranwai nararṣabha ||14||

abrawītsa hi tānbhrātṛnmithobhedabhayānnṛpaḥ |
sarweṣāṃ draupadī bhāryā bhawiṣyati hi naḥ śubhā ||15||






                  183


waiśampāyana uwāca||

bhrāturwacastatprasamīkṣya sarwe; jyeṣṭhasya pāṇḍostanayāstadānīm |
tamewārthaṃ dhyāyamānā manobhi; rāsāṃ cakruratha tatrāmitaujāḥ ||1||

wṛṣṇiprawīrastu kuruprawīrā; nāśaṅkamānaḥ saharauhiṇeyaḥ |
jagāma tāṃ bhārgawakarmaśālāṃ; yatrāsate te puruṣaprawīrāḥ ||2||

tatropawiṣṭaṃ pṛthudīrghabāhuṃ; dadarśa kṛṣṇaḥ saharauhiṇeyaḥ |
ajātaśatruṃ pariwārya tāṃśca; upopawiṣṭāñjwalanaprakāśān ||3||

tato'brawīdwāsudewo'bhigamya; kuntīsutaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ wariṣṭham |
kṛṣṇo'hamasmīti nipīḍya pādau; yudhiṣṭhirasyājamīḍhasya rājñaḥ ||4||

tathaiwa tasyāpyanu rauhiṇeya; stau cāpi hṛṣṭāḥ kurawo'bhyanandan |
pitṛṣwasuścāpi yaduprawīrā; wagṛhṇatāṃ bhāratamukhya pādau ||5||

ajātaśatruśca kuruprawīraḥ; papraccha kṛṣṇaṃ kuśalaṃ niwedya |
kathaṃ wayaṃ wāsudewa twayeha; gūḍhā wasanto widitāḥ sma sarwe ||6||

tamabrawīdwāsudewaḥ prahasya; gūḍho'pyagnirjñāyata ewa rājan |
taṃ wikramaṃ pāṇḍaweyānatītya; ko'nyaḥ kartā widyate mānuṣeṣu ||7||

diṣṭyā tasmātpāwakātsampramuktā; yūyaṃ sarwe pāṇḍawāḥ śatrusāhāḥ |
diṣṭyā pāpo dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putraḥ; sahāmātyo na sakāmo'bhawiṣyat ||8||

bhadraṃ wo'stu nihitaṃ yadguhāyāṃ; wiwardhadhwaṃ jwalana iwedhyamānaḥ |
mā wo widyuḥ pārthiwāḥ kecaneha; yāsyāwahe śibirāyaiwa tāwat ||9||

so'nujñātaḥ pāṇḍawenāwyayaśrīḥ; prāyācchīghraṃ baladewena sārdham ||9||






                  184


waiśampāyana uwāca||

dhṛṣṭadyumnastu pāñcālyaḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ kurunandanau |
anwagacchattadā yāntau bhārgawasya niweśanam ||1||

so'jñāyamānaḥ puruṣānawadhāya samantataḥ |
swayamārānniwiṣṭo'bhūdbhārgawasya niweśane ||2||

sāye'tha bhīmastu ripupramāthī; jiṣṇuryamau cāpi mahānubhāwau |
bhaikṣaṃ caritwā tu yudhiṣṭhirāya; niwedayāṃ cakruradīnasattwāḥ ||3||

tatastu kuntī drupadātmajāṃ tā; muwāca kāle wacanaṃ wadānyā |
ato'gramādāya kuruṣwa bhadre; baliṃ ca wiprāya ca dehi bhikṣām ||4||

ye cānnamicchanti dadaswa tebhyaḥ; pariśritā ye parito manuṣyāḥ |
tataśca śeṣaṃ prawibhajya śīghra; mardhaṃ caturṇāṃ mama cātmanaśca ||5||

ardhaṃ ca bhīmāya dadāhi bhadre; ya eṣa mattarṣabhatulyarūpaḥ |
śyāmo yuwā saṃhananopapanna; eṣo hi wīro bahubhuksadaiwa ||6||

sā hṛṣṭarūpaiwa tu rājaputrī; tasyā wacaḥ sādhwawiśaṅkamānā |
yathāwaduktaṃ pracakāra sādhwī; te cāpi sarwe'bhyawajahrurannam ||7||

kuśaistu bhūmau śayanaṃ cakāra; mādrīsutaḥ sahadewastaraswī |
yathātmīyānyajināni sarwe; saṃstīrya wīrāḥ suṣupurdharaṇyām ||8||

agastyaśāstāmabhito diśaṃ tu; śirāṃsi teṣāṃ kurusattamānām |
kuntī purastāttu babhūwa teṣāṃ; kṛṣṇā tiraścaiwa babhūwa pattaḥ ||9||

aśeta bhūmau saha pāṇḍuputraiḥ; pādopadhānewa kṛtā kuśeṣu |
na tatra duḥkhaṃ ca babhūwa tasyā; na cāwamene kurupuṅgawāṃstān ||10||

te tatra śūrāḥ kathayāṃ babhūwuḥ; kathā wicitrāḥ pṛtanādhikārāḥ |
astrāṇi diwyāni rathāṃśca nāgā; nkhaḍgāngadāścāpi paraśwadhāṃśca ||11||

teṣāṃ kathāstāḥ parikīrtyamānāḥ; pāñcālarājasya sutastadānīm |
śuśrāwa kṛṣṇāṃ ca tathā niṣaṇṇāṃ; te cāpi sarwe dadṛśurmanuṣyāḥ ||12||

dhṛṣṭadyumno rājaputrastu sarwaṃ; wṛttaṃ teṣāṃ kathitaṃ caiwa rātrau |
sarwaṃ rājñe drupadāyākhilena; niwedayiṣyaṃstwarito jagāma ||13||

pāñcālarājastu wiṣaṇṇarūpa; stānpāṇḍawānapratiwindamānaḥ |
dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ paryapṛcchanmahātmā; kwa sā gatā kena nītā ca kṛṣṇā ||14||

kaccinna śūdreṇa na hīnajena; waiśyena wā karadenopapannā |
kaccitpadaṃ mūrdhni na me nidigdhaṃ; kaccinmālā patitā na śmaśāne ||15||

kaccitsawarṇaprawaro manuṣya; udriktawarṇo'pyuta weha kaccit |
kaccinna wāmo mama mūrdhni pādaḥ; kṛṣṇābhimarśena kṛto'dya putra ||16||

kaccicca yakṣye paramapratītaḥ; saṃyujya pārthena nararṣabheṇa |
brawīhi tattwena mahānubhāwaḥ; ko'sau wijetā duhiturmamādya ||17||

wicitrawīryasya tu kaccidadya; kuruprawīrasya dharanti putrāḥ |
kaccittu pārthena yawīyasādya; dhanurgṛhītaṃ nihataṃ ca lakṣyam ||18||






                  185


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tatastathoktaḥ parihṛṣṭarūpaḥ; pitre śaśaṃsātha sa rājaputraḥ |
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ somakānāṃ prabarho; wṛttaṃ yathā yena hṛtā ca kṛṣṇā ||1||

yo'sau yuwā swāyatalohitākṣaḥ; kṛṣṇājinī dewasamānarūpaḥ |
yaḥ kārmukāgryaṃ kṛtawānadhijyaṃ; lakṣyaṃ ca tatpātitawānpṛthiwyām ||2||

asajjamānaśca gatastaraswī; wṛto dwijāgryairabhipūjyamānaḥ |
cakrāma wajrīwa diteḥ suteṣu; sarwaiśca dewairṛṣibhiśca juṣṭaḥ ||3||

kṛṣṇā ca gṛhyājinamanwayāttaṃ; nāgaṃ yathā nāgawadhūḥ prahṛṣṭā |
amṛṣyamāṇeṣu narādhipeṣu; kruddheṣu taṃ tatra samāpatatsu ||4||

tato'paraḥ pārthiwarājamadhye; prawṛddhamārujya mahīpraroham |
prakālayannewa sa pārthiwaughā; nkruddho'ntakaḥ prāṇabhṛto yathaiwa ||5||

tau pārthiwānāṃ miṣatāṃ narendra; kṛṣṇāmupādāya gatau narāgryau |
wibhrājamānāwiwa candrasūryau; bāhyāṃ purādbhārgawakarmaśālām ||6||

tatropawiṣṭārciriwānalasya; teṣāṃ janitrīti mama pratarkaḥ |
tathāwidhairewa naraprawīrai; rupopawiṣṭaistribhiragnikalpaiḥ ||7||

tasyāstatastāwabhiwādya pādā; wuktwā ca kṛṣṇāmabhiwādayeti |
sthitau ca tatraiwa niwedya kṛṣṇāṃ; bhaikṣapracārāya gatā narāgryāḥ ||8||

teṣāṃ tu bhaikṣaṃ pratigṛhya kṛṣṇā; kṛtwā baliṃ brāhmaṇasācca kṛtwā |
tāṃ caiwa wṛddhāṃ pariwiṣya tāṃśca; naraprawīrānswayamapyabhuṅkta ||9||

suptāstu te pārthiwa sarwa ewa; kṛṣṇā tu teṣāṃ caraṇopadhānam |
āsītpṛthiwyāṃ śayanaṃ ca teṣāṃ; darbhājināgryāstaraṇopapannam ||10||

te nardamānā iwa kālameghāḥ; kathā wicitrāḥ kathayāṃ babhūwuḥ |
na waiśyaśūdraupayikīḥ kathāstā; na ca dwijāteḥ kathayanti wīrāḥ ||11||

niḥsaṃśayaṃ kṣatriyapuṅgawāste; yathā hi yuddhaṃ kathayanti rājan |
āśā hi no wyaktamiyaṃ samṛddhā; muktānhi pārthāñśṛṇumo'gnidāhāt ||12||

yathā hi lakṣyaṃ nihataṃ dhanuśca; sajyaṃ kṛtaṃ tena tathā prasahya |
yathā ca bhāṣanti parasparaṃ te; channā dhruwaṃ te pracaranti pārthāḥ ||13||

tataḥ sa rājā drupadaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ; purohitaṃ preṣayāṃ tatra cakre |
widyāma yuṣmāniti bhāṣamāṇo; mahātmanaḥ pāṇḍusutāḥ stha kaccit ||14||

gṛhītawākyo nṛpateḥ purodhā; gatwā praśaṃsāmabhidhāya teṣām |
wākyaṃ yathāwannṛpateḥ samagra; muwāca tānsa kramawitkrameṇa ||15||

wijñātumicchatyawanīśwaro waḥ; pāñcālarājo drupado warārhāḥ |
lakṣyasya weddhāramimaṃ hi dṛṣṭwā; harṣasya nāntaṃ paripaśyate saḥ ||16||

tadācaḍḍhwaṃ jñātikulānupūrwīṃ; padaṃ śiraḥsu dwiṣatāṃ kurudhwam |
prahlādayadhwaṃ hṛdayaṃ mamedaṃ; pāñcālarājasya sahānugasya ||17||

pāṇḍurhi rājā drupadasya rājñaḥ; priyaḥ sakhā cātmasamo babhūwa |
tasyaiṣa kāmo duhitā mameyaṃ; snuṣā yadi syāditi kaurawasya ||18||

ayaṃ ca kāmo drupadasya rājño; hṛdi sthito nityamaninditāṅgāḥ |
yadarjuno wai pṛthudīrghabāhu; rdharmeṇa windeta sutāṃ mameti ||19||

tathoktawākyaṃ tu purohitaṃ taṃ; sthitaṃ winītaṃ samudīkṣya rājā |
samīpasthaṃ bhīmamidaṃ śaśāsa; pradīyatāṃ pādyamarghyaṃ tathāsmai ||20||

mānyaḥ purodhā drupadasya rājña; stasmai prayojyābhyadhikaiwa pūjā |
bhīmastathā tatkṛtawānnarendra; tāṃ caiwa pūjāṃ pratisaṅgṛhītwā ||21||

sukhopawiṣṭaṃ tu purohitaṃ taṃ; yudhiṣṭhiro brāhmaṇamityuwāca |
pāñcālarājena sutā nisṛṣṭā; swadharmadṛṣṭena yathānukāmam ||22||

pradiṣṭaśulkā drupadena rājñā; sānena wīreṇa tathānuwṛttā |
na tatra warṇeṣu kṛtā wiwakṣā; na jīwaśilpe na kule na gotre ||23||

kṛtena sajyena hi kārmukeṇa; widdhena lakṣyeṇa ca saṃnisṛṣṭā |
seyaṃ tathānena mahātmaneha; kṛṣṇā jitā pārthiwasaṅghamadhye ||24||

naiwaṅgate saumakiradya rājā; santāpamarhatyasukhāya kartum |
kāmaśca yo'sau drupadasya rājñaḥ; sa cāpi sampatsyati pārthiwasya ||25||

aprāpyarūpāṃ hi narendrakanyā; mimāmahaṃ brāhmaṇa sādhu manye |
na taddhanurmandabalena śakyaṃ; maurwyā samāyojayituṃ tathā hi ||26||

na cākṛtāstreṇa na hīnajena; lakṣyaṃ tathā pātayituṃ hi śakyam ||26||

tasmānna tāpaṃ duhiturnimittaṃ; pāñcālarājo'rhati kartumadya |
na cāpi tatpātanamanyatheha; kartuṃ wiṣahyaṃ bhuwi mānawena ||27||

ewaṃ bruwatyewa yudhiṣṭhire tu; pāñcālarājasya samīpato'nyaḥ |
tatrājagāmāśu naro dwitīyo; niwedayiṣyanniha siddhamannam ||28||






                  186


dūta uwāca||

janyārthamannaṃ drupadena rājñā; wiwāhahetorupasaṃskṛtaṃ ca |
tadāpnuwadhwaṃ kṛtasarwakāryāḥ; kṛṣṇā ca tatraiwa ciraṃ na kāryam ||1||

ime rathāḥ kāñcanapadmacitrāḥ; sadaśwayuktā wasudhādhipārhāḥ |
etānsamāruhya paraita sarwe; pāñcālarājasya niweśanaṃ tat ||2||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ prayātāḥ kurupuṅgawāste; purohitaṃ taṃ prathamaṃ prayāpya |
āsthāya yānāni mahānti tāni; kuntī ca kṛṣṇā ca sahaiwa yāte ||3||

śrutwā tu wākyāni purohitasya; yānyuktawānbhārata dharmarājaḥ |
jijñāsayaiwātha kurūttamānāṃ; drawyāṇyanekānyupasañjahāra ||4||

phalāni mālyāni susaṃskṛtāni; carmāṇi warmāṇi tathāsanāni |
gāścaiwa rājannatha caiwa rajjū; rdrawyāṇi cānyāni kṛṣīnimittam ||5||

anyeṣu śilpeṣu ca yānyapi syuḥ; sarwāṇi kḷptānyakhilena tatra |
krīḍānimittāni ca yāni tāni; sarwāṇi tatropajahāra rājā ||6||

rathāśwawarmāṇi ca bhānumanti; khaḍgā mahānto'śwarathāśca citrāḥ |
dhanūṃṣi cāgryāṇi śarāśca mukhyāḥ; śaktyṛṣṭayaḥ kāñcanabhūṣitāśca ||7||

prāsā bhuśuṇḍyaśca paraśwadhāśca; sāṅgrāmikaṃ caiwa tathaiwa sarwam |
śayyāsanānyuttamasaṃskṛtāni; tathaiwa cāsanwiwidhāni tatra ||8||

kuntī tu kṛṣṇāṃ parigṛhya sādhwī; mantaḥpuraṃ drupadasyāwiweṣa |
striyaśca tāṃ kaurawarājapatnīṃ; pratyarcayāṃ cakruradīnasattwāḥ ||9||

tānsiṃhawikrāntagatīnawekṣya; maharṣabhākṣānajinottarīyān |
gūḍhottarāṃsānbhujagendrabhoga; pralambabāhūnpuruṣaprawīrān ||10||

rājā ca rājñaḥ saciwāśca sarwe; putrāśca rājñaḥ suhṛdastathaiwa |
preṣyāśca sarwe nikhilena rāja; nharṣaṃ samāpeturatīwa tatra ||11||

te tatra wīrāḥ paramāsaneṣu; sapādapīṭheṣwawiśaṅkamānāḥ |
yathānupūrwyā wiwiśurnarāgryā; stadā mahārheṣu na wismayantaḥ ||12||

uccāwacaṃ pārthiwabhojanīyaṃ; pātrīṣu jāmbūnadarājatīṣu |
dāsāśca dāsyaśca sumṛṣṭaweṣāḥ; bhojāpakāścāpyupajahrurannam ||13||

te tatra bhuktwā puruṣaprawīrā; yathānukāmaṃ subhṛśaṃ pratītāḥ |
utkramya sarwāṇi wasūni tatra; sāṅgrāmikānyāwiwiśurnṛwīrāḥ ||14||

tallakṣayitwā drupadasya putro; rājā ca sarwaiḥ saha mantrimukhyaiḥ |
samarcayāmāsurupetya hṛṣṭāḥ; kuntīsutānpārthiwaputrapautrān ||15||






                  187


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tata āhūya pāñcālyo rājaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram |
parigraheṇa brāhmeṇa parigṛhya mahādyutiḥ ||1||

paryapṛcchadadīnātmā kuntīputraṃ suwarcasam |
kathaṃ jānīma bhawataḥ kṣatriyānbrāhmaṇānuta ||2||

waiśyānwā guṇasampannānuta wā śūdrayonijān |
māyāmāsthāya wā siddhāṃścarataḥ sarwatodiśam ||3||

kṛṣṇāhetoranuprāptāndiwaḥ saṃdarśanārthinaḥ |
brawītu no bhawānsatyaṃ saṃdeho hyatra no mahān ||4||

api naḥ saṃśayasyānte manastuṣṭirihāwiśet |
api no bhāgadheyāni śubhāni syuḥ parantapa ||5||

kāmayā brūhi satyaṃ twaṃ satyaṃ rājasu śobhate |
iṣṭāpūrtena ca tathā waktawyamanṛtaṃ na tu ||6||

śrutwā hyamarasaṅkāśa tawa wākyamariṃdama |
dhruwaṃ wiwāhakaraṇamāsthāsyāmi widhānataḥ ||7||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

mā rājanwimanā bhūstwaṃ pāñcālya prītirastu te |
īpsitaste dhruwaḥ kāmaḥ saṃwṛtto'yamasaṃśayam ||8||

wayaṃ hi kṣatriyā rājanpāṇḍoḥ putrā mahātmanaḥ |
jyeṣṭhaṃ māṃ widdhi kaunteyaṃ bhīmasenārjunāwimau ||9||

yābhyāṃ tawa sutā rājannirjitā rājasaṃsadi ||9||

yamau tu tatra rājendra yatra kṛṣṇā pratiṣṭhitā |
wyetu te mānasaṃ duḥkhaṃ kṣatriyāḥ smo nararṣabha ||10||

padminīwa suteyaṃ te hradādanyaṃ hradaṃ gatā ||10||

iti tathyaṃ mahārāja sarwametadbrawīmi te |
bhawānhi gururasmākaṃ paramaṃ ca parāyaṇam ||11||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ sa drupado rājā harṣawyākulalocanaḥ |
pratiwaktuṃ tadā yuktaṃ nāśakattaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram ||12||

yatnena tu sa taṃ harṣaṃ saṃnigṛhya parantapaḥ |
anurūpaṃ tato rājā pratyuwāca yudhiṣṭhiram ||13||

papraccha cainaṃ dharmātmā yathā te pradrutāḥ purā |
sa tasmai sarwamācakhyāwānupūrwyeṇa pāṇḍawaḥ ||14||

tacchrutwā drupado rājā kuntīputrasya bhāṣitam |
wigarhayāmāsa tadā dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśwaram ||15||

āśwāsayāmāsa ca taṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram |
pratijajñe ca rājyāya drupado wadatāṃ waraḥ ||16||

tataḥ kuntī ca kṛṣṇā ca bhīmasenārjunāwapi |
yamau ca rājñā saṃdiṣṭau wiwiśurbhawanaṃ mahat ||17||

tatra te nyawasanrājanyajñasenena pūjitāḥ |
pratyāśwastāṃstato rājā saha putrairuwāca tān ||18||

gṛhṇātu widhiwatpāṇimadyaiwa kurunandanaḥ |
puṇye'hani mahābāhurarjunaḥ kurutāṃ kṣaṇam ||19||

tatastamabrawīdrājā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
mamāpi dārasambandhaḥ kāryastāwadwiśāṃ pate ||20||

drupada uwāca||

bhawānwā widhiwatpāṇiṃ gṛhṇātu duhiturmama |
yasya wā manyase wīra tasya kṛṣṇāmupādiśa ||21||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

sarweṣāṃ draupadī rājanmahiṣī no bhawiṣyati |
ewaṃ hi wyāhṛtaṃ pūrwaṃ mama mātrā wiśāṃ pate ||22||

ahaṃ cāpyaniwiṣṭo wai bhīmasenaśca pāṇḍawaḥ |
pārthena wijitā caiṣā ratnabhūtā ca te sutā ||23||

eṣa naḥ samayo rājanratnasya sahabhojanam |
na ca taṃ hātumicchāmaḥ samayaṃ rājasattama ||24||

sarweṣāṃ dharmataḥ kṛṣṇā mahiṣī no bhawiṣyati |
ānupūrwyeṇa sarweṣāṃ gṛhṇātu jwalane karam ||25||

drupada uwāca||

ekasya bahwyo wihitā mahiṣyaḥ kurunandana |
naikasyā bahawaḥ puṃso widhīyante kadācana ||26||

lokawedawiruddhaṃ twaṃ nādharmaṃ dhārmikaḥ śuciḥ |
kartumarhasi kaunteya kasmātte buddhirīdṛśī ||27||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

sūkṣmo dharmo mahārāja nāsya widmo wayaṃ gatim |
pūrweṣāmānupūrwyeṇa yātaṃ wartmānuyāmahe ||28||

na me wāganṛtaṃ prāha nādharme dhīyate matiḥ |
ewaṃ caiwa wadatyambā mama caiwa manogatam ||29||

eṣa dharmo dhruwo rājaṃścarainamawicārayan |
mā ca te'tra wiśaṅkā bhūtkathañcidapi pārthiwa ||30||

drupada uwāca||

twaṃ ca kuntī ca kaunteya dhṛṣṭadyumnaśca me sutaḥ |
kathayantwitikartawyaṃ śwaḥ kāle karawāmahe ||31||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

te sametya tataḥ sarwe kathayanti sma bhārata |
atha dwaipāyano rājannabhyāgacchadyadṛcchayā ||32||






                  188


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataste pāṇḍawāḥ sarwe pāñcālyaśca mahāyaśāḥ |
pratyutthāya mahātmānaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dṛṣṭwābhyapūjayan ||1||

pratinandya sa tānsarwānpṛṣṭwā kuśalamantataḥ |
āsane kāñcane śubhre niṣasāda mahāmanāḥ ||2||

anujñātāstu te sarwe kṛṣṇenāmitatejasā |
āsaneṣu mahārheṣu niṣedurdwipadāṃ warāḥ ||3||

tato muhūrtānmadhurāṃ wāṇīmuccārya pārṣataḥ |
papraccha taṃ mahātmānaṃ draupadyarthe wiśāṃ patiḥ ||4||

kathamekā bahūnāṃ syānna ca syāddharmasaṅkaraḥ |
etanno bhagawānsarwaṃ prabrawītu yathātatham ||5||

wyāsa uwāca||

asmindharme wipralambhe lokawedawirodhake |
yasya yasya mataṃ yadyacchrotumicchāmi tasya tat ||6||

drupada uwāca||

adharmo'yaṃ mama mato wiruddho lokawedayoḥ |
na hyekā widyate patnī bahūnāṃ dwijasattama ||7||

na cāpyācaritaḥ pūrwairayaṃ dharmo mahātmabhiḥ |
na ca dharmo'pyanekasthaścaritawyaḥ sanātanaḥ ||8||

ato nāhaṃ karomyewaṃ wyawasāyaṃ kriyāṃ prati |
dharmasaṃdehasaṃdigdhaṃ pratibhāti hi māmidam ||9||

dhṛṣṭadyumna uwāca||

yawīyasaḥ kathaṃ bhāryāṃ jyeṣṭho bhrātā dwijarṣabha |
brahmansamabhiwarteta sadwṛttaḥ saṃstapodhana ||10||

na tu dharmasya sūkṣmatwādgatiṃ widmaḥ kathañcana |
adharmo dharma iti wā wyawasāyo na śakyate ||11||

kartumasmadwidhairbrahmaṃstato na wyawasāmyaham |
pañcānāṃ mahiṣī kṛṣṇā bhawatwiti kathañcana ||12||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

na me wāganṛtaṃ prāha nādharme dhīyate matiḥ |
wartate hi mano me'tra naiṣo'dharmaḥ kathañcana ||13||

śrūyate hi purāṇe'pi jaṭilā nāma gautamī |
ṛṣīnadhyāsitawatī sapta dharmabhṛtāṃ wara ||14||

gurośca wacanaṃ prāhurdharmaṃ dharmajñasattama |
gurūṇāṃ caiwa sarweṣāṃ janitrī paramo guruḥ ||15||

sā cāpyuktawatī wācaṃ bhaikṣawadbhujyatāmiti |
tasmādetadahaṃ manye dharmaṃ dwijawarottama ||16||

kuntyuwāca||

ewametadyathāhāyaṃ dharmacārī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
anṛtānme bhayaṃ tīwraṃ mucyeyamanṛtātkatham ||17||

wyāsa uwāca||

anṛtānmokṣyase bhadre dharmaścaiṣa sanātanaḥ |
na tu wakṣyāmi sarweṣāṃ pāñcāla śṛṇu me swayam ||18||

yathāyaṃ wihito dharmo yataścāyaṃ sanātanaḥ |
yathā ca prāha kaunteyastathā dharmo na saṃśayaḥ ||19||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tata utthāya bhagawānwyāso dwaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ |
kare gṛhītwā rājānaṃ rājaweśma samāwiśat ||20||

pāṇḍawāścāpi kuntī ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaśca pārṣataḥ |
wicetasaste tatraiwa pratīkṣante sma tāwubhau ||21||

tato dwaipāyanastasmai narendrāya mahātmane |
ācakhyau tadyathā dharmo bahūnāmekapatnitā ||22||






              pañcendropākhyānam
                  189


wyāsa uwāca||

purā wai naimiṣāraṇye dewāḥ satramupāsate |
tatra waiwaswato rājañśāmitramakarottadā ||1||

tato yamo dīkṣitastatra rāja; nnāmārayatkiñcidapi prajābhyaḥ |
tataḥ prajāstā bahulā babhūwuḥ; kālātipātānmaraṇātprahīṇāḥ ||2||

tatastu śakro waruṇaḥ kuberaḥ; sādhyā rudrā wasawaścāświnau ca |
praṇetāraṃ bhuwanasya prajāpatiṃ; samājagmustatra dewāstathānye ||3||

tato'bruwaṃllokaguruṃ sametā; bhayaṃ nastīwraṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ wiwṛddhyā |
tasmādbhayādudwijantaḥ sukhepsawaḥ; prayāma sarwe śaraṇaṃ bhawantam ||4||

brahmowāca||

kiṃ wo bhayaṃ mānuṣebhyo yūyaṃ sarwe yadāmarāḥ |
mā wo martyasakāśādwai bhayaṃ bhawatu karhicit ||5||

dewā ūcuḥ||

martyā hyamartyāḥ saṃwṛttā na wiśeṣo'sti kaścana |
awiśeṣādudwijanto wiśeṣārthamihāgatāḥ ||6||

brahmowāca||

waiwaswato wyāpṛtaḥ satraheto; stena twime na mriyante manuṣyāḥ |
tasminnekāgre kṛtasarwakārye; tata eṣāṃ bhawitaiwāntakālaḥ ||7||

waiwaswatasyāpi tanurwibhūtā; wīryeṇa yuṣmākamuta prayuktā |
saiṣāmanto bhawitā hyantakāle; tanurhi wīryaṃ bhawitā nareṣu ||8||

wyāsa uwāca||

tatastu te pūrwajadewawākyaṃ; śrutwā dewā yatra dewā yajante |
samāsīnāste sametā mahābalā; bhāgīrathyāṃ dadṛśuḥ puṇḍarīkam ||9||

dṛṣṭwā ca tadwismitāste babhūwu; steṣāmindrastatra śūro jagāma |
so'paśyadyoṣāmatha pāwakaprabhāṃ; yatra gaṅgā satataṃ samprasūtā ||10||

sā tatra yoṣā rudatī jalārthinī; gaṅgāṃ dewīṃ wyawagāhyāwatiṣṭhat |
tasyāśrubinduḥ patito jale wai; tatpadmamāsīdatha tatra kāñcanam ||11||

tadadbhutaṃ prekṣya wajrī tadānī; mapṛcchattāṃ yoṣitamantikādwai |
kā twaṃ kathaṃ rodiṣi kasya heto; rwākyaṃ tathyaṃ kāmayeha brawīhi ||12||

stryuwāca||

twaṃ wetsyase māmiha yāsmi śakra; yadarthaṃ cāhaṃ rodimi mandabhāgyā |
āgaccha rājanpurato'haṃ gamiṣye; draṣṭāsi tadrodimi yatkṛte'ham ||13||

wyāsa uwāca||

tāṃ gacchantīmanwagacchattadānīṃ; so'paśyadārāttaruṇaṃ darśanīyam |
siṃhāsanasthaṃ yuwatīsahāyaṃ; krīḍantamakṣairgirirājamūrdhni ||14||

tamabrawīddewarājo mamedaṃ; twaṃ widdhi wiśwaṃ bhuwanaṃ waśe sthitam |
īśo'hamasmīti samanyurabrawī; ddṛṣṭwā tamakṣaiḥ subhṛśaṃ pramattam ||15||

kruddhaṃ tu śakraṃ prasamīkṣya dewo; jahāsa śakraṃ ca śanairudaikṣata |
saṃstambhito'bhūdatha dewarāja; stenekṣitaḥ sthāṇuriwāwatasthe ||16||

yadā tu paryāptamihāsya krīḍayā; tadā dewīṃ rudatīṃ tāmuwāca |
ānīyatāmeṣa yato'hamārā; nmainaṃ darpaḥ punarapyāwiśeta ||17||

tataḥ śakraḥ spṛṣṭamātrastayā tu; srastairaṅgaiḥ patito'bhūddharaṇyām |
tamabrawīdbhagawānugratejā; maiwaṃ punaḥ śakra kṛthāḥ kathañcit ||18||

wiwartayainaṃ ca mahādrirājaṃ; balaṃ ca wīryaṃ ca tawāprameyam |
wiwṛtya caiwāwiśa madhyamasya; yatrāsate twadwidhāḥ sūryabhāsaḥ ||19||

sa tadwiwṛtya śikharaṃ mahāgire; stulyadyutīṃścaturo'nyāndadarśa |
sa tānabhiprekṣya babhūwa duḥkhitaḥ; kaccinnāhaṃ bhawitā wai yatheme ||20||

tato dewo giriśo wajrapāṇiṃ; wiwṛtya netre kupito'bhyuwāca |
darīmetāṃ prawiśa twaṃ śatakrato; yanmāṃ bālyādawamaṃsthāḥ purastāt ||21||

uktastwewaṃ wibhunā dewarājaḥ; prawepamāno bhṛśamewābhiṣaṅgāt |
srastairaṅgairanilenewa nunna; maśwatthapatraṃ girirājamūrdhni ||22||

sa prāñjalirwinatenānanena; prawepamānaḥ sahasaiwamuktaḥ |
uwāca cedaṃ bahurūpamugraṃ; draṣṭā śeṣasya bhagawaṃstwaṃ bhawādya ||23||

tamabrawīdugradhanwā prahasya; naiwaṃśīlāḥ śeṣamihāpnuwanti |
ete'pyewaṃ bhawitāraḥ purastā; ttasmādetāṃ darimāwiśya śedhwam ||24||

śeṣo'pyewaṃ bhawitā wo na saṃśayo; yoniṃ sarwe mānuṣīmāwiśadhwam |
tatra yūyaṃ karma kṛtwāwiṣahyaṃ; bahūnanyānnidhanaṃ prāpayitwā ||25||

āgantāraḥ punarewendralokaṃ; swakarmaṇā pūrwajitaṃ mahārham |
sarwaṃ mayā bhāṣitametadewaṃ; kartawyamanyadwiwidhārthawacca ||26||

pūrwendrā ūcuḥ||

gamiṣyāmo mānuṣaṃ dewalokā; ddurādharo wihito yatra mokṣaḥ |
dewāstwasmānādadhīrañjananyāṃ; dharmo wāyurmaghawānaświnau ca ||27||

wyāsa uwāca||

etacchrutwā wajrapāṇirwacastu; dewaśreṣṭhaṃ punarewedamāha |
wīryeṇāhaṃ puruṣaṃ kāryaheto; rdadyāmeṣāṃ pañcamaṃ matprasūtam ||28||

teṣāṃ kāmaṃ bhagawānugradhanwā; prādādiṣṭaṃ sannisargādyathoktam |
tāṃ cāpyeṣāṃ yoṣitaṃ lokakāntāṃ; śriyaṃ bhāryāṃ wyadadhānmānuṣeṣu ||29||

tairewa sārdhaṃ tu tataḥ sa dewo; jagāma nārāyaṇamaprameyam |
sa cāpi tadwyadadhātsarwamewa; tataḥ sarwe sambabhūwurdharaṇyām ||30||

sa cāpi keśau harirudbabarha; śuklamekamaparaṃ cāpi kṛṣṇam |
tau cāpi keśau wiśatāṃ yadūnāṃ; kule striyau rohiṇīṃ dewakīṃ ca ||31||

tayoreko baladewo babhūwa; kṛṣṇo dwitīyaḥ keśawaḥ sambabhūwa ||31||

ye te pūrwaṃ śakrarūpā niruddhā; stasyāṃ daryāṃ parwatasyottarasya |
ihaiwa te pāṇḍawā wīryawantaḥ; śakrasyāṃśaḥ pāṇḍawaḥ sawyasācī ||32||

ewamete pāṇḍawāḥ sambabhūwu; rye te rājanpūrwamindrā babhūwuḥ |
lakṣmīścaiṣāṃ pūrwamewopadiṣṭā; bhāryā yaiṣā draupadī diwyarūpā ||33||

kathaṃ hi strī karmaṇo'nte mahītalā; tsamuttiṣṭhedanyato daiwayogāt |
yasyā rūpaṃ somasūryaprakāśaṃ; gandhaścāgryaḥ krośamātrātprawāti ||34||

idaṃ cānyatprītipūrwaṃ narendra; dadāmi te waramatyadbhutaṃ ca |
diwyaṃ cakṣuḥ paśya kuntīsutāṃstwaṃ; puṇyairdiwyaiḥ pūrwadehairupetān ||35||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato wyāsaḥ paramodārakarmā; śucirwiprastapasā tasya rājñaḥ |
cakṣurdiwyaṃ pradadau tānsa sarwā; nrājāpaśyatpūrwadehairyathāwat ||36||

tato diwyānhemakirīṭamālinaḥ; śakraprakhyānpāwakādityawarṇān |
baddhāpīḍāṃścārurūpāṃśca yūno; wyūḍhoraskāṃstālamātrāndadarśa ||37||

diwyairwastrairarajobhiḥ suwarṇai; rmālyaiścāgryaiḥ śobhamānānatīwa |
sākṣāttryakṣānwasawo wātha diwyā; nādityānwā sarwaguṇopapannān ||38||

tānpūrwendrānewamīkṣyābhirūpā; nprīto rājā drupado wismitaśca ||38||

diwyāṃ māyāṃ tāmawāpyāprameyāṃ; tāṃ caiwāgryāṃ śriyamiwa rūpiṇīṃ ca |
yogyāṃ teṣāṃ rūpatejoyaśobhiḥ; patnīmṛddhāṃ dṛṣṭawānpārthiwendraḥ ||39||

sa taddṛṣṭwā mahadāścaryarūpaṃ; jagrāha pādau satyawatyāḥ sutasya |
naitaccitraṃ paramarṣe twayīti; prasannacetāḥ sa uwāca cainam ||40||

wyāsa uwāca||

āsīttapowane kācidṛṣeḥ kanyā mahātmanaḥ |
nādhyagacchatpatiṃ sā tu kanyā rūpawatī satī ||41||

toṣayāmāsa tapasā sā kilogreṇa śaṅkaram |
tāmuwāceśwaraḥ prīto wṛṇu kāmamiti swayam ||42||

saiwamuktābrawītkanyā dewaṃ waradamīśwaram |
patiṃ sarwaguṇopetamicchāmīti punaḥ punaḥ ||43||

dadau tasyai sa deweśastaṃ waraṃ prītimāṃstadā |
pañca te patayaḥ śreṣṭhā bhawiṣyantīti śaṅkaraḥ ||44||

sā prasādayatī dewamidaṃ bhūyo'bhyabhāṣata |
ekaṃ patiṃ guṇopetaṃ twatto'rhāmīti wai tadā ||45||

tāṃ dewadewaḥ prītātmā punaḥ prāha śubhaṃ wacaḥ ||45||

pañcakṛtwastwayā uktaḥ patiṃ dehītyahaṃ punaḥ |
tattathā bhawitā bhadre tawa tadbhadramastu te ||46||

dehamanyaṃ gatāyāste yathoktaṃ tadbhawiṣyati ||46||

drupadaiṣā hi sā jajñe sutā te dewarūpiṇī |
pañcānāṃ wihitā patnī kṛṣṇā pārṣatyaninditā ||47||

swargaśrīḥ pāṇḍawārthāya samutpannā mahāmakhe |
seha taptwā tapo ghoraṃ duhitṛtwaṃ tawāgatā ||48||

saiṣā dewī rucirā dewajuṣṭā; pañcānāmekā swakṛtena karmaṇā |
sṛṣṭā swayaṃ dewapatnī swayambhuwā; śrutwā rājandrupadeṣṭaṃ kuruṣwa ||49||






              waiwāhikaparwa
                  190


drupada uwāca||

aśrutwaiwaṃ wacanaṃ te maharṣe; mayā pūrwaṃ yatitaṃ kāryametat |
na wai śakyaṃ wihitasyāpayātuṃ; tadewedamupapannaṃ widhānam ||1||

diṣṭasya granthiraniwartanīyaḥ; swakarmaṇā wihitaṃ neha kiñcit |
kṛtaṃ nimittaṃ hi waraikaheto; stadewedamupapannaṃ bahūnām ||2||

yathaiwa kṛṣṇoktawatī purastā; nnaikānpatīnme bhagawāndadātu |
sa cāpyewaṃ waramityabrawīttāṃ; dewo hi weda paramaṃ yadatra ||3||

yadi wāyaṃ wihitaḥ śaṅkareṇa; dharmo'dharmo wā nātra mamāparādhaḥ |
gṛhṇantwime widhiwatpāṇimasyā; yathopajoṣaṃ wihitaiṣāṃ hi kṛṣṇā ||4||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato'brawīdbhagawāndharmarāja; madya puṇyāhamuta pāṇḍaweya |
adya pauṣyaṃ yogamupaiti candramāḥ; pāṇiṃ kṛṣṇāyāstwaṃ gṛhāṇādya pūrwam ||5||

tato rājā yajñasenaḥ saputro; janyārtha yuktaṃ bahu tattadagryam |
samānayāmāsa sutāṃ ca kṛṣṇā; māplāwya ratnairbahubhirwibhūṣya ||6||

tataḥ sarwe suhṛdastatra tasya; samājagmuḥ saciwā mantriṇaśca |
draṣṭuṃ wiwāhaṃ paramapratītā; dwijāśca paurāśca yathāpradhānāḥ ||7||

tattasya weśmārthijanopaśobhitaṃ; wikīrṇapadmotpalabhūṣitājiram |
mahārharatnaughawicitramābabhau; diwaṃ yathā nirmalatārakācitam ||8||

tatastu te kaurawarājaputrā; wibhūṣitāḥ kuṇḍalino yuwānaḥ |
mahārhawastrā waracandanokṣitāḥ; kṛtābhiṣekāḥ kṛtamaṅgalakriyāḥ ||9||

purohitenāgnisamānawarcasā; sahaiwa dhaumyena yathāwidhi prabho |
krameṇa sarwe wiwiśuśca tatsado; maharṣabhā goṣṭhamiwābhinandinaḥ ||10||

tataḥ samādhāya sa wedapārago; juhāwa mantrairjwalitaṃ hutāśanam |
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ cāpyupanīya mantrawi; nniyojayāmāsa sahaiwa kṛṣṇayā ||11||

pradakṣiṇaṃ tau pragṛhītapāṇī; samānayāmāsa sa wedapāragaḥ |
tato'bhyanujñāya tamājiśobhinaṃ; purohito rājagṛhādwiniryayau ||12||

krameṇa cānena narādhipātmajā; warastriyāste jagṛhustadā karam |
ahanyahanyuttamarūpadhāriṇo; mahārathāḥ kaurawawaṃśawardhanāḥ ||13||

idaṃ ca tatrādbhutarūpamuttamaṃ; jagāda wiprarṣiratītamānuṣam |
mahānubhāwā kila sā sumadhyamā; babhūwa kanyaiwa gate gate'hani ||14||

kṛte wiwāhe drupado dhanaṃ dadau; mahārathebhyo bahurūpamuttamam |
śataṃ rathānāṃ warahemabhūṣiṇāṃ; caturyujāṃ hemakhalīnamālinām ||15||

śataṃ gajānāmabhipadmināṃ tathā; śataṃ girīṇāmiwa hemaśṛṅgiṇām |
tathaiwa dāsīśatamagryayauwanaṃ; mahārhaweṣābharaṇāmbarasrajam ||16||

pṛthakpṛthakcaiwa daśāyutānwitaṃ; dhanaṃ dadau saumakiragnisākṣikam |
tathaiwa wastrāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni; prabhāwayuktāni mahādhanāni ||17||

kṛte wiwāhe ca tataḥ sma pāṇḍawāḥ; prabhūtaratnāmupalabhya tāṃ śriyam |
wijahrurindrapratimā mahābalāḥ; pure tu pāñcālanṛpasya tasya ha ||18||






                  191


waiśampāyana uwāca||

pāṇḍawaiḥ saha saṃyogaṃ gatasya drupadasya tu |
na babhūwa bhayaṃ kiñciddewebhyo'pi kathañcana ||1||

kuntīmāsādya tā nāryo drupadasya mahātmanaḥ |
nāma saṅkīrtayantyastāḥ pādau jagmuḥ swamūrdhabhiḥ ||2||

kṛṣṇā ca kṣaumasaṃwītā kṛtakautukamaṅgalā |
kṛtābhiwādanā śwaśrwāstasthau prahwā kṛtāñjaliḥ ||3||

rūpalakṣaṇasampannāṃ śīlācārasamanwitām |
draupadīmawadatpremṇā pṛthāśīrwacanaṃ snuṣām ||4||

yathendrāṇī harihaye swāhā caiwa wibhāwasau |
rohiṇī ca yathā some damayantī yathā nale ||5||

yathā waiśrawaṇe bhadrā wasiṣṭhe cāpyarundhatī |
yathā nārāyaṇe lakṣmīstathā twaṃ bhawa bhartṛṣu ||6||

jīwasūrwīrasūrbhadre bahusaukhyasamanwitā |
subhagā bhogasampannā yajñapatnī swanuwratā ||7||

atithīnāgatānsādhūnbālānwṛddhāngurūṃstathā |
pūjayantyā yathānyāyaṃ śaśwadgacchantu te samāḥ ||8||

kurujāṅgalamukhyeṣu rāṣṭreṣu nagareṣu ca |
anu twamabhiṣicyaswa nṛpatiṃ dharmawatsalam ||9||

patibhirnirjitāmurwīṃ wikrameṇa mahābalaiḥ |
kuru brāhmaṇasātsarwāmaśwamedhe mahākratau ||10||

pṛthiwyāṃ yāni ratnāni guṇawanti gunānwite |
tānyāpnuhi twaṃ kalyāṇi sukhinī śaradāṃ śatam ||11||

yathā ca twābhinandāmi wadhwadya kṣaumasaṃwṛtām |
tathā bhūyo'bhinandiṣye sūtaputrāṃ guṇānwitām ||12||

tatastu kṛtadārebhyaḥ pāṇḍubhyaḥ prāhiṇoddhariḥ |
muktāwaiḍūryacitrāṇi haimānyābharaṇāni ca ||13||

wāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi nānādeśyāni mādhawaḥ |
kambalājinaratnāni sparśawanti śubhāni ca ||14||

śayanāsanayānāni wiwidhāni mahānti ca |
waiḍūryawajracitrāṇi śataśo bhājanāni ca ||15||

rūpayauwanadākṣiṇyairupetāśca swalaṅkṛtāḥ |
preṣyāḥ sampradadau kṛṣṇo nānādeśyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ||16||

gajānwinītānbhadrāṃśca sadaśwāṃśca swalaṅkṛtān |
rathāṃśca dāntānsauwarṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ paṭṭairalaṅkṛtān ||17||

koṭiśaśca suwarṇaṃ sa teṣāmakṛtakaṃ tathā |
wītīkṛtamameyātmā prāhiṇonmadhusūdanaḥ ||18||

tatsarwaṃ pratijagrāha dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
mudā paramayā yukto gowindapriyakāmyayā ||19||






              widurāgamanaparwa
                  192


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato rājñāṃ carairāptaiścāraḥ samupanīyata |
pāṇḍawairupasampannā draupadī patibhiḥ śubhā ||1||

yena taddhanurāyamya lakṣyaṃ widdhaṃ mahātmanā |
so'rjuno jayatāṃ śreṣṭho mahābāṇadhanurdharaḥ ||2||

yaḥ śalyaṃ madrarājānamutkṣipyābhrāmayadbalī |
trāsayaṃścāpi saṅkruddho wṛkṣeṇa puruṣānraṇe ||3||

na cāpi sambhramaḥ kaścidāsīttatra mahātmanaḥ |
sa bhīmo bhīmasaṃsparśaḥ śatrusenāṅgapātanaḥ ||4||

brahmarūpadharāñśrutwā pāṇḍurājasutāṃstadā |
kaunteyānmanujendrāṇāṃ wismayaḥ samajāyata ||5||

saputrā hi purā kuntī dagdhā jatugṛhe śrutā |
punarjātāniti smaitānmanyante sarwapārthiwāḥ ||6||

dhikkurwantastadā bhīṣmaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca kaurawam |
karmaṇā sunṛśaṃsena purocanakṛtena wai ||7||

wṛtte swayaṃware caiwa rājānaḥ sarwa ewa te |
yathāgataṃ wiprajagmurwiditwā pāṇḍawānwṛtān ||8||

atha duryodhano rājā wimanā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha |
aśwatthāmnā mātulena karṇena ca kṛpeṇa ca ||9||

winiwṛtto wṛtaṃ dṛṣṭwā draupadyā śwetawāhanam |
taṃ tu duḥśāsano wrīḍanmandaṃ mandamiwābrawīt ||10||

yadyasau brāhmaṇo na syādwindeta draupadīṃ na saḥ |
na hi taṃ tattwato rājanweda kaściddhanañjayam ||11||

daiwaṃ tu paramaṃ manye pauruṣaṃ tu nirarthakam |
dhigasmatpauruṣaṃ tāta yaddharantīha pāṇḍawāḥ ||12||

ewaṃ sambhāṣamāṇāste nindantaśca purocanam |
wiwiśurhāstinapuraṃ dīnā wigatacetasaḥ ||13||

trastā wigatasaṅkalpā dṛṣṭwā pārthānmahaujasaḥ |
muktānhawyawahāccainānsaṃyuktāndrupadena ca ||14||

dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca sañcintya tathaiwa ca śikhaṇḍinam |
drupadasyātmajāṃścānyānsarwayuddhawiśāradān ||15||

widurastwatha tāñśrutwā draupadyā pāṇḍawānwṛtān |
wrīḍitāndhārtarāṣṭrāṃśca bhagnadarpānupāgatān ||16||

tataḥ prītamanāḥ kṣattā dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ wiśāṃ pate |
uwāca diṣṭyā kurawo wardhanta iti wismitaḥ ||17||

waicitrawīryastu nṛpo niśamya widurasya tat |
abrawītparamaprīto diṣṭyā diṣṭyeti bhārata ||18||

manyate hi wṛtaṃ putraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ drupadakanyayā |
duryodhanamawijñānātprajñācakṣurnareśwaraḥ ||19||

atha twājñāpayāmāsa draupadyā bhūṣaṇaṃ bahu |
ānīyatāṃ wai kṛṣṇeti putraṃ duryodhanaṃ tadā ||20||

athāsya paścādwidura ācakhyau pāṇḍawānwṛtān |
sarwānkuśalino wīrānpūjitāndrupadena ca ||21||

teṣāṃ sambandhinaścānyānbahūnbalasamanwitān ||21||

dhṛtarāṣṭra uwāca||

yathaiwa pāṇḍoḥ putrāste tathaiwābhyadhikā mama |
seyamabhyadhikā prītirwṛddhirwidura me matā ||22||

yatte kuśalino wīrā mitrawantaśca pāṇḍawāḥ ||22||

ko hi drupadamāsādya mitraṃ kṣattaḥ sabāndhawam |
na bubhūṣedbhawenārthī gataśrīrapi pārthiwaḥ ||23||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

taṃ tathā bhāṣamāṇaṃ tu widuraḥ pratyabhāṣata |
nityaṃ bhawatu te buddhireṣā rājañśataṃ samāḥ ||24||

tato duryodhanaścaiwa rādheyaśca wiśāṃ pate |
dhṛtarāṣṭramupāgamya waco'brūtāmidaṃ tadā ||25||

saṃnidhau widurasya twāṃ waktuṃ nṛpa na śaknuwaḥ |
wiwiktamiti wakṣyāwaḥ kiṃ tawedaṃ cikīrṣitam ||26||

sapatnawṛddhiṃ yattāta manyase wṛddhimātmanaḥ |
abhiṣṭauṣi ca yatkṣattuḥ samīpe dwipadāṃ wara ||27||

anyasminnṛpa kartawye twamanyatkuruṣe'nagha |
teṣāṃ balawighāto hi kartawyastāta nityaśaḥ ||28||

te wayaṃ prāptakālasya cikīrṣāṃ mantrayāmahe |
yathā no na graseyuste saputrabalabāndhawān ||29||






                  193


dhṛtarāṣṭra uwāca||

ahamapyewamewaitaccintayāmi yathā yuwām |
wiwektuṃ nāhamicchāmi twākāraṃ widuraṃ prati ||1||

atasteṣāṃ guṇānewa kīrtayāmi wiśeṣataḥ |
nāwabudhyeta widuro mamābhiprāyamiṅgitaiḥ ||2||

yacca twaṃ manyase prāptaṃ tadbrūhi twaṃ suyodhana |
rādheya manyase twaṃ ca yatprāptaṃ tadbrawīhi me ||3||

duryodhana uwāca||

adya tānkuśalairwipraiḥ sukṛtairāptakāribhiḥ |
kuntīputrānbhedayāmo mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍawau ||4||

atha wā drupado rājā mahadbhirwittasañcayaiḥ |
putrāścāsya pralobhyantāmamātyāścaiwa sarwaśaḥ ||5||

parityajadhwaṃ rājānaṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram |
atha tatraiwa wā teṣāṃ niwāsaṃ rocayantu te ||6||

ihaiṣāṃ doṣawadwāsaṃ warṇayantu pṛthakpṛthak |
te bhidyamānāstatraiwa manaḥ kurwantu pāṇḍawāḥ ||7||

athawā kuśalāḥ kecidupāyanipuṇā narāḥ |
itaretarataḥ pārthānbhedayantwanurāgataḥ ||8||

wyutthāpayantu wā kṛṣṇāṃ bahutwātsukaraṃ hi tat |
athawā pāṇḍawāṃstasyāṃ bhedayantu tataśca tām ||9||

bhīmasenasya wā rājannupāyakuśalairnaraiḥ |
mṛtyurwidhīyatāṃ channaiḥ sa hi teṣāṃ balādhikaḥ ||10||

tasmiṃstu nihate rājanhatotsāhā hataujasaḥ |
yatiṣyante na rājyāya sa hi teṣāṃ wyapāśrayaḥ ||11||

ajeyo hyarjunaḥ saṅkhye pṛṣṭhagope wṛkodare |
tamṛte phalguno yuddhe rādheyasya na pādabhāk ||12||

te jānamānā daurbalyaṃ bhīmasenamṛte mahat |
asmānbalawato jñātwā naśiṣyantyabalīyasaḥ ||13||

ihāgateṣu pārtheṣu nideśawaśawartiṣu |
prawartiṣyāmahe rājanyathāśraddhaṃ nibarhaṇe ||14||

athawā darśanīyābhiḥ pramadābhirwilobhyatām |
ekaikastatra kaunteyastataḥ kṛṣṇā wirajyatām ||15||

preṣyatāṃ wāpi rādheyasteṣāmāgamanāya wai |
te loptrahāraiḥ sandhāya wadhyantāmāptakāribhiḥ ||16||

eteṣāmabhyupāyānāṃ yaste nirdoṣawānmataḥ |
tasya prayogamātiṣṭha purā kālo'tiwartate ||17||

yāwaccākṛtawiśwāsā drupade pārthiwarṣabhe |
tāwadewādya te śakyā na śakyāstu tataḥ param ||18||

eṣā mama matistāta nigrahāya prawartate |
sādhu wā yadi wāsādhu kiṃ wā rādheya manyase ||19||






                  194


karṇa uwāca||

duryodhana tawa prajñā na samyagiti me matiḥ |
na hyupāyena te śakyāḥ pāṇḍawāḥ kurunandana ||1||

pūrwamewa hi te sūkṣmairupāyairyatitāstwayā |
nigrahītuṃ yadā wīra śakitā na tadā twayā ||2||

ihaiwa wartamānāste samīpe tawa pārthiwa |
ajātapakṣāḥ śiśawaḥ śakitā naiwa bādhitum ||3||

jātapakṣā wideśasthā wiwṛddhāḥ sarwaśo'dya te |
nopāyasādhyāḥ kaunteyā mamaiṣā matiracyuta ||4||

na ca te wyasanairyoktuṃ śakyā diṣṭakṛtā hi te |
śaṅkitāścepsawaścaiwa pitṛpaitāmahaṃ padam ||5||

paraspareṇa bhedaśca nādhātuṃ teṣu śakyate |
ekasyāṃ ye ratāḥ patnyāṃ na bhidyante parasparam ||6||

na cāpi kṛṣṇā śakyeta tebhyo bhedayituṃ paraiḥ |
paridyūnānwṛtawatī kimutādya mṛjāwataḥ ||7||

īpsitaśca guṇaḥ strīṇāmekasyā bahubhartṛtā |
taṃ ca prāptawatī kṛṣṇā na sā bhedayituṃ sukham ||8||

āryawṛttaśca pāñcālyo na sa rājā dhanapriyaḥ |
na santyakṣyati kaunteyānrājyadānairapi dhruwam ||9||

tathāsya putro guṇawānanuraktaśca pāṇḍawān |
tasmānnopāyasādhyāṃstānahaṃ manye kathañcana ||10||

idaṃ twadya kṣamaṃ kartumasmākaṃ puruṣarṣabha |
yāwanna kṛtamūlāste pāṇḍaweyā wiśāṃ pate ||11||

tāwatpraharaṇīyāste rocatāṃ tawa wikramaḥ ||11||

asmatpakṣo mahānyāwadyāwatpāñcālako laghuḥ |
tāwatpraharaṇaṃ teṣāṃ kriyatāṃ mā wicāraya ||12||

wāhanāni prabhūtāni mitrāṇi bahulāni ca |
yāwanna teṣāṃ gāndhāre tāwadewāśu wikrama ||13||

yāwacca rājā pāñcālyo nodyame kurute manaḥ |
saha putrairmahāwīryaistāwadewāśu wikrama ||14||

yāwannāyāti wārṣṇeyaḥ karṣanyādawawāhinīm |
rājyārthe pāṇḍaweyānāṃ tāwadewāśu wikrama ||15||

wasūni wiwidhānbhogānrājyamewa ca kewalam |
nātyājyamasti kṛṣṇasya pāṇḍawārthe mahīpate ||16||

wikrameṇa mahī prāptā bharatena mahātmanā |
wikrameṇa ca lokāṃstrīñjitawānpākaśāsanaḥ ||17||

wikramaṃ ca praśaṃsanti kṣatriyasya wiśāṃ pate |
swako hi dharmaḥ śūrāṇāṃ wikramaḥ pārthiwarṣabha ||18||

te balena wayaṃ rājanmahatā caturaṅgiṇā |
pramathya drupadaṃ śīghramānayāmeha pāṇḍawān ||19||

na hi sāmnā na dānena na bhedena ca pāṇḍawāḥ |
śakyāḥ sādhayituṃ tasmādwikrameṇaiwa tāñjahi ||20||

tānwikrameṇa jitwemāmakhilāṃ bhuṅkṣwa medinīm |
nānyamatra prapaśyāmi kāryopāyaṃ janādhipa ||21||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

śrutwā tu rādheyawaco dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ pratāpawān |
abhipūjya tataḥ paścādidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||22||

upapannaṃ mahāprājñe kṛtāstre sūtanandane |
twayi wikramasampannamidaṃ wacanamīdṛśam ||23||

bhūya ewa tu bhīṣmaśca droṇo widura ewa ca |
yuwāṃ ca kurutāṃ buddhiṃ bhawedyā naḥ sukhodayā ||24||

tata ānāyya tānsarwānmantriṇaḥ sumahāyaśāḥ |
dhṛtarāṣṭro mahārāja mantrayāmāsa wai tadā ||25||






                  195


bhīṣma uwāca||

na rocate wigraho me pāṇḍuputraiḥ kathañcana |
yathaiwa dhṛtarāṣṭro me tathā pāṇḍurasaṃśayam ||1||

gāndhāryāśca yathā putrāstathā kuntīsutā matāḥ |
yathā ca mama te rakṣyā dhṛtarāṣṭra tathā tawa ||2||

yathā ca mama rājñaśca tathā duryodhanasya te |
tathā kurūṇāṃ sarweṣāmanyeṣāmapi bhārata ||3||

ewaṃ gate wigrahaṃ tairna rocaye; sandhāya wīrairdīyatāmadya bhūmiḥ |
teṣāmapīdaṃ prapitāmahānāṃ; rājyaṃ pituścaiwa kurūttamānām ||4||

duryodhana yathā rājyaṃ twamidaṃ tāta paśyasi |
mama paitṛkamityewaṃ te'pi paśyanti pāṇḍawāḥ ||5||

yadi rājyaṃ na te prāptāḥ pāṇḍaweyāstapaswinaḥ |
kuta ewa tawāpīdaṃ bhāratasya ca kasyacit ||6||

atha dharmeṇa rājyaṃ twaṃ prāptawānbharatarṣabha |
te'pi rājyamanuprāptāḥ pūrwameweti me matiḥ ||7||

madhureṇaiwa rājyasya teṣāmardhaṃ pradīyatām |
etaddhi puruṣawyāghra hitaṃ sarwajanasya ca ||8||

ato'nyathā cetkriyate na hitaṃ no bhawiṣyati |
tawāpyakīrtiḥ sakalā bhawiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ||9||

kīrtirakṣaṇamātiṣṭha kīrtirhi paramaṃ balam |
naṣṭakīrtermanuṣyasya jīwitaṃ hyaphalaṃ smṛtam ||10||

yāwatkīrtirmanuṣyasya na praṇaśyati kaurawa |
tāwajjīwati gāndhāre naṣṭakīrtistu naśyati ||11||

tamimaṃ samupātiṣṭha dharmaṃ kurukulocitam |
anurūpaṃ mahābāho pūrweṣāmātmanaḥ kuru ||12||

diṣṭyā dharanti te wīrā diṣṭyā jīwati sā pṛthā |
diṣṭyā purocanaḥ pāpo nasakāmo'tyayaṃ gataḥ ||13||

tadā prabhṛti gāndhāre na śaknomyabhiwīkṣitum |
loke prāṇabhṛtāṃ kañcicchrutwā kuntīṃ tathāgatām ||14||

na cāpi doṣeṇa tathā loko waiti purocanam |
yathā twāṃ puruṣawyāghra loko doṣeṇa gacchati ||15||

tadidaṃ jīwitaṃ teṣāṃ tawa kalmaṣanāśanam |
saṃmantawyaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍawānāṃ ca darśanam ||16||

na cāpi teṣāṃ wīrāṇāṃ jīwatāṃ kurunandana |
pitryoṃ'śaḥ śakya ādātumapi wajrabhṛtā swayam ||17||

te hi sarwe sthitā dharme sarwe caiwaikacetasaḥ |
adharmeṇa nirastāśca tulye rājye wiśeṣataḥ ||18||

yadi dharmastwayā kāryo yadi kāryaṃ priyaṃ ca me |
kṣemaṃ ca yadi kartawyaṃ teṣāmardhaṃ pradīyatām ||19||






                  196


droṇa uwāca||

mantrāya samupānītairdhṛtarāṣṭrahitairnṛpa |
dharmyaṃ pathyaṃ yaśasyaṃ ca wācyamityanuśuśrumaḥ ||1||

mamāpyeṣā matistāta yā bhīṣmasya mahātmanaḥ |
saṃwibhajyāstu kaunteyā dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ ||2||

preṣyatāṃ drupadāyāśu naraḥ kaścitpriyaṃwadaḥ |
bahulaṃ ratnamādāya teṣāmarthāya bhārata ||3||

mithaḥ kṛtyaṃ ca tasmai sa ādāya bahu gacchatu |
wṛddhiṃ ca paramāṃ brūyāttatsaṃyogodbhawāṃ tathā ||4||

samprīyamāṇaṃ twāṃ brūyādrājandūryodhanaṃ tathā |
asakṛddrupade caiwa dhṛṣṭadyumne ca bhārata ||5||

ucitatwaṃ priyatwaṃ ca yogasyāpi ca warṇayet |
punaḥ punaśca kaunteyānmādrīputrau ca sāntwayan ||6||

hiraṇmayāni śubhrāṇi bahūnyābharaṇāni ca |
wacanāttawa rājendra draupadyāḥ samprayacchatu ||7||

tathā drupadaputrāṇāṃ sarweṣāṃ bharatarṣabha |
pāṇḍawānāṃ ca sarweṣāṃ kuntyā yuktāni yāni ca ||8||

ewaṃ sāntwasamāyuktaṃ drupadaṃ pāṇḍawaiḥ saha |
uktwāthānantaraṃ brūyātteṣāmāgamanaṃ prati ||9||

anujñāteṣu wīreṣu balaṃ gacchatu śobhanam |
duḥśāsano wikarṇaśca pāṇḍawānānayantwiha ||10||

tataste pārthiwaśreṣṭha pūjyamānāḥ sadā twayā |
prakṛtīnāmanumate pade sthāsyanti paitṛke ||11||

ewaṃ tawa mahārāja teṣu putreṣu caiwa ha |
wṛttamaupayikaṃ manye bhīṣmeṇa saha bhārata ||12||

karṇa uwāca||

yojitāwarthamānābhyāṃ sarwakāryeṣwanantarau |
na mantrayetāṃ twacchreyaḥ kimadbhutataraṃ tataḥ ||13||

duṣṭena manasā yo wai pracchannenāntarātmanā |
brūyānniḥśreyasaṃ nāma kathaṃ kuryātsatāṃ matam ||14||

na mitrāṇyarthakṛcchreṣu śreyase wetarāya wā |
widhipūrwaṃ hi sarwasya duḥkhaṃ wā yadi wā sukham ||15||

kṛtaprajño'kṛtaprajño bālo wṛddhaśca mānawaḥ |
sasahāyo'sahāyaśca sarwaṃ sarwatra windati ||16||

śrūyate hi purā kaścidambuwīca iti śrutaḥ |
āsīdrājagṛhe rājā māgadhānāṃ mahīkṣitām ||17||

sa hīnaḥ karaṇaiḥ sarwairucchwāsaparamo nṛpaḥ |
amātyasaṃsthaḥ kāryeṣu sarweṣwewābhawattadā ||18||

tasyāmātyo mahākarṇirbabhūwaikeśwaraḥ purā |
sa labdhabalamātmānaṃ manyamāno'wamanyate ||19||

sa rājña upabhogyāni striyo ratnadhanāni ca |
ādade sarwaśo mūḍha aiśwaryaṃ ca swayaṃ tadā ||20||

tadādāya ca lubdhasya lābhāllobho wyawardhata |
tathā hi sarwamādāya rājyamasya jihīrṣati ||21||

hīnasya karaṇaiḥ sarwairucchwāsaparamasya ca |
yatamāno'pi tadrājyaṃ na śaśāketi naḥ śrutam ||22||

kimanyadwihitānnūnaṃ tasya sā puruṣendratā |
yadi te wihitaṃ rājyaṃ bhawiṣyati wiśāṃ pate ||23||

miṣataḥ sarwalokasya sthāsyate twayi taddhruwam |
ato'nyathā cedwihitaṃ yatamāno na lapsyase ||24||

ewaṃ widwannupādatswa mantriṇāṃ sādhwasādhutām |
duṣṭānāṃ caiwa boddhawyamaduṣṭānāṃ ca bhāṣitam ||25||

droṇa uwāca||

widma te bhāwadoṣeṇa yadarthamidamucyate |
duṣṭaḥ pāṇḍawahetostwaṃ doṣaṃ khyāpayase hi naḥ ||26||

hitaṃ tu paramaṃ karṇa brawīmi kuruwardhanam |
atha twaṃ manyase duṣṭaṃ brūhi yatparamaṃ hitam ||27||

ato'nyathā cetkriyate yadbrawīmi paraṃ hitam |
kurawo winaśiṣyanti nacireṇeti me matiḥ ||28||






                  197


widura uwāca||

rājanniḥsaṃśayaṃ śreyo wācyastwamasi bāndhawaiḥ |
na twaśuśrūṣamāṇeṣu wākyaṃ sampratitiṣṭhati ||1||

hitaṃ hi tawa tadwākyamuktawānkurusattamaḥ |
bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawo rājanpratigṛhṇāsi tanna ca ||2||

tathā droṇena bahudhā bhāṣitaṃ hitamuttamam |
tacca rādhāsutaḥ karṇo manyate na hitaṃ tawa ||3||

cintayaṃśca na paśyāmi rājaṃstawa suhṛttamam |
ābhyāṃ puruṣasiṃhābhyāṃ yo wā syātprajñayādhikaḥ ||4||

imau hi wṛddhau wayasā prajñayā ca śrutena ca |
samau ca twayi rājendra teṣu pāṇḍusuteṣu ca ||5||

dharme cānawamau rājansatyatāyāṃ ca bhārata |
rāmāddāśaratheścaiwa gayāccaiwa na saṃśayaḥ ||6||

na coktawantāwaśreyaḥ purastādapi kiñcana |
na cāpyapakṛtaṃ kiñcidanayorlakṣyate twayi ||7||

tāwimau puruṣawyāghrāwanāgasi nṛpa twayi |
na mantrayetāṃ twacchreyaḥ kathaṃ satyaparākramau ||8||

prajñāwantau naraśreṣṭhāwasmiṃlloke narādhipa |
twannimittamato nemau kiñcijjihmaṃ wadiṣyataḥ ||9||

iti me naiṣṭhikī buddhirwartate kurunandana ||9||

na cārthahetordharmajñau wakṣyataḥ pakṣasaṃśritam |
etaddhi paramaṃ śreyo menāte tawa bhārata ||10||

duryodhanaprabhṛtayaḥ putrā rājanyathā tawa |
tathaiwa pāṇḍaweyāste putrā rājanna saṃśayaḥ ||11||

teṣu cedahitaṃ kiñcinmantrayeyurabuddhitaḥ |
mantriṇaste na te śreyaḥ prapaśyanti wiśeṣataḥ ||12||

atha te hṛdaye rājanwiśeṣasteṣu wartate |
antarasthaṃ wiwṛṇwānāḥ śreyaḥ kuryurna te dhruwam ||13||

etadarthamimau rājanmahātmānau mahādyutī |
nocaturwiwṛtaṃ kiñcinna hyeṣa tawa niścayaḥ ||14||

yaccāpyaśakyatāṃ teṣāmāhatuḥ puruṣarṣabhau |
tattathā puruṣawyāghra tawa tadbhadramastu te ||15||

kathaṃ hi pāṇḍawaḥ śrīmānsawyasācī parantapaḥ |
śakyo wijetuṃ saṅgrāme rājanmaghawatā api ||16||

bhīmaseno mahābāhurnāgāyutabalo mahān |
kathaṃ hi yudhi śakyeta wijetumamarairapi ||17||

tathaiwa kṛtinau yuddhe yamau yamasutāwiwa |
kathaṃ wiṣahituṃ śakyau raṇe jīwitumicchatā ||18||

yasmindhṛtiranukrośaḥ kṣamā satyaṃ parākramaḥ |
nityāni pāṇḍawaśreṣṭhe sa jīyeta kathaṃ raṇe ||19||

yeṣāṃ pakṣadharo rāmo yeṣāṃ mantrī janārdanaḥ |
kiṃ nu tairajitaṃ saṅkhye yeṣāṃ pakṣe ca sātyakiḥ ||20||

drupadaḥ śwaśuro yeṣāṃ yeṣāṃ śyālāśca pārṣatāḥ |
dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhā wīrā bhrātaro drupadātmajāḥ ||21||

so'śakyatāṃ ca wijñāya teṣāmagreṇa bhārata |
dāyādyatāṃ ca dharmeṇa samyakteṣu samācara ||22||

idaṃ nirdigdhamayaśaḥ purocanakṛtaṃ mahat |
teṣāmanugraheṇādya rājanprakṣālayātmanaḥ ||23||

drupado'pi mahānrājā kṛtawairaśca naḥ purā |
tasya saṅgrahaṇaṃ rājanswapakṣasya wiwardhanam ||24||

balawantaśca dāśārhā bahawaśca wiśāṃ pate |
yataḥ kṛṣṇastataste syuryataḥ kṛṣṇastato jayaḥ ||25||

yacca sāmnaiwa śakyeta kāryaṃ sādhayituṃ nṛpa |
ko daiwaśaptastatkārtuṃ wigraheṇa samācaret ||26||

śrutwā ca jīwataḥ pārthānpaurajānapado janaḥ |
balawaddarśane gṛdhnusteṣāṃ rājankuru priyam ||27||

duryodhanaśca karṇaśca śakuniścāpi saubalaḥ |
adharmayuktā duṣprajñā bālā maiṣāṃ wacaḥ kṛthāḥ ||28||

uktametanmayā rājanpurā guṇawatastawa |
duryodhanāparādhena prajeyaṃ winaśiṣyati ||29||






                  198


dhṛtarāṣṭra uwāca||

bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawo widwāndroṇaśca bhagawānṛṣiḥ |
hitaṃ paramakaṃ wākyaṃ twaṃ ca satyaṃ brawīṣi mām ||1||

yathaiwa pāṇḍoste wīrāḥ kuntīputrā mahārathāḥ |
tathaiwa dharmataḥ sarwe mama putrā na saṃśayaḥ ||2||

yathaiwa mama putrāṇāmidaṃ rājyaṃ widhīyate |
tathaiwa pāṇḍuputrāṇāmidaṃ rājyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||3||

kṣattarānaya gacchaitānsaha mātrā susatkṛtān |
tayā ca dewarūpiṇyā kṛṣṇayā saha bhārata ||4||

diṣṭyā jīwanti te pārthā diṣṭyā jīwati sā pṛthā |
diṣṭyā drupadakanyāṃ ca labdhawanto mahārathāḥ ||5||

diṣṭyā wardhāmahe sarwe diṣṭyā śāntaḥ purocanaḥ |
diṣṭyā mama paraṃ duḥkhamapanītaṃ mahādyute ||6||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato jagāma widuro dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt |
sakāśaṃ yajñasenasya pāṇḍawānāṃ ca bhārata ||7||

tatra gatwā sa dharmajñaḥ sarwaśāstrawiśāradaḥ |
drupadaṃ nyāyato rājansaṃyuktamupatasthiwān ||8||

sa cāpi pratijagrāha dharmeṇa widuraṃ tataḥ |
cakratuśca yathānyāyaṃ kuśalapraśnasaṃwidam ||9||

dadarśa pāṇḍawāṃstatra wāsudewaṃ ca bhārata |
snehātpariṣwajya sa tānpapracchānāmayaṃ tataḥ ||10||

taiścāpyamitabuddhiḥ sa pūjito'tha yathākramam |
wacanāddhṛtarāṣṭrasya snehayuktaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ||11||

papracchānāmayaṃ rājaṃstatastānpāṇḍunandanān |
pradadau cāpi ratnāni wiwidhāni wasūni ca ||12||

pāṇḍawānāṃ ca kuntyāśca draupadyāśca wiśāṃ pate |
drupadasya ca putrāṇāṃ yathā dattāni kaurawaiḥ ||13||

prowāca cāmitamatiḥ praśritaṃ winayānwitaḥ |
drupadaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ saṃnidhau keśawasya ca ||14||

rājañśṛṇu sahāmātyaḥ saputraśca waco mama |
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputrastwāṃ sahāmātyaḥ sabāndhawaḥ ||15||

abrawītkuśalaṃ rājanprīyamāṇaḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
prītimāṃste dṛḍhaṃ cāpi sambandhena narādhipa ||16||

tathā bhīṣmaḥ śāntanawaḥ kaurawaiḥ saha sarwaśaḥ |
kuśalaṃ twāṃ mahāprājñaḥ sarwataḥ paripṛcchati ||17||

bhāradwājo maheṣwāso droṇaḥ priyasakhastawa |
samāśleṣamupetya twāṃ kuśalaṃ paripṛcchati ||18||

dhṛtarāṣṭraśca pāñcālya twayā sambandhamīyiwān |
kṛtārthaṃ manyate''tmānaṃ tathā sarwe'pi kaurawāḥ ||19||

na tathā rājyasamprāptisteṣāṃ prītikarī matā |
yathā sambandhakaṃ prāpya yajñasena twayā saha ||20||

etadwiditwā tu bhawānprasthāpayatu pāṇḍawān |
draṣṭuṃ hi pāṇḍudāyādāṃstwarante kurawo bhṛśam ||21||

wiproṣitā dīrghakālamime cāpi nararṣabhāḥ |
utsukā nagaraṃ draṣṭuṃ bhawiṣyanti pṛthā tathā ||22||

kṛṣṇāmapi ca pāñcālīṃ sarwāḥ kuruwarastriyaḥ |
draṣṭukāmāḥ pratīkṣante puraṃ ca wiṣayaṃ ca naḥ ||23||

sa bhawānpāṇḍuputrāṇāmājñāpayatu māciram |
gamanaṃ sahadārāṇāmetadāgamanaṃ mama ||24||

wisṛṣṭeṣu twayā rājanpāṇḍaweṣu mahātmasu |
tato'haṃ preṣayiṣyāmi dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śīghragān ||25||

āgamiṣyanti kaunteyāḥ kuntī ca saha kṛṣṇayā ||25||






              rājyālambhaparwa
                  199


drupada uwāca||

ewametanmahāprājña yathāttha widurādya mām |
mamāpi paramo harṣaḥ sambandhe'sminkṛte wibho ||1||

gamanaṃ cāpi yuktaṃ syādgṛhameṣāṃ mahātmanām |
na tu tāwanmayā yuktametadwaktuṃ swayaṃ girā ||2||

yadā tu manyate wīraḥ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
bhīmasenārjunau caiwa yamau ca puruṣarṣabhau ||3||

rāmakṛṣṇau ca dharmajñau tadā gacchantu pāṇḍawāḥ |
etau hi puruṣawyāghrāweṣāṃ priyahite ratau ||4||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

parawanto wayaṃ rājaṃstwayi sarwe sahānugāḥ |
yathā wakṣyasi naḥ prītyā kariṣyāmastathā wayam ||5||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato'brawīdwāsudewo gamanaṃ mama rocate |
yathā wā manyate rājā drupadaḥ sarwadharmawit ||6||

drupada uwāca||

yathaiwa manyate wīro dāśārhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ |
prāptakālaṃ mahābāhuḥ sā buddhirniścitā mama ||7||

yathaiwa hi mahābhāgāḥ kaunteyā mama sāmpratam |
tathaiwa wāsudewasya pāṇḍuputrā na saṃśayaḥ ||8||

na taddhyāyati kaunteyo dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
yadeṣāṃ puruṣawyāghraḥ śreyo dhyāyati keśawaḥ ||9||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataste samanujñātā drupadena mahātmanā |
pāṇḍawāścaiwa kṛṣṇaśca widuraśca mahāmatiḥ ||10||

ādāya draupadīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ kuntīṃ caiwa yaśaswinīm |
sawihāraṃ sukhaṃ jagmurnagaraṃ nāgasāhwayam ||11||

śrutwā copasthitānwīrāndhṛtarāṣṭro'pi kaurawaḥ |
pratigrahāya pāṇḍūnāṃ preṣayāmāsa kaurawān ||12||

wikarṇaṃ ca maheṣwāsaṃ citrasenaṃ ca bhārata |
droṇaṃ ca parameṣwāsaṃ gautamaṃ kṛpamewa ca ||13||

taiste pariwṛtā wīrāḥ śobhamānā mahārathāḥ |
nagaraṃ hāstinapuraṃ śanaiḥ prawiwiśustadā ||14||

kautūhalena nagaraṃ dīryamāṇamiwābhawat |
yatra te puruṣawyāghrāḥ śokaduḥkhawināśanāḥ ||15||

tata uccāwacā wācaḥ priyāḥ priyacikīrṣubhiḥ |
udīritā aśṛṇwaṃste pāṇḍawā hṛdayaṅgamāḥ ||16||

ayaṃ sa puruṣawyāghraḥ punarāyāti dharmawit |
yo naḥ swāniwa dāyādāndharmeṇa parirakṣati ||17||

adya pāṇḍurmahārājo wanādiwa wanapriyaḥ |
āgataḥ priyamasmākaṃ cikīrṣurnātra saṃśayaḥ ||18||

kiṃ nu nādya kṛtaṃ tāwatsarweṣāṃ naḥ paraṃ priyam |
yannaḥ kuntīsutā wīrā bhartāraḥ punarāgatāḥ ||19||

yadi dattaṃ yadi hutaṃ widyate yadi nastapaḥ |
tena tiṣṭhantu nagare pāṇḍawāḥ śaradāṃ śatam ||20||

tataste dhṛtarāṣṭrasya bhīṣmasya ca mahātmanaḥ |
anyeṣāṃ ca tadarhāṇāṃ cakruḥ pādābhiwandanam ||21||

kṛtwā tu kuśalapraśnaṃ sarweṇa nagareṇa te |
samāwiśanta weśmāni dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt ||22||

wiśrāntāste mahātmānaḥ kañcitkālaṃ mahābalāḥ |
āhūtā dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa rājñā śāntanawena ca ||23||

dhṛtarāṣṭra uwāca||

bhrātṛbhiḥ saha kaunteya nibodhedaṃ waco mama |
punarwo wigraho mā bhūtkhāṇḍawaprasthamāwiśa ||24||

na ca wo wasatastatra kaścicchaktaḥ prabādhitum |
saṃrakṣyamāṇānpārthena tridaśāniwa wajriṇā ||25||

ardhaṃ rājyasya samprāpya khāṇḍawaprasthamāwiśa ||25||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

pratigṛhya tu tadwākyaṃ nṛpaṃ sarwe praṇamya ca |
pratasthire tato ghoraṃ wanaṃ tanmanujarṣabhāḥ ||26||

ardhaṃ rājyasya samprāpya khāṇḍawaprasthamāwiśan ||26||

tataste pāṇḍawāstatra gatwā kṛṣṇapurogamāḥ |
maṇḍayāṃ cakrire tadwai puraṃ swargawadacyutāḥ ||27||

tataḥ puṇye śiwe deśe śāntiṃ kṛtwā mahārathāḥ |
nagaraṃ māpayāmāsurdwaipāyanapurogamāḥ ||28||

sāgarapratirūpābhiḥ parikhābhiralaṅkṛtam |
prākāreṇa ca sampannaṃ diwamāwṛtya tiṣṭhatā ||29||

pāṇḍurābhraprakāśena himarāśinibhena ca |
śuśubhe tatpuraśreṣṭhaṃ nāgairbhogawatī yathā ||30||

dwipakṣagaruḍaprakhyairdwārairghorapradarśanaiḥ |
guptamabhracayaprakhyairgopurairmandaropamaiḥ ||31||

wiwidhairatinirwiddhaiḥ śastropetaiḥ susaṃwṛtaiḥ |
śaktibhiścāwṛtaṃ taddhi dwijihwairiwa pannagaiḥ ||32||

talpaiścābhyāsikairyuktaṃ śuśubhe yodharakṣitam ||32||

tīkṣṇāṅkuśaśataghnībhiryantrajālaiśca śobhitam |
āyasaiśca mahācakraiḥ śuśubhe tatpurottamam ||33||

suwibhaktamahārathyaṃ dewatābādhawarjitam |
wirocamānaṃ wiwidhaiḥ pāṇḍurairbhawanottamaiḥ ||34||

tattriwiṣṭapasaṅkāśamindraprasthaṃ wyarocata |
meghawṛndamiwākāśe wṛddhaṃ widyutsamāwṛtam ||35||

tatra ramye śubhe deśe kaurawyasya niweśanam |
śuśubhe dhanasampūrṇaṃ dhanādhyakṣakṣayopamam ||36||

tatrāgacchandwijā rājansarwawedawidāṃ warāḥ |
niwāsaṃ rocayanti sma sarwabhāṣāwidastathā ||37||

waṇijaścābhyayustatra deśe digbhyo dhanārthinaḥ |
sarwaśilpawidaścaiwa wāsāyābhyāgamaṃstadā ||38||

udyānāni ca ramyāṇi nagarasya samantataḥ |
āmrairāmrātakairnīpairaśokaiścampakaistathā ||39||

puṃnāgairnāgapuṣpaiśca lakucaiḥ panasaistathā |
śālatālakadambaiśca bakulaiśca saketakaiḥ ||40||

manoharaiḥ puṣpitaiśca phalabhārāwanāmitaiḥ |
prācīnāmalakairlodhrairaṅkolaiśca supuṣpitaiḥ ||41||

jambūbhiḥ pāṭalābhiśca kubjakairatimuktakaiḥ |
karawīraiḥ pārijātairanyaiśca wiwidhairdrumaiḥ ||42||

nityapuṣpaphalopetairnānādwijagaṇāyutam |
mattabarhiṇasaṅghuṣṭaṃ kokilaiśca sadāmadaiḥ ||43||

gṛhairādarśawimalairwiwidhaiśca latāgṛhaiḥ |
manoharaiścitragṛhaistathā jagatiparwataiḥ ||44||

wāpībhirwiwidhābhiśca pūrṇābhiḥ paramāmbhasā ||44||

sarobhiratiramyaiśca padmotpalasugandhibhiḥ |
haṃsakāraṇḍawayutaiścakrawākopaśobhitaiḥ ||45||

ramyāśca wiwidhāstatra puṣkariṇyo wanāwṛtāḥ |
taḍāgāni ca ramyāṇi bṛhanti ca mahānti ca ||46||

teṣāṃ puṇyajanopetaṃ rāṣṭramāwasatāṃ mahat |
pāṇḍawānāṃ mahārāja śaśwatprītirawardhata ||47||

tatra bhīṣmeṇa rājñā ca dharmapraṇayane kṛte |
pāṇḍawāḥ samapadyanta khāṇḍawaprasthawāsinaḥ ||48||

pañcabhistairmaheṣwāsairindrakalpaiḥ samanwitam |
śuśubhe tatpuraśreṣṭhaṃ nāgairbhogawatī yathā ||49||

tānniweśya tato wīro rāmeṇa saha keśawaḥ |
yayau dwārawatīṃ rājanpāṇḍawānumate tadā ||50||






              arjunawanawāsaparwa
                  200


janamejaya uwāca||

ewaṃ samprāpya rājyaṃ tadindraprasthe tapodhana |
ata ūrdhwaṃ mahātmānaḥ kimakurwanta pāṇḍawāḥ ||1||

sarwa ewa mahātmānaḥ pūrwe mama pitāmahāḥ |
draupadī dharmapatnī ca kathaṃ tānanwawartata ||2||

kathaṃ wā pañca kṛṣṇāyāmekasyāṃ te narādhipāḥ |
wartamānā mahābhāgā nābhidyanta parasparam ||3||

śrotumicchāmyahaṃ sarwaṃ wistareṇa tapodhana |
teṣāṃ ceṣṭitamanyonyaṃ yuktānāṃ kṛṣṇayā tayā ||4||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

dhṛtarāṣṭrābhyanujñātāḥ kṛṣṇayā saha pāṇḍawāḥ |
remire puruṣawyāghrāḥ prāptarājyāḥ parantapāḥ ||5||

prāpya rājyaṃ mahātejāḥ satyasandho yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
pālayāmāsa dharmeṇa pṛthiwīṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha ||6||

jitārayo mahāprājñāḥ satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ |
mudaṃ paramikāṃ prāptāstatroṣuḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ ||7||

kurwāṇāḥ paurakāryāṇi sarwāṇi puruṣarṣabhāḥ |
āsāṃ cakrurmahārheṣu pārthiweṣwāsaneṣu ca ||8||

atha teṣūpawiṣṭeṣu sarweṣwewa mahātmasu |
nāradastwatha dewarṣirājagāma yadṛcchayā ||9||

āsanaṃ ruciraṃ tasmai pradadau swaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||9||

dewarṣerupawiṣṭasya swayamarghyaṃ yathāwidhi |
prādādyudhiṣṭhiro dhīmānrājyaṃ cāsmai nyawedayat ||10||

pratigṛhya tu tāṃ pūjāmṛṣiḥ prītamanābhawat |
āśīrbhirwardhayitwā tu tamuwācāsyatāmiti ||11||

niṣasādābhyanujñātastato rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
preṣayāmāsa kṛṣṇāyai bhagawantamupasthitam ||12||

śrutwaiwa draupadī cāpi śucirbhūtwā samāhitā |
jagāma tatra yatrāste nāradaḥ pāṇḍawaiḥ saha ||13||

tasyābhiwādya caraṇau dewarṣerdharmacāriṇī |
kṛtāñjaliḥ susaṃwītā sthitātha drupadātmajā ||14||

tasyāścāpi sa dharmātmā satyawāgṛṣisattamaḥ |
āśiṣo wiwidhāḥ procya rājaputryāstu nāradaḥ ||15||

gamyatāmiti howāca bhagawāṃstāmaninditām ||15||

gatāyāmatha kṛṣṇāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhirapurogamān |
wiwikte pāṇḍawānsarwānuwāca bhagawānṛṣiḥ ||16||

pāñcālī bhawatāmekā dharmapatnī yaśaswinī |
yathā wo nātra bhedaḥ syāttathā nītirwidhīyatām ||17||

sundopasundāwasurau bhrātarau sahitāwubhau |
āstāmawadhyāwanyeṣāṃ triṣu lokeṣu wiśrutau ||18||

ekarājyāwekagṛhāwekaśayyāsanāśanau |
tilottamāyāstau hetoranyonyamabhijaghnatuḥ ||19||

rakṣyatāṃ sauhṛdaṃ tasmādanyonyapratibhāwikam |
yathā wo nātra bhedaḥ syāttatkuruṣwa yudhiṣṭhira ||20||

yudhiṣṭhira uwāca||

sundopasundāwasurau kasya putrau mahāmune |
utpannaśca kathaṃ bhedaḥ kathaṃ cānyonyamaghnatām ||21||

apsarā dewakanyā wā kasya caiṣā tilottamā |
yasyāḥ kāmena saṃmattau jaghnatustau parasparam ||22||

etatsarwaṃ yathāwṛttaṃ wistareṇa tapodhana |
śrotumicchāmahe wipra paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ||23||






              sundopasundopākhyānam
                  201


nārada uwāca||

śṛṇu me wistareṇemamitihāsaṃ purātanam |
bhrātṛbhīḥ sahitaḥ pārtha yathāwṛttaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ||1||

mahāsurasyānwawāye hiraṇyakaśipoḥ purā |
nikumbho nāma daityendrastejaswī balawānabhūt ||2||

tasya putrau mahāwīryau jātau bhīmaparākramau |
sahānyonyena bhuñjāte winānyonyaṃ na gacchataḥ ||3||

anyonyasya priyakarāwanyonyasya priyaṃwadau |
ekaśīlasamācārau dwidhaiwaikaṃ yathā kṛtau ||4||

tau wiwṛddhau mahāwīryau kāryeṣwapyekaniścayau |
trailokyawijayārthāya samāsthāyaikaniścayam ||5||

kṛtwā dīkṣāṃ gatau windhyaṃ tatrograṃ tepatustapaḥ |
tau tu dīrgheṇa kālena tapoyuktau babhūwatuḥ ||6||

kṣutpipāsāpariśrāntau jaṭāwalkaladhāriṇau |
malopacitasarwāṅgau wāyubhakṣau babhūwatuḥ ||7||

ātmamāṃsāni juhwantau pādāṅguṣṭhāgradhiṣṭhitau |
ūrdhwabāhū cānimiṣau dīrghakālaṃ dhṛtawratau ||8||

tayostapaḥprabhāweṇa dīrghakālaṃ pratāpitaḥ |
dhūmaṃ pramumuce windhyastadadbhutamiwābhawat ||9||

tato dewābhawanbhītā ugraṃ dṛṣṭwā tayostapaḥ |
tapowighātārthamatho dewā wighnāni cakrire ||10||

ratnaiḥ pralobhayāmāsuḥ strībhiścobhau punaḥ punaḥ |
na ca tau cakraturbhaṅgaṃ wratasya sumahāwratau ||11||

atha māyāṃ punardewāstayoścakrurmahātmanoḥ |
bhaginyo mātaro bhāryāstayoḥ parijanastathā ||12||

paripātyamānā witrastāḥ śūlahastena rakṣasā |
srastābharaṇakeśāntā ekāntabhraṣṭawāsasaḥ ||13||

abhidhāwya tataḥ sarwāstau trāhīti wicukruśuḥ |
na ca tau cakraturbhaṅgaṃ wratasya sumahāwratau ||14||

yadā kṣobhaṃ nopayāti nārtimanyatarastayoḥ |
tataḥ striyastā bhūtaṃ ca sarwamantaradhīyata ||15||

tataḥ pitāmahaḥ sākṣādabhigamya mahāsurau |
wareṇa chandayāmāsa sarwalokapitāmahaḥ ||16||

tataḥ sundopasundau tau bhrātarau dṛḍhawikramau |
dṛṣṭwā pitāmahaṃ dewaṃ tasthatuḥ prāñjalī tadā ||17||

ūcatuśca prabhuṃ dewaṃ tatastau sahitau tadā |
āwayostapasānena yadi prītaḥ pitāmahaḥ ||18||

māyāwidāwastrawidau balinau kāmarūpiṇau |
ubhāwapyamarau syāwaḥ prasanno yadi nau prabhuḥ ||19||

pitāmaha uwāca||

ṛte'maratwamanyadwāṃ sarwamuktaṃ bhawiṣyati |
anyadwṛṇītāṃ mṛtyośca widhānamamaraiḥ samam ||20||

kariṣyāwedamiti yanmahadabhyutthitaṃ tapaḥ |
yuwayorhetunānena nāmaratwaṃ widhīyate ||21||

trailokyawijayārthāya bhawadbhyāmāsthitaṃ tapaḥ |
hetunānena daityendrau na wāṃ kāmaṃ karomyaham ||22||

sundopasundāwūcatuḥ||

triṣu lokeṣu yadbhūtaṃ kiñcitsthāwarajaṅgamam |
sarwasmānnau bhayaṃ na syādṛte'nyonyaṃ pitāmaha ||23||

pitāmaha uwāca||

yatprārthitaṃ yathoktaṃ ca kāmametaddadāni wām |
mṛtyorwidhānametacca yathāwadwāṃ bhawiṣyati ||24||

nārada uwāca||

tataḥ pitāmaho dattwā warametattadā tayoḥ |
niwartya tapasastau ca brahmalokaṃ jagāma ha ||25||

labdhwā warāṇi sarwāṇi daityendrāwapi tāwubhau |
awadhyau sarwalokasya swamewa bhawanaṃ gatau ||26||

tau tu labdhawarau dṛṣṭwā kṛtakāmau mahāsurau |
sarwaḥ suhṛjjanastābhyāṃ pramodamupajagmiwān ||27||

tatastau tu jaṭā hitwā maulinau sambabhūwatuḥ |
mahārhābharaṇopetau wirajombaradhāriṇau ||28||

akālakaumudīṃ caiwa cakratuḥ sārwakāmikīm |
daityendrau paramaprītau tayoścaiwa suhṛjjanaḥ ||29||

bhakṣyatāṃ bhujyatāṃ nityaṃ ramyatāṃ gīyatāmiti |
pīyatāṃ dīyatāṃ ceti wāca āsangṛhe gṛhe ||30||

tatra tatra mahāpānairutkṛṣṭatalanāditaiḥ |
hṛṣṭaṃ pramuditaṃ sarwaṃ daityānāmabhawatpuram ||31||

taistairwihārairbahubhirdaityānāṃ kāmarūpiṇām |
samāḥ saṅkrīḍatāṃ teṣāmaharekamiwābhawat ||32||






                  202


nārada uwāca||

utsawe wṛttamātre tu trailokyākāṅkṣiṇāwubhau |
mantrayitwā tataḥ senāṃ tāwājñāpayatāṃ tadā ||1||

suhṛdbhirabhyanujñātau daityawṛddhaiśca mantribhiḥ |
kṛtwā prāsthānikaṃ rātrau maghāsu yayatustadā ||2||

gadāpaṭṭiśadhāriṇyā śūlamudgarahastayā |
prasthitau sahadharmiṇyā mahatyā daityasenayā ||3||

maṅgalaiḥ stutibhiścāpi wijayapratisaṃhitaiḥ |
cāraṇaiḥ stūyamānau tu jagmatuḥ parayā mudā ||4||

tāwantarikṣamutpatya daityau kāmagamāwubhau |
dewānāmewa bhawanaṃ jagmaturyuddhadurmadau ||5||

tayorāgamanaṃ jñātwā waradānaṃ ca tatprabhoḥ |
hitwā triwiṣṭapaṃ jagmurbrahmalokaṃ tataḥ surāḥ ||6||

tāwindralokaṃ nirjitya yakṣarakṣogaṇāṃstathā |
khecarāṇyapi bhūtāni jigyatustīwrawikramau ||7||

antarbhūmigatānnāgāñjitwā tau ca mahāsurau |
samudrawāsinaḥ sarwānmlecchajātīnwijigyatuḥ ||8||

tataḥ sarwāṃ mahīṃ jetumārabdhāwugraśāsanau |
sainikāṃśca samāhūya sutīkṣṇāṃ wācamūcatuḥ ||9||

rājarṣayo mahāyajñairhawyakawyairdwijātayaḥ |
tejo balaṃ ca dewānāṃ wardhayanti śriyaṃ tathā ||10||

teṣāmewaṃ prawṛddhānāṃ sarweṣāmasuradwiṣām |
sambhūya sarwairasmābhiḥ kāryaḥ sarwātmanā wadhaḥ ||11||

ewaṃ sarwānsamādiśya pūrwatīre mahodadheḥ |
krūrāṃ matiṃ samāsthāya jagmatuḥ sarwatomukham ||12||

yajñairyajante ye kecidyājayanti ca ye dwijāḥ |
tānsarwānprasabhaṃ dṛṣṭwā balinau jaghnatustadā ||13||

āśrameṣwagnihotrāṇi ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāwitātmanām |
gṛhītwā prakṣipantyapsu wiśrabdhāḥ sainikāstayoḥ ||14||

tapodhanaiśca ye śāpāḥ kruddhairuktā mahātmabhiḥ |
nākrāmanti tayoste'pi waradānena jṛmbhatoḥ ||15||

nākrāmanti yadā śāpā bāṇā muktāḥ śilāswiwa |
niyamāṃstadā parityajya wyadrawanta dwijātayaḥ ||16||

pṛthiwyāṃ ye tapaḥsiddhā dāntāḥ śamaparāyaṇāḥ |
tayorbhayāddudruwuste wainateyādiworagāḥ ||17||

mathitairāśramairbhagnairwikīrṇakalaśasruwaiḥ |
śūnyamāsījjagatsarwaṃ kālenewa hataṃ yathā ||18||

rājarṣibhiradṛśyadbhirṛṣibhiśca mahāsurau |
ubhau winiścayaṃ kṛtwā wikurwāte wadhaiṣiṇau ||19||

prabhinnakaraṭau mattau bhūtwā kuñjararūpiṇau |
saṃlīnānapi durgeṣu ninyaturyamasādanam ||20||

siṃhau bhūtwā punarwyāghrau punaścāntarhitāwubhau |
taistairupāyaistau krūrāwṛṣīndṛṣṭwā nijaghnatuḥ ||21||

niwṛttayajñaswādhyāyā praṇaṣṭanṛpatidwijā |
utsannotsawayajñā ca babhūwa wasudhā tadā ||22||

hāhābhūtā bhayārtā ca niwṛttawipaṇāpaṇā |
niwṛttadewakāryā ca puṇyodwāhawiwarjitā ||23||

niwṛttakṛṣigorakṣā widhwastanagarāśramā |
asthikaṅkālasaṅkīrṇā bhūrbabhūwogradarśanā ||24||

niwṛttapitṛkāryaṃ ca nirwaṣaṭkāramaṅgalam |
jagatpratibhayākāraṃ duṣprekṣyamabhawattadā ||25||

candrādityau grahāstārā nakṣatrāṇi diwaukasaḥ |
jagmurwiṣādaṃ tatkarma dṛṣṭwā sundopasundayoḥ ||26||

ewaṃ sarwā diśo daityau jitwā krūreṇa karmaṇā |
niḥsapatnau kurukṣetre niweśamabhicakratuḥ ||27||






                  203


nārada uwāca||

tato dewarṣayaḥ sarwe siddhāśca paramarṣayaḥ |
jagmustadā parāmārtiṃ dṛṣṭwā tatkadanaṃ mahat ||1||

te'bhijagmurjitakrodhā jitātmāno jitendriyāḥ |
pitāmahasya bhawanaṃ jagataḥ kṛpayā tadā ||2||

tato dadṛśurāsīnaṃ saha dewaiḥ pitāmaham |
siddhairbrahmarṣibhiścaiwa samantātpariwāritam ||3||

tatra dewo mahādewastatrāgnirwāyunā saha |
candrādityau ca dharmaśca parameṣṭhī tathā budhaḥ ||4||

waikhānasā wālakhilyā wānaprasthā marīcipāḥ |
ajāścaiwāwimūḍhāśca tejogarbhāstapaswinaḥ ||5||

ṛṣayaḥ sarwa ewaite pitāmahamupāsate ||5||

tato'bhigamya sahitāḥ sarwa ewa maharṣayaḥ |
sundopasundayoḥ karma sarwamewa śaśaṃsire ||6||

yathākṛtaṃ yathā caiwa kṛtaṃ yena krameṇa ca |
nyawedayaṃstataḥ sarwamakhilena pitāmahe ||7||

tato dewagaṇāḥ sarwe te caiwa paramarṣayaḥ |
tamewārthaṃ puraskṛtya pitāmahamacodayan ||8||

tataḥ pitāmahaḥ śrutwā sarweṣāṃ tadwacastadā |
muhūrtamiwa sañcintya kartawyasya winiścayam ||9||

tayorwadhaṃ samuddiśya wiśwakarmāṇamāhwayat |
dṛṣṭwā ca wiśwakarmāṇaṃ wyādideśa pitāmahaḥ ||10||

sṛjyatāṃ prārthanīyeha pramadeti mahātapāḥ ||10||

pitāmahaṃ namaskṛtya tadwākyamabhinandya ca |
nirmame yoṣitaṃ diwyāṃ cintayitwā prayatnataḥ ||11||

triṣu lokeṣu yatkiñcidbhūtaṃ sthāwarajaṅgamam |
samānayaddarśanīyaṃ tattadyatnāttatastataḥ ||12||

koṭiśaścāpi ratnāni tasyā gātre nyaweśayat |
tāṃ ratnasaṅghātamayīmasṛjaddewarūpiṇīm ||13||

sā prayatnena mahatā nirmitā wiśwakarmaṇā |
triṣu lokeṣu nārīṇāṃ rūpeṇāpratimābhawat ||14||

na tasyāḥ sūkṣmamapyasti yadgātre rūpasampadā |
na yuktaṃ yatra wā dṛṣṭirna sajjati nirīkṣatām ||15||

sā wigrahawatīwa śrīḥ kāntarūpā wapuṣmatī |
jahāra sarwabhūtānāṃ cakṣūṃṣi ca manāṃsi ca ||16||

tilaṃ tilaṃ samānīya ratnānāṃ yadwinirmitā |
tilottametyatastasyā nāma cakre pitāmahaḥ ||17||

pitāmaha uwāca||

gaccha sundopasundābhyāmasurābhyāṃ tilottame |
prārthanīyena rūpeṇa kuru bhadre pralobhanam ||18||

twatkṛte darśanādewa rūpasampatkṛtena wai |
wirodhaḥ syādyathā tābhyāmanyonyena tathā kuru ||19||

nārada uwāca||

sā tatheti pratijñāya namaskṛtya pitāmaham |
cakāra maṇḍalaṃ tatra wibudhānāṃ pradakṣiṇam ||20||

prāṅmukho bhagawānāste dakṣiṇena maheśwaraḥ |
dewāścaiwottareṇāsansarwatastwṛṣayo'bhawan ||21||

kurwantyā tu tayā tatra maṇḍalaṃ tatpradakṣiṇam |
indraḥ sthāṇuśca bhagawāndhairyeṇa pratyawasthitau ||22||

draṣṭukāmasya cātyarthaṃ gatāyāḥ pārśwatastadā |
anyadañcitapakṣmāntaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ niḥsṛtaṃ mukham ||23||

pṛṣṭhataḥ pariwartantyāḥ paścimaṃ niḥsṛtaṃ mukham |
gatāyāścottaraṃ pārśwamuttaraṃ niḥsṛtaṃ mukham ||24||

mahendrasyāpi netrāṇāṃ pārśwataḥ pṛṣṭhato'grataḥ |
raktāntānāṃ wiśālānāṃ sahasraṃ sarwato'bhawat ||25||

ewaṃ caturmukhaḥ sthāṇurmahādewo'bhawatpurā |
tathā sahasranetraśca babhūwa balasūdanaḥ ||26||

tathā dewanikāyānāmṛṣīṇāṃ caiwa sarwaśaḥ |
mukhānyabhiprawartante yena yāti tilottamā ||27||

tasyā gātre nipatitā teṣāṃ dṛṣṭirmahātmanām |
sarweṣāmewa bhūyiṣṭhamṛte dewaṃ pitāmaham ||28||

gacchantyāstu tadā dewāḥ sarwe ca paramarṣayaḥ |
kṛtamityewa tatkāryaṃ menire rūpasampadā ||29||

tilottamāyāṃ tu tadā gatāyāṃ lokabhāwanaḥ |
sarwānwisarjayāmāsa dewānṛṣigaṇāṃśca tān ||30||






                  204


nārada uwāca||

jitwā tu pṛthiwīṃ daityau niḥsapatnau gatawyathau |
kṛtwā trailokyamawyagraṃ kṛtakṛtyau babhūwatuḥ ||1||

dewagandharwayakṣāṇāṃ nāgapārthiwarakṣasām |
ādāya sarwaratnāni parāṃ tuṣṭimupāgatau ||2||

yadā na pratiṣeddhārastayoḥ santīha kecana |
nirudyogau tadā bhūtwā wijahrāte'marāwiwa ||3||

strībhirmālyaiśca gandhaiśca bhakṣairbhojyaiśca puṣkalaiḥ |
pānaiśca wiwidhairhṛdyaiḥ parāṃ prītimawāpatuḥ ||4||

antaḥpure wanodyāne parwatopawaneṣu ca |
yathepsiteṣu deśeṣu wijahrāte'marāwiwa ||5||

tataḥ kadācidwindhyasya pṛṣṭhe samaśilātale |
puṣpitāgreṣu śāleṣu wihāramabhijagmatuḥ ||6||

diwyeṣu sarwakāmeṣu samānīteṣu tatra tau |
warāsaneṣu saṃhṛṣṭau saha strībhirniṣedatuḥ ||7||

tato wāditranṛttābhyāmupātiṣṭhanta tau striyaḥ |
gītaiśca stutisaṃyuktaiḥ prītyarthamupajagmire ||8||

tatastilottamā tatra wane puṣpāṇi cinwatī |
weṣamākṣiptamādhāya raktenaikena wāsasā ||9||

nadītīreṣu jātānsā karṇikārānwicinwatī |
śanairjagāma taṃ deśaṃ yatrāstāṃ tau mahāsurau ||10||

tau tu pītwā waraṃ pānaṃ madaraktāntalocanau |
dṛṣṭwaiwa tāṃ warārohāṃ wyathitau sambabhūwatuḥ ||11||

tāwutpatyāsanaṃ hitwā jagmaturyatra sā sthitā |
ubhau ca kāmasaṃmattāwubhau prārthayataśca tām ||12||

dakṣiṇe tāṃ kare subhrūṃ sundo jagrāha pāṇinā |
upasundo'pi jagrāha wāme pāṇau tilottamām ||13||

warapradānamattau tāwaurasena balena ca |
dhanaratnamadābhyāṃ ca surāpānamadena ca ||14||

sarwairetairmadairmattāwanyonyaṃ bhrukuṭīkṛtau |
madakāmasamāwiṣṭau parasparamathocatuḥ ||15||

mama bhāryā tawa gururiti sundo'bhyabhāṣata |
mama bhāryā tawa wadhūrupasundo'bhyabhāṣata ||16||

naiṣā tawa mamaiṣeti tatra tau manyurāwiśat |
tasyā hetorgade bhīme tāwubhāwapyagṛhṇatām ||17||

tau pragṛhya gade bhīme tasyāḥ kāmena mohitau |
ahaṃ pūrwamahaṃ pūrwamityanyonyaṃ nijaghnatuḥ ||18||

tau gadābhihatau bhīmau petaturdharaṇītale |
rudhireṇāwaliptāṅgau dwāwiwārkau nabhaścyutau ||19||

tatastā widrutā nāryaḥ sa ca daityagaṇastadā |
pātālamagamatsarwo wiṣādabhayakampitaḥ ||20||

tataḥ pitāmahastatra saha dewairmaharṣibhiḥ |
ājagāma wiśuddhātmā pūjayiṣyaṃstilottamām ||21||

wareṇa chanditā sā tu brahmaṇā prītimewa ha |
warayāmāsa tatraināṃ prītaḥ prāha pitāmahaḥ ||22||

ādityacaritāṃllokānwicariṣyasi bhāmini |
tejasā ca sudṛṣṭāṃ twāṃ na kariṣyati kaścana ||23||

ewaṃ tasyai waraṃ dattwā sarwalokapitāmahaḥ |
indre trailokyamādhāya brahmalokaṃ gataḥ prabhuḥ ||24||

ewaṃ tau sahitau bhūtwā sarwārtheṣwekaniścayau |
tilottamārthe saṅkruddhāwanyonyamabhijaghnatuḥ ||25||

tasmādbrawīmi waḥ snehātsarwānbharatasattamān |
yathā wo nātra bhedaḥ syātsarweṣāṃ draupadīkṛte ||26||

tathā kuruta bhadraṃ wo mama cetpriyamicchatha ||26||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktā mahātmāno nāradena maharṣiṇā |
samayaṃ cakrire rājaṃste'nyonyena samāgatāḥ ||27||

samakṣaṃ tasya dewarṣernāradasyāmitaujasaḥ ||27||

draupadyā naḥ sahāsīnamanyo'nyaṃ yo'bhidarśayet |
sa no dwādaśa warṣāṇi brahmacārī wane waset ||28||

kṛte tu samaye tasminpāṇḍawairdharmacāribhiḥ |
nārado'pyagamatprīta iṣṭaṃ deśaṃ mahāmuniḥ ||29||

ewaṃ taiḥ samayaḥ pūrwaṃ kṛto naradacoditaiḥ |
na cābhidyanta te sārwe tadānyonyena bhārata ||30||






                  205


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ te samayaṃ kṛtwā nyawasaṃstatra pāṇḍawāḥ |
waśe śastrapratāpena kurwanto'nyānmahīkṣitaḥ ||1||

teṣāṃ manujasiṃhānāṃ pañcānāmamitaujasām |
babhūwa kṛṣṇā sarweṣāṃ pārthānāṃ waśawartinī ||2||

te tayā taiśca sā wīraiḥ patibhiḥ saha pañcabhiḥ |
babhūwa paramaprītā nāgairiwa saraswatī ||3||

wartamāneṣu dharmeṇa pāṇḍaweṣu mahātmasu |
wyawardhankurawaḥ sarwe hīnadoṣāḥ sukhānwitāḥ ||4||

atha dīrgheṇa kālena brāhmaṇasya wiśāṃ pate |
kasyacittaskarāḥ kecijjahrurgā nṛpasattama ||5||

hriyamāṇe dhane tasminbrāhmaṇaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ |
āgamya khāṇḍawaprasthamudakrośata pāṇḍawān ||6||

hriyate godhanaṃ kṣudrairnṛśaṃsairakṛtātmabhiḥ |
prasahya wo'smādwiṣayādabhidhāwata pāṇḍawāḥ ||7||

brāhmaṇasya pramattasya hawirdhwāṅkṣairwilupyate |
śārdūlasya guhāṃ śūnyāṃ nīcaḥ kroṣṭābhimarśati ||8||

brāhmaṇaswe hṛte corairdharmārthe ca wilopite |
rorūyamāṇe ca mayi kriyatāmastradhāraṇam ||9||

rorūyamāṇasyābhyāśe tasya wiprasya pāṇḍawaḥ |
tāni wākyāni śuśrāwa kuntīputro dhanañjayaḥ ||10||

śrutwā caiwa mahābāhurmā bhairityāha taṃ dwijam |
āyudhāni ca yatrāsanpāṇḍawānāṃ mahātmanām ||11||

kṛṣṇayā saha tatrāsīddharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||11||

sa praweśāya cāśakto gamanāya ca pāṇḍawaḥ |
tasya cārtasya tairwākyaiścodyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||12||

ākrande tatra kaunteyaścintayāmāsa duḥkhitaḥ ||12||

hriyamāṇe dhane tasminbrāhmaṇasya tapaswinaḥ |
aśrupramārjanaṃ tasya kartawyamiti niścitaḥ ||13||

upaprekṣaṇajo'dharmaḥ sumahānsyānmahīpateḥ |
yadyasya rudato dwāri na karomyadya rakṣaṇam ||14||

anāstikyaṃ ca sarweṣāmasmākamapi rakṣaṇe |
pratitiṣṭheta loke'sminnadharmaścaiwa no bhawet ||15||

anāpṛcchya ca rājānaṃ gate mayi na saṃśayaḥ |
ajātaśatrornṛpatermama caiwāpriyaṃ bhawet ||16||

anupraweśe rājñastu wanawāso bhawenmama |
adharmo wā mahānastu wane wā maraṇaṃ mama ||17||

śarīrasyāpi nāśena dharma ewa wiśiṣyate ||17||

ewaṃ winiścitya tataḥ kuntīputro dhanañjayaḥ |
anuprawiśya rājānamāpṛcchya ca wiśāṃ pate ||18||

dhanurādāya saṃhṛṣṭo brāhmaṇaṃ pratyabhāṣata |
brāhmaṇāgamyatāṃ śīghraṃ yāwatparadhanaiṣiṇaḥ ||19||

na dūre te gatāḥ kṣudrāstāwadgacchāmahe saha |
yāwadāwartayāmyadya corahastāddhanaṃ tawa ||20||

so'nusṛtya mahābāhurdhanwī warmī rathī dhwajī |
śarairwidhwaṃsitāṃścorānawajitya ca taddhanam ||21||

brāhmaṇasya upāhṛtya yaśaḥ pītwā ca pāṇḍawaḥ |
ājagāma puraṃ wīraḥ sawyasācī parantapaḥ ||22||

so'bhiwādya gurūnsarwāṃstaiścāpi pratinanditaḥ |
dharmarājamuwācedaṃ wratamādiśyatāṃ mama ||23||

samayaḥ samatikrānto bhawatsaṃdarśanānmayā |
wanawāsaṃ gamiṣyāmi samayo hyeṣa naḥ kṛtaḥ ||24||

ityukto dharmarājastu sahasā wākyamapriyam |
kathamityabrawīdwācā śokārtaḥ sajjamānayā ||25||

yudhiṣṭhiro guḍākeśaṃ bhrātā bhrātaramacyutam ||25||

pramāṇamasmi yadi te mattaḥ śṛṇu waco'nagha |
anupraweśe yadwīra kṛtawāṃstwaṃ mamāpriyam ||26||

sarwaṃ tadanujānāmi wyalīkaṃ na ca me hṛdi ||26||

guroranupraweśo hi nopaghāto yawīyasaḥ |
yawīyaso'nupraweśo jyeṣṭhasya widhilopakaḥ ||27||

niwartaswa mahābāho kuruṣwa wacanaṃ mama |
na hi te dharmalopo'sti na ca me dharṣaṇā kṛtā ||28||

arjuna uwāca||

na wyājena careddharmamiti me bhawataḥ śrutam |
na satyādwicaliṣyāmi satyenāyudhamālabhe ||29||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

so'bhyanujñāpya rājānaṃ brahmacaryāya dīkṣitaḥ |
wane dwādaśa warṣāṇi wāsāyopajagāma ha ||30||






                  206


waiśampāyana uwāca||

taṃ prayāntaṃ mahābāhuṃ kaurawāṇāṃ yaśaskaram |
anujagmurmahātmāno brāhmaṇā wedapāragāḥ ||1||

wedawedāṅgawidwāṃsastathaiwādhyātmacintakāḥ |
caukṣāśca bhagawadbhaktāḥ sūtāḥ paurāṇikāśca ye ||2||

kathakāścāpare rājañśramaṇāśca wanaukasaḥ |
diwyākhyānāni ye cāpi paṭhanti madhuraṃ dwijāḥ ||3||

etaiścānyaiśca bahubhiḥ sahāyaiḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ |
wṛtaḥ ślakṣṇakathaiḥ prāyānmarudbhiriwa wāsawaḥ ||4||

ramaṇīyāni citrāṇi wanāni ca sarāṃsi ca |
saritaḥ sāgarāṃścaiwa deśānapi ca bhārata ||5||

puṇyāni caiwa tīrthāni dadarśa bharatarṣabha |
sa gaṅgādwāramāsādya niweśamakarotprabhuḥ ||6||

tatra tasyādbhutaṃ karma śṛṇu me janamejaya |
kṛtawānyadwiśuddhātmā pāṇḍūnāṃ prawaro rathī ||7||

niwiṣṭe tatra kaunteye brāhmaṇeṣu ca bhārata |
agnihotrāṇi wiprāste prāduścakruranekaśaḥ ||8||

teṣu prabodhyamāneṣu jwaliteṣu huteṣu ca |
kṛtapuṣpopahāreṣu tīrāntaragateṣu ca ||9||

kṛtābhiṣekairwidwadbhirniyataiḥ satpathi sthitaiḥ |
śuśubhe'tīwa tadrājangaṅgādwāraṃ mahātmabhiḥ ||10||

tathā paryākule tasminniweśe pāṇḍunandanaḥ |
abhiṣekāya kaunteyo gaṅgāmawatatāra ha ||11||

tatrābhiṣekaṃ kṛtwā sa tarpayitwā pitāmahān |
uttitīrṣurjalādrājannagnikāryacikīrṣayā ||12||

apakṛṣṭo mahābāhurnāgarājasya kanyayā |
antarjale mahārāja ulūpyā kāmayānayā ||13||

dadarśa pāṇḍawastatra pāwakaṃ susamāhitam |
kaurawyasyātha nāgasya bhawane paramārcite ||14||

tatrāgnikāryaṃ kṛtawānkuntīputro dhanañjayaḥ |
aśaṅkamānena hutastenātuṣyaddhutāśanaḥ ||15||

agnikāryaṃ sa kṛtwā tu nāgarājasutāṃ tadā |
prahasanniwa kaunteya idaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||16||

kimidaṃ sāhasaṃ bhīru kṛtawatyasi bhāmini |
kaścāyaṃ subhago deśaḥ kā ca twaṃ kasya cātmajā ||17||

ulūpyuwāca||

airāwatakule jātaḥ kaurawyo nāma pannagaḥ |
tasyāsmi duhitā pārtha ulūpī nāma pannagī ||18||

sāhaṃ twāmabhiṣekārthamawatīrṇaṃ samudragām |
dṛṣṭawatyewa kaunteya kandarpeṇāsmi mūrcchitā ||19||

tāṃ māmanaṅgamathitāṃ twatkṛte kurunandana |
ananyāṃ nandayaswādya pradānenātmano rahaḥ ||20||

arjuna uwāca||

brahmacaryamidaṃ bhadre mama dwādaśawārṣikam |
dharmarājena cādiṣṭaṃ nāhamasmi swayaṃwaśaḥ ||21||

tawa cāpi priyaṃ kartumicchāmi jalacāriṇi |
anṛtaṃ noktapūrwaṃ ca mayā kiñcana karhicit ||22||

kathaṃ ca nānṛtaṃ tatsyāttawa cāpi priyaṃ bhawet |
na ca pīḍyeta me dharmastathā kuryāṃ bhujaṅgame ||23||

ulūpyuwāca||

jānāmyahaṃ pāṇḍaweya yathā carasi medinīm |
yathā ca te brahmacaryamidamādiṣṭawānguruḥ ||24||

parasparaṃ wartamānāndrupadasyātmajāṃ prati |
yo no'nuprawiśenmohātsa no dwādaśawārṣikam ||25||

wane caredbrahmacaryamiti waḥ samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ||25||

tadidaṃ draupadīhetoranyonyasya prawāsanam |
kṛtaṃ wastatra dharmārthamatra dharmo na duṣyati ||26||

paritrāṇaṃ ca kartawyamārtānāṃ pṛthulocana |
kṛtwā mama paritrāṇaṃ tawa dharmo na lupyate ||27||

yadi wāpyasya dharmasya sūkṣmo'pi syādwyatikramaḥ |
sa ca te dharma ewa syāddāttwā prāṇānmamārjuna ||28||

bhaktāṃ bhajaswa māṃ pārtha satāmetanmataṃ prabho |
na kariṣyasi cedewaṃ mṛtāṃ māmupadhāraya ||29||

prāṇadānānmahābāho cara dharmamanuttamam |
śaraṇaṃ ca prapannāsmi twāmadya puruṣottama ||30||

dīnānanāthānkaunteya parirakṣasi nityaśaḥ |
sāhaṃ śaraṇamabhyemi rorawīmi ca duḥkhitā ||31||

yāce twāmabhikāmāhaṃ tasmātkuru mama priyam |
sa twamātmapradānena sakāmāṃ kartumarhasi ||32||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastu kaunteyaḥ pannageśwarakanyayā |
kṛtawāṃstattathā sarwaṃ dharmamuddiśya kāraṇam ||33||

sa nāgabhawane rātriṃ tāmuṣitwā pratāpawān |
udite'bhyutthitaḥ sūrye kaurawyasya niweśanāt ||34||






                  207


waiśampāyana uwāca||

kathayitwā tu tatsarwaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sa bhārata |
prayayau himawatpārśwaṃ tato wajradharātmajaḥ ||1||

agastyawaṭamāsādya wasiṣṭhasya ca parwatam |
bhṛgutuṅge ca kaunteyaḥ kṛtawāñśaucamātmanaḥ ||2||

pradadau gosahasrāṇi tīrtheṣwāyataneṣu ca |
niweśāṃśca dwijātibhyaḥ so'dadatkurusattamaḥ ||3||

hiraṇyabindostīrthe ca snātwā puruṣasattamaḥ |
dṛṣṭawānparwataśreṣṭhaṃ puṇyānyāyatanāni ca ||4||

awatīrya naraśreṣṭho brāhmaṇaiḥ saha bhārata |
prācīṃ diśamabhiprepsurjagāma bharatarṣabhaḥ ||5||

ānupūrwyeṇa tīrthāni dṛṣṭawānkurusattamaḥ |
nadīṃ cotpalinīṃ ramyāmaraṇyaṃ naimiṣaṃ prati ||6||

nandāmaparanandāṃ ca kauśikīṃ ca yaśaswinīm |
mahānadīṃ gayāṃ caiwa gaṅgāmapi ca bhārata ||7||

ewaṃ sarwāṇi tīrthāni paśyamānastathāśramān |
ātmanaḥ pāwanaṃ kurwanbrāhmaṇebhyo dadau wasu ||8||

aṅgawaṅgakaliṅgeṣu yāni puṇyāni kānicit |
jagāma tāni sarwāṇi tīrthānyāyatanāni ca ||9||

dṛṣṭwā ca widhiwattāni dhanaṃ cāpi dadau tataḥ ||9||

kaliṅgarāṣṭradwāreṣu brāhmaṇāḥ pāṇḍawānugāḥ |
abhyanujñāya kaunteyamupāwartanta bhārata ||10||

sa tu tairabhyanujñātaḥ kuntīputro dhanañjayaḥ |
sahāyairalpakaiḥ śūraḥ prayayau yena sāgaram ||11||

sa kaliṅgānatikramya deśānāyatanāni ca |
dharmyāṇi ramaṇīyāni prekṣamāṇo yayau prabhuḥ ||12||

mahendraparwataṃ dṛṣṭwā tāpasairupaśobhitam |
samudratīreṇa śanairmaṇalūraṃ jagāma ha ||13||

tatra sarwāṇi tīrthāni puṇyānyāyatanāni ca |
abhigamya mahābāhurabhyagacchanmahīpatim ||14||

maṇalūreśwaraṃ rājandharmajñaṃ citrawāhanam ||14||

tasya citrāṅgadā nāma duhitā cārudarśanā |
tāṃ dadarśa pure tasminwicarantīṃ yadṛcchayā ||15||

dṛṣṭwā ca tāṃ warārohāṃ cakame caitrawāhinīm |
abhigamya ca rājānaṃ jñāpayatswaṃ prayojanam ||16||

tamuwācātha rājā sa sāntwapūrwamidaṃ wacaḥ ||16||

rājā prabhaṅkaro nāma kule asminbabhūwa ha |
aputraḥ prasawenārthī tapastepe sa uttamam ||17||

ugreṇa tapasā tena praṇipātena śaṅkaraḥ |
īśwarastoṣitastena mahādewa umāpatiḥ ||18||

sa tasmai bhagawānprādādekaikaṃ prasawaṃ kule |
ekaikaḥ prasawastasmādbhawatyasminkule sadā ||19||

teṣāṃ kumārāḥ sarweṣāṃ pūrweṣāṃ mama jajñire |
kanyā tu mama jāteyaṃ kulasyotpādanī dhruwam ||20||

putro mameyamiti me bhāwanā puruṣottama |
putrikā hetuwidhinā sañjñitā bharatarṣabha ||21||

etacchulkaṃ bhawatwasyāḥ kulakṛjjāyatāmiha |
etena samayenemāṃ pratigṛhṇīṣwa pāṇḍawa ||22||

sa tatheti pratijñāya kanyāṃ tāṃ pratigṛhya ca |
uwāsa nagare tasminkaunteyastrihimāḥ samāḥ ||23||






                  208


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ samudre tīrthāni dakṣiṇe bharatarṣabhaḥ |
abhyagacchatsupuṇyāni śobhitāni tapaswibhiḥ ||1||

warjayanti sma tīrthāni pañca tatra tu tāpasāḥ |
ācīrṇāni tu yānyāsanpurastāttu tapaswibhiḥ ||2||

agastyatīrthaṃ saubhadraṃ paulomaṃ ca supāwanam |
kārandhamaṃ prasannaṃ ca hayamedhaphalaṃ ca yat ||3||

bhāradwājasya tīrthaṃ ca pāpapraśamanaṃ mahat ||3||

wiwiktānyupalakṣyātha tāni tīrthāni pāṇḍawaḥ |
dṛṣṭwā ca warjyamānāni munibhirdharmabuddhibhiḥ ||4||

tapaswinastato'pṛcchatprājñaliḥ kurunandanaḥ |
tīrthānīmāni warjyante kimarthaṃ brahmawādibhiḥ ||5||

tāpasā ūcuḥ||

grāhāḥ pañca wasantyeṣu haranti ca tapodhanān |
ata etāni warjyante tīrthāni kurunandana ||6||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

teṣāṃ śrutwā mahābāhurwāryamāṇastapodhanaiḥ |
jagāma tāni tīrthāni draṣṭuṃ puruṣasattamaḥ ||7||

tataḥ saubhadramāsādya maharṣestīrthamuttamam |
wigāhya tarasā śūraḥ snānaṃ cakre parantapaḥ ||8||

atha taṃ puruṣawyāghramantarjalacaro mahān |
nijagrāha jale grāhaḥ kuntīputraṃ dhanañjayam ||9||

sa tamādāya kaunteyo wisphurantaṃ jalecaram |
udatiṣṭhanmahābāhurbalena balināṃ waraḥ ||10||

utkṛṣṭa ewa tu grāhaḥ so'rjunena yaśaswinā |
babhūwa nārī kalyāṇī sarwābharaṇabhūṣitā ||11||

dīpyamānā śriyā rājandiwyarūpā manoramā ||11||

tadadbhutaṃ mahaddṛṣṭwā kuntīputro dhanañjayaḥ |
tāṃ striyaṃ paramaprīta idaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||12||

kā wai twamasi kalyāṇi kuto wāsi jalecarī |
kimarthaṃ ca mahatpāpamidaṃ kṛtawatī purā ||13||

nāryuwāca||

apsarāsmi mahābāho dewāraṇyawicāriṇī |
iṣṭā dhanapaternityaṃ wargā nāma mahābala ||14||

mama sakhyaścatasro'nyāḥ sarwāḥ kāmagamāḥ śubhāḥ |
tābhiḥ sārdhaṃ prayātāsmi lokapālaniweśanam ||15||

tataḥ paśyāmahe sarwā brāhmaṇaṃ saṃśitawratam |
rūpawantamadhīyānamekamekāntacāriṇam ||16||

tasya wai tapasā rājaṃstadwanaṃ tejasāwṛtam |
āditya iwa taṃ deśaṃ kṛtsnaṃ sa wyawabhāsayat ||17||

tasya dṛṣṭwā tapastādṛgrūpaṃ cādbhutadarśanam |
awatīrṇāḥ sma taṃ deśaṃ tapowighnacikīrṣayā ||18||

ahaṃ ca saurabheyī ca samīcī budbudā latā |
yaugapadyena taṃ wipramabhyagacchāma bhārata ||19||

gāyantyo wai hasantyaśca lobhayantyaśca taṃ dwijam |
sa ca nāsmāsu kṛtawānmano wīra kathañcana ||20||

nākampata mahātejāḥ sthitastapasi nirmale ||20||

so'śapatkupito'smāṃstu brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyarṣabha |
grāhabhūtā jale yūyaṃ cariṣyadhwaṃ śataṃ samāḥ ||21||






                  209


wargowāca||

tato wayaṃ prawyathitāḥ sarwā bharatasattama |
āyāma śaraṇaṃ wipraṃ taṃ tapodhanamacyutam ||1||

rūpeṇa wayasā caiwa kandarpeṇa ca darpitāḥ |
ayuktaṃ kṛtawatyaḥ sma kṣantumarhasi no dwija ||2||

eṣa ewa wadho'smākaṃ suparyāptastapodhana |
yadwayaṃ saṃśitātmānaṃ pralobdhuṃ twāmihāgatāḥ ||3||

awadhyāstu striyaḥ sṛṣṭā manyante dharmacintakāḥ |
tasmāddharmeṇa dharmajña nāsmānhiṃsitumarhasi ||4||

sarwabhūteṣu dharmajña maitro brāhmaṇa ucyate |
satyo bhawatu kalyāṇa eṣa wādo manīṣiṇām ||5||

śaraṇaṃ ca prapannānāṃ śiṣṭāḥ kurwanti pālanam |
śaraṇaṃ twāṃ prapannāḥ sma tasmāttwaṃ kṣantumarhasi ||6||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastu dharmātmā brāhmaṇaḥ śubhakarmakṛt |
prasādaṃ kṛtawānwīra rawisomasamaprabhaḥ ||7||

brāhmaṇa uwāca||

śataṃ sahasraṃ wiśwaṃ ca sarwamakṣayawācakam |
parimāṇaṃ śataṃ twetannaitadakṣayawācakam ||8||

yadā ca wo grāhabhūtā gṛhṇantīḥ puruṣāñjale |
utkarṣati jalātkaścitsthalaṃ puruṣasattamaḥ ||9||

tadā yūyaṃ punaḥ sarwāḥ swarūpaṃ pratipatsyatha |
anṛtaṃ noktapūrwaṃ me hasatāpi kadācana ||10||

tāni sarwāṇi tīrthāni itaḥ prabhṛti caiwa ha |
nārītīrthāni nāmneha khyātiṃ yāsyanti sarwaśaḥ ||11||

puṇyāni ca bhawiṣyanti pāwanāni manīṣiṇām ||11||

wargowāca||

tato'bhiwādya taṃ wipraṃ kṛtwā caiwa pradakṣiṇam |
acintayāmopasṛtya tasmāddeśātsuduḥkhitāḥ ||12||

kwa nu nāma wayaṃ sarwāḥ kālenālpena taṃ naram |
samāgacchema yo nastadrūpamāpādayetpunaḥ ||13||

tā wayaṃ cintayitwaiwaṃ muhūrtādiwa bhārata |
dṛṣṭawatyo mahābhāgaṃ dewarṣimuta nāradam ||14||

sarwā hṛṣṭāḥ sma taṃ dṛṣṭwā dewarṣimamitadyutim |
abhiwādya ca taṃ pārtha sthitāḥ sma wyathitānanāḥ ||15||

sa no'pṛcchadduḥkhamūlamuktawatyo wayaṃ ca tat |
śrutwā tacca yathāwṛttamidaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||16||

dakṣiṇe sāgarānūpe pañca tīrthāni santi wai |
puṇyāni ramaṇīyāni tāni gacchata māciram ||17||

tatrāśu puruṣawyāghraḥ pāṇḍawo wo dhanañjayaḥ |
mokṣayiṣyati śuddhātmā duḥkhādasmānna saṃśayaḥ ||18||

tasya sarwā wayaṃ wīra śrutwā wākyamihāgatāḥ |
tadidaṃ satyamewādya mokṣitāhaṃ twayānagha ||19||

etāstu mama wai sakhyaścatasro'nyā jale sthitāḥ |
kuru karma śubhaṃ wīra etāḥ sarwā wimokṣaya ||20||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tatastāḥ pāṇḍawaśreṣṭhaḥ sarwā ewa wiśāṃ pate |
tasmācchāpādadīnātmā mokṣayāmāsa wīryawān ||21||

utthāya ca jalāttasmātpratilabhya wapuḥ swakam |
tāstadāpsaraso rājannadṛśyanta yathā purā ||22||

tīrthāni śodhayitwā tu tathānujñāya tāḥ prabhuḥ |
citrāṅgadāṃ punardraṣṭuṃ maṇalūrapuraṃ yayau ||23||

tasyāmajanayatputraṃ rājānaṃ babhruwāhanam |
