taṃ dṛṣṭwā pāṇḍawo rājangokarṇamabhito'gamat ||24||






                  210


waiśampāyana uwāca||

so'parānteṣu tīrthāni puṇyānyāyatanāni ca |
sarwāṇyewānupūrwyeṇa jagāmāmitawikramaḥ ||1||

samudre paścime yāni tīrthānyāyatanāni ca |
tāni sarwāṇi gatwā sa prabhāsamupajagmiwān ||2||

prabhāsadeśaṃ samprāptaṃ bībhatsumaparājitam |
tīrthānyanucarantaṃ ca śuśrāwa madhusūdanaḥ ||3||

tato'bhyagacchatkaunteyamajñāto nāma mādhawaḥ |
dadṛśāte tadānyonyaṃ prabhāse kṛṣṇapāṇḍawau ||4||

tāwanyonyaṃ samāśliṣya pṛṣṭwā ca kuśalaṃ wane |
āstāṃ priyasakhāyau tau naranārāyaṇāwṛṣī ||5||

tato'rjunaṃ wāsudewastāṃ caryāṃ paryapṛcchata |
kimarthaṃ pāṇḍawemāni tīrthānyanucarasyuta ||6||

tato'rjuno yathāwṛttaṃ sarwamākhyātawāṃstadā |
śrutwowāca ca wārṣṇeya ewametaditi prabhuḥ ||7||

tau wihṛtya yathākāmaṃ prabhāse kṛṣṇapāṇḍawau |
mahīdharaṃ raiwatakaṃ wāsāyaiwābhijagmatuḥ ||8||

pūrwamewa tu kṛṣṇasya wacanāttaṃ mahīdharam |
puruṣāḥ samalañcakrurupajahruśca bhojanam ||9||

pratigṛhyārjunaḥ sarwamupabhujya ca pāṇḍawaḥ |
sahaiwa wāsudewena dṛṣṭawānnaṭanartakān ||10||

abhyanujñāpya tānsarwānarcayitwā ca pāṇḍawaḥ |
satkṛtaṃ śayanaṃ diwyamabhyagacchanmahādyutiḥ ||11||

tīrthānāṃ darśanaṃ caiwa parwatānāṃ ca bhārata |
āpagānāṃ wanānāṃ ca kathayāmāsa sātwate ||12||

sa kathāḥ kathayannewa nidrayā janamejaya |
kaunteyo'pahṛtastasmiñśayane swargasaṃmite ||13||

madhureṇa sa gītena wīṇāśabdena cānagha |
prabodhyamāno bubudhe stutibhirmaṅgalaistathā ||14||

sa kṛtwāwaśyakāryāṇi wārṣṇeyenābhinanditaḥ |
rathena kāñcanāṅgena dwārakāmabhijagmiwān ||15||

alaṅkṛtā dwārakā tu babhūwa janamejaya |
kuntīsutasya pūjārthamapi niṣkuṭakeṣwapi ||16||

didṛkṣawaśca kaunteyaṃ dwārakāwāsino janāḥ |
narendramārgamājagmustūrṇaṃ śatasahasraśaḥ ||17||

awalokeṣu nārīṇāṃ sahasrāṇi śatāni ca |
bhojawṛṣṇyandhakānāṃ ca samawāyo mahānabhūt ||18||

sa tathā satkṛtaḥ sarwairbhojawṛṣṇyandhakātmajaiḥ |
abhiwādyābhiwādyāṃśca sarwaiśca pratinanditaḥ ||19||

kumāraiḥ sarwaśo wīraḥ satkāreṇābhiwāditaḥ |
samānawayasaḥ sarwānāśliṣya sa punaḥ punaḥ ||20||

kṛṣṇasya bhawane ramye ratnabhojyasamāwṛte |
uwāsa saha kṛṣṇena bahulāstatra śarwarīḥ ||21||






              subhadrāharaṇaparwa
                  211


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ katipayāhasya tasminraiwatake girau |
wṛṣṇyandhakānāmabhawatsumahānutsawo nṛpa ||1||

tatra dānaṃ dadurwīrā brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraśaḥ |
bhojawṛṣṇyandhakāścaiwa mahe tasya girestadā ||2||

prāsādai ratnacitraiśca girestasya samantataḥ |
sa deśaḥ śobhito rājandīpawṛkṣaiśca sarwaśaḥ ||3||

wāditrāṇi ca tatra sma wādakāḥ samawādayan |
nanṛturnartakāścaiwa jagurgānāni gāyanāḥ ||4||

alaṅkṛtāḥ kumārāśca wṛṣṇīnāṃ sumahaujasaḥ |
yānairhāṭakacitrāṅgaiścañcūryante sma sarwaśaḥ ||5||

paurāśca pādacāreṇa yānairuccāwacaistathā |
sadārāḥ sānuyātrāśca śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ||6||

tato haladharaḥ kṣībo rewatīsahitaḥ prabhuḥ |
anugamyamāno gandharwairacarattatra bhārata ||7||

tathaiwa rājā wṛṣṇīnāmugrasenaḥ pratāpawān |
upagīyamāno gandharwaiḥ strīsahasrasahāyawān ||8||

raukmiṇeyaśca sāmbaśca kṣībau samaradurmadau |
diwyamālyāmbaradharau wijahrāte'marāwiwa ||9||

akrūraḥ sāraṇaścaiwa gado bhānurwiḍūrathaḥ |
niśaṭhaścārudeṣṇaśca pṛthurwipṛthurewa ca ||10||

satyakaḥ sātyakiścaiwa bhaṅgakārasahācarau |
hārdikyaḥ kṛtawarmā ca ye cānye nānukīrtitāḥ ||11||

ete pariwṛtāḥ strībhirgandharwaiśca pṛthakpṛthak |
tamutsawaṃ raiwatake śobhayāṃ cakrire tadā ||12||

tadā kolāhale tasminwartamāne mahāśubhe |
wāsudewaśca pārthaśca sahitau parijagmatuḥ ||13||

tatra caṅkramyamāṇau tau wāsudewasutāṃ śubhām |
alaṅkṛtāṃ sakhīmadhye bhadrāṃ dadṛśatustadā ||14||

dṛṣṭwaiwa tāmarjunasya kandarpaḥ samajāyata |
taṃ tathaikāgramanasaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pārthamalakṣayat ||15||

athābrawītpuṣkarākṣaḥ prahasanniwa bhārata |
wanecarasya kimidaṃ kāmenāloḍyate manaḥ ||16||

mamaiṣā bhaginī pārtha sāraṇasya sahodarā |
yadi te wartate buddhirwakṣyāmi pitaraṃ swayam ||17||

arjuna uwāca||

duhitā wasudewasya wāsudewasya ca swasā |
rūpeṇa caiwa sampannā kamiwaiṣā na mohayet ||18||

kṛtamewa tu kalyāṇaṃ sarwaṃ mama bhaweddhruwam |
yadi syānmama wārṣṇeyī mahiṣīyaṃ swasā tawa ||19||

prāptau tu ka upāyaḥ syāttadbrawīhi janārdana |
āsthāsyāmi tathā sarwaṃ yadi śakyaṃ nareṇa tat ||20||

wāsudewa uwāca||

swayaṃwaraḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ wiwāhaḥ puruṣarṣabha |
sa ca saṃśayitaḥ pārtha swabhāwasyānimittataḥ ||21||

prasahya haraṇaṃ cāpi kṣatriyāṇāṃ praśasyate |
wiwāhahetoḥ śūrāṇāmiti dharmawido widuḥ ||22||

sa twamarjuna kalyāṇīṃ prasahya bhaginīṃ mama |
hara swayaṃware hyasyāḥ ko wai weda cikīrṣitam ||23||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tato'rjunaśca kṛṣṇaśca winiścityetikṛtyatām |
śīghragānpuruṣānrājanpreṣayāmāsatustadā ||24||

dharmarājāya tatsarwamindraprasthagatāya wai |
śrutwaiwa ca mahābāhuranujajñe sa pāṇḍawaḥ ||25||






                  212


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ saṃwādite tasminnanujñāto dhanañjayaḥ |
gatāṃ raiwatake kanyāṃ widitwā janamejaya ||1||

wāsudewābhyanujñātaḥ kathayitwetikṛtyatām |
kṛṣṇasya matamājñāya prayayau bharatarṣabhaḥ ||2||

rathena kāñcanāṅgena kalpitena yathāwidhi |
sainyasugrīwayuktena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā ||3||

sarwaśastropapannena jīmūtarawanādinā |
jwalitāgniprakāśena dwiṣatāṃ harṣaghātinā ||4||

saṃnaddhaḥ kawacī khaḍgī baddhagodhāṅgulitrawān |
mṛgayāwyapadeśena yaugapadyena bhārata ||5||

subhadrā twatha śailendramabhyarcya saha raiwatam |
daiwatāni ca sarwāṇi brāhmaṇānswasti wācya ca ||6||

pradakṣiṇaṃ giriṃ kṛtwā prayayau dwārakāṃ prati |
tāmabhidrutya kaunteyaḥ prasahyāropayadratham ||7||

tataḥ sa puruṣawyāghrastāmādāya śucismitām |
rathenākāśagenaiwa prayayau swapuraṃ prati ||8||

hriyamāṇāṃ tu tāṃ dṛṣṭwā subhadrāṃ sainiko janaḥ |
wikrośanprādrawatsarwo dwārakāmabhitaḥ purīm ||9||

te samāsādya sahitāḥ sudharmāmabhitaḥ sabhām |
sabhāpālasya tatsarwamācakhyuḥ pārthawikramam ||10||

teṣāṃ śrutwā sabhāpālo bherīṃ sāṃnāhikīṃ tataḥ |
samājaghne mahāghoṣāṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtām ||11||

kṣubdhāstenātha śabdena bhojawṛṣṇyandhakāstadā |
annapānamapāsyātha samāpetuḥ sabhāṃ tataḥ ||12||

tato jāmbūnadāṅgāni spardhyāstaraṇawanti ca |
maṇiwidrumacitrāṇi jwalitāgniprabhāṇi ca ||13||

bhejire puruṣawyāghrā wṛṣṇyandhakamahārathāḥ |
siṃhāsanāni śataśo dhiṣṇyānīwa hutāśanāḥ ||14||

teṣāṃ samupawiṣṭānāṃ dewānāmiwa saṃnaye |
ācakhyau ceṣṭitaṃ jiṣṇoḥ sabhāpālaḥ sahānugaḥ ||15||

tacchrutwā wṛṣṇiwīrāste madaraktāntalocanāḥ |
amṛṣyamāṇāḥ pārthasya samutpeturahaṅkṛtāḥ ||16||

yojayadhwaṃ rathānāśu prāsānāharateti ca |
dhanūṃṣi ca mahārhāṇi kawacāni bṛhanti ca ||17||

sūtānuccukruśuḥ keccidrathānyojayateti ca |
swayaṃ ca turagānkecinninyurhemawibhūṣitān ||18||

ratheṣwānīyamāneṣu kawaceṣu dhwajeṣu ca |
abhikrande nṛwīrāṇāṃ tadāsītsaṅkulaṃ mahat ||19||

wanamālī tataḥ kṣībaḥ kailāsaśikharopamaḥ |
nīlawāsā madotsikta idaṃ wacanamabrawīt ||20||

kimidaṃ kuruthāprajñāstūṣṇīṃ bhūte janārdane |
asya bhāwamawijñāya saṅkruddhā moghagarjitāḥ ||21||

eṣa tāwadabhiprāyamākhyātu swaṃ mahāmatiḥ |
yadasya rucitaṃ kartuṃ tatkurudhwamatandritāḥ ||22||

tataste tadwacaḥ śrutwā grāhyarūpaṃ halāyudhāt |
tūṣṇīṃ bhūtāstataḥ sarwe sādhu sādhwiti cābruwan ||23||

samaṃ waco niśamyeti baladewasya dhīmataḥ |
punarewa sabhāmadhye sarwe tu samupāwiśan ||24||

tato'brawītkāmapālo wāsudewaṃ parantapam |
kimawāgupawiṣṭo'si prekṣamāṇo janārdana ||25||

satkṛtastwatkṛte pārthaḥ sarwairasmābhiracyuta |
na ca so'rhati tāṃ pūjāṃ durbuddhiḥ kulapāṃsanaḥ ||26||

ko hi tatraiwa bhuktwānnaṃ bhājanaṃ bhettumarhati |
manyamānaḥ kule jātamātmānaṃ puruṣaḥ kwacit ||27||

īpsamānaśca sambandhaṃ kṛtapūrwaṃ ca mānayan |
ko hi nāma bhawenārthī sāhasena samācaret ||28||

so'wamanya ca nāmāsmānanādṛtya ca keśawam |
prasahya hṛtawānadya subhadrāṃ mṛtyumātmanaḥ ||29||

kathaṃ hi śiraso madhye padaṃ tena kṛtaṃ mama |
marṣayiṣyāmi gowinda pādasparśamiworagaḥ ||30||

adya niṣkaurawāmekaḥ kariṣyāmi wasundharām |
na hi me marṣaṇīyo'yamarjunasya wyatikramaḥ ||31||

taṃ tathā garjamānaṃ tu meghadundubhiniḥswanam |
anwapadyanta te sarwe bhojawṛṣṇyandhakāstadā ||32||






              haraṇahārikaparwa
                  213


waiśampāyana uwāca||

uktawanto yadā wākyamasakṛtsarwawṛṣṇayaḥ |
tato'brawīdwāsudewo wākyaṃ dharmārthasaṃhitam ||1||

nāwamānaṃ kulasyāsya guḍākeśaḥ prayuktawān |
saṃmāno'bhyadhikastena prayukto'yamasaṃśayam ||2||

arthalubdhānna waḥ pārtho manyate sātwatānsadā |
swayaṃwaramanādhṛṣyaṃ manyate cāpi pāṇḍawaḥ ||3||

pradānamapi kanyāyāḥ paśuwatko'numaṃsyate |
wikrayaṃ cāpyapatyasya kaḥ kuryātpuruṣo bhuwi ||4||

etāndoṣāṃśca kaunteyo dṛṣṭawāniti me matiḥ |
ataḥ prasahya hṛtawānkanyāṃ dharmeṇa pāṇḍawaḥ ||5||

ucitaścaiwa sambandhaḥ subhadrā ca yaśaswinī |
eṣa cāpīdṛśaḥ pārthaḥ prasahya hṛtawāniti ||6||

bharatasyānwaye jātaṃ śantanośca mahātmanaḥ |
kuntibhojātmajāputraṃ ko bubhūṣeta nārjunam ||7||

na ca paśyāmi yaḥ pārthaṃ wikrameṇa parājayet |
api sarweṣu lokeṣu sendrarudreṣu māriṣa ||8||

sa ca nāma rathastādṛṅmadīyāste ca wājinaḥ |
yoddhā pārthaśca śīghrāstraḥ ko nu tena samo bhawet ||9||

tamanudrutya sāntwena parameṇa dhanañjayam |
niwartayadhwaṃ saṃhṛṣṭā mamaiṣā paramā matiḥ ||10||

yadi nirjitya waḥ pārtho balādgacchetswakaṃ puram |
praṇaśyedwo yaśaḥ sadyo na tu sāntwe parājayaḥ ||11||

tacchrutwā wāsudewasya tathā cakrurjanādhipa |
niwṛttaścārjunastatra wiwāhaṃ kṛtawāṃstataḥ ||12||

uṣitwā tatra kaunteyaḥ saṃwatsaraparāḥ kṣapāḥ |
puṣkareṣu tataḥ śiṣṭaṃ kālaṃ wartitawānprabhuḥ ||13||

pūrṇe tu dwādaśe warṣe khāṇḍawaprasthamāwiśat ||13||

abhigamya sa rājānaṃ winayena samāhitaḥ |
abhyarcya brāhmaṇānpārtho draupadīmabhijagmiwān ||14||

taṃ draupadī pratyuwāca praṇayātkurunandanam |
tatraiwa gaccha kaunteya yatra sā sātwatātmajā ||15||

subaddhasyāpi bhārasya pūrwabandhaḥ ślathāyate ||15||

tathā bahuwidhaṃ kṛṣṇāṃ wilapantīṃ dhanañjayaḥ |
sāntwayāmāsa bhūyaśca kṣamayāmāsa cāsakṛt ||16||

subhadrāṃ twaramāṇaśca raktakauśeyawāsasam |
pārthaḥ prasthāpayāmāsa kṛtwā gopālikāwapuḥ ||17||

sādhikaṃ tena rūpeṇa śobhamānā yaśaswinī |
bhawanaṃ śreṣṭhamāsādya wīrapatnī warāṅganā ||18||

wawande pṛthutāmrākṣī pṛthāṃ bhadrā yaśaswinī ||18||

tato'bhigamya twaritā pūrṇendusadṛśānanā |
wawande draupadīṃ bhadrā preṣyāhamiti cābrawīt ||19||

pratyutthāya ca tāṃ kṛṣṇā swasāraṃ mādhawasya tām |
saswaje cāwadatprītā niḥsapatno'stu te patiḥ ||20||

tathaiwa muditā bhadrā tāmuwācaiwamastwiti ||20||

tataste hṛṣṭamanasaḥ pāṇḍaweyā mahārathāḥ |
kuntī ca paramaprītā babhūwa janamejaya ||21||

śrutwā tu puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ samprāptaṃ swapurottamam |
arjunaṃ pāṇḍawaśreṣṭhamindraprasthagataṃ tadā ||22||

ājagāma wiśuddhātmā saha rāmeṇa keśawaḥ |
wṛṣṇyandhakamahāmātraiḥ saha wīrairmahārathaiḥ ||23||

bhrātṛbhiśca kumāraiśca yodhaiśca śataśo wṛtaḥ |
sainyena mahatā śaurirabhiguptaḥ parantapaḥ ||24||

tatra dānapatirdhīmānājagāma mahāyaśāḥ |
akrūro wṛṣṇiwīrāṇāṃ senāpatirariṃdamaḥ ||25||

anādhṛṣṭirmahātejā uddhawaśca mahāyaśāḥ |
sākṣādbṛhaspateḥ śiṣyo mahābuddhirmahāyaśāḥ ||26||

satyakaḥ sātyakiścaiwa kṛtawarmā ca sātwataḥ |
pradyumnaścaiwa sāmbaśca niśaṭhaḥ śaṅkurewa ca ||27||

cārudeṣṇaśca wikrānto jhillī wipṛthurewa ca |
sāraṇaśca mahābāhurgadaśca widuṣāṃ waraḥ ||28||

ete cānye ca bahawo wṛṣṇibhojāndhakāstathā |
ājagmuḥ khāṇḍawaprasthamādāya haraṇaṃ bahu ||29||

tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā śrutwā mādhawamāgatam |
pratigrahārthaṃ kṛṣṇasya yamau prāsthāpayattadā ||30||

tābhyāṃ pratigṛhītaṃ tadwṛṣṇicakraṃ samṛddhimat |
wiweśa khāṇḍawaprasthaṃ patākādhwajaśobhitam ||31||

siktasaṃmṛṣṭapanthānaṃ puṣpaprakaraśobhitam |
candanasya rasaiḥ śītaiḥ puṇyagandhairniṣewitam ||32||

dahyatāguruṇā caiwa deśe deśe sugandhinā |
susaṃmṛṣṭajanākīrṇaṃ waṇigbhirupaśobhitam ||33||

pratipede mahābāhuḥ saha rāmeṇa keśawaḥ |
wṛṣṇyandhakamahābhojaiḥ saṃwṛtaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ||34||

sampūjyamānaḥ pauraiśca brāhmaṇaiśca sahasraśaḥ |
wiweśa bhawanaṃ rājñaḥ puraṃdaragṛhopamam ||35||

yudhiṣṭhirastu rāmeṇa samāgacchadyathāwidhi |
mūrdhni keśawamāghrāya paryaṣwajata bāhunā ||36||

taṃ prīyamāṇaṃ kṛṣṇastu winayenābhyapūjayat |
bhīmaṃ ca puruṣawyāghraṃ widhiwatpratyapūjayat ||37||

tāṃśca wṛṣṇyandhakaśreṣṭhāndharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
pratijagrāha satkārairyathāwidhi yathopagam ||38||

guruwatpūjayāmāsa kāṃścitkāṃścidwayasyawat |
kāṃścidabhyawadatpremṇā kaiścidapyabhiwāditaḥ ||39||

tato dadau wāsudewo janyārthe dhanamuttamam |
haraṇaṃ wai subhadrāyā jñātideyaṃ mahāyaśāḥ ||40||

rathānāṃ kāñcanāṅgānāṃ kiṅkiṇījālamālinām |
caturyujāmupetānāṃ sūtaiḥ kuśalasaṃmataiḥ ||41||

sahasraṃ pradadau kṛṣṇo gawāmayutamewa ca ||41||

śrīmānmāthuradeśyānāṃ dogdhrīṇāṃ puṇyawarcasām |
waḍawānāṃ ca śubhrāṇāṃ candrāṃśusamawarcasām ||42||

dadau janārdanaḥ prītyā sahasraṃ hemabhūṣaṇam ||42||

tathaiwāśwatarīṇāṃ ca dāntānāṃ wātaraṃhasām |
śatānyañjanakeśīnāṃ śwetānāṃ pañca pañca ca ||43||

snāpanotsādane caiwa suyuktaṃ wayasānwitam |
strīṇāṃ sahasraṃ gaurīṇāṃ suweṣāṇāṃ suwarcasām ||44||

suwarṇaśatakaṇṭhīnāmarogāṇāṃ suwāsasām |
paricaryāsu dakṣāṇāṃ pradadau puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ ||45||

kṛtākṛtasya mukhyasya kanakasyāgniwarcasaḥ |
manuṣyabhārāndāśārho dadau daśa janārdanaḥ ||46||

gajānāṃ tu prabhinnānāṃ tridhā prasrawatāṃ madam |
girikūṭanikāśānāṃ samareṣwaniwartinām ||47||

kḷptānāṃ paṭughaṇṭānāṃ warāṇāṃ hemamālinām |
hastyārohairupetānāṃ sahasraṃ sāhasapriyaḥ ||48||

rāmaḥ pādagrāhaṇikaṃ dadau pārthāya lāṅgalī |
prīyamāṇo haladharaḥ sambandhaprītimāwahan ||49||

sa mahādhanaratnaugho wastrakambalaphenawān |
mahāgajamahāgrāhaḥ patākāśaiwalākulaḥ ||50||

pāṇḍusāgaramāwiddhaḥ prawiweśa mahānadaḥ |
pūrṇamāpūrayaṃsteṣāṃ dwiṣacchokāwaho'bhawat ||51||

pratijagrāha tatsarwaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
pūjayāmāsa tāṃścaiwa wṛṣṇyandhakamahārathān ||52||

te sametā mahātmānaḥ kuruwṛṣṇyandhakottamāḥ |
wijahruramarāwāse narāḥ sukṛtino yathā ||53||

tatra tatra mahāpānairutkṛṣṭatalanāditaiḥ |
yathāyogaṃ yathāprīti wijahruḥ kuruwṛṣṇayaḥ ||54||

ewamuttamawīryāste wihṛtya diwasānbahūn |
pūjitāḥ kurubhirjagmuḥ punardwārawatīṃ purīm ||55||

rāmaṃ puraskṛtya yayurwṛṣṇyandhakamahārathāḥ |
ratnānyādāya śubhrāṇi dattāni kurusattamaiḥ ||56||

wāsudewastu pārthena tatraiwa saha bhārata |
uwāsa nagare ramye śakraprasthe mahāmanāḥ ||57||

wyacaradyamunākūle pārthena saha bhārata ||57||

tataḥ subhadrā saubhadraṃ keśawasya priyā swasā |
jayantamiwa paulomī dyutimantamajījanat ||58||

dīrghabāhuṃ mahāsattwamṛṣabhākṣamariṃdamam |
subhadrā suṣuwe wīramabhimanyuṃ nararṣabham ||59||

abhīśca manyumāṃścaiwa tatastamarimardanam |
abhimanyumiti prāhurārjuniṃ puruṣarṣabham ||60||

sa sātwatyāmatirathaḥ sambabhūwa dhanañjayāt |
makhe nirmathyamānādwā śamīgarbhāddhutāśanaḥ ||61||

yasmiñjāte mahābāhuḥ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ |
ayutaṃ gā dwijātibhyaḥ prādānniṣkāṃśca tāwataḥ ||62||

dayito wāsudewasya bālyātprabhṛti cābhawat |
pitṛṇāṃ caiwa sarweṣāṃ prajānāmiwa candramāḥ ||63||

janmaprabhṛti kṛṣṇaśca cakre tasya kriyāḥ śubhāḥ |
sa cāpi wawṛdhe bālaḥ śuklapakṣe yathā śaśī ||64||

catuṣpādaṃ daśawidhaṃ dhanurwedamariṃdamaḥ |
arjunādweda wedajñātsakalaṃ diwyamānuṣam ||65||

wijñāneṣwapi cāstrāṇāṃ sauṣṭhawe ca mahābalaḥ |
kriyāswapi ca sarwāsu wiśeṣānabhyaśikṣayat ||66||

āgame ca prayoge ca cakre tulyamiwātmanaḥ |
tutoṣa putraṃ saubhadraṃ prekṣamāṇo dhanañjayaḥ ||67||

sarwasaṃhananopetaṃ sarwalakṣaṇalakṣitam |
durdharṣamṛṣabhaskandhaṃ wyāttānanamiworagam ||68||

siṃhadarpaṃ maheṣwāsaṃ mattamātaṅgawikramam |
meghadundubhinirghoṣaṃ pūrṇacandranibhānanam ||69||

kṛṣṇasya sadṛśaṃ śaurye wīrye rūpe tathākṛtau |
dadarśa putraṃ bībhatsurmaghawāniwa taṃ yathā ||70||

pāñcālyapi ca pañcabhyaḥ patibhyaḥ śubhalakṣaṇā |
lebhe pañca sutānwīrāñśubhānpañcācalāniwa ||71||

yudhiṣṭhirātpratiwindhyaṃ sutasomaṃ wṛkodarāt |
arjunācchrutakarmāṇaṃ śatānīkaṃ ca nākulim ||72||

sahadewācchrutasenametānpañca mahārathān |
pāñcālī suṣuwe wīrānādityānaditiryathā ||73||

śāstrataḥ pratiwindhyaṃ tamūcurwiprā yudhiṣṭhiram |
parapraharaṇajñāne pratiwindhyo bhawatwayam ||74||

sute somasahasre tu somārkasamatejasam |
sutasomaṃ maheṣwāsaṃ suṣuwe bhīmasenataḥ ||75||

śrutaṃ karma mahatkṛtwā niwṛttena kirīṭinā |
jātaḥ putrastawetyewaṃ śrutakarmā tato'bhawat ||76||

śatānīkasya rājarṣeḥ kaurawyaḥ kurunandanaḥ |
cakre putraṃ sanāmānaṃ nakulaḥ kīrtiwardhanam ||77||

tatastwajījanatkṛṣṇā nakṣatre wahnidaiwate |
sahadewātsutaṃ tasmācchrutaseneti taṃ widuḥ ||78||

ekawarṣāntarāstwewa draupadeyā yaśaswinaḥ |
anwajāyanta rājendra parasparahite ratāḥ ||79||

jātakarmāṇyānupūrwyāccūḍopanayanāni ca |
cakāra widhiwaddhaumyasteṣāṃ bharatasattama ||80||

kṛtwā ca wedādhyayanaṃ tataḥ sucaritawratāḥ |
jagṛhuḥ sarwamiṣwastramarjunāddiwyamānuṣam ||81||

dewagarbhopamaiḥ putrairwyūḍhoraskairmahābalaiḥ |
anwitā rājaśārdūla pāṇḍawā mudamāpnuwan ||82||






              khāṇḍawadāhaparwa
                  214


waiśampāyana uwāca||

indraprasthe wasantaste jaghnuranyānnarādhipān |
śāsanāddhṛtarāṣṭrasya rājñaḥ śāntanawasya ca ||1||

āśritya dharmarājānaṃ sarwaloko'wasatsukham |
puṇyalakṣaṇakarmāṇaṃ swadehamiwa dehinaḥ ||2||

sa samaṃ dharmakāmārthānsiṣewe bharatarṣabhaḥ |
trīniwātmasamānbandhūnbandhumāniwa mānayan ||3||

teṣāṃ samawibhaktānāṃ kṣitau dehawatāmiwa |
babhau dharmārthakāmānāṃ caturtha iwa pārthiwaḥ ||4||

adhyetāraṃ paraṃ wedāḥ prayoktāraṃ mahādhwarāḥ |
rakṣitāraṃ śubhaṃ warṇā lebhire taṃ janādhipam ||5||

adhiṣṭhānawatī lakṣmīḥ parāyaṇawatī matiḥ |
bandhumānakhilo dharmastenāsītpṛthiwīkṣitā ||6||

bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito rājā caturbhiradhikaṃ babhau |
prayujyamānairwitato wedairiwa mahādhwaraḥ ||7||

taṃ tu dhaumyādayo wiprāḥ pariwāryopatasthire |
bṛhaspatisamā mukhyāḥ prajāpatimiwāmarāḥ ||8||

dharmarāje atiprītyā pūrṇacandra iwāmale |
prajānāṃ remire tulyaṃ netrāṇi hṛdayāni ca ||9||

na tu kewaladaiwena prajā bhāwena remire |
yadbabhūwa manaḥkāntaṃ karmaṇā sa cakāra tat ||10||

na hyayuktaṃ na cāsatyaṃ nānṛtaṃ na ca wipriyam |
bhāṣitaṃ cārubhāṣasya jajñe pārthasya dhīmataḥ ||11||

sa hi sarwasya lokasya hitamātmana ewa ca |
cikīrṣuḥ sumahātejā reme bharatasattamaḥ ||12||

tathā tu muditāḥ sarwe pāṇḍawā wigatajwarāḥ |
awasanpṛthiwīpālāṃstrāsayantaḥ swatejasā ||13||

tataḥ katipayāhasya bībhatsuḥ kṛṣṇamabrawīt |
uṣṇāni kṛṣṇa wartante gacchāmo yamunāṃ prati ||14||

suhṛjjanawṛtāstatra wihṛtya madhusūdana |
sāyāhne punareṣyāmo rocatāṃ te janārdana ||15||

wāsudewa uwāca||

kuntīmātarmamāpyetadrocate yadwayaṃ jale |
suhṛjjanawṛtāḥ pārtha wiharema yathāsukham ||16||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

āmantrya dharmarājānamanujñāpya ca bhārata |
jagmatuḥ pārthagowindau suhṛjjanawṛtau tataḥ ||17||

wihāradeśaṃ samprāpya nānādrumawaduttamam |
gṛhairuccāwacairyuktaṃ puraṃdaragṛhopamam ||18||

bhakṣyairbhojyaiśca peyaiśca rasawadbhirmahādhanaiḥ |
mālyaiśca wiwidhairyuktaṃ yuktaṃ wārṣṇeyapārthayoḥ ||19||

āwiweśaturāpūrṇaṃ ratnairuccāwacaiḥ śubhaiḥ |
yathopajoṣaṃ sarwaśca janaścikrīḍa bhārata ||20||

wane kāścijjale kāścitkāścidweśmasu cāṅganāḥ |
yathādeśaṃ yathāprīti cikrīḍuḥ kṛṣṇapārthayoḥ ||21||

draupadī ca subhadrā ca wāsāṃsyābharaṇāni ca |
prayacchetāṃ mahārhāṇi strīṇāṃ te sma madotkaṭe ||22||

kāścitprahṛṣṭā nanṛtuścukruśuśca tathāparāḥ |
jahasuścāparā nāryaḥ papuścānyā warāsawam ||23||

ruruduścāparāstatra prajaghnuśca parasparam |
mantrayāmāsuranyāśca rahasyāni parasparam ||24||

weṇuwīṇāmṛdaṅgānāṃ manojñānāṃ ca sarwaśaḥ |
śabdenāpūryate ha sma tadwanaṃ susamṛddhimat ||25||

tasmiṃstathā wartamāne kurudāśārhanandanau |
samīpe jagmatuḥ kañciduddeśaṃ sumanoharam ||26||

tatra gatwā mahātmānau kṛṣṇau parapurañjayau |
mahārhāsanayo rājaṃstatastau saṃniṣīdatuḥ ||27||

tatra pūrwawyatītāni wikrāntāni ratāni ca |
bahūni kathayitwā tau remāte pārthamādhawau ||28||

tatropawiṣṭau muditau nākapṛṣṭhe'śwināwiwa |
abhyagacchattadā wipro wāsudewadhanañjayau ||29||

bṛhacchālapratīkāśaḥ prataptakanakaprabhaḥ |
haripiṅgo hariśmaśruḥ pramāṇāyāmataḥ samaḥ ||30||

taruṇādityasaṅkāśaḥ kṛṣṇawāsā jaṭādharaḥ |
padmapatrānanaḥ piṅgastejasā prajwalanniwa ||31||

upasṛṣṭaṃ tu taṃ kṛṣṇau bhrājamānaṃ dwijottamam |
arjuno wāsudewaśca tūrṇamutpatya tasthatuḥ ||32||






                  215


waiśampāyana uwāca||

so'brawīdarjunaṃ caiwa wāsudewaṃ ca sātwatam |
lokaprawīrau tiṣṭhantau khāṇḍawasya samīpataḥ ||1||

brāhmaṇo bahubhoktāsmi bhuñje'parimitaṃ sadā |
bhikṣe wārṣṇeyapārthau wāmekāṃ tṛptiṃ prayacchatām ||2||

ewamuktau tamabrūtāṃ tatastau kṛṣṇapāṇḍawau |
kenānnena bhawāṃstṛpyettasyānnasya yatāwahe ||3||

ewamuktaḥ sa bhagawānabrawīttāwubhau tataḥ |
bhāṣamāṇau tadā wīrau kimannaṃ kriyatāmiti ||4||

nāhamannaṃ bubhukṣe wai pāwakaṃ māṃ nibodhatam |
yadannamanurūpaṃ me tadyuwāṃ samprayacchatam ||5||

idamindraḥ sadā dāwaṃ khāṇḍawaṃ parirakṣati |
taṃ na śaknomyahaṃ dagdhuṃ rakṣyamāṇaṃ mahātmanā ||6||

wasatyatra sakhā tasya takṣakaḥ pannagaḥ sadā |
sagaṇastatkṛte dāwaṃ parirakṣati wajrabhṛt ||7||

tatra bhūtānyanekāni rakṣyante sma prasaṅgataḥ |
taṃ didhakṣurna śaknomi dagdhuṃ śakrasya tejasā ||8||

sa māṃ prajwalitaṃ dṛṣṭwā meghāmbhobhiḥ prawarṣati |
tato dagdhuṃ na śaknomi didhakṣurdāwamīpsitam ||9||

sa yuwābhyāṃ sahāyābhyāmastrawidbhyāṃ samāgataḥ |
daheyaṃ khāṇḍawaṃ dāwametadannaṃ wṛtaṃ mayā ||10||

yuwāṃ hyudakadhārāstā bhūtāni ca samantataḥ |
uttamāstrawido samyaksarwato wārayiṣyathaḥ ||11||

ewamukte pratyuwāca bībhatsurjātawedasam |
didhakṣuṃ khāṇḍawaṃ dāwamakāmasya śatakratoḥ ||12||

uttamāstrāṇi me santi diwyāni ca bahūni ca |
yairahaṃ śaknuyāṃ yoddhumapi wajradharānbahūn ||13||

dhanurme nāsti bhagawanbāhuwīryeṇa saṃmitam |
kurwataḥ samare yatnaṃ wegaṃ yadwiṣaheta me ||14||

śaraiśca me'rtho bahubhirakṣayaiḥ kṣipramasyataḥ |
na hi woḍhuṃ rathaḥ śaktaḥ śarānmama yathepsitān ||15||

aśwāṃśca diwyāniccheyaṃ pāṇḍurānwātaraṃhasaḥ |
rathaṃ ca meghanirghoṣaṃ sūryapratimatejasam ||16||

tathā kṛṣṇasya wīryeṇa nāyudhaṃ widyate samam |
yena nāgānpiśācāṃśca nihanyānmādhawo raṇe ||17||

upāyaṃ karmaṇaḥ siddhau bhagawanwaktumarhasi |
niwārayeyaṃ yenendraṃ warṣamāṇaṃ mahāwane ||18||

pauruṣeṇa tu yatkāryaṃ tatkartārau swa pāwaka |
karaṇāni samarthāni bhagawandātumarhasi ||19||






                  216


waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktastu bhagawāndhūmaketurhutāśanaḥ |
cintayāmāsa waruṇaṃ lokapālaṃ didṛkṣayā ||1||

ādityamudake dewaṃ niwasantaṃ jaleśwaram ||1||

sa ca taccintitaṃ jñātwā darśayāmāsa pāwakam |
tamabrawīddhūmaketuḥ pratipūjya jaleśwaram ||2||

caturthaṃ lokapālānāṃ rakṣitāraṃ maheśwaram ||2||

somena rājñā yaddattaṃ dhanuścaiweṣudhī ca te |
tatprayacchobhayaṃ śīghraṃ rathaṃ ca kapilakṣaṇam ||3||

kāryaṃ hi sumahatpārtho gāṇḍīwena kariṣyati |
cakreṇa wāsudewaśca tanmadarthe pradīyatām ||4||

dadānītyewa waruṇaḥ pāwakaṃ pratyabhāṣata ||4||

tato'dbhutaṃ mahāwīryaṃ yaśaḥkīrtiwiwardhanam |
sarwaśastrairanādhṛṣyaṃ sarwaśastrapramāthi ca ||5||

sarwāyudhamahāmātraṃ parasenāpradharṣaṇam ||5||

ekaṃ śatasahasreṇa saṃmitaṃ rāṣṭrawardhanam |
citramuccāwacairwarṇaiḥ śobhitaṃ ślakṣṇamawraṇam ||6||

dewadānawagandharwaiḥ pūjitaṃ śāśwatīḥ samāḥ |
prādādwai dhanuratnaṃ tadakṣayyau ca maheṣudhī ||7||

rathaṃ ca diwyāśwayujaṃ kapiprawaraketanam |
upetaṃ rājatairaśwairgāndharwairhemamālibhiḥ ||8||

pāṇḍurābhrapratīkāśairmanowāyusamairjawe ||8||

sarwopakaraṇairyuktamajayyaṃ dewadānawaiḥ |
bhānumantaṃ mahāghoṣaṃ sarwabhūtamanoharam ||9||

sasarja yatswatapasā bhauwano bhuwanaprabhuḥ |
prajāpatiranirdeśyaṃ yasya rūpaṃ raweriwa ||10||

yaṃ sma somaḥ samāruhya dānawānajayatprabhuḥ |
nagameghapratīkāśaṃ jwalantamiwa ca śriyā ||11||

āśritā taṃ rathaśreṣṭhaṃ śakrāyudhasamā śubhā |
tāpanīyā surucirā dhwajayaṣṭiranuttamā ||12||

tasyāṃ tu wānaro diwyaḥ siṃhaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥ |
winardanniwa tatrasthaḥ saṃsthito mūrdhnyaśobhata ||13||

dhwaje bhūtāni tatrāsanwiwidhāni mahānti ca |
nādena ripusainyānāṃ yeṣāṃ sañjñā praṇaśyati ||14||

sa taṃ nānāpatākābhiḥ śobhitaṃ rathamuttamam |
pradakṣiṇamupāwṛtya daiwatebhyaḥ praṇamya ca ||15||

saṃnaddhaḥ kawacī khaḍgī baddhagodhāṅgulitrawān |
āruroha rathaṃ pārtho wimānaṃ sukṛtī yathā ||16||

tacca diwyaṃ dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ brahmaṇā nirmitaṃ purā |
gāṇḍīwamupasaṅgṛhya babhūwa mudito'rjunaḥ ||17||

hutāśanaṃ namaskṛtya tatastadapi wīryawān |
jagrāha balamāsthāya jyayā ca yuyuje dhanuḥ ||18||

maurwyāṃ tu yujyamānāyāṃ balinā pāṇḍawena ha |
ye'śṛṇwankūjitaṃ tatra teṣāṃ wai wyathitaṃ manaḥ ||19||

labdhwā rathaṃ dhanuścaiwa tathākṣayyau maheṣudhī |
babhūwa kalyaḥ kaunteyaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ sāhyakarmaṇi ||20||

wajranābhaṃ tataścakraṃ dadau kṛṣṇāya pāwakaḥ |
āgneyamastraṃ dayitaṃ sa ca kalyo'bhawattadā ||21||

abrawītpāwakaścainametena madhusūdana |
amānuṣānapi raṇe wijeṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ ||22||

anena twaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ dewānāmapi cāhawe |
rakṣaḥpiśācadaityānāṃ nāgānāṃ cādhikaḥ sadā ||23||

bhawiṣyasi na saṃdehaḥ prawarārinibarhaṇe ||23||

kṣiptaṃ kṣiptaṃ raṇe caitattwayā mādhawa śatruṣu |
hatwāpratihataṃ saṅkhye pāṇimeṣyati te punaḥ ||24||

waruṇaśca dadau tasmai gadāmaśaniniḥswanām |
daityāntakaraṇīṃ ghorāṃ nāmnā kaumodakīṃ hareḥ ||25||

tataḥ pāwakamabrūtāṃ prahṛṣṭau kṛṣṇapāṇḍawau |
kṛtāstrau śastrasampannau rathinau dhwajināwapi ||26||

kalyau swo bhagawanyoddhumapi sarwaiḥ surāsuraiḥ |
kiṃ punarwajriṇaikena pannagārthe yuyutsunā ||27||

arjuna uwāca||

cakramastraṃ ca wārṣṇeyo wisṛjanyudhi wīryawān |
triṣu lokeṣu tannāsti yanna jīyājjanārdanaḥ ||28||

gāṇḍīwaṃ dhanurādāya tathākṣayyau maheṣudhī |
ahamapyutsahe lokānwijetuṃ yudhi pāwaka ||29||

sarwataḥ pariwāryainaṃ dāwena mahatā prabho |
kāmaṃ samprajwalādyaiwa kalyau swaḥ sāhyakarmaṇi ||30||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktaḥ sa bhagawāndāśārheṇārjunena ca |
taijasaṃ rūpamāsthāya dāwaṃ dagdhuṃ pracakrame ||31||

sarwataḥ pariwāryātha saptārcirjwalanastadā |
dadāha khāṇḍawaṃ kruddho yugāntamiwa darśayan ||32||

parigṛhya samāwiṣṭastadwanaṃ bharatarṣabha |
meghastanitanirghoṣaṃ sarwabhūtāni nirdahan ||33||

dahyatastasya wibabhau rūpaṃ dāwasya bhārata |
meroriwa nagendrasya kāñcanasya mahādyuteḥ ||34||






                  217


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tau rathābhyāṃ narawyāghrau dāwasyobhayataḥ sthitau |
dikṣu sarwāsu bhūtānāṃ cakrāte kadanaṃ mahat ||1||

yatra yatra hi dṛśyante prāṇinaḥ khāṇḍawālayāḥ |
palāyantastatra tatra tau wīrau paryadhāwatām ||2||

chidraṃ hi na prapaśyanti rathayorāśuwikramāt |
āwiddhāwiwa dṛśyete rathinau tau rathottamau ||3||

khāṇḍawe dahyamāne tu bhūtānyatha sahasraśaḥ |
utpeturbhairawānnādānwinadanto diśo daśa ||4||

dagdhaikadeśā bahawo niṣṭaptāśca tathāpare |
sphuṭitākṣā wiśīrṇāśca wiplutāśca wicetasaḥ ||5||

samāliṅgya sutānanye pitṛnmātṛṃstathāpare |
tyaktuṃ na śekuḥ snehena tathaiwa nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ||6||

wikṛtairdarśanairanye samutpetuḥ sahasraśaḥ |
tatra tatra wighūrṇantaḥ punaragnau prapedire ||7||

dagdhapakṣākṣicaraṇā wiceṣṭanto mahītale |
tatra tatra sma dṛśyante winaśyantaḥ śarīriṇaḥ ||8||

jalasthāneṣu sarweṣu kwāthyamāneṣu bhārata |
gatasattwāḥ sma dṛśyante kūrmamatsyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ||9||

śarīraiḥ sampradīptaiśca dehawanta iwāgnayaḥ |
adṛśyanta wane tasminprāṇinaḥ prāṇasaṅkṣaye ||10||

tāṃstathotpatataḥ pārthaḥ śaraiḥ sañchidya khaṇḍaśaḥ |
dīpyamāne tataḥ prāsyatprahasankṛṣṇawartmani ||11||

te śarācitasarwāṅgā winadanto mahārawān |
ūrdhwamutpatya wegena nipetuḥ pāwake punaḥ ||12||

śarairabhyāhatānāṃ ca dahyatāṃ ca wanaukasām |
wirāwaḥ śrūyate ha sma samudrasyewa mathyataḥ ||13||

wahneścāpi prahṛṣṭasya khamutpeturmahārciṣaḥ |
janayāmāsurudwegaṃ sumahāntaṃ diwaukasām ||14||

tato jagmurmahātmānaḥ sarwa ewa diwaukasaḥ |
śaraṇaṃ dewarājānaṃ sahasrākṣaṃ puraṃdaram ||15||

dewā ūcuḥ||

kiṃ nwime mānawāḥ sarwe dahyante kṛṣṇawartmanā |
kaccinna saṅkṣayaḥ prāpto lokānāmamareśwara ||16||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tacchrutwā wṛtrahā tebhyaḥ swayamewānwawekṣya ca |
khāṇḍawasya wimokṣārthaṃ prayayau hariwāhanaḥ ||17||

mahatā meghajālena nānārūpeṇa wajrabhṛt |
ākāśaṃ samawastīrya prawawarṣa sureśwaraḥ ||18||

tato'kṣamātrā wisṛjandhārāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ |
abhyawarṣatsahasrākṣaḥ pāwakaṃ khāṇḍawaṃ prati ||19||

asamprāptāstu tā dhārāstejasā jātawedasaḥ |
kha ewa samaśuṣyanta na kāścitpāwakaṃ gatāḥ ||20||

tato namucihā kruddho bhṛśamarciṣmatastadā |
punarewābhyawarṣattamambhaḥ prawisṛjanbahu ||21||

arcirdhārābhisambaddhaṃ dhūmawidyutsamākulam |
babhūwa tadwanaṃ ghoraṃ stanayitnusaghoṣawat ||22||






                  218


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tasyābhiwarṣato wāri pāṇḍawaḥ pratyawārayat |
śarawarṣeṇa bībhatsuruttamāstrāṇi darśayan ||1||

śaraiḥ samantataḥ sarwaṃ khāṇḍawaṃ cāpi pāṇḍawaḥ |
chādayāmāsa tadwarṣamapakṛṣya tato wanāt ||2||

na ca sma kiñcicchaknoti bhūtaṃ niścarituṃ tataḥ |
sañchādyamāne khagamairasyatā sawyasācinā ||3||

takṣakastu na tatrāsītsarparājo mahābalaḥ |
dahyamāne wane tasminkurukṣetre'bhawattadā ||4||

aśwasenastu tatrāsīttakṣakasya suto balī |
sa yatnamakarottīwraṃ mokṣārthaṃ hawyawāhanāt ||5||

na śaśāka winirgantuṃ kaunteyaśarapīḍitaḥ |
mokṣayāmāsa taṃ mātā nigīrya bhujagātmajā ||6||

tasya pūrwaṃ śiro grastaṃ pucchamasya nigīryate |
ūrdhwamācakrame sā tu pannagī putragṛddhinī ||7||

tasyāstīkṣṇena bhallena pṛthudhāreṇa pāṇḍawaḥ |
śiraściccheda gacchantyāstāmapaśyatsureśwaraḥ ||8||

taṃ mumocayiṣurwajrī wātawarṣeṇa pāṇḍawam |
mohayāmāsa tatkālamaśwasenastwamucyata ||9||

tāṃ ca māyāṃ tadā dṛṣṭwā ghorāṃ nāgena wañcitaḥ |
dwidhā tridhā ca ciccheda khagatānewa bhārata ||10||

śaśāpa taṃ ca saṅkruddho bībhatsurjihmagāminam |
pāwako wāsudewaśca apratiṣṭho bhawediti ||11||

tato jiṣṇuḥ sahasrākṣaṃ khaṃ witatyeṣubhiḥ śitaiḥ |
yodhayāmāsa saṅkruddho wañcanāṃ tāmanusmaran ||12||

dewarāḍapi taṃ dṛṣṭwā saṃrabdhamiwa phalgunam |
swamastramasṛjaddīptaṃ yattatānākhilaṃ nabhaḥ ||13||

tato wāyurmahāghoṣaḥ kṣobhayansarwasāgarān |
wiyatstho'janayanmeghāñjaladhārāmuco''kulān ||14||

tadwighātārthamasṛjadarjuno'pyastramuttamam |
wāyawyamewābhimantrya pratipattiwiśāradaḥ ||15||

tenendrāśanimeghānāṃ wīryaujastadwināśitam |
jaladhārāśca tāḥ śoṣaṃ jagmurneśuśca widyutaḥ ||16||

kṣaṇena cābhawadwyoma sampraśāntarajastamaḥ |
sukhaśītānilaguṇaṃ prakṛtisthārkamaṇḍalam ||17||

niṣpratīkārahṛṣṭaśca hutabhugwiwidhākṛtiḥ |
prajajwālātulārciṣmānswanādaiḥ pūrayañjagat ||18||

kṛṣṇābhyāṃ rakṣitaṃ dṛṣṭwā taṃ ca dāwamahaṅkṛtāḥ |
samutpeturathākāśaṃ suparṇādyāḥ patatriṇaḥ ||19||

garuḍā wajrasadṛśaiḥ pakṣatuṇḍanakhaistathā |
prahartukāmāḥ sampeturākāśātkṛṣṇapāṇḍawau ||20||

tathaiworagasaṅghātāḥ pāṇḍawasya samīpataḥ |
utsṛjanto wiṣaṃ ghoraṃ niścerurjwalitānanāḥ ||21||

tāṃścakarta śaraiḥ pārthaḥ saroṣāndṛśya khecarān |
wiwaśāścāpatandīptaṃ dehābhāwāya pāwakam ||22||

tataḥ surāḥ sagandharwā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ |
utpeturnādamatulamutsṛjanto raṇārthiṇaḥ ||23||

ayaḥkaṇapacakrāśmabhuśuṇḍyudyatabāhawaḥ |
kṛṣṇapārthau jighāṃsantaḥ krodhasaṃmūrcchitaujasaḥ ||24||

teṣāmabhiwyāharatāṃ śastrawarṣaṃ ca muñcatām |
pramamāthottamāṅgāni bībhatsurniśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ||25||

kṛṣṇaśca sumahātejāścakreṇārinihā tadā |
daityadānawasaṅghānāṃ cakāra kadanaṃ mahat ||26||

athāpare śarairwiddhāścakrawegeritāstadā |
welāmiwa samāsādya wyātiṣṭhanta mahaujasaḥ ||27||

tataḥ śakro'bhisaṅkruddhastridaśānāṃ maheśwaraḥ |
pāṇḍuraṃ gajamāsthāya tāwubhau samabhidrawat ||28||

aśaniṃ gṛhya tarasā wajramastramawāsṛjat |
hatāwetāwiti prāha surānasurasūdanaḥ ||29||

tataḥ samudyatāṃ dṛṣṭwā dewendreṇa mahāśanim |
jagṛhuḥ sarwaśastrāṇi swāni swāni surāstadā ||30||

kāladaṇḍaṃ yamo rājā śibikāṃ ca dhaneśwaraḥ |
pāśaṃ ca waruṇastatra wicakraṃ ca tathā śiwaḥ ||31||

oṣadhīrdīpyamānāśca jagṛhāte'śwināwapi |
jagṛhe ca dhanurdhātā musalaṃ ca jayastathā ||32||

parwataṃ cāpi jagrāha kruddhastwaṣṭā mahābalaḥ |
aṃśastu śaktiṃ jagrāha mṛtyurdewaḥ paraśwadham ||33||

pragṛhya parighaṃ ghoraṃ wicacārāryamā api |
mitraśca kṣuraparyantaṃ cakraṃ gṛhya wyatiṣṭhata ||34||

pūṣā bhagaśca saṅkruddhaḥ sawitā ca wiśāṃ pate |
āttakārmukanistriṃśāḥ kṛṣṇapārthāwabhidrutāḥ ||35||

rudrāśca wasawaścaiwa marutaśca mahābalāḥ |
wiśwedewāstathā sādhyā dīpyamānāḥ swatejasā ||36||

ete cānye ca bahawo dewāstau puruṣottamau |
kṛṣṇapārthau jighāṃsantaḥ pratīyurwiwidhāyudhāḥ ||37||

tatrādbhutānyadṛśyanta nimittāni mahāhawe |
yugāntasamarūpāṇi bhūtotsādāya bhārata ||38||

tathā tu dṛṣṭwā saṃrabdhaṃ śakraṃ dewaiḥ sahācyutau |
abhītau yudhi durdharṣau tasthatuḥ sajjakārmukau ||39||

āgatāṃścaiwa tāndṛṣṭwā dewānekaikaśastataḥ |
nyawārayetāṃ saṅkruddhau bāṇairwajropamaistadā ||40||

asakṛdbhagnasaṅkalpāḥ surāśca bahuśaḥ kṛtāḥ |
bhayādraṇaṃ parityajya śakramewābhiśiśriyuḥ ||41||

dṛṣṭwā niwāritāndewānmādhawenārjunena ca |
āścaryamagamaṃstatra munayo diwi wiṣṭhitāḥ ||42||

śakraścāpi tayorwīryamupalabhyāsakṛdraṇe |
babhūwa paramaprīto bhūyaścaitāwayodhayat ||43||

tato'śmawarṣaṃ sumahadwyasṛjatpākaśāsanaḥ |
bhūya ewa tadā wīryaṃ jijñāsuḥ sawyasācinaḥ ||44||

taccharairarjuno warṣaṃ pratijaghne'tyamarṣaṇaḥ ||44||

wiphalaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ tatsamprekṣya ca śatakratuḥ |
bhūyaḥ saṃwardhayāmāsa tadwarṣaṃ dewarāḍatha ||45||

so'śmawarṣaṃ mahāwegairiṣubhiḥ pākaśāsaniḥ |
wilayaṃ gamayāmāsa harṣayanpitaraṃ tadā ||46||

samutpāṭya tu pāṇibhyāṃ mandarācchikharaṃ mahat |
sadrumaṃ wyasṛjacchakro jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍunandanam ||47||

tato'rjuno wegawadbhirjwalitāgrairajihmagaiḥ |
bāṇairwidhwaṃsayāmāsa gireḥ śṛṅgaṃ sahasradhā ||48||

girerwiśīryamāṇasya tasya rūpaṃ tadā babhau |
sārkacandragrahasyewa nabhasaḥ prawiśīryataḥ ||49||

tenāwākpatatā dāwe śailena mahatā bhṛśam |
bhūya ewa hatāstatra prāṇinaḥ khāṇḍawālayāḥ ||50||






                  219


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tathā śailanipātena bhīṣitāḥ khāṇḍawālayāḥ |
dānawā rākṣasā nāgāstarakṣwṛkṣawanaukasaḥ ||1||

dwipāḥ prabhinnāḥ śārdūlāḥ siṃhāḥ kesariṇastathā ||1||

mṛgāśca mahiṣāścaiwa śataśaḥ pakṣiṇastathā |
samudwignā wisasṛpustathānyā bhūtajātayaḥ ||2||

taṃ dāwaṃ samudīkṣantaḥ kṛṣṇau cābhyudyatāyudhau |
utpātanādaśabdena santrāsita iwābhawan ||3||

swatejobhāswaraṃ cakramutsasarja janārdanaḥ |
tena tā jātayaḥ kṣudrāḥ sadānawaniśācarāḥ ||4||

nikṛttāḥ śataśaḥ sarwā nipeturanalaṃ kṣaṇāt ||4||

adṛśyanrākṣasāstatra kṛṣṇacakrawidāritāḥ |
wasārudhirasampṛktāḥ sandhyāyāmiwa toyadāḥ ||5||

piśācānpakṣiṇo nāgānpaśūṃścāpi sahasraśaḥ |
nighnaṃścarati wārṣṇeyaḥ kālawattatra bhārata ||6||

kṣiptaṃ kṣiptaṃ hi taccakraṃ kṛṣṇasyāmitraghātinaḥ |
hatwānekāni sattwāni pāṇimeti punaḥ punaḥ ||7||

tathā tu nighnatastasya sarwasattwāni bhārata |
babhūwa rūpamatyugraṃ sarwabhūtātmanastadā ||8||

sametānāṃ ca dewānāṃ dānawānāṃ ca sarwaśaḥ |
wijetā nābhawatkaścitkṛṣṇapāṇḍawayormṛdhe ||9||

tayorbalātparitrātuṃ taṃ dāwaṃ tu yadā surāḥ |
nāśaknuwañśamayituṃ tadābhūwanparāṅmukhāḥ ||10||

śatakratuśca samprekṣya wimukhāndewatāgaṇān |
babhūwāwasthitaḥ prītaḥ praśaṃsankṛṣṇapāṇḍawau ||11||

niwṛtteṣu tu deweṣu wāguwācāśarīriṇī |
śatakratumabhiprekṣya mahāgambhīraniḥswanā ||12||

na te sakhā saṃnihitastakṣakaḥ pannagottamaḥ |
dāhakāle khāṇḍawasya kurukṣetraṃ gato hyasau ||13||

na ca śakyau twayā jetuṃ yuddhe'sminsamawasthitau |
wāsudewārjunau śakra nibodhedaṃ waco mama ||14||

naranārāyaṇau dewau tāwetau wiśrutau diwi |
bhawānapyabhijānāti yadwīryau yatparākramau ||15||

naitau śakyau durādharṣau wijetumajitau yudhi |
api sarweṣu lokeṣu purāṇāwṛṣisattamau ||16||

pūjanīyatamāwetāwapi sarwaiḥ surāsuraiḥ |
sayakṣarakṣogandharwanarakiṃnarapannagaiḥ ||17||

tasmāditaḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ gantumarhasi wāsawa |
diṣṭaṃ cāpyanupaśyaitatkhāṇḍawasya wināśanam ||18||

iti wācamabhiśrutya tathyamityamareśwaraḥ |
kopāmarṣau samutsṛjya sampratasthe diwaṃ tadā ||19||

taṃ prasthitaṃ mahātmānaṃ samawekṣya diwaukasaḥ |
twaritāḥ sahitā rājannanujagmuḥ śatakratum ||20||

dewarājaṃ tadā yāntaṃ saha dewairudīkṣya tu |
wāsudewārjunau wīrau siṃhanādaṃ winedatuḥ ||21||

dewarāje gate rājanprahṛṣṭau kṛṣṇapāṇḍawau |
nirwiśaṅkaṃ punardāwaṃ dāhayāmāsatustadā ||22||

sa māruta iwābhrāṇi nāśayitwārjunaḥ surān |
wyadhamaccharasampātaiḥ prāṇinaḥ khāṇḍawālayān ||23||

na ca sma kiñcicchaknoti bhūtaṃ niścarituṃ tataḥ |
sañchidyamānamiṣubhirasyatā sawyasācinā ||24||

nāśakaṃstatra bhūtāni mahāntyapi raṇe'rjunam |
nirīkṣitumamogheṣuṃ kariṣyanti kuto raṇam ||25||

śatenaikaṃ ca wiwyādha śataṃ caikena patriṇā |
wyasawaste'patannagnau sākṣātkālahatā iwa ||26||

na cālabhanta te śarma rodhaḥsu wiṣameṣu ca |
pitṛdewaniwāseṣu santāpaścāpyajāyata ||27||

bhūtasaṅghasahasrāśca dīnāścakrurmahāswanam |
ruruwurwāraṇāścaiwa tathaiwa mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ||28||

tena śabdena witresurgaṅgodadhicarā jhaṣāḥ ||28||

na hyarjunaṃ mahābāhuṃ nāpi kṛṣṇaṃ mahābalam |
nirīkṣituṃ wai śaknoti kaścidyoddhuṃ kutaḥ punaḥ ||29||

ekāyanagatā ye'pi niṣpatantyatra kecana |
rākṣasāndānawānnāgāñjaghne cakreṇa tānhariḥ ||30||

te wibhinnaśirodehāścakrawegādgatāsawaḥ |
peturāsye mahākāyā dīptasya wasuretasaḥ ||31||

sa māṃsarudhiraughaiśca medaughaiśca samīritaḥ |
uparyākāśago wahnirwidhūmaḥ samadṛśyata ||32||

dīptākṣo dīptajihwaśca dīptawyāttamahānanaḥ |
dīptordhwakeśaḥ piṅgākṣaḥ pibanprāṇabhṛtāṃ wasām ||33||

tāṃ sa kṛṣṇārjunakṛtāṃ sudhāṃ prāpya hutāśanaḥ |
babhūwa muditastṛptaḥ parāṃ nirwṛtimāgataḥ ||34||

athāsuraṃ mayaṃ nāma takṣakasya niweśanāt |
wipradrawantaṃ sahasā dadarśa madhusūdanaḥ ||35||

tamagniḥ prārthayāmāsa didhakṣurwātasārathiḥ |
dehawānwai jaṭī bhūtwā nadaṃśca jalado yathā ||36||

jighāṃsurwāsudewaśca cakramudyamya wiṣṭhitaḥ ||36||

sa cakramudyataṃ dṛṣṭwā didhakṣuṃ ca hutāśanam |
abhidhāwārjunetyewaṃ mayaścukrośa bhārata ||37||

tasya bhītaswanaṃ śrutwā mā bhairiti dhanañjayaḥ |
pratyuwāca mayaṃ pārtho jīwayanniwa bhārata ||38||

taṃ pārthenābhaye datte namucerbhrātaraṃ mayam |
na hantumaicchaddāśārhaḥ pāwako na dadāha ca ||39||

tasminwane dahyamāne ṣaḍagnirna dadāha ca |
aśwasenaṃ mayaṃ cāpi caturaḥ śārṅgakāniti ||40||






              śārṃgakopākhyānam
                  220


janamejaya uwāca||

kimarthaṃ śārṅgakānagnirna dadāha tathāgate |
tasminwane dahyamāne brahmannetadwadāśu me ||1||

adāhe hyaśwasenasya dānawasya mayasya ca |
kāraṇaṃ kīrtitaṃ brahmañśārṅgakānāṃ na kīrtitam ||2||

tadetadadbhutaṃ brahmañśārṅgānāmawināśanam |
kīrtayaswāgnisaṃmarde kathaṃ te na wināśitāḥ ||3||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

yadarthaṃ śārṅgakānagnirna dadāha tathāgate |
tatte sarwaṃ yathāwṛttaṃ kathayiṣyāmi bhārata ||4||

dharmajñānāṃ mukhyatamastapaswī saṃśitawrataḥ |
āsīnmaharṣiḥ śrutawānmandapāla iti śrutaḥ ||5||

sa mārgamāsthito rājannṛṣīṇāmūrdhwaretasām |
swādhyāyawāndharmaratastapaswī wijitendriyaḥ ||6||

sa gatwā tapasaḥ pāraṃ dehamutsṛjya bhārata |
jagāma pitṛlokāya na lebhe tatra tatphalam ||7||

sa lokānaphalāndṛṣṭwā tapasā nirjitānapi |
papraccha dharmarājasya samīpasthāndiwaukasaḥ ||8||

kimarthamāwṛtā lokā mamaite tapasārjitāḥ |
kiṃ mayā na kṛtaṃ tatra yasyedaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam ||9||

tatrāhaṃ tatkariṣyāmi yadarthamidamāwṛtam |
phalametasya tapasaḥ kathayadhwaṃ diwaukasaḥ ||10||

dewā ūcuḥ||

ṛṇino mānawā brahmañjāyante yena tacchṛṇu |
kriyābhirbrahmacaryeṇa prajayā ca na saṃśayaḥ ||11||

tadapākriyate sarwaṃ yajñena tapasā sutaiḥ |
tapaswī yajñakṛccāsi na tu te widyate prajā ||12||

ta ime prasawasyārthe tawa lokāḥ samāwṛtāḥ |
prajāyaswa tato lokānupabhoktāsi śāśwatān ||13||

punnāmno narakātputrastrātīti pitaraṃ mune |
tasmādapatyasantāne yataswa dwijasattama ||14||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tacchrutwā mandapālastu teṣāṃ wākyaṃ diwaukasām |
kwa nu śīghramapatyaṃ syādbahulaṃ cetyacintayat ||15||

sa cintayannabhyagacchadbahulaprasawānkhagān |
śārṅgikāṃ śārṅgako bhūtwā jaritāṃ samupeyiwān ||16||

tasyāṃ putrānajanayaccaturo brahmawādinaḥ |
tānapāsya sa tatraiwa jagāma lapitāṃ prati ||17||

bālānsutānaṇḍagatānmātrā saha munirwane ||17||

tasmingate mahābhāge lapitāṃ prati bhārata |
apatyasnehasaṃwignā jaritā bahwacintayat ||18||

tena tyaktānasantyājyānṛṣīnaṇḍagatānwane |
nājahatputrakānārtā jaritā khāṇḍawe nṛpa ||19||

babhāra caitānsañjātānswawṛttyā snehawiklawā ||19||

tato'gniṃ khāṇḍawaṃ dagdhumāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭawānṛṣiḥ |
mandapālaścaraṃstasminwane lapitayā saha ||20||

taṃ saṅkalpaṃ widitwāsya jñātwā putrāṃśca bālakān |
so'bhituṣṭāwa wiprarṣirbrāhmaṇo jātawedasam ||21||

putrānparidadadbhīto lokapālaṃ mahaujasam ||21||

mandapāla uwāca||

twamagne sarwadewānāṃ mukhaṃ twamasi hawyawāṭ |
twamantaḥ sarwabhūtānāṃ gūḍhaścarasi pāwaka ||22||

twāmekamāhuḥ kawayastwāmāhustriwidhaṃ punaḥ |
twāmaṣṭadhā kalpayitwā yajñawāhamakalpayan ||23||

twayā sṛṣṭamidaṃ wiśwaṃ wadanti paramarṣayaḥ |
twadṛte hi jagatkṛtsnaṃ sadyo na syāddhutāśana ||24||

tubhyaṃ kṛtwā namo wiprāḥ swakarmawijitāṃ gatim |
gacchanti saha patnībhiḥ sutairapi ca śāśwatīm ||25||

twāmagne jaladānāhuḥ khe wiṣaktānsawidyutaḥ |
dahanti sarwabhūtāni twatto niṣkramya hāyanāḥ ||26||

jātawedastawaiweyaṃ wiśwasṛṣṭirmahādyute |
tawaiwa karma wihitaṃ bhūtaṃ sarwaṃ carācaram ||27||

twayāpo wihitāḥ pūrwaṃ twayi sarwamidaṃ jagat |
twayi hawyaṃ ca kawyaṃ ca yathāwatsampratiṣṭhitam ||28||

agne twamewa jwalanastwaṃ dhātā twaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ |
twamaświnau yamau mitraḥ somastwamasi cānilaḥ ||29||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewaṃ stutastatastena mandapālena pāwakaḥ |
tutoṣa tasya nṛpate muneramitatejasaḥ ||30||

uwāca cainaṃ prītātmā kimiṣṭaṃ karawāṇi te ||30||

tamabrawīnmandapālaḥ prāñjalirhawyawāhanam |
pradahankhāṇḍawaṃ dāwaṃ mama putrānwisarjaya ||31||

tatheti tatpratiśrutya bhagawānhawyawāhanaḥ |
khāṇḍawe tena kālena prajajwāla didhakṣayā ||32||






                  221


waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataḥ prajwalite śukre śārṅgakāste suduḥkhitāḥ |
wyathitāḥ paramodwignā nādhijagmuḥ parāyaṇam ||1||

niśāmya putrakānbālānmātā teṣāṃ tapaswinī |
jaritā duḥkhasantaptā wilalāpa nareśwara ||2||

ayamagnirdahankakṣamita āyāti bhīṣaṇaḥ |
jagatsaṃdīpayanbhīmo mama duḥkhawiwardhanaḥ ||3||

ime ca māṃ karṣayanti śiśawo mandacetasaḥ |
abarhāścaraṇairhīnāḥ pūrweṣāṃ naḥ parāyaṇam ||4||

trāsayaṃścāyamāyāti lelihāno mahīruhān ||4||

aśaktimattwācca sutā na śaktāḥ saraṇe mama |
ādāya ca na śaktāsmi putrānsaritumanyataḥ ||5||

na ca tyaktumahaṃ śaktā hṛdayaṃ dūyatīwa me |
kaṃ nu jahyāmahaṃ putraṃ kamādāya wrajāmyaham ||6||

kiṃ nu me syātkṛtaṃ kṛtwā manyadhwaṃ putrakāḥ katham |
cintayānā wimokṣaṃ wo nādhigacchāmi kiñcana ||7||

chādayitwā ca wo gātraiḥ kariṣye maraṇaṃ saha ||7||

jaritārau kulaṃ hīdaṃ jyeṣṭhatwena pratiṣṭhitam |
sārisṛkwaḥ prajāyeta pitṛṇāṃ kulawardhanaḥ ||8||

stambamitrastapaḥ kuryāddroṇo brahmawiduttamaḥ |
ityewamuktwā prayayau pitā wo nirghṛṇaḥ purā ||9||

kamupādāya śakyeta gantuṃ kasyāpaduttamā |
kiṃ nu kṛtwā kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ bhawediti ca wihwalā ||10||

nāpaśyatswadhiyā mokṣaṃ swasutānāṃ tadānalāt |
ewaṃ bruwantīṃ śārṅgāste pratyūcuratha mātaram ||11||

snehamutsṛjya mātastwaṃ pata yatra na hawyawāṭ |
asmāsu hi winaṣṭeṣu bhawitāraḥ sutāstawa ||12||

twayi mātarwinaṣṭāyāṃ na naḥ syātkulasantatiḥ ||12||

anwawekṣyaitadubhayaṃ kṣamaṃ syādyatkulasya naḥ |
tadwai kartuṃ paraḥ kālo mātareṣa bhawettawa ||13||

mā wai kulawināśāya snehaṃ kārṣīḥ suteṣu naḥ |
na hīdaṃ karma moghaṃ syāllokakāmasya naḥ pituḥ ||14||

jaritowāca||

idamākhorbilaṃ bhūmau wṛkṣasyāsya samīpataḥ |
tadāwiśadhwaṃ twaritā wahneratra na wo bhayam ||15||

tato'haṃ pāṃsunā chidramapidhāsyāmi putrakāḥ |
ewaṃ pratikṛtaṃ manye jwalataḥ kṛṣṇawartmanaḥ ||16||

tata eṣyāmyatīte'gnau wihartuṃ pāṃsusañcayam |
rocatāmeṣa wopāyo wimokṣāya hutāśanāt ||17||

śārṅgakā ūcuḥ||

abarhānmāṃsabhūtānnaḥ krawyādākhurwināśayet |
paśyamānā bhayamidaṃ na śakṣyāmo niṣewitum ||18||

kathamagnirna no dahyātkathamākhurna bhakṣayet |
kathaṃ na syātpitā moghaḥ kathaṃ mātā dhriyeta naḥ ||19||

bila ākhorwināśaḥ syādagnerākāśacāriṇām |
anwawekṣyaitadubhayaṃ śreyāndāho na bhakṣaṇam ||20||

garhitaṃ maraṇaṃ naḥ syādākhunā khādatā bile |
śiṣṭādiṣṭaḥ parityāgaḥ śarīrasya hutāśanāt ||21||






                  222


jaritowāca||

asmādbilānniṣpatitaṃ śyena ākhuṃ jahāra tam |
kṣudraṃ gṛhītwā pādābhyāṃ bhayaṃ na bhawitā tataḥ ||1||

śārṅgakā ūcuḥ||

na hṛtaṃ taṃ wayaṃ widmaḥ śyenenākhuṃ kathañcana |
anye'pi bhawitāro'tra tebhyo'pi bhayamewa naḥ ||2||

saṃśayo hyagnirāgaccheddṛṣṭaṃ wāyorniwartanam |
mṛtyurno bilawāsibhyo bhawenmātarasaṃśayam ||3||

niḥsaṃśayātsaṃśayito mṛtyurmātarwiśiṣyate |
cara khe twaṃ yathānyāyaṃ putrānwetsyasi śobhanān ||4||

jaritowāca||

ahaṃ wai śyenamāyāntamadrākṣaṃ bilamantikāt |
sañcarantaṃ samādāya jahārākhuṃ bilādbalī ||5||

taṃ patantamahaṃ śyenaṃ twaritā pṛṣṭhato'nwagām |
āśiṣo'sya prayuñjānā harato mūṣakaṃ bilāt ||6||

yo no dweṣṭāramādāya śyenarāja pradhāwasi |
bhawa twaṃ diwamāsthāya niramitro hiraṇmayaḥ ||7||

yadā sa bhakṣitastena kṣudhitena patatriṇā |
tadāhaṃ tamanujñāpya pratyupāyāṃ gṛhānprati ||8||

prawiśadhwaṃ bilaṃ putrā wiśrabdhā nāsti wo bhayam |
śyenena mama paśyantyā hṛta ākhurna saṃśayaḥ ||9||

śārṅgakā ūcuḥ||

na widma wai wayaṃ mātarhṛtamākhumitaḥ purā |
awijñāya na śakṣyāmo bilamāwiśatuṃ wayam ||10||

jaritowāca||

ahaṃ hi taṃ prajānāmi hṛtaṃ śyenena mūṣakam |
ata ewa bhayaṃ nāsti kriyatāṃ wacanaṃ mama ||11||

śārṅgakā ūcuḥ||

na twaṃ mithyopacāreṇa mokṣayethā bhayaṃ mahat |
samākuleṣu jñāneṣu na buddhikṛtamewa tat ||12||

na copakṛtamasmābhirna cāsmānwettha ye wayam |
pīḍyamānā bharasyasmānkā satī ke wayaṃ tawa ||13||

taruṇī darśanīyāsi samarthā bhartureṣaṇe |
anugaccha swabhartāraṃ putrānāpsyasi śobhanān ||14||

wayamapyagnimāwiśya lokānprāpsyāmahe śubhān |
athāsmānna dahedagnirāyāstwaṃ punarewa naḥ ||15||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamuktā tataḥ śārṅgī putrānutsṛjya khāṇḍawe |
jagāma twaritā deśaṃ kṣemamagneranāśrayam ||16||

tatastīkṣṇārcirabhyāgājjwalito hawyawāhanaḥ |
yatra śārṅgā babhūwuste mandapālasya putrakāḥ ||17||

te śārṅgā jwalanaṃ dṛṣṭwā jwalitaṃ swena tejasā |
jaritāristato wācaṃ śrāwayāmāsa pāwakam ||18||






                  223


jaritāriruwāca||

purataḥ kṛcchrakālasya dhīmāñjāgarti pūruṣaḥ |
sa kṛcchrakālaṃ samprāpya wyathāṃ naiwaiti karhicit ||1||

yastu kṛcchramasamprāptaṃ wicetā nāwabudhyate |
sa kṛcchrakāle wyathito na prajānāti kiñcana ||2||

sārisṛkwa uwāca||

dhīrastwamasi medhāwī prāṇakṛcchramidaṃ ca naḥ |
śūraḥ prājño bahūnāṃ hi bhawatyeko na saṃśayaḥ ||3||

stambamitra uwāca||

jyeṣṭhastrātā bhawati wai jyeṣṭho muñcati kṛcchrataḥ |
jyeṣṭhaścenna prajānāti kanīyānkiṃ kariṣyati ||4||

droṇa uwāca||

hiraṇyaretāstwarito jwalannāyāti naḥ kṣayam |
saptajihwo'nalaḥ kṣāmo lelihānopasarpati ||5||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamukto bhrātṛbhistu jaritārirwibhāwasum |
tuṣṭāwa prāñjalirbhūtwā yathā tacchṛṇu pārthiwa ||6||

jaritāriruwāca||

ātmāsi wāyoḥ pawanaḥ śarīramuta wīrudhām |
yonirāpaśca te śukra yonistwamasi cāmbhasaḥ ||7||

ūrdhwaṃ cādhaśca gacchanti wisarpanti ca pārśwataḥ |
arciṣaste mahāwīrya raśmayaḥ sawituryathā ||8||

sārisṛkwa uwāca||

mātā prapannā pitaraṃ na widmaḥ; pakṣāśca no na prajātābjaketo |
na nastrātā widyate'gne twadanya; stasmāddhi naḥ parirakṣaikawīra ||9||

yadagne te śiwaṃ rūpaṃ ye ca te sapta hetayaḥ |
tena naḥ parirakṣādya īḍitaḥ śaraṇaiṣiṇaḥ ||10||

twamewaikastapase jātawedo; nānyastaptā widyate goṣu dewa |
ṛṣīnasmānbālakānpālayaswa; pareṇāsmānpraihi wai hawyawāha ||11||

stambamitra uwāca||

sarwamagne twamewaikastwayi sarwamidaṃ jagat |
twaṃ dhārayasi bhūtāni bhuwanaṃ twaṃ bibharṣi ca ||12||

twamagnirhawyawāhastwaṃ twamewa paramaṃ hawiḥ |
manīṣiṇastwāṃ yajante bahudhā caikadhaiwa ca ||13||

sṛṣṭwā lokāṃstrīnimānhawyawāha; prāpte kāle pacasi punaḥ samiddhaḥ |
sarwasyāsya bhuwanasya prasūti; stwamewāgne bhawasi punaḥ pratiṣṭhā ||14||

twamannaṃ prāṇināṃ bhuktamantarbhūto jagatpate |
nityaṃ prawṛddhaḥ pacasi twayi sarwaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||15||

droṇa uwāca||

sūryo bhūtwā raśmibhirjātawedo; bhūmerambho bhūmijātānrasāṃśca |
wiśwānādāya punarutsargakāle; sṛṣṭwā wṛṣṭyā bhāwayasīha śukra ||16||

twatta etāḥ punaḥ śukra wīrudho haritacchadāḥ |
jāyante puṣkariṇyaśca samudraśca mahodadhiḥ ||17||

idaṃ wai sadma tigmāṃśo waruṇasya parāyaṇam |
śiwastrātā bhawāsmākaṃ māsmānadya wināśaya ||18||

piṅgākṣa lohitagrīwa kṛṣṇawartmanhutāśana |
pareṇa praihi muñcāsmānsāgarasya gṛhāniwa ||19||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamukto jātawedā droṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā |
droṇamāha pratītātmā mandapālapratijñayā ||20||

ṛṣirdroṇastwamasi wai brahmaitadwyāhṛtaṃ twayā |
īpsitaṃ te kariṣyāmi na ca te widyate bhayam ||21||

mandapālena yūyaṃ hi mama pūrwaṃ niweditāḥ |
warjayeḥ putrakānmahyaṃ dahandāwamiti sma ha ||22||

yacca tadwacanaṃ tasya twayā yacceha bhāṣitam |
ubhayaṃ me garīyastadbrūhi kiṃ karawāṇi te ||23||

bhṛśaṃ prīto'smi bhadraṃ te brahmanstotreṇa te wibho ||23||

droṇa uwāca||

ime mārjārakāḥ śukra nityamudwejayanti naḥ |
etānkuruṣwa daṃṣṭrāsu hawyawāha sabāndhawān ||24||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tathā tatkṛtawānwahnirabhyanujñāya śārṅgakān |
dadāha khāṇḍawaṃ caiwa samiddho janamejaya ||25||






                  224


waiśampāyana uwāca||

mandapālo'pi kaurawya cintayānaḥ sutāṃstadā |
uktawānapyaśītāṃśuṃ naiwa sa sma na tapyate ||1||

sa tapyamānaḥ putrārthe lapitāmidamabrawīt |
kathaṃ nwaśaktāḥ plawane lapite mama putrakāḥ ||2||

wardhamāne hutawahe wāte śīghraṃ prawāyati |
asamarthā wimokṣāya bhawiṣyanti mamātmajāḥ ||3||

kathaṃ nwaśaktā trāṇāya mātā teṣāṃ tapaswinī |
bhawiṣyatyasukhāwiṣṭā putratrāṇamapaśyatī ||4||

kathaṃ nu saraṇe'śaktānpatane ca mamātmajān |
santapyamānā abhito wāśamānābhidhāwatī ||5||

jaritāriḥ kathaṃ putraḥ sārisṛkwaḥ kathaṃ ca me |
stambamitraḥ kathaṃ droṇaḥ kathaṃ sā ca tapaswinī ||6||

lālapyamānaṃ tamṛṣiṃ mandapālaṃ tathā wane |
lapitā pratyuwācedaṃ sāsūyamiwa bhārata ||7||

na te suteṣwawekṣāsti tānṛṣīnuktawānasi |
tejaswino wīryawanto na teṣāṃ jwalanādbhayam ||8||

tathāgnau te parīttāśca twayā hi mama saṃnidhau |
pratiśrutaṃ tathā ceti jwalanena mahātmanā ||9||

lokapālo'nṛtāṃ wācaṃ na tu waktā kathañcana |
samarthāste ca waktāro na te teṣwasti mānasam ||10||

tāmewa tu mamāmitrīṃ cintayanparitapyase |
dhruwaṃ mayi na te sneho yathā tasyāṃ purābhawat ||11||

na hi pakṣawatā nyāyyaṃ niḥsnehena suhṛjjane |
pīḍyamāna upadraṣṭuṃ śaktenātmā kathañcana ||12||

gaccha twaṃ jaritāmewa yadarthaṃ paritapyase |
cariṣyāmyahamapyekā yathā kāpuruṣe tathā ||13||

mandapāla uwāca||

nāhamewaṃ care loke yathā twamabhimanyase |
apatyahetorwicare tacca kṛcchragataṃ mama ||14||

bhūtaṃ hitwā bhawiṣye'rthe yo'walambeta mandadhīḥ |
awamanyeta taṃ loko yathecchasi tathā kuru ||15||

eṣa hi jwalamāno'gnirlelihāno mahīruhān |
dweṣyaṃ hi hṛdi santāpaṃ janayatyaśiwaṃ mama ||16||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tasmāddeśādatikrānte jwalane jaritā tataḥ |
jagāma putrakānewa twaritā putragṛddhinī ||17||

sā tānkuśalinaḥ sarwānnirmuktāñjātawedasaḥ |
rorūyamāṇā kṛpaṇā sutāndṛṣṭawatī wane ||18||

aśraddheyatamaṃ teṣāṃ darśanaṃ sā punaḥ punaḥ |
ekaikaśaśca tānputrānkrośamānānwapadyata ||19||

tato'bhyagacchatsahasā mandapālo'pi bhārata |
atha te sarwa ewainaṃ nābhyanandanta wai sutāḥ ||20||

lālapyamānamekaikaṃ jaritāṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ |
nocuste wacanaṃ kiñcittamṛṣiṃ sādhwasādhu wā ||21||

mandapāla uwāca||

jyeṣṭhaḥ sutaste katamaḥ katamastadanantaraḥ |
madhyamaḥ katamaḥ putraḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ katamaśca te ||22||

ewaṃ bruwantaṃ duḥkhārtaṃ kiṃ māṃ na pratibhāṣase |
kṛtawānasmi hawyāśe naiwa śāntimito labhe ||23||

jaritowāca||

kiṃ te jyeṣṭhe sute kāryaṃ kimanantarajena wā |
kiṃ ca te madhyame kāryaṃ kiṃ kaniṣṭhe tapaswini ||24||

yastwaṃ māṃ sarwaśo hīnāmutsṛjyāsi gataḥ purā |
tāmewa lapitāṃ gaccha taruṇīṃ cāruhāsinīm ||25||

mandapāla uwāca||

na strīṇāṃ widyate kiñcidanyatra puruṣāntarāt |
sāpatnakamṛte loke bhawitawyaṃ hi tattathā ||26||

suwratāpi hi kalyāṇī sarwalokapariśrutā |
arundhatī paryaśaṅkadwasiṣṭhamṛṣisattamam ||27||

wiśuddhabhāwamatyantaṃ sadā priyahite ratam |
saptarṣimadhyagaṃ wīramawamene ca taṃ munim ||28||

apadhyānena sā tena dhūmāruṇasamaprabhā |
lakṣyālakṣyā nābhirūpā nimittamiwa lakṣyate ||29||

apatyahetoḥ samprāptaṃ tathā twamapi māmiha |
iṣṭamewaṅgate hitwā sā tathaiwa ca wartase ||30||

naiwa bhāryeti wiśwāsaḥ kāryaḥ puṃsā kathañcana |
na hi kāryamanudhyāti bhāryā putrawatī satī ||31||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

tataste sarwa ewainaṃ putrāḥ samyagupāsire |
sa ca tānātmajānrājannāśwāsayitumārabhat ||32||






                  225


mandapāla uwāca||

yuṣmākaṃ parirakṣārthaṃ wijñapto jwalano mayā |
agninā ca tathetyewaṃ pūrwamewa pratiśrutam ||1||

agnerwacanamājñāya māturdharmajñatāṃ ca waḥ |
yuṣmākaṃ ca paraṃ wīryaṃ nāhaṃ pūrwamihāgataḥ ||2||

na santāpo hi waḥ kāryaḥ putrakā maraṇaṃ prati |
ṛṣīnweda hutāśo'pi brahma tadwiditaṃ ca waḥ ||3||

waiśampāyana uwāca||

ewamāśwāsya putrānsa bhāryāṃ cādāya bhārata |
mandapālastato deśādanyaṃ deśaṃ jagāma ha ||4||

bhagawānapi tigmāṃśuḥ samiddhaṃ khāṇḍawaṃ wanam |
dadāha saha kṛṣṇābhyāṃ janayañjagato'bhayam ||5||

wasāmedowahāḥ kulyāstatra pītwā ca pāwakaḥ |
agacchatparamāṃ tṛptiṃ darśayāmāsa cārjunam ||6||

tato'ntarikṣādbhagawānawatīrya sureśwaraḥ |
marudgaṇawṛtaḥ pārthaṃ mādhawaṃ cābrawīdidam ||7||

kṛtaṃ yuwābhyāṃ karmedamamarairapi duṣkaram |
warānwṛṇītaṃ tuṣṭo'smi durlabhānapyamānuṣān ||8||

pārthastu warayāmāsa śakrādastrāṇi sarwaśaḥ |
grahītuṃ tacca śakro'sya tadā kālaṃ cakāra ha ||9||

yadā prasanno bhagawānmahādewo bhawiṣyati |
tubhyaṃ tadā pradāsyāmi pāṇḍawāstrāṇi sarwaśaḥ ||10||

ahamewa ca taṃ kālaṃ wetsyāmi kurunandana |
tapasā mahatā cāpi dāsyāmi tawa tānyaham ||11||

āgneyāni ca sarwāṇi wāyawyāni tathaiwa ca |
madīyāni ca sarwāṇi grahīṣyasi dhanañjaya ||12||

wāsudewo'pi jagrāha prītiṃ pārthena śāśwatīm |
dadau ca tasmai dewendrastaṃ waraṃ prītimāṃstadā ||13||

dattwā tābhyāṃ waraṃ prītaḥ saha dewairmarutpatiḥ |
hutāśanamanujñāpya jagāma tridiwaṃ punaḥ ||14||

pāwakaścāpi taṃ dāwaṃ dagdhwā samṛgapakṣiṇam |
ahāni pañca caikaṃ ca wirarāma sutarpitaḥ ||15||

jagdhwā māṃsāni pītwā ca medāṃsi rudhirāṇi ca |
yuktaḥ paramayā prītyā tāwuwāca wiśāṃ pate ||16||

yuwābhyāṃ puruṣāgryābhyāṃ tarpito'smi yathāsukham |
anujānāmi wāṃ wīrau carataṃ yatra wāñchitam ||17||

ewaṃ tau samanujñātau pāwakena mahātmanā |
arjuno wāsudewaśca dānawaśca mayastathā ||18||

parikramya tataḥ sarwe trayo'pi bharatarṣabha |
ramaṇīye nadīkūle sahitāḥ samupāwiśan ||19||
